nānāmunijanākīrṇe nānāpuṣpopaśobhite ।। āmrajambūkapitthaiś ca nyagrodhair devadārubhiḥ ।। bakulaiḥ saptaparṇaiś ca puṃnāgair nāgakesaraiḥ ।। anyaiś ca bahubhir vṛkṣaiś campakādyaiś ca śobhite ।।
nānājalāśayaiḥ puṇyair dīrghikādyair alaṃkṛte ।। vānaprasthair gṛhasthaiś ca yatibhir brahmacāribhiḥ ।। yavagodhūmacaṇakair māṣamudgatilekṣubhiḥ ।। tatra dīpte hutavahe hūyamāne mahāmakhe ।।
ājagmus tatra munayas tathānye api dvijātayaḥ ।। teṣu tatropaviṣṭeṣu ṛtvigbhiḥ sahiteṣu ca ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā te munivarāḥ pūjāṃ cakrur mudānvitāḥ ।। kathāṃ cakrus tadānyonyaṃ sūtena sahitā dvijāḥ ।।
ṛtvigbhiḥ sahitāḥ sarve sadasyaiḥ saha dīkṣitāḥ ।। jānāsi devadaityānāṃ caritaṃ janma karma ca ।। purāṇe mokṣaśāstre ca sarvajño asi mahāmate ।। sasurāsuragandharvaṃ sayakṣoragarākṣasam ।।
babhūva bhūyaś ca yathā mahābhāga bhaviṣyati ।। līnam āsīt tathā yatra layam eṣyati yatra ca ।। sadaikarūparūpāya viṣṇave sarvajiṣṇave ।। vāsudevāya tārāya sargasthityantakarmaṇe ।।
avyaktavyaktabhūtāya viṣṇave muktihetave ।। mūlabhūto namas tasmai viṣṇave paramātmane ।। praṇamya sarvabhūtastham acyutaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tam evārthasvarūpeṇa bhrāntidarśanataḥ sthitam ।।
sarvajñaṃ jagatām īśam ajam akṣayam avyayam ।। itihāsapurāṇajñaṃ vedavedāṅgapāragam ।। guruṃ praṇamya vakṣyāmi purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmitam ।। pṛṣṭaḥ provāca bhagavān abjayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ ।।
kathyamānāṃ mayā citrāṃ bahvarthāṃ śrutivistarām ।। svavaṃśadhāraṇaṃ kṛtvā svargaloke mahīyate ।। pradhānaṃ puruṣas tasmān nirmame viśvam īśvaraḥ ।। sraṣṭāraṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ nārāyaṇaparāyaṇam ।।
bhūtabhedāś ca bhūtebhya iti sargaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। kīrtyamānaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ vaḥ sarveṣāṃ kīrtivardhanam ।। tataḥ svayaṃbhūr bhagavān sisṛkṣur vividhāḥ prajāḥ ।। āpo nārā iti proktā āpo vai narasūnavaḥ ।।
hiraṇyavarṇam abhavat tad aṇḍam udakeśayam ।। hiraṇyavarṇo bhagavān uṣitvā parivatsaram ।। tayoḥ śakalayor madhya ākāśam akarot prabhuḥ ।। tatra kālaṃ mano vācaṃ kāmaṃ krodham atho ratim ।।
marīcim atryaṅgirasau pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum ।। sapta brahmāṇa ity ete purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ ।। tato asṛjat purā brahmā rudraṃ roṣātmasaṃbhavam ।। saptasv etā ajāyanta prajā rudrāś ca bho dvijāḥ ।।
teṣāṃ sapta mahāvaṃśā divyā devagaṇānvitāḥ ।। vidyuto aśanimeghāṃś ca rohitendradhanūṃṣi ca ।। ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni nirmame yajñasiddhaye ।। uccāvacāni bhūtāni gātrebhyas tasya jajñire ।।
sṛjyamānāḥ prajā naiva vivardhante yadā tadā ।। ardhena nārī tasyāṃ tu so asṛjad dvividhāḥ prajāḥ ।। virājam asṛjad viṣṇuḥ so asṛjat puruṣaṃ virāṭ ।। dvitīyaṃ mānasasyaitan manor antaram ucyate ।।
nārāyaṇavisargasya prajās tasyāpy ayonijāḥ ।। ādisargaṃ viditvemaṃ yatheṣṭāṃ cāpnuyād gatim ।। lebhe vai puruṣaḥ patnīṃ śatarūpām ayonijām ।। dharmeṇaiva muniśreṣṭhāḥ śatarūpā vyajāyata ।।
bhartāraṃ dīptatapasaṃ puruṣaṃ pratyapadyata ।। tasyaikasaptatiyugaṃ manvantaram ihocyate ।। priyavratottānapādau vīrāt kāmyā vyajāyata ।। kāmyāputrās tu catvāraḥ samrāṭ kukṣir virāṭ prabhuḥ ।।
uttānapādāc caturaḥ sūnṛtā suṣuve sutān ।। utpannā vājimedhena dhruvasya jananī śubhā ।। uttānapādo ajanayat sūnṛtāyāṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। tapas tepe mahābhāgaḥ prārthayan sumahad yaśaḥ ।।
acalaṃ caiva purataḥ saptarṣīṇāṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। devāsurāṇām ācāryaḥ ślokaṃ prāg uśanā jagau ।। yam adya purataḥ kṛtvā dhruvaṃ saptarṣayaḥ sthitāḥ ।। śliṣṭer ādhatta succhāyā pañca putrān akalmaṣān ।।
ripor ādhatta bṛhatī cakṣuṣaṃ sarvatejasam ।। prajāpater ātmajāyāṃ vīraṇyasya mahātmanaḥ ।। kanyāyāṃ muniśārdūlā vairājasya prajāpateḥ ।। agniṣṭud atirātraś ca sudyumnaś ceti te nava ।।
puror ajanayat putrān ṣaḍ āgneyī mahāprabhān ।। aṅgāt sunīthāpatyaṃ vai veṇam ekaṃ vyajāyata ।। prajārtham ṛṣayo yasya mamanthur dakṣiṇaṃ karam ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ prāhur eṣa vai muditāḥ prajāḥ ।।
sa dhanvī kavacī jāto jvalajjvalanasaṃnibhaḥ ।। rājasūyābhiṣiktānām ādyaḥ sa vasudhāpatiḥ ।। teneyaṃ gaur muniśreṣṭhā dugdhā sasyāni bhūbhṛtā ।। pitṛbhir dānavaiś caiva gandharvair apsarogaṇaiḥ ।।
teṣu teṣu ca pātreṣu duhyamānā vasuṃdharā ।। pṛthos tu putrau dharmajñau yajñānte antardhipātinau ।। havirdhānāt ṣaḍ āgneyī dhiṣaṇājanayat sutān ।। prācīnabarhir bhagavān mahān āsīt prajāpatiḥ ।।
prācīnabarhir bhagavān pṛthivītalacāriṇīḥ ।। mahatas tapasaḥ pāre savarṇāyāṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। sarvān pracetaso nāma dhanurvedasya pāragān ।। daśa varṣasahasrāṇi samudrasalileśayāḥ ।।
arakṣamāṇām āvavrur babhūvātha prajākṣayaḥ ।। daśa varṣasahasrāṇi na śekuś ceṣṭituṃ prajāḥ ।। mukhebhyo vāyum agniṃ ca sasṛjur jātamanyavaḥ ।। tān agnir adahad ghora evam āsīd drumakṣayaḥ ।।
upagamyābravīd etāṃs tadā somaḥ prajāpatīn ।। vṛkṣaśūnyā kṛtā pṛthvī śāmyetām agnimārutau ।। bhaviṣyaṃ jānatā tāta dhṛtā garbheṇa vai mayā ।। bhāryā vo astu mahābhāgāḥ somavaṃśavivardhinī ।।
asyām utpatsyate vidvān dakṣo nāma prajāpatiḥ ।। agnināgnisamo bhūyaḥ prajāḥ saṃvardhayiṣyati ।। saṃhṛtya kopaṃ vṛkṣebhyaḥ patnīṃ dharmeṇa māriṣām ।। dakṣo jajñe mahātejāḥ somasyāṃśena bho dvijāḥ ।।
sa sṛṣṭvā manasā dakṣaḥ paścād asṛjata striyaḥ ।। śiṣṭāḥ somāya rājñe ca nakṣatrākhyā dadau prabhuḥ ।। gandharvāpsarasaś caiva jajñire anyāś ca jātayaḥ ।। saṃkalpād darśanāt sparśāt pūrveṣāṃ procyate prajā ।।
saṃbhavas tu śruto asmābhir dakṣasya ca mahātmanaḥ ।। vāmāṅguṣṭhāt tathā caivaṃ tasya patnī vyajāyata ।। dauhitraś caiva somasya kathaṃ śvaśuratāṃ gataḥ ।। ṛṣayo atra na muhyanti vidyāvantaś ca ye janāḥ ।।
punaś caiva nirudhyante vidvāṃs tatra na muhyati ।। tapa eva garīyo abhūt prabhāvaś caiva kāraṇam ।। prajāvān āyur uttīrṇaḥ svargaloke mahīyate ।। utpattiṃ vistareṇaiva lomaharṣaṇa kīrtaya ।।
yathā sasarja bhūtāni tathā śṛṇuta bho dvijāḥ ।। ṛṣīn devān sagandharvān asurān yakṣarākṣasān ।। tadā saṃcintya dharmātmā prajāhetoḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। asiknīm āvahat patnīṃ vīraṇasya prajāpateḥ ।।
atha putrasahasrāṇi vairaṇyāṃ pañca vīryavān ।। tāṃs tu dṛṣṭvā mahābhāgān saṃvivardhayiṣūn prajāḥ ।। nāśāya vacanaṃ teṣāṃ śāpāyaivātmanas tathā ।। dakṣasya vai duhitari dakṣaśāpabhayān muniḥ ।।
asiknyām atha vairaṇyāṃ bhūyo devarṣisattamaḥ ।। tena dakṣasya vai putrā haryaśvā iti viśrutāḥ ।। tasyodyatas tadā dakṣo nāśāyāmitavikramaḥ ।। tato abhisaṃdhiś cakre vai dakṣasya parameṣṭhinā ।।
sa tasyāṃ nārado jajñe bhūyaḥ śāpabhayād ṛṣiḥ ।। prajāpateḥ sūtavarya śrotum icchāma tattvataḥ ।। samāgatā mahāvīryā nāradas tān uvāca ha ।। pramāṇaṃ sraṣṭukāmā vai prajāḥ prācetasātmajāḥ ।।
te tu tadvacanaṃ śrutvā prayātāḥ sarvato diśaḥ ।। haryaśveṣv atha naṣṭeṣu dakṣaḥ prācetasaḥ punaḥ ।। vivardhayiṣavas te tu śabalāśvās tathā prajāḥ ।। anyonyam ūcus te sarve samyag āha mahān ṛṣiḥ ।।
jñātvā pramāṇaṃ pṛthvyāś ca sukhaṃ srakṣyāmahe prajāḥ ।। adyāpi na nivartante samudrebhya ivāpagāḥ ।। prayāto naśyati kṣipraṃ tan na kāryaṃ vipaścitā ।। ṣaṣṭiṃ tato asṛjat kanyā vairaṇyām iti naḥ śrutam ।।
somo dharmaś ca bho viprās tathaivānye maharṣayaḥ ।। saptaviṃśati somāya catasro ariṣṭanemine ।। dve kṛśāśvāya viduṣe tāsāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।। saṃkalpā ca muhūrtā ca sādhyā viśvā ca bho dvijāḥ ।।
viśvedevās tu viśvāyāḥ sādhyā sādhyān vyajāyata ।। bhānos tu bhānavaḥ putrā muhūrtās tu muhūrtajāḥ ।। pṛthivī viṣayaṃ sarvam arundhatyāṃ vyajāyata ।। nāgavīthyāṃ ca yāminyāṃ vṛṣalaś ca vyajāyata ।।
sarvā nakṣatranāmnyas tā jyotiṣe parikīrtitāḥ ।। vasavo aṣṭau samākhyātās teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi vistaram ।। pratyūṣaś ca prabhāsaś ca vasavo nāmabhiḥ smṛtāḥ ।। dhruvasya putro bhagavān kālo lokaprakālanaḥ ।।
manoharāyāḥ śiśiraḥ prāṇo atha ramaṇas tathā ।। avijñātagatiś caiva dvau putrāv anilasya ca ।। tasya śākho viśākhaś ca naigameyaś ca pṛṣṭhajaḥ ।। pratyūṣasya viduḥ putram ṛṣiṃ nāmnātha devalam ।।
bṛhaspates tu bhaginī varastrī brahmavādinī ।। prabhāsasya tu sā bhāryā vasūnām aṣṭamasya tu ।। kartā śilpasahasrāṇāṃ tridaśānāṃ ca vārdhakiḥ ।। yaḥ sarveṣāṃ vimānāni daivatānāṃ cakāra ha ।।
surabhī kaśyapād rudrān ekādaśa vinirmame ।। ajaikapād ahirbudhnyas tvaṣṭā rudraś ca vīryavān ।। vṛṣākapiś ca śaṃbhuś ca kapardī raivatas tathā ।। ekādaśaite vikhyātā rudrās tribhuvaneśvarāḥ ।।
purāṇe muniśārdūlā yair vyāptaṃ sacarācaram ।। aditir ditir danuś caiva ariṣṭā surasā khasā ।। kadrur muniś ca bho viprās tāsv apatyāni bodhata ।। tuṣitā nāma te anyonyam ūcur vaivasvate antare ।।
hitārthaṃ sarvalokānāṃ samāgamya parasparam ।। manvantare prasūyāmas tan naḥ śreyo bhaviṣyati ।। mārīcāt kaśyapāj jātās tv adityā dakṣakanyayā ।। aryamā caiva dhātā ca tvaṣṭā pūṣā tathaiva ca ।।
aṃśo bhagaś cātitejā ādityā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ ।। tāsām apatyāny abhavan dīptāny amitatejasaḥ ।। bahuputrasya viduṣaś catasro vidyutaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। kṛśāśvasya ca devarṣer devapraharaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
sarve devagaṇāś cātra trayastriṃśat tu kāmajāḥ ।। yathā sūryasya gagana udayāstamayāv iha ।। dityāḥ putradvayaṃ jajñe kaśyapād iti naḥ śrutam ।। siṃhikā cābhavat kanyā vipracitteḥ parigrahaḥ ।।
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putrāś catvāraḥ prathitaujasaḥ ।। saṃhrādaś ca caturtho abhūd dhrādaputro hradas tathā ।। virocanaś ca prāhrādir balir jajñe virocanāt ।। dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca sūryaś ca candramāś candratāpanaḥ ।।
bāṇas teṣām atibalo jyeṣṭhaḥ paśupateḥ priyaḥ ।। pārśvato vihariṣyāmi ity evaṃ yācito varaḥ ।। bharbharaḥ śakuniś caiva bhūtasaṃtāpanas tathā ।। abhavan danuputrāś ca śataṃ tīvraparākramāḥ ।।
dvimūrdhā śaṅkukarṇaś ca tathā hayaśirā vibhuḥ ।। mārīcir maghavāṃś caiva ilvalaḥ svasṛmas tathā ।। indrajit sarvajic caiva vajranābhas tathaiva ca ।। vaiśvānaraḥ pulomā ca vidrāvaṇamahāśirāḥ ।।
sarva ete danoḥ putrāḥ kaśyapād abhijajñire ।। eteṣāṃ putrapautraṃ tu na tac chakyaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। svarbhānos tu prabhā kanyā pulomnas tu śacī sutā ।। pulomā kālikā caiva vaiśvānarasute ubhe ।।
tayoḥ putrasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭir dānavanandanāḥ ।। marīcir janayām āsa mahatā tapasānvitaḥ ।। avadhyā devatānāṃ hi hiraṇyapuravāsinaḥ ।। tato apare mahāvīryā dānavās tv atidāruṇāḥ ।।
daityadānavasaṃyogāj jātās tīvraparākramāḥ ।। vaṃśyaḥ śalyaś ca balinau nalaś caiva tathā balaḥ ।। añjiko narakaś caiva kālanābhas tathaiva ca ।। ete vai dānavāḥ śreṣṭhā danor vaṃśavivardhanāḥ ।।
saṃhrādasya tu daityasya nivātakavacāḥ kule ।। tisraḥ koṭyaḥ sutās teṣāṃ maṇivatyāṃ nivāsinaḥ ।। ṣaṭ sutāḥ sumahābhāgās tāmrāyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। krauñcī tu janayām āsa ulūkapratyulūkakān ।।
śucir audakān pakṣigaṇān sugrīvī tu dvijottamāḥ ।। vinatāyās tu dvau putrau vikhyātau garuḍāruṇau ।। surasāyāḥ sahasraṃ tu sarpāṇām amitaujasām ।। kādraveyās tu balinaḥ sahasram amitaujasaḥ ।।
yeṣāṃ pradhānāḥ satataṃ śeṣavāsukitakṣakāḥ ।। elāpattraś ca śaṅkhaś ca karkoṭakadhanaṃjayau ।। kuharaḥ puṣpadaṃṣṭraś ca durmukhaḥ sumukhas tathā ।। nahuṣaḥ śaṅkharomā ca maṇir ity evamādayaḥ ।।
caturdaśasahasrāṇi krūrāṇām anilāśinām ।। sthalajāḥ pakṣiṇo abjāś ca dharāyāḥ prasavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। irā vṛkṣalatā vallīs tṛṇajātīś ca sarvaśaḥ ।। ariṣṭā tu mahāsiddhā gandharvān amitaujasaḥ ।।
yeṣāṃ putrāś ca pautrāś ca śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। vaivasvate atimahati vāruṇe vitate kratau ।। pūrvaṃ yatra samutpannān brahmarṣīn sapta mānasān ।। tato virodhe devānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca bho dvijāḥ ।।
kaśyapas tu prasannātmā samyag ārādhitas tayā ।। putram indravadhārthāya samartham amitaujasam ।। dattvā ca varam atyugro mārīcaḥ samabhāṣata ।। yadi dhārayase śauca- tatparā vratam āsthitā ।।
dhārayām āsa garbhaṃ tu śuciḥ sā munisattamāḥ ।। rodhayan vai gaṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ devānām amitaujasam ।। jagāma parvatāyaiva tapase saṃśitavratā ।। jāte varṣaśate cāsyā dadarśāntaram acyutaḥ ।।
nidrāṃ cāhārayām āsa tasyāṃ kukṣiṃ praviśya saḥ ।। sa pāṭyamāno garbho atha vajreṇa praruroda ha ।। so abhavat saptadhā garbhas tam indro ruṣitaḥ punaḥ ।। maruto nāma te devā babhūvur dvijasattamāḥ ।।
devāś caikonapañcāśat sahāyā vajrapāṇinaḥ ।। rocayan vai gaṇaśreṣṭhān devānām amitaujasām ।। kramaśas tāni rājyāni pṛthupūrvāṇi bho dvijāḥ ।। parjanyas tapano anantas tasya sarvam idaṃ jagat ।।
nāvṛttibhayam astīha paralokabhayaṃ kutaḥ ।। tataḥ krameṇa rājyāni vyādeṣṭum upacakrame ।। yajñānāṃ tapasāṃ caiva somaṃ rājye abhyaṣecayat ।। ādityānāṃ tathā viṣṇuṃ vasūnām atha pāvakam ।।
daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ vai prahrādam amitaujasam ।। yakṣāṇāṃ rākṣasānāṃ ca pārthivānāṃ tathaiva ca ।। śailānāṃ himavantaṃ ca nadīnām atha sāgaram ।। nāgānāṃ vāsukiṃ cakre sarpāṇām atha takṣakam ।।
uccaiḥśravasam aśvānāṃ garuḍaṃ caiva pakṣiṇām ।। vanaspatīnāṃ rājānaṃ plakṣam evābhyaṣecayat ।। diśāṃ pālān atha tataḥ sthāpayām āsa sa prabhuḥ ।। diśaḥ pālaṃ sudhanvānaṃ rājānaṃ so abhyaṣecayat ।।
putraṃ śaṅkhapadaṃ nāma rājānaṃ so abhyaṣecayat ।। ketumantaṃ mahātmānaṃ rājānaṃ so abhyaṣecayat ।। udīcyāṃ diśi durdharṣaṃ rājānaṃ so abhyaṣecayat ।। yathāpradeśam adyāpi dharmeṇa pratipālyate ।।
vedadṛṣṭena vidhinā rājā rājye narādhipaḥ ।। vaivasvatāya manave pṛthivyāṃ rājyam ādiśat ।। mahad etad adhiṣṭhānaṃ purāṇe tad adhiṣṭhitam ।। yathā mahātmanā tena dugdhā veyaṃ vasuṃdharā ।।
yathā daityaiś ca nāgaiś ca yathā yakṣair yathā drumaiḥ ।। rākṣasaiś ca mahāsattvair yathā dugdhā vasuṃdharā ।। vatsakṣīraviśeṣāṃś ca dogdhāraṃ cānupūrvaśaḥ ।। kruddhair maharṣibhis tāta kāraṇaṃ tac ca kīrtaya ।।
ekāgrāḥ prayatāś caiva puṇyārthaṃ vai dvijarṣabhāḥ ।। kīrtayeyam idaṃ viprāḥ kṛtaghnāyāhitāya ca ।। rahasyam ṛṣibhiḥ proktaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ vai yathātatham ।। brāhmaṇebhyo namaskṛtya na sa śocet kṛtākṛtam ।।
atrivaṃśe samutpannas tv aṅgo nāma prajāpatiḥ ।। jāto mṛtyusutāyāṃ vai sunīthāyāṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। svadharmaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā kāmalobheṣv avartata ।। vedadharmān atikramya so adharmanirato abhavat ।।
pravṛttaṃ na papuḥ somaṃ hutaṃ yajñeṣu devatāḥ ।। āsīt pratijñā krūreyaṃ vināśe pratyupasthite ।। mayi yajño vidhātavyo mayi hotavyam ity api ।। ūcur maharṣayaḥ sarve marīcipramukhās tadā ।।
adharmaṃ kuru mā veṇa eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। prajāś ca pālayiṣye aham itīha samayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। veṇaḥ prahasya durbuddhir imam artham anarthavit ।। śrutavīryatapaḥsatyair mayā vā kaḥ samo bhuvi ।।
saṃmūḍhā na vidur nūnaṃ bhavanto māṃ vicetasaḥ ।। dyāṃ vai bhuvaṃ ca rundheyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। apanetuṃ tadā veṇas tataḥ kruddhā maharṣayaḥ ।। tato asya savyam ūruṃ te mamanthur jātamanyavaḥ ।।
hrasvo atimātraḥ puruṣaḥ kṛṣṇaś ceti babhūva ha ।। tam atrir vihvalaṃ dṛṣṭvā niṣīdety abravīt tadā ।। dhīvarān asṛjac cāpi veṇakalmaṣasaṃbhavān ।। adharmarucayo viprās te tu vai veṇakalmaṣāḥ ।।
araṇīm iva saṃrabdhā mamanthur jātamanyavaḥ ।। dīpyamānaḥ svavapuṣā sākṣād agnir iva jvalan ।। śarāṃś ca divyān rakṣārthaṃ kavacaṃ ca mahāprabham ।। samāpetur mahābhāgā veṇas tu tridivaṃ yayau ।।
trātaḥ sa puruṣavyāghraḥ puṃnāmno narakāt tadā ।। toyāni cābhiṣekārthaṃ sarva evopatasthire ।। sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni jaṅgamāni ca sarvaśaḥ ।। mahatā rājarājena prajās tenānurañjitāḥ ।।
ādhirājye tadā rājñāṃ pṛthur vaiṇyaḥ pratāpavān ।। anurāgāt tatas tasya nāma rājābhyajāyata ।। parvatāś ca dadur mārgaṃ dhvajabhaṅgaś ca nābhavat ।। sarvakāmadughā gāvaḥ puṭake puṭake madhu ।।
sūtaḥ sūtyāṃ samutpannaḥ sautye ahani mahāmatiḥ ।। pṛthoḥ stavārthaṃ tau tatra samāhūtau maharṣibhiḥ ।। karmaitad anurūpaṃ vāṃ pātraṃ cāyaṃ narādhipaḥ ।। āvāṃ devān ṛṣīṃś caiva prīṇayāvaḥ svakarmabhiḥ ।।
stotraṃ yenāsya kuryāva rājñas tejasvino dvijāḥ ।। yāni karmāṇi kṛtavān pṛthuḥ paścān mahābalaḥ ।। āśīrvādāḥ prayujyante sūtamāgadhabandibhiḥ ।। anūpadeśaṃ sūtāya magadhaṃ māgadhāya ca ।।
vṛttīnām eṣa vo dātā bhaviṣyati narādhipaḥ ।। tvaṃ no vṛttiṃ vidhatsveti maharṣivacanāt tadā ।। dhanur gṛhya pṛṣatkāṃś ca pṛthivīm ādravad balī ।। tāṃ pṛthur dhanur ādāya dravantīm anvadhāvata ।।
pradadarśāgrato vaiṇyaṃ pragṛhītaśarāsanam ।। mahāyogaṃ mahātmānaṃ durdharṣam amarair api ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭā bhūtvā pūjyā lokais tribhis tadā ।। kathaṃ dhārayitā cāsi prajā rājan vinā mayā ।।
madvināśe vinaśyeyuḥ prajāḥ pārthiva viddhi tat ।। prajānāṃ pṛthivīpāla śṛṇu cedaṃ vaco mama ।। upāyaṃ paśya yena tvaṃ dhārayethāḥ prajām imām ।। anukūlā bhaviṣyāmi yaccha kopaṃ mahāmate ।।
yady evaṃ pṛthivīpāla na dharmaṃ tyaktum arhasi ।। kopaṃ nigṛhya dharmātmā vasudhām idam abravīt ।। bahūn vā prāṇino anantaṃ bhavet tasyeha pātakam ।। tasmin hate nāsti bhadre pātakaṃ copapātakam ।।
yadi me vacanān nādya kariṣyasi jagaddhitam ।। ātmānaṃ prathayitvāhaṃ prajā dhārayitā svayam ।। saṃjīvaya prajāḥ sarvāḥ samarthā hy asi dhāraṇe ।। niyaccheyaṃ tvadvadhārtham udyantaṃ ghoradarśanam ।।
vatsaṃ tu mama saṃpaśya kṣareyaṃ yena vatsalā ।। yathā visyandamānaṃ me kṣīraṃ sarvatra bhāvayet ।। dhanuṣkoṭyā tadā vaiṇyas tena śailā vivardhitāḥ ।। saṃvibhāgaḥ purāṇāṃ vā grāmāṇāṃ vābhavat tadā ।।
naiva satyānṛtaṃ cāsīn na lobho na ca matsaraḥ ।। vaiṇyāt prabhṛti vai viprāḥ sarvasyaitasya saṃbhavaḥ ।। tatra tatra prajāḥ sarvā nivāsaṃ samarocayan ।। kṛcchreṇa mahatā yukta ity evam anuśuśruma ।।
svapāṇau puruṣavyāghro dudoha pṛthivīṃ tataḥ ।। tenānnena prajāḥ sarvā vartante adyāpi sarvaśaḥ ।। daityā yakṣāḥ puṇyajanā gandharvāḥ parvatā nagāḥ ।। kṣīraṃ vatsaś ca pātraṃ ca teṣāṃ dogdhā pṛthak pṛthak ।।
kṣīraṃ teṣāṃ tapo brahma pātraṃ chandāṃsi bho dvijāḥ ।। kṣīram ojaskaraṃ caiva dogdhā ca bhagavān raviḥ ।। antakaś cābhavad dogdhā kṣīraṃ teṣāṃ sudhā smṛtā ।। dogdhā tv airāvato nāgas teṣāṃ kṣīraṃ viṣaṃ smṛtam ।।
virocanas tu vatso abhūd āyasaṃ pātram eva ca ।। dogdhā rajatanābhas tu kṣīrāntardhānam eva ca ।। dogdhā rajatanābhas tu kapālaṃ pātram eva ca ।। dogdhā ca suruciḥ kṣīraṃ teṣāṃ gandhaḥ śuciḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
vatsas tu himavān āsīd dogdhā merur mahāgiriḥ ।। pālāśapātraṃ kṣīraṃ ca cchinnadagdhaprarohaṇam ।। carācarasya sarvasya pratiṣṭhā yonir eva ca ।। āsīd iyaṃ samudrāntā medinī pariviśrutā ।।
teneyaṃ medinī devī ucyate brahmavādibhiḥ ।। duhitṛtvam anuprāptā devī pṛthvīti cocyate ।। sasyākaravatī sphītā purapattanaśālinī ।। namasyaś caiva pūjyaś ca bhūtagrāmair na saṃśayaḥ ।।
pṛthur eva namaskāryo brahmayoniḥ sanātanaḥ ।। ādirājo namaskāryaḥ pṛthur vaiṇyaḥ pratāpavān ।। ādirājo namaskāryo yodhānāṃ prathamo nṛpaḥ ।। sa ghorarūpāt saṃgrāmāt kṣemī bhavati kīrtimān ।।
pṛthur eva namaskāryo vṛttidātā mahāyaśāḥ ।। pṛthur eva namaskāryaḥ śreyaḥ param ihepsubhiḥ ।। pātrāṇi ca mayoktāni kiṃ bhūyo varṇayāmi vaḥ ।। teṣāṃ pūrvavisṛṣṭiṃ ca lomaharṣaṇa kīrtaya ।।
manvantarāṇi bhoḥ sūta śrotum icchāma tattvataḥ ।। manvantarāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ saṃkṣepāc chṛṇuta dvijāḥ ।। uttamas tāmasaś caiva raivataś cākṣuṣas tathā ।। sāvarṇiś ca manus tadvad raibhyo raucyas tathaiva ca ।।
atītā vartamānāś ca tathaivānāgatā dvijāḥ ।। ṛṣīṃs tv eṣāṃ pravakṣyāmi putrān devagaṇāṃs tathā ।। pulastyaś ca vasiṣṭhaś ca saptaite brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ ।। āgniidhraś cāgnibāhuś ca medhyo medhātithir vasuḥ ।।
manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasyaite daśa putrā mahaujasaḥ ।। aurvo vasiṣṭhaputraś ca stambaḥ kaśyapa eva ca ।। ete maharṣayo viprā vāyuproktā mahāvratāḥ ।। havighnaḥ sukṛtir jyotir āpo mūrtir api smṛtaḥ ।।
svārociṣasya putrās te manor viprā mahātmanaḥ ।। dvitīyam etat kathitaṃ viprā manvantaraṃ mayā ।। vasiṣṭhaputrāḥ saptāsan vāsiṣṭhā iti viśrutāḥ ।। ṛṣayo atra mayā proktāḥ kīrtyamānān nibodhata ।।
iṣa ūrjas tanūrjas tu madhur mādhava eva ca ।। bhānavas tatra devāś ca manvantaram udāhṛtam ।। kāvyaḥ pṛthus tathaivāgnir jahnur dhātā dvijottamāḥ ।। purāṇe kīrtitā viprāḥ putrāḥ pautrāś ca bho dvijāḥ ।।
dyutis tapasyaḥ sutapās tapobhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। tāmasasya manor ete daśa putrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। devabāhur yadudhraś ca munir vedaśirās tathā ।। satyanetras tathātreya ete saptarṣayo apare ।।
vāriplavaś ca raibhyaś ca manor antaram ucyate ।। dhṛtimān avyayo yuktas tattvadarśī nirutsukaḥ ।। raivatasya manoḥ putrāḥ pañcamaṃ caitad antaram ।। bhṛgur nabho vivasvāṃś ca sudhāmā virajās tathā ।।
cākṣuṣasyāntare viprā manor devās tv ime smṛtāḥ ।। lekhāś ca nāmato viprāḥ pañca devagaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। nāḍvaleyā muniśreṣṭhā daśa putrās tu viśrutāḥ ।। ṣaṣṭhaṃ manvantaraṃ proktaṃ saptamaṃ tu nibodhata ।।
gautamo atha bharadvājo viśvāmitras tathaiva ca ।। saptamo jamadagniś ca ṛṣayaḥ sāṃprataṃ divi ।। ādityāś cāśvinau cāpi devau vaivasvatau smṛtau ।। ikṣvākupramukhāś caiva daśa putrā mahātmanaḥ ।।
teṣāṃ putrāś ca pautrāś ca dikṣu sarvāsu bho dvijāḥ ।। loke dharmavyavasthārthaṃ lokasaṃrakṣaṇāya ca ।। kṛtvā karma divaṃ yānti brahmalokam anāmayam ।। atītā vartamānāś ca krameṇaitena bho dvijāḥ ।।
manor antaram āsādya sāvarṇasyeha bho dvijāḥ ।। bhāradvājas tathā drauṇir aśvatthāmā mahādyutiḥ ।। kauśiko gālavaś caiva aurvaḥ kāśyapa eva ca ।। vairī caivādhvarīvāṃś ca śamano dhṛtimān vasuḥ ।।
sāvarṇasya manoḥ putrā bhaviṣyā munisattamāḥ ।। yaśaś cāpnoti sumahad āyuṣmāṃś ca bhaven naraḥ ।। manvantarāṇi saṃkṣepāc chṛṇutānāgatāny api ।। eko vaivasvatas teṣāṃ catvāras tu prajāpateḥ ।।
dakṣasyaite hi dauhitrāḥ priyāyās tanayā nṛpāḥ ।। ruceḥ prajāpateḥ putro raucyo nāma manuḥ smṛtaḥ ।। anāgatāś ca saptaite kalpe asmin manavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। pūrṇaṃ yugasahasraṃ tu paripālyā dvijottamāḥ ।।
yugāni saptatis tāni sāgrāṇi kathitāni ca ।। caturdaśaite manavaḥ kathitāḥ kīrtivardhanāḥ ।। prajānāṃ patayo viprā dhanyam eṣāṃ prakīrtanam ।। na śakyate antas teṣāṃ vai vaktuṃ varṣaśatair api ।।
manvantareṣu saṃhārāḥ śrūyante dvijasattamāḥ ।। tapasā brahmacaryeṇa śrutena ca samanvitāḥ ।। tatra bhūtāni sarvāṇi dagdhāny ādityaraśmibhiḥ ।। praviśanti suraśreṣṭhaṃ harinārāyaṇaṃ prabhum ।।
avyaktaḥ śāśvato devas tasya sarvam idaṃ jagat ।। visargaṃ muniśārdūlāḥ sāṃpratasya mahādyuteḥ ।। yatrotpanno mahātmā sa harir vṛṣṇikule prabhuḥ ।। tasya bhāryābhavat saṃjñā tvāṣṭrī devī vivasvataḥ ।।
sā vai bhāryā bhagavato mārtaṇḍasya mahātmanaḥ ।। saṃjñā nāma sutapasā sudīptena samanvitā ।। gātreṣu paridagdhaṃ vai nātikāntam ivābhavat ।। ajānan kāśyapas tasmān mārtaṇḍa iti cocyate ।।
yenātitāpayām āsa trīṃl lokān kaśyapātmajaḥ ।। ādityo janayām āsa kanyāṃ dvau ca prajāpatī ।। yamaś ca yamunā caiva yamajau saṃbabhūvatuḥ ।। asahantī tu svāṃ chāyāṃ savarṇāṃ nirmame tataḥ ।।
prāñjaliḥ praṇatā bhūtvā chāyā saṃjñāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। sthitāsmi tava nirdeśe śādhi māṃ varavarṇini ।। tvayaiva bhavane mahyaṃ vastavyaṃ nirviśaṅkayā ।। saṃbhāvyās te na cākhyeyam idaṃ bhagavate kvacit ।।
ākhyāsyāmi namas tubhyaṃ gaccha devi yathāsukham ।। tvaṣṭuḥ samīpam agamad vrīḍiteva tapasvinī ।। bhartuḥ samīpaṃ gaccheti niyuktā ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। kurūn athottarān gatvā tṛṇāny atha cacāra ha ।।
ādityo janayām āsa putram ātmasamaṃ tadā ।। manur evābhavan nāmnā sāvarṇa iti cocyate ।। saṃjñā tu pārthivī viprāḥ svasya putrasya vai tadā ।। manus tasyāḥ kṣamat tat tu yamas tasyā na cakṣame ।।
padā saṃtarjayām āsa saṃjñāṃ vaivasvato yamaḥ ।। caraṇaḥ patatām eṣa taveti bhṛśaduḥkhitā ।। bhṛśaṃ śāpabhayodvignaḥ saṃjñāvākyair viśaṅkitaḥ ।। mātrā snehena sarveṣu vartitavyaṃ suteṣu vai ।।
tasyāṃ mayodyataḥ pādo na tu dehe nipātitaḥ ।। tava prasādāc caraṇo na paten mama gopate ।। yena tvām āviśat krodho dharmajñaṃ satyavādinam ।। kṛmayo māṃsam ādāya yāsyanty avanim eva ca ।।
śāpasya parihāreṇa tvaṃ ca trāto bhaviṣyasi ।। tulyeṣv abhyadhikaḥ sneha ekasmin kriyate tvayā ।। sa cātmānaṃ samādhāya yogāt tathyam apaśyata ।। mūrdhajeṣu nijagrāha sa tu tāṃ munisattamāḥ ।।
vivasvān atha tac chrutvā kruddhas tvaṣṭāram abhyagāt ।। nirdagdhukāmaṃ roṣeṇa sāntvayām āsa vai tadā ।। asahantī ca saṃjñā sā vane carati śāḍvale ।। ślāghyāṃ yogabalopetāṃ yogam āsthāya gopate ।।
rūpaṃ nirvartayāmy adya tava kāntam ariṃdama ।। bhramim āropya tat tejaḥ śātayām āsa bho dvijāḥ ।। kāntāt kāntataraṃ draṣṭum adhikaṃ śuśubhe tadā ।। adhṛṣyāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tejasā niyamena ca ।।
so aśvarūpeṇa bhagavāṃs tāṃ mukhe samabhāvayat ।। sā tan niravamac chukraṃ nāsikābhyāṃ vivasvataḥ ।। nāsatyaś caiva dasraś ca smṛtau dvāv aśvināv iti ।। tāṃ tu rūpeṇa kāntena darśayām āsa bhāskaraḥ ।।
yamas tu karmaṇā tena bhṛśaṃ pīḍitamānasaḥ ।। sa lebhe karmaṇā tena śubhena paramadyutiḥ ।। manuḥ prajāpatis tv āsīt sāvarṇiḥ sa tapodhanāḥ ।। merupṛṣṭhe tapo nityam adyāpi sa caraty uta ।।
tvaṣṭā tu tejasā tena viṣṇoś cakram akalpayat ।। yavīyasī tu sāpy āsīd yamī kanyā yaśasvinī ।। manur ity ucyate loke sāvarṇa iti cocyate ।। grahatvaṃ sa ca lebhe vai sarvalokābhipūjitaḥ ।।
āpadaṃ prāpya mucyeta prāpnuyāc ca mahad yaśaḥ ।। ikṣvākuś caiva nābhāgo dhṛṣṭaḥ śaryātir eva ca ।। karūṣaś ca pṛṣadhraś ca navaite munisattamāḥ ।। mitrāvaruṇayor viprāḥ pūrvam eva mahāmatiḥ ।।
tasyāṃ ca vartamānāyām iṣṭyāṃ ca dvijasattamāḥ ।। tatra divyāmbaradharā divyābharaṇabhūṣitā ।। tām ilety eva hovāca manur daṇḍadharas tadā ।। dharmayuktam idaṃ vākyaṃ putrakāmaṃ prajāpatim ।।
tayoḥ sakāśaṃ yāsyāmi na māṃ dharmahatāṃ kuru ।। gatvāntikaṃ varārohā prāñjalir vākyam abravīt ।। manunā cāham uktā vāai anugacchasva mām iti ।। mitraś ca varuṇaś cobhāv ūcatus tāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।।
satyena caiva suśroṇi prītau svo varavarṇini ।। āvayos tvaṃ mahābhāge khyātiṃ kanyeti yāsyasi ।। sudyumna iti vikhyātas triṣu lokeṣu śobhane ।। nivṛttā sā tu tac chrutvā gacchantī pitur antikāt ।।
somaputrād budhād viprās tasyāṃ jajñe purūravāḥ ।। sudyumnasya tu dāyādās trayaḥ paramadhārmikāḥ ।। utkalasyotkalā viprā vinatāśvasya paścimāḥ ।। praviṣṭe tu manau viprā divākaram ariṃdamam ।।
ikṣvākur jyeṣṭhadāyādo madhyadeśam avāptavān ।। vasiṣṭhavacanāt tv āsīt pratiṣṭhāne mahātmanaḥ ।। tat purūravase prādād rājyaṃ prāpya mahāyaśāḥ ।। dhṛtavāṃs tām ilety evaṃ sudyumneti ca viśrutaḥ ।।
ambarīṣo abhavat putraḥ pārthivarṣabhasattamaḥ ।। karūṣasya ca kārūṣāḥ kṣatriyā yuddhadurmadāḥ ।। prāṃśor eko abhavat putraḥ prajāpatir iti smṛtaḥ ।। śaryāter mithunaṃ tv āsīd ānarto nāma viśrutaḥ ।।
ānartasya tu dāyādo raivo nāma mahādyutiḥ ।। raivasya raivataḥ putraḥ kakudmī nāma dhārmikaḥ ।। sa kanyāsahitaḥ śrutvā gāndharvaṃ brahmaṇo antike ।। ājagāma sa caivātha svāṃ purīṃ yādavair vṛtām ।।
bhojavṛṣṇyandhakair guptāṃ vasudevapurogamaiḥ ।। kanyāṃ tāṃ baladevāya subhadrāṃ nāma revatīm ।। reme rāmo api dharmātmā revatyā sahitaḥ sukhī ।। na jarā revatīṃ prāptā raivataṃ ca kakudminam ।।
sthitā pṛthivyām adyāpi śrotum icchāma tattvataḥ ।। kakudminaḥ svarlokaṃ tu raivatasya gatasya ha ।। tasya bhrātṛśataṃ tv āsīd dhārmikasya mahātmanaḥ ।। vidrutasya ca viprendrās tasya bhrātṛśatasya vai ।।
teṣāṃ hy ete muniśreṣṭhāḥ śaryātā iti viśrutāḥ ।। śarvaśaḥ sarvagahanaṃ praviṣṭās te mahaujasaḥ ।। karūṣasya tu kārūṣāḥ kṣatriyā yuddhadurmadāḥ ।। śāpāc chūdratvam āpanno navaite parikīrtitāḥ ।।
kṣuvatas tu manor viprā ikṣvākur abhavat sutaḥ ।। teṣāṃ vikukṣir jyeṣṭhas tu vikukṣitvād ayodhatām ।। śakunipramukhās tasya putrāḥ pañcaśataṃ smṛtāḥ ।। catvāriṃśad daśāṣṭau ca dakṣiṇasyāṃ tathā diśi ।।
ikṣvākus tu vikukṣiṃ vāai aṣṭakāyām athādiśat ।। śrāddhakarmaṇi coddiṣṭo akṛte śrāddhakarmaṇi ।। ikṣvākuṇā parityakto vasiṣṭhavacanāt prabhuḥ ।। śaśādasya tu dāyādaḥ kakutstho nāma vīryavān ।।
viṣṭarāśvaḥ pṛthoḥ putras tasmād ārdras tv ajāyata ।। jajñe śrāvastako rājā śrāvastī yena nirmitā ।। kuvalāśvaḥ sutas tasya rājā paramadhārmikaḥ ।। yaḥ sa dhundhuvadhād rājā dhundhumāratvam āgataḥ ।।
yadvadhāt kuvalāśvo asau dhundhumāratvam āgataḥ ।। sarve vidyāsu niṣṇātā balavanto durāsadāḥ ।। kuvalāśvaṃ pitā rājye bṛhadaśvo nyayojayat ।। tam uttaṅko atha viprarṣiḥ prayāntaṃ pratyavārayat ।।
nirudvignas tapaś cartuṃ nahi śaknomi pārthiva ।। samudro vālukāpūrṇa uddālaka iti smṛtaḥ ।। antarbhūmigatas tatra vālukāntarhito mahān ।। śete lokavināśāya tapa āsthāya dāruṇam ।।
yadā tadā mahī tatra calati sma narādhipa ।। ādityapatham āvṛtya saptāhaṃ bhūmikampanam ।। tena tāta na śaknomi tasmin sthātuṃ sva āśrame ।। lokāḥ svasthā bhavanty adya tasmin vinihate tvayā ।।
viṣṇunā ca varo datto mahyaṃ pūrvayuge nṛpa ।। tasya tvaṃ varadānena tejaś cākhyāpayiṣyasi ।। nirdagdhuṃ pṛthivīpāla ciraṃ yugaśatair api ।। kuvalāśvaṃ sutaṃ prādāt tasmai dhundhunibarhaṇe ।।
bhaviṣyati dvijaśreṣṭha dhundhumāro na saṃśayaḥ ।। jagāma parvatāyaiva nṛpatiḥ saṃśitavrataḥ ।। prāyād uttaṅkasahito dhundhos tasya nibarhaṇe ।। uttaṅkasya niyogād vai lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।।
eṣa śrīmān avadhyo adya dhundhumāro bhaviṣyati ।। devadundubhayaś caiva praṇedur dvijasattamāḥ ।। samudraṃ khānayām āsa vālukāntaram avyayam ।। dhundhur āsādito viprā diśam āvṛtya paścimām ।।
vāri susrāva vegena mahodadhir ivodaye ।। tasya putraśataṃ dagdhaṃ tribhir ūnaṃ tu rakṣasā ।। āsasāda mahātejā dhundhuṃ dhundhuvināśanaḥ ।। yogī yogena vahniṃ ca śamayām āsa vāriṇā ।।
uttaṅkaṃ darśayām āsa kṛtakarmā narādhipaḥ ।। dadau tasyākṣayaṃ vittaṃ śatrubhiś cāparājitam ।। putrāṇāṃ cākṣayāṃl lokān svarge ye rakṣasā hatāḥ ।। candrāśvakapilāśvau tu kanīyāṃsau kumārakau ।।
haryaśvasya nikumbho abhūt kṣatradharmarataḥ sadā ।। akṛśāśvakṛśāśvau tu saṃhatāśvasutau dvijāḥ ।। vikhyātā triṣu lokeṣu putraś cāsyāḥ prasenajit ।। abhiśastā tu sā bhartrā nadī vai bāhudābhavat ।।
māndhātā yuvanāśvasya trilokavijayī sutaḥ ।। sādhvī bindumatī nāma rūpeṇāsadṛśī bhuvi ।। tasyām utpādayām āsa māndhātā dvau sutau dvijāḥ ।। purukutsasutas tv āsīt trasadasyur mahīpatiḥ ।।
saṃbhūtasya tu dāyādas tridhanvā ripumardanaḥ ।। tasya satyavrato nāma kumāro abhūn mahābalaḥ ।। yena bhāryā kṛtodvāhā hṛtā caiva parasya ha ।। jahāra kanyāṃ kāmārtaḥ kasyacit puravāsinaḥ ।।
apadhvaṃseti bahuśo vadan krodhasamanvitaḥ ।। pitā ca tam athovāca śvapākaiḥ saha vartaya ।। ity uktaḥ sa nirākrāman nagarād vacanāt pituḥ ।। sa tu satyavrato viprāḥ śvapākāvasathāntike ।।
tatas tasmiṃs tu viṣaye nāvarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ ।। dārāṃs tu tasya viṣaye viśvāmitro mahātapāḥ ।। tasya patnī gale baddhvā madhyamaṃ putram aurasam ।। taṃ ca baddhaṃ gale dṛṣṭvā vikrayārthaṃ nṛpātmajaḥ ।।
satyavrato mahābāhur bharaṇaṃ tasya cākarot ।। maharṣiḥ kauśiko dhīmāṃs tena vīreṇa mokṣitaḥ ।। viśvāmitrakalatraṃ tu babhāra vinaye sthitaḥ ।। viśvāmitrāśramābhyāśe māṃsaṃ vṛkṣe babandha ca ।।
pitur niyogād avasat tasmin vanagate nṛpe ।। yājyopādhyāyasaṃyogād vasiṣṭhaḥ paryarakṣata ।। vasiṣṭhe abhyadhikaṃ manyuṃ dhārayām āsa nityaśaḥ ।। nivārayām āsa munir bahunā kāraṇena na ।।
na ca satyavratas tasmād dhatavān saptame pade ।। satyavratas tadā roṣaṃ vasiṣṭhe manasākarot ।। na ca satyavratas tasya tam upāṃśum abudhyata ।। tena dvādaśa varṣāṇi nāvarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ ।।
kulasya niṣkṛtir viprāḥ kṛtā sā vai bhaved iti ।। abhiṣekṣyāmy ahaṃ putram asyety evaṃmatir muniḥ ।। avidyamāne māṃse tu vasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ ।। tāṃ vai krodhāc ca mohāc ca śramāc caiva kṣudhānvitaḥ ।।
tanmāṃsaṃ sa svayaṃ caiva viśvāmitrasya cātmajān ।। bhojayām āsa tac chrutvā vasiṣṭho apy asya cukrudhe ।। yadi te dvāv imau śaṅkū na syātāṃ vai kṛtau punaḥ ।। aprokṣitopayogāc ca trividhas te vyatikramaḥ ।।
triśaṅkur iti hovāca triśaṅkus tena sa smṛtaḥ ।। tena tasmai varaṃ prādān muniḥ prītas triśaṅkave ।। saśarīro vraje svargam ity evaṃ yācito varaḥ ।। pitrye rājye abhiṣicyātha yājayām āsa pārthivam ।।
divam āropayām āsa saśarīraṃ mahātapāḥ ।। kumāraṃ janayām āsa hariścandram akalmaṣam ।। āhartā rājasūyasya samrāḍ iti ha viśrutaḥ ।। harito rohitasyātha cañcur hārita ucyate ।।
jetā sa sarvapṛthivīṃ vijayas tena sa smṛtaḥ ।। rurukasya vṛkaḥ putro vṛkād bāhus tu jajñivān ।। tatpatnī garbham ādāya aurvasyāśramam āviśat ।। sagaras tu suto bāhor yajñe saha gareṇa vai ।।
āgneyam astraṃ labdhvā ca bhārgavāt sagaro nṛpaḥ ।। kṣatriyāṇāṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ pāradānāṃ ca dharmavit ।। kimarthaṃ ca śakādīnāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahaujasām ।। etan naḥ sarvam ācakṣva vistareṇa mahāmate ।।
haihayais tālajaṅghaiś ca śakaiḥ sārdhaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। ete hy api gaṇāḥ pañca haihayārthe parākraman ।। patnyā cānugato duḥkhī tatra prāṇān avāsṛjat ।। sapatnyā ca garas tasyai dattaḥ pūrvaṃ kilānaghāḥ ।।
aurvas tāṃ bhārgavo viprāḥ kāruṇyāt samavārayat ।। vyajāyata mahābāhuḥ sagaro nāma pārthivaḥ ।। adhyāpya vedaśāstrāṇi tato astraṃ pratyapādayat ।। sa tenāstrabalenājau balena ca samanvitaḥ ।।
ājahāra ca lokeṣu kīrtiṃ kīrtimatāṃ varaḥ ।। pahnavāṃś caiva niḥśeṣān kartuṃ vyavasito nṛpaḥ ।। vasiṣṭhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā praṇipetur manīṣiṇam ।। sagaraṃ vārayām āsa teṣāṃ dattvābhayaṃ tadā ।।
dharmaṃ jaghāna teṣāṃ vai veṣān anyāṃś cakāra ha ।। yavanānāṃ śiraḥ sarvaṃ kāmbojānāṃ tathaiva ca ।। niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkārāḥ kṛtās tena mahātmanā ।। koṇisarpā māhiṣakā darvāś colāḥ sakeralāḥ ।।
vasiṣṭhavacanād rājñā sagareṇa mahātmanā ।। aśvaṃ pracārayām āsa vājimedhāya dīkṣitaḥ ।। velāsamīpe apahṛto bhūmiṃ caiva praveśitaḥ ।। āsedus te tadā tatra khanyamāne mahārṇave ।।
viṣṇuṃ kapilarūpeṇa svapantaṃ puruṣaṃ tadā ।। dagdhāḥ sarve muniśreṣṭhāś catvāras tv avaśeṣitāḥ ।। śūraḥ pañcanadaś caiva tasya vaṃśakarā nṛpāḥ ।। akṣayaṃ vaṃśam ikṣvākoḥ kīrtiṃ cāpy anivartinīm ।।
samudraś cārgham ādāya vavande taṃ mahīpatim ।। taṃ cāśvamedhikaṃ so aśvaṃ samudrād upalabdhavān ।। putrāṇāṃ ca sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭis tasyeti naḥ śrutam ।। vikrāntāḥ ṣaṣṭisāhasrā vidhinā kena sattama ।।
jyeṣṭhā vidarbhaduhitā keśinī nāma nāmataḥ ।। ariṣṭanemiduhitā rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvi ।। ṣaṣṭiṃ putrasahasrāṇi gṛhṇātv ekā nitambinī ।। tatraikā jagṛhe putrān ṣaṣṭisāhasrasaṃmitān ।।
rājā pañcajano nāma babhūva sa mahādyutiḥ ।। tatra ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi garbhās te tilasaṃmitāḥ ।। ghṛtapūrṇeṣu kumbheṣu tān garbhān nidadhe tataḥ ।। tato daśasu māseṣu samuttasthur yathākramam ।।
ṣaṣṭiputrasahasrāṇi tasyaivam abhavan dvijāḥ ।। teṣāṃ nārāyaṇaṃ tejaḥ praviṣṭānāṃ mahātmanām ।। śūraḥ pañcajanasyāsīd aṃśumān nāma vīryavān ।। yena svargād ihāgatya muhūrtaṃ prāpya jīvitam ।।
dilīpasya tu dāyādo mahārājo bhagīrathaḥ ।। samudram ānayac caināṃ duhitṛtve apy akalpayat ।। bhagīrathasuto rājā śruta ity abhiviśrutaḥ ।। ambarīṣas tu nābhāgiḥ sindhudvīpapitābhavat ।।
ayutājitsutas tv āsīd ṛtuparṇo mahāyaśāḥ ।। ṛtuparṇasutas tv āsīd ārtaparṇir mahāyaśāḥ ।। sudāsasya sutaḥ proktaḥ saudāso nāma pārthivaḥ ।। kalmāṣapādasya sutaḥ sarvakarmeti viśrutaḥ ।।
anaraṇyasuto nighno nighnato dvau babhūvatuḥ ।। anamitrasuto rājā vidvān duliduho abhavat ।। dīrghabāhur dilīpasya raghur nāmnā suto abhavat ।। ajas tu rāghavo jajñe tathā daśaratho apy ajāt ।।
rāmasya tanayo jajñe kuśa ity abhisaṃjñitaḥ ।। atithes tv abhavat putro niṣadho nāma vīryavān ।। nabhasya puṇḍarīkas tu kṣemadhanvā tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। āsīd ahīnagur nāma devānīkātmajaḥ prabhuḥ ।।
sudhanvanaḥ sutaś cāpi tato jajñe śalo nṛpaḥ ।। vajranābhaḥ sutas tasya nalas tasya mahātmanaḥ ।। vīrasenātmajaś caiva yaś cekṣvākukulodvahaḥ ।। ete vivasvato vaṃśe rājāno bhūritejasaḥ ।।
prajāvān eti sāyujyam ādityasya vivasvataḥ ।। brahmaṇo mānasāt pūrvaṃ prajāsargaṃ vidhitsataḥ ।। trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi divyānīti hi naḥ śrutam ।। netrābhyāṃ vāri susrāva daśadhā dyotayan diśaḥ ।।
sametya dhārayām āsur na ca tāḥ samaśaknuvan ।। tatas tābhiḥ sa tyaktas tu nipapāta vasuṃdharām ।। ratham āropayām āsa lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। tuṣṭuvur brahmaṇaḥ putrās tathānye munisattamāḥ ।।
āpyāyanāya lokānāṃ bhāvayām āsa sarvataḥ ।। triḥsaptakṛtvo atiyaśāś cakārābhipradakṣiṇām ।। oṣadhyas tāḥ samudbhūtā yābhiḥ saṃdhāryate jagat ।। tapas tepe mahābhāgaḥ padmānāṃ darśanāya saḥ ।।
bījauṣadhīnāṃ viprāṇām apāṃ ca munisattamāḥ ।। samājahre rājasūyaṃ sahasraśatadakṣiṇam ।। tebhyo brahmarṣimukhyebhyaḥ sadasyebhyaś ca bho dvijāḥ ।। sadasyo abhūd dharis tatra munibhir bahubhir vṛtaḥ ।।
kīrtir dhṛtiś ca lakṣmīś ca nava devyaḥ siṣevire ।। virarājādhirājendro daśadhā bhāsayan diśaḥ ।। vibabhrāma matis tātā- vinayād anayāhṛtā ।। jahāra tarasā somo vimatyāṅgirasaḥ sutam ।।
naiva vyasarjayat tārāṃ tasmāy aṅgirase tadā ।। rudraś ca pārṣṇiṃ jagrāha gṛhītvājagavaṃ dhanuḥ ।। uddiśya devān utsṛṣṭaṃ yenaiṣāṃ nāśitaṃ yaśaḥ ।। devānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca lokakṣayakaraṃ mahat ।।
brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmur ādidevaṃ sanātanam ।। dadāv aṅgirase tārāṃ svayam eva pitāmahaḥ ।। madīyāyāṃ na te yonau garbho dhāryaḥ kathaṃcana ।। jātamātraḥ sa bhagavān devānām ākṣipad vapuḥ ।।
satyaṃ brūhi sutaḥ kasya somasyātha bṛhaspateḥ ।। tadā tāṃ śaptum ārabdhaḥ kumāro dasyuhantamaḥ ।। yad atra tathyaṃ tad brūhi tāre kasya sutas tv ayam ।। tadā taṃ mūrdhni cāghrāya somo rājā sutaṃ prati ।।
pratikūlaṃ ca gagane samabhyuttiṣṭhate budhaḥ ।। tasyāpatyaṃ mahātejā babhūvailaḥ purūravāḥ ।। etat somasya vo janma kīrtitaṃ kīrtivardhanam ।। dhanyam āyuṣyam ārogyaṃ puṇyaṃ saṃkalpasādhanam ।।
somasya janma śrutvaiva pāpebhyo vipramucyate ।। tejasvī dānaśīlaś ca yajvā vipuladakṣiṇaḥ ।। āhartā cāgnihotrasya yajñānāṃ ca mahīpatiḥ ।। atīva triṣu lokeṣu yaśasāpratimaḥ sadā ।।
urvaśī varayām āsa hitvā mānaṃ yaśasvinī ।। ṣaṭ pañca sapta cāṣṭau ca daśa cāṣṭau ca bho dvijāḥ ।। alakāyāṃ viśālāyāṃ nandane ca vanottame ।। gandhamādanapādeṣu meruśṛṅge tathottare ।।
urvaśyā sahito rājā reme paramayā mudā ।। rājyaṃ sa kārayām āsa prayāge pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। uttare jāhnavītīre pratiṣṭhāne mahāyaśāḥ ।। gandharvaloke viditā āyur dhīmān amāvasuḥ ।।
dṛḍhāyuś ca vanāyuś ca bahvāyuś corvaśīsutāḥ ।। śrīmān bhīmasya dāyādo rājāsīt kāñcanaprabhaḥ ।। suhotrasyābhavaj jahnuḥ keśinyā garbhasaṃbhavaḥ ।। patilobhena yaṃ gaṅgā patitvena sasāra ha ।।
sa tayā plāvitaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñavāṭaṃ samantataḥ ।। eṣa te viphalaṃ yatnaṃ pibann ambhaḥ karomy aham ।। jahnurājarṣiṇā pītāṃ gaṅgāṃ dṛṣṭvā maharṣayaḥ ।। yuvanāśvasya putrīṃ tu kāverīṃ jahnur āvahat ।।
kāverīṃ saritāṃ śreṣṭhāṃ jahnor bhāryām aninditām ।। kāveryāṃ janayām āsa ajakas tasya cātmajaḥ ।। babhūva mṛgayāśīlaḥ kuśas tasyātmajo abhavat ।। kuśikaḥ kuśanābhaś ca kuśāmbo mūrtimāṃs tathā ।।
kuśikas tu tapas tepe putram indrasamaṃ prabhuḥ ।। pūrṇe varṣasahasre vai tataḥ śakro hy apaśyata ।। samarthaḥ putrajanane svayam evāsya śāśvataḥ ।। sa gādhir abhavad rājā maghavān kauśikaḥ svayam ।।
gādheḥ kanyā mahābhāgā nāmnā satyavatī śubhā ।। tasyāḥ prītaḥ sa vai bhartā bhārgavo bhṛgunandanaḥ ।। uvācāhūya tāṃ bhāryām ṛcīko bhārgavas tadā ।। tasyāṃ janiṣyate putro dīptimān kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ ।।
tavāpi putraṃ kalyāṇi dhṛtimantaṃ tapodhanam ।। evam uktvā tu tāṃ bhāryām ṛcīko bhṛgunandanaḥ ।। gādhiḥ sadāras tu tadā ṛcīkāśramam abhyagāt ।। carudvayaṃ gṛhītvā sā ṛṣeḥ satyavatī tadā ।।
mātā tu tasyā daivena duhitre svaṃ caruṃ dadau ।। atha satyavatī sarvaṃ kṣatriyāntakaraṃ tadā ।। tām ṛcīkas tato dṛṣṭvā yogenābhyupasṛtya ca ।। mātrāsi vañcitā bhadre caruvyatyāsahetunā ।।
bhrātā janiṣyate cāpi brahmabhūtas tapodhanaḥ ।। evam uktā mahābhāgā bhartrā satyavatī tadā ।। brāhmaṇāpasadas tvatta ity ukto munir abravīt ।। ugrakarmā bhavet putraḥ pitur mātuś ca kāraṇāt ।।
icchaṃl lokān api mune sṛjethāḥ kiṃ punaḥ sutam ।। kāmam evaṃvidhaḥ pautro mama syāt tava ca prabho ।। tataḥ prasādam akarot sa tasyās tapaso balāt ।। tvayā yathoktaṃ vacanaṃ tathā bhadre bhaviṣyati ।।
tapasy abhirataṃ dāntaṃ jamadagniṃ samātmakam ।। sā hi satyavatī puṇyā satyadharmaparāyaṇā ।। ikṣvākuvaṃśaprabhavo reṇur nāma narādhipaḥ ।। reṇukāyāṃ tu kāmalyāṃ tapovidyāsamanvitaḥ ।।
sarvavidyāntagaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dhanurvedasya pāragam ।। aurvasyaivam ṛcīkasya satyavatyāṃ mahāyaśāḥ ।। madhyamaś ca śunaḥśephaḥ śunaḥpucchaḥ kaniṣṭhakaḥ ।। janayām āsa putraṃ tu tapovidyāśamātmakam ।।
viśvāmitras tu dharmātmā nāmnā viśvarathaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। viśvāmitrasya ca sutā devarātādayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। devarātaḥ katiś caiva yasmāt kātyāyanāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। sāṃkṛtir gālavaś caiva mudgalaś caiva viśrutaḥ ।।
kacchapo hāritaś caiva viśvāmitrasya te sutāḥ ।। pāṇino babhravaś caiva dhyānajapyās tathaiva ca ।। lohitā yamadūtāś ca tathā kārūṣakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। saṃbandho apy asya vaṃśe asmin brahmakṣatrasya viśrutaḥ ।।
bhārgavaḥ kauśikatvaṃ hi prāptaḥ sa munisattamaḥ ।। haridaśvasya yajñe tu paśutve viniyojitaḥ ।। devair dattaḥ sa vai yasmād devarātas tato abhavat ।। dṛṣadvatīsutaś cāpi vaiśvāmitras tathāṣṭakaḥ ।।
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi vaṃśam āyor mahātmanaḥ ।। svarbhānutanayāyāṃ ca prabhāyāṃ jajñire nṛpāḥ ।। rambho rajir anenāś ca triṣu lokeṣu viśrutāḥ ।। rājeyam iti vikhyātaṃ kṣatram indrabhayāvaham ।।
devāś caivāsurāś caiva pitāmaham athābruvan ।। brūhi naḥ sarvabhūteśa śrotum icchāma tattvataḥ ।। yotsyate te vijeṣyanti trīṃl lokān nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। yato dhṛtiś ca śrīś caiva dharmas tatra jayas tathā ।।
abhyayur jayam icchanto vṛṇvānās taṃ nararṣabham ।। rājā paramatejasvī somavaṃśavivardhanaḥ ।। ūcur asmajjayāya tvaṃ gṛhāṇa varakārmukam ।। arthajñaḥ svārtham uddiśya yaśaḥ svaṃ ca prakāśayan ।।
indro bhavāmi dharmeṇa tato yotsyāmi saṃyuge ।। evaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ nṛpate kāmaḥ saṃpadyatāṃ tava ।। papracchāsuramukhyāṃs tu yathā devān apṛcchata ।। pratyūcus taṃ nṛpavaraṃ sābhimānam idaṃ vacaḥ ।।
asmiṃs tu samare rājaṃs tiṣṭha tvaṃ rājasattama ।। bhaviṣyasīndro jitvainaṃ devair uktas tu pārthivaḥ ।। sa vipranaṣṭāṃ devānāṃ paramaśrīḥ śriyaṃ vaśī ।। tato rajiṃ mahāvīryaṃ devaiḥ saha śatakratuḥ ।।
indro asi tāta devānāṃ sarveṣāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। sa tu śakravacaḥ śrutvā vañcitas tena māyayā ।। tasmiṃs tu devaiḥ sadṛśo divaṃ prāpte mahīpatau ।। pañca putraśatāny asya tad vai sthānaṃ śatakratoḥ ।।
te yadā tu svasaṃmūḍhā rāgonmattā vidharmiṇaḥ ।। tato lebhe svam aiśvaryam indraḥ sthānaṃ tathottamam ।। śṛṇuyād dhārayed vāpi na sa daurgatyam āpnuyāt ।। anenasaḥ suto rājā pratikṣatro mahāyaśāḥ ।।
saṃjayasya jayaḥ putro vijayas tasya cātmajaḥ ।। haryatvatasuto rājā sahadevaḥ pratāpavān ।। nadīnasya jayatseno jayatsenasya saṃkṛtiḥ ।। anenasaḥ samākhyātāḥ kṣatravṛddhasya cāparaḥ ।।
sunahotrasya dāyādās trayaḥ paramadhārmikāḥ ।। putro gṛtsamadasyāpi śunako yasya śaunakaḥ ।। śalātmaja ārṣṭiseṇas tanayas tasya kāśyapaḥ ।। dhanus tu dīrghatapaso vidvān dhanvantaris tataḥ ।।
punar dhanvantarir devo mānuṣeṣv iha janmani ।। kāśirājo mahārājaḥ sarvarogapraṇāśanaḥ ।। tam aṣṭadhā punar vyasya śiṣyebhyaḥ pratyapādayat ।। atha ketumataḥ putro vīro bhīmarathaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
divodāsas tu dharmātmā vārāṇasyadhipo abhavat ।। śūnyāṃ niveśayām āsa kṣemako nāma rākṣasaḥ ।। śūnyā varṣasahasraṃ vai bhavitrī tu na saṃśayaḥ ।। viṣayānte purīṃ ramyāṃ gomatyāṃ saṃnyaveśayat ।।
bhadraśreṇyasya putrāṇāṃ śatam uttamadhanvinām ।। bhadraśreṇyasya tad rājyaṃ hṛtaṃ yena balīyasā ।। divodāsena bāleti ghṛṇayā sa visarjitaḥ ।। ājahre pitṛdāyādyaṃ divodāsahṛtaṃ balāt ।।
vairasyānto mahābhāgāḥ kṛtaś cātmīyatejasā ।। tena bālena putreṇa prahṛtaṃ tu punar balam ।। vatsaputro hy alarkas tu saṃnatis tasya cātmajaḥ ।। alarkaṃ prati rājarṣiṃ śloko gītaḥ purātanaiḥ ।।
yuvā rūpeṇa saṃpannaḥ prāg āsīc ca kulodvahaḥ ।। tasyāsīt sumahad rājyaṃ rūpayauvanaśālinaḥ ।। ramyāṃ niveśayām āsa purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ punaḥ ।। sunīthasya tu dāyādaḥ kṣemo nāma mahāyaśāḥ ।।
suketos tanayaś cāpi dharmaketur iti smṛtaḥ ।। satyaketusutaś cāpi vibhur nāma prajeśvaraḥ ।। sukumārasya putras tu dhṛṣṭaketuḥ sudhārmikaḥ ।। veṇuhotrasutaś cāpi bhārgo nāma prajeśvaraḥ ।।
ete tv aṅgirasaḥ putrā jātā vaṃśe atha bhārgava ।। ity ete kāśyapāḥ proktā nahuṣasya nibodhata ।। nahuṣasya tu dāyādāḥ ṣaḍ indropamatejasaḥ ।। yatir jyeṣṭhas tu teṣāṃ vai yayātis tu tataḥ param ।।
yatis tu mokṣam āsthāya brahmabhūto abhavan muniḥ ।। devayānīm uśanasaḥ sutāṃ bhāryām avāpa saḥ ।। yaduṃ ca turvasuṃ caiva devayānī vyajāyata ।। tasmai śakro dadau prīto rathaṃ paramabhāsvaram ।।
yuktaṃ manojavaiḥ śubhrair yena kāryaṃ samudvahan ।। yayātir yudhi durdharṣas tathā devān sadānavān ।। saṃvartavasunāmnas tu kauravāj janamejayāt ।। jagāma sa ratho nāśaṃ śāpād gargasya dhīmataḥ ।।
kālena hiṃsayām āsa brahmahatyām avāpa saḥ ।। paurajānapadais tyakto na lebhe śarma karhicit ।। viprendraṃ śaunakaṃ rājā śaraṇaṃ pratyapadyata ।। aśvamedhena rājānaṃ pāvanārthaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।।
sa ca divyaratho rājño vaśaś cedipates tadā ।। bṛhadrathāt krameṇaiva gato bārhadrathaṃ nṛpam ।। pradadau vāsudevāya prītyā kauravanandanaḥ ।। vibhajya pañcadhā rājyaṃ putrāṇāṃ nāhuṣas tadā ।।
madhye puruṃ ca rājānam abhyaṣiñcat sa nāhuṣaḥ ।। tair iyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā sapattanā ।। prajās teṣāṃ purastāt tu vakṣyāmi munisattamāḥ ।। jarāvān abhavad rājā bhāram āveśya bandhuṣu ।।
prītimān abhavad rājā yayātir aparājitaḥ ।। jarāṃ me pratigṛhṇīṣva putra kṛtyāntareṇa vai ।। jarāṃ tvayi samādhāya taṃ yaduḥ pratyuvāca ha ।। anapākṛtya tāṃ rājan na grahīṣyāmi te jarām ।।
tasmāj jarāṃ na te rājan grahītum aham utsahe ।। pratigrahītuṃ dharmajña putram anyaṃ vṛṇīṣva vai ।। uvāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭho yayātir garhayan sutam ।। mām anādṛtya durbuddhe yad ahaṃ tava deśikaḥ ।।
arājyā te prajā mūḍha bhavitrīti na saṃśayaḥ ।। evam evābravīd rājā pratyākhyātaś ca tair api ।। yathāvat kathitaṃ sarvaṃ mayāsya dvijasattamāḥ ।। tad eva vacanaṃ rājā purum apy āha bho dvijāḥ ।।
jarāṃ tvayi samādhāya tvaṃ puro yadi manyase ।। yayātir api rūpeṇa puroḥ paryacaran mahīm ।। viśvācyā sahito reme vane caitrarathe prabhuḥ ।। tadā puroḥ sakāśād vai svāṃ jarāṃ pratyapadyata ।।
yābhiḥ pratyāharet kāmān sarvaśo aṅgāni kūrmavat ।। haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate ।। nālam ekasya tat sarvam iti kṛtvā na muhyati ।। karmaṇā manasā vācā brahma saṃpadyate tadā ।।
yadā necchati na dveṣṭi brahma saṃpadyate tadā ।। yo asau prāṇāntiko rogas tāṃ tṛṣṇāṃ tyajataḥ sukham ।। dhanāśā jīvitāśā ca jīryato api na jīryati ।। tṛṣṇākṣayasukhasyaite nārhanti ṣoḍaśīṃ kalām ।।
kālena mahatā cāyaṃ cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ ।। anaśnan deham utsṛjya sadāraḥ svargam āptavān ।। yair vyāptā pṛthivī sarvā sūryasyeva gabhastibhiḥ ।। yatra nārāyaṇo jajñe harir vṛṣṇikulodvahaḥ ।।
yayāticaritaṃ nityam idaṃ śṛṇvan dvijottamāḥ ।। druhyasyānor yadoś caiva turvasoś ca pṛthak pṛthak ।। vistareṇānupūrvyā ca prathamaṃ vadato mama ।। rājā cābhayado nāma manasyor abhavat sutaḥ ।।
sudhanvanaḥ subāhuś ca raudrāśvas tasya cātmajaḥ ।। kakṣeyusthaṇḍileyuś ca sannateyus tathaiva ca ।। dhaneyuś ca vaneyuś ca putrakāś ca daśa striyaḥ ।। khaladā ca tato viprā naladā surasāpi ca ।।
ṛṣir jāto atrivaṃśe ca tāsāṃ bhartā prabhākaraḥ ।। svarbhānunā hate sūrye patamāne divo mahīm ।। svasti te astv iti coktvā vai patamāno divākaraḥ ।। atriśreṣṭhāni gotrāṇi yaś cakāra mahātapāḥ ।।
sa tāsu janayām āsa putrikāsv ātmakāmajān ।। te tu gotrakarā viprā ṛṣayo vedapāragāḥ ।। kakṣeyos tanayās tv āsaṃs traya eva mahārathāḥ ।। sabhānarasya putras tu vidvān kālānalo nṛpaḥ ।।
sṛñjayasyābhavat putro vīro rājā puraṃjayaḥ ।। janamejayasya rājarṣer mahāśālo abhavat sutaḥ ।। mahāmanā nāma suto mahāśālasya viśrutaḥ ।। mahāmanās tu putrau dvau janayām āsa bho dvijāḥ ।।
uśīnarasya patnyas tu pañca rājarṣivaṃśajāḥ ।। uśīnarasya putrās tu pañca tāsu kulodvahāḥ ।। nṛgāyās tu nṛgaḥ putraḥ kṛmyāṃ kṛmir ajāyata ।। dṛṣadvatyās tu saṃjajñe śibir auśīnaro nṛpaḥ ।।
navasya navarāṣṭraṃ tu kṛmes tu kṛmilā purī ।। śibes tu śibayaḥ putrāś catvāro lokaviśrutāḥ ।। teṣāṃ janapadāḥ sphītā kekayā madrakās tathā ।। titikṣur abhavad rājā pūrvasyāṃ diśi bho dvijāḥ ।।
phenasya sutapā jajñe tataḥ sutapaso baliḥ ।। mahāyogī sa tu balir babhūva nṛpatiḥ purā ।। aṅgaḥ prathamato jajñe vaṅgaḥ suhmas tathaiva ca ।। bāleyā brāhmaṇāś caiva tasya vaṃśakarā bhuvi ।।
mahāyogitvam āyuś ca kalpasya parimāṇataḥ ।। saṃgrāme cāpy ajeyatvaṃ dharme caiva pradhānatām ।। caturo niyatān varṇāṃs tvaṃ ca sthāpayiteti ca ।। kālena mahatā viprāḥ svaṃ ca sthānam upāgamat ।।
kaliṅgāḥ puṇḍrakāś caiva prajās tv aṅgasya sāṃpratam ।। dadhivāhanaputras tu rājā diviratho abhavat ।। vidvān dharmaratho nāma tasya citrarathaḥ sutaḥ ।। yajatā saha śakreṇa somaḥ pīto mahātmanā ।।
lomapāda iti khyāto yasya śāntā sutābhavat ।। ṛṣyaśṛṅgaprasādena jajñe vaṃśavivardhanaḥ ।। pṛthulākṣasuto rājā campo nāma mahāyaśāḥ ।। pūrṇabhadraprasādena haryaṅgo asya suto abhavat ।।
avatārayām āsa mahīṃ mantrair vāhanam uttamam ।। putro bhadrarathasyāsīd bṛhatkarmā prajeśvaraḥ ।। bṛhanmanās tu rājendro janayām āsa vai sutam ।। āsīd dṛḍharathasyāpi viśvajij janamejayī ।।
tasya putraśataṃ tv āsīd aṅgānāṃ kulavardhanam ।। satyavratā mahātmānaḥ prajāvanto mahārathāḥ ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi vaṃśaṃ rājñas tu bho dvijāḥ ।। matinārasutās tv āsaṃs trayaḥ paramadhārmikāḥ ।।
sarve vedavidaś caiva brahmaṇyāḥ satyavādinaḥ ।। brahmavādiny adhistrī sā taṃsus tām abhyagacchata ।। brahmavādī parākrāntas tasya bhāryopadānavī ।। duṣyantam atha suṣmantaṃ pravīram anaghaṃ tathā ।।
sa sarvadamano nāma nāgāyutabalo mahān ।। śakuntalāyāṃ bharato yasya nāmnā tu bhāratāḥ ।। mātṝṇāṃ tu prakopeṇa mayā tat kathitaṃ purā ।। ayājayad bharadvājo mahadbhiḥ kratubhir vibhuḥ ।।
tato atha vitatho nāma bharadvājāt suto abhavat ।। vitathaṃ cābhiṣicyātha bharadvājo vanaṃ yayau ।। suhotraṃ ca suhotāraṃ gayaṃ gargaṃ tathaiva ca ।। kāśikaṃ ca mahāsatyaṃ tathā gṛtsamatiṃ nṛpam ।।
kāśikasya tu kāśeyaḥ putro dīrghatapās tathā ।। dhanvantares tu tanayaḥ ketumān iti viśrutaḥ ।। putro bhīmarathasyāpi vārāṇasyadhipo abhavat ।। divodāsasya putras tu vīro rājā pratardanaḥ ।।
alarko rājaputras tu rājā sanmatimān bhuvi ।। ājahre pitṛdāyādyaṃ divodāsahṛtaṃ balāt ।। divodāsena bāleti ghṛṇayāsau visarjitaḥ ।। tena putreṇa bālasya prahṛtaṃ tasya bho dvijāḥ ।।
alarkaḥ kāśirājas tu brahmaṇyaḥ satyasaṃgaraḥ ।। yuvā rūpeṇa saṃpanna āsīt kāśikulodvahaḥ ।। vayaso ante muniśreṣṭhā hatvā kṣemakarākṣasam ।। alarkasya tu dāyādaḥ kṣemako nāma pārthivaḥ ।।
varṣaketoś ca dāyādo vibhur nāma prajeśvaraḥ ।। sukumārasya putras tu satyaketur mahārathaḥ ।। vatsasya vatsabhūmis tu bhargabhūmis tu bhārgavāt ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca munisattamāḥ ।।
suhotrasya bṛhat putro bṛhatas tanayās trayaḥ ।। ajamīḍhasya patnyas tu tisro vai yaśasānvitāḥ ।। ajamīḍhasya keśinyāṃ jajñe jahnuḥ pratāpavān ।। patilobhena yaṃ gaṅgā vinīteva sasāra ha ।।
tat tayā plāvitaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñavāṭaṃ samantataḥ ।। asya gaṅge avalepasya sadyaḥ phalam avāpnuhi ।। upaninyur mahābhāgā duhitṛtvena jāhnavīm ।। gaṅgāśāpena dehārdhaṃ yasyāḥ paścān nadīkṛtam ।।
ajakasya tu dāyādo balākāśvo mahīpatiḥ ।। pahnavaiḥ saha saṃvṛddho rājā vanacaraiḥ saha ।। labheyam iti taṃ śakras trāsād abhyetya jajñivān ।। viśvāmitras tu gādheyo viśvāmitrāt tathāṣṭakaḥ ।।
ājamīḍho aparo vaṃśaḥ śrūyatāṃ munisattamāḥ ।। purujātiḥ suśānteś ca bāhyāśvaḥ purujātitaḥ ।। mudgalaḥ sṛñjayaś caiva rājā bṛhadiṣus tadā ।। pañcaite rakṣaṇāyālaṃ deśānām iti viśrutāḥ ।।
alaṃ saṃrakṣaṇe teṣāṃ pañcālā iti viśrutāḥ ।। indrasenā yato garbhaṃ vadhnyaṃ ca pratyapadyata ।। sutaḥ pañcajanasyāpi somadatto mahīpatiḥ ।। sahadevasutaś cāpi somako nāma viśrutaḥ ।।
somakasya suto jantur yasya putraśataṃ babhau ।। ājamīḍhāḥ smṛtāś caite mahātmānas tu somakāḥ ।। pativratā mahābhāgā kulajā munisattamāḥ ।। tato varṣāyutaṃ taptvā tapaḥ paramaduścaram ।।
agnihotrakuśeṣv eva suṣvāpa munisattamāḥ ।। ṛkṣaṃ saṃjanayām āsa dhūmravarṇaṃ sudarśanam ।। yaḥ prayāgād atikramya kurukṣetraṃ cakāra ha ।। tasyānvavāyaḥ sumahān yasya nāmnātha kauravāḥ ।।
parīkṣic ca mahābāhuḥ pravaraś cārimejayaḥ ।। śrutaseno agrasenaś ca bhīmasenaś ca nāmataḥ ।। janamejayasya putras tu suratho matimāṃs tathā ।। vidūrathasya dāyāda ṛkṣa eva mahārathaḥ ।।
dvāv ṛkṣau somavaṃśe asmin dvāv eva ca parīkṣitau ।। ṛkṣasya tu dvitīyasya bhīmaseno abhavat sutaḥ ।। devāpir bāhlikaś caiva traya eva mahārathāḥ ।। bāhlikasya tu rājarṣer vaṃśaṃ śṛṇuta bho dvijāḥ ।।
jajñire somadattāt tu bhūrir bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ ।। cyavanaputraḥ kṛtaka iṣṭa āsīn mahātmanaḥ ।। śāṃtanoḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi vaṃśaṃ trailokyaviśrutam ।। sa tu bhīṣma iti khyātaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ pitāmahaḥ ।।
śāṃtanor dayitaṃ putraṃ dharmātmānam akalmaṣam ।। dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca pāṇḍuṃ ca viduraṃ cāpy ajījanat ।। teṣāṃ duryodhanaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarveṣām api sa prabhuḥ ।। abhimanyoḥ parīkṣit tu pitā pārīkṣitasya ha ।।
candrāpīḍas tu nṛpatiḥ sūryāpīḍaś ca mokṣavit ।। jānamejayam ity evaṃ kṣātraṃ bhuvi pariśrutam ।। satyakarṇo mahābāhur yajvā vipuladakṣiṇaḥ ।। aputraḥ sa tu dharmātmā praviveśa tapovanam ।।
sucāror duhitā subhrūr mālinī grāhamālinī ।। anvagacchat kṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ mahāprasthānam acyutam ।। sucāror duhitā sādhvī vane rājīvalocanā ।। tam apāsyātha tatraiva rājānaṃ sānvagacchata ।।
kumāraḥ sukumāro asau giripṛṣṭhe ruroda ha ।। śraviṣṭhāyās tu putrau dvau paippalādiś ca kauśikaḥ ।। nighṛṣṭau tasya pārśvau tu śilāyāṃ rudhiraplutau ।। ajaśyāmau tu tatpārśvau devena saṃbabhūvatuḥ ।।
sa tu remakaśālāyāṃ dvijābhyām abhivardhitaḥ ।। rematyāḥ sa tu putro abhūd brāhmaṇau sacivau tu tau ।। sa eṣa pauravo vaṃśaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām ।। jarāsaṃkramaṇe pūrvaṃ tadā prītena dhīmatā ।।
apauravā mahī naiva bhaviṣyati kadācana ।। turvasos tu pravakṣyāmi druhyoś cānor yados tathā ।। gobhānos tu suto rājā aiśānur aparājitaḥ ।। anyas tv āvikṣito rājā maruttaḥ kathito mayā ।।
duhitā saṃyatā nāma tasyāsīt pṛthivīpateḥ ।। duṣyantaṃ pauravaṃ cāpi lebhe putram akalmaṣam ।। pauravaṃ turvasor vaṃśaṃ praviveśa dvijottamāḥ ।। karūromād athāhrīdaś catvāras tasya cātmajāḥ ।।
druhyoś ca tanayo rājan babhrusetuś ca pārthivaḥ ।। yauvanāśvena samare kṛcchreṇa nihato balī ।। aṅgārasetor dāyādo gāndhāro nāma pārthivaḥ ।। gāndhāradeśajāś caiva turagā vājināṃ varāḥ ।।
dyūtād vanaduho jajñe pracetās tasya cātmajaḥ ।। babhūvus tu yadoḥ putrāḥ pañca devasutopamāḥ ।। sahasrādasya dāyādās trayaḥ paramadhārmikāḥ ।। haihayasyābhavat putro dharmanetra iti śrutaḥ ।।
sāhañjanī nāma purī tena rājñā niveśitā ।। bhadraśreṇyasya dāyādo durdamo nāma viśrutaḥ ।। kanakasya tu dāyādāś catvāro lokaviśrutāḥ ।। kṛtāgnis tu caturtho abhūt kṛtavīryād athārjunaḥ ।।
jigāya pṛthivīm eko rathenādityavarcasā ।। dattam ārādhayām āsa kārtavīryo atrisaṃbhavam ।। pūrvaṃ bāhusahasraṃ tu prārthitaṃ sumahad varam ।। ugreṇa pṛthivīṃ jitvā dharmeṇaivānurañjanam ।।
saṃgrāme vartamānasya vadhaṃ cābhyadhikād raṇe ।। yogād yogīśvarasyeva prādurbhavati māyayā ।। sasamudrā sanagarā ugreṇa vidhinā jitā ।। prāptāni vidhinā rājñā śrūyante munisattamāḥ ।।
sarve kāñcanayūpāś ca sarve kāñcanavedayaḥ ।। gandharvair apsarobhiś ca nityam evopaśobhitāḥ ।। varīdāsātmajo vidvān mahimnā tasya vismitaḥ ।। yajñair dānais tapobhiś ca vikrameṇa śrutena ca ।।
rathī dvīpān anucaran yogī saṃdṛśyate nṛbhiḥ ।। prabhāveṇa mahārājñaḥ prajā dharmeṇa rakṣataḥ ।। sa eva paśupālo abhūt kṣetrapālaḥ sa eva ca ।। sa vai bāhusahasreṇa jyāghātakaṭhinatvacā ।।
sa hi nāgān manuṣyeṣu māhiṣmatyāṃ mahādyutiḥ ।। sa vai vegaṃ samudrasya prāvṛṭkāle ambujekṣaṇaḥ ।। luṇṭhitā krīḍatā tena nadī tadgrāmamālinī ।। tasya bāhusahasreṇa kṣipyamāṇe mahodadhau ।।
cūrṇīkṛtamahāvīciṃ calanmīnamahātimim ।। prāvartayat tadā rājā sahasreṇa ca bāhunā ।। mandarakṣobhacakitā amṛtotpādaśaṅkitāḥ ।। natā niścalamūrdhāno babhūvus te mahoragāḥ ।।
sa vai baddhvā dhanur jyābhir utsiktaṃ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ ।। nirjitya vaśam ānīya māhiṣmatyāṃ babandha tam ।। tato gatvā pulastyas tam arjunaṃ dadṛśe svayam ।। yasya bāhusahasrasya babhūva jyātalasvanaḥ ।।
aho bata mṛdhe vīryaṃ bhārgavasya yad acchinat ।। tṛṣitena kadācit sa bhikṣitaś citrabhānunā ।। purāṇi grāmaghoṣāṃś ca viṣayāṃś caiva sarvaśaḥ ।। sa tasya puruṣendrasya prabhāveṇa mahātmanaḥ ।।
sa śūnyam āśramaṃ ramyaṃ varuṇasyātmajasya vai ।। yaṃ lebhe varuṇaḥ putraṃ purā bhāsvantam uttamam ।। yatrāpavas tu taṃ krodhāc chaptavān arjunaṃ vibhuḥ ।। tasmāt te duṣkaraṃ karma kṛtam anyo haniṣyati ।।
chittvā bāhusahasraṃ te pramathya tarasā balī ।। anaṣṭadravyatā yasya babhūvāmitrakarṣiṇaḥ ।। prāptas tato asya mṛtyur vai tasya śāpān mahāmuneḥ ।। tasya putraśataṃ tv āsīt pañca śeṣā mahātmanaḥ ।।
śūrasenaś ca śūraś ca vṛṣaṇo madhupadhvajaḥ ।। kārtavīryasya tanayā vīryavanto mahābalāḥ ।। tasya putraśataṃ khyātās tālajaṅghā iti smṛtāḥ ।। vītihotrāḥ sujātāś ca bhojāś cāvantayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
bharatāś ca sujātāś ca bahutvān nānukīrtitāḥ ।। vṛṣo vaṃśadharas tatra tasya putro abhavan madhuḥ ।। vṛṣaṇād vṛṣṇayaḥ sarve madhos tu mādhavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। na tasya vittanāśaḥ syān naṣṭaṃ prati labhec ca saḥ ।।
ete yayātiputrāṇāṃ pañca vaṃśā dvijottamāḥ ।। bhūtānīva muniśreṣṭhāḥ pañca sthāvarajaṅgamān ।। vaśī bhavati pañcānām ātmajānāṃ tatheśvaraḥ ।। āyuḥ kīrtiṃ tathā putrān aiśvaryaṃ bhūtim eva ca ।।
kroṣṭor vaṃśaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ gadato mama ।। yasyānvavāyajo viṣṇur harir vṛṣṇikulodvahaḥ ।। gāndhārī janayām āsa anamitraṃ mahābalam ।। teṣāṃ vaṃśas tridhā bhūto vṛṣṇīnāṃ kulavardhanaḥ ।।
jajñāte tanayau vṛṣṇeḥ śvaphalkaś citrakas tathā ।। nāsti vyādhibhayaṃ tatra nāvarṣas tapam eva ca ।। trīṇi varṣāṇi pūrṇāni nāvarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ ।। śvaphalkaparivartena vavarṣa harivāhanaḥ ।।
gāndinīṃ nāma gāṃ sā ca dadau viprāya nityaśaḥ ।। akrūraḥ suṣuve tasmāc chvaphalkād bhūridakṣiṇaḥ ।। avikṣitas tathākṣepaḥ śatrughnaś cārimardanaḥ ।। āvāhaprativāhau ca sundarī ca varāṅganā ।।
prasenaś copadevaś ca jajñāte devavarcasau ।। aśvagrīvo aśvabāhuś ca svapārśvakagaveṣaṇau ।। subāhur bahubāhuś ca śraviṣṭhāśravaṇe striyau ।। mahiṣyāṃ jajñire śūrā bhojyāyāṃ puruṣā daśa ।।
jajñe yasya prasūtasya dundubhyaḥ prāṇadan divi ।। papāta puṣpavarṣaś ca śūrasya janane mahān ।। yasyāsīt puruṣāgryasya kāntiś candramaso yathā ।। anādhṛṣṭiḥ kanavako vatsavān atha gṛñjamaḥ ।।
pṛthukīrtiḥ pṛthā caiva śrutadevā śrutaśravā ।। śrutaśravāyāṃ caidyas tu śiśupālo abhavan nṛpaḥ ।। pṛthukīrtyāṃ tu saṃjajñe tanayo vṛddhaśarmaṇaḥ ।। pṛthāṃ duhitaraṃ cakre kuntis tāṃ pāṇḍur āvahat ।।
bhīmasenas tathā vātād indrāc caiva dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। anamitrāc chanir jajñe kaniṣṭhād vṛṣṇinandanāt ।। uddhavo devabhāgasya mahābhāgaḥ suto abhavat ।। aśmakyaṃ prāptavān putram anādhṛṣṭir yaśasvinam ।।
śrutadevātmajās te tu naiṣādir yaḥ pariśrutaḥ ।। adbhir dadau sutaṃ vīraṃ śauriḥ kauśikam aurasam ।। cārudeṣṇaṃ sudeṣṇaṃ ca pañcālaṃ kṛtalakṣaṇam ।। raukmiṇeyo mahābāhuḥ kanīyān dvijasattamāḥ ।।
cārūn adyopabhokṣyāmaś cārudeṣṇahatān iti ।। vīruś cāśvahanuś caiva vīrau tāv atha gṛñjimau ।। jugupsamāno bhojatvād rājasūyam avāpa saḥ ।। vasudevasutān vīrān kīrtayiṣyāmy ataḥ param ।।
dhārayan vipulaṃ vaṃśaṃ nānarthair iha yujyate ।। pauravī rohiṇī nāma madirāditathāvarā ।। sahadevā śāntidevā śrīdevī devarakṣitā ।। sutanur vaḍavā caiva dve ete paricārike ।।
jyeṣṭhā patnī muniśreṣṭhā dayitānakadundubheḥ ।। durdamaṃ damanaṃ śubhraṃ piṇḍārakam uśīnaram ।। citrā subhadreti punar vikhyātā munisattamāḥ ।। rāmāc ca niśaṭho jajñe revatyāṃ dayitaḥ sutaḥ ।।
akrūrāt kāśikanyāyāṃ satyaketur ajāyata ।। ye putrā jajñire śūrāḥ samastāṃs tān nibodhata ।। vṛkadevaḥ sunāmāyāṃ gadaś cāstāṃ sutāv ubhau ।। kanyā trigartarājasya bhāryā vai śiśirāyaṇeḥ ।।
kṛṣṇāyasasamaprakhyo varṣe dvādaśame tathā ।। ghoṣakanyām upādāya maithunāyopacakrame ।। dhārayām āsa gārgyasya garbhaṃ durdharam acyutam ।। sa kālayavano nāma jajñe rājā mahābalaḥ ।।
aputrasya sa rājñas tu vavṛdhe antaḥpure śiśuḥ ।। āyudhyamāno nṛpatiḥ paryapṛcchad dvijottamam ।। akṣauhiṇyā tu sainyasya mathurām abhyayāt tadā ।। tato vṛṣṇyandhakāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ puraskṛtya mahāmatim ।।
kṛtvā viniścayaṃ sarve palāyanam arocayan ।। kuśasthalīṃ dvāravatīṃ niveśayitum īpsavaḥ ।। parvasu śrāvayed vidvān anṛṇaḥ sa sukhī bhavet ।। vārjinīvatam icchanti svāhiṃ svāhākṛtāṃ varam ।।
mahākratubhir īje yo vividhair bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ ।। jajñe citrarathas tasya putraḥ karmabhir anvitaḥ ।। śaśabinduḥ paraṃ vṛttaṃ rājarṣīṇām anuṣṭhitaḥ ।। śaṃsanti ca purāṇajñāḥ pārthaśravasam antaram ।।
uṣato yajñam akhilaṃ svadharme ca kṛtādaraḥ ।। marutas tasya tanayo rājarṣir abhavan nṛpaḥ ।। cacāra vipulaṃ dharmam amarṣāt pratyabhāg api ।। babhūva rukmakavacaḥ śataprasavataḥ sutaḥ ।।
dhanvināṃ niśitair bāṇair avāpa śriyam uttamām ।। jajñire pañca putrās tu mahāvīryāḥ parājitāḥ ।। pālitaṃ ca hariṃ caiva videhebhyaḥ pitā dadau ।। tābhyāṃ pravrājito rājā jyāmagho avasad āśrame ।।
jagāma dhanur ādāya deśam anyaṃ dhvajī rathī ।। ṛkṣavantaṃ giriṃ jitvā śuktimatyām uvāsa saḥ ।। aputro api sa rājā vai nānyāṃ bhāryām avindata ।। bhāryām uvāca saṃtrastaḥ snuṣeti sa janeśvaraḥ ।।
abravīt tad upaśrutya jyāmagho rājasattamaḥ ।। yas te janiṣyate putras tasya bhāryopapāditā ।। putraṃ vidarbhaṃ subhāgā śaibyā pariṇatā satī ।। paścād vidarbho ajanayac chūrau raṇaviśāradau ।।
kunter dhṛṣṭaḥ suto jajñe raṇadhṛṣṭaḥ pratāpavān ।। āvantaś ca daśārhaś ca balī viṣaharaś ca saḥ ।। jīmūtaputro vikṛtis tasya bhīmarathaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tasya cāsīd daśarathaḥ śakunis tasya cātmajaḥ ।।
devakṣatro abhavat tasya vṛddhakṣatro mahāyaśāḥ ।। madhūnāṃ vaṃśakṛd rājā madhur madhuravāg api ।। aikṣvākī cābhavad bhāryā madhos tasyāṃ vyajāyata ।। yujyate paramaprītyā prajāvāṃś ca bhavet sadā ।।
bhāginaṃ bhajamānaṃ ca divyaṃ devāvṛdhaṃ nṛpam ।। teṣāṃ visargāś catvāro vistareṇeha kīrtitāḥ ।। āstāṃ bhārye tayos tasmāj jajñire bahavaḥ sutāḥ ।। ete bāhyakasṛñjayyāṃ bhajamānād vijajñire ।।
upabāhyakasṛñjayyāṃ bhajamānād vijajñire ।। putraḥ sarvaguṇopeto mama syād iti niścitaḥ ।। sadopaspṛśatas tasya cakāra priyam āpagā ।। kalyāṇatvān narapates tasya sā nimnagottamā ।।
bhavet tasmāt svayaṃ gatvā bhavāmy asya sahānugā ।। varayām āsa nṛpatiṃ tām iyeṣa ca sa prabhuḥ ।। atha sā daśame māsi suṣuve saritāṃ varā ।। atra vaṃśe purāṇajñā gāyantīti pariśrutam ।।
yathaivāgre tathā dūrāt paśyāmas tāvad antikāt ।। ṣaṣṭiś ca ṣaṭ ca puruṣāḥ sahasrāṇi ca sapta ca ।। yajvā dānapatir dhīmān brahmaṇyaḥ sudṛḍhāyudhaḥ ।। andhakāt kāśyaduhitā caturo alabhatātmajān ।।
kukurasya suto vṛṣṭir vṛṣṭes tu tanayas tathā ।। jajñe punar vasus tasmād abhijic ca punar vasoḥ ।। āhukaḥ śrāhukaś caiva khyātau khyātimatāṃ varau ।। śvetena parivāreṇa kiśorapratimo mahān ।।
nāputravān nāśatado nāsahasraśatāyuṣaḥ ।। pūrvasyāṃ diśi nāgānāṃ bhojasya prayayuḥ kila ।। rathānāṃ meghaghoṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi daśaiva tu ।। tāvaty eva sahasrāṇi uttarasyāṃ tathā diśi ।।
āhuḥ kiṃ cāpy avantibhyaḥ svasāraṃ dadur andhakāḥ ।। devakaś cograsenaś ca devagarbhasamāv ubhau ।। devavān upadevaś ca saṃdevo devarakṣitaḥ ।। devakī śāntidevā ca sudevā devarakṣitā ।।
navograsenasya sutās teṣāṃ kaṃsas tu pūrvajaḥ ।। rāṣṭrapālo atha sutanur anāvṛṣṭis tu puṣṭimān ।। sutanū rāṣṭrapālī ca kaṅkā caiva varāṅganā ।। kukurāṇām imaṃ vaṃśaṃ dhārayann amitaujasām ।।
ātmano vipulaṃ vaṃśaṃ prajāvān āpnuyān naraḥ ।। rājādhidevaḥ śūras tu vidūrathasuto abhavat ।। dattātidattau balinau śoṇāśvaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ ।। śravaṇā ca śraviṣṭhā ca svasārau saṃbabhūvatuḥ ।।
svayaṃbhojaḥ svayaṃbhojād bhadikaḥ saṃbabhūva ha ।। kṛtavarmāgrajas teṣāṃ śatadhanvā tu madhyamaḥ ।। sudāntaś cātidāntaś ca nikāśyaḥ kāmadambhakaḥ ।। asamaujāḥ sutas tasya nāsamaujāś ca tāv ubhau ।।
sudaṃṣṭraś ca sucāruś ca kṛṣṇa ity andhakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। gāndhārī janayām āsa anamitraṃ mahābalam ।। anamitram amitrāṇāṃ jetāram aparājitam ।। prasenaś cātha satrājic chatrusenājitāv ubhau ।।
divyaṃ syamantakaṃ nāma sa sūryād upalabdhavān ।। sa kadācin niśāpāye rathena rathināṃ varaḥ ।। tasyopatiṣṭhataḥ sūryaṃ vivasvān agrataḥ sthitaḥ ।। atha rājā vivasvantam uvāca sthitam agrataḥ ।।
tejomaṇḍalinaṃ devaṃ tathaiva purataḥ sthitam ।। etac chrutvā tu bhagavān maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam ।। tato vigrahavantaṃ taṃ dadarśa nṛpatis tadā ।। tam abhiprasthitaṃ bhūyo vivasvantaṃ sa satrajit ।।
tad etan maṇiratnaṃ me bhagavan dātum arhasi ।। sa tam ābadhya nagarīṃ praviveśa mahīpatiḥ ।। svāṃ purīṃ sa visiṣmāya rājā tv antaḥpuraṃ tathā ।। dadau bhrātre narapatiḥ premṇā satrājid uttamam ।।
kālavarṣī ca parjanyo na ca vyādhibhayaṃ hy abhūt ।। govindo na ca taṃ lebhe śakto api na jahāra saḥ ।। syamantakakṛte siṃhād vadhaṃ prāpa vanecarāt ।। nihatya maṇiratnaṃ tad ādāya prāviśad guhām ।।
prārthanāṃ tāṃ maṇer baddhvā sarva eva śaśaṅkire ।। āhariṣye maṇim iti pratijñāya vanaṃ yayau ।। prasenasya padaṃ gṛhya puruṣair āptakāribhiḥ ।। anveṣayan pariśrāntaḥ sa dadarśa mahāmanāḥ ।।
atha siṃhaḥ prasenasya śarīrasyāvidūrataḥ ।। padais tair anviyāyātha guhām ṛkṣasya mādhavaḥ ।। dhātryā kumāram ādāya sutaṃ jāmbavato dvijāḥ ।। krīḍayantyā ca maṇinā mā rodīr ity atheritām ।।
sukumāraka mā rodīs tava hy eṣa syamantakaḥ ।। praviśya tatra bhagavāṃs tad ṛkṣabilam añjasā ।। śārṅgadhanvā bilasthaṃ tu jāmbavantaṃ dadarśa saḥ ।। bāhubhyām eva govindo divasān ekaviṃśatim ।।
purīṃ dvāravatīm etya hataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ nyavedayan ।। lebhe jāmbavatīṃ kanyām ṛkṣarājasya saṃmatām ।। anunīyarkṣarājaṃ tu niryayau ca tato bilāt ।। evaṃ sa maṇim āhṛtya viśodhyātmānam acyutaḥ ।।
evaṃ mithyābhiśastena kṛṣṇenāmitraghātinā ।। satrājito daśa tv āsan bhāryās tāsāṃ śataṃ sutāḥ ।। vīro vātapatiś caiva vasumedhas tathaiva ca ।। satyabhāmottamā tāsāṃ vratinī ca dṛḍhavratā ।।
sabhākṣo bhaṅgakāris tu nāveyaś ca narottamau ।। mādryāḥ putro atha jajñe atha vṛṣṇiputro yudhājitaḥ ।। śvaphalkaḥ kāśirājasya sutāṃ bhāryām avindata ।। tasyāṃ jajñe mahābāhuḥ śrutavān atithipriyaḥ ।।
upamadgus tathā madgur mudaraś cārimardanaḥ ।। dharmabhṛc cāpi dharmā ca gṛdhrabhojāndhakas tathā ।। viśrutāśvasya mahiṣī kanyā cāsya vasuṃdharā ।। akrūreṇograsenāyāṃ sutau vai kulanandanau ।।
citrakasyābhavan putrāḥ pṛthur vipṛthur eva ca ।। ariṣṭanemiś ca sutā dharmo dharmabhṛd eva ca ।। imāṃ mithyābhiśastiṃ yaḥ kṛṣṇasya samudāhṛtām ।। veda mithyābhiśāpās taṃ na spṛśanti kadācana ।।
dadāv ahārayad babhrur bhojena śatadhanvanā ।। akrūro antaram anviṣyan maṇiṃ caiva syamantakam ।। rātrau taṃ maṇim ādāya tato akrūrāya dattavān ।। samayaṃ kārayāṃ cakre nāvedyo ahaṃ tvayety uta ।।
mamādya dvārakā sarvā vaśe tiṣṭhaty asaṃśayam ।। prayayau ratham āruhya nagaraṃ vāraṇāvatam ।। bhartur nivedya duḥkhārtā pārśvasthāśrūṇy avartayat ।। kulyārthe cāpi pāṇḍūnāṃ nyayojayata sātyakim ।।
pūrvajaṃ halinaṃ śrīmān idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। syamantakas tu madnāmī tasya prabhur ahaṃ vibho ।। syamantako mahābāho asmākaṃ sa bhaviṣyati ।। śatadhanvā tato akrūraṃ sarvatodiśam aikṣata ।।
śakto api śāpād dhārdikyam akrūro nānvapadyata ।। yojanānāṃ śataṃ sāgraṃ hṛdayā pratyapadyata ।। bhojasya vaḍavā viprā yayā kṛṣṇam ayodhayat ।। dṛṣṭvā rathasya svāṃ vṛddhiṃ śatadhanvānam ardayat ।।
kham utpetur atha prāṇāḥ kṛṣṇo rāmam athābravīt ।। padbhyāṃ gatvā hariṣyāmi maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam ।। mithilām abhito viprā jaghāna paramāstravit ।। nivṛttaṃ cābravīt kṛṣṇaṃ maṇiṃ dehīti lāṅgalī ।।
dhikśabdapūrvam asakṛt pratyuvāca janārdanam ।। kṛtyaṃ na me dvārakayā na tvayā na ca vṛṣṇibhiḥ ।। sarvakāmair upahṛtair mithilenābhipūjitaḥ ।। nānārūpān kratūn sarvān ājahāra nirargalān ।।
syamantakakṛte prājño gāndīputro mahāyaśāḥ ।। ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣāṇi dharmātmā yajñeṣv eva nyayojayat ।। bahvannadakṣiṇāḥ sarve sarvakāmapradāyinaḥ ।। gadāśikṣāṃ tato divyāṃ baladevād avāptavān ।।
ānīto dvārakām eva kṛṣṇena ca mahātmanā ।। hatvā satrājitaṃ suptaṃ sahabandhuṃ mahābalaḥ ।। apayāte tadākrūre nāvarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ ।। tataḥ prasādayām āsur akrūraṃ kukurāndhakāḥ ।।
pravavarṣa sahasrākṣaḥ kakṣe jalanidhes tadā ।। akrūraḥ pradadau dhīmān prītyarthaṃ munisattamāḥ ।। sabhāmadhyagataḥ prāha tam akrūraṃ janārdanaḥ ।। tat prayaccha ca mānārha mayi mānāryakaṃ kṛthāḥ ।।
sa saṃrūḍho asakṛt prāptas tataḥ kālātyayo mahān ।। pradadau taṃ maṇiṃ babhrur akleśena mahāmatiḥ ।। dadau hṛṣṭamanāḥ kṛṣṇas taṃ maṇiṃ babhrave punaḥ ।। ābadhya gāndinīputro virarājāṃśumān iva ।।
bhāratānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ pārthivānāṃ tathaiva ca ।। daityānām atha siddhānāṃ guhyakānāṃ tathaiva ca ।। vividhāś ca kathā divyā janma cāgryam anuttamam ।। prajāpatīnāṃ sarveṣāṃ guhyakāpsarasāṃ tathā ।।
tvayā proktaṃ mahābhāga śrutaṃ caitan manoharam ।। manaḥkarṇasukhaṃ samyak prīṇāty amṛtasaṃmitam ।। vaktum arhasi sarvajña paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। vanāni saritaḥ puṇya- devādīnāṃ mahāmate ।।
saṃsthānam asya jagato yathāvad vaktum arhasi ।। nāsya varṣaśatenāpi vaktuṃ śakyo ativistaraḥ ।। kuśaḥ krauñcas tathā śākaḥ puṣkaraś caiva saptamaḥ ।। lavaṇekṣusurāsarpir dadhidugdhajalaiḥ samam ।।
tasyāpi madhye viprendrā meruḥ kanakaparvataḥ ।। praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśādhastād dvātriṃśan mūrdhni vistṛtaḥ ।। bhūpadmasyāsya śailo asau karṇikākārasaṃsthitaḥ ।। nīlaḥ śvetaś ca śṛṅgī ca uttare varṣaparvatāḥ ।।
sahasradvitayocchrāyās tāvadvistāriṇaś ca te ।। harivarṣaṃ tathaivānyan meror dakṣiṇato dvijāḥ ।। uttarāḥ kuravaś caiva yathā vai bhārataṃ tathā ।। ilāvṛtaṃ ca tanmadhye sauvarṇo merur ucchritaḥ ।।
ilāvṛtaṃ mahābhāgāś catvāraś cātra parvatāḥ ।। pūrveṇa mandaro nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ ।। kadambas teṣu jambūś ca pippalo vaṭa eva ca ।। jambūdvīpasya sā jambūr nāmahetur dvijottamāḥ ।।
patanti bhūbhṛtaḥ pṛṣṭhe śīryamāṇāni sarvataḥ ।। sarit pravartate sā ca pīyate tannivāsibhiḥ ।। tatpānasvasthamanasāṃ janānāṃ tatra jāyate ।। jāmbūnadākhyaṃ bhavati suvarṇaṃ siddhabhūṣaṇam ।।
varṣe dve tu muniśreṣṭhās tayor madhye tv ilāvṛtam ।। vaibhrājaṃ paścime tadvad uttare nandanaṃ smṛtam ।। sarāṃsy etāni catvāri devabhogyāni sarvadā ।। vaikaṅkapramukhā meroḥ pūrvataḥ kesarācalāḥ ।।
niṣadhādayo dakṣiṇatas tasya kesaraparvatāḥ ।। jānudhipramukhās tadvat paścime kesarācalāḥ ।। śaṅkhakūṭo atha ṛṣabho haṃso nāgas tathāparāḥ ।। caturdaśa sahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ mahāpurī ।।
tasyāṃ samantataś cāṣṭau diśāsu vidiśāsu ca ।। viṣṇupādaviniṣkrāntā plāvayantīndumaṇḍalam ।। sā tatra patitā dikṣu caturdhā pratyapadyata ।। pūrveṇa sītā śailāc ca śailaṃ yānty antarikṣagā ।।
tathaivālakanandā ca dakṣiṇenaitya bhāratam ।। cakṣuś ca paścimagirīn atītya sakalāṃs tataḥ ।। bhadrā tathottaragirīn uttarāṃś ca tathā kurūn ।। ānīlaniṣadhāyāmau mālyavadgandhamādanau ।।
bhāratāḥ ketumālāś ca bhadrāśvāḥ kuravas tathā ।। jaṭharo devakūṭaś ca maryādāparvatāv ubhau ।। gandhamādanakailāsau pūrvapaścāt tu tāv ubhau ।। niṣadhaḥ pāriyātraś ca maryādāparvatāv ubhau ।।
meroḥ paścimadigbhāge yathā pūrvau tathā sthitau ।। pūrvapaścāyatāv etāv arṇavāntarvyavasthitau ।। jaṭharāvasthitā meror yeṣāṃ dvau dvau caturdiśam ।। śītāntādyā dvijās teṣām atīva hi manoharāḥ ।।
suramyāṇi tathā tāsu kānanāni purāṇi ca ।। tāsv āyatanavaryāṇi juṣṭāni narakiṃnaraiḥ ।। krīḍanti tāsu ramyāsu śailadroṇīṣv aharniśam ।। naiteṣu pāpakartāro yānti janmaśatair api ।।
vārāhaḥ ketumāle tu bhārate kūrmarūpadhṛk ।। viśvarūpeṇa sarvatra sarvaḥ sarveśvaro hariḥ ।। yāni kiṃpuruṣādyāni varṣāṇy aṣṭau dvijottamāḥ ।। susthāḥ prajā nirātaṅkāḥ sarvaduḥkhavivarjitāḥ ।।
naiteṣu bhaumāny anyāni kṣutpipāsādi no dvijāḥ ।। nadyaś ca śataśas tebhyaḥ prasūtā yā dvijottamāḥ ।। varṣaṃ tad bhārataṃ nāma bhāratī yatra saṃtatiḥ ।। karmabhūmir iyaṃ svargam apavargaṃ ca pṛcchatām ।।
vindhyaś ca pāriyātraś ca saptātra kulaparvatāḥ ।। tiryaktvaṃ narakaṃ cāpi yānty ataḥ puruṣā dvijāḥ ।। na khalv anyatra martyānāṃ karma bhūmau vidhīyate ।। indradvīpaḥ kasetumāṃs tāmraparṇo gabhastimān ।।
ayaṃ tu navamas teṣāṃ dvīpaḥ sāgarasaṃvṛtaḥ ।। pūrve kirātās tiṣṭhanti paścime yavanāḥ sthitāḥ ।। ijyāyuddhavaṇijyādya- vṛttimanto vyavasthitāḥ ।। vedasmṛtimukhāś cānyāḥ pāriyātrodbhavā mune ।।
tāpīpayoṣṇīnirvindhyā- kāverīpramukhā nadīḥ ।। godāvarībhīmarathī- kṛṣṇaveṇyādikās tathā ।। kṛtamālātāmraparṇī- pramukhā malayodbhavāḥ ।। ṛṣikulyākumārādyāḥ śuktimatpādasaṃbhavāḥ ।।
tāsv ime kurupañcāla- madhyadeśādayo janāḥ ।। pauṇḍrāḥ kaliṅgā magadhā dākṣiṇātyāś ca sarvaśaḥ ।। mārukā mālavāś caiva pāriyātranivāsinaḥ ।। madrārāmās tathāmbaṣṭhāḥ pārasīkādayas tathā ।।
samopetā mahābhāga hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulāḥ ।। kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca kaliś cānyatra na kvacit ।। dānāni cātra dīyante paralokārtham ādarāt ।। yajñair yajñamayo viṣṇur anyadvīpeṣu cānyathā ।।
yato hi karmabhūr eṣā yato anyā bhogabhūmayaḥ ।। kadācil labhate jantur mānuṣyaṃ puṇyasaṃcayan ।। lakṣayojanavistāraṃ saṃkṣepāt kathitaṃ dvijāḥ ।। bho dvijā valayākāraḥ sthitaḥ kṣīrodadhir bahiḥ ।।
saṃveṣṭya kṣāram udadhiṃ plakṣadvīpas tathā sthitaḥ ।। sa eva dviguṇo viprāḥ plakṣadvīpe apy udāhṛtaḥ ।। śreṣṭhaḥ śāntabhayo nāma śiśiras tadanantaram ।। dhruvaś ca saptamas teṣāṃ plakṣadvīpeśvarā hi te ।।
ānandaṃ ca śivaṃ caiva kṣemakaṃ dhruvam eva ca ।। saptaiva teṣāṃ nāmāni śṛṇudhvaṃ munisattamāḥ ।। somakaḥ sumanāḥ śailo vaibhrājaś caiva saptamaḥ ।। vasanti devagandharva- sahitāḥ sahitaṃ prajāḥ ।।
nādhayo vyādhayo vāpi sarvakālasukhaṃ hi tat ।। nāmatas tāḥ pravakṣyāmi śrutāḥ pāpaṃ haranti yāḥ ।। amṛtā sukṛtā caiva saptaitās tatra nimnagāḥ ।। kṣudranadyas tathā śailās tatra santi sahasraśaḥ ।।
avasarpiṇī nadī teṣāṃ na caivotsarpiṇī dvijāḥ ।। tretāyugasamaḥ kālaḥ sarvadaiva dvijottamāḥ ।। pañcavarṣasahasrāṇi janā jīvanty anāmayāḥ ।। varṇāś ca tatra catvāras tān budhāḥ pravadāmi vaḥ ।।
viprakṣatriyavaiśyās te śūdrāś ca munisattamāḥ ।। plakṣas tannāmasaṃjño ayaṃ plakṣadvīpo dvijottamāḥ ।। somarūpī jagatsraṣṭā sarvaḥ sarveśvaro hariḥ ।। tathaivekṣurasodena pariveṣānukāriṇā ।।
saṃkṣepeṇa mayā bhūyaḥ śālmalaṃ taṃ nibodhata ।। teṣāṃ tu nāma saṃjñāni saptavarṣāṇi tāni vai ।। vaidyuto mānasaś caiva suprabhaś ca dvijottamāḥ ।। vistārād dviguṇenātha sarvataḥ saṃvṛtaḥ sthitaḥ ।।
varṣābhivyañjakās te tu tathā saptaiva nimnagāḥ ।। droṇo yatra mahauṣadhyaḥ sa caturtho mahīdharaḥ ।। kakudmān parvatavaraḥ sarinnāmāny ato dvijāḥ ।। nivṛttiḥ saptamī tāsāṃ smṛtās tāḥ pāpaśāntidāḥ ।।
vaidyutaṃ mānasaṃ caiva suprabhaṃ nāma saptamam ।। varṇāś ca śālmale ye ca vasanty eṣu dvijottamāḥ ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś caiva yajanti tam ।। vāyubhūtaṃ makhaśreṣṭhair yajvāno yajñasaṃsthitam ।।
śālmaliś ca mahāvṛkṣo nāmanirvṛttikārakaḥ ।। vistārāc chālmaleś caiva samena tu samantataḥ ।। śālmalasya tu vistārād dviguṇena samantataḥ ।। udbhido veṇumāṃś caiva svairatho randhano dhṛtiḥ ।।
tasyāṃ vasanti manujaiḥ saha daiteyadānavāḥ ।। varṇās tatrāpi catvāro nijānuṣṭhānatatparāḥ ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś cānukramoditāḥ ।। tatra te tu kuśadvīpe brahmarūpaṃ janārdanam ।।
vidrumo hemaśailaś ca dyutimān puṣṭimāṃs tathā ।। varṣācalās tu saptaite dvīpe tatra dvijottamāḥ ।। dhūtapāpā śivā caiva pavitrā saṃmatis tathā ।। anyāḥ sahasraśas tatra kṣudranadyas tathācalāḥ ।।
tatpramāṇena sa dvīpo ghṛtodena samāvṛtaḥ ।। krauñcadvīpo muniśreṣṭhāḥ śrūyatāṃ cāparo mahān ।। krauñcadvīpe dyutimataḥ putrāḥ sapta mahātmanaḥ ।। kuśago mandagaś coṣṇaḥ pīvaro athāndhakārakaḥ ।।
tatrāpi devagandharva- sevitāḥ sumanoramāḥ ।। krauñcaś ca vāmanaś caiva tṛtīyaś cāndhakārakaḥ ।। dundubhiś ca mahāśailo dviguṇās te parasparam ।। varṣeṣv eteṣu ramyeṣu varṣaśailavareṣu ca ।।
puṣkalā puṣkarā dhanyās te khyātāś ca dvijottamāḥ ।। tatra nadyo muniśreṣṭhā yāḥ pibanti tu te sadā ।। gaurī kumudvatī caiva saṃdhyā rātrir manojavā ।। tatrāpi varṇair bhagavān puṣkarādyair janārdanaḥ ।।
krauñcadvīpaḥ samudreṇa dadhimaṇḍodakena tu ।। dadhimaṇḍodakaś cāpi śākadvīpena saṃvṛtaḥ ।। śākadvīpeśvarasyāpi bhavyasya sumahātmanaḥ ।। jaladaś ca kumāraś ca sukumāro manīrakaḥ ।।
tatsaṃjñāny eva tatrāpi sapta varṣāṇy anukramāt ।। pūrvas tatrodayagirir jaladhāras tathāparaḥ ।। āstikeyas tathā ramyaḥ kesarī parvatottamaḥ ।। yatpattravātasaṃsparśād āhlādo jāyate paraḥ ।।
nivasanti mahātmāno nirātaṅkā nirāmayāḥ ।। sukumārī kumārī ca nalinī reṇukā ca yā ।। anyās tv ayutaśas tatra kṣudranadyo dvijottamāḥ ।। tāḥ pibanti mudā yuktā jaladādiṣu ye sthitāḥ ।।
nadyaś cātra mahāpuṇyāḥ svargād abhyetya medinīm ।। maryādāvyutkramaś cāpi teṣu deśeṣu saptasu ।। magā brāhmaṇabhūyiṣṭhā māgadhāḥ kṣatriyās tu te ।। śākadvīpe sthitair viṣṇuḥ sūryarūpadharo hariḥ ।।
śākadvīpas tato viprāḥ kṣīrodena samantataḥ ।। kṣīrābdhiḥ sarvato viprāḥ puṣkarākhyena veṣṭitaḥ ।। puṣkare savanasyāpi mahāvīto abhavat sutaḥ ।। mahāvītaṃ tathaivānyad dhātakīkhaṇḍasaṃjñitam ।।
mānasottarasaṃjño vai madhyato valayākṛtiḥ ।। tāvad eva ca vistīrṇaḥ sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ ।। sthito asau tena vicchinnaṃ jātaṃ varṣadvayaṃ hi tat ।। daśavarṣasahasrāṇi tatra jīvanti mānavāḥ ।।
adhamottamau na teṣv āstāṃ- na vadhyavadhakau dvijāḥ ।। mahāvītaṃ bahir varṣaṃ dhātakīkhaṇḍam antataḥ ।। satyānṛte na tatrāstāṃ dvīpe puṣkarasaṃjñite ।। tulyaveṣās tu manujā devais tatraikarūpiṇaḥ ।।
trayīvārttādaṇḍanīti- śuśrūṣārahitaṃ ca tat ।। sarvasya sukhadaḥ kālo jarārogavivarjitaḥ ।। nyagrodhaḥ puṣkaradvīpe brahmaṇaḥ sthānam uttamam ।। svādūdakenodadhinā puṣkaraḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ ।।
evaṃ dvīpāḥ samudrais tu sapta saptabhir āvṛtāḥ ।। payāṃsi sarvadā sarva- samudreṣu samāni vai ।। sthālīstham agnisaṃyogād udreki salilaṃ yathā ।। anyūnānatiriktāś ca vardhanty āpo hrasanti ca ।।
daśottarāṇi pañcaiva aṅgulānāṃ śatāni ca ।। bhojanaṃ puṣkaradvīpe tatra svayam upasthitam ।। svādūdakasya parito dṛśyate lokasaṃsthitiḥ ।। lokālokas tataḥ śailo yojanāyutavistṛtaḥ ।।
tatas tamaḥ samāvṛtya taṃ śailaṃ sarvataḥ sthitam ।। pañcāśatkoṭivistārā seyam urvī dvijottamāḥ ।। ādhārabhūtā jagatāṃ sarveṣāṃ sā dvijottamāḥ ।। saptatis tu sahasrāṇi taducchrāyo api kathyate ।।
atalaṃ vitalaṃ caiva nitalaṃ sutalaṃ tathā ।। kṛṣṇā śuklāruṇā pītā śarkarā śailakāñcanī ।। teṣu dānavadaiteya- jātayaḥ śataśaḥ sthitāḥ ।। svarlokād api ramyāṇi pātālānīti nāradaḥ ।।
āhlādakāriṇaḥ śubhrā maṇayo yatra suprabhāḥ ।। daityadānavakanyābhir itaś cetaś ca śobhite ।। divārkaraśmayo yatra prabhās tanvanti nātapam ।। bhakṣyabhojyamahāpāna- madamattaiś ca bhogibhiḥ ।।
vanāni nadyo ramyāṇi sarāṃsi kamalākarāḥ ।। bhūṣaṇāny atiramyāṇi gandhādyaṃ cānulepanam ।। etāny anyāni ramyāṇi bhāgyabhogyāni dānavaiḥ ।। pātālānām adhaś cāste viṣṇor yā tāmasī tanuḥ ।।
yo anantaḥ paṭhyate siddhair devadevarṣipūjitaḥ ।। phaṇāmaṇisahasreṇa yaḥ sa vidyotayan diśaḥ ।। madāghūrṇitanetro asau yaḥ sadaivaikakuṇḍalaḥ ।। nīlavāsā madotsiktaḥ śvetahāropaśobhitaḥ ।।
lāṅgalāsaktahastāgro bibhran muśalam uttamam ।। kalpānte yasya vaktrebhyo viṣānalaśikhojjvalaḥ ।। sa bibhracchikharībhūtam aśeṣaṃ kṣitimaṇḍalam ।। tasya vīryaṃ prabhāvaś ca svarūpaṃ rūpam eva ca ।।
yasyaiṣā sakalā pṛthvī phaṇāmaṇiśikhāruṇā ।। yadā vijṛmbhate ananto madāghūrṇitalocanaḥ ।। gandharvāpsarasaḥ siddhāḥ kiṃnaroragavāraṇāḥ ।। yasya nāgavadhūhastair lāpitaṃ haricandanam ।।
yam ārādhya purāṇarṣir gargo jyotīṃṣi tattvataḥ ।। bibharti sakalāṃl lokān sadevāsuramānuṣān ।। pāpino yeṣu pātyante tāñ śṛṇudhvaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। mahājvālas taptakuḍyo mahālobho vimohanaḥ ।।
asipattravanaṃ kṛṣṇo lālābhakṣaś ca dāruṇaḥ ।। sadaṃśaḥ kṛṣṇasūtraś ca tamaś cāvīcir eva ca ।। ity evamādayaś cānye narakā bhṛśadāruṇāḥ ।। patanti yeṣu puruṣāḥ pāpakarmaratāś ca ye ।।
yaś cānyad anṛtaṃ vakti sa naro yāti rauravam ।। yānti te rauravaṃ ghoraṃ yaś cocchvāsanirodhakaḥ ।। prayāti narake yaś ca taiḥ saṃsargam upaiti vai ।। taptakumbhe svasṛgāmī hanti rājabhaṭaṃ ca yaḥ ।।
taptalohe patanty ete yaś ca bhaktaṃ parityajet ।। avamantā gurūṇāṃ yo yaś cākroṣṭā narādhamaḥ ।। agamyagāmī yaś ca syāt te yānti śabalaṃ dvijāḥ ।। devadvijapitṛdveṣṭā ratnadūṣayitā ca yaḥ ।।
pitṛdevātithīn yas tu paryaśnāti narādhamaḥ ।। karoti karṇino yaś ca yaś ca khaḍgādikṛn naraḥ ।। asatpratigrahītā ca narake yāty adhomukhe ।। kṛmipūye naraś caiko yāti miṣṭānnabhuk sadā ।।
vikretā brāhmaṇo yāti tam eva narakaṃ dvijāḥ ।। poṣayan narakaṃ yāti tam eva dvijasattamāḥ ।। sūcī māhiṣikaś caiva parvagāmī ca yo dvijaḥ ।। rudhirāndhe patanty ete somaṃ vikrīṇate ca ye ।।
retaḥpānādikartāro maryādābhedinaś ca ye ।। asipattravanaṃ yāti vanacchedī vṛthaiva yaḥ ।। yānti tatraiva te viprā yaś cāpākeṣu vahnidaḥ ।। saṃdaṃśayātanāmadhye patatas tāv ubhāv api ।।
putrair adhyāpitā ye tu te patanti śvabhojane ।। yeṣu duṣkṛtakarmāṇaḥ pacyante yātanāgatāḥ ।। bhujyante jātipuruṣair narakāntaragocaraiḥ ।। karmaṇā manasā vācā nirayeṣu patanti te ।।
devāś cādhomukhān sarvān adhaḥ paśyanti nārakān ।। dhārmikās tridaśās tadvan mokṣiṇaś ca yathākramam ।। sarve hy ete mahābhāgā yāvan muktisamāśrayāḥ ।। pāpakṛd yāti narakaṃ prāyaścittaparāṅmukhaḥ ।।
tathā tathaiva saṃsmṛtya proktāni paramarṣibhiḥ ।। prāyaścittāni viprendrā jaguḥ svāyaṃbhuvādayaḥ ।। yāni teṣām aśeṣāṇāṃ kṛṣṇānusmaraṇaṃ param ।। prāyaścittaṃ tu tasyaikaṃ harisaṃsmaraṇaṃ param ।।
nārāyaṇam avāpnoti sadyaḥ pāpakṣayān naraḥ ।। muktiṃ prayāti bho viprā viṣṇos tasyānukīrtanāt ।। tasyāntarāyo viprendrā devendratvādikaṃ phalam ।। kva japo vāsudeveti muktibījam anuttamam ।।
na yāti narakaṃ śuddhaḥ saṃkṣīṇākhilapātakaḥ ।। narakasvargasaṃjñe vai pāpapuṇye dvijottamāḥ ।। kopāya ca yatas tasmād vastu duḥkhātmakaṃ kutaḥ ।। tad eva kopālayataḥ prasādāya ca jāyate ।।
manasaḥ pariṇāmo ayaṃ sukhaduḥkhādilakṣaṇaḥ ।। jñānātmakam idaṃ viśvaṃ na jñānād vidyate param ।। evam etad mayākhyātaṃ bhavatāṃ maṇḍalaṃ bhuvaḥ ।। saṃkṣepāt sarvam ākhyātaṃ kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotum icchatha ।।
bhuvarlokādikāṃl lokāñ śrotum icchāmahe vayam ।। samācakṣva mahābhāga yathāval lomaharṣaṇa ।। sasamudrasaricchailā tāvatī pṛthivī smṛtā ।। nabhas tāvatpramāṇaṃ hi vistāraparimaṇḍalam ।।
lakṣe divākarāc cāpi maṇḍalaṃ śaśinaḥ sthitam ।। nakṣatramaṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnam upariṣṭāt prakāśate ।। tāvatpramāṇabhāge tu budhasyāpy uśanā sthitaḥ ।। lakṣadvayena bhaumasya sthito devapurohitaḥ ।।
saptarṣimaṇḍalaṃ tasmāl lakṣam ekaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। meḍhībhūtaḥ samastasya jyotiś cakrasya vai dhruvaḥ ।। ijyāphalasya bhūr eṣā ijyā cātra pratiṣṭhitā ।। ekayojanakoṭī tu maharloko vidhīyate ।।
sanandanādyāḥ kathitā viprāś cāmalacetasaḥ ।। vairājā yatra te devāḥ sthitā dehavivarjitāḥ ।। apunarmārakaṃ yatra siddhādimunisevitam ।। sa bhūrlokaḥ samākhyāto vistāro asya mayoditaḥ ।।
bhuvarlokas tu so apy ukto dvitīyo munisattamāḥ ।। svarlokaḥ so api kathito lokasaṃsthānacintakaiḥ ।। janas tapas tathā satyam iti cākṛtakaṃ trayam ।। śūnyo bhavati kalpānte yo antaṃ na ca vinaśyati ।।
pātālāni ca saptaiva brahmāṇḍasyaiṣa vistaraḥ ।। kapitthasya yathā bījaṃ sarvato vai samāvṛtam ।। sa cāmbuparivāro asau vahninā veṣṭito bahiḥ ।। ākāśo api muniśreṣṭhā mahatā pariveṣṭitaḥ ।।
mahāntaṃ ca samāvṛtya pradhānaṃ samavasthitam ।। tad anantam asaṃkhyātaṃ pramāṇenāpi vai yataḥ ।। aṇḍānāṃ tu sahasrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇy ayutāni ca ।। dāruṇy agnir yathā tailaṃ tile tadvat pumān iha ।।
pradhānaṃ ca pumāṃś caiva sarvabhūtānubhūtayā ।। tayoḥ saiva pṛthagbhāve kāraṇaṃ saṃśrayasya ca ।। yathā śaityaṃ jale vāto bibharti kaṇikāgatam ।। yathā ca pādapo mūla- skandhaśākhādisaṃyutaḥ ।।
prabhavanti tatas tebhyo bhavanty anye pare drumāḥ ।। evam avyākṛtāt pūrvaṃ jāyante mahadādayaḥ ।। tebhyaś ca putrās teṣāṃ tu putrāṇāṃ parame sutāḥ ।। bhūtānāṃ bhūtasargeṇa naivāsty apacayas tathā ।।
tathaivāpariṇāmena viśvasya bhagavān hariḥ ।। kāṇḍakoṣās tathā puṣpaṃ kṣīraṃ tadvac ca taṇḍulaḥ ।। prarohahetusāmagryam āsādya munisattamāḥ ।। viṣṇuśaktiṃ samāsādya praroham upayānti vai ।।
jagac ca yo yatra cedaṃ yasmin vilayam eṣyati ।। yasya sarvam abhedena jagad etac carācaram ।। tasminn eva layaṃ sarvaṃ yāti tatra ca tiṣṭhati ।। divi rūpaṃ harer yat tu tasya pucche sthito dhruvaḥ ।।
bhramantam anu taṃ yānti nakṣatrāṇi ca cakravat ।। vātānīkamayair bandhair dhruve baddhāni tāni vai ।। nārāyaṇaḥ paraṃ dhāma tasyādhāraḥ svayaṃ hṛdi ।। sa tārāśiśumārasya dhruvaḥ pucche vyavasthitaḥ ।।
dhruvasya śiśumāraś ca dhruve bhānur vyavasthitaḥ ।। yena viprā vidhānena tan me śṛṇuta sāṃpratam ।। varṣaty ambu tataś cānnam annādam akhilaṃ jagat ।। somaṃ puṣyaty athenduś ca vāyunāḍīmayair divi ।।
na bhraśyanti yatas tebhyo jalāny abhrāṇi tāny ataḥ ।। saṃskāraṃ kālajanitaṃ viprāś cāsādya nirmalāḥ ।। catuṣprakārā bhagavān ādatte savitā dvijāḥ ।। anabhragatam evorvyāṃ sadyaḥ kṣipati raśmibhiḥ ।।
