na yāti narakaṃ martyo divyaṃ snānaṃ hi tat smṛtam ।। ākāśagaṅgāsalilaṃ tad gobhiḥ kṣipyate raveḥ ।। dṛṣṭvārkaṃ patitaṃ jñeyaṃ tad gāṅgaṃ diggajohnitam ।। tat sūryaraśmibhiḥ sadyaḥ samādāya nirasyate ।।
ākāśagaṅgāsalilaṃ divyaṃ snānaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। puṣṇāty oṣadhayaḥ sarvā jīvanāyāmṛtaṃ hi tat ।। sādhakaḥ phalapākāntaḥ prajānāṃ tu prajāyate ।। kurvate aharahaś caiva devān āpyāyayanti te ।।
sarvadevanikāyāś ca paśubhūtagaṇāś ca ye ।। sāpi niṣpādyate vṛṣṭiḥ savitrā munisattamāḥ ।। dhruvasya śiśumāro asau so api nārāyaṇāśrayaḥ ।। vibhartā sarvabhūtānām ādibhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।
bhūsamudrādibhir yuktaṃ kim anyac chrotum icchatha ।। vaktum arhasi dharmajña śrotuṃ no vartate manaḥ ।। vidyā tapaś ca kīrtiś ca sa tīrthaphalam aśnute ।। śataśo api jalair dhautaṃ surābhāṇḍam ivāśuci ।।
duṣṭāśayaṃ dambharuciṃ punanti vyutthitendriyam ।। tatra tatra kurukṣetraṃ prayāgaṃ puṣkaraṃ tathā ।। saṃkṣepeṇa muniśreṣṭhāḥ pṛthivyāṃ yāni kāni vai ।। prathamaṃ puṣkaraṃ tīrthaṃ naimiṣāraṇyam eva ca ।।
dhenukaṃ campakāraṇyaṃ saindhavāraṇyam eva ca ।। gayā prabhāsaṃ śrītīrthaṃ divyaṃ kanakhalaṃ tathā ।। lohākulaṃ sakedāraṃ mandarāraṇyam eva ca ।। rūpatīrthaṃ śūkaravaṃ cakratīrthaṃ mahāphalam ।।
tīrthaṃ kokāmukhaṃ puṇyaṃ badarīśailam eva ca ।। koṭitīrthaṃ cāgnipadaṃ tīrthaṃ pañcaśikhaṃ tathā ।। gaṅgādvāraṃ pañcakūṭaṃ madhyakesaram eva ca ।। daṃṣṭrākuṇḍaṃ viṣṇutīrthaṃ sārvakāmikam eva ca ।।
brahmakuṇḍaṃ vahnikuṇḍaṃ tīrthaṃ satyapadaṃ tathā ।। mānasaṃ sthūlaśṛṅgaṃ ca sthūladaṇḍaṃ tathorvaśī ।। sadāprabhaṃ merukuṇḍaṃ tīrthaṃ somābhiṣecanam ।। saptadhāraikadhāraṃ ca tīrthaṃ cāmarakaṇṭakam ।।
bilvaprabhaṃ devahradaṃ tīrthaṃ viṣṇuhradaṃ tathā ।। agniprabhaṃ ca puṃnāgaṃ devaprabham anuttamam ।। sātīrthaṃ lokapālākhyaṃ maṇipuragiriṃ tathā ।। malavyaṃ goprabhāvaṃ ca govaraṃ vaṭamūlakam ।।
kanyāśramaṃ vāyukuṇḍaṃ jambūmārgaṃ tathottamam ।। koṭitīrthaṃ bhadravaṭaṃ mahākālavanaṃ tathā ।। piṅgutīrthaṃ savāsiṣṭhaṃ tīrthaṃ ca pṛthasaṃgamam ।। ṛṣitīrthaṃ brahmatuṅgaṃ vasutīrthaṃ kumārikam ।।
paitāmahaṃ ca vimalaṃ rudrapādaṃ tathottamam ।। yajanaṃ yājanaṃ caiva tathaiva brahmavālukam ।। dīrghasattraṃ hayapadaṃ tīrthaṃ cānaśanaṃ tathā ।। vastrāpadaṃ dāruvalaṃ chāyārohaṇam eva ca ।।
vaṭāvaṭaṃ bhadravaṭaṃ kauśāmbī ca divākaram ।। rudrakoṭiṃ sumanasaṃ tīrthaṃ sadrāvanāmitam ।। satataṃ pṛthivīsarvaṃ pāriplavapṛthūdakau ।। koṭitīrthaṃ pañcanadaṃ vārāhaṃ yakṣiṇīhradam ।।
badarīvanam āsīnaṃ ratnamūlakam eva ca ।। sūryatīrthaṃ śaṅkhinī ca gavāṃ bhavanam eva ca ।। kāmeśvaraṃ mātritīrthaṃ tīrthaṃ śītavanaṃ tathā ।। daśāśvamedhaṃ kedāraṃ brahmodumbaram eva ca ।।
īṭāspadaṃ koṭikūṭaṃ kiṃdānaṃ kiṃjapaṃ tathā ।। pāṇiṣātaṃ miśrakaṃ ca madhūvaṭamanojavau ।। divyaṃ ca nṛgadhūmākhyaṃ tīrthaṃ viṣṇupadaṃ tathā ।। śrīkuñjaṃ śālitīrthaṃ ca naimiṣeyaṃ ca viśrutam ।।
brahmatīrthaṃ manastīrthaṃ tīrthaṃ vai kārupāvanam ।। īśānatīrthaṃ pravaraṃ pāvanaṃ pāñcayajñikam ।। śākaṃbharī devatīrthaṃ suvarṇākhyaṃ kilaṃ hradam ।। brahmatīrthaṃ brahmayoniṃ nīlaparvatam eva ca ।।
svargadvāraṃ prajādvāraṃ kālikāśramam eva ca ।। bhadrakarṇahradaṃ caiva śaṅkukarṇahradaṃ tathā ।। kapālamocanaṃ caiva avakīrṇaṃ ca kāmyakam ।। reṇukaṃ pañcavaṭakaṃ vimocanam athaujasam ।।
viśveśvaraṃ mānavakaṃ kūpaṃ nārāyaṇāśrayam ।। indramārgam ekarātraṃ kṣīrakāvāsam eva ca ।। koṭitīrthasthalīṃ caiva bhadrakālīhradaṃ tathā ।। aśvavedī kubjāvanaṃ yamunāprabhavaṃ tathā ।।
urvīsaṃkramaṇaṃ caiva māyāvidyodbhavaṃ tathā ।। bāhutīrthaṃ cārunadīṃ vimalāśokam eva ca ।। somatīrthaṃ sitodaṃ ca tīrthaṃ matsyodarīṃ tathā ।। aruṇāspadaṃ kāmadaṃ ca śukratīrthaṃ savālukam ।।
kuṇḍaṃ vimaladaṇḍasya tīrthaṃ caṇḍeśvarasya ca ।। jaigīṣavyaguhā caiva harikeśavanaṃ tathā ।। puṇḍarīkahradaṃ caiva vāpī karkoṭakasya ca ।। kuṇḍaṃ ghargharikāyāś ca śyāmakūpaṃ ca candrikā ।।
kūpaṃ sindhūdbhavaṃ caiva puṇyaṃ brahmasaraṃ tathā ।। bhaktahradaṃ kṣīrasaraḥ pretādhāraṃ kumārakam ।। śṛṅgatīrthaṃ mahātīrthaṃ tīrthaśreṣṭhā mahānadī ।। dakṣiṇaṃ cottaraṃ caiva gomayaṃ rūpaśītikam ।।
prabhāsanaṃ sītavanaṃ yonidvāraṃ ca dhenukam ।। pitṛkūpaṃ rudratīrthaṃ śakratīrthaṃ sumālinam ।। kauśikyaṃ bharataṃ caiva tīrthaṃ jyeṣṭhālikā tathā ।। niścīvā prabhavaś caiva vasiṣṭhāśramam eva ca ।।
vīrāśramaṃ brahmasaro brahmavīrāvakāpilī ।। śunaḥ kuṇḍo atha tīrthaṃ ca nanditīrthaṃ tathaiva ca ।। kumbhakarṇahradaṃ caiva kauśikīhradam eva ca ।। saṃdhyātīrthaṃ kāratoyaṃ kapilaṃ lohitārṇavam ।।
puṇyāvatīhradaṃ tīrthaṃ tīrthaṃ badarikāśramam ।। mārkaṇḍeyavanaṃ caiva kṛṣṇatīrthaṃ tathā vaṭam ।। sānugartaṃ samāhendraṃ śrītīrthaṃ śrīnadaṃ tathā ।। kanyātīrthaṃ ca gokarṇaṃ gāyatrīsthānam eva ca ।।
jātīhradaṃ devakūpaṃ kuśapravaṇam eva ca ।। tathānyad vālakhilyānāṃ sapūrvāṇāṃ tathāparam ।। tīrtheṣv eteṣu vidhivat samyak śraddhāsamanvitaḥ ।। devān ṛṣīn manuṣyāṃś ca pitṝn saṃtarpya ca kramāt ।।
pṛthak pṛthak phalaṃ teṣu pratitīrtheṣu bho dvijāḥ ।। paṭhec ca śrāvayed vāpi sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। tīrthānām uttamaṃ tīrthaṃ brūhi no vadatāṃ vara ।। tam ahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yat pṛcchadhvaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।।
nānādrumalatākīrṇe nānāmṛgagaṇair yute ।। śālais tālais tamālaiś ca panasair dhavakhādiraiḥ ।। anyaiś ca vividhair vṛkṣair nānāpuṣpopaśobhitaiḥ ।। mahābhāratakartāraṃ sarvaśāstraviśāradam ।।
purāṇāgamavaktāraṃ vedavedāṅgapāragam ।। draṣṭum abhyāyayuḥ prītyā munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ ।। vasiṣṭho jaiminir dhaumyo mārkaṇḍeyo atha vālmikiḥ ।। sumantur bhārgavo nāma kaṇvo medhātithir guruḥ ।।
maudgalyas tṛṇayajñaś ca pippalādo akṛtavraṇaḥ ।। śāṇḍilyaś ca vibhāṇḍaś ca durvāsā lomaśas tathā ।। bhāskariḥ pūraṇaḥ sūtaḥ pulastyaḥ kapilas tathā ।। sanatkumāraḥ pailaś ca kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇānubhautikaḥ ।।
rarāja sa muniḥ śrīmān nakṣatrair iva candramāḥ ।। te api taṃ pratipūjyaiva kathāṃ cakruḥ parasparam ।। papracchuḥ saṃśayaṃ sarve tapovananivāsinaḥ ।। bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca sarvaṃ jānāsi vāṅmayam ।।
rāgagrāhākule raudre viṣayodakasaṃplave ।। mohapaṅkāvile durge lobhagambhīradustare ।। pṛcchāmas tvāṃ mahābhāgaṃ brūhi no munisattama ।। upadeśapradānena lokān uddhartum arhasi ।।
pṛthivyāṃ karmabhūmiṃ ca śrotum icchāmahe vayam ।। prāpnoti paramāṃ siddhiṃ narakaṃ ca vikarmataḥ ।। tasmād brūhi mahāprājña yat pṛṣṭo asi dvijottama ।। vyāsaḥ provāca bhagavān bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyavit ।।
yaḥ saṃvādo abhavat pūrvam ṛṣīṇāṃ brahmaṇā saha ।। nānādrumalatākīrṇe nānāpuṣpopaśobhite ।। nānāsattvasamākīrṇe nānāścaryasamanvite ।। nānāmunijanākīrṇe nānāśramasamanvite ।।
jagatpatiṃ jagadvandyaṃ jagadādhāram īśvaram ।। munisiddhāpsarobhiś ca vṛtam anyair divālayaiḥ ।। kecid vādyāni vādyante kecin nṛtyanti cāpare ।। nānākusumagandhāḍhye dakṣiṇānilasevite ।।
imam artham ṛṣivarāḥ papracchuḥ pitaraṃ dvijāḥ ।। vaktum arhasi deveśa mokṣakṣetraṃ ca durlabham ।। papracchus te yathā praśnaṃ tat sarvaṃ munisattamāḥ ।। purāṇaṃ vedasaṃbaddhaṃ bhuktimuktipradaṃ śubham ।।
karmaṇaḥ phalabhūmiś ca svargaṃ ca narakaṃ tathā ।। avaśyaṃ phalam āpnoti aśubhasya śubhasya ca ।। prāpnuvanti parāṃ siddhiṃ tasmin varṣe na saṃśayaḥ ।। prāpnoti puruṣaḥ sarvaṃ tasmin varṣe susaṃyataḥ ।।
kṛtvā suśobhanaṃ karma devatvaṃ pratipedire ।। tasmin varṣe budhāḥ śāntā vītarāgā vimatsarāḥ ।। te api kṛtvā śubhaṃ karma tasmin varṣe divaṃ gatāḥ ।। svargāpavargaphalade tat paśyāmaḥ kadā vayam ।।
pāpāya vā suraśreṣṭha varjayitvā ca bhāratam ।। na khalv anyatra martyānāṃ bhūmau karma vidhīyate ।। yadi te asti dayāsmāsu yathāvasthitir eva ca ।। bhedāś ca tasya varṣasya brūhi sarvān aśeṣataḥ ।।
samudrāntaritā jñeyās te samāś ca parasparam ।। nāgadvīpas tathā saumyo gāndharvo vāruṇas tathā ।। yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ vai dvīpo ayaṃ dakṣiṇottaraḥ ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś cānte sthitā dvijāḥ ।।
teṣāṃ saṃvyavahāraś ca ebhiḥ karmabhir iṣyate ।। mahendro malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimān ṛkṣaparvataḥ ।। teṣāṃ sahasraśaś cānye bhūdharā ye samīpagāḥ ।। kolāhalaḥ sa vaibhrājo mandaro dardalācalaḥ ।।
tuṅgaprastho nāgagirir godhanaḥ pāṇḍarācalaḥ ।। ṛṣyamūkaḥ sa gomanthaḥ kṛtaśailaḥ kṛtācalaḥ ।। tair vimiśrā janapadā mlecchādyāś caiva bhāgaśaḥ ।। gaṅgā sarasvatī sindhuś candrabhāgā tathāparā ।।
gomatī dhūtapāpā ca bāhudā ca dṛṣadvatī ।। kauśikī cāpagā caiva himavatpādaniḥsṛtāḥ ।। veṇyā tu candanā caiva sadānīrā mahī tathā ।। siprā hy avantī ca tathā pāriyātrānugāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
mandākinī daśārṇā ca citrakūṭā tathāparā ।। tathānyātilaghuśroṇī vipāpmā śaivalā nadī ।। ṛkṣapādaprasūtā vai tathānyā vegavāhinī ।। veṇā vaitaraṇī caiva sinīvālī kumudvatī ।।
vindhyapādaprasūtās tā nadyaḥ puṇyajalāḥ śubhāḥ ।। tuṅgabhadrā suprayogā tathānyā pāpanāśinī ।। kṛtamālā tāmraparṇī puṣyajā pratyalāvatī ।। pitṛsomarṣikulyā ca vañjulā tridivā ca yā ।।
suvikālā kumārī ca manūgā mandagāminī ।। sarvāḥ puṇyāḥ sarasvatyaḥ sarvā gaṅgāḥ samudragāḥ ।। anyāḥ sahasraśaḥ proktāḥ kṣudranadyo dvijottamāḥ ।। matsyā mukuṭakulyāś ca kuntalāḥ kāśikośalāḥ ।।
madhyadeśā janapadāḥ prāyaśo amī prakīrtitāḥ ।। pṛthivyām api kṛtsnāyāṃ sa pradeśo manoramaḥ ।। vāhīkarāṭadhānāś ca sutīrāḥ kālatoyadāḥ ।। gāndhārā yavanāś caiva sindhusauvīramadrakāḥ ।।
māṭharāś caiva kanakāḥ kaikeyā dambhamālikāḥ ।। kāmbojāś caiva viprendrā barbarāś ca salaukikāḥ ।। ātreyāś ca bharadvājāḥ puṣkalāś ca daśerakāḥ ।। auṣadhyaś calacandrā ca kirātānāṃ ca jātayaḥ ।।
śūlikāḥ kuhakāś caiva māgadhāś ca tathaiva ca ।। andhā vāmaṅkurākāś ca vallakāś ca makhāntakāḥ ।। bhadratuṅgāḥ pratijayā bhāryāṅgāś cāpamardakāḥ ।। mallā magadhakā nandāḥ prācyā janapadās tathā ।।
pūrṇāś ca kevalāś caiva golāṅgūlās tathaiva ca ।। mahārāṣṭrā māhiṣakāḥ kaliṅgāś caiva sarvaśaḥ ।। pulindāś caiva mauleyā vaidarbhā daṇḍakaiḥ saha ।। kaulikāḥ kuntalāś caiva dambhakā nīlakālakāḥ ।।
śūrpārakāḥ kālidhanā lolās tālakaṭaiḥ saha ।। malajāḥ karkaśāś caiva melakāś colakaiḥ saha ।। toṣalāḥ kośalāś caiva traipurā vaidiśās tathā ।। abhayā ruṇḍikerāś ca carcarā hotradhartayaḥ ।।
ato deśān pravakṣyāmi parvatāśrayiṇaś ca ye ।। karṇaprāvaraṇāś caiva ūrṇā darghāḥ sakuntakāḥ ।। kṛtatretādikaś cātra caturyugakṛto vidhiḥ ।। dakṣiṇe parato yasya pūrve caiva mahodadhiḥ ।।
tad etad bhārataṃ varṣaṃ sarvabījaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। mṛgayakṣāpsaroyoniṃ tadvat sarpasarīsṛpāḥ ।। prayānti karmabhūr viprā nānyā lokeṣu vidyate ।। api mānuṣyam āpsyāmo devatvāt pracyutāḥ kṣitau ।।
tatkarmanigaḍagrastais tatkarmakṣapaṇonmukhaiḥ ।। yatra viprādayo varṇāḥ prāpnuvanty abhivāñchitam ।। dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ prāpnuvanti mahāphalam ।। sarvadānaphalaṃ caiva sarvayajñaphalaṃ tathā ।।
devatārādhanaphalaṃ svādhyāyasya phalaṃ dvijāḥ ।। nānāvrataphalaṃ caiva nānāśāstraphalaṃ tathā ।। brahmacaryaphalaṃ caiva gārhasthyena ca yat phalam ।। iṣṭāpūrtaphalaṃ caiva tathānyac chubhakarmaṇām ।।
kaḥ śaknoti guṇān vaktuṃ bhāratasyākhilān dvijāḥ ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ dhanyaṃ buddhivivardhanam ।। sarvapāpair vinirmukto viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। oṇḍradeśa iti khyātaḥ svargamokṣapradāyakaḥ ।।
deśo asau puṇyaśīlānāṃ guṇaiḥ sarvair alaṃkṛtaḥ ।। tapaḥsvādhyāyaniratā vandyāḥ pūjyāś ca te sadā ।। praśastāḥ sarvakāryeṣu tatradeśodbhavā dvijāḥ ।। itihāsavidaś caiva purāṇārthaviśāradāḥ ।।
agnihotraratāḥ kecit kecit smārtāgnitatparāḥ ।। nivasanty utkale puṇye yajñotsavavibhūṣite ।। svakarmaniratāḥ śāntās tatra tiṣṭhanti dhārmikāḥ ।। yaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhāskaraṃ martyaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।
tasmin deśe suraśreṣṭha yatrāste sa divākaraḥ ।। sarvatra vālukākīrṇe deśe sarvaguṇānvite ।। puṃnāgaiḥ karṇikāraiś ca bakulair nāgakesaraiḥ ।। mālatīkundapuṣpaiś ca tathānyair mallikādibhiḥ ।।
kadambair lakucaiḥ śālaiḥ panasair devadārubhiḥ ।। aśvatthaiḥ saptaparṇaiś ca āmrair āmrātakais tathā ।। anyaiś ca vividhair vṛkṣaiḥ sarvataḥ samalaṃkṛtam ।। samantād yojanaṃ sāgraṃ bhuktimuktiphalapradam ।।
koṇāditya iti khyāto bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ ।। kṛtopavāso yatretya snātvā tu makarālaye ।। sāgare vidhivat snātvā śarvaryante samāhitaḥ ।। uttīrya vāsasī dhaute paridhāya sunirmale ।।
upaviśyodaye kāle prāṅmukhaḥ savitus tadā ।। aṣṭapattraṃ kesarāḍhyaṃ vartulaṃ cordhvakarṇikam ।। raktapuṣpaṃ sadarbhaṃ ca prakṣipet tāmrabhājane ।। pidhāya tan muniśreṣṭhāḥ pātraṃ pātreṇa vinyaset ।।
ātmānaṃ bhāskaraṃ dhyātvā samyak śraddhāsamanvitaḥ ।। kāmārigocare caiva punar madhye ca pūjayet ।। saṃpūjya padmam āvāhya gaganāt tatra bhāskaram ।। kṛtvā snānādikaṃ sarvaṃ dhyātvā taṃ susamāhitaḥ ।।
piṅgākṣaṃ dvibhujaṃ raktaṃ padmapattrāruṇāmbaram ।। surūpaṃ varadaṃ śāntaṃ prabhāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitam ।। tatas tat pātram ādāya jānubhyāṃ dharaṇīṃ gataḥ ।। tryakṣareṇa tu mantreṇa sūryāyārghyaṃ nivedayet ।।
śraddhayā bhāvayuktena bhaktigrāhyo ravir yataḥ ।। hṛc chiraś ca śikhāvarma- netrāṇy astraṃ ca pūjayet ।। japtvā stutvā namas kṛtvā mudrāṃ baddhvā visarjayet ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ striyaḥ śūdrāś ca saṃyatāḥ ।।
te bhuktvābhimatān kāmān prāpnuvanti parāṃ gatim ।। ye saṃśrayanti manujās te syuḥ sukhasya bhājanam ।। tāvan na pūjayed viṣṇuṃ śaṃkaraṃ vā sureśvaram ।। ādityāya śucir bhūtvā puṣpair gandhair manoramaiḥ ।।
ādityāya śuciḥ snātaḥ sa labhed īpsitaṃ phalam ।। vidyāṃ prāpnoti vidyārthī sutārthī putravān bhavet ।। tasya tasya phalaṃ samyak prāpnoti puruṣaḥ sudhīḥ ।। naro vā yadi vā nārī sarvakāmaphalaṃ labhet ।।
praviśya pūjayed bhānuṃ kṛtvā tu triḥ pradakṣiṇam ।। gandhaiḥ puṣpais tathā dīpair dhūpair naivedyakair api ।। evaṃ saṃpūjya taṃ devaṃ sahasrāṃśuṃ jagatpatim ।। sarvapāpavinirmukto yuvā divyavapur naraḥ ।।
vimānenārkavarṇena kāmagena suvarcasā ।। bhuktvā tatra varān bhogān yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam ।। caturvedo bhaved vipraḥ svadharmanirataḥ śuciḥ ।। caitre māsi site pakṣe yātrāṃ damanabhañjikām ।।
śayanotthāpane bhānoḥ saṃkrāntyāṃ viṣuvāyane ।। ye tatra yātrāṃ kurvanti śraddhayā saṃyatendriyāḥ ।। āste tatra mahādevas tīre nadanadīpateḥ ।। ye taṃ paśyanti kāmāriṃ snātvā samyaṅ mahodadhau ।।
praṇipātais tathā stotrair gītair vādyair manoharaiḥ ।। prāpnuvanti mahātmānaḥ saṃsiddhiṃ paramāṃ tathā ।। upagīyamānā gandharvaiḥ śivalokaṃ vrajanti te ।। puṇyakṣayād ihāgatya cāturvedā bhavanti te ।।
yas tatra savituḥ kṣetre prāṇāṃs tyajati mānavaḥ ।। punar mānuṣatāṃ prāpya rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ ।। evaṃ mayā muniśreṣṭhāḥ proktaṃ kṣetraṃ sudurlabham ।। koṇārkasyodadhes tīre bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ ।।
bhāskarasya paraṃ kṣetraṃ bhuktimuktiphalapradam ।। tava vaktrodbhavāṃ puṇyām ādityasyāghanāśinīm ।। devapūjāphalaṃ yac ca yac ca dānaphalaṃ prabho ।। dīpadhūpapradāne ca saṃmārjanavidhau ca yat ।।
arghaś ca kīdṛśaḥ proktaḥ kutra vā saṃpradīyate ।। etat sarvaṃ suraśreṣṭha śrotum icchāmahe vayam ।। bhaktiṃ śraddhāṃ samādhiṃ ca kathyamānaṃ nibodhata ।। dhyānaṃ samādhir ity uktaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ susamāhitāḥ ।।
agniśuśrūṣakaś caiva sa vai bhaktaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। tatkarmakṛd bhaved yas tu sa vai bhaktaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। kīrtanād vā paro viprāḥ sa vai bhaktataro naraḥ ।। ādityavratacārī ca sa vai bhaktataro naraḥ ।।
yaḥ smared bhāskaraṃ nityaṃ sa vai bhaktataro naraḥ ।। bhaktyā samādhinā caiva stavena manasā tathā ।। pratigṛhṇanti taṃ devā manuṣyāḥ pitaras tathā ।। pratigṛhṇanti tad devā nāstikān varjayanti ca ।।
bhāvaśuddhyā kriyate yat tat sarvaṃ saphalaṃ bhavet ।। upavāsena bhaktyā vai sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। tatkṣaṇāt sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। pradakṣiṇīkṛtā tena saptadvīpā vasuṃdharā ।।
pradakṣiṇīkṛtās tena sarve devā bhavanti hi ।। niyamavratacārī ca bhaved bhaktisamanvitaḥ ।। ahorātropavāsena pūjayed yas tu bhāskaram ।। kṛṣṇapakṣasya saptamyāṃ sopavāso jitendriyaḥ ।।
padmaprabheṇa yānena sūryalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। sarvaśuklopahāreṇa pūjayed yas tu bhāskaram ।। arkasaṃpuṭasaṃyuktam udakaṃ prasṛtaṃ pibet ।। dvābhyāṃ saṃvatsarābhyāṃ tu samāptaniyamo bhavet ।।
śuklapakṣasya saptamyāṃ yadādityadinaṃ bhavet ।। snānaṃ dānaṃ tapo homa upavāsas tathaiva ca ।। ye cādityadine prāpte śrāddhaṃ kurvanti mānavāḥ ।। yeṣāṃ dharmyāḥ kriyāḥ sarvāḥ sadaivoddiśya bhāskaram ।।
śvetayā raktayā vāpi pītamṛttikayāpi vā ।। citrabhānuṃ vicitrais tu kusumaiś ca sugandhibhiḥ ।। ghṛtena dīpaṃ prajvālya tilatailena vā punaḥ ।। dīpadātā naro nityaṃ jñānadīpena dīpyate ।।
agnikārye ca dīpe ca mahāpātakanāśanam ।। catuṣpatheṣu rathyāsu rūpavān subhago bhavet ।। vasāmedosthiniryāsair na tu deyaḥ kathaṃcana ।। dātā dīpyati cāpy evaṃ na tiryaggatim āpnuyāt ।।
dīpahartā naro bandhaṃ nāśaṃ krodhaṃ tamo vrajet ।। yaḥ samālabhate nityaṃ kuṅkumāgurucandanaiḥ ।। raktacandanasaṃmiśrai raktapuṣpaiḥ śucir naraḥ ।। udayāt parivarteta yāvad astamane sthitaḥ ।।
ādityavratam etat tu mahāpātakanāśanam ।। udaye śraddhayā yuktaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। arghyapradātā labhate saptajanmānugaṃ phalam ।। pratimāyāṃ tathā piṇḍyāṃ deyam arghyaṃ prayatnataḥ ।।
saghṛtaṃ guggulaṃ vāpi raver bhaktisamanvitaḥ ।। śrīvāsaṃ caturasraṃ ca devadāruṃ tathaiva ca ।। ayane tūttare sūryam athavā dakṣiṇāyane ।। viṣuveṣūparāgeṣu ṣaḍaśītimukheṣu ca ।।
evaṃ velāsu sarvāsu sarvakālaṃ ca mānavaḥ ।। kṛsaraiḥ pāyasaiḥ pūpaiḥ phalamūlaghṛtaudanaiḥ ।। ghṛtena tarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā sarvasiddho bhaven naraḥ ।। dadhnā tu tarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā kāryasiddhiṃ labhen naraḥ ।।
tīrtheṣu śucitāpannaḥ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। śraddhayā bhānave dattvā gatim iṣṭām avāpnuyāt ।। tat tasya śatasāhasram utpādayati bhāskaraḥ ।। sarvaṃ sūryaprasādena tad aśeṣaṃ vyapohati ।।
yathoktadakṣiṇair viprair na tat kratuśatair api ।। bhāskarasya suraśreṣṭha vadatas teṣu durlabham ।। śrotum icchāmahe brahman paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। ya icchen mokṣam āsthātuṃ devatāṃ kāṃ yajeta saḥ ।।
svargataś caiva kiṃ kuryād yena na cyavate punaḥ ।। yasmāt parataraṃ nāsti tan me brūhi sureśvara ।। pralaye ca kam abhyeti tad bhavān vaktum arhati ।। nātaḥ parataro devaḥ kaścid anyo dvijottamāḥ ।।
tāpayaty eṣa trīṃl lokān bhavan raśmibhir ulbaṇaḥ ।। sarvasya jagato nāthaḥ sarvasākṣī jagatpatiḥ ।। eṣa bhāti tapaty eṣa varṣaty eṣa gabhastibhiḥ ।। na hy eṣa kṣayam āyāti nityam akṣayamaṇḍalaḥ ।।
dhruvaṃ sthānaṃ smṛtaṃ hy etad yasmān na cyavate punaḥ ।। pralaye ca tam abhyeti bhāskaraṃ dīptatejasam ।। vāyur bhūtvā viśanty asmiṃs tejorāśau divākare ।। vasanty āśritya munayaḥ saṃsiddhā daivataiḥ saha ।।
vālakhilyādayaś caiva ṛṣayo brahmavādinaḥ ।। yogam āsthāya sarve te praviṣṭāḥ sūryamaṇḍalam ।। ādityakiraṇān gatvā hy apunarbhāvam āsthitaḥ ।। pratyakṣo ayaṃ paro devaḥ sūryas timiranāśanaḥ ।।
yasmād dṛṣṭer agamyās te devā viṣṇupurogamāḥ ।। sa hi mātā pitā caiva kṛtsnasya jagato guruḥ ।। mitratve ca sthito yasmāt tapas tepe dvijottamāḥ ।। sṛṣṭvā sasāgarān dvīpān bhuvanāni caturdaśa ।।
sṛṣṭvā prajāpatīn sarvān sṛṣṭvā ca vividhāḥ prajāḥ ।। kṛtvā dvādaśadhātmānam ādityam upapadyate ।। vivasvān viṣṇur aṃśaś ca varuṇo mitra eva ca ।। kṛtsnaṃ jagad idaṃ vyāptaṃ mūrtibhiś ca dvijottamāḥ ।।
sthitā sā devarājatve devānāṃ ripunāśinī ।। sthitā prajāpatitvena vividhāḥ sṛjate prajāḥ ।। megheṣv eva sthitā sā tu varṣate ca gabhastibhiḥ ।। sthitā vanaspatau sā tu oṣadhīṣu ca sarvataḥ ।।
anne vyavasthitā sā tu prajāṃ puṣṇāti nityaśaḥ ।। vāyoḥ saṃsaraṇā sā tu deveṣv eva samāśritā ।। bhūyiṣv avasthitā sā tu śarīreṣu ca dehinām ।। agnau pratiṣṭhitā sā tu pacaty annaṃ śarīriṇām ।।
prādurbhavati sā nityaṃ devānām arisūdanī ।। vāyau pratiṣṭhitā sā tu prahlādayati vai prajāḥ ।। jaleṣv avasthitā sā tu prajāṃ puṣṇāti nityaśaḥ ।। lokānāṃ sā hitārthāya sthitā candrasarittaṭe ।।
anugṛhṇan sadā bhaktān varair nānāvidhais tu saḥ ।। tatra mitraḥ sthito yasmāt tasmān mitraṃ paraṃ smṛtam ।। kṛtsnaṃ jagad idaṃ vyāptaṃ mūrtibhiś ca dvijottamāḥ ।। bhaktimadbhir narair nityaṃ tadgatenāntarātmanā ।।
nityaṃ śrutvā paṭhitvā ca sūryaloke mahīyate ।। tataḥ kasmāt tapas tepe varepsuḥ prākṛto yathā ।। pṛṣṭaṃ mitreṇa yat pūrvaṃ nāradāya mahātmane ।। mitraś ca varuṇaś cobhau tāsāṃ tapasi saṃsthitau ।।
mitro mitravane cāsmin vāyubhakṣo abhavat tadā ।। nāradas tu mahāyogī sarvāṃl lokāṃś caran vaśī ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā tu tapasyantaṃ tasya kautūhalaṃ hy abhūt ।। dhṛtam ekātmakaṃ yena trailokyaṃ sumahātmanā ।।
iti saṃcintya manasā taṃ devaṃ nārado abravīt ।। tvam ajaḥ śāśvato dhātā tvaṃ nidhānam anuttamam ।। catvāraś cāśramā deva gṛhasthādyās tathaiva hi ।। pitā mātā ca sarvasya daivataṃ tvaṃ hi śāśvatam ।।
yajase pitaraṃ kaṃ tvaṃ devaṃ vāpi na vidmahe ।। tvayi bhaktimati brahman pravakṣyāmi yathātatham ।। indriyair indriyārthaiś ca sarvabhūtair vivarjitam ।। triguṇād vyatirikto asau puruṣaś caiva kalpitaḥ ।।
mahān iti ca yogeṣu pradhānam iti kathyate ।। sa ca trirūpo viśvātmā śarvo akṣara iti smṛtaḥ ।। aśarīraḥ śarīreṣu sarveṣu nivasaty asau ।। mamāntarātmā tava ca ye cānye dehasaṃsthitāḥ ।।
saguṇo nirguṇo viśvo jñānagamyo hy asau smṛtaḥ ।। sarvataḥśrutimāṃl loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati ।। ekaś carati vai kṣetre svairacārī yathāsukham ।। tāni vetti sa yogātmā tataḥ kṣetrajña ucyate ।।
viśvaṃ bahuvidhaṃ jñeyaṃ sa ca sarvatra ucyate ।। tasyaikasya mahattvaṃ hi sa caikaḥ puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। sa tu vidhikriyāyattaḥ sṛjaty ātmānam ātmanā ।। koṭiśaś ca karoty eṣa pratyagātmānam ātmanā ।।
bhūme rasaviśeṣeṇa tathā guṇarasāt tu saḥ ।। ekatvaṃ ca pṛthaktvaṃ ca tathā tasya na saṃśayaḥ ।। saṃjñāṃ tathā mune so ayaṃ brahmādiṣu tathāpnuyāt ।। tathā rūpasahasrāṇi sa ekaḥ saṃprasūyate ।।
ekatvapralaye cāsya bahutvaṃ ca pravartate ।। akṣayaś cāprameyaś ca sarvagaś ca sa ucyate ।। avyaktāvyaktabhāvasthā yā sā prakṛtir ucyate ।। loke ca pūjyate yo asau daive pitrye ca karmaṇi ।।
ātmanā sa tu vijñeyas tatas taṃ pūjayāmy aham ।। tena gacchanti devarṣe tenoddiṣṭaphalāṃ gatim ।। bhaktyā saṃpūjayanty ādyaṃ gatiś caiṣāṃ dadāti saḥ ।। evaṃ matvā yathājñānaṃ pūjayāmi divākaram ।।
etad apy adhikaṃ teṣāṃ yad ekaṃ praviśanty uta ।। asmadbhaktyāpi devarṣe tvayāpi paramaṃ smṛtam ।। sarve ca paramātmānaṃ pūjayanti divākaram ।। mayāpi ca samākhyātā kathā bhānor dvijottamāḥ ।।
na hy anādityabhaktāya idaṃ deyaṃ kadācana ।। sa sahasrārciṣaṃ devaṃ praviśen nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। jijñāsur labhate jñānaṃ gatim iṣṭāṃ tathaiva ca ।। yo yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ sa taṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam ।।
sa ca dhātā vidhātā ca sarvasya jagataḥ prabhuḥ ।। bhavaty asmāj jagat sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।। mahādyutimatāṃ caiva tejo ayaṃ sārvalaukikam ।। sūrya eva trilokasya mūlaṃ paramadaivatam ।।
ādityāj jāyate vṛṣṭir vṛṣṭer annaṃ tataḥ prajāḥ ।। bhāvābhāvau hi lokānām ādityān niḥsṛtau purā ।। tatra gacchanti nirvāṇaṃ jāyante asmāt punaḥ punaḥ ।। māsāḥ saṃvatsarāś caiva ṛtavaś ca yugāni ca ।।
kālād ṛte na niyamo nāgnau viharaṇakriyā ।। kuto vai sasyaniṣpattis tṛṇauṣadhigaṇaḥ kutaḥ ।। jagatprabhāvād viśate bhāskarād vāritaskarāt ।। nāvṛṣṭyā paridhiṃ dhatte vāriṇā dīpyate raviḥ ।।
śveto varṣāsu varṇena pāṇḍuḥ śaradi bhāskaraḥ ।। iti varṇāḥ samākhyātāḥ sūryasya ṛtusaṃbhavāḥ ।। athādityasya nāmāni sāmānyāni dvijottamāḥ ।। ādityaḥ savitā sūryo mihiro arkaḥ prabhākaraḥ ।।
ravir dvādaśabhis teṣāṃ jñeyaḥ sāmānyanāmabhiḥ ।। vivasvān aṃśumāṃs tvaṣṭā parjanyo dvādaśaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। uttiṣṭhanti sadā hy ete māsair dvādaśabhiḥ kramāt ।। vivasvāñ jyeṣṭhamāse tu āṣāḍhe cāṃśumān smṛtaḥ ।।
indra āśvayuje māsi dhātā tapati kārttike ।। māghe bhagas tu vijñeyas tvaṣṭā tapati phālgune ।। dīpyate gosahasreṇa śataiś ca tribhir aryamā ।। vivasvān iva parjanyo varuṇaś cāryamā tathā ।।
indras tu dviguṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhir dhātaikādaśabhiḥ śataiḥ ।। uttaropakrame arkasya vardhante raśmayas tathā ।। evaṃ raśmisahasraṃ tu sūryalokād anugraham ।। vistareṇa sahasraṃ tu punar anyat prakīrtitam ।।
teṣāṃ bhavati kiṃ puṇyaṃ gatiś ca parameśvara ।। alaṃ nāmasahasreṇa paṭhann evaṃ stavaṃ śubham ।। tāni vaḥ kīrtayiṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ bhāskarasya vai ।। lokaprakāśakaḥ śrīmāṃl lokacakṣur maheśvaraḥ ।।
tapanas tāpanaś caiva śuciḥ saptāśvavāhanaḥ ।। ekaviṃśati ity eṣa stava iṣṭaḥ sadā raveḥ ।। stavarāja iti khyātas triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ ।। stauti sūryaṃ śucir bhūtvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।
ekajapyena tat sarvaṃ naśyaty arkasya saṃnidhau ।। dhūpamantrārghyamantraś ca balimantras tathaiva ca ।। pūjito ayaṃ mahāmantraḥ sarvapāpaharaḥ śubhaḥ ।। stuvīdhvaṃ varadaṃ devaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam ।।
punar dvādaśadhā jātaḥ śruto asmābhis tvayoditaḥ ।। saṃbhūto bhāskaro jātas tatra naḥ saṃśayo mahān ।। aditir ditir danuś caiva vinatādyās tathaiva ca ।। aditir janayām āsa devāṃs tribhuvaneśvarān ।।
vinatādyās tathā cānyāḥ suṣuvuḥ sthānujaṅgamān ।। vyāptam etaj jagat sarvaṃ teṣāṃ tāsāṃ ca vai mune ।। sāttvikā rājasāś cānye tāmasāś ca gaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। sraṣṭā brahmavidāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ parameṣṭhī prajāpatiḥ ।।
tato nirākṛtān putrān daiteyair dānavais tathā ।। ācchinad yajñabhāgāṃś ca kṣudhā saṃpīḍitān bhṛśam ।। tuṣṭāva tejasāṃ rāśiṃ gaganasthaṃ divākaram ।। dhāma dhāmavatām īśaṃ dhāmādhāraṃ ca śāśvatam ।।
ādadānasya yad rūpaṃ tīvraṃ tasmai namāmy aham ।। bibhratas tava yad rūpam atitīvraṃ natāsmi tat ।। yad rūpam ṛgyajuḥsāmnām aikyena tapate tava ।। asthūlaṃ sthūlam amalaṃ namas tasmai sanātana ।।
nirāhārā vivasvantam ārirādhayiṣur dvijāḥ ।। pratyakṣatām agāt tasyā dākṣāyaṇyā dvijottamāḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā ca tato devī sādhvasaṃ paramaṃ gatā ।। bhaktānukampaka vibho tvadbhaktān pāhi me sutān ।।
adṛśyata tadādityas taptatāmropamaḥ prabhuḥ ।। prāha bhāsvān vṛṇuṣvaikaṃ varaṃ matto yam icchasi ।। pratyuvāca vivasvantaṃ varadaṃ samupasthitam ।। yajñabhāgāś ca daiteyair dānavaiś ca balādhikaiḥ ।।
aṃśena teṣāṃ bhrātṛtvaṃ gatvā tān nāśaye ripūn ।। bhaveyur adhipāś caiva trailokyasya divākara ।। kuru prasannārtihara kāryaṃ kartā tvam ucyate ।। praṇatām aditiṃ viprāḥ prasādasumukho vibhuḥ ।।
tvatputraśatrūn dakṣo ahaṃ nāśayāmy āśu nirvṛtaḥ ।। nivṛttā sāpi tapasaḥ saṃprāptākhilavāñchitā ।। tataḥ saṃvatsarasyānte tatkāmapūraṇāya saḥ ।। kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādīṃś ca sā cakre susamāhitā ।।
tatas tāṃ kaśyapaḥ prāha kiṃcitkopaplutākṣaram ।। na māritaṃ vipakṣāṇāṃ mṛtyur eva bhaviṣyati ।। jājvalyamānaṃ tejobhiḥ patyur vacanakopitā ।। tuṣṭāva praṇato bhūtvā vāgbhir ādyābhir ādarāt ।।
padmapattrasavarṇābhas tejasā vyāptadiṅmukhaḥ ।। satoyameghagambhīrā vāg uvācāśarīriṇī ।। tasmān mune sutas te ayaṃ mārtaṇḍākhyo bhaviṣyati ।। devā niśamyeti vaco gaganāt samupāgatam ।।
tato yuddhāya daiteyān ājuhāva śatakratuḥ ।। teṣāṃ yuddham abhūd ghoraṃ devānām asuraiḥ saha ।। tasmin yuddhe bhagavatā mārtaṇḍena nirīkṣitāḥ ।। tataḥ praharṣam atulaṃ prāptāḥ sarve divaukasaḥ ।।
svādhikārāṃs tataḥ prāptā yajñabhāgāṃś ca pūrvavat ।। vṛto agnipiṇḍasadṛśo dadhre nātisphuṭaṃ vapuḥ ।। kadambagolakākāraṃ tan me brūhi jagatpate ।। prasādya praṇato bhūtvā viśvakarmā prajāpatiḥ ।।
dvau putrau sumahābhāgau kanyāṃ ca yamunāṃ tathā ।। tenātitāpayām āsa trīṃl lokān sacarācarān ।। asahantī mahat tejaḥ svāṃ chāyāṃ vākyam abravīt ।। nirvikāraṃ tvayātraiva stheyaṃ macchāsanāc chubhe ।।
saṃbhāvyā naiva cākhyeyam idaṃ bhagavate tvayā ।। ākhyāsyāmi mataṃ tubhyaṃ gamyatāṃ yatra vāñchitam ।। vatsarāṇāṃ sahasraṃ tu vasamānā pitur gṛhe ।। āgacchad vaḍavā bhūtvā kurūn athottarāṃs tataḥ ।।
pituḥ samīpaṃ yātāyāṃ saṃjñāyāṃ vākyatatparā ।। tasyāṃ ca bhagavān sūryaḥ saṃjñeyam iti cintayan ।। saṃjñā tu pārthivī teṣām ātmajānāṃ tathākarot ।। manus tat kṣāntavāṃs tasyā yamas tasyā na cakṣame ।।
padā saṃtarjayām āsa na tu dehe nyapātayat ।। tasmāt tavaiṣa caraṇaḥ patiṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। manunā saha dharmātmā pitre sarvaṃ nyavedayat ।। visṛjya jyāyasaṃ bhaktyā kanīyāṃsaṃ bubhūṣati ।।
bālyād vā yadi vā mohāt tad bhavān kṣantum arhasi ।। tato manye na jananīm imāṃ vai tapatāṃ vara ।। mātṛśāpād ayaṃ me adya tathā cintaya gopate ।। yena tvām āviśat krodho dharmajñaṃ dharmaśīlinam ।।
na tu mātrābhiśaptānāṃ kvacic chāpanivartanam ।। kiṃcit te ahaṃ vidhāsyāmi putrasnehād anugraham ।। kṛtaṃ tasyā vacaḥ satyaṃ tvaṃ ca trāto bhaviṣyasi ।। tulyeṣv apy adhikaḥ sneha ekaṃ prati kṛtas tvayā ।।
nirguṇeṣv apy apatyeṣu mātā śāpaṃ na dāsyati ।। kathayām āsa vṛttāntaṃ sa śrutvā śvaśuraṃ yayau ।। nirdagdhukāmaṃ roṣeṇa sāntvayānas tam abravīt ।। asahantī tu tat saṃjñā vane carati vai tapaḥ ।।
rūpārthaṃ bhavato araṇye carantīṃ sumahat tapaḥ ।। rūpaṃ nirvartayāmy adya tava kāntaṃ divaspate ।। tato vivasvato rūpaṃ prāg āsīt parimaṇḍalam ।। bhramim āropya tattejaḥ- śātanāyopacakrame ।।
samudrādrivanopetā tv āruroha mahī nabhaḥ ।। adhogataṃ mahābhāgā babhūvākṣiptam ākulam ।। vyabhidyanta mahāśailāḥ śīrṇasānunibandhanāḥ ।। truṭyadraśminibandhīni bandhanāni adho yayuḥ ।।
vyaśīryanta mahāmeghā ghorārāvavirāviṇaḥ ।। jagad ākulam atyarthaṃ tadāsīn munisattamāḥ ।। devāś ca brahmaṇā sārdhaṃ bhāsvantam abhituṣṭuvuḥ ।। sargasthityantakāleṣu tridhā bhedena tiṣṭhasi ।।
indrādayas tadā devā likhyamānam athāstuvan ।। ṛṣayaś ca tataḥ sapta vasiṣṭhātripurogamāḥ ।। vedoktibhir athāgryābhir vālakhilyāś ca tuṣṭuvuḥ ।। tvaṃ nātha mokṣiṇāṃ mokṣo dhyeyas tvaṃ dhyānināṃ paraḥ ।।
saṃpūjyas tvaṃ tu deveśa śaṃ no astu jagatāṃ pate ।। tato vidyādharagaṇā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ ।। ūcus te vividhā vāco manaḥśrotrasukhāvahāḥ ।। tato hāhāhūhūś caiva nāradas tumburus tathā ।।
ṣaḍjamadhyamagāndhāra- gānatrayaviśāradāḥ ।। viśvācī ca ghṛtācī ca urvaśy atha tilottamāḥ ।। nanṛtur jagatām īśe likhyamāne vibhāvasau ।। prāvādyanta tatas tatra vīṇā veṇvādijharjharāḥ ।।
devadundubhayaḥ śaṅkhāḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। tūryavāditraghoṣaiś ca sarvaṃ kolāhalīkṛtam ।। likhyamānaṃ sahasrāṃśuṃ praṇemuḥ sarvadevatāḥ ।। tejasaḥ śātanaṃ cakre viśvakarmā śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।।
nābhyanandat tu likhanaṃ tatas tenāvatāritaḥ ।। kāntāt kāntataraṃ rūpam adhikaṃ śuśubhe tataḥ ।। rūpaṃ ca paramaṃ tasya mayā saṃparikīrtitam ।। na tṛptim adhigacchāmaḥ śṛṇvantas tāṃ kathāṃ śubhām ।।
etad veditum icchāmaḥ prabhāvo asya kutaḥ prabho ।। prakṛter guṇahetus tu pūrvaṃ buddhir ajāyata ।। vāyvagnir āpaḥ khaṃ bhūmis tatas tv aṇḍam ajāyata ।। pṛthivī saptabhir dvīpaiḥ samudraiś caiva saptabhiḥ ।।
vimūḍhās tāmasāḥ sarve pradhyāyanti tam īśvaram ।। dhyānayogena cāsmābhir vijñātaḥ savitā tadā ।। divyābhiḥ stutibhir devaḥ stuto asmābhis tadeśvaraḥ ।। ādikartāsi bhūtānāṃ devadevo divākaraḥ ।।
munikiṃnarasiddhānāṃ tathaivoragapakṣiṇām ।। vāyur indraś ca somaś ca vivasvān varuṇas tathā ।। saritaḥ sāgarāḥ śailā vidyudindradhanūṃṣi ca ।। īśvarāt parato vidyā vidyāyāḥ parataḥ śivaḥ ।।
sarvataḥpāṇipādāntaḥ sarvatokṣiśiromukhaḥ ।। bhūtādir bhūr bhuvaḥ svaś ca mahaḥ satyaṃ tapo janaḥ ।। durnirīkṣaṃ surendrāṇāṃ yad rūpaṃ tasya te namaḥ ।। stutaṃ paramam avyaktaṃ yad rūpaṃ tasya te namaḥ ।।
sarvadevātidevasya yad rūpaṃ tasya te namaḥ ।। viśvasthitam acintyaṃ ca yad rūpaṃ tasya te namaḥ ।। paramātmety abhikhyātaṃ yad rūpaṃ tasya te namaḥ ।। anādinidhanaṃ caiva yad rūpaṃ tasya te namaḥ ।।
uvāca vācā kalyāṇyā ko varo vaḥ pradīyatām ।। sahanīyaṃ tad bhavatu hitāya jagataḥ prabho ।। lokānāṃ kāryasiddhyarthaṃ gharmavarṣahimapradaḥ ।। dhyāyanti dhyāyino devaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ divākaram ।।
sarvaṃ ca tarate pāpaṃ devam arkaṃ samāśritaḥ ।। bhānor bhaktinamaskāra- kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।। pavitraṃ ca pavitrāṇāṃ prapadyante divākaram ।। sarvakilbiṣanirmuktāḥ sūryalokaṃ vrajanti te ।।
nāmnām aṣṭaśataṃ brūhi yat tvayoktaṃ purā raveḥ ।। bhāskarasya paraṃ guhyaṃ svargamokṣapradaṃ dvijāḥ ।। gabhastimān ajaḥ kālo mṛtyur dhātā prabhākaraḥ ।। somo bṛhaspatiḥ śukro budho aṅgāraka eva ca ।।
brahmā viṣṇuś ca rudraś ca skando vaiśravaṇo yamaḥ ।। dharmadhvajo vedakartā vedāṅgo vedavāhanaḥ ।। kalākāṣṭhāmuhūrtāś ca kṣapā yāmās tathā kṣaṇāḥ ।। puruṣaḥ śāśvato yogī vyaktāvyaktaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।
varuṇaḥ sāgaro aṃśaś ca jīmūto jivano arihā ।। sraṣṭā saṃvartako vahniḥ sarvasyādir alolupaḥ ।। jayo viśālo varadaḥ sarvabhūtaniṣevitaḥ ।। dhanvantarir dhūmaketur ādidevo aditeḥ sutaḥ ।।
svargadvāraṃ prajādvāraṃ mokṣadvāraṃ triviṣṭapam ।। carācarātmā sūkṣmātmā maitreyaḥ karuṇānvitaḥ ।। nāmnām aṣṭaśataṃ ramyaṃ mayā proktaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। umāpriyakaro rudraś candrārdhakṛtaśekharaḥ ।।
gandharvayakṣanāgāṃś ca tathānyāṃś ca samāgatān ।। yajñaṃ samṛddhaṃ ratnāḍhyaṃ sarvasaṃbhārasaṃbhṛtam ।। śāntiṃ na lebhire viprāḥ kailāsaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। pinākapāṇir bhagavān dakṣayajñavināśanaḥ ।।
ekāmrake muniśreṣṭhāḥ sarvakāmaprado haraḥ ।। jaghāna yajñaṃ dakṣasya devaiḥ sarvair alaṃkṛtam ।। śrotum icchāmahe brūhi paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। svebhyo gṛhebhyaś cānīya tāḥ pitābhyarcayad gṛhe ।।
tāsāṃ jyeṣṭhā satī nāma patnī yā tryambakasya vai ।। akarot saṃnatiṃ dakṣe na ca kāṃcin maheśvaraḥ ।। tato jñātvā satī sarvās tās tu prāptāḥ pitur gṛham ।। tato abravīt sā pitaraṃ devī krodhasamākulā ।।
ahaṃ jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā ca māṃ tvaṃ satkartum arhasi ।। evam ukto abravīd enāṃ dakṣaḥ saṃraktalocanaḥ ।। tāsāṃ ye caiva bhartāras te me bahumatāḥ sati ।। guṇaiś caivādhikāḥ ślāghyāḥ sarve te tryambakāt sati ।।
bhṛgur marīciś ca tathā śreṣṭhā jāmātaro mama ।। tena tvāṃ na bubhūṣāmi pratikūlo hi me bhavaḥ ।। tathoktā pitaraṃ sā vai kruddhā devī tam abravīt ।। tasmāt tyajāmy ahaṃ deham imaṃ tāta tavātmajam ।।
abravīd vacanaṃ devī namaskṛtya svayaṃbhuve ।। gaccheyaṃ dharmapatnītvaṃ tryambakasyaiva dhīmataḥ ।। dhārayām āsa cāgneyīṃ dhāraṇām ātmanātmani ।। sarvāṅgebhyo viniḥsṛtya vahnir bhasma cakāra tām ।।
dakṣasya ca vināśāya cukopa bhagavān prabhuḥ ।। praśastāś cetarāḥ sarvās tvatsutā bhartṛbhiḥ saha ।। utpatsyanti dvitīye vai tava yajñe hy ayonijāḥ ।। abhivyāhṛtya saptarṣīn dakṣaṃ so abhyaśapat punaḥ ।।
prācīnabarhiṣaḥ pautraḥ putraś cāpi pracetasaḥ ।। kanyāyāṃ śākhināṃ caiva prāpte vai cākṣuṣāntare ।। dharmakāmārthayukteṣu karmasv iha punaḥ punaḥ ।। tato vai vyāhṛto dakṣo rudraṃ so abhyaśapat punaḥ ।।
tasmāt sārdhaṃ surair yajñe na tvāṃ yakṣyanti vai dvijāḥ ।। tato devais tu te sārdhaṃ na tu pūjā bhaviṣyati ।। na bhokṣye sahitas tais tu tato bhokṣyāmy ahaṃ pṛthak ।। tam ahaṃ dhārayāmy ekaḥ svecchayā na tavājñayā ।।
tasmād ahaṃ vasāmīha satataṃ na tavājñayā ।। svāyaṃbhuvīṃ tanuṃ tyaktvā utpanno mānuṣeṣv iha ।। samasteneha yajñena so ayajad daivataiḥ saha ।। menāyāṃ tām umāṃ devīṃ janayām āsa śailarāṭ ।।
sahavratā bhavasyaiṣā naitayā mucyate bhavaḥ ।। mārīcaṃ kaśyapaṃ devī yathāditir anuvratā ।। viṣṇuṃ kīrtir uṣā sūryaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ cāpy arundhatī ।। evaṃ prācetaso dakṣo jajñe vai cākṣuṣe antare ।।
daśabhyas tu pracetobhyo māriṣāyāṃ punar nṛpa ।। bhṛgvādayas tu te sarve jajñire vai maharṣayaḥ ।। devasya mahato yajñe vāruṇīṃ bibhratas tanum ।। prajāpateś ca dakṣasya tryambakasya ca dhīmataḥ ।।
jantor na bhūtaye khyātis tan na kāryaṃ vijānatā ।। tyaktvā dehaṃ punar jātā girirājagṛhe prabho ।। bhavena saha saṃyogaḥ saṃvādaś ca tayoḥ katham ।। vivāhaś ca jagannātha sarvāścaryasamanvitaḥ ।।
śrotum icchāmahe puṇyāṃ kathāṃ cātimanoharām ।। umāśaṃkarayoḥ puṇyāṃ sarvakāmaphalapradām ।। apṛcchad dhimavān vṛttaṃ loke khyātikaraṃ hitam ।। tathaiva cārcanīyatvaṃ satsu tat kathayasva me ।।
mamākhyātir apatyena brahmaṇā ṛṣibhiḥ saha ।। vartayiṣyāmi yac cāpi yathādṛṣṭaṃ purācala ।। vimānaṃ sunavaṃ divyam anaupamyaṃ mahardhimat ।। tam ahaṃ tapasā jñātvā tatraivāntarhitaḥ sthitaḥ ।।
tīrthābhiṣekapūtātmā pare tapasi saṃsthitaḥ ।। viveśa taṃ tadā deśaṃ sa garto yatra bhūdhara ।। apaśyad ārto duḥkhārtāṃs tān apṛcchac ca sa dvijaḥ ।। duḥkhitāḥ kena mokṣaś ca yuṣmākaṃ bhavitānaghāḥ ।।
prapitāmahāś ca kliśyāmas tava duṣṭena karmaṇā ।। tvaṃ cāpi vīraṇastambas tvayi lambāmahe vayam ।। mṛte tvayi gamiṣyāmo narakaṃ pāpacetasaḥ ।। utpādayasi tenāsmān mucyema vayam enasaḥ ।।
etat kuru mahābuddhe tārayasva pitṝn bhayāt ।। pitṝn gartāt samuddhṛtya gaṇapān pracakāra ha ।। saṃmato balavāṃś caiva rudrasya gaṇapo abhavat ।। utpādayasva śailendra sutāṃ tvaṃ varavarṇinīm ।।
tapaś cakārāpy atulaṃ yena tuṣṭir abhūn mama ।। brūhi tuṣṭo asmi śailendra tapasānena suvrata ।। evaṃ varaṃ prayacchasva yadi tuṣṭo asi me prabho ।। tadā tasmai varaṃ cāhaṃ dattavān manasepsitam ।।
yasyāḥ prabhāvāt sarvatra kīrtim āpsyasi śobhanām ।। pāvanaś caiva puṇyena devānām api sarvataḥ ।। jyeṣṭhā ca sā bhavitrī te anye cātra tataḥ śubhe ।। aparṇām ekaparṇāṃ ca tathā caivaikapāṭalām ।।
aśitvā tv ekaparṇāṃ tu aniketas tapo acarat ।। āhāram ekaparṇaṃ tu ekaparṇā samācarat ।। pūrṇe varṣasahasre tu āhāraṃ tāḥ pracakratuḥ ।। niṣedhayantī co meti mātṛsnehena duḥkhitā ।।
tenaiva nāmnā lokeṣu vikhyātā surapūjitā ।। etāsāṃ tapasāṃ vṛttaṃ yāvad bhūmir dhariṣyati ।। sarvāś caiva mahābhāgās tathā ca sthirayauvanāḥ ।। anugṛhṇanti lokāṃś ca tapasā svena sarvadā ।।
mahāyogabalopetā mahādevam upasthitā ।। āsīt tasyaikaparṇā tu devalaṃ suṣuve sutam ।। putraṃ sā tam alarkasya jaigīṣavyam upasthitā ।। umā tu yā mayā tubhyaṃ kīrtitā varavarṇinī ।।
pradhūpitam ihālakṣya vacas tām aham abravam ।। tvayā sṛṣṭam idaṃ sarvaṃ mā kṛtvā tad vināśaya ।। brūhi kiṃ te jaganmātaḥ prārthitaṃ saṃpratīha naḥ ।। tvam eva tad vijānīṣe tataḥ pṛcchasi kiṃ punaḥ ।।
sa tvāṃ svayam upāgamya ihaiva varayiṣyati ।। vayaṃ sadaiva yasyeme vaśyā vai kiṃkarāḥ śubhe ।। devi śīghreṇa kālena dhūrjaṭir nīlalohitaḥ ।। tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya devā viprā gireḥ sutām ।।
sā devī sūktam ity evam uktvā svasyāśrame śubhe ।। athāgāc candratilakas tridaśārtiharo haraḥ ।। vibhagnanāsiko bhūtvā kubjaḥ keśāntapiṅgalaḥ ।। athomā yogasaṃsiddhā jñātvā śaṃkaram āgatam ।।
tam uvācārghapādyābhyāṃ madhuparkeṇa caiva ha ।। saṃpūjya sumanobhis taṃ brāhmaṇaṃ brāhmaṇapriyā ।। sa prabhur mama dāne vai kanyāhaṃ dvijapuṃgava ।। sa ced dadāti māṃ vipra tubhyaṃ tad ucitaṃ mama ।।
uvāca śailarājānaṃ sutāṃ me yaccha śailarāṭ ।। bhītaḥ śāpāc ca vimanā idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। manīṣitaṃ tu yat pūrvaṃ tac chṛṇuṣva mahāmate ।। varayed yaṃ svayaṃ tatra sa bhartāsyā bhaviṣyati ।।
devyāḥ samīpam āgatya idam āha mahāmanāḥ ।। tatra tvaṃ varayitrī yaṃ sa te bhartā bhaved iti ।। rūpavantaṃ samutsṛjya vṛṇoṣy asadṛśaṃ katham ।। bhāvaṃ ca rudranihitaṃ prasādaṃ manasas tathā ।।
ahaṃ tvāṃ varayiṣyāmi nādbhutaṃ tu kathaṃcana ।। ihaiva tvāṃ mahābhāga varayāmi manogatam ।। skandhe śaṃbhoḥ samādhāya devī prāha vṛto asi me ।। uvāca tam aśokaṃ vai vācā saṃjīvayann iva ।।
tasmāt tvaṃ jarayā tyaktas tv amaraḥ saṃbhaviṣyasi ।। sarvābharaṇapuṣpāḍhyaḥ sarvapuṣpaphalopagaḥ ।। sarvagandhaś ca devānāṃ bhaviṣyasi dṛḍhapriyaḥ ।। āśramaṃ vedam atyarthaṃ citrakūṭeti viśrutam ।।
yas tu tatra mṛtaś cāpi brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। sa devyās tapasā yukto mahāgaṇapatir bhavet ।। antardadhe jagatsraṣṭā sarvabhūtapa īśvaraḥ ।। tata evonmukhī bhūtvā śilāyāṃ saṃbabhūva ha ।।
niśeva candrarahitā na babhau vimanās tadā ।। sarasy udakasaṃpūrṇe samīpe cāśramasya ca ।। krīḍāhetoḥ saromadhye grāhagrasto abhavat tadā ।। tad rūpaṃ saraso madhye kṛtvaivaṃ samabhāṣata ।।
dhik kaṣṭaṃ bāla evāham aprāptārthamanorathaḥ ।। śocāmi na svakaṃ dehaṃ grāhagrastaḥ suduḥkhitaḥ ।। grāhagṛhītaṃ māṃ śrutvā prāptaṃ nidhanam utsukau ।। antargrāheṇa grastas tu yāsyāmi nidhanaṃ kila ।।
utthāya prasthitā tatra yatra tiṣṭhaty asau dvijaḥ ।। grāhasya mukham āpannaṃ vepamānam avasthitam ।। taṃ gṛhītvā drutaṃ yāto madhyaṃ sarasa eva hi ।। athāha devī duḥkhārtā bālaṃ dṛṣṭvā grahāvṛtam ।।
vimuñcemaṃ mahādaṃṣṭra kṣipraṃ bhīmaparākrama ।। sa āhāro mama purā vihito lokakartṛbhiḥ ।। brahmaṇā prerito nūnaṃ nainaṃ mokṣye kathaṃcana ।। tena bālam imaṃ muñca grāharāja namo astu te ।।
yad bravīmi kuru śreṣṭhe tathā mokṣam avāpsyati ।। tat kṛtaṃ nātra saṃdeho yato me brāhmaṇāḥ priyāḥ ।। tat sarvaṃ me prayacchāśu tato mokṣam avāpsyati ।। tat te sarvaṃ mayā dattaṃ bālaṃ muñca mahāgraha ।।
uvāca caivaṃ tuṣṭātmā devīṃ lokasya dhāriṇīm ।। tapaso apy arjanaṃ duḥkhaṃ tasya tyāgo na śasyate ।। sā tv evam uktā grāheṇa uvācedaṃ mahāvratā ।। tapaḥ punar mayā prāpyaṃ na prāpyo brāhmaṇaḥ punaḥ ।।
na viprebhyas tapaḥ śreṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhā me brāhmaṇā matāḥ ।। nahi kaścin naro grāha pradattaṃ punar āharet ।। tvayy eva ramatām etad bālaś cāyaṃ vimucyatām ।। devīm ādityāvabhāsas tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।
svapnalabdha ivārthaughas tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। bhūya eva tapaḥ kartum ārebhe niyamasthitā ।। provāca vacanaṃ viprā mā kṛthās tapa ity uta ।। tat tenaivākṣayaṃ tubhyaṃ bhaviṣyati sahasradhā ।।
svayaṃvaram udīkṣantī tasthau prītā mudā yutā ।। abhavat sa tu kālena śailaputryāḥ svayaṃvaraḥ ।। duhitur devadevena jñātvā tad abhimantritam ।। svayaṃvaraṃ tato devyāḥ sarvalokeṣv aghoṣayat ।।
vṛṇuyāt parameśānaṃ samakṣaṃ yadi me sutā ।। iti saṃcintya śailendraḥ kṛtvā hṛdi maheśvaram ।। kṛtvā ratnākulaṃ deśaṃ svayaṃvaram acīkarat ।। śakrādyair āgatair devaiḥ svayaṃvara upāgate ।।
utsaṅgatalasaṃsupto babhūva sahasā vibhuḥ ।। jñātvā taṃ samavadhyānāj jagṛhe prītisaṃyutā ।। nivṛttā ca tadā tasthau kṛtvā sā hṛdi taṃ vibhum ।। ko ayam atreti saṃmantrya cukruśur bhṛśamohitāḥ ।।
sa bāhur utthitas tasya tathaiva samatiṣṭhata ।। vajraṃ kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka vṛtrahā calituṃ na ca ।। utkṣipya āyudhaṃ dīptaṃ chettum icchan vimohitaḥ ।। balaṃ tejaś ca yogaś ca tathaivāstambhayad vibhuḥ ।।
atha teṣu sthiteṣv evaṃ manyumatsu sureṣu ca ।। buddhavān devadeveśam umotsaṅge samāsthitam ।। vavande caraṇaṃ śaṃbhoḥ stutavāṃs tam ahaṃ dvijāḥ ।। ajas tvam ajaro devaḥ sraṣṭā vibhuḥ parāparam ।।
amṛtaṃ paramātmā ca īśvaraḥ kāraṇaṃ mahat ।। iyaṃ ca prakṛtir devī sadā te sṛṣṭikāraṇam ।। namas tubhyaṃ mahādeva devyā vai sahitāya ca ।। devādyās tu imāḥ sṛṣṭā mūḍhās tvadyogamāyayā ।।
tata evam ahaṃ viprā vijñāpya parameśvaram ।। mūḍhāś ca devatāḥ sarvā nainaṃ budhyata śaṃkaram ।। sārdhaṃ mayaiva deveśaṃ paramātmānam avyayam ।। praṇemur manasā śarvaṃ bhāvaśuddhena cetasā ।।
yathāpūrvaṃ cakārāśu devatānāṃ tanūs tadā ।। vapuś cakāra deveśas tryakṣaṃ paramam adbhutam ।। tebhyaḥ sa paramaṃ cakṣuḥ svavapurdṛṣṭiśaktimat ।। te dṛṣṭvā parameśānaṃ tṛtīyekṣaṇadhāriṇam ।।
tasya devī tadā hṛṣṭā samakṣaṃ tridivaukasām ।। sādhu sādhv iti te hocuḥ sarve devāḥ punar vibhum ।। athāsminn antare viprās tam ahaṃ daivataiḥ saha ।। ślāghyaḥ pūjyaś ca vandyaś ca sarveṣāṃ tvaṃ mahān asi ।।
tataḥ praṇamya himavāṃs tadā māṃ pratyabhāṣata ।। udvāhas tu yadā yādṛk tad vidhatsva pitāmaha ।। udvāhaḥ kriyatāṃ deva ity ahaṃ coktavān vibhum ।। tatkṣaṇāc ca tato viprā asmābhir nirmitaṃ puram ।।
ratnāni maṇayaś citrā hemamauktikam eva ca ।। citrā mārakatī bhūmiḥ suvarṇastambhaśobhitā ।। tasmin dvāri pure ramya udvāhārthaṃ vinirmitā ।। somādityau samaṃ tatra tāpayantau mahāmaṇī ।।
pravavau sukhasaṃsparśo bhavabhaktiṃ pradarśayan ।। devanadyo mahānadyaḥ siddhā munaya eva ca ।। audakāḥ khecarāś cānye kiṃnarā devacāraṇāḥ ।। ramyāṇy ādāya vādyāni tatrājagmus tadā puram ।।
puṇyān vaivāhikān mantrāñ jepuḥ saṃhṛṣṭamānasāḥ ।। gāyanti harṣitāḥ sarvā udvāhe parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। udvāhaḥ śaṃkarasyeti mūrtimanta upasthitāḥ ।। kekāyamānaiḥ śikhibhir nṛtyamānaiś ca sarvaśaḥ ।।
kumudāpīḍaśuklābhir balākābhiś ca śobhitā ।। caladvidyullatāhārā spaṣṭapadmavilocanā ।। haṃsanūpuranihrādā sarvasasyadigantarā ।। praphullendīvaraśyāma- vilocanamanoharā ।।
navaśyāmalatāśyāma- romarājipuraskṛtā ।। prahlādayantī cetāṃsi sarveṣāṃ tridivaukasām ।। calatkumudasaṃghāta- cārukuṇḍalaśobhinī ।। tatpuṣpasaṃcayamayair vāsobhiḥ samalaṃkṛtā ।।
kadalīstambhavāmorūḥ śaśāṅkavadanā tathā ।। premṇā spṛśati kānteva sānurāgā manoramā ।। ṛtū hemantaśiśirau ājagmatur atidyutī ।। prāleyacūrṇavarṣibhyāṃ kṣipraṃ raupyaharo babhau ।।
agādhena tadā reje kṣīroda iva sāgaraḥ ।। sādhūpacārāt sahasā kṛtārtha iva durjanaḥ ।। chattrair iva mahābhāgaiḥ pāṇḍaraiḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। vivāhe gurukanyāyā vasantaḥ samagād ṛtuḥ ।।
tarjayanta ivānyonyaṃ mañjarībhiś cakāśire ।। śuśubhuḥ kāryam uddiśya vṛddhā iva samāgatāḥ ।। kāminya iva kāntānāṃ kaṇṭhālambitabāhavaḥ ।। parasparaṃ hi mālatyo bhāvayantyo virejire ।।
nānāvihaṃgasaṃjuṣṭā haimasopānapaṅktayaḥ ।। samucchritāny aviralair hemānīva babhur dvijāḥ ।। saṃbabhūvur diśaḥ sarvāḥ pavanākampimūrtibhiḥ ।। girau vavṛdhire phullāḥ spardhayantaḥ parasparam ।।
parvatasya nitambeṣu sarveṣu ca virejire ।। nīlajīmūtasaṃghātair nilīnair iva saṃdhiṣu ।। devīvivāhasamaye grīṣma āgād dhimācalam ।। śobhayām āsa śṛṅgāṇi prāleyādreḥ samantataḥ ।।
vavuḥ pāṭalavistīrṇa- kadambārjunagandhinaḥ ।। abhavaṃs taṭasaṃghuṣṭa- phalahaṃsakadambakāḥ ।। sarveṣu nagaśṛṅgeṣu bhramarāvalisevitāḥ ।। utsasarja manojñāni kusumāni samantataḥ ।।
nānāvādyasamākīrṇe ahaṃ tatra dvijātayaḥ ।। puraṃ praveśitavāṃs tāṃ svayam ādāya bho dvijāḥ ।। havir juhomi vahnau te upādhyāyapade sthitaḥ ।। mām āha śaṃkaraś caivaṃ devadevo jagatpatiḥ ।।
kartāsmi vacanaṃ sarvaṃ brahmaṃs tava jagadvibho ।। hastaṃ devasya devyāś ca yogabandhena yuktavān ।। śrutigītair mahāmantrair mūrtimadbhir upasthitaiḥ ।। tatas taṃ jvalanaṃ sarvaṃ kārayitvā pradakṣiṇam ।।
putraiś ca mānasaiḥ siddhaiḥ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā ।। yogenaiva tayor viprās tad umāparameśayoḥ ।। udvāhaś caiva devasya śṛṇudhvaṃ paramādbhutam ।। tuṣṭuvur vāgbhir ādyābhiḥ praṇemus te maheśvaram ।।
namaḥ kleśavināśāya dātre ca śubhasaṃpadām ।। namaḥ pavanarūpāya śatarūpāya vai namaḥ ।। namaḥ sahasranetrāya sahasracaraṇāya ca ।। viṣṭambhanāya śakrasya bāhvor vedāṅkurāya ca ।।
salilāśayaliṅgāya yugāntāya namo namaḥ ।। namaḥ kapālahastāya daṇḍine gadine namaḥ ।। namaḥ khaṭvāṅgahastāya pramathārtiharāya ca ।। bhaganetranipātāya pūṣṇo dantaharāya ca ।।
namo astu kālakālāya tṛtīyanayanāya ca ।। suvarṇaretase caiva namaḥ kuṇḍaladhāriṇe ।। śaśāṅkādityanetrāya lalāṭanayanāya ca ।। namo daivatanāthāya tryambakāya namo namaḥ ।।
namo muṇḍārdhamuṇḍāya paśūnāṃ pataye namaḥ ।। namaḥ śāntāya dāntāya pralayotpattikāriṇe ।। namo rudrāya vasava ādityāyāśvine namaḥ ।। namaḥ śarvāya ugrāya śivāya varadāya ca ।।
śucaye vairihānāya sadyojātāya vai namaḥ ।। pradhānāyāprameyāya kāryāya kāraṇāya ca ।। namaḥ puruṣasaṃyoga- pradhānaguṇakāriṇe ।। kṛtākṛtasya satkartre phalasaṃyogadāya ca ।।
namo vaiṣamyakartre ca guṇānāṃ vṛttidāya ca ।। śiva saumyamukho draṣṭuṃ bhava saumyo hi naḥ prabho ।। stūyamānaḥ suraiḥ sarvair amarān idam abravīt ।। varaṃ varayata kṣipraṃ dātāsmi tam asaṃśayam ।।
tatas te praṇatāḥ sarve surā ūcus trilocanam ।। yadā kāryaṃ tadā nas tvaṃ dāsyase varam īpsitam ।। lokāṃś ca pramathaiḥ sārdhaṃ viveśa bhavanaṃ svakam ।। sa sarvalokago devaiḥ pūjyate amararāḍ iva ।।
sa vakro manmathaḥ krūro devaṃ veddhumanā bhavat ।। lokān sarvān pīḍayantaṃ sarvāṅgāvaraṇātmakam ।। cakrāhvayasya rūpeṇa ratyā saha samāgatam ।। nayanena tṛtīyena sāvajñaṃ samavaikṣata ।।
sahasā ratibhartāram adahat saparicchadam ।। prasādayaṃś ca taṃ devaṃ papāta dharaṇītale ।। papāta sahasā mūrchāṃ kṣaṇena samapadyata ।। devīṃ devaṃ ca duḥkhārtā ayācat karuṇāvatī ।।
ūcatus tāṃ samālokya samāśvāsya ca duḥkhitām ।। aśarīro api te bhadre kāryaṃ sarvaṃ kariṣyati ।। tadā tasya suto yaś ca patis te saṃbhaviṣyati ।। jagāmeṣṭaṃ tadā deśaṃ prītiyuktā gataklamā ।।
reme tatromayā sārdhaṃ prahṛṣṭas tu himācale ।। nirjhareṣu ca ramyeṣu karṇikāravaneṣu ca ।। śṛṅgeṣu śailarājasya taḍāgeṣu saraḥsu ca ।। tīrtheṣu puṇyatoyeṣu munīnām āśrameṣu ca ।।
akarot kiṃ mahādeva etad icchāma veditum ।। gaṇeśair vividhākārair hāsaṃ saṃjanayan muhuḥ ।। mahānubhāvaiḥ sarvajñaiḥ kāmarūpadharaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। āsīnāṃ kāñcane śubhra āsane paramādbhute ।।
āsīnāṃ tām athovāca menā himavataḥ priyā ।। daridrā krīḍanais tvaṃ hi bhartrā krīḍasi saṃgatā ।। ume ta evaṃ krīḍanti yathā tava patiḥ śubhe ।। visṛṣṭā ca tadā mātrā gatvā devam uvāca ha ।।
anyaṃ kuru mamāvāsaṃ bhuvaneṣu mahādyute ।। anyaṃ na rocitavatī vāsaṃ vai devi karhicit ।। kasmān mṛgayase devi brūhi tan me śucismite ।। dṛṣṭvā ca tatra me mātā vijane lokabhāvane ।।
ume tava sadā bhartā daridraḥ krīḍanaiḥ śubhe ।। ramase tad aniṣṭaṃ hi mama mātur vṛṣadhvaja ।। tato devaḥ prahasyāha devīṃ hāsayituṃ prabhuḥ ।। kṛttivāsā hy avāsāś ca śmaśānanilayaś ca ha ।।
vicarāmi gaṇair nagnair vṛto ambhojavilocane ।। nahi mātṛsamo bandhur jantūnām asti bhūtale ।। tathā kuru mahādeva yathāhaṃ sukham āpnuyām ।। vināśam agamad brahman hayamedhaḥ prajāpateḥ ।।
mahādevena roṣād vai tan naḥ prabrūhi vistarāt ।। krodhād vidhvaṃsito yajño devyāḥ priyacikīrṣayā ।। jyotiḥsthalaṃ nāma citraṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitam ।। tatra devo giritaṭe sarvadhātuvicitrite ।।
śailarājasutā cāsya nityaṃ pārśvasthitābhavat ।। tathaiva ca mahātmānāv aśvinau bhiṣajāṃ varau ।। yakṣāṇām īśvaraḥ śrīmān kailāsanilayaḥ prabhuḥ ।। sanatkumārapramukhās tathaiva paramarṣayaḥ ।।
viśvāvasuś ca gandharvas tathā nāradaparvatau ।। vavau sukhaśivo vāyur nānāgandhavahaḥ śuciḥ ।। tathā vidyādharāḥ sādhyāḥ siddhāś caiva tapodhanāḥ ।। bhūtāni ca tathānyāni nānārūpadharāṇy atha ।।
bahurūpadharā dhṛṣṭā nānāpraharaṇāyudhāḥ ।। nandīśvaraś ca bhagavān devasyānumate sthitaḥ ।। gaṅgā ca saritāṃ śreṣṭhā sarvatīrthajalodbhavā ।। evaṃ sa bhagavāṃs tatra pūjyamānaḥ surarṣibhiḥ ।।
kasyacit tv atha kālasya dakṣo nāma prajāpatiḥ ।। tatas tasya makhe devāḥ sarve śakrapurogamāḥ ।। te vimānair mahātmāno jvaladbhir jvalanaprabhāḥ ।। gandharvāpsarasākīrṇaṃ nānādrumalatāvṛtam ।।
pṛthivyām antarikṣe ca ye ca svarlokavāsinaḥ ।। ādityā vasavo rudrāḥ sādhyāḥ sarve marudgaṇāḥ ।। ūṣmapā dhūmapāś caiva ājyapāḥ somapās tathā ।। ete cānye ca bahavo bhūtagrāmās tathaiva ca ।।
āgatāḥ sattriṇaḥ sarve devāḥ strībhiḥ saharṣibhiḥ ।। tān dṛṣṭvā manyunāviṣṭo dadhīcir vākyam abravīt ।। naraḥ pāpam avāpnoti mahad vai nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। evam uktvā tu viprarṣiḥ punar dakṣam abhāṣata ।।
pūjyaṃ ca paśubhartāraṃ kasmān nārcayase prabhum ।। ekādaśasthānagatā nānyaṃ vidmo maheśvaram ।। tathā dakṣasya vipulo yajño ayaṃ na bhaviṣyati ।। uvāca vacanaṃ śarvaṃ devaṃ paśupatiṃ patim ।।
brūhi tattvena tattvajña saṃśayo me mahān ayam ।। hayamedhena yajate tatra yānti divaukasaḥ ।। kena vā pratiṣedhena gamanaṃ te na vidyate ।। yajñeṣu mama sarveṣu na bhāga upakalpitaḥ ।।
na me surāḥ prayacchanti bhāgaṃ yajñasya dharmataḥ ।। ajeyaś cāpy adhṛṣyaś ca tejasā yaśasā śriyā ।। atīva duḥkham āpannā vepathuś ca mahān ayam ।। stauṣi garvāyase cāpi svam ātmānaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।।
saṃsrakṣyāmi varārohe bhāgārthe varavarṇini ।। so asṛjad bhagavān vaktrād bhūtaṃ krodhāgnisaṃbhavam ।। nāśayāśu kratuṃ tasya dakṣasya madanujñayā ।। devyā manyukṛtaṃ jñātvā hato dakṣasya sa kratuḥ ।।
ātmanaḥ karmasākṣitve tena sārdhaṃ sahānugā ।। vīrabhadreti vikhyāto devyā manyupramārjakaḥ ।। rudrānugān gaṇān raudrān rudravīryaparākramān ।। te nipetus tatas tūrṇaṃ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।।
samabhūt sumahān viprāḥ sarvarudragaṇaiḥ kṛtaḥ ।। parvatāś ca vyaśīryanta cakampe ca vasuṃdharā ।। agnayo vai na dīpyante na cādīpyata bhāskaraḥ ।। ṛṣayo na prabhāsante na devā na ca dānavāḥ ।।
prabhañjanty apare yūpān ghorān utpāṭayanti ca ।। tvaritaṃ vai pradhāvanti vāyuvegā manojavāḥ ।। śīryamāṇāny adṛśyanta tārā iva nabhastalāt ।। kṣīranadyas tathā cānyā ghṛtapāyasakardamāḥ ।।
ṣaḍrasān nivahanty anyā guḍakulyā manoramāḥ ।। yāni kāni ca divyāni lehyacoṣyāṇi yāni ca ।। rudrakopā mahākopāḥ kālāgnisadṛśopamāḥ ।। krīḍanti vividhākārāś cikṣipuḥ surayoṣitaḥ ।।
rudrakopaprayuktaś ca sarvadevaiḥ surakṣitam ।। cakrur anye tathā nādān sarvabhūtabhayaṃkarān ।। ūcuḥ prāñjalayo bhūtvā kathyatāṃ ko bhavān iti ।। naiva draṣṭuṃ ca devendrā na ca kautūhalānvitāḥ ।।
vīrabhadreti vikhyāto rudrakopād viniḥsṛtaḥ ।। preṣitā devadevena yajñāntikam upāgatā ।। varaṃ krodho api devasya na varaḥ paricārakaiḥ ।। utpatadbhiḥ patadbhiś ca gṛdhrair āmiṣagṛdhnubhiḥ ।।
sa tasya yajño nṛpater bādhyamānas tadā gaṇaiḥ ।। taṃ tu yajñaṃ tathārūpaṃ gacchantam upalabhya saḥ ।। tatas tasya gaṇeśasya krodhād amitatejasaḥ ।। tasmin patitamātre ca svedabindau tadā bhuvi ।।
tatrodapadyata tadā puruṣo dvijasattamāḥ ।। ūrdhvakeśo atiromāṅgaḥ śoṇakarṇas tathaiva ca ।। taṃ yajñaṃ sa mahāsattvo adahat kakṣam ivānalaḥ ।। tena tasmin vicaratā vikrameṇa tadā tu vai ।।
mahābhūte pravṛtte tu devalokabhayaṃkare ।। bhavate api surāḥ sarve bhāgaṃ dāsyanti vai prabho ।। imāś ca devatāḥ sarvā ṛṣayaś ca sahasraśaḥ ।। yaś caiṣa puruṣo jātaḥ svedajas te surarṣabha ।।
ekībhūtasya na hy asya dhāraṇe tejasaḥ prabho ।। ity uktaḥ sa mayā devo bhāge cāpi prakalpite ।। parāṃ ca prītim agamat sa svayaṃ ca pinākadhṛk ।। prāṇāpānau samārudhya cakṣuḥsthāne prayatnataḥ ।।
smitaṃ kṛtvābravīd vākyaṃ brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi te ।। bhītaḥ śaṅkitacittas tu sabāṣpavadanekṣaṇaḥ ।। yadi cāham anugrāhyo yadi deyo varo mama ।। cūrṇīkṛtāpaviddhaṃ ca yajñasaṃbhāram īdṛśam ।।
na ca mithyā bhaven mahyaṃ tvatprasādān maheśvara ।। dharmādhyakṣaṃ mahādevaṃ tryambakaṃ ca prajāpatiḥ ।। nāmnāṃ cāṣṭasahasreṇa stutavān vṛṣabhadhvajam ।। prāñjaliḥ praṇato bhūtvā saṃstotum upacakrame ।।
devendra tvaṃ balaśreṣṭha devadānavapūjita ।। sarvataḥpāṇipādas tvaṃ sarvatokṣiśiromukhaḥ ।। śaṅkukarṇo mahākarṇaḥ kumbhakarṇo arṇavālayaḥ ।। śatodaraḥ śatāvartaḥ śatajihvaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।
devadānavagoptā ca brahmā ca tvaṃ śatakratuḥ ।। tvayi sarvā devatā hi gāvo goṣṭha ivāsate ।। ādityam atha viṣṇuṃ ca brahmāṇaṃ sabṛhaspatim ।। asac ca sadasac caiva tathaiva prabhavāvyayau ।।
paśūnāṃ pataye caiva namo astv andhakaghātine ।। tryambakāya trinetrāya tripuraghnāya vai namaḥ ।। daṇḍine śaṅkukarṇāya daṇḍidaṇḍāya vai namaḥ ।। vilohitāya dhūmrāya nīlagrīvāya vai namaḥ ।।
sūryāya sūryapataye sūryadhvajapatākine ।। namo hiraṇyagarbhāya hiraṇyakavacāya ca ।। śatrughātāya caṇḍāya parṇasaṃghaśayāya ca ।। sarvāya sarvabhakṣāya sarvabhūtāntarātmane ।।
namo anamyāya namyāya namaḥ kilakilāya ca ।। sthitāya dhāvamānāya kubjāya kuṭilāya ca ।। bādhāpahāya lubdhāya gītavāditrakāriṇe ।। ugrāya ca namo nityaṃ namaś ca daśabāhave ।।
vibhīṣaṇāya bhīmāya bhīṣmavratadharāya ca ।। pakṣamāsalavārdhāya tumbīvīṇāpriyāya ca ।। namaḥ śivāya śāntāya namaḥ śāntatamāya ca ।। pavanāya pataṃgāya namaḥ sāṃkhyaparāya ca ।।
sahasraśataghaṇṭāya ghaṇṭāmālāpriyāya ca ।। hūṃhūṃkārāya rudrāya bhagākārapriyāya ca ।। namo yajñādhipataye bhūtāya prasutāya ca ।। namas taṭāya taṭyāya taṭinīpataye namaḥ ।।
namaḥ sahasraśīrṣāya sahasracaraṇāya ca ।। namo bālārkavarṇāya bālarūpadharāya ca ।। namaḥ śuddhāya buddhāya kṣobhaṇāya kṣayāya ca ।। namaḥ ṣaṭkarmaniṣṭhāya trikarmaniyatāya ca ।।
namaḥ śreṣṭhāya jyeṣṭhāya namaḥ kalakalāya ca ।। dharmakāmārthamokṣāya krathāya krathanāya ca ।। namo rathyādhirathyāya catuṣpathapathāya ca ।। īśāna rudrasaṃghāta harikeśa namo astu te ।।
kālakāmadakāmaghna duṣṭodvṛttaniṣūdana ।। unmādana śatāvarta- gaṅgātoyārdramūrdhaja ।। namo annadānakartre ca annadaprabhave namaḥ ।। jarāyujāṇḍajāś caiva svedajodbhijja eva ca ।।
carācarasya sraṣṭā tvaṃ pratihartā tvam eva ca ।। sarvasya paramā yoniḥ sudhāṃśo jyotiṣāṃ nidhiḥ ।। hāyi hāyi hare hāyi huvāhāveti vāsakṛt ।। yajurmaya ṛṅmayaś ca sāmātharvayutas tathā ।।
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā varṇāśramāś ca ye ।। saṃvatsaras tvam ṛtavo māsā māsārdham eva ca ।। vṛṣāṇāṃ kakudaṃ tvaṃ hi girīṇāṃ śikharāṇi ca ।। kṣīrodo hy udadhīnāṃ ca mantrāṇāṃ praṇavas tathā ।।
tvam evecchā ca dveṣaś ca rāgo mohaḥ śamaḥ kṣamā ।। tvaṃ gadī tvaṃ śarī cāpī khaṭvāṅgī mudgarī tathā ।। daśalakṣaṇasaṃyukto dharmo arthaḥ kāma eva ca ।। latāvallyas tṛṇauṣadhyaḥ paśavo mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ ।।
ādiś cāntaś ca madhyaś ca gāyatry oṃkāra eva ca ।। kadruś ca kapilo babhruḥ kapoto macchakas tathā ।। suvarṇanāmā ca tathā suvarṇapriya eva ca ।। utphullaś citrabhānuś ca svarbhānur bhānur eva ca ।।
trisauparṇas tathā brahman yajuṣāṃ śatarudriyam ।। prāṇaś ca tvaṃ rajaś ca tvaṃ tamaḥ sattvayutas tathā ।। unmeṣaś ca nimeṣaś ca kṣuttṛṅjṛmbhā tathaiva ca ।। śuciromā haricchmaśrur ūrdhvakeśaś calācalaḥ ।।
matsyo jālo jalo ajayyo jalavyālaḥ kuṭīcaraḥ ।। mṛtyuś caivākṣayo antaś ca kṣamāmāyākarotkaraḥ ।। ghaṇṭākī ghaṇṭakī ghaṇṭī cūḍālo lavaṇodadhiḥ ।। caturyugaś caturvedaś caturhotraś catuṣpathaḥ ।।
kṣarākṣaraḥ priyo dhūrto gaṇair gaṇyo gaṇādhipaḥ ।। śilpīśaḥ śilpinaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvaśilpipravartakaḥ ।। svāhā svadhā vaṣaṭkāro namaskāra namo astu te ।। taraṇas tāraṇaś caiva sarvabhūteṣu tāraṇaḥ ।।
tapo brahma ca satyaṃ ca brahmacaryaṃ tathārjavam ।। bhūr bhuvaḥ svaritaś caiva bhūto hy agnir maheśvaraḥ ।। kāmabimbavinirhantā karṇikārasrajapriyaḥ ।। trailokyagoptā govindo goptā gogarga eva ca ।।
caturmukho bahumukho raṇeṣv abhimukhaḥ sadā ।। adharmahā mahādakṣo daṇḍadhāro raṇapriyaḥ ।। durvāraṇo durviṣaho duḥsaho duratikramaḥ ।। śaśaḥ śaśāṅkanayana- śītoṣṇaḥ kṣut tṛṣā jarā ।।
sahyo yajñamṛgavyādho vyādhīnām ākaro akaraḥ ।। daṇḍadhṛk cakradaṇḍaś ca raudrabhāgavināśanaḥ ।। madhupaś cāpapaś caiva sarvapaś ca balābalaḥ ।। vṛṣabhaś caiva vikhyāto lokānāṃ lokasaṃskṛtaḥ ।।
agniṣṭomas tathā deho dharmakarmaprasādhitaḥ ।। māhātmyaṃ vedituṃ śaktā yāthātathyena te śiva ।। tābhir māṃ sarvato rakṣa pitā putram ivaurasam ।। bhaktānukampī bhagavān bhaktaś cāhaṃ sadā tvayi ।।
tiṣṭhaty ekaḥ samudrānte sa me goptāstu nityaśaḥ ।। jyotiḥ paśyanti yuñjānās tasmai yogātmane namaḥ ।। yaḥ śete jalamadhyasthas taṃ prapadye ambuśāyinam ।। grasaty arkaṃ ca svarbhānur bhūtvā somāgnir eva ca ।।
rakṣantu te ca māṃ nityaṃ nityaṃ cāpyāyayantu mām ।। teṣāṃ svāhā svadhā caiva āpnuvanti svadanti ca ।। harṣayanti na kṛṣyanti namas tebhyas tu nityaśaḥ ।। vṛkṣamūleṣu goṣṭheṣu kāntāragahaneṣu ca ।।
hastyaśvarathaśālāsu jīrṇodyānālayeṣu ca ।। indrārkayor madhyagatā ye ca candrārkaraśmiṣu ।। namas tebhyo namas tebhyo namas tebhyas tu sarvaśaḥ ।। sarvabhūtāntarātmā ca tena tvaṃ na nimantritaḥ ।।
tvam eva kartā sarvasya tena tvaṃ na nimantritaḥ ।। tasmāt tu kāraṇād vāpi tvaṃ mayā na nimantritaḥ ।। tvaṃ gatis tvaṃ pratiṣṭhā ca na cānyo astīti me matiḥ ।। bhagavān api suprītaḥ punar dakṣam abhāṣata ।।
bahunā tu kim uktena matsamīpaṃ gamiṣyasi ।। kṛtvāśvāsakaraṃ vākyaṃ sarvajño vākyasaṃhitam ।। ahaṃ yajñahanas tubhyaṃ dṛṣṭam etat purānagha ।। prasannasumukho bhūtvā mamaikāgramanāḥ śṛṇu ।।
prajāpate matprasādāt phalabhāgī bhaviṣyasi ।। tapaś ca vipulaṃ taptvā duścaraṃ devadānavaiḥ ।। varṇāśramakṛtair dharmair vinītaṃ na kvacit kvacit ।। sarveṣām āśramāṇāṃ ca mayā pāśupataṃ vratam ।।
tac cāstu sumahābhāga mānasas tyajyatāṃ jvaraḥ ।। adarśanam anuprāpto dakṣasyāmitatejasaḥ ।। jvaraṃ ca sarvadharmajño bahudhā vyabhajat tadā ।। śikhābhitāpo nāgānāṃ parvatānāṃ śilājatu ।।
khorakaḥ saurabheyāṇām ūkharaḥ pṛthivītale ।। randhrāgatam athāśvānāṃ śikhodbhedaś ca barhiṇām ।। janānām api bhedaś ca sarveṣām iti naḥ śrutam ।। śārdūleṣv atha vai viprāḥ śramo jvara ihocyate ।।
maraṇe janmani tathā madhye cāpi niveśitaḥ ।। namasyaś caiva mānyaś ca sarvaprāṇibhir īśvaraḥ ।। nāśubhaṃ prāpnuyāt kiṃcid dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt ।। tathā stavo variṣṭho ayaṃ stavānāṃ dakṣanirmitaḥ ।।
stotavyo bhaktim āsthāya vidyākāmaiś ca yatnataḥ ।। rājakāryaniyukto vā mucyate mahato bhayāt ।। iha loke sukhaṃ prāpya gaṇarāḍ upajāyate ।। kuryur vighnaṃ gṛhe tasya yatra saṃstūyate bhavaḥ ।।
pitṛpakṣe bhartṛpakṣe pūjyā bhavati caiva ha ।। tasya sarvāṇi kāryāṇi siddhiṃ gacchanty avighnataḥ ।। sarvaṃ saṃpadyate tasya stavasyāsyānukīrtanāt ।। baliṃ vibhajataḥ kṛtvā damena niyamena ca ।।
īpsitāṃl labhate apy arthān kāmān bhogāṃś ca mānavaḥ ।। sarvakāmasuyukto vā yukto vā sarvapātakaiḥ ।। mṛtaś ca gaṇasāyujyaṃ pūjyamānaḥ surāsuraiḥ ।। ābhūtasaṃplavasthāyī rudrasyānucaro bhavet ।।
naitad vedayate kaścin naitac chrāvyaṃ ca kasyacit ।। vaiśyāḥ striyaś ca śūdrāś ca rudralokam avāpnuyuḥ ।। rudralokam avāpnoti dvijo vai nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। rudrakrodhodbhavāṃ puṇyāṃ vyāsasya vadato dvijāḥ ।।
utpattiṃ vīrabhadrasya bhadrakālyāś ca saṃbhavam ।। punaḥ prasādaṃ devasya dakṣasya sumahātmanaḥ ।। hṛṣṭā babhūvuḥ saṃprītā vismitāś ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। pṛṣṭaḥ provāca tān vyāsaḥ kṣetram ekāmrakaṃ punaḥ ।।
praśaśaṃsus tadā hṛṣṭā romāñcitatanūruhāḥ ।। dakṣasya ca suraśreṣṭha yajñavidhvaṃsanaṃ tathā ।। śrotum icchāmahe brahman paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। provāca śaṃbhos tat kṣetraṃ bhūtale duṣkṛtacchadam ।।
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ kṣetraṃ paramadurlabham ।। ekāmraketi vikhyātaṃ tīrthāṣṭakasamanvitam ।। nāmnā tasyaiva tat kṣetram ekāmrakam iti śrutam ।। vidvāṃsagaṇa bhūyiṣṭhaṃ dhanadhānyādisaṃyutam ।।
nānāvaṇiksamākīrṇaṃ nānāratnopaśobhitam ।। rājahaṃsanibhaiḥ śubhraiḥ prāsādair upaśobhitam ।। rakṣitaṃ śastrasaṃghaiś ca parikhābhir alaṃkṛtam ।। samīraṇoddhatābhiś ca patākābhir alaṃkṛtam ।।
vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgaiś ca kṣepaṇībhir alaṃkṛtam ।। pūjāvicitraracitaiḥ sarvatra samalaṃkṛtam ।। hārair alaṃkṛtagrīvāḥ padmapattrāyatekṣaṇāḥ ।। sthirālakāḥ sukapolāḥ kāñcīnūpuranāditāḥ ।।
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। haṃsavāraṇagāminyaḥ kucabhārāvanāmitāḥ ।। madālasāś ca suśroṇyo nityaṃ prahasitānanāḥ ।। tāmbūlarañjitamukhā vidagdhāḥ priyadarśanāḥ ।।
divyavastradharāḥ sarvāḥ sadā cāritramaṇḍitāḥ ।। sve sve gṛhe pramuditā divā rātrau varānanāḥ ।। sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ sumṛṣṭamaṇikuṇḍalāḥ ।। svadharmaniratās tatra nivasanti sudhārmikāḥ ।।
ghṛtācīmenakātulyās tathā samatilottamāḥ ।। viśvācīsahajanyābhāḥ pramlocāsadṛśās tathā ।। kalākauśalasaṃyuktāḥ sarvās tā guṇasaṃyutāḥ ।। nivasanti muniśreṣṭhāḥ sarvastrīguṇagarvitāḥ ।।
na rūpahīnā durvṛttā na paradrohakārikāḥ ।। na tatra nirdhanāḥ santi na mūrkhā na paradviṣaḥ ।। na rūpahīnā durvṛttā na paradrohakāriṇaḥ ।। sarvatra sukhasaṃcāraṃ sarvasattvasukhāvaham ।।
karṇikāraiś ca panasaiś campakair nāgakesaraiḥ ।। cūtanimbakadambaiś ca tathānyaiḥ puṣpajātibhiḥ ।। śālais tālais tamālaiś ca nārikelaiḥ śubhāñjanaiḥ ।। lakucaiḥ saralair lodhrair hintālair devadārubhiḥ ।।
kadalīvanakhaṇḍaiś ca jambūpūgaphalais tathā ।। mandārakundapuṣpaiś ca tathānyaiḥ puṣpajātibhiḥ ।। phalabhārānatair vṛkṣaiḥ sarvartukusumotkaraiḥ ।। kalaviṅkair mayūraiś ca priyaputraiḥ śukais tathā ।।
nānāpakṣigaṇaiś cānyaiḥ kūjadbhir madhurasvaraiḥ ।। nānājalāśayaiś cānyaiḥ padminīkhaṇḍamaṇḍitaiḥ ।। kādambaiś cakravākaiś ca tathaiva jalakukkuṭaiḥ ।। evaṃ nānāvidhair vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpair nānāvidhair varaiḥ ।।
āste tatra svayaṃ devaḥ kṛttivāsā vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।। pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni saritaś ca sarāṃsi ca ।। tebhyaḥ pūrvaṃ samāhṛtya jalabindūn pṛthak pṛthak ।। tīrthaṃ bindusaro nāma tasmin kṣetre dvijottamāḥ ।।
aṣṭamyāṃ bahule pakṣe mārgaśīrṣe dvijottamāḥ ।। vidhivad bindusarasi snātvā śraddhāsamanvitaḥ ।। tilodakena vidhinā nāmagotravidhānavit ।। grahoparāge viṣuve saṃkrāntyām ayane tathā ।।
ye tatra dānaṃ viprebhyaḥ prayacchanti dhanādikam ।। piṇḍaṃ ye saṃprayacchanti pitṛbhyaḥ sarasas taṭe ।। tataḥ śaṃbhor gṛhaṃ gatvā vāgyataḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ ।। ghṛtakṣīrādibhiḥ snānaṃ kārayitvā bhavaṃ śuciḥ ।।
tataḥ saṃpūjayed devaṃ candramaulim umāpatim ।। āgamoktena mantreṇa vedoktena ca śaṃkaram ।। evaṃ saṃpūjya taṃ devaṃ gandhapuṣpānurāgibhiḥ ।। daṇḍavatpraṇipātaiś ca gītair vādyair manoharaiḥ ।।
evaṃ saṃpūjya vidhivad devadevam umāpatim ।। kulaikaviṃśam uddhṛtya divyābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। upagīyamāno gandharvair apsarobhir alaṃkṛtaḥ ।। bhuktvā tatra sukhaṃ viprā manasaḥ prītidāyakam ।।
tatas tasmād ihāyātaḥ pṛthivyāṃ puṇyasaṃkṣaye ।। yogaṃ pāśupataṃ prāpya tato mokṣam avāpnuyāt ।। aśokākhyāṃ tathāṣṭamyāṃ pavitrāropaṇe tathā ।। vimānenārkavarṇena śivalokaṃ vrajanti te ।।
te api pāpavinirmuktāḥ śivalokaṃ vrajanti vai ।। yojanadvitayaṃ sārdhaṃ kṣetraṃ tad bhuktimuktidam ।। paśyanti ye tu taṃ devaṃ snātvā kuṇḍe maheśvaram ।। sarvapāpavinirmuktā vimānavaram āsthitāḥ ।।
tiṣṭhanti tatra muditāḥ kalpam ekaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। puṇyakṣayād ihāyātā jāyante pravare kule ।। utpadyante dvijavarāḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ ।। yogaṃ śaṃbhor varaṃ prāpya tato mokṣaṃ vrajanti te ।।
pūjyāpūjyaṃ ca sarvatra vane rathyāntare api vā ।। dṛṣṭvā tal liṅgam avyagraḥ śraddhayā susamāhitaḥ ।। dhūpair dīpaiḥ sanaivedyair namaskārais tathā stavaiḥ ।। saṃpūjyaivaṃ vidhānena śivalokaṃ vrajen naraḥ ।।
pūrvoktaṃ phalam āpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। tasya kṣetravarasyātha ṛte devān maheśvarāt ।। mādhavādiṣu māseṣu naro vā yadi vāṅganā ।। paśyed devaṃ virūpākṣaṃ devīṃ ca varadāṃ śivām ।।
kalpadrumaṃ ca sāvitrīṃ śivalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। prāpnoty abhimatān kāmāñ śivalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। kulaikaviṃśam uddhṛtya śivalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। snānaṃ karoti yas tatra mokṣaṃ sa labhate dhruvam ।।
yasyāḥ saṃdarśanān martyaḥ punāty āsaptamaṃ kulam ।। naraḥ svavaṃśam uddhṛtya mama lokaṃ sa gacchati ।। sarvapāpaharā devyo varadā bhaktivatsalāḥ ।। yasyāṃ snātvā naraśreṣṭhaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।
dṛṣṭvā praṇamya taṃ bhaktyā paraṃ viṣṇuṃ vrajanti te ।। mṛtyuṃjaye kroḍatīrthe vāsuke siddhakeśvare ।। gatvāṣṭatīrthaṃ vidhivat snātvā devān praṇamya ca ।। upagīyamāno gandharvair mama loke mahīyate ।।
sa karoty akṣayāṃ tṛptiṃ pitṝṇāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। parityajanti puruṣās te mokṣaṃ prāpnuvanti vai ।। paśyed devīṃ ca vārāhīṃ sa yāti tridaśālayam ।। tatkāle tu muniśreṣṭhā veditavyāni tāni vai ।।
āste guhyaṃ paraṃ kṣetraṃ muktidaṃ pāpanāśanam ।। daśayojanavistīrṇaṃ kṣetraṃ paramadurlabham ।। panasair nārikelaiś ca śālais tālaiḥ kapitthakaiḥ ।। kadambaiḥ kovidāraiś ca lakucair nāgakesaraiḥ ।।
sarjabhūrjāśvakarṇaiś ca tamālair devadārubhiḥ ।। kharjūrāmrātakaiḥ siddhair mucukundaiḥ sakiṃśukaiḥ ।। śiṃśapāmalakair nīpair nimbatinduvibhītakaiḥ ।। manohlādakaraiḥ śubhrair nānāvihaganāditaiḥ ।।
manasaḥ prītijanakaiḥ śabdaiḥ khagamukheritaiḥ ।। kokilaiḥ kalaviṅkaiś ca hārītair jīvajīvakaiḥ ।। śrotraramyaiḥ priyakaraiḥ kūjadbhiś cārvadhiṣṭhitaiḥ ।। mālatīkundabāṇaiś ca karavīraiḥ sitetaraiḥ ।।
mātuluṅgaiḥ pūgaphalair hintālaiḥ kadalīvanaiḥ ।। latāvitānagulmaiś ca vividhaiś ca jalāśayaiḥ ।। nānājalāśayaiḥ puṇyaiḥ padminīkhaṇḍamaṇḍitaiḥ ।। kumudaiḥ puṇḍarīkaiś ca tathā nīlotpalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।।
kādambaiś cakravākaiś ca tathaiva jalakukkuṭaiḥ ।। dātyūhasārasākīrṇaiḥ koyaṣṭibakaśobhitaiḥ ।। khagair jalacaraiś cānyaiḥ kusumaiś ca jalodbhavaiḥ ।। brahmacārigṛhasthaiś ca vānaprasthaiś ca bhikṣubhiḥ ।।
hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākīrṇaṃ naranārīsamākulam ।। evaṃ sarvaguṇopetaṃ kṣetraṃ paramadurlabham ।। yāvad utkalamaryādā dik krameṇa prakīrtitā ।। yatra tiṣṭhati viśvātmā deśe sa puruṣottamaḥ ।।
ahaṃ rudraś ca śakraś ca devāś cāgnipurogamāḥ ।। gandharvāpsarasaḥ sarvāḥ pitaro devamānuṣāḥ ।। ṛṣayo vālakhilyāś ca kaśyapādyāḥ prajeśvarāḥ ।। sāṅgāś ca caturo vedāḥ śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca ।।
nadyaś ca vividhāḥ puṇyās tīrthāny āyatanāni ca ।। evaṃ puṇyatame deśe devarṣipitṛsevite ।। śreṣṭhatvaṃ kasya deśasya kiṃ cānyad adhikaṃ tataḥ ।। dhanyās te vibudhaprakhyā ye vasanty utkale narāḥ ।।
svarge vasanti te martyā na te yānti yamālaye ।। saphalaṃ jīvitaṃ teṣām utkalānāṃ sumedhasām ।। cārubhrūkeśamukuṭaṃ cārukarṇāvataṃsakam ।। sunāsaṃ sukapolaṃ ca sulalāṭaṃ sulakṣaṇam ।।
trailokyānandajananaṃ kṛṣṇasya mukhapaṅkajam ।। babhūva nṛpatiḥ śrīmān indradyumna iti śrutaḥ ।। rūpavān subhagaḥ śūro dātā bhoktā priyaṃvadaḥ ।। dhanurvede ca vede ca śāstre ca nipuṇaḥ kṛtī ।।
āditya iva duṣprekṣyaḥ śatrusaṃghabhayaṃkaraḥ ।। adhyetā yogasāṃkhyānāṃ mumukṣur dharmatatparaḥ ।। tasya buddhiḥ samutpannā harer ārādhanaṃ prati ।। kasmin kṣetre athavā tīrthe nadītīre tathāśrame ।।
ālokya sarvatīrthāni kṣetrāṇy atha purāṇy api ।। vikhyātaṃ paramaṃ kṣetraṃ muktidaṃ puruṣottamam ।। ayajac cāśvamedhena vidhivad bhūridakṣiṇaḥ ।। tatra saṃkarṣaṇaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ subhadrāṃ sthāpya vīryavān ।।
snānaṃ dānaṃ tapo homaṃ devatāprekṣaṇaṃ tathā ।। prasādād devadevasya tato mokṣam avāptavān ।। sāgare cendradyumnākhye snātvā mokṣaṃ labhed dhruvam ।। jagāma paramaṃ kṣetraṃ muktidaṃ puruṣottamam ।।
vājimedhena vidhivad iṣṭavān puruṣottamam ।। prāsādaṃ kārayām āsa ceṣṭaṃ trailokyaviśrutam ।। nirmame rājaśārdūlaḥ kṣetraṃ rakṣitavān katham ।। sthāpayām āsa matimān kṛṣṇādīṃs tridaśārcitān ।।
vaktum arhasy aśeṣeṇa caritaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ ।। śrotum icchāmahe brahman paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ bhuktimuktipradaṃ śubham ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ muniśārdūlāḥ prayatāḥ saṃyatendriyāḥ ।।
babhūva tasya nṛpateḥ pṛthivī kakudopamā ।। dṛḍhayantrārgaladvārā parikhābhir alaṃkṛtā ।। rathyāpaṇavatī ramyā suvibhaktacatuṣpathā ।। rājahaṃsanibhaiḥ śubhraiś citragrīvair manoharaiḥ ।।
yajñotsavapramuditā gītavāditranisvanā ।। hastyaśvarathasaṃkīrṇā padātigaṇasaṃkulā ।। brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiś caiva dvijātibhiḥ ।। na tatra malināḥ santi na mūrkhā nāpi nirdhanāḥ ।।
sadā hṛṣṭāḥ sumanaso dṛśyante puruṣāḥ striyaḥ ।। suveṣāḥ puruṣās tatra dṛśyante mṛṣṭakuṇḍalāḥ ।। kāmadevapratīkāśāḥ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitāḥ ।। jñātāraḥ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ bhettāraḥ śatruvāhinīm ।।
striyas tatra muniśreṣṭhā dṛśyante sumanoharāḥ ।। sumadhyamāḥ sujaghanāḥ pīnonnatapayodharāḥ ।। hāvabhāvānatagrīvāḥ karṇābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। suvarṇābharaṇopetāḥ sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ ।।
divyamālyāmbaradharā divyagandhānulepanāḥ ।। rūpalāvaṇyasaṃyuktāḥ sarvāḥ prahasitānanāḥ ।। gītavādyakathālāpai ramayantyaś ca tāḥ striyaḥ ।। prekṣaṇālāpakuśalāḥ sarvayoṣidguṇānvitāḥ ।।
pativratāś ca subhagā guṇaiḥ sarvair alaṃkṛtāḥ ।। devatāyatanair divyair nānākusumaśobhitaiḥ ।। pippalaiḥ karṇikāraiś ca candanāgurucampakaiḥ ।। nāraṅgair lakucair lodhraiḥ saptaparṇaiḥ śubhāñjanaiḥ ।।
pāṭalāśokatagaraiḥ karavīraiḥ sitetaraiḥ ।। nyagrodhāśvatthakāśmaryaiḥ palāśair devadārubhiḥ ।। prācīnāmalakaiḥ plakṣair jambūśirīṣapādapaiḥ ।। kharjūrāgastyabakulaiḥ śākhoṭakaharītakaiḥ ।।
ketakīvanakhaṇḍaiś ca atimuktaiḥ sakubjakaiḥ ।। mātuluṅgaiḥ pūgaphalaiḥ karuṇaiḥ sindhuvārakaiḥ ।। anyaiś ca vividhaiḥ puṣpa- vṛkṣaiś cānyair manoharaiḥ ।। sadā kusumagandhāḍhyaiḥ sadā phalabharānataiḥ ।।
cakoraiḥ śatapattraiś ca bhṛṅgāraiḥ priyaputrakaiḥ ।। kapotaiḥ khañjarīṭaiś ca śyenaiḥ pārāvatais tathā ।। saritaḥ puṣkariṇyaś ca sarāṃsi subahūni ca ।। padmaiḥ sitetaraiḥ śubhraiḥ kahlāraiś ca sugandhibhiḥ ।।
gandhāmodakarair divyaiḥ sarvartukusumojjvalaiḥ ।। sārasaiś ca balākaiś ca kūrmair matsyaiḥ sanakrakaiḥ ।। khagair jalacaraiś cānyair nānāravavibhūṣitaiḥ ।। evaṃ nānāvidhaiḥ puṣpair vividhaiś ca jalāśayaiḥ ।।
jalasthalacaraiś caiva vihagaiś cārvadhiṣṭhitaiḥ ।। tatrāste bhagavān devas tripurāris trilocanaḥ ।। śivakuṇḍe naraḥ snātvā vidhivat pāpanāśane ।। gatvā śivālayaṃ paścāt kṛtvā taṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇam ।।
snānaiḥ puṣpais tathā gandhair dhūpair dīpaiś ca bhaktitaḥ ।। daṇḍavatpraṇipātaiś ca nṛtyaiḥ stotraiś ca śaṃkaram ।। aśvamedhasahasrasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।। āruhya tridivaṃ yāti yatra śaṃbhor niketanam ।।
bhuṅkte tatra varān bhogān yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam ।। puṇyakṣayād ihāyātaḥ pravare brāhmaṇe kule ।। yogaṃ pāśupataṃ prāpya tato mokṣam avāpnuyāt ।। tasyāṃ snātas tu vidhivat saṃtarpya pitṛdevatāḥ ।।
bhuṅkte bahuvidhān bhogān svargaloke narottamaḥ ।। govindasvāmināmāsau bhuktimuktiprado hariḥ ।। vimānenārkavarṇena kiṅkiṇījālamālinā ।। upagīyamāno gandharvair viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।।
ābhūtasaṃplavaṃ yāvat surūpaḥ subhagaḥ sukhī ।। pravare yogināṃ gehe vedaśāstrārthatattvavit ।। vikramasvāmināmānaṃ viṣṇuṃ tatraiva bho dvijāḥ ।। anye api tatra tiṣṭhanti devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā tān vidhivad bhaktyā saṃpūjya praṇipatya ca ।। evaṃ sā nagarī ramyā rājasiṃhena pālitā ।। purāṣṭādaśasaṃyuktā suvistīrṇacatuṣpathā ।। vidyāvadgaṇabhūyiṣṭhā vedanirghoṣanāditā ।।
kāvyālāpakathāś caiva śrūyante aharniśaṃ dvijāḥ ।। yasyāṃ rājābhavat pūrvam indradyumno mahāmatiḥ ।। pālayām āsa matimān prajāḥ putrān ivaurasān ।। matimān dharmasaṃpannaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।।
āditya iva tejobhī rūpair āśvinayor iva ।। śāradendur ivābhāti lakṣaṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ ।। dānair yajñais tapobhiś ca tattulyo nāsti bhūpatiḥ ।। pradadau vipramukhyebhyo yāge yāge mahādhanam ।।
ratnānāṃ dhanadhānyānām antas tasya na vidyate ।। sarvakāmasamṛddhātmā kurvan rājyam akaṇṭakam ।। katham ārādhayiṣyāmi bhuktimuktipradaṃ prabhum ।। itihāsapurāṇāni vedāṅgāni ca sarvaśaḥ ।।
vedāṅgāni ca śāstrāṇi vidyāsthānāni yāni ca ।। ādhāya paramāṃ kāṣṭhāṃ kṛtakṛtyo abhavat tadā ।। bhrāntijñānād atītas tu mumukṣuḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ ।। pītavastraṃ caturbāhuṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।।
śrīvatsoraḥsamāyuktaṃ mukuṭāṅgadaśobhitam ।। balena mahatā yuktaḥ sabhṛtyaḥ sapurohitaḥ ।। rathair vimānasaṃkāśaiḥ patākādhvajasevitaiḥ ।। aśvaiḥ pavanasaṃkāśair anujagmus tu taṃ nṛpam ।।
īṣādantaiḥ sadā mattaiḥ pracaṇḍaiḥ ṣaṣṭihāyanaiḥ ।। anujagmuś ca taṃ sarve gajayuddhaviśāradāḥ ।। divyamālyāmbaradharā divyagandhānulepanāḥ ।। sarvāstrakuśalāḥ śūrāḥ sadā saṃgrāmalālasāḥ ।।
bimbauṣṭhacārudaśanāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। divyagandhānuliptāṅgāḥ śaraccandranibhānanāḥ ।। tāmbūlarañjitamukhā rakṣibhiś ca surakṣitāḥ ।। upagīyamānās tāḥ sarvā gāyanaiḥ stutipāṭhakaiḥ ।।
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā anujagmuś ca taṃ nṛpam ।। dhanai ratnaiḥ suvarṇaiś ca sadārāḥ saparicchadāḥ ।। tṛṇavikrayakāś caiva kāṣṭhavikrayakārakāḥ ।। tailavikrayakāś caiva vastravikrayakās tathā ।।
tathā javasahārāś ca rajakāś ca sahasraśaḥ ।। meṣapālāś cājapālā mṛgapālāś ca haṃsakāḥ ।। guḍavikrayikāś caiva tathā lavaṇajīvinaḥ ।। śailūṣāḥ kathakāś caiva purāṇārthaviśāradāḥ ।।
viṣaghnā gāruḍāś caiva nānāratnaparīkṣakāḥ ।। kauṣakārāś citrakārāḥ kundakārāś ca pāvakāḥ ।। mallā dūtāś ca kāyasthā ye cānye karmakāriṇaḥ ।। lāvajīvās taittirikā mṛgapakṣyupajīvinaḥ ।।
vṛkṣavaidyāś ca govaidyā ye cānye chedadāhakāḥ ।। anujagmus tu rājānaṃ samastapuravāsinaḥ ।। anuyānti yathā putrās tathā taṃ te api nāgarāḥ ।। hastyaśvarathapādātair jagāma ca śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।।
sarvais tair dīrghakālena balair anugataḥ prabhuḥ ।। anekaśatasāhasrair ūrmibhiś ca samākulam ।। vīcītaraṅgabahulaṃ mahāścaryasamanvitam ।। meghavṛndapratīkāśam agādhaṃ makarālayam ।।
śiṃśumāraiḥ karkaṭaiś ca vṛtaṃ sarpair mahāviṣaiḥ ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvavāñchāphalapradam ।। amṛtasyāraṇiṃ divyaṃ devayonim apāṃ patim ।। supavitraṃ pavitrāṇāṃ maṅgalānāṃ ca maṅgalam ।।
candravṛddhikṣayasyeva yasya mānaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। utpattisthitisaṃhāra- hetubhūtaṃ sanātanam ।। dṛṣṭvā taṃ nṛpatiśreṣṭho vismayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ ।। puṇye manohare deśe sarvabhūmiguṇair yute ।।
panasair nārikelaiś ca bakulair nāgakesaraiḥ ।। śālair āmrātakair lodhrair bakulair bahuvārakaiḥ ।। dāḍimaiś ca tamālaiś ca pārijātais tathārjunaiḥ ।। iṅgudīsaptaparṇaiś ca aśvatthāgastyajambukaiḥ ।।
palāśabadarair nīpaiḥ siddhanimbaśubhāñjanaiḥ ।। iti hintālakāṅkolaiḥ karañjaiḥ savibhītakaiḥ ।। śākhoṭhakair nimbavaṭaiḥ kumbhīkauṣṭhaharītakaiḥ ।। jambīrakaruṇair vṛkṣais tintiḍīraktacandanaiḥ ।।
kalpadrumair nityaphalaiḥ sarvartukusumotkaraiḥ ।। mayūravarasaṃghuṣṭaiḥ śukasārikasaṃkulaiḥ ।। jīvaṃjīvakakākolaiḥ kalaviṅkaiḥ kapotakaiḥ ।। puṣpitāgreṣu vṛkṣeṣu kūjadbhiś cārvadhiṣṭhitaiḥ ।।
mallikākundakusumair yūthikātagarais tathā ।। mālatīkaravīraiś ca tathā kadalakāñcanaiḥ ।। vanodyānopavanajair nānāvarṇaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ ।। gandharvoragarakṣobhir bhūtāpsarasakiṃnaraiḥ ।।
mṛgaiḥ śākhāmṛgaiḥ siṃhair varāhamahiṣākulaiḥ ।। śārdūlair dīptamātaṅgais tathānyair vanacāribhiḥ ।। latāgulmavitānaiś ca vividhaiś ca jalāśayaiḥ ।। kādambaiś ca plavair haṃsaiś cakravākopaśobhitaiḥ ।।
khagair jalacaraiś cānyaiḥ puṣpair jalasamudbhavaiḥ ।। nānāvṛkṣasamākīrṇair nānādhātuvibhūṣitaiḥ ।। sarvauṣadhisamāyuktair vipulaiś citrasānubhiḥ ।। dadarśa sa mahīpālaḥ sthānaṃ trailokyapūjitam ।।
nānāścaryasamāyuktaṃ kṣetraṃ paramadurlabham ।। kiṃ tatra pratimā pūrvaṃ na sthitā vaiṣṇavī prabho ।। sthāpayām āsa kṛṣṇaṃ ca rāmaṃ bhadrāṃ śubhapradām ।। śrotum icchāmahe sarvaṃ brūhi tatkāraṇaṃ ca naḥ ।।
pravakṣyāmi samāsena śriyā pṛṣṭaḥ purā hariḥ ।। siddhavidyādharair yakṣaiḥ kiṃnarair upaśobhite ।। munibhir guhyakaiḥ siddhaiḥ sauparṇaiḥ samarudgaṇaiḥ ।। vālakhilyādibhiś caiva śobhite sumanohare ।।
jātarūpapratīkāśair bhūṣite sūryasaṃnibhaiḥ ।। puṃnāgāśokasarala- nyagrodhāmrātakārjunaiḥ ।। dhavakhādirapālāśa- śīrṣāmalakatindukaiḥ ।। sarjaiś ca karṇais tagaraiḥ śiśibhūrjavanimbakaiḥ ।।
nānākusumagandhāḍhyair bhūṣite puṣpapādapaiḥ ।। pāṭalāgastyakuṭaja- mandārakusumādibhiḥ ।। nānāvihagasaṃghaiś ca kūjadbhir madhurasvaraiḥ ।। evaṃ nānāvidhair vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpair nānāvidhais tathā ।।
tatra sthitaṃ jagannāthaṃ jagatsraṣṭāram avyayam ।। papracchemaṃ mahāpraśnaṃ padmajā tam anuttamam ।। martyaloke mahāścarye karmabhūmau sudurlabhe ।। yena mucyeta deveśa asmāt saṃsārasāgarāt ।।
tvadṛte nāsti loke asmin vaktā saṃśayanirṇaye ।। provāca parayā prītyā paraṃ sārāmṛtopamam ।। āste tīrthavare devi vikhyātaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।। kīrtanād yasya deveśi mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ।।
marīcyādyair munivarair gopitaṃ me varānane ।। bhāvenaikena suśroṇi śṛṇuṣva varavarṇini ।। pralīnā devagandharva- daityavidyādharoragāḥ ।। tasmiñ jāgarti bhūtātmā paramātmā jagadguruḥ ।।
vāsudeveti vikhyāto yogātmā harir īśvaraḥ ।। padmakeśarasaṃkāśaṃ brahmāṇaṃ bhūtam avyayam ।। pañcabhūtasamāyuktaṃ sṛjate ca śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।। caturvidhāni sarvāṇi sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।।
saṃcintya manasātmānaṃ sasarja vividhāḥ prajāḥ ।। yakṣavidyādharāṃś cānyān gaṅgādyāḥ saritas tathā ।। jarāyūn aṇḍajān devi svedajodbhedajāṃs tathā ।। antyajātāṃś ca mlecchāṃś ca sasarja vividhān pṛthak ।।
brahmā bhūtvā jagat sarvaṃ nirmame sa carācaram ।। vāme caiva tu nārīṃ sa dvidhā bhūtam akalpayat ।। adhamottamamadhyāś ca mama kṣetrāṇi yāni ca ।। jagāma dhyānam āsthāya vāsudevātmikāṃ tanum ।।
tasmin kṣaṇe samutpannaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt ।। saliladhvāntameghābhaḥ śrīmāñ śrīvatsalakṣaṇaḥ ।। āsanair arghyapādyaiś ca akṣatair abhinandya ca ।। kāraṇaṃ vada māṃ tāta mama dhyānasya sāṃpratam ।।
svargadvārasya mārgāṇi yajñadānavratāni ca ।। vihāya sarvam eteṣāṃ sukhaṃ tatsādhanaṃ vada ।। sarveṣām uttamaṃ sthānaṃ brūhi me puruṣottama ।। śṛṇu brahman pravakṣyāmi nirmalaṃ bhuvi durlabham ।।
gobrāhmaṇahitaṃ puṇyaṃ cāturvarṇyasukhodayam ।। mahāpuṇyaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ siddhidaṃ vai pitāmahe ।। vikhyātaṃ paramaṃ kṣetraṃ caturyuganiṣevitam ।। daityadānavasiddhānāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasām ।।
uttamaḥ puruṣo yasmāt tasmāt sa puruṣottamaḥ ।। daśayojanavistīrṇaṃ kṣetraṃ paramadurlabham ।। vināśaṃ naivam abhyeti svayaṃ tatraivam āsthitaḥ ।। brahmahatyāt pramucyeta pāpeṣv anyeṣu kā kathā ।।
sarve vidhūtapāpmānas te gatāḥ keśavālayam ।। prāsādas tatra tiṣṭhet tu padaṃ dharmamayaṃ hi tat ।। anāyāsena vai yānti bhuvanaṃ me tato narāḥ ।। madantikam anuprāpya praṇamya śirasābravīt ।।
kṣīrodavāsinaṃ devaṃ śeṣabhogānuśāyinam ।। viśveśvaram ajaṃ viṣṇuṃ sarvajñam aparājitam ।। sarvajñaṃ nirguṇaṃ śāntaṃ jagaddhātāram avyayam ।। purāṇaṃ puruṣaṃ vedyaṃ vyaktāvyaktaṃ sanātanam ।।
śrīvatsoraskasaṃyuktaṃ vanamālāvibhūṣitam ।। hārakeyūrasaṃyuktaṃ mukuṭāṅgadadhāriṇam ।। kūṭastham acalaṃ sūkṣmaṃ jyotīrūpaṃ sanātanam ।। namasyāmi jagannātham īśvaraṃ sukhadaṃ prabhum ।।
stutvā nānāvidhaiḥ stotraiḥ praṇāmam akarot tadā ।। stotrasya kāraṇaṃ devi pṛṣṭavān aham antakam ।। kimarthaṃ stutavān māṃ tvaṃ saṃkṣepāt tad bravīhi me ।। indranīlamayī śreṣṭhā pratimā sārvakāmikī ।।
śvetākhyaṃ bhavanaṃ yānti niṣkāmāś caiva mānavāḥ ।। prasīda sumahādeva saṃhara pratimāṃ vibho ।। yama tāṃ gopayiṣyāmi sikatābhiḥ samantataḥ ।। yathā tatra na paśyanti manujāḥ svargakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।।
yamaṃ prasthāpayām āsa svāṃ purīṃ dakṣiṇāṃ diśam ।। tasmin kṣetravare puṇye vikhyāte puruṣottame ।। taṃ sarvaṃ kathayām āsa sa tasyai bhagavān purā ।। kṣetrasya varṇanaṃ caiva prāsādakaraṇaṃ tathā ।।
lavaṇasyodadhes tīre kāṣṭhasya darśanaṃ tathā ।। nirmāṇaṃ pratimāyās tu yathāvarṇaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। yātrākāle ca viprendrāḥ kalpasaṃkīrtanaṃ tathā ।। pañcatīrthasya māhātmyaṃ darśanaṃ śūlapāṇinaḥ ।।
darśanaṃ baladevasya kṛṣṇasya ca viśeṣataḥ ।। darśanaṃ narasiṃhasya vyuṣṭisaṃkīrtanaṃ tathā ।। śvetamādhavamāhātmyaṃ svargadvārasya darśanam ।। samudrasnānamāhātmyam indradyumnasya ca dvijāḥ ।।
sthānaṃ kṛṣṇasya halinaḥ parvayātrāphalaṃ tathā ।। pūrvaṃ kathitavān sarvaṃ tasyai sa puruṣottamaḥ ।। tasmin kṣetravare gatvā kiṃ cakāra narādhipaḥ ।। kṣetrasaṃdarśanaṃ caiva kṛtyaṃ tasya ca bhūpateḥ ।।
dadarśa ramaṇīyāni sthānāni saritas tathā ।। svittropaleti vikhyātā sarvapāpaharā śivā ।। mahānadīti nāmnā sā puṇyatoyā saridvarā ।। ubhayos taṭayor yasyā grāmāś ca nagarāṇi ca ।।
hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākīrṇā vastrālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ ।। svadharmaniratāḥ śāntā dṛśyante śubhalakṣaṇāḥ ।। vedapūrṇamukhā viprāḥ saṣaḍaṅgapadakramāḥ ।। sarvaśāstrārthakuśalā yajvāno bhūridakṣiṇāḥ ।।
sabhāmaṇḍalaharmyeṣu devatāyataneṣu ca ।। kāvyaśāstrakathās tatra śrūyante ca mahājanaiḥ ।। saṃpūrṇalakṣaṇopetā vistīrṇaśroṇimaṇḍalāḥ ।। pīnonnatastanāḥ sarvāḥ samṛddhyā cārudarśanāḥ ।।
kadalīgarbhasaṃkāśāḥ padmakiñjalkasaprabhāḥ ।। sumukhāś cārukeśāś ca hāvabhāvāvanāmitāḥ ।। vidyudvispaṣṭadaśanās tanvaṅgyaś ca tathāparāḥ ।। grīvābharaṇasaṃyuktā mālyadāmavibhūṣitāḥ ।।
devayoṣitpratīkāśā dṛśyante śubhalakṣaṇāḥ ।। vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgaiś ca paṇavaiś caiva gomukhaiḥ ।। krīḍantyas tāḥ sadā hṛṣṭā vilāsinyaḥ parasparam ।। divā rātrau samāyuktāḥ kāmonmattā varāṅganāḥ ।।
mantrasiddhais tapaḥsiddhair yajñasiddhair niṣevitam ।। atraivārādhayiṣyāmi bhagavantaṃ sanātanam ।। sarveśvareśvaraṃ viṣṇum anantam aparājitam ।। kalpavṛkṣo mahākāyo nyagrodho yatra tiṣṭhati ।।
na cātra dṛśyate cānyā pratimā vaiṣṇavī śubhā ।। pratyakṣaṃ mama cābhyeti viṣṇuḥ satyaparākramaḥ ।। upavāsaiś ca vidhivac careyaṃ vratam uttamam ।। viṣṇvāyatanavinyāse prārambhaṃ ca karomy aham ।।
prāsādārthaṃ hares tatra prārambham akarot tadā ।। bhūmiṃ saṃśodhya yatnena rājā tu parayā mudā ।। amātyair mantribhiś caiva vāstuvidyāviśāradaiḥ ।। sucandratārāsaṃyoge grahānukūlyasaṃyute ।।
vedādhyayananirghoṣair gītaiḥ sumadhurasvaraiḥ ।। dadāv arghyaṃ tato rājā śraddhayā susamāhitaḥ ।। kośalādhipatiṃ caiva tān uvāca tadā nṛpaḥ ।। gṛhītvā śilpimukhyāṃś ca śilākarmaviśāradān ।।
saṃvāhyantāṃ ca śakaṭair naukābhir mā vilambatha ।। punar evābravīd vākyaṃ sāmātyān sapurohitān ।। yatra tiṣṭhanti rājānaḥ pṛthivyāṃ tān suśīghragāḥ ।। gacchata sahitāḥ sarva indradyumnasya śāsanāt ।।
gatvā tadā nṛpān ūcur vacanaṃ tasya bhūpateḥ ।। ājagmus tvaritāḥ sarve svasainyaiḥ parivāritāḥ ।। paścimāyāṃ sthitā ye ca uttarāpathasaṃsthitāḥ ।। pārvatīyāś ca ye kecit tathā dvīpanivāsinaḥ ।।
saṃprāptā bahuśo viprāḥ śrutvendradyumnaśāsanam ।। provāca rājā hṛṣṭātmā kāryam uddiśya sādaram ।। asmin kṣetravare puṇye bhuktimuktiprade śive ।। kathaṃ śaknomy ahaṃ kartum iti cintākulaṃ manaḥ ।।
yadi yūyaṃ sahāyā me bhavadhvaṃ nṛpasattamāḥ ।। sarve pramuditā hṛṣṭā bhūpās te tasya śāsanāt ।। kambalājinaratnaiś ca rāṅkavāstaraṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। gajair aśvair dhanaiś cānyai rathaiś caiva kareṇubhiḥ ।।
śālivrīhiyavaiś caiva māṣamudgatilais tathā ।। śyāmākair madhukaiś caiva nīvāraiḥ sakulatthakaiḥ ।। bahudhānyasahasrāṇāṃ taṇḍulānāṃ ca rāśibhiḥ ।। tathānyair vividhair dravyair bhakṣyabhojyānulepanaiḥ ।।
tān dṛṣṭvā yajñasaṃbhārān sarvasaṃpatsamanvitān ।। śāstreṣu nipuṇān dakṣān kuśalān sarvakarmasu ।। brahmacārigṛhasthāṃś ca vānaprasthān yatīṃs tathā ।। ācāryopādhyāyavarān svādhyāyatapasānvitān ।।
dṛṣṭvā tān nṛpatiḥ śrīmān uvāca svaṃ purohitam ।। vājimedhārthasiddhyarthaṃ deśaṃ paśyantu yajñiyam ।। hṛṣṭaḥ sa mantribhiḥ sārdhaṃ tadā rājapurohitaḥ ।। brāhmaṇān agrataḥ kṛtvā kuśalān yajñakarmaṇi ।।
kārayām āsa vipro asau yajñavāṭaṃ yathāvidhi ।। indrasadmanibhaṃ ramyaṃ hemaratnavibhūṣitam ।। yajñāyatanadeśeṣu dattvā śuddhaṃ ca kāñcanam ।। kārayām āsa dharmātmā tatra tatra yathāvidhi ।।
