kārayām āsa vidhivac chālās tatrāpy anekaśaḥ ।। ratnāny anekāny ādāya striyaś cāyayur utsave ।। nadataḥ sāgarasyeva divispṛg abhavad dhvaniḥ ।। vyādideśāyatanāni śayyāś cāpy upacārataḥ ।।
upetya nṛpatiśreṣṭho vyādideśa svayaṃ tadā ।। ye ca dvijātipravarās tatrāsan dvijasattamāḥ ।। sarvāṃś ca tān anuyayau yāvad āvasathān iti ।। tataḥ kṛtvā svaśilpaṃ ca śilpino anye ca ye tadā ।।
hṛṣṭaromābhavad rājā saha mantribhir acyutaḥ ।। hetuvādān bahūn āhuḥ parasparajigīṣavaḥ ।। dadṛśus toraṇāny atra śātakumbhamayāni ca ।। ghaṭapātrīkaṭāhāni kalaśān vardhamānakān ।।
yūpāṃś ca śāstrapaṭhitān dāravān hemabhūṣitān ।। sthalajā jalajā ye ca paśavaḥ kecana dvijāḥ ।। gāś caiva mahiṣīś caiva tathā vṛddhastriyo api ca ।। jarāyujāṇḍajātāni svedajāny udbhidāni ca ।।
evaṃ pramuditaṃ sarvaṃ paśuto dhanadhānyataḥ ।। brāhmaṇānāṃ viśāṃ caiva bahumiṣṭānnam ṛddhimat ।। dundubhir meghanirghoṣān muhurmuhur athākarot ।। evaṃ sa vavṛdhe yajñas tasya rājñas tu dhīmataḥ ।।
dadhikulyāś ca dadṛśuḥ payasaś ca hradāṃs tathā ।। dvijāś ca tatra dṛśyante rājñas tasya mahāmakhe ।। gṛhītvā bhājanaṃ jagmur bahūni dvijasattamāḥ ।। paryaveṣayan dvijātīñ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।।
te vai nṛpopabhojyāni brāhmaṇebhyo daduḥ saha ।। pūjāṃ cakre tadā teṣāṃ vidhivad bhūridakṣiṇaḥ ।। naṭanartakakādīṃś ca gītastutiviśāradān ।। indīvarapalāśākṣyaḥ śaraccandranibhānanāḥ ।।
evaṃ tadbhūpaparama- patnīgaṇasamanvitam ।। ratnahārayutaṃ ramyaṃ candrakāntisamaprabham ।। śataśaḥ koṭisaṃghātair dantibhir dantabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।। śvetāśvaiḥ śyāmakarṇaiś ca koṭyanekair javānvitaiḥ ।।
asaṃkhyeyaiḥ padātaiś ca devaputropamais tathā ।। mudaṃ lebhe tadā rājā saṃhṛṣṭo vākyam abravīt ।। cārayadhvaṃ pṛthivyāṃ vai rājaputrāḥ susaṃyatāḥ ।। kṛṣṇacchāgaṃ ca mahiṣaṃ kṛṣṇasāramṛgaṃ dvijān ।।
iṣṭayaś ca pravartantāṃ prāsādaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tataḥ ।। striyaś ca ratnakoṭyaś ca grāmāś ca nagarāṇi ca ।। anyāni dravyajātāni manojñāni bahūni ca ।। pratyakṣaṃ mama cābhyeti yajñasyāsya samīpataḥ ।।
dadau suvarṇasaṃghātaṃ koṭīnāṃ caiva bhūṣaṇam ।। arbudaṃ caiva vṛṣabhaṃ svarṇaśṛṅgīś ca dhenukāḥ ।। prāyacchat sa tu viprebhyo vedavidbhyo mudā yutaḥ ।। suśuklāni ca śubhrāṇi pravālamaṇim uttamam ।।
adadāt sa mahāyajñe ratnāni vividhāni ca ।। alaṃkāravatīḥ śubhrāḥ kanyā rājīvalocanāḥ ।। striyaḥ pīnapayobhārāḥ kañcukaiḥ svastanāvṛtāḥ ।। hāvabhāvānvitagrīvā bahvyo valayabhūṣitāḥ ।।
ekaikaśo adadāt tasmin kāmyāś ca kāminīr bahūḥ ।। bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ ca saṃpūrṇaṃ nānāsaṃbhārasaṃyutam ।। annāny anyāni medhyāṃś ca ghṛtapūrāṃś ca khāṇḍavān ।। prītyarthaṃ sarvasattvānāṃ dīyate annaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।।
evaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahāyajñaṃ devadaityāḥ savāraṇāḥ ।। vismayaṃ paramaṃ yātā dṛṣṭvā kratuvaraṃ śubham ।। na tatra malinaḥ kaścin na dīno na kṣudhānvitaḥ ।। nākālamaraṇaṃ tatra na daṃśo na grahā viṣam ।।
ye ca tatra tapaḥsiddhā munayaś cirajīvinaḥ ।। kratuṃ samāpayām āsa prāsādaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।। yathā tāḥ pratimāḥ pūrvam indradyumnena nirmitāḥ ।। tat sarvaṃ vada cāsmākaṃ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।।
kathayāmi purā vṛttaṃ pratimānāṃ ca saṃbhavam ।। cintā tasya babhūvātha pratimārtham aharniśam ।। sargasthityantakartāraṃ paśyāmi puruṣottamam ।। na bhuṅkte vividhān bhogān na ca snānaṃ prasādhanam ।।
na gajair madayuktaiś ca na cānekair hayānvitaiḥ ।। suvarṇarajatādyaiś ca vajrasphaṭikasaṃyutaiḥ ।। babhūva tasya nṛpater manasas tuṣṭivardhanam ।। viṣṇupratimāyogyaṃ ca sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam ।।
sthāpite prītim abhyeti iti cintāparo abhavat ।। cintāviṣṭo mahīpālaḥ saṃstotum upacakrame ।। trāhi māṃ sarvalokeśa janmasaṃsārasāgarāt ।। saṃkarṣaṇa namas te astu trāhi māṃ dharaṇīdhara ।।
ratikānta namas te astu trāhi māṃ saṃvarāntaka ।। aniruddha namas te astu trāhi māṃ varado bhava ।। nārāyaṇa namas te astu trāhi māṃ śaraṇāgatam ।। caturmukha jagaddhāma trāhi māṃ prapitāmaha ।।
trāhi viṣṇo jagannātha magnaṃ māṃ bhavasāgare ।। narasiṃha mahāvīrya trāhi māṃ dīptalocana ।। tathā mahāvarāhas tvaṃ trāhi māṃ duḥkhasāgarāt ।। taveme baladevādyāḥ pṛthagrūpeṇa saṃsthitāḥ ।।
dikpālāḥ sāyudhāś caiva keśavādyās tathācyuta ।। te api sarve jagannātha prasannāyatalocana ।। prayacchata varaṃ mahyaṃ dharmakāmārthamokṣadam ।। tava pūjārthasaṃbhūtās tatas tvayi samāśritāḥ ।।
vividhaṃ tava yad rūpam uktaṃ tad upacārataḥ ।। ekas tvaṃ hi hare vyāpī citsvabhāvo nirañjanaḥ ।। nirlepaṃ nirguṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ kūṭastham acalaṃ dhruvam ।। tad devāś ca na jānanti kathaṃ jānāmy ahaṃ prabho ।।
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇi- mukuṭāṅgadadhāriṇam ।। tad arcayanti vibudhā ye cānye tava saṃśrayāḥ ।। trāhi māṃ padmapattrākṣa magnaṃ viṣayasāgare ।। tvām ṛte kamalākānta prasīda madhusūdana ।।
harṣaśokānvito mūḍhaḥ karmapāśaiḥ suyantritaḥ ।। viṣamodakaduṣpāre rāgadveṣajhaṣākule ।। nirāśraye nirālambe niḥsāre atyantacañcale ।। nānājātisahasreṣu jāyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।
vividhāny anubhūtāni saṃsāre asmiñ janārdana ।। itihāsapurāṇāni tathā śilpāny anekaśaḥ ।। mayā prāptā jagannātha kṣayavṛddhyakṣayetarāḥ ।। pitaro vividhā dṛṣṭā mātaraś ca tathā mayā ।।
prāptāś ca bāndhavāḥ putrā bhrātaro jñātayas tathā ।। garbhavāse mahāduḥkham anubhūtaṃ tathā prabho ।। vārdhake ca hṛṣīkeśa tāni prāptāni vai mayā ।। mayā tāny anubhūtāni narake yātanās tathā ।।
mahiṣoṣṭragavāṃ caiva tathānyeṣāṃ vanaukasām ।। dhanināṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ ca daridrāṇāṃ tapasvinām ।। gṛheṣu teṣām utpanno deva cāhaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।। daridratvaṃ ceśvaratvaṃ svāmitvaṃ ca tathā gataḥ ।।
dattaṃ mamānyair anyebhyo mayā dattam anekaśaḥ ।। dhanināṃ śrotriyāṇāṃ ca daridrāṇāṃ tapasvinām ।। devatiryaṅmanuṣyeṣu sthāvareṣu careṣu ca ।। kadā me narake vāsaḥ kadā svarge jagatpate ।।
jalayantre yathā cakre ghaṭī rajjunibandhanā ।। tathā cāhaṃ suraśreṣṭha karmarajjusamāvṛtaḥ ।। evaṃ saṃsāracakre asmin bhairave romaharṣaṇe ।। na jāne kiṃ karomy adya hare vyākulitendriyaḥ ।।
idānīṃ tvām ahaṃ deva vihvalaḥ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। kṛpāṃ kuru jagannātha bhaktaṃ māṃ yadi manyase ।। deva tvāṃ nātham āsādya na bhayaṃ me asti kutracit ।। ye tu tvāṃ vidhivad deva nārcayanti narādhamāḥ ।।
kiṃ teṣāṃ kulaśīlena vidyayā jīvitena ca ।। prakṛtiṃ tv āsurīṃ prāpya ye tvāṃ nindanti mohitāḥ ।। na teṣāṃ niṣkṛtis tasmād vidyate narakārṇavāt ।। yatra yatra bhavej janma mama karmanibandhanāt ।।
ārādhya tvāṃ surā daityā narāś cānye api saṃyatāḥ ।। na śaknuvanti brahmādyāḥ stotuṃ tvāṃ tridaśā hare ।। tathā cājñānabhāvena saṃstuto asi mayā prabho ।। kṛtāparādhe api hare kṣamāṃ kurvanti sādhavaḥ ।।
sāṅgaṃ bhavatu tat sarvaṃ vāsudeva namo astu te ।। dadau tasmai muniśreṣṭhāḥ sakalaṃ manasepsitam ।। stotreṇānena matimān sa mokṣaṃ labhate dhruvam ।। dharmaṃ cārthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca labhate naraḥ ।।
sa lokaṃ śāśvataṃ viṣṇor yāti nirdhūtakalmaṣaḥ ।। guhyaṃ sudurlabhaṃ puṇyaṃ na deyaṃ yasya kasyacit ।। na duṣṭamataye dadyān nābhaktāya kadācana ।। viṣṇubhaktāya śāntāya śraddhānuṣṭhānaśāline ।।
vāsudevaṃ jagannāthaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam ।। vastraṃ ca tanmanā bhūtvā suṣvāpa dharaṇītale ।। mama cārtiharo devas tadāsāv iti cintayan ।। ātmānaṃ darśayām āsa śaṅkhacakragadābhṛtam ।।
śaṅkhacakradharaṃ devaṃ gadācakrograpāṇinam ।। yugāntādityavarṇābhaṃ nīlavaidūryasaṃnibham ।। sa cāsmai prābravīd dhīrāḥ sādhu rājan mahāmate ।। tuṣṭo asmi te mahīpāla vṛthā kim anuśocasi ।।
yathā sā prāpyate bhūpa tadupāyaṃ bravīmi te ।। sāgarasya jalasyānte nānādrumavibhūṣite ।। lavaṇasyodadhe rājaṃs taraṅgaiḥ samabhiplutam ।। velābhir hanyamānaś ca na cāsau kampate drumaḥ ।।
ekākī viharan rājan sa tvaṃ paśyasi pādapam ।। chedyamānaṃ tu taṃ vṛkṣaṃ prātar adbhutadarśanam ।। kuru tāṃ pratimāṃ divyāṃ jahi cintāṃ vimohinīm ।। sa cāpi svapnam ālokya paraṃ vismayam āgataḥ ।।
vyāharan vaiṣṇavān mantrān sūktaṃ caiva tadātmakam ।। sa snātvā sāgare samyag yathāvad vidhinā tataḥ ।। kṛtvā paurvāhṇikaṃ karma jagāma sa nṛpottamaḥ ।। ekākī sa mahāvelāṃ praviveśa mahīpatiḥ ।।
mahātigamahārohaṃ puṇyaṃ vipulam eva ca ।। sāndramāñjiṣṭhavarṇābhaṃ nāmajātivivarjitam ।। paraśunā śātayām āsa niśitena dṛḍhena ca ।। nirīkṣyamāṇe kāṣṭhe tu babhūvādbhutadarśanam ।।
ājagmatur mahābhāgau tadā tulyāgrajanmanau ।। atha tau taṃ samāgamya nṛpam indrasakhaṃ tadā ।। kimarthaṃ ca mahābāho śātitaś ca vanaspatiḥ ।। mahāsindhutaṭe caiva kathaṃ vai śātito drumaḥ ।।
babhāṣe vacanaṃ tābhyāṃ mṛdulaṃ madhuraṃ tathā ।। namaskṛtya jagannāthāv avāṅmukham avasthitaḥ ।। ārādhayituṃ pratimāṃ karomīti matir mama ।। svapnānte ca samuddiṣṭo bhavadbhyāṃ śrāvitaṃ mayā ।।
prahasya tasmai viśveśas tuṣṭo vacanam abravīt ।। saṃsārasāgare ghore kadalīdalasaṃnibhe ।। indriyāvartakalile dustare romaharṣaṇe ।। yatas te matir utpannā viṣṇor ārādhanāya vai ।।
saprajā pṛthivī dhanyā saśailavanakānanā ।। yatra tvaṃ nṛpaśārdūla prajāḥ pālayitā prabhuḥ ।। āvābhyāṃ saha tiṣṭha tvaṃ kathābhir dharmasaṃśritaḥ ।। mayoddiṣṭāṃ tu pratimāṃ karoty eṣa taṭaṃ tyaja ।।
sāgarasya taṭaṃ tyaktvā gatvā tasya samīpataḥ ।। tatas tasmai sa viśvātmā dadāv ājñāṃ dvijākṛtiḥ ।। kṛṣṇarūpaṃ paraṃ śāntaṃ padmapattrāyatekṣaṇam ।। gaurāṅgaṃ kṣīravarṇābhaṃ dvitīyaṃ svastikāṅkitam ।।
devadānavagandharva- yakṣavidyādharoragaiḥ ।। bhaginīṃ vāsudevasya rukmavarṇāṃ suśobhanām ।। tṛtīyāṃ vai subhadrāṃ ca sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitām ।। tatkṣaṇāt kārayām āsa pratimāḥ śubhalakṣaṇāḥ ।।
āraktākṣaṃ mahākāyaṃ sphaṭāvikaṭamastakam ।। kuṇḍalaikadharaṃ divyaṃ gadāmuśaladhāriṇam ।। atasīpuṣpasaṃkāśaṃ padmapattrāyatekṣaṇam ।। cakrapūrṇakaraṃ divyaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ harim ।।
vicitravastrasaṃchannāṃ hārakeyūrabhūṣitām ।। pīnonnatakucāṃ ramyāṃ viśvakarmā vinirmame ।। divyavastrayugacchannā nānāratnair alaṃkṛtāḥ ।। vismayaṃ paramaṃ gatvā idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।
ubhau cādbhutakarmāṇau devavṛttāv amānuṣau ।। kiṃ nu brahmahṛṣīkeśau kiṃ vasū kim utāśvinau ।। yuvāṃ gato asmi śaraṇam ātmā tu me prakāśyatām ।। na brahmā na ca rudro ahaṃ viddhi māṃ puruṣottamam ।।
ārādhanīyo bhūtānām anto yasya na vidyate ।। yam āhur jñānagamyeti vāsudeveti yoginaḥ ।। indro ahaṃ devarājaś ca jagatsaṃyamano yamaḥ ।। varuṇo apāṃ patiś cāhaṃ dharitrī ca mahīdharaḥ ।।
carācaraṃ ca yad viśvaṃ madanyan nāsti kiṃcana ।। yad iṣṭaṃ tat prayacchāmi hṛdi yat te vyavasthitam ।। tvaṃ punar dṛḍhabhaktitvāt pratyakṣaṃ dṛṣṭavān asi ।। romāñcitatanur bhūtvā idaṃ stotraṃ jagau nṛpaḥ ।।
śrīda śrīśa śrīnivāsa namas te śrīniketana ।। niṣkalaṃ paramaṃ devaṃ praṇato asmi sanātanam ।। nirlepaṃ nirguṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ sarvajñaṃ sarvabhāvanam ।। sarveṣām eva goptāraṃ vyāpinaṃ sarvabhāvinam ।।
namasye varadaṃ devaṃ nīlotpaladalacchavim ।। namasye ahaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ harim ।। sarvalokeśvaraṃ viṣṇuṃ mokṣakāraṇam avyayam ।। uvāca praṇato bhūtvā nipatya dharaṇītale ।।
devāsurāḥ sagandharvā yakṣarakṣomahoragāḥ ।। ṛṣayo ye mahābhāgā nānāśāstraviśāradāḥ ।। mokṣamārgavido ye anye dhyāyanti paramaṃ padam ।। tat padaṃ gantum icchāmi tvatprasādāt sudurlabham ।।
bhaviṣyati yathākāmaṃ matprasādān na saṃśayaḥ ।। avicchinnaṃ mahārājyaṃ kuru tvaṃ nṛpasattama ।। pūrṇamanorathaṃ śāntaṃ guhyam avyaktam avyayam ।। cintāśokavinirmuktaṃ kriyākāraṇavarjitam ।।
yaṃ prāpya paramānandaṃ prāpsyasi paramāṃ gatim ।। yāvad ghanā nabho yāvad yāvac candrārkatārakam ।। tiṣṭhanti divi devāś ca tāvat sarvatra cāvyayā ।। yatra snātvā sakṛl lokaḥ śakralokam avāpnuyāt ।।
kulaikaviṃśam uddhṛtya śakralokaṃ gamiṣyati ।। vimānena vaset tatra yāvad indrāś caturdaśa ।। nyagrodhas tiṣṭhate tatra tatsamīpe tu maṇḍapaḥ ।। nārikelair asaṃkhyeyaiś campakair bakulāvṛtaiḥ ।।
pāṭalāmrātasaralaiś candanair devadārubhiḥ ।। hintālaiś caiva tālaiś ca śiṃśapair badarais tathā ।। anyair bahuvidhair vṛkṣaiḥ śobhitaḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ ।। ṛkṣe neṣyanti nas tatra nītvā sapta dināni vai ।।
krīḍāviśeṣabahulair nṛtyagītamanoharaiḥ ।। vījayantas tathāsmabhyaṃ sthāpayiṣyanti maṅgalāḥ ।। vānaprasthā gṛhasthāś ca siddhāś cānye ca brāhmaṇāḥ ।। kariṣyanti stutiṃ rājan rāmakeśavayoḥ punaḥ ।।
naro varṣāyutaṃ divyaṃ śrīmaddharipure vaset ।। harer anucaras tatra krīḍate keśavena vai ।। sarvakāmair mahābhogais tiṣṭhate bhuvanottame ।। koṭīdhanapatiḥ śrīmāṃś caturvedī bhaved dhruvam ।।
jagāmādarśanaṃ viprāḥ sahito viśvakarmaṇā ।। kṛtakṛtyam ivātmānaṃ mene saṃdarśanād dhareḥ ।। rathair vimānasaṃkāśair maṇikāñcanacitritaiḥ ।। ānayām āsa matimān sāmātyaḥ sapurohitaḥ ।।
saṃsthāpya ca śubhe deśe pavitre sumanohare ।। pratiṣṭhāṃ kārayām āsa sumuhūrte dvijaiḥ saha ।। ācāryānumatenaiva sarvaṃ kṛtvā mahīpatiḥ ।। ṛtvigbhyaś ca vidhānena tathānyebhyo dhanaṃ dadau ।।
sthāpayām āsa tān sarvān vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।। suvarṇamaṇimuktādyair nānāvastraiḥ suśobhanaiḥ ।। dadau cānyān sa viṣayān purāṇi nagarāṇi ca ।। iṣṭvā ca vividhair yajñair dattvā dānāny anekaśaḥ ।।
jagāma paramaṃ sthānaṃ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। kṣetrasya caiva māhātmyaṃ kim anyac chrotum icchatha ।। āścaryaṃ menire viprāḥ papracchuś ca punar mudā ।। vidhinā kena kartavyaṃ pañcatīrtham iti prabho ।।
devatāprekṣaṇe caiva brūhi sarvaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।। jitendriyo jitakrodhaḥ saptasaṃvatsarāyutam ।। kṛtopavāsaḥ prāpnoti tato adhikataraṃ phalam ।। svargalokepsuviprādyair draṣṭavyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।।
śuklapakṣasya dvādaśyāṃ paśyet taṃ puruṣottamam ।। te viṣṇulokam āsādya na cyavante kadācana ।। kṛtvā tasmin pañcatīrthaṃ draṣṭavyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।। ahany ahani śuddhātmā so api viṣṇupuraṃ vrajet ।।
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇulokaṃ vrajen naraḥ ।। sahasā mucyate pāpān naro bhaktyā praṇamya tat ।। naṣṭe arkacandre pavane naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame ।। vidyudutpātasaṃghātaiḥ saṃbhagne taruparvate ।।
śuṣkeṣu sarvatoyeṣu saraḥsu ca saritsu ca ।। lokaṃ tu prāviśat sarvam ādityair upaśobhitam ।। devadānavayakṣāṇāṃ bhayaṃ janayate mahat ।। adhastān muniśārdūlāḥ sarvaṃ nāśayate kṣaṇāt ।।
nirdahaty āśugo vāyuḥ sa ca saṃvartako analaḥ ।। tato dahati saṃdīptaḥ sarvam eva jagat prabhuḥ ।। mahājvālo mahārciṣmān saṃpradīptamahāsvanaḥ ।। trailokyaṃ cādahat tūrṇaṃ sasurāsuramānuṣam ।।
ṛṣiḥ paramadharmātmā dhyānayogaparo abhavat ।। mohapāśair nibaddho asau kṣuttṛṣṇākulitendriyāḥ ।। tṛṣṇārtaḥ praskhalan viprās tadāsau bhayavihvalaḥ ।। trātāraṃ nādhigacchan vai itaś cetaś ca dhāvati ।।
karomi kiṃ na jānāmi yasyāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje ।। iti saṃcintayan devam ekāgreṇa sanātanam ।। puruṣeśam iti khyātaṃ vaṭarājaṃ sanātanam ।। āsādya taṃ muniśreṣṭhās tasya mūle samāviśat ।।
na saṃvartāgamas tatra na ca vajrāśanis tathā ।। samuttasthur mahāmeghā nabhasy adbhutadarśanāḥ ।। kecit kiñjalkasaṃkāśāḥ kecit pītāḥ payodharāḥ ।। kecit kamalapattrābhāḥ kecid dhiṅgulasaṃnibhāḥ ।।
kecid añjanasaṃkāśāḥ kecin marakataprabhāḥ ।। ghorarūpā mahābhāgā ghorasvananināditāḥ ।। tair iyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saparvatavanākarā ।। tatas te jaladā ghorā vāriṇā munisattamāḥ ।।
varṣamāṇā mahātoyaṃ pūrayanto vasuṃdharām ।। tato dvādaśa varṣāṇi payodāḥ samupaplave ।। tataḥ samudrāḥ svāṃ velām atikrāmanti bho dvijāḥ ।। sarvataḥ sumahābhrāntās te payodā nabhastalam ।।
tatas taṃ mārutaṃ ghoraṃ sa viṣṇur munisattamāḥ ।। tasminn ekārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame ।। tato muniḥ sa viśrānto dhyātvā ca puruṣottamam ।। nāpaśyat taṃ vaṭaṃ norvīṃ na digādi na bhāskaram ।।
tasminn ekārṇave ghore tamobhūte nirāśraye ।। babhrāmāsau muniś cārta itaś cetaś ca saṃplavan ।। provāca muniśārdūlās tadā dhyānena toṣitaḥ ।। āgacchāgaccha śīghraṃ tvaṃ mārkaṇḍeya mamāntikam ।।
mārkaṇḍeya mune dhīra bālas tvaṃ śramapīḍitaḥ ।। uvāca sa tadā viprā vismitaś cābhavan muhuḥ ।। bahuvarṣasahasrākhyaṃ dharṣayann iva me vapuḥ ।। māṃ brahmā sa ca deveśo dīrghāyur iti bhāṣate ।।
mārkaṇḍeyeti coktvā man- mṛtyuṃ gantum ihecchati ।। kiṃ svapno ayaṃ mayā dṛṣṭaḥ kiṃ vā moho ayam āgataḥ ।। vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ devaṃ bhaktyāhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। dadarśa taṃ vaṭaṃ bhūyo viśālaṃ salilopari ।।
ruciraṃ divyaparyaṅkaṃ racitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā ।। padmarāgādibhir juṣṭaṃ ratnair anyair alaṃkṛtam ।। nānāścaryasamāyuktaṃ prabhāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitam ।। sūryakoṭipratīkāśaṃ dīpyamānaṃ suvarcasam ।।
śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ devaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।। hārabhārārpitagrīvaṃ divyaratnavibhūṣitam ।। romāñcitatanur devaṃ praṇipatyedam abravīt ।। katham eko hy ayaṃ bālas tiṣṭhaty atra sunirbhayaḥ ।।
yadā na bubudhe cainaṃ tadā khedād uvāca ha ।। vṛthā me jīvitaṃ dīrghaṃ vṛthā mānuṣyam eva ca ।। yo ahaṃ suptaṃ na jānāmi paryaṅke divyabālakam ।। trāṇārthaṃ vihvalaś cāsau nirvedaṃ gatavāṃs tadā ।।
sarvatejomayaṃ viprā na śaśākābhivīkṣitum ।। provāca muniśārdūlās tadā meghaughanisvanaḥ ।। śarīraṃ viśa me kṣipraṃ viśrāmas te mayoditaḥ ।। viveśa vadanaṃ tasya vivṛtaṃ cāvaśo muniḥ ।।
dadarśa pṛthivīṃ kṛtsnāṃ nānājanapadair vṛtām ।। dadarśa tān samudrāṃś ca jambu plakṣaṃ ca śālmalam ।। bhāratādīni varṣāṇi tathā sarvāṃś ca parvatān ।। nānāratnānvitaiḥ śṛṅgair bhūṣitaṃ bahukandaram ।।
nānāsattvasamāyuktaṃ nānāścaryasamanvitam ।। mṛgaiḥ śākhāmṛgaiś cānyair bhūṣitaṃ sumanoharam ।। muniyakṣāpsarobhiś ca vṛtaiś cānyaiḥ surālayaiḥ ।। paryaṭan sa tadā vipras tasya bālasya codare ।।
śvetaṃ ca durdharaṃ nīlaṃ kailāsaṃ mandaraṃ girim ।। sahyaṃ ca śuktimantaṃ ca mainākaṃ vakraparvatam ।। tatas tāṃs tu muniśreṣṭhāḥ so apaśyad ratnabhūṣitān ।। bāhlīkān śūrasenāṃś ca kāśmīrāṃs taṅgaṇān khasān ।।
antyajān antyajātīṃś ca so apaśyat tasya codare ।। gajāṃś cānyāṃs tathā sattvān so apaśyat tasya codare ।। kṛṣigorakṣavāṇijyaṃ krayavikrayaṇaṃ tathā ।। gandharvāpsaraso yakṣān ṛṣīṃś caiva sanātanān ।।
siṃhikātanayāṃś caiva ye cānye suraśatravaḥ ।। apaśyat sa tadā sarvaṃ tasya kukṣau dvijottamāḥ ।। brahmādistambaparyantaṃ yat kiṃcit sacarācaram ।। mahar janas tapaḥ satyam atalaṃ vitalaṃ tathā ।।
mahātalaṃ ca brahmāṇḍam apaśyat tasya codare ।। prasādāt tasya devasya smṛtilopaś ca nābhavat ।। nāntaṃ jagāma dehasya tasya viṣṇoḥ kadācana ।। tadā taṃ varadaṃ devaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatavān muniḥ ।।
mahātmano mukhāt tasya vivṛtāt puruṣasya saḥ ।। punaś caikārṇavām urvīm apaśyaj janavarjitām ।। śākhāyāṃ vaṭavṛkṣasya paryaṅkopari saṃsthitam ।। jagad ādāya tiṣṭhantaṃ padmapattrāyatekṣaṇam ।।
dṛṣṭvā mukhād viniṣkrāntaṃ provāca prahasann iva ।। bhramamāṇaś ca kiṃ tatra āścaryaṃ dṛṣṭavān asi ।। tena tvām upakārāya saṃbhāṣe paśya mām iha ।। dadarśa taṃ suduṣprekṣaṃ ratnair divyair alaṃkṛtam ।।
prasādāt tasya devasya prādurbhūtā punar navā ।। praṇamya śirasā viprā harṣagadgadayā girā ।। dṛṣṭvā taṃ paramātmānaṃ saṃstotum upacakrame ।। trāhi māṃ cārupadmākṣa duḥkhitaṃ śaraṇāgatam ।।
aṅgāravarṣabhītaṃ ca trāhi māṃ puruṣottama ।। vihvalo ahaṃ tathā śrāntas trāhi māṃ puruṣottama ।। na śāntim adhigacchāmi trāhi māṃ puruṣottama ।। trātāraṃ nātra paśyāmi trāhi māṃ puruṣottama ।।
na cāntam adhigacchāmi trāhi māṃ puruṣottama ।। vismito ahaṃ viṣaṇṇaś ca trāhi māṃ puruṣottama ।। prasīda vibudhaśreṣṭha prasīda vibudhapriya ।। prasīda sarvalokeśa jagatkāraṇakāraṇa ।।
prasīda salilāvāsa prasīda madhusūdana ।। prasīda kaṃsakeśīghna prasīdāriṣṭanāśana ।। prasīda mathurāvāsa prasīda yadunandana ।। tvaṃ mahī tvaṃ jalaṃ deva tvam agnis tvaṃ samīraṇaḥ ।।
tvaṃ buddhiḥ prakṛtiś caiva sattvādyās tvaṃ jagatpate ।। tvam indriyāṇi sarvāṇi śabdādyā viṣayāḥ prabho ।। tvam indras tvaṃ śivo devas tvaṃ havis tvaṃ hutāśanaḥ ।। varuṇas tvam apāṃ nātha tvaṃ vāyus tvaṃ dhaneśvaraḥ ।।
vasavas tvaṃ tathā rudrās tvam ādityāś ca khecarāḥ ।। siddhāś cāpsaraso nāgā gandharvās tvaṃ sacāraṇāḥ ।। munayas tvam ṛṣigaṇās tvam aśvinau niśācarāḥ ।। kiṃ cātra bahunoktena brahmādistambagocaram ।।
yat te rūpaṃ paraṃ deva kūṭastham acalaṃ dhruvam ।। deva śuddhasvabhāvo asi nityas tvaṃ prakṛteḥ paraḥ ।। tvam ākāśaḥ paraḥ śānto ajas tvaṃ vibhur avyayaḥ ।। tat sarvaṃ devadeveśa kṣantum arhasi cāvyaya ।।
prītaḥ provāca bhagavān meghagambhīrayā girā ।। dadāmi sarvaṃ viprarṣe matto yad abhivāñchasi ।। uvāca paramaprīto munis tadgatamānasaḥ ।। tvatprasādāc ca deveśa smṛtir na parihīyate ।।
icchāmi puṇḍarīkākṣa jñātuṃ tvām aham avyayam ।। pītvā jagad idaṃ sarvam etad ākhyātum arhasi ।। kiyantaṃ ca tvayā kālam iha stheyam ariṃdama ।। mahad etad acintyaṃ ca yad ahaṃ dṛṣṭavān prabho ।।
sāntvayan sa tadā vākyam uvāca vadatāṃ varaḥ ।। tava prītyā pravakṣyāmi yathedaṃ visṛjāmy aham ।। tato dṛṣṭo asmi te sākṣād brahmacaryaṃ ca te mahat ।। tena nārāyaṇo asmy ukto mama tās tv ayanaṃ sadā ।।
vidhātā sarvabhūtānāṃ saṃhartā ca dvijottama ।। ahaṃ vaiśravaṇo rājā yamaḥ pretādhipas tathā ।। ahaṃ dhātā vidhātā ca yajñaś cāhaṃ dvijottama ।। dyaur mūrdhā khaṃ diśaḥ śrotre tathāpaḥ svedasaṃbhavāḥ ।।
mayā kratuśatair iṣṭaṃ bahubhiś cāptadakṣiṇaiḥ ।। pṛthivyāṃ kṣatriyendrāś ca pārthivāḥ svargakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। catuḥsamudraparyantāṃ merumandarabhūṣaṇām ।। vārāhaṃ rūpam āsthāya mameyaṃ jagatī purā ।।
agniś ca vāḍavo vipra bhūtvāhaṃ dvijasattama ।। brahma vaktraṃ bhujau kṣatram ūrū me saṃśritā viśaḥ ।। ṛgvedaḥ sāmavedaś ca yajurvedas tv atharvaṇaḥ ।। yatayaḥ śāntiparamā yatātmāno bubhutsavaḥ ।।
sattvasthā nirahaṃkārā nityam adhyātmakovidāḥ ।। ahaṃ saṃvartako jyotir ahaṃ saṃvartako analaḥ ।। tārārūpāṇi dṛśyante yāny etāni nabhastale ।। ratnākarāḥ samudrāś ca sarva eva caturdiśaḥ ।।
kāmaḥ krodhaś ca harṣaś ca bhayaṃ mohas tathaiva ca ।। prāpnuvanti narā vipra yat kṛtvā karma śobhanam ।। madvidhānena vihitā mama dehavicāriṇaḥ ।। samyag vedam adhīyānā yajanto vividhair makhaiḥ ।।
prāptuṃ śakyo na caivāhaṃ narair duṣkṛtakarmabhiḥ ।। tan māṃ mahāphalaṃ viddhi narāṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।। yadā yadā hi dharmasya glānir bhavati sattama ।। daityā hiṃsānuraktāś ca avadhyāḥ surasattamaiḥ ।।
tadāhaṃ saṃprasūyāmi gṛheṣu puṇyakarmaṇām ।। sṛṣṭvā devamanuṣyāṃś ca gandharvoragarākṣasān ।। karmakāle punar deham anucintya sṛjāmy aham ।। śvetaḥ kṛtayuge dharmaḥ śyāmas tretāyuge mama ।।
trayo bhāgā hy adharmasya tasmin kāle bhavanti ca ।। trailokyaṃ nāśayāmy ekaḥ sarvaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। abhinnaḥ sarvago ananto hṛṣīkeśa urukramaḥ ।। śamanaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvabhūtakṛtodyamam ।।
sarvabhūteṣu viprendra na ca māṃ vetti kaścana ।। yac ca kiṃcit tvayā prāptaṃ mayi kleśātmakaṃ dvija ।। yac ca kiṃcit tvayā loke dṛṣṭaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। ahaṃ nārāyaṇo nāma śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।।
tāvat svapimi viśvātmā sarvaviśvāni mohayan ।। aśiśuḥ śiśurūpeṇa yāvad brahmā na budhyate ।। asakṛt parituṣṭena viprarṣigaṇapūjita ।। nirgato asi mayājñātas tatas te darśitaṃ jagat ।।
dṛṣṭvā lokaṃ samastaṃ hi vismito nāvabudhyase ।। ākhyātas te mayā cātmā durjñeyo hi surāsuraiḥ ।। tāvat tvam iha viprarṣe viśrabdhaś cara vai sukham ।। eko bhūtāni srakṣyāmi śarīrāṇi dvijottama ।।
loke yac ca bhavet kiṃcid iha sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। pūrṇe yugasahasre tu meghagambhīranisvanaḥ ।। varaṃ vṛṇīṣva yac chreṣṭhaṃ dadāmi nacirād aham ।। tena tvam asi viprendra punar dīrghāyur āpnuhi ।।
mūrdhnā nipatya sahasā praṇamya punar abravīt ।। moho ayaṃ vigataḥ satyaṃ tvayi dṛṣṭe tu me hare ।। lokānāṃ ca hitārthāya nānābhāvapraśāntaye ।। asmin kṣetravare puṇye nirmale puruṣottame ।।
pratiṣṭheya tathā tatra tava sthāne ca śaṃkaram ।। pratyuvāca jagannāthaḥ sa punas taṃ mahāmunim ।। liṅgam ārādhanārthāya nānābhāvapraśāntaye ।। tatprabhāvāc chivaloke tiṣṭha tvaṃ ca tathākṣayam ।।
nāvayor antaraṃ kiṃcid ekabhāvau dvidhā kṛtau ।। ubhayor antaraṃ nāsti pavanākāśayor iva ।। vṛṣadhvajaḥ sa eveti tripuraghnaṃ trilocanam ।। uttare devadevasya kuru tīrthaṃ suśobhanam ।।
bhaviṣyati dvijaśreṣṭha sarvapāpapraṇāśanaḥ ।। mārkaṇḍeyaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ sarvavyāpī janārdanaḥ ।। yat phalaṃ snānadānena devatāprekṣaṇena ca ।। nimajjet tatra vārāṃs trīn imaṃ mantram udīrayet ।।
trāhi māṃ bhaganetraghna tripurāre namo astu te ।। snānaṃ karomi deveśa mama naśyatu pātakam ।। tilodakena matimān pitṝṃś cānyāṃś ca tarpayet ।। praviśya devatāgāraṃ kṛtvā taṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇam ।।
aghoreṇa ca bho viprāḥ praṇipatya prasādayet ।। trāhi māṃ tvaṃ virūpākṣa mahādeva namo astu te ।। daśānām aśvamedhānāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।। tatra bhuktvā varān bhogān yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam ।।
śāṃkaraṃ yogam āsādya tato mokṣam avāpnuyāt ।। pūjayet parayā bhaktyā mantreṇānena taṃ vaṭam ।। mahadrasopaviṣṭāya nyagrodhāya namo astu te ।। nyagrodha hara me pāpaṃ kalpavṛkṣa namo astu te ।।
sahasā mucyate pāpāj jīrṇatvaca ivoragaḥ ।। brahmahatyāṃ naro jahyāt pāpeṣv anyeṣu kā kathā ।। nyagrodhākṛtikaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇipatya ca bho dvijāḥ ।। tathā svavaṃśam uddhṛtya viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
sarvapāpavinirmuktas tato viṣṇupuraṃ vrajet ।। saṃkarṣaṇaṃ subhadrāṃ ca sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। saṃkarṣaṇaṃ svamantreṇa bhaktyāpūjya prasādayet ।। namas te revatīkānta namas te bhaktavatsala ।।
pralambāre namas te astu trāhi māṃ kṛṣṇapūrvaja ।। kailāsaśikharākāraṃ candrāt kāntatarānanam ।। mahābalaṃ haladharaṃ kuṇḍalaikavibhūṣitam ।। sarvapāpair vinirmukto viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
puṇyakṣayād ihāgatya pravare yogināṃ kule ।। jñānaṃ tatra samāsādya muktiṃ prāpnoti durlabhām ।। dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa pūjayet susamāhitaḥ ।। pūjayanti sadā dhīrās te mokṣaṃ prāpnuvanti vai ।।
yāṃ gatiṃ yānti bho viprā dvādaśākṣaratatparāḥ ।। saṃpūjya gandhapuṣpādyaiḥ praṇipatya prasādayet ।। jaya cāṇūrakeśighna jaya kaṃsaniṣūdana ।। jaya nīlāmbudaśyāma jaya sarvasukhaprada ।।
jaya lokapate nātha jaya vāñchāphalaprada ।। krodhagrāhākule raudre viṣayodakasaṃplave ।। nimagno ahaṃ suraśreṣṭha trāhi māṃ puruṣottama ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ devaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam ।।
mahoraskaṃ mahābāhuṃ pītavastraṃ śubhānanam ।। sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ vanamālāvibhūṣitam ।। aśvamedhasahasrāṇāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti vai dvijāḥ ।। naras tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ praṇamya ca ।।
naras tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ praṇamya ca ।। tat phalaṃ samavāpnoti naraḥ kṛṣṇaṃ praṇamya ca ।। naras tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ praṇamya ca ।। naras tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ praṇamya ca ।।
naras tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ praṇamya ca ।। naras tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ praṇamya ca ।। naras tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ praṇamya ca ।। naras tat phalam āpnoti dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ praṇamya ca ।।
dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ naro bhaktyā mokṣaṃ prāpnoti durlabham ।। śriyā paramayā yuktaḥ sarvaiḥ samudito guṇaiḥ ।। trisaptakulam uddhṛtya naro viṣṇupuraṃ vrajet ।। gandharvāpsarasaiḥ sārdhaṃ yathā viṣṇuś caturbhujaḥ ।।
sarvajñaḥ sarvavedī ca jāyate gatamatsaraḥ ।। āsādya vaiṣṇavaṃ jñānaṃ tato muktim avāpnuyāt ।। prasādayet tato viprāḥ praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। trāhi māṃ padmapattrākṣi kātyāyani namo astu te ।।
baladevasya bhaginīṃ subhadrāṃ varadāṃ śivām ।। ābhūtasaṃplavaṃ yāvat krīḍitvā tatra devavat ।। prāpya yogaṃ hares tatra mokṣaṃ ca labhate dhruvam ।। dharmaṃ cārthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca labhate dhruvam ।।
praṇamyāyatanaṃ paścād vrajet tatra samāhitaḥ ।। antardhānagataṃ natvā tato viṣṇupuraṃ vrajet ।। sa āste tatra bho viprāḥ siṃhārdhakṛtavigrahaḥ ।। mucyate pātakair martyaḥ samastair nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
na teṣāṃ duṣkṛtaṃ kiṃcit phalaṃ syād yad yad īpsitam ।। dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ phalaṃ yasmāt prayacchati ।। yathā kathayase deva tena no vismayo mahān ।। śrotum icchāmahe brūhi paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।।
bhaktānām upakārāya brūhi deva namo astu te ।। brūhi tāḥ kuru cāsmākaṃ prasādaṃ prapitāmaha ।। ajitasyāprameyasya bhuktimuktipradasya ca ।। siṃhārdhakṛtadehasya pravakṣyāmi samāsataḥ ।।
prasādāt tasya tāḥ sarvāḥ sidhyanti nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। prasādāt tasya devasya bhavaty avyāhatā gatiḥ ।। narasiṃhasya bho viprāḥ sadā bhaktānukampinaḥ ।। yena prasīdec caivāsau siṃhārdhakṛtavigrahaḥ ।।
narasiṃhasya tattvaṃ ca yan na jñātaṃ surāsuraiḥ ।। payobhakṣeṇa viprendrā vartayet sādhakottamaḥ ।। araṇye vijane deśe parvate sindhusaṃgame ।। pratiṣṭhāpya svayaṃ vāpi pūjāṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ ।।
japel lakṣāṇi vai viṃśan manasā saṃyatendriyaḥ ।। mukto bhavet tato viprāḥ sādhako nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। puṇyagandhādibhir dhūpaiḥ praṇamya śirasā prabhum ।। pradadyān narasiṃhasya tataḥ siddhiḥ prajāyate ।।
tejaḥ soḍhuṃ na śaktāḥ syur brahmarudrādayaḥ surāḥ ।। vidyādharā yakṣagaṇāḥ sakiṃnaramahoragāḥ ।। te sarve pralayaṃ yānti dṛṣṭvādityāgnivarcasaḥ ।। dvirjaptaṃ kavacaṃ divyaṃ rakṣate devadānavāt ।।
bhūtāḥ piśācā rakṣāṃsi ye cānye paripanthinaḥ ।। dvādaśābhyantare caiva yojanānāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। tato gatvā biladvāram upoṣya rajanītrayam ।। palāśasamidhas tatra juhuyāt trimadhuplutāḥ ।।
tato vivaradvāraṃ tu prakaṭaṃ jāyate kṣaṇāt ।। gacchataḥ saṃkaṭaṃ tasya tamomohaś ca naśyati ।। narasiṃhaṃ smaraṃs tatra pātālaṃ viśate dvijāḥ ।। tataḥ strīṇāṃ sahasrāṇi vīṇāvādanakarmaṇām ।।
praveśayanti tā haste gṛhītvā sādhakeśvaram ।। pītamātre divyadeho jāyate sumahābalaḥ ।। bhinnadeho vāsudeve līyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। paṭṭaṃ śūlaṃ ca khaḍgaṃ ca rocanāṃ ca maṇiṃ tathā ।।
kṛṣṇājinaṃ muniśreṣṭhā guṭikāṃ ca manoharām ।। siddhavidyāṃ ca śāstrāṇi gṛhītvā sādhakeśvaraḥ ।। sakṛn nyastaṃ dahet sarvaṃ vṛjinaṃ janmakoṭijam ।। svadehe bhrūṇahatyādi kṛtvā divyena śudhyati ।।
hṛdante vai tataḥ śīghraṃ naśyeyur dāruṇā grahāḥ ।। gaṇḍapiṇḍakalūtānāṃ nāśanaṃ kurute dhruvam ।। trisaṃdhyaṃ māsam ekaṃ tu sarvarogān vināśayet ।। yāṃ yāṃ kāmayate siddhiṃ tāṃ tāṃ prāpnoti sa dhruvam ।।
mṛttikāḥ sapta valmīke śmaśāne ca catuṣpathe ।। siṃhasya pratimāṃ kṛtvā pramāṇena ṣaḍaṅgulām ।। narasiṃhasya kaṇṭhe tu baddhvā caiva hi mantravit ।। yāvat saptāhamātraṃ tu japet saṃyamitendriyaḥ ।।
athavā śuṣkavṛkṣāgre narasiṃhaṃ tu pūjayet ।। tam evaṃ piñjake baddhvā bhrāmayet sādhakottamaḥ ।। punaś ca dhārayet kṣipraṃ saptasaptena vāriṇā ।। gotrotsādo bhavet tasya uddhṛte caiva śāntidaḥ ।।
mṛgarājaṃ mahāvīryaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ striyaḥ śūdrāntyajātayaḥ ।। mucyante cāśubhair duḥkhair janmakoṭisamudbhavaiḥ ।। devatvam amareśatvaṃ gandharvatvaṃ ca bho dvijāḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā stutvā namaskṛtvā saṃpūjya narakesarīm ।। narasiṃhaṃ naro dṛṣṭvā labhed abhimataṃ phalam ।। sakṛd dṛṣṭvā tu taṃ devaṃ bhaktyā siṃhavapurdharam ।। saṃgrāme saṃkaṭe durge coravyāghrādipīḍite ।।
rājādibhyaḥ samudrebhyo graharogādipīḍite ।। sūryodaye yathā nāśaṃ tamo abhyeti mahattaram ।। guṭikāñjanapātāla- pāduke ca rasāyanam ।। yān yān kāmān abhidhyāyan bhajate narakesarīm ।।
dṛṣṭvā taṃ devadeveśaṃ bhaktyāpūjya praṇamya ca ।। pāpaiḥ sarvair vinirmukto guṇaiḥ sarvair alaṃkṛtaḥ ।। sauvarṇena vimānena kiṅkiṇījālamālinā ।। taruṇādityavarṇena muktāhārāvalambinā ।।
kulaikaviṃśam uddhṛtya devavan muditaḥ sukhī ।। bhuktvā tatra varān bhogān viṣṇuloke dvijottamāḥ ।। manohlādakaraṃ saukhyaṃ yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam ।। vaiṣṇavaṃ yogam āsthāya tato mokṣam avāpnuyāt ।।
sarvapāpavinirmukto naro yāti paraṃ padam ।। vibhīṣaṇena rāmeṇa kas taṃ nārādhayet pumān ।। matsyākhyaṃ mādhavaṃ caiva śvetadvīpaṃ sa gacchati ।। vistareṇa jagannātha pratimāṃ tasya vai hareḥ ।।
śvetākhyaṃ mādhavaṃ devaṃ kas taṃ sthāpitavān purā ।। matimān dharmavic chūraḥ satyasaṃdho dṛḍhavrataḥ ।। bhavanty āyuṣmanto lokā bālas tasmin na sīdati ।। kapālagautamo nāma ṛṣiḥ paramadhārmikaḥ ।।
tam ādāya ṛṣir dhīmān nṛpasyāntikam ānayat ।। pratijñām akarod viprā jīvanārthaṃ śiśos tadā ।। nānaye saptarātreṇa citāṃ dīptāṃ samāruhe ।। saṃpūjya ca mahādevaṃ rājā vidyāṃ punar japet ।।
sāṃnidhyam agamat tuṣṭo śmīty uvāca sahomayā ।। bhasmadigdhaṃ virūpākṣaṃ śaratkundenduvarcasam ।। mahīṃ nipatya sahasā praṇamya sa tadābravīt ।। kālasya vaśam āpanno bālako dvijaputrakaḥ ।।
yathoktāyuṣyasaṃyuktaṃ kṣemaṃ kuru maheśvara ।। kālam ājñāpayām āsa sarvabhūtabhayaṃkaram ।। bālaṃ saṃjīvayām āsa mṛtyor mukhagataṃ punaḥ ।। devyā sahomayā devas tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।
evaṃ saṃjīvayām āsa muneḥ putraṃ nṛpottamaḥ ।। brūhi naḥ paramaṃ tathyaṃ śvetākhyasya ca sāṃpratam ।। pravakṣyāmi yathātathyaṃ yat pṛcchatha mamānaghāḥ ।। yac chrutvābhimatān kāmān dhruvaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।।
śṛṇudhvaṃ tāṃ kathāṃ divyāṃ bhayaśokārtināśinīm ।। vicārya laukikān dharmān vaidikān niyamāṃs tathā ।। sa gatvā paramaṃ kṣetraṃ sāgaraṃ dakṣiṇāśrayam ।। śveto atha kārayām āsa prāsādaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam ।।
tataḥ śvetena viprendrāḥ śvetaśailamayena ca ।। pratiṣṭhāṃ vidhivac cakre yathoddiṣṭāṃ svayaṃ tu saḥ ।। athānantarato rājā mādhavasya ca saṃnidhau ।। japan sa maunam āsthāya māsam ekaṃ samādhinā ।।
japānte sa tu deveśaṃ saṃstotum upacakrame ।। pradyumnāyāniruddhāya namo nārāyaṇāya ca ।। nirguṇāyāpratarkyāya śucaye śuklakarmaṇe ।। namo astu padmavarṇāya padmahastāya te namaḥ ।।
namaḥ sahasrapādāya sahasrabhujamanyave ।। variṣṭhāya vareṇyāya śaraṇyāyācyutāya ca ।। bālārkasomanetrāya muñjakeśāya dhīmate ।। mādhavāya variṣṭhāya govindāya namo namaḥ ।।
madhusūdanāya namaḥ śuddhāyāṃśudharāya ca ।। trivikramāya ca namo divyapītāmbarāya ca ।। namo astu guṇabhūtāya nirguṇāya namo namaḥ ।। namo vāmananetrāya namo vāmanavāhine ।।
apratarkyāya śuddhāya namo bhayaharāya ca ।। śivāya saumyarūpāya rudrāyottāraṇāya ca ।। bhavasaṃghātarūpāya bhavasṛṣṭikṛte namaḥ ।। somasūryāṃśukeśāya gobrāhmaṇahitāya ca ।।
ṛkstutāya namas tubhyaṃ nama ṛksādhanāya ca ।। yajuryājyāya juṣṭāya yajuṣāṃ pataye namaḥ ।। śriyaḥ kāntāya dāntāya yogicintyāya yogine ।। oṃ namaḥ sāmasaumyāya sāmayogavide namaḥ ।।
sāmayajñavide caiva namaḥ sāmakarāya ca ।। namo astv atharvapādāya namo atharvakarāya ca ।। mahodadhijalasthāya vedāharaṇakāriṇe ।। namo bhagavate tubhyaṃ vāsudevāya te namaḥ ।।
oṃ namo mohanāśāya bhavabhaṅgakarāya ca ।। trailokyatejasāṃ kartre namas tejaḥsvarūpiṇe ।। sukhāya sukhanetrāya namaḥ sukṛtadhāriṇe ।। dehināṃ dehakartre ca bhedabhaṅgakarāya ca ।।
namo vāsanivāsāya vāsavyavaharāya ca ।। namo yajñasvarūpāya yajñeśāya ca yogine ।। saṃkarṣaṇāya ca namaḥ pralambamathanāya ca ।। namo astu jñānināṃ jñāna nārāyaṇaparāyaṇa ।।
atas tvāṃ sarvabhāvena praṇato natavatsala ।। na tasyānyo asti deveśa kṣālakas tvām ṛte acyuta ।। saṅgo me astu tvayā sārdham ātmalābhāya keśava ।। tāpatrayaparikliṣṭas tena tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।।
ākarṣitaṃ ca lobhādyair atas tvām aham āśritaḥ ।। yathā yathā hi yajñeśa tvayi cetaḥ pravartate ।। naṣṭo vivekaśūnyo asmi dṛśyate jagad āturam ।। uddhartā puṇḍarīkākṣa tvām ṛte anyo na vidyate ।।
tasmin kṣetravare divye vikhyāte puruṣottame ।। ājagāma nṛpasyāgre sarvair devair vṛto hariḥ ।। dadhat sudarśanaṃ dhīmān karāgre dīptamaṇḍalam ।। rarāja vāmahaste asya pāñcajanyo mahādyutiḥ ।।
yad iṣṭaṃ vara bhadraṃ te prasanno asmi tavānagha ।। praṇamya śirasovāca śvetas tadgatamānasaḥ ।। ābrahmabhavanād ūrdhvaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ padam avyayam ।। tat padaṃ gantum icchāmi tvatprasādāj jagatpate ।।
nābhigacchanti yad ramyaṃ paraṃ padam anāmayam ।। sarvāṃl lokān atikramya mama lokaṃ gamiṣyasi ।। sāṃnidhyaṃ mama caivātra sarvadaiva bhaviṣyati ।। kuśāgreṇāpi rājendra śvetagāṅgeyam ambu ca ।।
yas tv imāṃ pratimāṃ gacchen mādhavākhyāṃ śaśiprabhām ।। tāṃ praṇamya sakṛd bhaktyā puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇām ।। manvantarāṇi tatraiva devakanyābhir āvṛtaḥ ।। bhunakti vipulān bhogān yatheṣṭaṃ māmakaiḥ saha ।।
vedavedāṅgavic chrīmān bhogavāṃś cirajīvitaḥ ।। rūpavān bahubhāgyaś ca putrapautrasamanvitaḥ ।। tyaktvā dehaṃ hariṃ smṛtvā tataḥ śāntapadaṃ vrajet ।। ekārṇavajale pūrvaṃ rohitaṃ rūpam āsthitam ।।
cintayitvā kṣitiṃ samyak tasmin sthāne pratiṣṭhitam ।। praṇamya praṇato bhūtvā sarvaduḥkhād vimucyate ।। kāle punar ihāyāto rājā syāt pṛthivītale ।। dātā bhoktā bhaved yajvā vaiṣṇavaḥ satyasaṃgaraḥ ।।
yaṃ dṛṣṭvā muniśārdūlāḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt ।। kriyate snānadānādi tasyāśeṣaphalaṃ vada ।। bhaktyā tu tanmanā bhūtvā saṃprāpya puṇyam uttamam ।। caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣeṇa sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।।
paurṇamāsyāṃ viśeṣeṇa hayamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।। indradyumnasaraś caiva pañcatīrthīvidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tadā gacched viśeṣeṇa tīrtharājaṃ paraṃ śubham ।। sarvadvaṃdvavinirmukto vītarāgo vimatsaraḥ ।।
pradakṣiṇaṃ prakurvīta trivāraṃ susamāhitaḥ ।। puṇyaṃ cāpnoti vipulaṃ gatim iṣṭāṃ ca bho dvijāḥ ।। yathāsaṃkhyaṃ ca bho viprāḥ kṛtādiṣu yathākramam ।। vaṭasyaitāni nāmāni kīrtitāni kṛtādiṣu ।।
pramāṇaṃ kalpavṛkṣasya kṛtādau parikīrtitam ।। dakṣiṇābhimukho gacched dhanvantaraśatatrayam ।। sāgarāmbhaḥsamākṛṣṭaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ sarvaguṇānvitam ।। mucyate sarvarogādyais tathā pāpair grahādibhiḥ ।।
gatvācamya śucis tatra dhyātvā nārāyaṇaṃ param ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāyeti yaṃ vadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ ।। viṣṇos tās tv ayanaṃ pūrvaṃ tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
nārāyaṇaparā yajñā nārāyaṇaparāḥ kriyāḥ ।। nārāyaṇaparo vahnir nārāyaṇaparaṃ nabhaḥ ।। ahaṃkāraś ca buddhiś ca ubhe nārāyaṇātmake ।। sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ paraṃ caiva sarvaṃ nārāyaṇātmakam ।।
prakṛtiḥ puruṣaś caiva sarve nārāyaṇātmakāḥ ।। avaṣṭabhya idaṃ sarvam āste nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। brahmādistambaparyantaṃ sarvaṃ nārāyaṇātmakam ।। tena vyāptam idaṃ sarvaṃ dṛśyādṛśyaṃ carācaram ।।
tasmād apsu smaren nityaṃ nārāyaṇam aghāpaham ।। smaren nārāyaṇaṃ dhyāyed dhaste kāye ca vinyaset ।। śeṣair hastatalaṃ yāvat tarjanyādiṣu vinyaset ।। mokāraṃ vāmakaṭyāṃ tu nākāraṃ dakṣiṇe nyaset ।।
ṇākāraṃ dakṣiṇe nyasya yakāraṃ mūrdhni vinyaset ।। dhyātvā nārāyaṇaṃ paścād ārabhet kavacaṃ budhaḥ ।। paścime śrīdharo devaḥ keśavas tu tathottare ।। vāyavye tu hṛṣīkeśas tatheśāne ca vāmanaḥ ।।
kṛtvaivaṃ kavacaṃ paścād ātmānaṃ cintayet tataḥ ।। evaṃ dhyātvā tadātmānam imaṃ mantram udīrayet ।। pradhānaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ jīvānāṃ prabhur avyayaḥ ।। vṛjinaṃ hara me sarvaṃ tīrtharāja namo astu te ।।
anyathā bho dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ snānaṃ tatra na śasyate ।। antar jale japet paścāt trir āvṛttyāghamarṣaṇam ।। tathāghamarṣaṇaṃ cātra sūktaṃ sarvāghanāśanam ।। prāṇān āyamya cācamya saṃdhyāṃ copāsya bhāskaram ।।
upasthāyordhvabāhuś ca talliṅgair bhāskaraṃ tataḥ ।। anyāṃś ca sauramantrāṃś ca japtvā tiṣṭhan samāhitaḥ ।। svādhyāyaṃ prāṅmukhaḥ kṛtvā tarpayed daivatāny ṛṣīn ।। toyena tilamiśreṇa vidhivat susamāhitaḥ ।।
adhikārī bhavet paścāt pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇe dvijaḥ ।। tarpaṇe tūbhayaṃ kuryād eṣa eva vidhiḥ sadā ।। tṛpyatām iti siñcet tu nāmagotreṇa vāgyataḥ ।। tarpitās tena pitaras tvaṅmāṃsarudhirāsthibhiḥ ।।
rudhiraṃ tad bhavet toyaṃ pradātā kilbiṣī bhavet ।। vṛthā tan muniśārdūlā nopatiṣṭhati kasyacit ।। pitṝṇāṃ nopatiṣṭheta salilaṃ tan nirarthakam ।। uttīrya tu śucau deśe kuryād udakatarpaṇam ।।
nopatiṣṭhati tat toyaṃ yad bhūmyāṃ na pradīyate ।। tasmāt tatraiva dātavyaṃ pitṝṇāṃ prītim icchatā ।। bhūmyāṃ caiva layaṃ yātā bhūmau dadyāt tato jalam ।। prācīnāgreṣu vai devān yāmyāgreṣu tathā pitṝn ।।
hastamātraṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ caturdvāraṃ suśobhanam ।। madhye tatra likhet padmam aṣṭapattraṃ sakarṇikam ।। aṣṭākṣaravidhānena nārāyaṇam ajaṃ vibhum ।। akāraṃ hṛdaye dhyātvā cakrarekhāsamanvitam ।।
candramaṇḍalamadhyasthaṃ rākāraṃ mūrdhni cintayet ।। evaṃ nirdhūtapāpas tu divyadehas tato bhavet ।। vāmapādaṃ samārabhya kramaśaś caiva vinyaset ।। karaśuddhiṃ prakurvīta mūlamantreṇa sādhakaḥ ।।
oṃkāraṃ pṛthivīṃ śuklāṃ vāmapāde tu vinyaset ।। mokāraṃ kālam evāhur vāmakaṭyāṃ nidhāpayet ।। rākāras teja ity āhur nābhideśe vyavasthitaḥ ।। yakāro ayaṃ śirasthaś ca yatra lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।।
oṃ viṣṇave namaḥ śiraḥ oṃ jvalanāya namaḥ śikhā । oṃ viṣṇave namaḥ kavacam oṃ viṣṇave namaḥ sphuraṇaṃ diśobandhāya । oṃ huṃphaḍastram oṃ śirasi śuklo vāsudeva iti । oṃ āṃ lalāṭe raktaḥ saṃkarṣaṇo garutmān vahnis teja āditya iti ।
oṃ āṃ grīvāyāṃ pītaḥ pradyumno vāyumegha iti । oṃ āṃ hṛdaye kṛṣṇo aniruddhaḥ sarvaśaktisamanvita iti । evaṃ caturvyūham ātmānaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ karma samācaret ।। govindo dakṣiṇe pārśve vāme tu madhusūdanaḥ ।।
avāntaradiśo yās tu tāsu sarvāsu mādhavaḥ ।। narasiṃhakṛtā guptir vāsudevamayo hy aham ।। yathā dehe tathā deve sarvatattvāni yojayet ।। phaṭkārāntaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ sarvavighnaharaṃ śubham ।।
padmamadhye nyased viṣṇuṃ pavanasyāmbarasya ca ।। karṇikāyāṃ samāsīnaṃ jyotīrūpaṃ sanātanam ।। tena vyastasamastena pūjanaṃ paramaṃ smṛtam ।। tato avadhārya hṛdaye karṇikāyāṃ bahir nyaset ।।
tataś cāvāhayen mantraṃ krameṇācintya mānase ।। āvāhanamantraḥ mīnarūpo varāhaś ca narasiṃho atha vāmanaḥ । āyātu devo varado mama nārāyaṇo agrataḥ ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।।
sarvasattvahitārthāya tiṣṭha tvaṃ madhusūdana ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।। arghamantraḥ oṃ trailokyapatīnāṃ pataye devadevāya hṛṣīkeśāya viṣṇave namaḥ । oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।।
viṣṇo kamalapattrākṣa gṛhāṇa madhusūdana ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।। mayā niveditaṃ bhaktyā gṛhāṇa puruṣottama ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।।
gṛhāṇācamanīyaṃ tvaṃ mayā bhaktyā niveditam ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।। lokeśa vṛttimātreṇa vāriṇā snāpayāmy aham ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।।
svarṇavarṇaprabhe deva vāsasī tava keśava ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।। mayā nivedito gandhaḥ pratigṛhya vilipyatām ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।।
sāvitrīgranthisaṃyuktam upavītaṃ tavārpaye ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।। gātrāṇi tava śobhantu sālaṃkārāṇi mādhava ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।।
oṃ nama iti pratyakṣaraṃ samastena mūlamantreṇa vā pūjayet ।। mayā nivedito bhaktyā dhūpo ayaṃ pratigṛhyatām ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।। tvam eva jyotiṣāṃ deva dīpo ayaṃ pratigṛhyatām ।।
oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।। mayā niveditaṃ bhaktyā naivedyaṃ tava keśava ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya namaḥ ।। pradyumnaṃ paścime kuryād aniruddhaṃ tathottare ।।
vāyavye mādhavaṃ caiva tathaiśāne trivikramam ।। vāmapārśve tathā cakraṃ śaṅkhaṃ dakṣiṇato nyaset ।। tataḥ śārṅgaṃ dhanur vidvān nyased devasya vāmataḥ ।। śriyaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ sthāpya puṣṭim uttarato nyaset ।।
vinyased dhṛdayādīni pūrvādiṣu caturdiśam ।। indram agniṃ yamaṃ caiva nairṛtaṃ varuṇaṃ tathā ।। pūjayet tāntrikair mantrair adhaś cordhvaṃ tathaiva ca ।। labhed abhimatān kāmān naro nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ ।।
pūjitaṃ yaḥ saṃpaśyeta sa viśed viṣṇum avyayam ।। janmamṛtyujarāṃ tīrtvā sa viṣṇoḥ padam āpnuyāt ।। anvahaṃ tasya vāsāya śvetadvīpaḥ prakalpitaḥ ।। tannāma sarvatattvānāṃ mantra ity abhidhīyate ।।
ekaikasya prakurvīta yathoddiṣṭaṃ krameṇa tu ।। japaṃ caiva prakurvīta mūlamantreṇa mantravit ।। kāmeṣu ca yathāproktaṃ yathāśakti samāhitaḥ ।। cakraṃ khaḍgaś ca śārṅgaṃ ca aṣṭau mudrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।
yatra brahmādayo devā vindanti paramaṃ padam ।। te tatra mūlamantreṇa pūjayantv acyutaṃ sadā ।। praṇamya śirasā paścāt sāgaraṃ ca prasādayet ।। tīrtharāja namas te astu trāhi mām acyutapriya ।।
tīre cābhyarcya vidhivan nārāyaṇam anāmayam ।। śatānām aśvamedhānāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।। vṛndāraka iva śrīmān rūpayauvanagarvitaḥ ।। kulaikaviṃśam uddhṛtya viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
manvantaraśataṃ sāgraṃ jarāmṛtyuvivarjitaḥ ।। rūpavān subhagaḥ śrīmān satyavādī jitendriyaḥ ।। yogaṃ ca vaiṣṇavaṃ prāpya tato mokṣam avāpnuyāt ।। yugādiṣu ṣaḍaśītyāṃ vyatīpāte dinakṣaye ।।
ye tatra dānaṃ viprebhyaḥ prayacchanti sumedhasaḥ ।। pitṝṇāṃ ye prayacchanti piṇḍaṃ tatra vidhānataḥ ।। evaṃ snānaphalaṃ samyak sāgarasya mayoditam ।। dharmārthamokṣaphaladam āyuṣkīrtiyaśaskaram ।।
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam ।। tāvad garjanti tīrthāni māhātmyaiḥ svaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।। puṣkarādīni tīrthāni prayacchanti svakaṃ phalam ।। bhūtale yāni tīrthāni saritaś ca sarāṃsi ca ।।
rājā samastatīrthānāṃ sāgaraḥ saritāṃ patiḥ ।। tamo nāśaṃ yathābhyeti bhāskare abhyudite dvijāḥ ।। tīrtharājasamaṃ tīrthaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati ।। kaḥ śaknoti guṇān vaktuṃ tīrtharājasya bho dvijāḥ ।।
yat kiṃcit kriyate tatra cākṣayaṃ kriyate dvijāḥ ।। indradyumnasaro nāma yatrāste pāvanaṃ śubham ।। dhyātvopasthāya ca jalam imaṃ mantram udīrayet ।। snānaṃ tvayi karomy adya pāpaṃ hara namo astu te ।।
tilodakena cānyāṃś ca saṃtarpyācamya vāgyataḥ ।। daśāśvamedhikaṃ samyak phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।। kāmagena vimānena viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। cyutas tasmād ihāyāto mokṣaṃ ca labhate dhruvam ।।
jyeṣṭhaśuklapañcadaśyāṃ yaḥ paśyet puruṣottamam ।। prayāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ yasmān nāvartate punaḥ ।। praśaṃsasi kathaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ brūhi tatkāraṇaṃ prabho ।। jyeṣṭhaṃ māsaṃ yathā tebhyaḥ praśaṃsāmi punaḥ punaḥ ।।
puṣkariṇyas taḍāgāni vāpyaḥ kūpās tathā hradāḥ ।। jyeṣṭhaśukladaśamyādi pratyakṣaṃ yānti sarvadā ।। yat kiṃcit kriyate tatra tasmin kāle akṣayaṃ bhavet ।। harate daśa pāpāni tasmād daśaharā smṛtā ।।
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇulokaṃ vrajen naraḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā rāmaṃ subhadrāṃ ca viṣṇulokaṃ vrajen naraḥ ।। phālgunyāṃ prayato bhūtvā govindasya puraṃ vrajet ।। kṛtvā saṃkarṣaṇaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhadrāṃ ca bho dvijāḥ ।।
vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati ।। vaiśākhasyāsite pakṣe sa yāty acyutamandiram ।। kulaikaviṃśam uddhṛtya viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। prayatnena tadā martyair gantavyaṃ puruṣottamam ।।
naro dvādaśayātrāyāḥ phalaṃ prāpnoti cādhikam ।। gaṅgādvāre kuśāvarte gaṅgāsāgarasaṃgame ।। śālagrāme vāyutīrthe mandare sindhusāgare ।। śaṅkhoddhāre dvārakāyāṃ tathā badarikāśrame ।।
kāmālaye koṭitīrthe tathā cāmarakaṇṭake ।। utpalāvartake caiva pṛthutuṅge sukubjake ।। kālañjare ca gokarṇe śrīśaile gandhamādane ।। sahye ca śuktimante ca gomante cārbude tathā ।।
sārasvateṣu gomatyāṃ brahmaputreṣu saptasu ।। tāpī payouṣṇī kāverī śiprā carmaṇvatī dvijāḥ ।। ṛṣikulyā kumārī ca vipāśā ca dṛṣadvatī ।। kauśikī karatoyā ca trisrotā madhuvāhinī ।।
athavā kiṃ bahūktena bhāṣitena dvijottamāḥ ।। sāgareṣu ca śaileṣu nadīṣu ca saraḥsu ca ।। tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mahājyaiṣṭhyāṃ labhen naraḥ ।। mahājyaiṣṭhyāṃ muniśreṣṭhā sarvakāmaphalepsubhiḥ ।।
viṣṇulokaṃ naro yāti samuddhṛtya samaṃ kulam ।। puṇyakṣayād ihāgatya caturvedī dvijo bhavet ।। vaiṣṇavaṃ yogam āsthāya tato mokṣam avāpnuyāt ।। vidhinā kena tad brūhi tato vidhividāṃ vara ।।
rāmasya ca subhadrāyāḥ puṇyaṃ sarvāghanāśanam ।। paurṇamāsyāṃ tadā snānaṃ sarvakālaṃ harer dvijāḥ ।। tadā bhogavatī tatra pratyakṣā bhavati dvijāḥ ।। kṛṣṇarāmābhiṣekārthaṃ subhadrāyāś ca bho dvijāḥ ।।
sudṛḍhaṃ sukhasaṃcāraṃ vastraiḥ puṣpair alaṃkṛtam ।। sitavastraparicchannaṃ muktāhārāvalambitam ।। madhye subhadrāṃ cāsthāpya jayamaṅgalanisvanaiḥ ।। anekaśatasāhasrair vṛtaṃ strīpuruṣair dvijāḥ ।।
snāpayanti tadā kṛṣṇaṃ mañcasthaṃ sahalāyudham ।। svodakaiḥ puṣpamiśraiś ca snāpayanti pṛthak pṛthak ।। kāhalais tālaśabdaiś ca mṛdaṅgair jharjharais tathā ।। strīṇāṃ maṅgalaśabdaiś ca stutiśabdair manoharaiḥ ।।
śrūyate sumahāñ śabdaḥ sāgarasyeva garjataḥ ।। nānāstotraravaiḥ puṇyaiḥ sāmaśabdopabṛṃhitaiḥ ।। snānakāle suraśreṣṭha stuvanti parayā mudā ।। pītaraktāmbarābhiś ca mālyadāmāvanāmibhiḥ ।।
cāmarai ratnadaṇḍaiś ca vījyete rāmakeśavau ।। parivāryāmbaragatair devagandharvacāraṇaiḥ ।। lokapālās tathā cānye stuvanti puruṣottamam ।। sargasthityantakṛd deva lokanātha jagatpate ।।
taṃ namasyāmahe bhaktyā sarvakāmaphalapradam ।। subhadrāṃ ca muniśreṣṭhās tadākāśe vyavasthitāḥ ।। devatūryāṇy avādyanta vātā vānti suśītalāḥ ।। jayaśabdaṃ ca kurvanti munayaḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ ।।
prajānāṃ patayo nāgā ye cānye svargavāsinaḥ ।। ābhiṣecanikaṃ dravyaṃ gṛhītvā devatāgaṇāḥ ।। dhātā caiva vidhātā ca tathā caivānilānalau ।। patnībhyāṃ sahito dhīmān mitreṇa varuṇena ca ।।
viśvair devair marudbhiś ca sādhyaiś ca pitṛbhiḥ saha ।। devarṣibhir asaṃkhyeyais tathā brahmarṣibhir varaiḥ ।। bhṛgubhiś cāṅgirobhiś ca sarvavidyāsuniṣṭhitaiḥ ।। pitāmahaḥ pulastyaś ca pulahaś ca mahātapāḥ ।।
kratur haraḥ pracetāś ca manur dakṣas tathaiva ca ।। mūrtimatyaś ca sarito devāś caiva sanātanāḥ ।। pṛthivī dyaur diśaś caiva pādapāś ca dvijottamāḥ ।। umā śacī sinīvālī tathā cānumatiḥ kuhūḥ ।।
himavāṃś caiva vindhyaś ca meruś cānekaśṛṅgavān ।। māsārdhaṃ māsa-ṛtavas tathā rātryahanī samāḥ ।। aruṇo garuḍaś caiva vṛkṣāś cauṣadhibhiḥ saha ।। kālo yamaś ca mṛtyuś ca yamasyānucarāś ca ye ।।
te devasyābhiṣekārthaṃ samāyānti tatas tataḥ ।। ābhiṣecanikaṃ dravyaṃ maṅgalāni ca sarvaśaḥ ।। sārasvatībhiḥ puṇyābhir divyatoyābhir eva ca ।। sapuṣpaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ kumbhaiḥ snāpayanty avanisthitāḥ ।।
uccāvacāni divyāni kāmagāni sthirāṇi ca ।। gītair vādyaiḥ patākābhiḥ śobhitāni samantataḥ ।। snāpayitvā subhadrāṃ ca saṃstuvanti mudānvitāḥ ।। jaya jaya lokapāla bhaktarakṣaka jaya jaya praṇatavatsala jaya jaya bhūtacaraṇa jaya jayādideva bahukāraṇa jaya jaya vāsudeva jaya jayāsurasaṃharaṇa jaya jaya divyamīna jaya jaya tridaśavara jaya jaya jaladhiśayana । ।
jaya jaya yogivara jaya jaya sūryanetra jaya jaya devarāja jaya jaya kaiṭabhāre jaya jaya vedavara jaya jaya kūrmarūpa jaya jaya yajñavara jaya jaya kamalanābha jaya jaya śailacara । । jaya jaya yogaśāyiñ jaya jaya vegadhara jaya jaya viśvamūrte jaya jaya cakradhara jaya jaya bhūtanātha jaya jaya dharaṇīdhara jaya jaya śeṣaśāyiñ jaya jaya pītavāso jaya jaya somakānta । । jaya jaya yogavāsa jaya jaya dahanavaktra jaya jaya dharmavāsa jaya jaya guṇanidhāna jaya jaya śrīnivāsa jaya jaya garuḍagamana jaya jaya sukhanivāsa jaya jaya dharmaketo jaya jaya mahīnivāsa । । jaya jaya gahanacaritra jaya jaya yogigamya jaya jaya makhanivāsa jaya jaya vedavedya jaya śāntikara jaya jaya yogicintya jaya jaya puṣṭikara jaya jaya jñānamūrte jaya jaya kamalākara । ।
jaya jaya bhāvavedya jaya jaya muktikara jaya jaya vimaladeha jaya jaya sattvanilaya jaya jaya guṇasamṛddha jaya jaya yajñakara jaya jaya guṇavihīna jaya jaya mokṣakara jaya jaya bhūśaraṇya । । jaya jaya kāntiyuta jaya jaya lokaśaraṇa jaya jaya lakṣmīyuta jaya jaya paṅkajākṣa jaya jaya sṛṣṭikara jaya jaya yogayuta jaya jayātasīkusumaśyāmadeha jaya jaya samudrāviṣṭadeha jaya jaya lakṣmīpaṅkajaṣaṭcaraṇa । । jaya jaya bhaktavaśa jaya jaya lokakānta jaya jaya paramaśānta jaya jaya paramasāra jaya jaya cakradhara jaya jaya bhogiyuta jaya jaya nīlāmbara jaya jaya śāntikara jaya jaya mokṣakara jaya jaya kaluṣahara । । jaya padmapalāśākṣa jaya vāñchāphalaprada ।।
jaya padmālayākānta jaya viṣṇo namo astu te ।। siddhacāraṇasaṃghāś ca ye cānye svargavāsinaḥ ।। subhadrāṃ ca muniśreṣṭhāḥ praṇipatyāmbare sthitāḥ ।। kṛṣṇaṃ rāmaṃ subhadrāṃ ca yānti svaṃ svaṃ niveśanam ।।
uccāvacāni divyāni kāmagāni sthirāṇi ca ।। gītair vādyaiḥ patākābhiḥ śobhitāni samantataḥ ।। balabhadraṃ subhadrāṃ ca te yānti padam avyayam ।। dṛṣṭvā nirāmayaṃ sthānaṃ yānti nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ ।।
subhadrāṃ ca muniśreṣṭhāḥ prāpnoti śubhakṛn naraḥ ।। tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।। tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।। tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।।
tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।। tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।। tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।। tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।।
tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।। tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।। tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।। tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।।
tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।। tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।। tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ labhate naraḥ ।। tasya devasya māhātmyaṃ mañcasthasya dvijottamāḥ ।।
tat phalaṃ kṛṣṇam ālokya mañcasthaṃ sahalāyudham ।। tasmān naro athavā nārī paśyet taṃ puruṣottamam ।। snānaśeṣeṇa kṛṣṇasya toyenātmābhiṣicyate ।। rākṣasādyair gṛhītā vā tathā rogaiś ca saṃhatāḥ ।।
prāpnuvantīpsitān kāmān yān yān vāñchanti cepsitān ।। rogārtā mucyate rogād dhanaṃ ca dhanakāṅkṣiṇī ।। tāni snānāvaśeṣasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।। tenābhiṣiñced gātrāṇi sarvakāmapradaṃ hi tat ।।
brahmahatyādibhiḥ pāpair mucyante te na saṃśayaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā naro labhet kṛṣṇaṃ vrajantaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।। dṛṣṭvā naro labhet kṛṣṇaṃ tat phalaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।। dṛṣṭvā naro labhet kṛṣṇaṃ tat phalaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।।
dṛṣṭvā naro labhet kṛṣṇaṃ tat phalaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।। dṛṣṭvā naro labhet kṛṣṇaṃ tat phalaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।। dṛṣṭvā naro labhet kṛṣṇaṃ tat phalaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।। dṛṣṭvā naro labhet kṛṣṇaṃ tat phalaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।।
dṛṣṭvā naro labhet kṛṣṇaṃ tat phalaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।। dṛṣṭvā naro labhet kṛṣṇaṃ tat phalaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।। sārasvateṣu tīrtheṣu tathānyeṣu saraḥsu ca ।। dṛṣṭvā naro labhet kṛṣṇaṃ tat phalaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।।
naimiṣādiṣu tīrtheṣu kṣetreṣv āyataneṣu ca ।। dṛṣṭvā naro labhet kṛṣṇaṃ tat phalaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।। yat kiṃcit kathitaṃ cātra phalaṃ puṇyasya karmaṇaḥ ।। dharmaśāstreṣu sarveṣu tathānyatra manīṣibhiḥ ।।
sakalaṃ bhadrayā sārdhaṃ vrajantaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।। kṛṣṇaṃ balaṃ subhadrāṃ ca te yānti bhavanaṃ hareḥ ।। halinaṃ ca subhadrāṃ ca viṣṇulokaṃ vrajanti te ।। yātrāphalaṃ ca kiṃ tatra prāpyate brūhi mānavaiḥ ।।
pavitre vijane deśe gatvā tatra ca maṇḍape ।। svasthānaṃ saṃparityajya saptarātraṃ vasanti vai ।। saptāhaṃ sarasas tīre mama yātrā bhavatv iti ।। tasmai kila varaṃ cāsau dadau sa puruṣottamaḥ ।।
guḍivā nāma yātrā me sarvakāmaphalapradā ।। saṃkarṣaṇaṃ subhadrāṃ ca vidhivat susamāhitāḥ ।। puṣpair gandhais tathā dhūpair dīpair naivedyakair varaiḥ ।। jayaśabdais tathā stotrair gītair vādyair manoharaiḥ ।।
bhaviṣyati nṛpaśreṣṭha matprasādād asaṃśayam ।। sa tu rājavaraḥ śrīmān kṛtakṛtyo abhavat tadā ।। sarvakāmapradaṃ devaṃ paśyet taṃ puruṣottamam ।। rogāc ca mucyate rogī kanyā prāpnoti satpatim ।।
naraḥ saṃtatim āpnoti rūpayauvanasaṃpadam ।। naro vāpy athavā nārī tāṃs tān prāpnoty asaṃśayam ।। āṣāḍhasya site pakṣe naro yoṣid athāpi vā ।। daśapañcāśvamedhānāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti cādhikam ।।
kāmagena vimānena sarvaratnair alaṃkṛtaḥ ।। rūpavān subhagaḥ śūro naro viṣṇupuraṃ vrajet ।। sarvakāmasamṛddhātmā jarāmaraṇavarjitaḥ ।। vaiṣṇavaṃ yogam āsthāya tato mokṣam avāpnuyāt ।।
yat prāpnoti naraḥ kṛtvā nārī vā tatra saṃyatā ।। yat prāpnoti naraḥ kṛtvā tasmin kṣetre susaṃyataḥ ।। yātrāṃ kṛtvā vidhānena dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ praṇamya ca ।। naro gacched viṣṇuloke yāvad indrāś caturdaśa ।।
tāvat kalpaṃ viṣṇuloke sukhaṃ bhuṅkte na saṃśayaḥ ।। bhuktimuktiprade nṝṇāṃ sarvasattvasukhāvahe ।। yathoktena vidhānena daśa dve ca samāhitaḥ ।। sa bhuktvā vividhān bhogān mokṣaṃ cānte labhed dhruvam ।।
vidhānaṃ cārcanaṃ dānaṃ phalaṃ tatra jagatpateḥ ।। yāṃ kṛtvā tu naro bhaktyā nārī vā labhate phalam ।। tadā kurvīta vidhivat pratiṣṭhāṃ pāpanāśinīm ।। gatvā jalāśayaṃ puṇyam ācamya prayataḥ śuciḥ ।।
tataḥ snānaṃ prakurvīta vidhivat susamāhitaḥ ।। tenaiva tu vidhānena snānaṃ tasya vidhīyate ।। saṃtarpayet tathānyāṃś ca nāmagotravidhānavit ।। upaspṛśya vidhānena bhāskarābhimukhas tataḥ ।।
sarvapāpaharāṃ puṇyāṃ japed aṣṭottaraṃ śatam ।। triḥ pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya bhāskaraṃ praṇamet tataḥ ।। strīśūdrayoḥ snānajāpyaṃ vedoktavidhivarjitam ।। prakṣālya hastau pādau ca upaspṛśya yathāvidhi ।।
madhugandhodakenaiva tīrthacandanavāriṇā ।। candanāgarukarpūraiḥ kuṅkumena vilepayet ।। anyaiś ca vaiṣṇavaiḥ puṣpair arcayen mallikādibhiḥ ।। dhūpaṃ cāgurusaṃyuktaṃ dahed devasya cāgrataḥ ।।
dīpaṃ prajvālayed bhaktyā yathāśaktyā ghṛtena vai ।। ghṛtena ca muniśreṣṭhās tilatailena vā punaḥ ।। modakaṃ phāṇitaṃ vālpaṃ phalāni ca nivedayet ।। namaḥ puruṣottamāyeti japed aṣṭottaraṃ śatam ।।
namas te sarvalokeśa bhaktānām abhayaprada ।। yās te mayā kṛtā yātrā dvādaśaiva jagatpate ।। evaṃ prasādya taṃ devaṃ daṇḍavat praṇipatya ca ।। nānayor antaraṃ yasmād vidyate munisattamāḥ ।।
nānāpuṣpair muniśreṣṭhā vicitraṃ puṣpamaṇḍapam ।। kathāṃ ca vāsudevasya gītikāṃ cāpi kārayet ।। tataḥ prabhāte vimale dvādaśyāṃ dvādaśaiva tu ।। itihāsapurāṇajñāñ śrotriyān saṃyatendriyān ।।
snāpayet pūrvavat tatra pūjayet puruṣottamam ।। upacārair bahuvidhaiḥ praṇipātaiḥ pradakṣiṇaiḥ ।। saṃpūjyaivaṃ jagannāthaṃ brāhmaṇān pūjayet tataḥ ।। chattropānadyugaṃ caiva śraddhābhaktisamanvitaḥ ।।
sadbhāvena tu govindas toṣyate pūjito yataḥ ।। chattropānadyugaṃ cānyat kāṃsyapātraṃ ca bhaktitaḥ ।। pakvānnaṃ bhakṣyabhojyaṃ ca guḍasarpiḥsamanvitam ।। dvādaśaivodakumbhāṃś ca dadyāt tebhyaḥ samodakān ।।
kumbhaṃ ca dakṣiṇāṃ caiva ācāryāya nivedayet ।। pūjayet parayā bhaktyā viṣṇutulyaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। saṃpūjya taṃ namaskṛtya imaṃ mantram udīrayet ।। anādinidhano devaḥ prīyatāṃ puruṣottamaḥ ।।
praṇamya śirasā bhaktyā ācāryaṃ tu visarjayet ।। anuvrajya tu tān sarvān namaskṛtya nivartayet ।। anyaiś copāsakair dīnair bhikṣukaiś cānnakāṅkṣibhiḥ ।। aśvamedhasahasrāṇāṃ rājasūyaśatasya ca ।।
bhaviṣyaṃ ca śataṃ viprāḥ svargatyā divyarūpadhṛk ।। sarvakāmasamṛddhātmā devavad vigatajvaraḥ ।। stūyamāno apsarobhiś ca gandharvaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ ।। patākādhvajayuktena sarvaratnair alaṃkṛtaḥ ।।
yuvā mahābalo dhīmān viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। siddhāpsarobhir gandharvaiḥ suravidyādharoragaiḥ ।। yathā devo jagannāthaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।। bhuktvā tatra varān bhogān krīḍāṃ kṛtvā suraiḥ saha ।।
siddhavidyādharaiś cāpi śobhitaṃ surakiṃnaraiḥ ।। tasmād āyāti viprendrāḥ sarvakāmaphalapradam ।। anekaśatasāhasrair vimānaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam ।। aśītikalpakālaṃ tu tatra bhuktvā sukhaṃ naraḥ ।।
surasiddhāpsarobhiś ca śobhitaṃ sumanoharam ।। durlabhaṃ triṣu lokeṣu svasthacitto yathāmaraḥ ।। gandharvāpsarasaiḥ siddhair munividyādharair vṛtaḥ ।। tadante śakrabhavanaṃ nānāścaryasamanvitam ।।
guhyakāpsarasaiḥ sādhyair vṛtaiś cānyaiḥ surottamaiḥ ।। suralokaṃ tato gatvā vimānaiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ ।। āgacchate tato lokaṃ nakṣatrākhyaṃ sudurlabham ।। tasmād āgacchate lokaṃ śaśāṅkasya dvijottamāḥ ।।
tatra viṃśatikalpāṃs tu bhuktvā bhogaṃ sudurlabham ।। nānāścaryamayaṃ puṇyaṃ gandharvāpsaraḥsevitam ।। tasmād āyāti bhuvanaṃ gandharvāṇāṃ sudurlabham ।। bhuktvā cāyāti medinyāṃ rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ ।।
kṛtvā rājyaṃ svadharmeṇa yajñair iṣṭvā sudakṣiṇaiḥ ।। tatra bhuktvā varān bhogān yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam ।। pravare vaiṣṇave viprā durlabhe sādhusaṃmate ।। vaiṣṇavaṃ yogam āsthāya tato mokṣam avāpnuyāt ।।
bhuktimuktipradaṃ nṝṇāṃ kim anyac chrotum icchatha ।। lokānandakaraṃ kāntaṃ sarvāścaryasamanvitam ।। karmaṇā kena gacchanti tatra dharmaparāyaṇāḥ ।। vistarād brūhi tattvena paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।।
bhaktānām īhitaṃ dhanyaṃ puṇyaṃ saṃsāranāśanam ।। sarvāścaryamayaṃ puṇyaṃ sthānaṃ trailokyapūjitam ।। mālatīmallikākundair bakulair nāgakesaraiḥ ।। pāṭalācūtakhadiraiḥ karṇikāravanojjvalaiḥ ।।
drākṣālakucakharjūrair madhukendraphalair drumaiḥ ।। kalpavṛkṣair asaṃkhyaiś ca vanyair anyaiḥ suśobhanaiḥ ।। jātīlavaṅgakaṅkolaiḥ karpūrāmodavāsibhiḥ ।। anyaiś ca vividhair vṛkṣaiḥ sarvartuphalaśobhitaiḥ ।।
nānājalāśayaiḥ puṇyair nānāpakṣirutair varaiḥ ।। kumudaiḥ śatapattraiś ca puṣpaiḥ kokanadair varaiḥ ।। anyaiś ca jalajaiḥ puṣpair nānāvarṇaiḥ suśobhanaiḥ ।। koyaṣṭikaiś ca dātyūhaiḥ kāraṇḍavaravākulaiḥ ।।
anyair divyair jalacarair vihāramadhurasvanaiḥ ।। vṛkṣair jalāśayaiḥ puṇyair bhūṣitaṃ sumanoharaiḥ ।। kāmagaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ śubhrair divyagandharvanāditaiḥ ।। hemaśayyāsanayutair nānābhogasamanvitaiḥ ।।
nānāvarṇair asaṃkhyātair jātarūpaparicchadaiḥ ।। sukhapracārabahulair nānāvāditraniḥsvanaiḥ ।। viharanti pure tasmin vaiṣṇave lokapūjite ।। candrānanābhiḥ kāntābhir yoṣidbhiḥ sumanoharaiḥ ।।
śyāmāvadātavarṇābhir mattamātaṅgagāmibhiḥ ।। cāmarai rukmadaṇḍaiś ca nānāratnavibhūṣitaiḥ ।। yakṣavidyādharaiḥ siddhair gandharvair apsarogaṇaiḥ ।। tatra prāpya mahābhogān prāpnuvanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
dṛṣṭo yair bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ puṣkarākṣo jagatpatiḥ ।। prataptahemasaṃkāśā jarāmaraṇavarjitāḥ ।। caturbhujā mahāvīryā vanamālāvibhūṣitāḥ ।। kecin nīlotpalaśyāmāḥ kecit kāñcanasaṃnibhāḥ ।।
śyāmavarṇāḥ kuṇḍalinas tathānye vajrasaṃnibhāḥ ।। yādṛg bhāti harer lokaḥ sarvāścaryasamanvitaḥ ।। prabhāvāt tasya devasya yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam ।। kṛṣṇaṃ rāmaṃ subhadrāṃ ca paśyanti puruṣottame ।।
puramadhye harer bhāti mandiraṃ ratnabhūṣitam ।। yojanāyutavistīrṇaṃ hemaprākāraveṣṭitam ।। vibhāti śārado yadvan nakṣatraiḥ saha candramāḥ ।। purasaptakasaṃyuktaṃ mahotsekaṃ manoharam ।।
indranīlaṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu mahānīlaṃ tataḥ param ।। ṣaṣṭhaṃ vajramayaṃ viprā vaidūryaṃ saptamaṃ puram ।। stambhair adbhutasaṃkāśair bhāti tad bhavanaṃ mahat ।। paurṇamāsyāṃ sanakṣatro yathā bhāti niśākaraḥ ।।
pītāmbaradharaḥ śyāmaḥ śrīvatsalakṣmasaṃyutaḥ ।। dadhāra dakṣiṇe haste sarvatejomayaṃ hariḥ ।। ādāya taṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ savyahastena keśavaḥ ।। viśrutaṃ pāñcajanyeti sahasrāvartabhūṣitam ।।
jvaladvahniśikhākārāṃ duḥsahāṃ tridaśair api ।। vāme visphurati hy asya śārṅgaṃ sūryasamaprabham ।। yo asau saṃharate devas trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।। sarvalokagurur devaḥ sarvair devair namaskṛtaḥ ।।
sahasrākhyaḥ sahasrāṅgaḥ sahasrabhujavān prabhuḥ ।। vidyudvispaṣṭasaṃkāśo jagannātho jagadguruḥ ।। yakṣavidyādharair nāgair munisiddhaiḥ sacāraṇaiḥ ।। anyair devagaṇair divyaiḥ stūyamāno virājate ।।
buddhir matis tathā kṣāntiḥ siddhimūrtis tathā dyutiḥ ।। prabhā matis tathā kāntis tatra nārāyaṇī sthitā ।। nidrā rātris tathā māyā tathānyāmarayoṣitaḥ ।। atha kiṃ bahunoktena sarvaṃ tatra pratiṣṭhitam ।।
urvaśī caiva nimlocā tathānyā vāmanā parā ।। bhadrāṅgī citrasenā ca pramlocā sumanoharā ।। sukeśī nīlakeśā ca tathā manmathadīpinī ।। kratusthalā varāṅgī ca pūrvacittis tathā parā ।।
haṃsalīlānugāminyo mattavāraṇagāminī ।। etāś cānyā apsaraso rūpayauvanagarvitāḥ ।। gītamādhuryasaṃyuktāḥ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutāḥ ।। nṛtyanty anudinaṃ tatra yatrāsau puruṣottamaḥ ।।
na kṣut pipāsā na jarā na vairūpyaṃ na cāsukham ।। viṣṇulokāt paraṃ lokaṃ nātra paśyāmi bho dvijāḥ ।। viṣṇulokasya te viprāḥ kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।। sarvasaukhyakaraṃ puṇyaṃ sarvāścaryamayaṃ dvijāḥ ।।
na kṛtaghnā na piśunā no stenā nājitendriyāḥ ।। te tatra vaiṣṇavā yānti viṣṇulokaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaṃ ca rāmaṃ ca subhadrāṃ ca dvijottamāḥ ।। te tatra manujā yānti mṛtā ye puruṣottame ।।
te api tatra narā yānti ye mṛtāḥ puruṣottame ।। sarvānandakaraḥ prokto bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ ।। nityānandakaraḥ śrīmān bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ ।। tyaktvā yatra naro dehaṃ yāti sālokyatāṃ hareḥ ।।
yatra svadehasaṃtyāgād viṣṇulokaṃ vrajen naraḥ ।। narāṇām upakārāya puruṣākhye na saṃśayaḥ ।। tasmin kṣetre paraṃ viṣṇoḥ padaṃ yānti nirāmayam ।। prayāgapuṣkarādīni kṣetrāṇy āyatanāni ca ।।
na tathā tāni sarvāṇi praśaṃsasi surottama ।। jñāto asmābhir abhiprāyas tavedānīṃ pitāmaha ।। tena tvaṃ vibudhaśreṣṭha praśaṃsasi punaḥ punaḥ ।। puruṣākhyasamaṃ kṣetraṃ nāsty atra pṛthivītale ।।
tāni śrīpuruṣākhyasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।।
tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।।
tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।।
tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।।
tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tat puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tat puruṣottamam ।।
tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।।
tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।।
tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ variṣṭhaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tathā samastatīrthānāṃ kṣetraṃ ca tad dvijottamāḥ ।। tathā samastatīrthānām uttamaṃ puruṣottamam ।।
tathā samastatīrthānāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tat puruṣottamam ।। japahomavratānāṃ ca tapodānaphalāni ca ।। kiṃ cātra bahunoktena bhāṣitena punaḥ punaḥ ।। puruṣākhyaṃ sakṛd dṛṣṭvā sāgarāmbhaḥsamāplutam ।।
hareḥ saṃnihite sthāna uttame puruṣottame ।। tena japtaṃ hutaṃ tena tena taptaṃ tapo mahat ।। bhuktvā bhogān vicitrāṃś ca devayoṣitsamanvitaḥ ।। jāyate yogināṃ viprā jñānajñeyodyato gṛhe ।।
kalpavṛkṣasya rāmasya kṛṣṇasya bhadrayā saha ।। svargadvārasya māhātmyaṃ sāgarasya vidhiḥ kramāt ।। sarvam etan mayā khyātaṃ yat paraṃ śrotum icchatha ।। purāṇaṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ dhanyaṃ saṃsāramocanam ।।
paraṃ tīrthasya māhātmyaṃ sarvatīrthottamottamam ।। nāradena prayatnena tadā taṃ proktavān aham ।। sarvaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tvatto jagadyone jagatpate ।। sarveṣām eva tīrthānāṃ sarvadā kiṃ viśiṣyate ।।
daivāni muniśārdūla āsurāṇy āruṣāṇi ca ।। mānuṣebhyaś ca tīrthebhya ārṣaṃ tīrtham anuttamam ।। āsurebhyas tathā puṇyaṃ daivaṃ tat sārvakāmikam ।। tribhyo yad ekaṃ jāyeta tasmān nātaḥ paraṃ viduḥ ।।
tatrāpi jāmbavaṃ dvīpaṃ tīrthaṃ bahuguṇodayam ।। karmabhūmir yataḥ putra tasmāt tīrthaṃ tad ucyate ।। himavadvindhyayor madhye ṣaṇnadyo devasaṃbhavāḥ ।। etā dvādaśa nadyas tu prādhānyena prakīrtitāḥ ।।
karmabhūmir ato devair varṣaṃ tasmāt prakīrtitam ।। āsurair āvṛtāny āsaṃs tad evāsuram ucyate ।। daivaprabhāvāt tapasa ārṣāṇy api ca tāny api ।। ātmanaḥ phalabhūtyarthaṃ yaśaso avāptaye punaḥ ।।
evaṃ caturvidho bhedas tīrthānāṃ munisattama ।। sukṛtī ko api jānāti vaktuṃ śrotuṃ nijair guṇaiḥ ।। yac chrutvā sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। tīrthasevāṃ vinā svalpā- yāsenābhīṣṭadāyinīm ।।
tvaṃ nābhikamale viṣṇoḥ saṃjāto akhilapūrvajaḥ ।। tāpī payouṣṇī vindhyasya dakṣiṇe tu prakīrtitāḥ ।। viśokā ca vitastā ca himavatparvatāśritāḥ ।। gayaḥ kollāsuro vṛtras tripuro hy andhakas tathā ।।
yamaḥ pātālaketuś ca mayaḥ puṣkara eva ca ।। prabhāso bhārgavo agastir naranārāyaṇau tathā ।। ityādimunijuṣṭāni ṛṣitīrthāni nārada ।। kuruḥ kanakhalaś caiva bhadrāśvaḥ sagaras tathā ।।
ityādimānuṣair vipra nirmitāni śubhāni ca ।। puṇyatīrthāni tāny āhus tīrthabhedo mayoditaḥ ।। tasya svarūpabhedaṃ ca vistareṇa bravītu me ।। tāvad yajñādayo yāvat tridaivatyaṃ na dṛśyate ।।
tridaivatyā muniśreṣṭha tadutpattim ataḥ śṛṇu ।। tārako balavān āsīn madvarād atigarvitaḥ ।। tatas te śaraṇaṃ jagmur devāḥ sendrapurogamāḥ ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭā devā viṣṇum ūcur ananyagāḥ ।।
sarveśvara jagadyone trayīmūrte namo astu te ।। sthityutpattivināśānāṃ kāraṇaṃ tvaṃ jaganmaya ।। ityādirūpabhedair no rakṣase bhaya āgate ।। kasmān na rakṣase deva ananyaśaraṇān hare ।।
tataḥ śriyaḥ patiṃ prāhus taṃ tārakavadhaṃ prati ।। na yuddhais tapasā śāpair hantuṃ naiva kṣamā vayam ।। tasmād deva na cānyebhyas tatra nītir vidhīyatām ।। na matto madapatyāc ca na devebhyo vadho bhavet ।।
tasmād vadham avāpnoti tārako lokadāruṇaḥ ।। bhāryārthaṃ prathamo yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ prabhaviṣṇubhiḥ ।। himavantaṃ ratnamayaṃ menāṃ ca himavatpriyām ।। idam ūcuḥ sarva eva sabhāryaṃ tuhinaṃ girim ।।
buddhiḥ prajñā dhṛtir medhā lajjā puṣṭiḥ sarasvatī ।। devānāṃ kāryasiddhyarthaṃ yuvayor garbham āviśat ।। asmākaṃ bhavatāṃ cāpi pālanī ca bhaviṣyati ।। menā cāpi mahotsāhā astv ity evaṃ vaco abravīt ।।
śivadhyānaratā nityaṃ tanniṣṭhā tanmanogatā ।। tathā himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe gaurī tepe tapo mahat ।। ātmānaṃ vā tathānyad vā na jānīmaḥ kathaṃ bhavaḥ ।। tataḥ prāha mahābuddhir vācaspatir udāradhīḥ ।।
sa vidhyatu śivaṃ śāntaṃ bāṇaiḥ puṣpamayaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। pariṇeṣyaty asau nūnaṃ tadā tāṃ girijāṃ haraḥ ।। tathoḍhāyāṃ jagaddhātryāṃ śaṃbhoḥ putro bhaviṣyati ।। vasantaṃ ca sahāyārthaṃ śobhiṣṭhaṃ kusumākaram ।।
āhlādanaṃ ca manasā kāmāyainaṃ prayacchatha ।। preṣayām āsur avyagrāḥ śivāntikam ariṃdamāḥ ।। ratyā ca sahitaḥ kāmaḥ kartuṃ karma suduṣkaram ।। mayā vedhyas tv avedhyo vai śaṃbhur lokaguruḥ prabhuḥ ।।
tenāsau cāgninetreṇa bhasmaśeṣas tadā kṛtaḥ ।। ājagmus tatra yad vṛttaṃ śṛṇu vismayakārakam ।। tuṣṭuvus tridaśeśānaṃ kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ surāḥ ।। tārakād bhayam āpannaṃ kuru patnīṃ gireḥ sutām ।।
arundhatīṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca māṃ tu cakradharaṃ tathā ।। saṃbandho api tathāpy āsīd dhimavallokanāthayoḥ ।। nānāvṛkṣalatākīrṇe nānādvijaniṣevite ।। devagandharvayakṣādi- siddhacāraṇasevite ।।
merumandarakailāsa- mainākādinagair vṛte ।। mahotsave vartamāne vivāhaḥ samajāyata ।। vajramāṇikyavaidūrya- tanmayastambhaśobhitā ।। merumandarakailāsa- raivataiḥ pariśobhitaiḥ ।।
mainākaḥ parvataśreṣṭho reje atīva hiraṇmayaḥ ।। vivāhe vedikāṃ cakrur devadevasya śūlinaḥ ।। surabhī nandinī nandā sunandā kāmadohinī ।। samudrāḥ sarito nāgā oṣadhyo lokamātaraḥ ।।
bhuvaḥ karma ilā cakre oṣadhyas tv annakarma ca ।। agniś cakāra tatrānnaṃ yac ceṣṭaṃ lokanāthayoḥ ।। vedāś ca sarahasyā vai gāyanti ca hasanti ca ।। lājādhṛk cāpi maināko babhūva munisattama ।।
vedikāyām upāviṣṭau daṃpatī surasattamau ।। hutvā lājāṃś ca vidhivat pradakṣiṇam athākarot ।। viṣṇunā preritaḥ śaṃbhur dakṣiṇasya padasya ca ।। dṛṣṭe aṅguṣṭhe duṣṭabuddhyā vīryaṃ susrāva me tadā ।।
madvīryāc cūrṇitāt sūkṣmād vālakhilyās tu jajñire ।। lajjayā paribhūto ahaṃ nirgatas tu tadāsanāt ।। gacchantaṃ māṃ mahādevo dṛṣṭvā nandinam abravīt ।। mohayanty api vidvāṃsaṃ viṣayāṇām iyaṃ sthitiḥ ।।
mamānukampayā caiva lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। pāpināṃ pāpamokṣāya bhūmir āpo bhaviṣyati ।। evaṃ niścitya bhagavāṃs tayoḥ sāraṃ samāharat ।। pāvamānyādibhiḥ sūktair abhimantrya ca yatnataḥ ।।
mām uvāca sa lokeśo gṛhāṇemaṃ kamaṇḍalum ।। sthityutpattivināśānāṃ hetutvam ubhayoḥ sthitam ।। atra bhuktiś ca muktiś ca sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ tathā ।। snānapānābhiṣekāc ca praṇaśyaty api kāyikam ।।
mayābhimantritaṃ brahman gṛhāṇemaṃ kamaṇḍalum ।। sa sarvakāmān āpnoti gṛhāṇemaṃ kamaṇḍalum ।। tāsām utkṛṣṭam etasmād gṛhāṇemaṃ kamaṇḍalum ।। spṛṣṭvā smṛtvā ca dṛṣṭvā ca brahman pāpād vimokṣyase ।।
āhlādaś ca mahāṃs tatra jayaśabdo vyavartata ।। yathā martyaṃ gatā nātha tan me vistarato vada ।। dharmeṇa yaśasā caiva prajāsaṃrakṣaṇena ca ।। tyāgena kṣamayā caiva trailokye nopamīyate ।।
mithaḥ samūcur amarā jeṣyāmo vai kathaṃ balim ।। nārayo vyādhayo vāpi nādhayo vā kathaṃcana ।। svapne api naiva dṛśyeta balau rājyaṃ praśāsati ।। tasyājñāśaktibhinnāṅgā devāḥ śarma na lebhire ।।
tadyaśognipradīptāṅgā viṣṇuṃ jagmuḥ suvihvalāḥ ।। asmadarthe bhavān nityam āyudhāni bibharti ca ।। tvāṃ tu praṇamatī vāṇī kathaṃ daityaṃ namasyati ।। tvadaṅghriśaraṇāḥ santaḥ kathaṃ daityaṃ namemahi ।।
tvadekaśaraṇāḥ santaḥ kathaṃ daityaṃ namemahi ।। tvayā dattaṃ padaṃ prāpya kathaṃ daityaṃ namemahi ।। saṃhartā rudraśaktyā tvaṃ kathaṃ daityaṃ namemahi ।। hataiśvaryāḥ sureśāna kathaṃ daityaṃ namemahi ।।
antavantam amuṃ śatruṃ kathaṃ daityaṃ namemahi ।। sthirāḥ syāmaḥ sureśāna kathaṃ daityaṃ namemahi ।। uvāca sarvān amarān devānāṃ kāryasiddhaye ।। yathā bhavanto matpoṣyās tathā poṣyo balir mama ।।
baliṃ nibadhya mantroktyā rājyaṃ vaḥ pradadāmy aham ।। bhagavān api deveśo hy adityā garbham āviśat ।। jāto asau vāmano brahman yajñeśo yajñapūruṣaḥ ।। balir balavatāṃ śreṣṭha ṛṣimukhyaiḥ samāhitaḥ ।।
makhe tasmin vartamāne yajamāne balau tathā ।। havirbhāgārtham āsanna- devagandharvapannage ।। paripūrṇaṃ punaḥ pūrṇam evaṃ vākye pravartati ।। yajñavāṭam anuprāpto vāmanaś citrakuṇḍalaḥ ।।
brahmarūpadharaṃ devaṃ vāmanaṃ daityasūdanam ।। jñātvā tvarann athovāca rājānaṃ bhūritejasam ।। baliṃ balavatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sabhāryaṃ dīkṣitaṃ makhe ।। tam āha bhṛguśārdūlaḥ śukraḥ paramabuddhimān ।।
nāsau vipro bale satyaṃ yajñeśo yajñavāhanaḥ ।। mayā ca saha saṃmantrya paścād deyaṃ tvayā prabho ।। balis tu bhārgavaṃ prāha purodhasam ariṃdamaḥ ।। āgatya yācate kiṃcit kiṃ mantryam avaśiṣyate ।।
jagāma yatra viprendro vāmano aditinandanaḥ ।। vāmano api tadā prāha padatrayamitāṃ bhuvam ।। tathety uktvā tu kalaśān nānāratnavibhūṣitāt ।। paśyatsu ṛṣimukhyeṣu śukre caiva purodhasi ।।
paśyatsu daityasaṃgheṣu jayaśabde pravartati ।। dehi me saṃmitāṃ bhūmiṃ tripadām āśu gamyate ।। yajñeśo yajñapuruṣaś candrādityau stanāntare ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā daityarāṭ prāha sabhāryo vinayānvitaḥ ।।
jitaṃ mayā sureśāna sarvabhāvena viśvakṛt ।। tadvākyasamakālaṃ tu viṣṇuḥ prāha mahākratuḥ ।। daityeśvara mahābāho kramiṣye paśya daityarāṭ ।। evaṃ vadantaṃ sa prāha krama viṣṇo punaḥ punaḥ ।।
dvitīyaṃ tu padaṃ prāpa brahmalokaṃ sanātanam ।। vihasya balir apy āha sabhāryaḥ sa kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। tvaddoṣād alpam abhavat kiṃ karomi jaganmaya ।। satyavākyaṃ ca māṃ kurvan matpṛṣṭhe hi padaṃ nyasa ।।
tataḥ prasanno bhagavāṃs trayīmūrtiḥ surārcitaḥ ।। varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te bhaktyā prīto asmi daityarāṭ ।। sa tu prādāt svayaṃ viṣṇuḥ prītaḥ san manasepsitam ।। ātmādhipatyaṃ ca harir avināśi yaśo vibhuḥ ।।
rasātale hariḥ sthāpya baliṃ tv amaravairiṇam ।। etasminn antare tatra padaṃ prāgāt surārcitam ।। yat padaṃ samanuprāptaṃ gṛhaṃ dṛṣṭvāpy acintayam ।। sarvasvaṃ ca samālokya śreṣṭho me syāt kamaṇḍaluḥ ।।
varaṃ vareṇyaṃ varadaṃ varaṃ śāntikaraṃ param ।। mātṛsvarūpaṃ lokānām amṛtaṃ bheṣajaṃ śuci ।। smaraṇād eva lokānāṃ pāvanaṃ kiṃ nu darśanāt ।। iti saṃcintya tad vāri gṛhītvārghāya kalpitam ।।
tad vāri patitaṃ merau caturdhā vyagamad bhuvam ।। dakṣiṇe yat tu patitaṃ jaṭābhiḥ śaṃkaro mune ।। uttare patitaṃ yat tu viṣṇur jagrāha taj jalam ।। jagṛhuḥ śubhadaṃ vāri tasmāc chreṣṭhaṃ tad ucyate ।।
viṣṇupādaprasūtās tā brahmaṇyā lokamātaraḥ ।। tāsāṃ prabhāvasmaraṇāt sarvakāmān avāpnuyāt ।। śrutā deva yathā martyam āgatā tad bravītu me ।। tāsāṃ ca dvividho bheda āhartur dvayakāraṇāt ।।
gotamena śivaṃ pūjya āhṛto lokaviśrutaḥ ।। ārādhya śaṃkaraṃ devaṃ tapobhir niyamais tathā ।। evaṃ dvairūpyam abhavad gaṅgāyā munisattama ।। āhartā kṣatriyeṇāpi āhṛtā kena tad vada ।।
tat sarvaṃ vistareṇāhaṃ vadiṣye prītaye tava ।। tasminn evābhavad gaṅgā priyā śaṃbhor mahāmate ।। umayā sahitaḥ śrīmān devīṃ prekṣya viśeṣataḥ ।। rasikatvāt priyatvāc ca straiṇatvāt pāvanatvataḥ ।।
sa tu saṃgopayām āsa gaṅgāṃ śaṃbhur jaṭāgatām ।। soḍhuṃ brahmañ jaṭājūṭe sthitāṃ dṛṣṭvā punaḥ punaḥ ।। naivāsau prairayac chaṃbhū rasiko rasam uttamam ।। vināyakaṃ jayāṃ skandaṃ raho vacanam abravīt ।।
sāpi priyā śivasyādya kathaṃ tyajati tāṃ priyām ।। evaṃ vimṛśya bahuśo gaurī cāha vināyakam ।। na rājabhir athānyair vā na gaṅgāṃ tyajati prabhuḥ ।। athavā brāhmaṇaiḥ puṇyais tapobhir hatakalmaṣaiḥ ।।
tair vā jaṭāsthitā gaṅgā prārthitā bhuvam āpnuyāt ।। bhrātrā skandena jayayā saṃmantryeha ca yujyate ।। etasminn antare brahmann anāvṛṣṭir ajāyata ।। tato vinaṣṭam abhavaj jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam ।।
sraṣṭukāmaḥ purā putra sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ tathā ।। mannāmā tatra vikhyātas tato brahmagiriḥ sadā ।। tasyāśrame mahāpuṇye śreṣṭhe brahmagirau śubhe ।। bhayaśokau ca dāridryaṃ na śrūyante kadācana ।।
nāsti putra tathā dātā hotā yaṣṭā tathaiva ca ।। tadaivāpy ayanaṃ svarge surāṇām api nānyataḥ ।। hotā dātā ca bhoktā ca sa eveti janā viduḥ ।। gautamāśramam āpṛcchann āgacchantas tapodhanāḥ ।।
śiṣyavat putravad bhaktyā pitṛvat poṣako abhavat ।। yathānurūpaṃ sarveṣāṃ śuśrūṣām akaron muniḥ ।। ārādhitāḥ punas tena brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ।। saṃpatsyante tadopyante gautamasya tapobalāt ।।
pratyahaṃ vakti vinayād gautamas tv āgatān munīn ।। pitṛvat poṣayām āsa saṃvatsaragaṇān bahūn ।। tato vināyakaḥ prāha mātaraṃ bhrātaraṃ jayām ।। yan na sādhyaṃ suragaṇair gautamaḥ kṛtavān iti ।।
sa vipraś cālayed enāṃ mātar gaṅgāṃ jaṭāgatām ।। sa eva cyāvayed enāṃ jaṭāsthāṃ me pitṛpriyām ।। tatprabhāvāt saricchreṣṭhā śiraso avataraty api ।। jagāma gautamo yatra brahmasūtradharaḥ kṛśaḥ ।।
uvāca brāhmaṇān sarvāṃs tatra tatra ca vighnarāṭ ।। puṣṭāḥ sma gautamānnena pṛcchāmo gautamaṃ munim ।। sa tān nivārayām āsa snehabuddhyā munīn pṛthak ।। yuṣmaccaraṇaśuśrūṣāṃ karomi munipuṃgavāḥ ।।
bhavatāṃ bhūmidevānām āśramāntarasevanam ।। alam anyena munaya āśrameṇa gatena vā ।। uvāca prāñjalir bhūtvā brāhmaṇān sa gaṇādhipaḥ ।। sāmnā naiva vayaṃ śaktā gantuṃ svaṃ svaṃ niveśanam ।।
tasmād buddhyā vyavasyāmi tat sarvair anumanyatām ।। etasya tūpakārāya lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। brāhmaṇānāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā mene vākyaṃ gaṇādhipaḥ ।। kriyate guṇarūpaṃ yad gautamasya viśeṣataḥ ।।
mātur mate sthito vidvāñ jayāṃ prāha gaṇeśvaraḥ ।। gorūpadhāriṇī gaccha gautamo yatra tiṣṭhati ।। pata dīnaṃ svanaṃ kṛtvā na mriyasva na jīva ca ।। yatrāsīd gautamo vipro jayā gorūpadhāriṇī ।।
gāṃ dṛṣṭvā vikṛtāṃ vipras tāṃ tṛṇena nyavārayat ।। tasyāṃ tu patitāyāṃ ca hāhākāro mahān abhūt ।। vyathitā brāhmaṇāḥ prāhur vighnarājapuraskṛtāḥ ।। putravat poṣitāḥ sarve pṛṣṭo asi munipuṃgava ।।
vajrāhata ivāsīt sa viprāṇāṃ purato apatat ।। rudrāṇāṃ mātaraṃ devīṃ jagatāṃ pāvanīṃ priyām ।। patitāyāṃ muniśreṣṭha gantavyam avaśiṣyate ।। vayaṃ nānyadhanā brahman kevalaṃ tu tapodhanāḥ ।।
viprāṇāṃ purataḥ sthitvā vinītaḥ prāha gautamaḥ ।। bhavanta eva śaraṇaṃ pūtaṃ māṃ kartum arhatha ।। tataḥ provāca bhagavān vighnarāḍ brāhmaṇair vṛtaḥ ।। vadāmo asmin susaṃdigdhe niṣkṛtiṃ gatim eva vā ।।
vaktum arhatha tat sarvaṃ kariṣye aham asaṃśayam ।। etad vākyam athāsmākaṃ pramāṇaṃ tava gautama ।। vighnakṛd brahmavapuṣā prāha sarvān idaṃ vacaḥ ।। anumanyantu munayo madvākyaṃ gautamo api ca ।।
kamaṇḍalusthitaṃ vāri tiṣṭhatīti hi śuśruma ।। tato vatsyāmahe sarve pūrvavat tava veśmani ।। tataḥ kṛtāñjalir namro gautamo vākyam abravīt ।। bhavatāṃ ca prasādena matsaṃkalpo anusidhyatām ।।
svāni sthānāni te jagmuḥ samṛddhāny annavāribhiḥ ।। jayayā saha suprītaḥ kṛtakṛtyo nyavartata ।। gautamo api muniśreṣṭhas tapasā hatakalmaṣaḥ ।। ity evaṃ bahuśo dhyāyañ jñānena jñātavān dvija ।।
lokānām upakāraṃ ca śaṃbhoḥ prīṇanam eva ca ।। sarvaṃ śreyaskaraṃ manye mayi naiva ca kilbiṣam ।। ārādhya jagatām īśaṃ trinetraṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam ।। sapatnī jagadambāyā maheśvarajaṭāsthitā ।।
kiṃ cakāra tapo vāpi kāṃ cakre stutim uttamām ।। āstīrya sa kuśān prājñaḥ kailāse parvatottame ।। apatat puṣpavṛṣṭiś ca stūyamāne maheśvare ।। umayā sahitaḥ śrīmān gaṇeśādigaṇair vṛtaḥ ।।
sākṣād āgatya taṃ śaṃbhuḥ prasanno vākyam abravīt ।। parituṣṭo asmi yācasva devānām api duṣkaram ।। harṣabāṣpaparītāṅgo gautamaḥ paryacintayat ।। aho lokagatiś citrā aho dhātar namo astu te ।।
yadi tuṣṭo asi deveśa trayīdhāma namo astu te ।। ātmanas tūpakārāya tad yācasvākutobhayaḥ ।। sarvakāmasamṛddhāḥ syur etad dhi varayāmy aham ।। anyān api varān matto yācasva vigatajvaraḥ ।।
evam uktas tu harṣeṇa gautamaḥ prāha śaṃkaram ।। tava priyāṃ jagannātha utsṛja brahmaṇo girau ।। brahmahatyādipāpāni manovākkāyikāni ca ।। candrasūryoparāge ca ayane viṣuve tathā ।।
asyās tu smaraṇād eva tat puṇyaṃ jāyatāṃ hara ।। dvāpare yajñadāne ca dānam eva kalau yuge ।। deśakālādisaṃyoge yo dharmo yatra śasyate ।। asyās tu smaraṇād eva tat puṇyaṃ jāyatāṃ hara ।।
tatra tatra tvayā bhāvyam eṣa cāstu varo varaḥ ।। tadantarapraviṣṭānāṃ mahāpātakinām api ।। snāne cāpy antare mṛtyor muktibhājo bhavantu vai ।। eṣā tebhyo viśiṣṭā tu alaṃ śaṃbho namo astu te ।।
asyāḥ parataraṃ tīrthaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati ।। sarveṣāṃ gautamī puṇyā ity uktvāntaradhīyata ।। puṣpavṛṣṭir abhūt tatra samājagmuḥ sureśvarāḥ ।। jayaśabdena taṃ vipraṃ pūjayanto mudānvitāḥ ।।
āgatya brahmaṇaḥ puṇye tataḥ kim akarod girau ।। pūjito devagandharvais tathā girinivāsibhiḥ ।। uvāca prāñjalir bhūtvā gaṅgāṃ sa dvijasattamaḥ ।। kṣamasva mātaḥ śāntāsi sukhaṃ yāhi hitaṃ kuru ।।
divyarūpadharā devī divyasraganulepanā ।। rasātalaṃ vā gaccheyaṃ jātas tvaṃ satyavāg asi ।। śaṃbhunā ca tathā dattā devi tan nānyathā bhavet ।। tredhātmānaṃ vibhajyātha svargamartyarasātale ।।
rasātale caturdhaiva saivaṃ pañcadaśākṛtiḥ ।। sarvakāmapradā nityaṃ saiva vede pragīyate ।। naiva svargagatāṃ martyāḥ paśyanty ajñānabuddhayaḥ ।। utsṛṣṭā gautamenaiva prāyāt pūrvārṇavaṃ prati ।।
gautamo muniśārdūlaḥ pradakṣiṇam athākarot ।। ubhayos tīrayoḥ snānaṃ karomīti dadhe matim ।। tatra snānaṃ kathaṃ sidhyed ity evaṃ śarvam abravīt ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā bhaktinamras trilocanam ।।
brūhi samyaṅ maheśāna lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। pūrvaṃ nāndīmukhaṃ kṛtvā dehaśuddhiṃ vidhāya ca ।। brahmacaryeṇa gacchanti patitālāpavarjitāḥ ।। vidyā tapaś ca kīrtiś ca sa tīrthaphalam aśnute ।।
śrāntasaṃvāhanaṃ kurvan dadyād annaṃ yathocitam ।। anena vidhinā gacchan samyak tīrthaphalaṃ labhet ।। tryambakaś ca iti prāha gautamaṃ munibhir vṛtam ।। sarvatrāhaṃ saṃnihitaḥ sarvakāmapradas tathā ।।
eteṣu puṇyadā puṃsāṃ muktidā sā bhagīrathī ।। yamunā saṃgatā tatra prabhāse tu sarasvatī ।। tisṛṇāṃ saṃgamo yatra tat tīrthaṃ muktidaṃ nṛṇām ।। iyaṃ tu gautamī vatsa yatra kvāpi mamājñayā ।।
kiṃcitkāle puṇyatamaṃ kiṃcittīrthaṃ surāgame ।। tisraḥ koṭyo ardhakoṭī ca yojanānāṃ śatadvaye ।। iyaṃ māheśvarī gaṅgā gautamī vaiṣṇavīti ca ।। brahmatejaḥsamānītā sarvapāpapraṇāśanī ।।
pañcānām api bhūtānām āpaḥ śreṣṭhatvam āgatāḥ ।। tāsāṃ bhāgīrathī śreṣṭhā tābhyo api gautamī tathā ।। svarge bhuvi tale vāpi tīrthaṃ sarvārthadaṃ mune ।। sākṣād dhareṇa tuṣṭena mayā tava niveditam ।।
tatsvarūpaṃ ca kathitaṃ kuto anyā śravaṇaspṛhā ।। eko bhedas tu kathito brāhmaṇenāhṛto yataḥ ।। bhavasya devadevasya āhṛtas tad vadasva me ।। purā vai sagaro nāma rājāsīd atidhārmikaḥ ।।
tasya bhāryādvayaṃ cāsīt patibhaktiparāyaṇam ।। vasiṣṭhaṃ gṛham āhūya saṃpūjya vidhivat tataḥ ।। iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā dhyātvā rājānam abravīt ।। sapatnīkaḥ sadā rājann ṛṣipūjāparo bhava ।।
ekadā tasya rājarṣer gṛham āgāt taponidhiḥ ।। varaṃ brūhi mahābhāgety ukte putrān sa cāvṛṇot ।। putro bhūyāt tathānyasyāṃ ṣaṣṭisāhasrakaṃ sutāḥ ।। sa yajñān subahūṃś cakre hayamedhān sudakṣiṇān ।।
putrān nyayojayad rājā sasainyān hayarakṣaṇe ।। mārgamāṇāś ca te putrā naivāpaśyan hayaṃ tadā ।। teṣu paśyatsu rakṣāṃsi putreṣu sagarasya hi ।। rākṣasān māyayā yuktān naivāpaśyanta sāgarāḥ ।।
itaś cetaś carantas te naivāpaśyan hayaṃ tadā ।। vanāni ca vicinvanto naivāpaśyan hayaṃ tadā ।। adṛṣṭvā tu paśuṃ ramyaṃ rājā cintām upeyivān ।। hayaṃ tam anucinvantas tatrāpi na hayo abhavat ।।
tatrāpi ca hayaṃ naiva dṛṣṭavanto nṛpātmajāḥ ।। rasātale hayo baddha āste nānyatra sāgarāḥ ।। akhanan pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ paritaḥ sāgarās tataḥ ।। nyakhanaṃś cāpi jagmuś ca satvarās te rasātalam ।।
śrutvā rakṣāṃsi saṃtrastā vyagaman kapilāntikam ।। purā ca sādhitaṃ tena devānāṃ kāryam uttamam ।। abravīt kapilaḥ śrīmān nidrāsthānaṃ prayacchatha ।। yo mām utthāpayen mando bhasmī bhūyāc ca satvaram ।।
tathety uktaḥ suragaṇais tatra śete rasātale ।। sāgarāṇāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ vadhopāyaṃ pracakrire ।। āgatya yatra sa muniḥ kapilaḥ kopano mahān ।। dūre sthitvā mauninaś ca prekṣantaḥ kiṃ bhaved iti ।।
dadṛśus te hayaṃ baddhaṃ śayānaṃ puruṣaṃ tathā ।। enaṃ hatvā mahāpāpaṃ nayāmo aśvaṃ nṛpāntikam ।। tadāhur apare śūrā rājānaḥ śāsakā vayam ।। te taṃ jaghnur muniṃ pādair bruvanto niṣṭhurāṇi ca ।।
sāgarān īkṣayām āsa tān kopād bhasmasāt karot ।। tat tu sarvaṃ na jānāti dīkṣitaḥ sagaro nṛpaḥ ।। kapilasya tu saṃsthānaṃ hayasyāpi tu saṃsthitim ।। tataś cintāparo rājā kartavyaṃ nāvabudhyata ।।
sa tu bālāṃs tathā paurān maurkhyāt kṣipati cāmbhasi ।। durnayaṃ tasya taṃ jñātvā tataḥ kruddho abravīn nṛpaḥ ।। asamañjāḥ kṣatradharma- tyāgī vai bālaghātakaḥ ।। tatyajur nṛpateḥ putram asamañjā gato vanam ।।
eko api ca vanaṃ prāpta idānīṃ kā gatir mama ।। ānāyya bālakaṃ rājā kāryaṃ tasmai nyavedayat ।। sagarāya hayaṃ prādāt tataḥ pūrṇo abhavat kratuḥ ।। tasyāpi putro matimān bhagīratha iti śrutaḥ ।।
sagaraṃ nṛpaśārdūlaṃ papraccha vinayānvitaḥ ।। bhagīrathaṃ nṛpaḥ prāha kapilo vetti putraka ।। kapilaṃ ca namaskṛtvā sarvaṃ tasmai nyavedayat ।। jaṭājalena svapitṝn āplāvya nṛpasattama ।।
