tathā karomīti muniṃ praṇamya punar abravīt ।। kva gacche ahaṃ muniśreṣṭha kartavyaṃ cāpi tad vada ।। tapaḥ kuru yathāśakti tataś cepsitam āpsyasi ।। tapase niścayaṃ kṛtvā uvāca sa bhagīrathaḥ ।।
nāhaṃ kimapi jānāmi tataḥ prīto bhava prabho ।। vareṇa cchandayāno vai bhagīratham uvāca ha ।। vadasva nirbhayo bhūtvā bhagīratha mahāmate ।। bhagīrathaḥ praṇamyeśaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ provāca śaṃkaram ।।
tām eva dehi deveśa sarvam āptaṃ tato bhavet ।। maheśo api vihasyātha bhagīratham uvāca ha ।। dattā mayeyaṃ te putra punas tāṃ stuhi suvrata ।। stutiṃ cakāra gaṅgāyā bhaktyā prayatamānasaḥ ।।
gaṅgāṃ maheśvarāt prāptām ādāyāgād rasātalam ।। yathoditaprakāreṇa gaṅgāṃ saṃsthāpya yatnataḥ ।। pradakṣiṇam athāvartya kṛtāñjalipuṭo abravīt ।। prāptās te vigatiṃ mātas tasmāt tān pātum arhasi ।।
lokānām upakārārthaṃ pitṝṇāṃ pāvanāya ca ।। smaraṇād eva pāpānāṃ nāśāya suranimnagā ।। bhasmībhūtān nṛpasutān sāgarāṃś ca viśeṣataḥ ।। tato meruṃ samāplāvya sthitāṃ bālo abravīn nṛpaḥ ।।
himavatparvatāt puṇyād bhārataṃ varṣam abhyagāt ।। evam eṣāpi te proktā gaṅgā kṣātrā mahāmune ।। bhāgīrathī devanadī himavacchikharāśrayā ।। uttare sāpi vindhyasya bhāgīrathy abhidhīyate ।।
pṛthak tīrthaphalaṃ śrotuṃ pravṛttaṃ mama mānasam ।। pṛthak tīrthaphalaṃ puṇyaṃ setihāsaṃ yathākramam ।। sarvaṃ vaktuṃ na śaknomi na ca tvaṃ śravaṇe kṣamaḥ ।। yāny uktāni ca tīrthāni śrutivākyāni yāni ca ।।
yatrāsau bhagavān āsīt pratyakṣas tryambako mune ।। vārāham aparaṃ tīrthaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam ।। purā devān parābhūya yajñam ādāya rākṣasaḥ ।। yajñe talam anuprāpte niryajñā hy abhavan mahī ।।
surās tam eva viviśū rasātalam anudviṣam ।। viṣṇuṃ purāṇapuruṣaṃ gatvā tasmai nyavedayan ।। tataḥ provāca bhagavān vārāhaṃ vapur āsthitaḥ ।। ānayiṣye makhaṃ puṇyaṃ hatvā rākṣasapuṃgavān ।।
yena gaṅgā talaṃ prāptā pathā tenaiva cakradhṛk ।। sa varāhavapuḥ śrīmān rasātalanivāsinaḥ ।। vārāharūpī bhagavān makham ādāya yajñabhuk ।। mukhe nyasya mahāyajñaṃ niścakrāma rasātalāt ।।
pathas tasmād viniḥsṛtya gaṅgāsravaṇam abhyagāt ।। gaṅgāmbhasā tatra kuṇḍaṃ vārāham abhavat tataḥ ।। dattavāṃs tridaśaśreṣṭho mukhād yajño abhyajāyata ।। vārāharūpam abhavad evaṃ vai kāraṇāntarāt ।।
tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvakratuphalapradam ।। vimuktāḥ sarvapāpebhyaḥ pitaraḥ svargam āpnuyuḥ ।। tasya smaraṇamātreṇa kṛtakṛtyo bhaven naraḥ ।। kuśenāvartitaṃ yatra gautamena mahātmanā ।।
tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ tṛptidāyakam ।। tatra snānādi yat kiṃcit karoti prayato naraḥ ।। viśrutaṃ triṣu lokeṣu kapotaṃ tīrtham uttamam ।। tatra brahmagirau kaścid vyādhaḥ paramadāruṇaḥ ।।
evaṃbhūtaḥ sa pāpātmā krodhano anṛtabhāṣaṇaḥ ।। danturo naṣṭanāsākṣo hrasvapāt pṛthukukṣikaḥ ।। pāśahastaḥ pāpacittaḥ pāpiṣṭhaḥ sadhanuḥ sadā ।। tayā tu preryamāṇo asau viveśa gahanaṃ vanam ।।
pañjare prākṣipat kāṃścij jīvamānāṃs tathetarān ।। bhrāntadeśo bahutaraṃ nyavartata gṛhaṃ prati ।। kṣaṇāt taḍid garjitaṃ ca sābhraṃ caivābhavat tadā ।। sa gacchaṃl lubdhakaḥ śrāntaḥ panthānaṃ nāvabudhyata ।।
na bubodha tadā pāpaḥ śrāntaḥ śaraṇam apy atha ।। sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ prāṇān āhartāhaṃ yathāntakaḥ ।। trātāraṃ naiva paśyāmi śilāṃ vā vṛkṣam antike ।। vane vanaspatim iva nakṣatrāṇāṃ yathātrijam ।।
indriyāṇāṃ mana iva trātāraṃ prāṇināṃ nagam ।। tam āśrityopaviṣṭo abhūt klinnavāsā sa lubdhakaḥ ।। etasminn antare tatra cāstaṃ prāpto divākaraḥ ।। putrapautraiḥ parivṛto hy āste tatra nagottame ।।
bahavo vatsarā yātā vasatas tasya pakṣiṇaḥ ।। koṭare tannage śreṣṭhe jalavāyvagnivarjite ।। tasmin dine daivavaśāt kapotaś ca kapotakī ।। sāpi daivavaśāt putra pañjarasthaiva vartate ।।
kapotako apy apatyāni mātṛhīnāny udīkṣya ca ।। svakoṭaraṃ tayā hīnam ālokya vilalāpa saḥ ।। anvārebhe kapoto vai priyāyā guṇakīrtanam ।। mama dharmasya jananī mama dehasya ceśvarī ।।
tuṣṭe hasantī ruṣṭe ca mama duḥkhapramārjanī ।। nādyāpy āyāti kalyāṇī saṃprayāte api bhāskare ।। pativratā patiprāṇā patimantrā patipriyā ।। kiṃ me gṛhaṃ kānanaṃ ca tayā hīnaṃ hi dṛśyate ।।
nādyāpy āyāti me kāntā yayā gṛham udīritam ।। kiṃ kurvantu tv apatyāni luptadharmas tv ahaṃ punaḥ ।। pañjarasthaiva sā vākyaṃ bhartāram idam abravīt ।। ānītāhaṃ lubdhakena baddhā pāśair mahāmate ।।
sato vāpy asato vāpi kṛtārthāhaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। viparyaye tu nārīṇām avaśyaṃ nāśam āpnuyāt ।। tvaṃ vrataṃ tvaṃ paraṃ brahma svargo mokṣas tvam eva ca ।। alaṃ khedena majjena dharme buddhiṃ kuru sthirām ।।
yatra sā pañjarasthā tu kapotī vartate tvaram ।। mocayāmīti tām āha niśceṣṭo lubdhako adhunā ।। lubdhānāṃ khecarā hy annaṃ jīvo jīvasya cāśanam ।। gurur agnir dvijātīnāṃ varṇānāṃ brāhmaṇo guruḥ ।।
abhyāgatam anuprāptaṃ vacanais toṣayanti ye ।। tasyānnasya pradānena śakras tṛptim avāpnuyāt ।। tasyopacārād vai lakṣmīr viṣṇunā prītim āpnuyāt ।। taṃ vidyād devarūpeṇa sarvakratuphalo hy asau ।।
kṛtvā tiṣṭha śubhāṃ buddhiṃ dharmakṛtyaṃ samācara ।। upakāriṣu sarvo api karoty upakṛtiṃ punaḥ ।। apakāriṣu yaḥ sādhuḥ puṇyabhāk sa udāhṛtaḥ ।। kiṃtu vaktavyam apy asti tac chṛṇuṣva varānane ।।
ātmānaṃ ca sukhenānyo vayaṃ kaṣṭodaraṃbharāḥ ।। ghaṭakṣiptadhanāḥ kecic cañcukṣiptadhanā vayam ।। pūjayāmi kathaṃ śrāntam abhyāgatam imaṃ śubhe ।। etad apy arthine deyaṃ śītārto lubdhakas tv ayam ।।
ālokayām āsa tadā vahniṃ dūraṃ dadarśa ha ।। puro agniṃ jvālayām āsa lubdhakasya kapotakaḥ ।। agnau nikṣepayām āsa niśīthe sa kapotarāṭ ।। avaśāni svakāṅgāni pratāpya sukham āptavān ।।
mā muñcasva mahābhāga iti bhartāram abravīt ।। iṣṭātithīnāṃ ye lokās tāṃs tvaṃ prāpnuhi suvrata ।। iṣṭātithir bhavāmīha anujānīhi māṃ śubhe ।। viśvātmakaṃ mahāviṣṇuṃ śaraṇyaṃ bhaktavatsalam ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvāgnau kṣiptajīvaṃ lubdhako vākyam abravīt ।। yad idaṃ pakṣirājena madarthe sāhasaṃ kṛtam ।। evaṃ bruvantaṃ taṃ lubdhaṃ pakṣiṇī vākyam abravīt ।। māṃ tvaṃ muñca mahābhāga dūraṃ yāty eṣa me patiḥ ।।
lubdhako mocayām āsa tarasā bhītavat tadā ।। sāpi pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā patim agniṃ tadā jagau ।। vede ca vihito mārgaḥ sarvalokeṣu pūjitaḥ ।। evaṃ tv anugatā nārī saha bhartrā divaṃ vrajet ।।
tāvatkālaṃ vaset svarge bhartāraṃ yānugacchati ।। āśvāsya tāny apatyāni lubdhakaṃ vākyam abravīt ।। apatyānāṃ kṣamasveha bhartrā yāmi triviṣṭapam ।। praviṣṭāyāṃ hutavahe jayaśabdo nyavartata ।।
tadārūḍhau suranibhau daṃpatī dadṛśe tataḥ ।। harṣeṇa procatur ubhau lubdhakaṃ vismayānvitam ।। āvayoḥ svargasopānam atithis tvaṃ namo astu te ।। sadhanuḥ pañjaraṃ tyaktvā kṛtāñjalir abhāṣata ।।
aham atrātithir mānyo niṣkṛtiṃ vaktum arhathaḥ ।। tatraivāplavanāt pakṣaṃ sarvapāpair vimokṣyase ।। aśvamedhaphalaṃ puṇyaṃ prāpya puṇyo bhaviṣyasi ।। punar āplavanād eva tyaktvā dehaṃ malīmasam ।।
vimānavaram ārūḍhaḥ svargaṃ gantāsy asaṃśayam ।। vimānavaram ārūḍho divyarūpadharo abhavat ।। gaṅgāyāś ca prabhāveṇa sarve vai divam ākraman ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca pitṛpūjanam eva ca ।।
japayajñādikaṃ karma tad ānantyāya kalpate ।। yannāmaśravaṇād eva kulavān rūpavān bhavet ।। kārttikeyaṃ sutaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ prītyā provāca pārvatī ।। mamājñayā prītamanāḥ pituś caiva prasādataḥ ।।
yathāsukhaṃ balād reme devapatnyo api remire ।। nāśaknuvan vārayituṃ kārttikeyaṃ divaukasaḥ ।। asakṛd vāryamāṇo api mātrā devaiḥ sa śaktidhṛk ।। abhiśāpabhayād bhītā pārvatī paryacintayat ।।
devapatnyaś ciraṃ rakṣyā iti matvā punaḥ punaḥ ।। tadrūpam ātmanaḥ kṛtvā vartayām āsa pārvatī ।। yāvat paśyati tasyāṃ tu mātṛrūpam apaśyata ।। tasyāṃ tu mātṛrūpaṃ sa prekṣya lajjām upeyivān ।।
iti saṃcintya gāṅgeyo vairāgyam agamat tadā ।। nivāryaś ced ahaṃ bhogāt kiṃtu pūrvaṃ pravartitaḥ ।। lajjayā parayā yukto gautamīm agamat tadā ।। itaḥ strīnāmadheyaṃ yan mama mātṛsamaṃ matam ।।
putraṃ nivārayām āsa vṛttam ity abravīd guruḥ ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ skandaḥ pitaraṃ punar abravīt ।। alam etena deveśa kiṃ varaiḥ surapūjita ।। yāce ahaṃ nātmanā deva tad anujñātum arhasi ।।
atrāplavanamātreṇa dhautapāpā bhavantu te ।। kurūpo rūpasaṃpattim atra snānād avāpnuyāt ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvakratuphalapradam ।। tasya śravaṇamātreṇa somapānaphalaṃ labhet ।।
retogarbhaṃ kaviṃ dṛṣṭvā ṛṣipatnyo aspṛhan mune ।। tāsu garbhaḥ samabhavat ṣaṭsu strīṣu tadāgnitaḥ ।। kiṃ kurmaḥ kva nu gacchāmaḥ kiṃ kṛtvā sukṛtaṃ bhavet ।। tābhyas te niḥsṛtā garbhāḥ phenarūpās tadāmbhasi ।।
ekarūpas tadā tābhyaḥ ṣaṇmukhaḥ samajāyata ।। tāsāṃ vikṛtarūpāṇi dṛṣṭvā te ṛṣayo abruvan ।। strīṇām iti tato vatsa nirastāḥ patibhis tu tāḥ ।। tā dṛṣṭvā nāradaḥ prāha kārttikeyo harodbhavaḥ ।।
taṃ yāntu na cirād eva prīto bhogaṃ pradāsyati ।। kṛttikāḥ svayam evaitad yathāvṛttaṃ nyavedayat ।। gautamīṃ yāntu sarvāś ca snātvāpūjya maheśvaram ।। tathety uktvā kṛttikāś ca snātvā gaṅgāṃ ca gautamīm ।।
deveśvaraprasādena prayayuḥ suramandiram ।। kārttikyāṃ kṛttikāyoge tatra yaḥ snānam ācaret ।। sarvapāpavinirmukto dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt ।। yasya śravaṇamātreṇa hayamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।।
tasyāpi prathamaḥ putras tatputro bhauvano vibhuḥ ।। tam apṛcchan mahābāhur bhauvanaḥ sārvabhauvanaḥ ।। ity apṛcchad guruṃ vipraṃ kva yakṣyāmi surān iti ।। yatra yatra dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ prāvartanta mahākratūn ।।
yugapad daśamedhāni pravṛttāni purodhasā ।। vihāya devayajanaṃ punar anyatra tān kratūn ।। dṛṣṭvāpūrṇāṃs tato yajñān rājā gurum abhāṣata ।। pūrṇatāṃ nāpnuvanti sma daśamedhāni vājinaḥ ।।
gīṣpater bhrātaraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ gatvā saṃvartam ūcatuḥ ।। daśa saṃpūrṇatāṃ yānti taṃ deśaṃ taṃ guruṃ vada ।। abravīd gaccha brahmāṇaṃ guruṃ deśaṃ vadiṣyati ।। āgatya mām abravīc ca guruṃ deśādikaṃ ca yat ।।
gautamīṃ gaccha rājendra sa deśaḥ kratupuṇyavān ।। guror asya prasādena gautamyāś ca prasādataḥ ।। setsyanti tatra yajñāś ca daśamedhāni vājinaḥ ।। kaśyapena sahāyena hayamedhāya dīkṣitaḥ ।।
saṃpūrṇe tu tadā rājā pṛthivīṃ dātum udyataḥ ।। pūjayitvā sthitaṃ viprān ṛtvijo atha sadaspatīn ।। pṛthivīṃ dātukāmena dattaṃ sarvaṃ tvayā nṛpa ।। nānnadānasamaṃ puṇyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu vidyate ।।
kṛtakṛtyo asi bhadraṃ te nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। tathāpi dātukāmaṃ taṃ mahī provāca bhauvanam ।। nimajje ahaṃ salilasya madhye tasmān na dīyatām ।। punaś covāca sā pṛthvī bhauvanaṃ brāhmaṇair vṛtam ।।
sarvaṃ tad akṣayaṃ dānaṃ kiṃ māṃ bhauvana dāsyasi ।। tenāhaṃ sakalā dattā kiṃ māṃ bhauvana dāsyasi ।। tatheti matvā viprebhyo hy annaṃ prādāt suvistaram ।। daśānām aśvamedhānāṃ phalaṃ snānād avāpyate ।।
tasya svarūpaṃ vakṣyāmi gautamyā dakṣiṇe taṭe ।। tasmiñ śaile munivara śāpabhraṣṭā varāpsarā ।। kesarī nāma tadbhartā adriketi tathāparā ।। uttamāṅgena mārjārī sāpy āste añjanaparvate ।।
etasminn antare agastyo añjanaṃ parvatam abhyagāt ।। pūjayām āsatur ubhe yathānyāyaṃ yathāsukham ।। te āhatur ubhe agastyaṃ putrau dehi munīśvara ।। tathety uktvā muniśreṣṭho jagāmāśāṃ sa dakṣiṇām ।।
gītaṃ nṛtyaṃ ca hāsyaṃ ca kurvatyau girimūrdhani ।। kāmākrāntadhiyau cobhau tadā satvaram īyatuḥ ।। te apy ūcatur astv etad remāte girimūrdhani ।। adrikāyāṃ ca nirṛter adrir nāma piśācarāṭ ।।
āvayor vikṛtaṃ rūpam uttamāṅgena dūṣitam ।। tataḥ provāca bhagavān vāyuś ca nirṛtis tathā ।। ity uktvā tāv ubhau prītau tatraivāntaradhīyatām ।। bhrātur hanumataḥ prītyai snāpayām āsa mātaram ।।
mārjārarūpiṇīṃ nītvā gautamyās tīram āptavān ।। brahmaṇo girim āsādya sarvakāmapradaṃ śubham ।। mārjārasaṃjñitāt tasmād dhanūmantaṃ vṛṣākapim ।। tasya svarūpaṃ vyuṣṭiś ca tatraiva procyate śubhā ।।
kathyamānaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ sarvakāmapradaṃ nṛṇām ।। paribhramann āśramāṇi kṣudhayā paripīḍitaḥ ।। ātmānaṃ ca kṣudhāyuktaṃ samṛddhaṃ cāpi gautamam ।। gautamo api dvijaśreṣṭho hy ahaṃ tapasi niṣṭhitaḥ ।।
na bhokṣye ahaṃ kṣudhārto api pīḍite api kalevare ।। iti niścitya medhāvī gatvā gaṅgāṃ ca pāvanīm ।। tuṣṭāva gautamīṃ gaṅgāṃ kṣudhāṃ ca paramāpadam ।। saridrūpeṇa sarveṣāṃ tāpapāpāpahāriṇi ।।
namaḥ śāntikari devi namo dāridryanāśini ।। punaḥ kṛtāñjalir bhūtvā namaskṛtvā dvijottamaḥ ।। vaiṣṇavi tryambake devi godāvari namo astu te ।। saptadhā sāgaraṃ yānti godāvari namo astu te ।।
duḥkhalobhamayi devi kṣudhe tubhyaṃ namo namaḥ ।। tat kaṇvavacanaṃ śrutvā suprīte āhatur dvijam ।। abhīṣṭaṃ vada kalyāṇa varān varaya suvrata ।। provāca praṇato gaṅgāṃ kaṇvaḥ kṣudhāṃ yathākramam ।।
āyur vittaṃ ca bhuktiṃ ca muktiṃ gaṅge prayaccha me ।। ity uktvā gautamīṃ gaṅgāṃ kṣudhāṃ cāha dvijottamaḥ ।। yāhi pāpatare rūkṣe na bhūyās tvaṃ kadācana ।। teṣāṃ dāridryaduḥkhāni na bhaveyur varo aparaḥ ।।
ye kurvanti narā bhaktyā lakṣmībhājo bhavantu te ।। tasya dāridryaduḥkhebhyo na bhayaṃ syād varo aparaḥ ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ vatsa pitṝṇāṃ prītivardhanam ।। tatra snānān naro bhaktyā harer lokam avāpnuyāt ।।
gaṇikāsaṃgame snātvā prāpnuyād akṣayaṃ padam ।। āsīd viśvadharo nāma vaiśyo bahudhanānvitaḥ ।। guṇavān rūpasaṃpanno vilāsī śubhadarśanaḥ ।। tathā dṛṣṭvā tu taṃ putraṃ daṃpatī duḥkhapīḍitau ।।
hā putra hanta kālena pāpena sudurātmanā ।। āvayoś ca tathaiva tvaṃ prāṇebhyo api sudurlabhaḥ ।। tyaktvā nijapuraṃ tūrṇaṃ kṛpayāviṣṭamānasaḥ ।। api svalpena kālena prajā vṛddhāḥ samantataḥ ।।
na kaścin mriyate jantur bhārākrāntā vasuṃdharā ।। dṛṣṭvā vasuṃdharām indraḥ praṇipatyedam abravīt ।। kim āgamanakāryaṃ ta iti me pṛthvi kathyatām ।। kāraṇaṃ praṣṭum āyātā kim idaṃ kathyatāṃ mama ।।
iti śrutvā mahīvākyam indro vacanam abravīt ।। surāṇāṃ hi patir yasmād ahaṃ sarvāsu medini ।। yama ādiśyatāṃ tarhi yathā saṃharate prajāḥ ।। yamasyānayane śīghraṃ mahendreṇa mahāmune ।।
tathāgatya punar vegād vārttā śakre niveditā ।। mahatāpi suyatnena vīkṣyamāṇaḥ samantataḥ ।। savitā sa pitā tasya yamaḥ kutrāsta ity atha ।। caraṃs tatra tapas tīvraṃ na jāne kiṃ nu kāraṇam ।।
iti śrutvā vaco bhānoḥ śakraḥ śaṅkām upāviśat ।। jighṛkṣur matpadaṃ nūnaṃ devā iti matir mama ।। ity uktvā sahasendreṇa āhūtaś cāpsarogaṇaḥ ।। tapaḥpraṇāśane śaktā iti me śīghram ucyatām ।।
atha śakraḥ prakopeṇa pratyuvācāpsarogaṇam ।। ghātayāmo vayaṃ śatruṃ tapasā svargakāmukam ।। itīndrahṛdayaṃ jñātvā hariṇā lokadhāriṇā ।। cakraṃ yatrābhavat tatra cakratīrtham anuttamam ।।
athendraṃ menakā prāha śaṅkiteti vacas tadā ।। maraṇaṃ ca varaṃ deva bhavato na yamāt punaḥ ।। preṣaṇaṃ tat prayacchaiṣā svāmitvaṃ manyate tvayā ।। ādideśābalāṃ kṣāmāṃ satkṛtya gaṇikāṃ tathā ।।
kṛtakṛtyāgatā bhūyo vallabhā me yathā śacī ।। kṣaṇena yamasāṃnidhyam āyātā cārurūpiṇī ।। salīlaṃ lalitaṃ bālā jagau hindolakaṅkalam ।। athonmīlya yamo netre kāmapāvakapūrite ।।
tato vilīya sā sadyaḥ sarittvam agamat tadā ।। gīyamānā gatā svarge tasya tīrthaprabhāvataḥ ।। athādityena cāgatya evam ukto yamas tadā ।। paryaṭantaṃ trilokīṃ māṃ vahantīṃ vasudhāṃ prajāḥ ।।
iti śrutvā yamo vākyaṃ pitur vacanam abravīt ।। karmaṇy asmin mahākrūre samādeṣṭuṃ na vārhasi ।। kiṃ nāma garhitaṃ karma tava kartum alaṃ yama ।। gīyamānā divaṃ sadyo gautamītoyam āplutā ।।
naivāntaṃ tasya paśyāmi tasmād gaccha nijaṃ puram ।। yamo api saṃgame snātvā tato nijapuraṃ yayau ।। tathā dṛṣṭvā yamaṃ yāntaṃ cakre cakraṃ prayāṇakam ।। iti yaḥ śṛṇuyān martyaḥ paṭhed vāpi samāhitaḥ ।।
āpadas tasya naśyanti dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt ।। śṛṇu samyaṅ muniśreṣṭha tatra vṛttam idaṃ yathā ।। sṛṣṭā kanyā bahuvidhā rūpavatyo guṇānvitāḥ ।। tāṃ bālāṃ cārusarvāṅgīṃ dṛṣṭvā rūpaguṇānvitām ।।
na daityānāṃ surāṇāṃ ca na munīnāṃ tathaiva ca ।। guṇajyeṣṭhāya viprāya tapoyuktāya dhīmate ।। gautamāya mahāprājñām adadāṃ poṣaṇāya tām ।। yauvanasthāṃ punaḥ sādhvīm ānayethā mamāntikam ।।
tām ādāya muniśreṣṭha tapasā hatakalmaṣaḥ ।। nirvikāro muniśreṣṭho hy ahalyām ānayat tadā ।। mama deyā sureśāna ity ūcus te pṛthak pṛthak ।। tān sarvān āgatān dṛṣṭvā kanyārtham atha saṃgatān ।।
gautamasya tu māhātmyaṃ gāmbhīryaṃ dhairyam eva ca ।। deyeyaṃ gautamāyaiva nānyayogyā śubhānanā ।। sarveṣāṃ ca matir dhairyaṃ mathitaṃ bālayānayā ।। devān ṛṣīṃs tadā vīkṣya mayā tatroktam uccakaiḥ ।।
kṛtvopatiṣṭhate pūrvaṃ na cānyasmai punaḥ punaḥ ।। ahalyārthaṃ surā jagmuḥ pṛthivyāś ca pradakṣiṇe ।। prayatnam akarot kiṃcid ahalyārtham imaṃ tathā ।। ardhaprasūtā hy abhavat tāṃ dadarśa sa gautamaḥ ।।
liṅgasya ca sureśasya pradakṣiṇam athākarot ।। sarveṣāṃ caiva devānām ekaṃ cāpi pradakṣiṇam ।। evaṃ niścitya sa munir mamāntikam athābhyagāt ।। kamalāsana viśvātman namas te astu punaḥ punaḥ ।।
yad atra yuktaṃ deveśa jānīte tad bhavān svayam ।। tavaiva dīyate subhrūḥ pradakṣiṇam idaṃ kṛtam ।। ardhaprasūtā surabhiḥ saptadvīpavatī mahī ।। liṅgaṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tad eva phalam āpnuyāt ।।
tuṣṭo ahaṃ tava dhairyeṇa jñānena tapasā tathā ।। ity uktvāhaṃ gautamāya ahalyām adadāṃ mune ।। śanaiḥ śanair athāgatya dadṛśuḥ sarva eva te ।। te cāgatyātha paśyanto vismitāś cābhavan surāḥ ।।
samatsaraḥ śacībhartā tām īkṣya ca divaṃ yayau ।। prādāṃ brahmagiriṃ puṇyaṃ sarvakāmapradaṃ śubham ।। gautamasya kathāṃ puṇyāṃ śrutvā śakras triviṣṭape ।। bhūtvā brāhmaṇaveṣeṇa draṣṭum āgāc chatakratuḥ ।।
pāpīyasīṃ matiṃ kṛtvā ahalyāṃ samudaikṣata ।। na bubodha tadā vatsa kāmākṛṣṭaḥ śatakratuḥ ।। saṃtaptāṅgaḥ kathaṃ kuryāṃ praveśo me kathaṃ bhavet ।। sa kadācin mahāprājñaḥ kṛtvā paurvāhṇikīṃ kriyām ।।
āśramaṃ gautamīṃ viprān dhānyāni vividhāni ca ।। idam antaram ity uktvā cakre kāryaṃ manaḥpriyam ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭvā cārusarvāṅgīm ahalyāṃ vākyam abravīt ।। iti bruvan hasan hastam ādāyāntaḥ samāviśat ।।
ramamāṇā yathāsaukhyaṃ prāgāc chiṣyaiḥ sa gautamaḥ ।। pratiyāti priyaṃ vakti toṣayantī ca taṃ guṇaiḥ ।। dvārasthitaṃ muniśreṣṭhaṃ sarve paśyanti nārada ।। ūcur munivaraṃ bhītā gautamaṃ vismayānvitāḥ ।।
aho tapaḥprabhāvo ayaṃ nānārūpadharo bhavān ।। ity ṛṣer vacanaṃ śrutvā ahalyā jāram abravīt ।। iti bruvatī śayanād utthitā satvaraṃ bhayāt ।। trastāṃ ca vikṛtāṃ dṛṣṭvā svapriyāṃ dūṣitāṃ tadā ।।
iti bruvantaṃ bhartāraṃ sāpi novāca lajjitā ।। ko bhavān iti taṃ prāha bhasmīkuryāṃ mṛṣāvadan ।। śacībhartā purāṃ bhettā tapodhana puruṣṭutaḥ ।। mahadvigarhitaṃ karma kṛtavān asmy ahaṃ mune ।।
brahman mayi mahāpāpe kṣamasva karuṇānidhe ।। niśamya tad vaco vipro harim āha ruṣānvitaḥ ।। tām apy āha muniḥ kopāt tvaṃ ca śuṣkanadī bhava ।। tataḥ prasādayām āsa kathayantī tadākṛtim ।।
akṣayān yānti narakāṃs tāsāṃ sarve api pūrvajāḥ ।। tava rūpeṇa cāgatya mām agāt sākṣiṇas tv ime ।। dhyānenāpi munir jñātvā śāntaḥ prāha pativratām ।। nadī bhūtvā punā rūpaṃ prāpsyase priyakṛn mama ।।
tayā tu saṃgatā devyā ahalyā gautamapriyā ।। tataḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ surarāṭ prāha gautamam ।। pādayoḥ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛpayā prāha gautamaḥ ।। kṣaṇān nirdhūtapāpas tvaṃ sahasrākṣo bhaviṣyasi ।।
ahalyāyāḥ punarbhāvaṃ śacībhartā sahasradṛk ।। indratīrtham iti khyātaṃ sarvakāmapradaṃ nṛṇām ।। caturyojanavistīrṇaṃ smaraṇān muktidaṃ nṛṇām ।। so apāṃpates tu tanujām upayeme guṇārṇavām ।।
anurūpaguṇatvāc ca tasya bhāryā guṇārṇavā ।। tam apṛcchan nṛpaśreṣṭho yājñavalkyaṃ purohitam ।। dāsīdāsebhaturaga- rathādyair bhuktir uttamā ।। bhukter muktiḥ śreṣṭhatamā bhuktyā muktiṃ kathaṃ vrajet ।।
tad brūhi dvijaśārdūla sukhān muktiḥ kathaṃ bhavet ।। taṃ gatvā pṛccha nṛpate upadekṣyati te hitam ।। gatvā cocatur avyagrau muktimārgaṃ yathākramam ।। vede ca niścito mārgaḥ karma jyāyo hy akarmaṇaḥ ।।
akarmaṇaivāpyata iti muktimārgo mṛṣocyate ।। tasmāt sarvātmanā karma kartavyaṃ vaidikaṃ nṛbhiḥ ।। akarmaṇaḥ karma puṇyaṃ karma cāpy āśrameṣu ca ।। āśramāṇi ca catvāri karmadvārāṇi mānada ।।
tasmād bhuktiś ca muktiś ca bhavatīti matir mama ।। varuṇaṃ pūjayitvā tu punar vacanam ūcatuḥ ।। tad vadasva suraśreṣṭha sarvajño asi namo astu te ।। tasmin kṣetre kṛtaṃ karma bhuktimuktipradaṃ nṛṇām ।।
tatra yajñena dānena bhogān muktim avāpsyati ।। varuṇena hy anujñātau svapurīṃ jagmatus tadā ।। yājayām āsa viprendro yājñavalkyaś ca taṃ nṛpam ।। tathā janakarājāno bahavas tatra karmaṇā ।।
tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ janasthāneti viśrutam ।। caturyojanavistīrṇaṃ smaraṇāt sarvapāpanut ।। tīrthasya smaraṇād vāpi gamanād bhaktisevanāt ।। sarvān kāmān avāpnoti muktiṃ ca samavāpnuyāt ।।
tayoś ca saṃgamaḥ puṇyo gaṅgāyāṃ munisattama ।। kaśyapasya suto jyeṣṭha ādityo lokaviśrutaḥ ।। tasya patnī uṣā khyātā tvāṣṭrī trailokyasundarī ।। cintayām āsa kiṃ kṛtyaṃ mama syād iti bhāminī ।।
yamunā ca nadī puṇyā śṛṇu vismayakāraṇam ।। tām abravīt tataś coṣā tvaṃ ca matsadṛśī bhava ।। yāvad āgamanaṃ me syāt patyus tāvat priyā bhava ।। tathety āha ca sā chāyā nirjagāma gṛhād uṣā ।।
tvaṣṭāpi cakitaḥ prāha tāṃ sutāṃ sutavatsalaḥ ।। bibhemi bhadre śiṣṭo ahaṃ bhartur gehaṃ punar vraja ।। uttaraṃ ca kuror deśaṃ jagāma tapase tvarā ।। duṣprekṣaṃ taṃ svakaṃ kāntaṃ dhyāyantī niścalā uṣā ।।
patyau sā vartayām āsa apatyāny atha jajñire ।। sā chāyā vartayām āsa vaiṣamyeṇaiva nityaśaḥ ।। vaiṣamyeṇātha vartantīṃ chāyāṃ tāṃ mātaraṃ tadā ।। putradaurjanyasaṃkṣobhāc chāyā vaivasvataṃ yamam ।।
savitre taṃ tu vṛttāntaṃ nyavedayad aśeṣataḥ ।। apatyeṣu viruddheṣu jananī naiva kupyate ।। naiva kupyati sā mātā tasmān neyaṃ mamāmbikā ।। māty asyāṃ sarvam apy etat tasmān māteti gīyate ।।
vakty agnikālasadṛśā vācā neyaṃ madambikā ।। iyaṃ chāyā nāsya mātā uṣā mātā tu sānyataḥ ।। uttare ca kurau tvāṣṭrī vaḍavārūpadhāriṇī ।। yatra sā vartate kāntā aśvarūpaḥ svayaṃ tadā ।।
kāmāturaṃ hayaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutvā vai heṣitasvanam ।। hayadharṣaṇasaṃbhītā ko nv ayaṃ cety ajānatī ।। ko nu me rakṣako atra syād ṛṣayo vāthavā surāḥ ।। paryadhāvad yato yāti uṣā bhānus tatas tataḥ ।।
bhāgīrathīṃ nadīś cānyā vanāny upavanāni ca ।। atikramya bhayodvignā tvāṣṭry abhyagāc ca gautamīm ।। ṛṣīṇām āśramaṃ sāśvā praviṣṭā gautamīṃ tathā ।। tataḥ kopād ṛṣīṃs tāṃś ca śaśāpoṣāpatiḥ prabhuḥ ।।
nivārayatha māṃ yasmād vaṭā yūyaṃ bhaviṣyatha ।। stuvanto devadeveśaṃ bhānuṃ taṃ munayo mudā ।। vaḍavāyā mukhe lagnaṃ mukhaṃ cāśvasvarūpiṇam ।। tayor vīryeṇa gaṅgāyām aśvinau samajāyatām ।।
nadyo gāvas tathauṣadhyo devā jyotirgaṇās tathā ।। yamo manuś ca varuṇaḥ śanir vaivasvatas tathā ।। tattadrūpaṃ samāsthāya nadyas tā vismayān mune ।। abhiprāyaṃ viditvā tu śvaśuraṃ bhānur abravīt ।।
yāvat saukhyaṃ bhaved asyās tāvac chindhi prajāpate ।। tejasāṃ chedanaṃ cakre prabhāsaṃ tu tato viduḥ ।। aśvinor yatra cotpattir aśvatīrthaṃ tad ucyate ।। tāpī ca yamunā caiva pitaraṃ draṣṭum āgate ।।
devānāṃ tatra tīrthānām āgatānāṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvam akṣayapuṇyadam ।। sarvapāpavinirmukto dharmavān sa sukhī bhavet ।। tasya prabhāvaṃ vakṣyāmi śṛṇu nārada yatnataḥ ।।
garuḍasya bhayād bhaktyā toṣayām āsa śaṃkaram ।। tam uvāca mahānāgaṃ varaṃ varaya pannaga ।। tathety āha ca taṃ śaṃbhur garuḍād abhayaṃ bhavet ।। kṣīrodaśāyī yatrāste kṣīrārṇavasamīpataḥ ।।
garuḍo api ca yatrāste taṃ deśam api yāty asau ।। taṃ gṛhītvā mahānāgaṃ prākṣipat svasya veśmani ।। etasminn antare nandī provāceśaṃ jagatprabhum ।। garuḍena sureśāna jīvan nāgo na saṃvrajet ।।
nandino vacanaṃ śrutvā jñātvā śaṃbhur athābravīt ।। gatvā taṃ jagatām īśaṃ viṣṇuṃ stuhi janārdanam ।। tat prabhor vacanaṃ śrutvā nandī gatvā śriyaḥ patim ।। nārāyaṇaḥ prītamanā garuḍaṃ vākyam abravīt ।।
viṣṇum apy abravīt kopāt suparṇo nandino antike ।। dāsyanty anye bhavān naiva mayānītaṃ hariṣyati ।। mayopapāditaṃ nāgaṃ tvaṃ tu dāsyasi nandine ।। mayopapāditaṃ nāgaṃ vaktuṃ dehīti nocitam ।।
santo dāsyanti bhṛtyebhyo madupāttaharo bhavān ।। ahaṃ mahābalīty evaṃ mudhaiva ślāghate bhavān ।। vihasya nandinaḥ pārśve paśyadbhir lokapālakaiḥ ।। tvadbalād asurān sarvāñ jeṣye ahaṃ khagasattama ।।
vahāṅguliṃ karasyāśu kaniṣṭhāṃ nandino antike ।। satyaṃ māṃ vahase nityaṃ paśya dharmaṃ vihaṃgama ।। tataḥ kṛtāñjalir dīno vyathito lajjayānvitaḥ ।। tvaṃ prabhuḥ sarvalokānāṃ dhartā dhāryas tvam eva ca ।।
kṛtāparādhe api jane mahatī yasya vai kṛpā ।। kamale bālakaṃ dīnam ārtaṃ tanayavatsale ।। tataḥ kṛpānvitā devī śrīr apy āha janārdanam ।। janārdana uvācedaṃ nandinaṃ śaṃbhuvāhanam ।।
ātmīyaṃ ca punā rūpaṃ garuḍaḥ samavāpsyati ।। śaṃkaro api garutmantaṃ provāca śaśiśekharaḥ ।। sarvakāmapradāṃ śāntāṃ tām āplutya punar vapuḥ ।। prāṇino abhīṣṭadā teṣāṃ śaraṇaṃ khaga gautamī ।।
gaṅgām āplutya garuḍaḥ śivaṃ viṣṇuṃ nanāma saḥ ।। vegī bhavan muniśreṣṭha punar viṣṇum iyāt sudhīḥ ।। sarvaṃ tad akṣayaṃ vatsa śivaviṣṇupriyāvaham ।। pitṝṇāṃ puṇyajananaṃ smaraṇād api pāpanut ।।
brāhmaṇaḥ karṣakaḥ kaścij jābālir iti viśrutaḥ ।। pratodena pratudati pṛṣṭhato api ca pārśvayoḥ ।। surabhir jagatāṃ mātā nandine sarvam abravīt ।। śaṃbhuś ca vṛṣabhaṃ prāha sarvaṃ sidhyatu te vacaḥ ।।
naṣṭeṣu goṣu sarveṣu svarge martye tatas tvarā ।। tān avocaṃ surān sarvāñ śaṃkaraṃ yāta yācata ।। īśo api vibudhān āha jānāti vṛṣabho mama ।। vṛṣo api vibudhān āha gosavaḥ kriyatāṃ kratuḥ ।।
tataḥ pravartate yajño gosavo devanirmitaḥ ।। govardhanaṃ tu tat tīrthaṃ devānāṃ prītivardhanam ।। kiṃcid dānādinā yat syāt phalaṃ tat tu na vidmahe ।। nāmadheyaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu nārada yatnataḥ ।।
tasya bhāryā mahī nāma taruṇī lokasundarī ।। dhṛtavrataṃ tathākarṣan mṛtyuḥ kālerito mune ।। trātāraṃ naiva paśyantī gālavāśramam abhyagāt ।। sā babhrāma bahūn deśān puṃskāmā kāmacāriṇī ।।
jāto api mātṛdoṣeṇa veśyeritamatis tv abhūt ।। tatrāsau paṇyaveṣeṇa adhyāste ca mahī tathā ।। so api kālavaśāt tatra janasthāne avasat tadā ।। mahī cāpi dhanaṃ dātṝn puruṣān samapekṣate ।।
tayoḥ samāgamaś cāsīd vidhinā mātṛputrayoḥ ।। tayoḥ parasparaṃ jñānaṃ naivāsīn mātṛputrayoḥ ।। āsīt tasyāpy asadvṛtteḥ śṛṇu nārada citravat ।। brāhmīṃ saṃdhyām anuṣṭhāya tad ūrdhvaṃ tu dhanārjanam ।।
tathā sa prātar utthāya gaṅgāṃ gatvā yathāvidhi ।। kṛtvā tu brāhmaṇān natvā tato abhyeti svakarmasu ।। kuṣṭhasarvāṅgaśithilaḥ pūyaśoṇitaniḥsravaḥ ।। śāntaḥ sūryāgnisadṛśo mūrtimān iva bhāskaraḥ ।।
gālavo yatra bhagavāṃs tapojñānaparāyaṇaḥ ।। brāhmaṇo api ca tatraiva nityaṃ tīrthaṃ sametya ca ।। gaṅgāyāḥ sevanāt pūrvaṃ sanājjātasya yad vapuḥ ।। ubhayaṃ tasya tad rūpaṃ gālavo nityam eva ca ।।
evaṃ savismayo bhūtvā gālavaḥ prāha taṃ dvijam ।। āhūya yatnato dhīmān kṛpayā vismayena ca ।। kiṃnāmā tvaṃ kva śayyā te kā te bhāryā vadasva me ।। gālavasya vacaḥ śrutvā brāhmaṇo apy āha taṃ munim ।।
śvaḥ kathyate mayā sarvaṃ jñātvā kāryavinirṇayam ।। uvāca cakitaḥ smṛtvā gālavasya tu yad vacaḥ ।। āvayoḥ sadṛśī prītir yāvajjīvaṃ pravartatām ।। kiṃ nu sthānaṃ kva vā bandhur mama sarvaṃ nivedyatām ।।
tasya bhāryā mahī cāhaṃ matputro gālavāśrame ।। svairiṇī tv iha varte ahaṃ viddhi māṃ brāhmaṇīṃ dvija ।। papāta sahasā bhūmau veśyā taṃ vākyam abravīt ।। kiṃ tu vākyaṃ mayā coktaṃ tava cittavirodhakṛt ।।
ātmānam ātmanāśvāsya brāhmaṇo vākyam abravīt ।। mātā mahī mama iyaṃ mama daivād upāgatā ।। gālavaṃ muniśārdūlaṃ gatvā vipro nyavedayat ।। upanītas tvayā caiva mahī mātā mama prabho ।।
kiṃ karomi ca kiṃ kṛtvā niṣkṛtir mama vai bhavet ।। tavedaṃ dvividhaṃ rūpaṃ nityaṃ paśyāmy apūrvavat ।। yat kṛtyaṃ tava tat sarvaṃ gaṅgāyāṃ pratyagāt kṣayam ।। pūto asi pratyahaṃ vatsa nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।
paśye ahaṃ punar apy eva rūpaṃ tava guṇottamam ।। paśyāmi nityaṃ tasmāt tvaṃ pūto devyā kṛto adhunā ।। iyaṃ ca mātā te vipra jñātā yā caiva bandhakī ।। bhūtānāṃ viṣaye prītir vatsa svābhāvikī yataḥ ।।
atyartham anutapteyaṃ prāgācaritapuṇyataḥ ।। tathā tau cakratur ubhau mātāputrau ca nārada ।। tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ dhautapāpaṃ pracakṣate ।। tat sarvaṃ nāśayed etad dhautapāpaṃ supuṇyadam ।।
pitṝn saṃtarpayām āsa pitṛtīrthaṃ tato viduḥ ।। sarvam akṣayatām eti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। pūjayām āsa rājendro munibhis tattvadarśibhiḥ ।। tatsvarūpaṃ ca vakṣyāmi paṭhitaṃ vedavādibhiḥ ।।
viśvāmitro mahāprājñaḥ saśiṣyo gautamīm agāt ।। vyathitaḥ kauśikaḥ śrīmāñ śiṣyān idam uvāca ha ।। idānīm eva gantavyam ānetavyaṃ kṣaṇena tu ।। aṭamānā itaś ceto mṛtaṃ dadṛśire śunam ।।
so api taṃ bhadram ity uktvā pratijagrāha pāṇinā ।। pacadhvaṃ mantravac cāpi hutvāgnau tu yathāvidhi ।। sarve bhokṣyāmahe śeṣam ity uvāca sa kauśikaḥ ।। devānāṃ sadane sarvaṃ devebhyas tan nyavedayat ।।
devaiḥ śvamāṃsaṃ bhoktavyam āpannam ṛṣikalpitam ।। sthālīm athāharat pūrṇāṃ māṃsena pihitāṃ tadā ।। hṛtā sthālī muniśreṣṭha śyenenākṛtabuddhinā ।। tato jñātvā surapatiḥ sthālīṃ cakre madhuplutām ।।
sthālīṃ vīkṣya tataḥ kopād idam āha sa kauśikaḥ ।। no cet tvāṃ bhasmasāt kuryām indro bhītas tadābravīt ।। kim anena śvamāṃsena amedhyena mahāmune ।। prajāḥ sarvāś ca sīdanti kiṃ tena madhunā hare ।।
athavā devapitaro bhokṣyantīdaṃ śvamāṃsakam ।। tato bhītaḥ sahasrākṣo meghān āhūya tatkṣaṇāt ।। paścāt tad amṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ haridattaṃ yathāvidhi ।। vipraḥ saṃbhuktavāñ śiṣyair viśvāmitraḥ svabhāryayā ।।
yatrāgataḥ surapatir lokānām amṛtārpaṇam ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvakratuphalapradam ।। madhutīrtham athaindraṃ ca śyenaṃ parjanyam eva ca ।। tasya śravaṇamātreṇa sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।
ātithyapūjānirato gautamītīram āśritaḥ ।। dhyāyantaṃ taṃ dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ pūjayantaṃ sadā śivam ।। netuṃ dūtāḥ samājagmur dakṣiṇāśāpates tadā ।। tadā kāle vyatikrānte citrako mṛtyum abravīt ।।
nādyāpy āyānti dūtās te mṛtyor naivocitaṃ tu te ।। provāca kim idaṃ dūtā mṛtyum ūcuś ca dūtakāḥ ।। yeṣāṃ prasanno giriśas teṣāṃ kā nāma bhītayaḥ ।। nāsau vipro vijānāti mṛtyuṃ vā yamakiṃkarān ।।
mṛtyuṃ pāśadharaṃ dṛṣṭvā daṇḍī provāca vismitaḥ ।। kim atra vīkṣase mṛtyo daṇḍinaṃ mṛtyur abravīt ।। śvetaṃ netum ihāyātas tasmād vīkṣe dvijottamam ।। śvetāya muniśārdūla tato daṇḍī cukopa ha ।।
tataḥ pāśadharo mṛtyuḥ papāta dharaṇītale ।। yamāya sarvam avadan vadhaṃ mṛtyos tu daṇḍinā ।। citraguptaṃ bahubalaṃ yamadaṇḍaṃ ca rakṣakam ।। akṣirogān kukṣirogān karṇaśūlaṃ tathaiva ca ।।
tvarantām iti tān uktvā jagāma tvarito yamaḥ ।। tam āyāntaṃ yamaṃ dṛṣṭvā nandī provāca sāyudhaḥ ।। tatra tad yuddham abhavat sarvalokabhayāvaham ।। dakṣiṇāśāpatiṃ cāpi nijaghāna balānvitam ।।
ādityo api suraiḥ sārdhaṃ śrutvā tan mahad adbhutam ।। ahaṃ viṣṇuś ca bhagavān indro agnir varuṇas tathā ।। ete cānye ca bahavo vayaṃ yātā yamāntikam ।। samudrāś ca nadā nāgā nānābhūtāny anekaśaḥ ।।
kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ śaṃbhum ūcuḥ sarve punaḥ punaḥ ।। brahmapriya namas te astu devapriya namo astu te ।। tvāṃ vinā kaḥ samartho atra vyavasthāṃ kartum īśvaraḥ ।। kiṃ dadāmīti tān āha idam ūcuḥ surā api ।।
dharmādharmavyavasthāyāṃ sthāpito lokapālakaḥ ।। vinā tena jagaddhātur naiva kiṃcid bhaviṣyati ।। prārthanā saphalā nātha mahatsu na vṛthā bhavet ।। yamaṃ yadi vaco me adya anumanyanti devatāḥ ।।
haribrahmādisahitaṃ vaśe yasyākhilaṃ jagat ।। madbhakto na mṛtiṃ yātu nety ūcur amarāḥ punaḥ ।। amartyamartyabhedo ayaṃ na syād deva jaganmaya ।। madbhaktānāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ gautamīm anusevatām ।।
vārttāpy eṣāṃ na kartavyā yamena tu kadācana ।। ye śivaṃ śaraṇaṃ yātās te muktās tatkṣaṇād api ।। tathety ūcuḥ suragaṇā devadevaṃ śivaṃ prati ।। tataś ca bhagavān nātho nandinaṃ prāha vāhanam ।।
gautamyā udakena tvam abhiṣiñca mṛtaṃ yamam ।। utthitāś ca sajīvās te dakṣiṇāśāṃ tato gatāḥ ।। sthitā āsan pūjayanto devadevaṃ maheśvaram ।। tathā ṣaṭ ca sahasrāṇi punaḥ ṣaṭ ca tathaiva ca ।।
puṇyam ākhyānam etad dhi śvetatīrthasya nārada ।। tasya śravaṇamātreṇa sahasraṃ jīvate samāḥ ।। karoti sarvalokānāṃ bhuktimuktipradāyakam ।। sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam ।।
tayoḥ putrau mahāprājñau rūpabuddhivilāsinau ।। upanītau sutau dṛṣṭvā pitarāv ūcatur mithaḥ ।। tasmād ekaḥ śāsitā syāt tiṣṭhatv eko yathāsukham ।। adhyāpayiṣye sadṛśaṃ sukhaṃ tiṣṭhatu bhārgavaḥ ।।
tatheti matvāṅgirase śukraṃ tasmai nyavedayat ।। vaiṣamyabuddhyā tau bālau cirāc chukro abravīd idam ।। gurūṇāṃ nedam ucitaṃ vaiṣamyaṃ putraśiṣyayoḥ ।। naiṣā viṣamabuddhīnāṃ saṃkhyā pāpasya vidyate ।।
gaccheyaṃ gurum anyaṃ vai mām anujñātum arhasi ।। tato vānyatra gacchāmi svāmin pṛṣṭo asi gamyate ।। avāptavidyaḥ pitaraṃ gaccheyaṃ cety acintayat ।। iti smaran mahāprājñam apṛcchad vṛddhagautamam ।।
trayāṇām api lokānāṃ yo gurus taṃ vrajāmy aham ।। kvārādhayāmi giriśam ity uktaḥ prāha gautamaḥ ।। tatas tuṣṭo jagannāthaḥ sa te vidyāṃ pradāsyati ।। snātvā bhūtvā śuciḥ samyak stutiṃ cakre sa bālakaḥ ।।
nāhaṃ jānāmi te kiṃcit stutiṃ kartuṃ namo astu te ।। tvaṃ prabhuḥ sarvabhāvena jagannātha namo astu te ।। aham alpataro bālo jaganmaya namo astu te ।। māṃ tvaṃ ca kṛpayā paśya lokasākṣin namo astu te ।।
evaṃ tu stuvatas tasya prasanno abhūt sureśvaraḥ ।। kāmaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te yac cāpi suradurlabham ।। kavir apy āha deveśaṃ kṛtāñjalir udāradhīḥ ।। tāṃ vidyāṃ nātha yāciṣye tvaṃ gurur mama daivatam ।।
tāṃ dattavān suraśreṣṭhas tasmai śukrāya yācate ।। kiṃ punaḥ śaṃkare tuṣṭe vicāryam avaśiṣyate ।। daityānāṃ ca guruś cāsīd vidyayā pūjitaḥ kaviḥ ।। kaco bṛhaspatisuto vidyāṃ prāptaḥ kaves tu tām ।।
avāpur mahatīṃ vidyāṃ yām āhur mṛtajīvinīm ।। gautamyā uttare pāre śukratīrthaṃ tad ucyate ।। snānaṃ dānaṃ ca yat kiṃcit sarvam akṣayapuṇyadam ।। smaraṇād api pāpaugha- kleśasaṃghavināśanam ।।
śacīpatiṃ cānugatā tāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhītavad dhariḥ ।। yatra yatra tv asau yāti hatyā sāpīndragāminī ।। tatrāsau tantuvad bhūtvā vāsaṃ cakre śacīpatiḥ ।। etasminn antare devā nirindrā hy abhavan mune ।।
tatrāham avadaṃ devān hatyāsthānaṃ prakalpya ca ।। yatrābhiṣiktaḥ pūtātmā punar indro bhaviṣyati ।। tatra snātaṃ surapatiṃ devāś ca ṛṣayas tathā ।। abhiṣicyamānam indraṃ taṃ prakopād gautamo abravīt ।।
tān sarvān bhasmasāt kuryāṃ śīghraṃ yāntv asurārayaḥ ।। narmadām agaman sarva indram ādāya satvarāḥ ।। abhiṣekṣyamāṇam indraṃ taṃ māṇḍavyo bhagavān ṛṣiḥ ।। pūjayām āsur amarā māṇḍavyaṃ yuktibhiḥ stavaiḥ ।।
tatrātidāruṇaṃ vighnaṃ mune samupajāyate ।। malaniryātanaṃ yasmin kurmas tasmin varān bahūn ।। yasmin deśe surendrasya abhiṣeko bhaviṣyati ।। nānāvṛṣṭir na durbhikṣaṃ bhaved atra kadācana ।।
abhiṣekaḥ kṛtas tatra malaniryātanaṃ tathā ।। abhiṣikte surapatau jāte ca vimale tadā ।। surāś ca ṛṣayaś caiva ahaṃ viṣṇus tathaiva ca ।। ete cānye ca ṛṣayo devā yakṣāḥ sapannagāḥ ।।
mayā punaḥ śacībhartā kamaṇḍalubhavena ca ।। siktā ceti ca tatrāsīt te gaṅgāyāṃ ca saṃgate ।। tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ puṇyāsaṃgamam ucyate ।। tatra sapta sahasrāṇi tīrthāny āsañ śubhāni ca ।।
sarvaṃ tad akṣayaṃ vidyān nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। sarvapāpaiḥ sa mucyeta manovākkāyakarmajaiḥ ।। prabhāvaṃ tasya vakṣyāmi bhraṣṭarājyapradāyakam ।। purā laṅkāpatiś cāsīj jyeṣṭho viśravasaḥ sutaḥ ।।
sāpatnā rāvaṇaś caiva kumbhakarṇo vibhīṣaṇaḥ ।। maddattena vimānena dhanado bhrātṛbhiḥ saha ।। rāvaṇasya tu yā mātā kupitā sābravīt sutān ।। devāś ca dānavāś cāsan sāpatnā bhrātaro mithaḥ ।।
sāpatnyaṃ yo anumanyate tasya jīvo nirarthakaḥ ।। jagmus te tapase araṇyaṃ kṛtavantas tapo mahat ।। mātulena marīcena tathā mātāmahena tu ।। rakṣobhāvān mātṛdoṣād bhrātror vairam abhūn mahat ।।
yuddhe jitvāgrajaṃ śāntaṃ dhanadaṃ bhrātaraṃ tathā ।। rāvaṇo ghoṣayām āsa trailokye sacarācare ।। pitāmahaṃ pulastyaṃ taṃ gatvā natvābravīd vacaḥ ।। āśrayaḥ śaraṇaṃ yat syād daivaṃ vā tīrtham eva ca ।।
tat pautravacanaṃ śrutvā pulastyo vākyam abravīt ।। tatra nāsya praveśaḥ syād gaṅgāyā jalamadhyataḥ ।। siddhiṃ prāpsyasi kalyāṇīṃ tathā kuru mayā saha ।। pitrā mātrā ca vṛddhena pulastyena dhaneśvaraḥ ।।
tuṣṭāva devadeveśaṃ bhuktimuktipradaṃ śivam ।। vareṇa cchandayām āsa harṣān novāca kiṃcana ।। punaḥ punar varasveti śive vādini harṣite ।। prāptavyaṃ dhanapālatvaṃ vadantīdaṃ maheśvaram ।।
viditveva tadā vāṇī śubham artham udīrayat ।। prāptavyaṃ prāptavat tatra daivī vāg abhavac chubhā ।। evaṃ bhavatu nāmeti dhanado vākyam abravīt ।। pulastyaṃ ca varaiḥ puṇyais tathā viśravasaṃ munim ।।
tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ paulastyaṃ dhanadaṃ viduḥ ।। teṣu snānādi yat kiṃcit tat sarvaṃ bahupuṇyadam ।। sarvavighnopaśamanaṃ tattīrthasya phalaṃ śṛṇu ।। havyaṃ vahantaṃ devānāṃ gautamyās tīra eva tu ।।
bhrātuḥ priyaṃ tathā dakṣaṃ madhur ditisuto balī ।। havyaṃ devā naiva cāpur mṛte vai jātavedasi ।। kopena mahatāviṣṭo gāṅgam ambhaḥ samāviśat ।। jīvam utsarjayām āsur agnijīvā yato matāḥ ।।
ājagmur vibudhāḥ sarva ṛṣayaḥ pitaras tathā ।। agniṃ jalagataṃ dṛṣṭvā priyaṃ cocur divaukasaḥ ।। mānuṣān annapākena bījānāṃ kledanena ca ।। kriyamāṇe bhavatkārye yā gatir jātavedasaḥ ।।
kāryaṃ tu sarvatas tasya bhavatāṃ jātavedasaḥ ।। iha cāmutra ca vyāptau śaktir apy atra no bhavet ।। devās tam ūcur bhāvena sarveṇa ṛṣayas tathā ।। prayājān anuyājāṃś ca dāsyāmo havyavāhana ।।
tvayā dattaṃ tu yad dravyaṃ bhokṣyāmaḥ surasattama ।। iha cāmutra ca vyāptau havye vā laukike tathā ।। jātavedā bṛhadbhānuḥ saptārcir nīlalohitaḥ ।। jalād ākṛṣya vibudhā abhiṣicya vibhāvasum ।।
yathāgataṃ surā jagmur vahnitīrthaṃ tad ucyate ।। teṣu snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca yaḥ karoti jitātmavān ।। devatīrthaṃ ca tatraiva āgneyaṃ jātavedasam ।। taddevadarśanād eva sarvakratuphalaṃ labhet ।।
tasya svarūpaṃ vakṣyāmi śṛṇu nārada tanmanāḥ ।। na dārasaṃgrahaṃ lebhe vairāgyān nāgnipūjanam ।। nākarod dārakarmādi naivāgnīnām upāsanam ।। jyeṣṭhaṃ caiva kaniṣṭhaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthag idaṃ vacaḥ ।।
ṛṇatrayāpanodāya kriyatāṃ dārasaṃgrahaḥ ।। kanīyāṃs tu pitṝn prāha na yogyo dārasaṃgrahaḥ ।। tāv ubhau punar apy evam ūcus te vai pitāmahāḥ ।। kurutāṃ gautamīsnānaṃ sarvābhīṣṭapradāyakam ।।
snānaṃ ca tarpaṇaṃ tasyāṃ kurutāṃ śraddhayānvitau ।। jyeṣṭho anṛṇas tato bhūyāt parivittir na cetaraḥ ।। trayāṇām api lokānāṃ kākṣīvato anṛṇo abhavat ।। tatra snānena dānena ṛṇī muktaḥ sukhī bhavet ।।
maheśvaro yatra devo gaṅgāpulinam āśritaḥ ।। sauraṃ saumyaṃ tathā brāhmaṃ kaumāraṃ vāruṇaṃ tathā ।। tattīrthasmaraṇād eva kṛtakṛtyo bhaven naraḥ ।। dattārdhatapasaḥ sarve procus te kāśyapaṃ munim ।।
tapaso ardhaṃ tu dāsyāmas tathety āha munis tu tān ।। kadrvāṃ caiva śanair brahman sarpāṇāṃ sarpamātari ।। aparādho na ca kvāpi kāryo gamanam eva ca ।। anyatra gamanāc chāpo bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।।
tadaiva jagmatuḥ sattram ṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।। unmatte te ubhe nityaṃ vayaḥsaṃpattigarvite ।। vikurvatyau tatra sattre samāni ca havīṃṣi ca ।। te dṛṣṭvā cukṣubhur viprā apamārgarate ubhe ।।
suparṇā caiva kadrūś ca nadyau te saṃbabhūvatuḥ ।। ṛṣibhyas tatra vṛttāntaṃ śāpaṃ tābhyāṃ savistaram ।। ṛṣibhyaḥ kathayām āsa vālakhilyā iti śrutāḥ ।। tatra stuhi maheśānaṃ punar bhārye bhaviṣyataḥ ।।
gaṅgāmadhye sadā hy āste madhyameśvarasaṃjñayā ।। tuṣṭāva stavanaiḥ puṇyair devadevaṃ maheśvaram ।। prasanno hy adadāc chaṃbhuḥ kaśyapāya varān bahūn ।। nadīsvarūpe patnyau ye gaṅgāṃ prāpya saridvarām ।।
te garbhiṇyau punar jāte gaṅgāyāś ca prasādataḥ ।। āhvayām āsa tān viprān gautamītīram āśritān ।। brāhmaṇān pūjayām āsa vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।। bhartṛsamīpopaviṣṭā kadrūr viprān nirīkṣya ca ।।
yenākṣṇā hasitā pāpe bhajyatāṃ te akṣi pāpavat ।। tataḥ prasādayām āsa kaśyapo bhagavān ṛṣīn ।। aparādhasahasrebhyo rakṣiṣyati ca sevanāt ।। sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ sarvakratuphalapradam ।।
smaraṇād eva pāpānāṃ nāśanaṃ kiṃ tu darśanāt ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭvā rūpasaṃpannām urvaśīṃ prāha bhūpatiḥ ।। sarvāsām uttamā yoṣid dīpayantī sabhām imām ।। tac chrutvā vismito rājā ānayemāṃ mamāntikam ।।
urvaśī punar apy āha rājānaṃ bhūridakṣiṇam ।। ānīyate mahārāja tasyāḥ sarvaṃ nivedya ca ।। sā gatvā rājavacanaṃ nyavedayad athorvaśī ।। sā tatheti pratijñāya prāyād yatra purūravāḥ ।।
sarasvān abhavat putro yasya putro bṛhadrathaḥ ।। sarasvantaṃ tato lakṣma jñātvānyeṣu tathā kṛtam ।। macchāpabhītā vāgīśā prāgād devīṃ ca gautamīm ।। tāpatrayopaśamanīm aihikāmuṣmikapradām ।।
gaṅgāpi mām uvācedaṃ viśāpāṃ kartum arhasi ।। strīṇām eṣa svabhāvo vai puṃskāmā yoṣito yataḥ ।। tvaṃ kathaṃ tu na jānīṣe jagatsraṣṭāmbujāsana ।। tato viśāpam avadaṃ dṛśyāpi syāt sarasvatī ।।
yatraiṣā saṃgatā devī gaṅgāyāṃ śāpavihvalā ।। tapas taptvā samārādhya devaṃ siddheśvaraṃ haram ।। tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ purūravasam ucyate ।। siddheśvaro yatra devaḥ sarvakāmapradaṃ tu tat ।।
etāni pañca tīrthāni puṇyāni munayo viduḥ ।। sāvitrī caiva gāyatrī śraddhā medhā sarasvatī ।। sarvāsām uttamāṃ kāṃcin nirmame lokasundarīm ।। gṛhyamāṇā mayā bālā sā māṃ dṛṣṭvā palāyitā ।।
mṛgavyādho abhavac chaṃbhur dharmasaṃrakṣaṇāya ca ।। tato maheśvaraḥ prāyād dharmasaṃrakṣaṇāya saḥ ।। mām uvāca vadhiṣye tvāṃ mṛgavyādhas tadā haraḥ ।। sāvitryādyāḥ pañca sutā nadīrūpeṇa saṃgatāḥ ।।
yatra tāḥ saṃgatā devyā pañca tīrthāni nārada ।। teṣu snānaṃ tathā dānaṃ yat kiṃcit kurute naraḥ ।। svargamokṣaphalaṃ cānyad brahmatīrthaphalaṃ smṛtam ।। tasyākhyānaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu yatnena nārada ।।
gautamyā dakṣiṇe tīre dīkṣāṃ cakre purodhasā ।। tasya rājño mahābāhor vasiṣṭhas tu purohitaḥ ।। taṃ dānavam abhiprekṣya devās tv indrapurogamāḥ ।। aśvatthaṃ viṣṇur agamad bhānur arkaṃ vaṭaṃ śivaḥ ।।
aśvinau tu hayaṃ gṛhya vāyaso abhūd yamaḥ svayam ।। yaṣṭim ādāya daiteyān nyavārayad athājñayā ।। ārkaṃ śaivaṃ ca saumyaṃ ca vāsiṣṭhaṃ sarvakāmadam ।। tuṣṭāḥ procur vasiṣṭhaṃ taṃ yajamānaṃ priyavratam ।।
hayamedhasya niṣpattyai ete yātā itas tataḥ ।। hayamedhaphalaṃ puṇyaṃ prāpnoti na mṛṣā vacaḥ ।। vāruṇaṃ brāhmam āgneyam aindram aindavam aiśvaram ।। eteṣāṃ puṇyatīrthānāṃ nāmadheyaṃ śṛṇuṣva me ।।
kṛtvātithyaṃ tayoḥ samyag ghariścandro abravīd ṛṣī ।। etaṃ me saṃśayaṃ nityaṃ brūtām ṛṣivarāv ubhau ।। tāv ūcatur hariścandraṃ parvato nāradas tathā ।। uttaraṃ vidyate samyak tathāpy etad udīryate ।।
jāte putre pitā snānaṃ yaḥ karoti janādhipa ।। ātmapratiṣṭhā putrāt syāj jāyate cāmarottamaḥ ।। triṛṇān mocayet putraḥ pitaraṃ ca pitāmahān ।। vinā putreṇa rājendra svargo muktiḥ sutāt smṛtāḥ ।।
putro muktiḥ paraṃ jyotis tārakaḥ sarvadehinām ।। putra eva paro loke dharmakāmārthasiddhaye ।। vinā putreṇa yaj janma vyarthaṃ tad avabhāti me ।। tac chrutvā vismayavāṃs tāv uvāca nṛpaḥ punaḥ ।।
mantreṇa yāgadānābhyām utpādyo asau suto mayā ।। dhyātvā kṣaṇaṃ tathā samyag gautamīṃ yāhi mānada ।। varuṇaḥ sarvadātā vai munibhiḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। etac chrutvā nṛpaśreṣṭho munivākyaṃ tathākarot ।।
tataś ca tuṣṭo varuṇo hariścandram uvāca ha ।। yadi yakṣyasi tenaiva tava putro bhaved dhruvam ।। tato gatvā hariścandraś caruṃ kṛtvā tu vāruṇam ।। jāte putre apām īśaḥ provāca vadatāṃ varaḥ ।।
adyaiva putro yaṣṭavyaḥ smarase vacanaṃ purā ।। hariścandro api varuṇaṃ provācedaṃ kramāgatam ।। nirdaśo medhyatāṃ yāti paśur yakṣye tato hy aham ।। nirdaśe punar abhyetya yajasvety āha taṃ nṛpam ।।
paśor danteṣu jāteṣu ehi gacchādhunāppate ।। jāteṣu caiva danteṣu saptavarṣeṣu nārada ।। rājāpi varuṇaṃ prāha patsyantīme apāṃpate ।। yajasveti nṛpaṃ prāha rājā prāha tv apāṃpatim ।।
dhanurvedaṃ yadā vetti tadā syāt paśur uttamaḥ ।। yadāstreṣu ca śastreṣu samartho abhūt sa rohitaḥ ।। yuvarājyam anuprāpte rohite ṣoḍaśābdike ।। āgatya varuṇaḥ prāha yajasvādya sutaṃ svakam ।।
rohitaṃ ca sutaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ śṛṇvato varuṇasya ca ।। ehi putra mahāvīra yakṣye tvāṃ varuṇāya hi ।। rohitaḥ pitaraṃ prāha śṛṇvato varuṇasya ca ।। paśunā varuṇenātha tad anujñātum arhasi ।।
kopena mahatāviṣṭo jalodaram athākarot ।। gṛhītvā sa dhanur divyaṃ rathārūḍho gatavyathaḥ ।। gaṅgāyāṃ prāptavān putraṃ tatrāgāt so api rohitaḥ ।। tatra sthitvā nṛpasutaḥ śuśrāva nṛpate rujam ।।
kiṃ phalaṃ kiṃ nu kṛtyaṃ syād ity evaṃ paryacintayat ।। gaṅgātīre vartamānam apaśyad ṛṣisattamam ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpateḥ putro namasyedaṃ vaco abravīt ।। kṣīṇavṛttiḥ kṛśaḥ kasmād durmanā iva lakṣyase ।।
ajīgarto api covāca rohitaṃ nṛpateḥ sutam ।। vinānnena mariṣyāmo brūhi kiṃ karavāmahe ।। tac chrutvā punar apy āha nṛpaputra ṛṣiṃ tadā ।। tava kiṃ vartate citte tad brūhi vadatāṃ vara ।।
vidyate nṛpaśārdūla vartanaṃ nāsti me tataḥ ।। naiteṣāṃ katamasyāpi kretānnena nṛpottama ।। vada nānyac ca vaktavyaṃ viprā vai satyavādinaḥ ।। bhāryāṃ vāpi gṛhāṇemāṃ krītvā jīvāmahe vayam ।।
yuvānaṃ dehi putraṃ me putrāṇāṃ yaṃ tvam icchasi ।। madhyamaṃ tu śunaḥśepaṃ krīṇāmi vada taddhanam ।। yadi krīṇāsi mūlyaṃ tvaṃ vada satyaṃ mahāmune ।। rājaputra varaṃ dehi dāsyāmi svasutaṃ tava ।।
pitre nivedayām āsa krayakrītam ṛṣeḥ sutam ।। varuṇāya yajasva tvaṃ paśunā tvam arug bhava ।। tathovāca hariścandraḥ putravākyād anantaram ।। viśeṣatas tu varṇānāṃ guravo hi dvijottamāḥ ।।
avajñayāpi yeṣāṃ syān nṛpāṇāṃ svakulakṣayaḥ ।। ahaṃ ca brāhmaṇaṃ kuryāṃ paśuṃ naitad dhi yujyate ।। karomi tasmāt putra tvaṃ brāhmaṇena sukhaṃ vraja ।। etasminn antare tatra vāg uvācāśarīriṇī ।।
paśunā vipraputreṇa rohitena sutena ca ।। kratuḥ pūrṇo bhavet tatra tasmād yāhi mahāmate ।। viśvāmitreṇa ṛṣiṇā vasiṣṭhena purodhasā ।। prāpya gaṅgāṃ gautamīṃ tāṃ naramedhāya dīkṣitaḥ ।।
kṛtvā sarvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ tasmin yajñe pravartite ।। vāribhiḥ prokṣitaṃ dṛṣṭvā viśvāmitro abravīd idam ।। anujānantv imaṃ sarve śunaḥśepaṃ dvijottamam ।। anujānantu te sarve śunaḥśepaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।
agnau hoṣyaḥ paśuś cāyaṃ śunaḥśepo dvijottamaḥ ।। gautamīṃ yāntu viprendrāḥ snātvā devān pṛthak pṛthak ।। enaṃ rakṣantu munayo devāś ca haviṣo bhujaḥ ।। tato gatvā śunaḥśepo gaṅgāṃ trailokyapāvanīm ।।
avadanta surāḥ sarve viśvāmitrasya śṛṇvataḥ ।। kratuḥ pūrṇo bhavatv eṣa śunaḥśepavadhaṃ vinā ।। tataḥ pūrṇo abhavad rājño nṛmedho lokaviśrutaḥ ।। tīrthasya tu prasādena rājñaḥ pūrṇo abhavat kratuḥ ।।
akarod ātmanaḥ putraṃ pūjayitvā surāntike ।। na menire ye ca putrā viśvāmitrasya dhīmataḥ ।। jyaiṣṭhyaṃ ye menire putrāḥ pūjayām āsa tān sutān ।। etat sarvaṃ yatra jātaṃ gautamyā dakṣiṇe taṭe ।।
bahūni teṣāṃ nāmāni mattaḥ śṛṇu mahāmate ।। ityādy aṣṭa sahasrāṇi tīrthāny atha caturdaśa ।। ākhyātaṃ cāsya māhātmyaṃ tīrthasya munisattama ।। aputraḥ putram āpnoti yac cānyan manasaḥ priyam ।।
tatra vṛttaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ śṛṇu yatnena nārada ।। na devānāṃ tadā devā mām abhyetyedam abruvan ।। yathā syāt somo hy asmākaṃ tathā nītir vidhīyatām ।। tebhyo dattvātha māṃ devāḥ somam āhartum arhatha ।।
vinā tenāpi na sthātuṃ śakyaṃ naiva tvayā vinā ।। atra buddhir vidhātavyā kriyatāṃ kratur uttamaḥ ।। makhaṃ tu viṣayaṃ kṛtvā āyāntu surasattamāḥ ।। tathety uktvā suragaṇāḥ sarasvatyā vacaḥsthitāḥ ।।
āhvānaṃ cakrire tatra puṇye devagirau tadā ।। tatrāgaman suragaṇā gandharvā yakṣakiṃnarāḥ ।। ṛṣibhir gautamītīre kriyamāṇe mahādhvare ।। tatra devaiḥ parivṛtaḥ sahasrākṣo abhyabhāṣata ।।
sarasvatyā paṇadhvaṃ no yuṣmākam amṛtātmanā ।। somaṃ dattvā surebhyas tu jagṛhus tāṃ sarasvatīm ।। avasat tatra vāgīśā tathāpi ca surāntike ।। ata eva hi somasya krayo bhavati nārada ।।
tato abhavad devatānāṃ somaś cāpi sarasvatī ।। tatrāgaman sarva eva somārthaṃ gautamītaṭam ।। pūrṇāhutir yatra dattā pūrṇākhyānaṃ tad ucyate ।। tannāmadheyatīrthāni saṃkṣepāc chṛṇu nārada ।।
pūrṇātīrthaṃ tataḥ śālaṃ śrīparṇāsaṃgamaṃ tathā ।। puṣṭisaṃgamam ākhyātaṃ karṇikāsaṃgamaṃ śubham ।। vāsavīsaṃgamaś caiva śivaśaryā tathā śikhī ।। ajo vṛddhaḥ suro bhadro gautamyā saha saṃgatāḥ ।।
pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni hy agaman devaparvate ।। tāni tīrthāni gaṅgāyāṃ saṃgatāni yathākramam ।। sarorūpeṇa kāny atra stavarūpeṇa kānicit ।। teṣu snānaṃ japo homaḥ pitṛtarpaṇam eva ca ।।
sarvapāpavinirmukto yāti viṣṇupuraṃ janaḥ ।। yatra siddheśvaro devaḥ sarvalokopakārakṛt ।। teṣāṃ parasparaṃ vāpi prītiś cābhūn mahāmune ।। meruparvatam āsādya parasparahitaiṣiṇaḥ ।।
pibāmaḥ sarva evaite bhavāmaś cāmarā vayam ।। prāpsyāmaḥ saṃgaraṃ hitvā saṃgaro duḥkhakāraṇam ।। yataḥ snehena vṛttir yā sāsmākaṃ sukhadā sadā ।। tad ūrdhvam api vā yat tu nirvairatvād avāpyate ।।
ekībhūtāś ca suprītā vimathya varuṇālayam ।। devāś ca dānavāḥ sarve mamanthur varuṇālayam ।। niṣpanne cāmṛte puṇye te ca procuḥ parasparam ।। sarve samaṃ ca sarvebhyo yathāyogyaṃ vibhajyatām ।।
vibhajyatām idaṃ puṇyam amṛtaṃ surasattamāḥ ।। gateṣu daityasaṃgheṣu devāḥ sarve anvamantrayan ।। ripūṇām amṛtaṃ naiva deyaṃ bhavati sarvathā ।। bṛhaspatis tathety āha punar āha surān idam ।।
ayam evocito mantro yac chatrūṇāṃ parābhavaḥ ।। na viśvāsyā na cākhyeyā naiva mantryāś ca śatravaḥ ।। tāñ jetuṃ naiva śakṣyāmo na deyam amṛtaṃ tataḥ ।। iti saṃmantrya te devā vācaspatim athābruvan ।।
kurmas tad eva prathamaṃ vada vācaspate tathā ।। sa tu jñātā ca vaktā ca dātā caiva pitāmahaḥ ।। namasya māṃ surāḥ sarve yad vṛttaṃ tan nyavedayan ।। viṣṇave kathitaṃ sarvaṃ śaṃbhave viṣahāriṇe ।।
merukandaram āgatya na jānanti yathāsurāḥ ।। ādityas tatra vijñātā somabhojyān athetarān ।। naiva jānanti tad daityā danujā rākṣasās tathā ।। kāmarūpadharo rāhur marutāṃ madhyam āviśat ।।
jñātvā divākaro daityaṃ taṃ somāya nyavedayat ।। dattvā somaṃ tadā somo viṣṇave tan nyavedayat ।। ciccheda tarasā vatsa tacchiras tv amaraṃ tv abhūt ।। dehaṃ tad amṛtaspṛṣṭaṃ patitaṃ dakṣiṇe taṭe ।।
dehaṃ cāpy amaraṃ putra tad adbhutam ivābhavat ।। ubhayaṃ cāmaraṃ jātaṃ daityaś cāyaṃ mahābalaḥ ।। tatas te śaṃkaraṃ prāhur devāḥ sarve sasaṃbhramāḥ ।। tvaṃ deva karuṇāsindhuḥ śaraṇāgatarakṣakaḥ ।।
śirasā naiva yujyeta daityadehaṃ tathā kuru ।। mātṛbhiḥ sahitāṃ devīṃ mātaraṃ lokapālinīm ।। mahīgataṃ yatra dehaṃ tatrāgād bhakṣyakāṅkṣiṇī ।। deho devyā punas tatra yuyudhe bahavaḥ samāḥ ।।
atrāste rasam utkṛṣṭaṃ tad ākṛṣya śarīrataḥ ।। bhasmībhūyāt kṣaṇenaiva tasmāt kurvantu tat purā ।। abhyaṣiñcan grahāṇāṃ tvaṃ graho bhūyā mudānvitaḥ ।। dehaṃ bhittvā daityapateḥ suraśaktisamanvitā ।।
sthāpayitvā tu tad dehaṃ bhakṣayām āsa cāmbikā ।। sthāpitaṃ rasam utkṛṣṭaṃ rasānāṃ pravaraṃ rasam ।। ākṛṣṭam amṛtaṃ caiva sthāpitaṃ sāpy abhakṣayat ।। rāhudehasamudbhūtā rudraśaktisamanvitā ।।
tatra pañca sahasrāṇi tīrthāni guṇavanti ca ।। tasyai tuṣṭāḥ surāḥ sarve devyai nadyai pṛthak pṛthak ।। śaṃbhuḥ surapatir loke tathā pūjām avāpsyasi ।। sadā tiṣṭha raseśāni sarveṣāṃ sarvasiddhidā ।।
tvāṃ namasyanti ye bhaktyā kiṃcid āpekṣya sarvadā ।। śivaśaktyor yatas tasmin nivāso abhūt sanātanaḥ ।। pravarāyāḥ purā devāḥ suprītās te varān daduḥ ।। tatrāplutānāṃ sarveṣāṃ bhuktir vā muktir eva ca ।।
syāt teṣāṃ sarvam eveha evaṃ dattvā surā yayuḥ ।। preritā devadevena śaktir yā preritā tu sā ।। amṛtā saiva vikhyātā pravaraivaṃ mahānadī ।। tasyākhyānaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu pāpapraṇāśanam ।।
yadā purābhavad bālo gautamasya suto dvijaḥ ।। sa vairāgyāj jagāmātha deśaṃ tīrtham itas tataḥ ।। śiṣyair anyaiḥ sahādhyāyo lajjitasya ca nābhavat ।। etāvatā gautamo api vyagamac carituṃ bahiḥ ।।
naiva cādhyayanaṃ tasya saṃjātaṃ gautamasya hi ।। agnikāryaṃ tataś cakre nityam eva yatavrataḥ ।। agnyupāsanamātraṃ ca gāyatryabhyasanaṃ tathā ।। upāsato agniṃ vidhivad gāyatrīṃ ca mahātmanaḥ ।।
na dārasaṃgrahaṃ lebhe naiva dātāsti kanyakām ।। āśrameṣu ca puṇyeṣu aṭann āste sa gautamaḥ ।। tatrāpaśyad guhāṃ ramyāṃ vallīviṭapamālinīm ।। cintayaṃs tu praviṣṭo asāv apaśyat striyam uttamām ।।
brahmacaryeṇa vartantīṃ virāgāṃ rahasi sthitām ।। namasyantaṃ muniśreṣṭhaṃ taṃ gautamam avārayat ।। tasya naśyati vai sarvaṃ yaṃ namasyati vai guruḥ ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭas tāṃ vai gautamaḥ prāha vismitaḥ ।।
alpavidyas tv alpavayā ahaṃ tava guruḥ katham ।। guṇavān matimāñ śūraḥ kṣatradharmaparāyaṇaḥ ।। viśrāmam akarod asyāṃ guhāyāṃ sa ṛtadhvajaḥ ।। taṃ viśrāntaṃ nṛpavaram apsarā dadṛśe tataḥ ।।
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā cakame rājā rājānaṃ cakame ca sā ।। nivṛttakāmo rājendras tām āpṛcchyāgamad gṛham ।। gacchantī māṃ tadā mātā idam āha tapodhana ।। yas tv asyāṃ praviśed bhadre sa te bhartā bhaviṣyati ।।
tasmād atra praviṣṭas tvaṃ pumān nānyaḥ kadācana ।। atraiva ca tapas taptvā tataḥ svargam upeyivān ।। varṣāṇi muniśārdūla rājyaṃ kṛtvā tathā paraḥ ।। ahaṃ brahman nānyavṛttā na mātā na pitā mama ।।
tasmād bhajasva māṃ brahman vratasthāṃ puruṣārthinīm ।। ahaṃ bālas tvaṃ tu vṛddhā naivāyaṃ ghaṭate mithaḥ ।। dhātrā dattas tatas tvaṃ māṃ na nirākartum arhasi ।। tatas tyakṣyāmi jīvaṃ me idānīṃ tava paśyataḥ ।।
anuraktajanatyāge pātakānto na vidyate ।। vṛddhāyās tad vacaḥ śrutvā gautamo vākyam abravīt ।। nāhaṃ varo hi yogyas te kurūpo bhogavarjitaḥ ।। paścāt te vacanaṃ kāryaṃ tato vṛddhābravīd dvijam ।।
tathaivāpo rūpavatyo rūpadātāgnir eva ca ।। agniś ca rūpavān devas tava rūpaṃ pradāsyati ।। prārthayitvā suvidyaṃ taṃ surūpaṃ cākaron munim ।। guhāyāṃ muniśārdūla ājagmur munayo amalāḥ ।।
bhramantaḥ puṇyatīrthāni prāpnuvaṃs tasya tāṃ guhām ।। satkāram akarot teṣāṃ jahasus taṃ ca kecana ।। vṛddhāṃ ca gautamaṃ prekṣya jahasus tatra kecana ।। satyaṃ vadasva kalyāṇi ity evaṃ jahasur dvijāḥ ।।
iṣṭāniṣṭasamāyogo dṛṣṭo asmābhir aho cirāt ।। evam uktvā kṛtātithyā yayuḥ sarve maharṣayaḥ ।। papraccha muniśārdūlam agastyam ṛṣisattamam ।। śīghram eva mahāprājña bhuktimuktipradāyakam ।।
sarve kāmās tatra pūrṇā gautamyāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। ahaṃ tvām anuyāsyāmi yathecchasi tathā kuru ।। tatra tepe tapas tīvraṃ patnyā sa bhagavān ṛṣiḥ ।। gaṅgāṃ ca toṣayām āsa bhāryārthaṃ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ ।।
marubhūmāv adhvagānāṃ viṭapīva priyāyutaḥ ।। sasyānāṃ ghanavat kṛṣṇa tvam avagrahaśoṣiṇām ।। adhogatānāṃ taptānāṃ śaraṇaṃ bhava gautami ।। śaraṇāgatadīnārtaṃ śaraṇyā gautamī mudā ।।
kalaśair upacāraiś ca tataḥ patnī tava priyā ।। sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇā ramyarūpam avāpsyati ।। sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇaḥ kāntaṃ rūpam avāpsyasi ।। surūpatām ubhau prāptau gautamyāś ca prasādataḥ ।।
tasyā nāmnā tu vikhyātā vṛddhāyā munisattama ।। vṛddhā tu gautamīṃ prāha gaṅgāṃ pratyakṣarūpiṇīm ।। tvayā ca saṃgamas tasyās tasyās tīrtham anuttamam ।। snānadānādihomaiś ca pitṝṇāṃ pāvanaṃ param ।।
gautamasthāpitaṃ liṅgaṃ vṛddhānāmnaiva kīrtitam ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvābhīṣṭapradāyakam ।। tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ vṛddhāsaṃgamam ucyate ।। brahmahatyādipāpānāṃ pāvanaṃ sarvakāmadam ।।
mahatyā senayā sārdhaṃ jagāma mṛgayāvanam ।। nānākāradvijayutaṃ viṭapaiḥ pariśobhitam ।। tatraiva matim ādhatta ilo amātyān athābravīt ।। deśaṃ kośaṃ balaṃ rājyaṃ pālayantu punaś ca tam ।।
patnībhiḥ sahito dhīmān araṇye ahaṃ vasāmy atha ।। mṛgayāśīlibhiḥ kaiścid yāntu sarva itaḥ purīm ।। himavantaṃ ratnamayaṃ vasaṃs tatra ilo nṛpaḥ ।। tatra yakṣeśvaraḥ kaścit samanyur iti viśrutaḥ ।।
tasmin vasaty asau yakṣo ramaṇīye nagottame ।। svecchayā svavane yakṣaḥ krīḍate nṛtyagītakaiḥ ।। ilas tu taṃ na jānāti kandaraṃ yakṣapālitam ।। tatropaviṣṭo nṛpatir mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ ।।
sa yakṣo adharmakopena bhāryayā mṛgarūpadhṛk ।। hṛtaṃ gehaṃ mamānena kiṃ karomīty acintayat ।। ātmīyān preṣayām āsa yakṣāñ śūrān dhanurdharān ।। gṛhād yathānyato yāti mama tat kartum arhatha ।।
ilaṃ gatvābruvan sarve nirgacchāsmād guhālayāt ।। tad yakṣavacanāt kopād yuddhaṃ cakre sa rājarāṭ ।। yakṣeśvaro mṛgo bhūtvā bhāryayāpi vane vasan ।। prāha cintāparo bhūtvā mṛgīrūpadharāṃ priyām ।।
katham āyāti vipadaṃ tatropāyo vicintyatām ।। prāpayomāvanaṃ subhrūr mṛgī bhūtvā manoharā ।। ahaṃ tu puruṣo yena tvaṃ punaḥ strī ca yakṣiṇī ।। gate api tvayi ko doṣas tan me kathaya tattvataḥ ।।
pārvatī śaṃkaraṃ prāha kadācid rahasi sthitam ।। tasmān me niyataṃ deśam ājñayā rakṣitaṃ tava ।। vinā tvayā gaṇeśena kārttikeyena nandinā ।। yas tv atra praviśen nātha strītvaṃ tasya bhaved iti ।।
tasmān mayā na gantavyam umāyā vanam uttamam ।। mṛgī bhūtvā viśālākṣī ilasya purato abhavat ।। mṛgayāsaktacitto vai mṛgīṃ dṛṣṭvā viśeṣataḥ ।। sākarṣata śanais taṃ tu rājānaṃ mṛgayākulam ।।
adṛśyā tu mṛgī tasmai darśayantī kvacit kvacit ।। hariṇī capalākṣī sā tam ākarṣad umāvanam ।। umāvanaṃ praviṣṭaṃ taṃ jñātvā sā yakṣiṇī tadā ।। divyarūpaṃ samāsthāya cāśokatarusaṃnidhau ।।
divyarūpadharā tanvī kṛtakāryā samā tadā ।। mṛgīm ālokayantaṃ taṃ capalākṣam ilaṃ tadā ।। bhartṛvākyam aśeṣeṇa smarantī prāha bhūmipam ।। puruṣasya ca veṣeṇa ile kam anuyāsyasi ।।
yakṣiṇīṃ bhartsayitvāsau tām apṛcchan mṛgīṃ punaḥ ।। ileti vacanaṃ śrutvā dhṛtacāpo hayasthitaḥ ।। punaḥ sā prāha nṛpatiṃ mahātmānam ile svayam ।। tadā cālokayad rājā stanau tuṅgau bhujāntare ।।
kim idaṃ mama saṃjātam ity evaṃ cakito abhavat ।। vada sarvaṃ yathātathyaṃ tvaṃ kā vā vada suvrate ।। yakṣāṇām adhipaḥ śrīmāṃs tadbhāryāhaṃ tu yakṣiṇī ।। yasya yakṣā hatā mohāt tvayā hi saṃgaraṃ vinā ।।
praviṣṭā tvaṃ praviṣṭo asi purā prāha maheśvaraḥ ।। prauḍho api ko atra jānāti vicitrabhavitavyatām ।। tam āśvāsya punaḥ saiva yakṣiṇī vākyam abravīt ।। strīlālityaṃ strīvilāsaṃ strīkṛtyaṃ sarvam eva tat ।।
ilā sarvam athāvāpya yakṣiṇīṃ vākyam abravīt ।। ārtānām ārtiśamanāc chreyo nābhyadhikaṃ kvacit ।। āśramas tasya subhage pitaraṃ nityam eṣyati ।। draṣṭuṃ yāti tato nityaṃ namaskartuṃ tathaiva ca ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā tvaṃ tu subhage sarvakāmān avāpsyasi ।। yakṣiṇī sā tam ācaṣṭa yakṣo api sukham āptavān ।। umāvanasthitā celā gāyantī nṛtyatī punaḥ ।। kadācit kriyamāṇe tu ilayā nṛtyakarmaṇi ।।
ilāṃ dṛṣṭvā gatiṃ tyaktvā tām āgatyābravīd budhaḥ ।। bhāryā bhava mama svasthā sarvābhyas tvaṃ priyā bhava ।। smṛtvā ca yakṣiṇīvākyaṃ tatas tuṣṭābhavan mune ।। tato bahutithe kāle budhas tuṣṭo avadat priyām ।।
kiṃ te deyaṃ mayā bhadre priyaṃ yan manasi sthitam ।। ilā budhaṃ somasutaṃ prītimantaṃ priyaṃ tathā ।। putras te bhavitā tasmāt kṣatriyo lokaviśrutaḥ ।। buddhyā bṛhaspatisamaḥ kṣamayā pṛthivīsamaḥ ।।
vīryeṇājau harir iva kopena hutabhug yathā ।। jayaśabdaś ca sarvatra tv āsīc ca suraveśmani ।। aham apy āgamaṃ tatra mudā yukto mahāmate ।। tena sarve apy avocan vai saṃgatā ṛṣayaḥ surāḥ ।।
syād ity evaṃ nāma cakruḥ sarve saṃtuṣṭamānasāḥ ।। dhanurvedaṃ saprayogaṃ budhaḥ prādāt tadātmaje ।। namasyātha vinītātmā ilām ailo abravīd idam ।। ahaṃ ca putraḥ karmaṇyaḥ kasmāt te mānaso jvaraḥ ।।
bhartṛputrakṛtā cintā na mamāsti kadācana ।। cintayeyaṃ mahābuddhe tato mātaram abravīt ।। nivedayasva me mātas tad eva prathamaṃ mama ।। magnānāṃ duḥkhapāthobdhau putraḥ pravahaṇaṃ param ।।
pādayoḥ patitaś cāpi vada mātar yathā tathā ।। tatrotpattiṃ svasya nāma rājyaprāptiṃ priyān sutān ।। vananiryāṇam evātha amātyānāṃ purodhasaḥ ।। himavatkandaragatiṃ yakṣeśvaragṛhe gatim ।।
maheśvarājñayā tatra cāpraveśaṃ narasya tu ।। budhaprāptiṃ tathā prītiṃ putrotpattyādy aśeṣataḥ ।। purūravāḥ kiṃ karomi kiṃ kṛtvā sukṛtaṃ bhavet ।। yad apy anyan manovarti tad apy ājñāpayasva me ।।
abhiṣekaṃ ca putrāṇāṃ tava cāpi viśeṣataḥ ।। sarvaṃ ca kartum icchāmi tava putra prasādataḥ ।। tapaso vānyato vāpi vadasva mama tattvataḥ ।। sa tu sarvaṃ tu jānāti upadekṣyati te hitam ।।
uvāca praṇato bhūtvā mātuḥ kṛtyaṃ tathātmanaḥ ।। umāvanapraveśaṃ ca śaṃbhor ājñāṃ tathaiva ca ।। viśāpo bhavitā putra tāv ārādhya na cānyathā ।। tīrthād vā tapaso vāpi tat pitaḥ prathamaṃ vada ।।
umayā sahitaḥ śrīmāñ śāpahantā varapradaḥ ।। gautamīṃ tapase dhīmān gaṅgāṃ trailokyapāvanīm ।। himavantaṃ giriṃ natvā mātaraṃ pitaraṃ gurum ।। te sarve gautamīṃ prāptā himavatparvatottamāt ।।
bhavasya devadevasya stutikramam imaṃ śṛṇu ।। tataḥ purūravāḥ putro gaurīṃ devīṃ ca śaṃkaram ।। kṛtakṛtyāḥ stha bhadraṃ vo devānām api duṣkaram ।। tat kṣamasva sureśāni puṃstvaṃ dātuṃ tvam arhasi ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavān āha devīvākyarataḥ sadā ।। atrābhiṣekamātreṇa puṃstvaṃ prāpnotv ayaṃ nṛpaḥ ।। nṛtyaṃ gītaṃ ca lāvaṇyaṃ yakṣiṇyā yad upārjitam ।। nṛtyā gītā ca saubhāgyā imā nadyo babhūvire ।।
teṣu snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca surarājyaphalapradam ।। mahābhyudayasiddhyarthaṃ vājimedham athākarot ।। amātyāṃś ca balaṃ kośam ānīya sa nṛpottamaḥ ।। ilasya nāmnā vikhyātaṃ tatra tat puram ucyate ।।
rājye abhiṣicya paścāt tam ailaṃ snehād asiñcayat ।। sarvebhyo matimānebhyo jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭho abhavan mune ।। yatra puṃstvam avāpyātha yatra putrāḥ samāgatāḥ ।। nadyo bhūtvā yatra gaṅgāṃ saṃgatās tāni nārada ।।
teṣu snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvakratuphalapradam ।। yatra cakreśvaro devaś cakram āpa yato hariḥ ।। pūjayām āsa tat tīrthaṃ cakratīrtham udāhṛtam ।। dakṣakratau pravṛtte tu devānāṃ ca samāgame ।।
anāhvāne sureśasya dakṣacitte malīmase ।। ahalyāyāṃ coktavatyāṃ kupitābhūt sureśvarī ।। śṛṇvatī doṣavākyāni pitrā coktāni bhartari ।। yādṛśas tādṛśo vāpi patiḥ strīṇāṃ parā gatiḥ ।।
śrutaṃ tannindanaṃ tarhi dhārayāmi na dehakam ।। kopena mahatāviṣṭā prajajvāla sureśvarī ।। maheśvaro api sakalaṃ vṛttam ākarṇya nāradāt ।। te ūcatur ubhe devaṃ dakṣakratuvināśanam ।।
bhīmair gaṇaiḥ parivṛto bhūtanāthaiḥ samaṃ yayau ।। dakṣeṇa yajamānena śuddhabhāvena rakṣitaḥ ।। indrādityādyair vasubhiḥ sarvataḥparipālitaḥ ।। śraddhā puṣṭis tathā tuṣṭiḥ śāntir lajjā sarasvatī ।।
etābhiś ca tathānyābhiḥ sarvataḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ ।। surabhir nandinī dhenuḥ kāmadhuk kāmadohinī ।। kalpavṛkṣaḥ pārijāto latāḥ kalpalatādikāḥ ।। svayaṃ maghavatā pūṣṇā hariṇā parirakṣitaḥ ।।
etaiś ca sarvato vākyair dakṣasya pūjitaṃ makham ।। śokakopaparītātmā paścāc chūlapinākadhṛk ।। tāni bhūtāni parito makhe veṣṭya maheśvaram ।। palāyanta tataḥ kecit kecid gatvā tataḥ śivam ।।
evaṃ vidhvaṃsitaṃ yajñaṃ dṛṣṭvā pūṣā samabhyagāt ।। bhagasya cakṣuṣī vipra vīrabhadro vyapāṭayat ।। tataḥ suragaṇāḥ sarve viṣṇuṃ te śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।। tena dagdho makhaḥ sarvo vaiṣṇavaḥ paśyato hareḥ ।।
bhūtanātho api tac cakram āpatac ca tadāgrasat ।। tuṣṭāva śaṃkaraṃ devaṃ dakṣo bhaktyā prajāpatiḥ ।। jaya kalyāṇabhṛc chaṃbho jaya kālātmane namaḥ ।। brahmapriya namas te astu brahmarūpa namo astu te ।।
sarvamūrte namas te astu trailokyādhāra kāmada ।। yajñarūpa namas te astu yajñadhāma namo astu te ।। yajñahartre namas te astu phaladāya namo astu te ।। bhaktānām apy abhaktānāṃ tvam eva śaraṇaṃ prabho ।।
kiṃ dadāmīti taṃ prāha kratuḥ pūrṇo astu me prabho ।। śaṃkaraḥ sarvabhūtātmā karuṇāvaruṇālayaḥ ।। evam uktvā sa bhagavān bhūtair antaradhīyata ।। tataḥ kadācid devānāṃ daityānāṃ vigraho mahān ।।
tuṣṭuvuḥ sarvabhāvena vacobhis taṃ janārdanam ।। kimartham āgatāḥ sarve tatkartāsmīty uvāca tān ।। tatas trāṇāya devānāṃ matiṃ kuru janārdana ।। yāntu sarve devagaṇā rakṣā vaḥ kriyate mayā ।।
godāvarīṃ tato gatvā śaṃbhoḥ pūjāṃ pracakrame ।। bhaktito nityavat pūjāṃ cakre viṣṇur umāpateḥ ।। kamalānāṃ sahasre tu yadaikaṃ naiva pūryate ।। dhyātvā śaṃbhuṃ dadāv arghyam ananyaśaraṇo hariḥ ।।
tvam eva śaraṇo adhīśo atra kā bhaved vicāraṇā ।। bhavānīsahitaḥ śaṃbhuḥ purastād abhavat tadā ।। tad eva cakram abhavan netraṃ cāpi yathā purā ।। gaṅgāṃ cāpi saricchreṣṭhāṃ devaṃ ca vṛṣabhadhvajam ।।
yasyānuśravaṇenaiva mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ ।। tat tu cakrāṅkitaṃ tīrtham adyāpi paridṛśyate ।। yatra cakreśvaro devaś cakram āpa yato hariḥ ।। pūjayām āsa tat tīrthaṃ cakratīrtham udāhṛtam ।।
mahimānaṃ yasya vaktuṃ na kṣamo apy ahināyakaḥ ।। śṛṇu nārada tad bhaktyā sākṣād vedoditaṃ mayā ।। tasya bhāryā mahāprājñā kulīnā ca pativratā ।। iti nāmnā ca vikhyātā vaḍaveti prakīrtitā ।।
dadhīcir agnimān nityaṃ gṛhadharmaparāyaṇaḥ ।। svakalatrarataḥ śāntaḥ kumbhayonir ivāparaḥ ।। ājagmur muniśārdūla yatrāgastyasya cāśramaḥ ।। indro viṣṇur yamo agniś ca jitvā daityān upāgatān ।।
dadhīciṃ muniśārdūlaṃ dṛṣṭvā nemuḥ sureśvarāḥ ।। gṛhakṛtyaṃ tataś cakre surebhyo bhāryayā saha ।। dadhīcim abruvan devā bhāryayā sukhitaṃ punaḥ ।। āsīnaṃ hṛṣṭamanasa ṛṣiṃ natvā punaḥ punaḥ ।।
tvādṛśaḥ sakṛpo yeṣu munir bhūkalpapādapaḥ ।। tīrthāplutir bhūtadayā darśanaṃ ca bhavādṛśām ।। jitvā daityān iha prāptā hatvā rākṣasapuṃgavān ।। nāyudhaiḥ phalam asmākaṃ voḍhuṃ naiva kṣamā vayam ।।
svarge suradviṣo jñātvā sthāpitāni haranti ca ।। tasmāt tavāśrame puṇye sthāpyante astrāṇi mānada ।। pippalānāṃ samīpe tu nyasya bālaṃ namasya ca ।। viveśāgniṃ prātitheyī bhartrā saha divaṃ yayau ।।
putravat poṣitā yena ṛṣiṇā ca dadhīcinā ।। mṛgāś ca pakṣiṇaḥ sarve vṛkṣāḥ procuḥ parasparam ।। ye kurvanty aniśaṃ snehaṃ ta eva kṛtino narāḥ ।। tathā pitā na mātā vā dhig asmān pāpino vayam ।।
bālo dadhīciḥ prātitheyī bālo dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। somaṃ rājānam abhyetya yācire amṛtam uttamam ।। dadur bālāya te cāpi amṛtaṃ suravallabham ।। pravṛddhaḥ pippalān evam uvāca tv ativismitaḥ ।।
vārkṣas tv ahaṃ kathaṃ jāto hastapādādijīvavān ।। dadhīcer maraṇaṃ sādhvyās tathā cāgnipraveśanam ।। śrutvā duḥkhasamāviṣṭo nipapāta tadā bhuvi ।। āśvastaḥ sa punaḥ prāha tadauṣadhivanaspatīn ।।
pitur mitrāṇi śatrūṃś ca tathā putro anuvartate ।। vadanti pitṛmitrāṇi tārayanty ahitān api ।। śrutvā somo api taṃ bālaṃ pippalādam abhāṣata ।। pippalādas tam apy āha oṣadhīśaṃ vinītavat ।।
na karomy atra yāvac ca tasmāt tat prathamaṃ vada ।। yatra tīrthe ca sidhyeta matsaṃkalpaḥ surottama ।। sarvaṃ maheśvarād devāj jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। bālo ahaṃ bālabuddhiś ca na sāmarthyaṃ tapas tathā ।।
prasannas tu taveśāno hy alpāyāsena vatsaka ।। āste sākṣātkṛtaḥ śaṃbhur viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā ।। gaccha tatra mahābuddhe daṇḍake gautamīṃ nadīm ।। sa te prītamanās tāta sarvān kāmān pradāsyati ।।
ājagāma jagannātho yatra rudraḥ sa cakradaḥ ।। tuṣṭāva sarvabhāvena pippalādaḥ śivaṃ śuciḥ ।। tataḥ svayaṃbhūḥ suprītaḥ pippalādam abhāṣata ।। varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te pippalāda yathepsitam ।।
adāmbhikaḥ satyavādī tathā mātā pativratā ।। duḥkhakopasamāviṣṭo nāhaṃ jīvitum utsahe ।। avadhyasevyas trailokye tvam eva śaśiśekhara ।। tataḥ samartho bhavitā devāṃś chedayituṃ bhavān ।।
na śaśāka tadovāca na śakto asmīti śaṃkaram ।। tṛtīyaṃ tvaṃ tadābhīṣṭaṃ prāpsyase nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। dadhīcisūnur dharmātmā tatraiva bahulāḥ samāḥ ।। pratyahaṃ prātar utthāya snātvā natvā gurūn kramāt ।।
hastasvastikam āropya nābhau vismṛtasaṃsṛtiḥ ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā vinīta idam abravīt ।। tārtīyacakṣuṣo jyotir yadā paśyasi tatkṣaṇāt ।। tasmād ripuvināśāya hetubhūtāṃ prayaccha me ।।
mātā tava prātitheyī vadanty evaṃ divaṃ gatā ।। itas tato bhrāntacittāḥ patanti narakāvaṭe ।। abhimāne jvalaty antaḥ sādhuvādo nirarthakaḥ ।। vaḍaveti smaran vipraḥ kṛtyāpi vaḍavākṛtiḥ ।।
gabhastinī bālagarbhā yā mātā pippalāśinaḥ ।। utpannā sā mahāraudrā mṛtyujihveva bhīṣaṇā ।। pippalādo api tāṃ prāha devān khāda ripūn mama ।। sa prāha kim idaṃ kṛtye sā cāpy āha tvayoditam ।।
tuṣṭāva devaṃ sa muniḥ kṛtyāṃ prāha tadā śivaḥ ।। tasmād yāhi tato dūraṃ kṛtye kṛtyaṃ tataḥ kuru ।। prātiṣṭhad vaḍavārūpā kṛtyā sā ṛṣinirmitā ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā vibudhāḥ sarve trastāḥ śaṃbhum upāgaman ।।
stuvanto bhītamanasaḥ śaṃbhum ūcur divaukasaḥ ।। śaraṇaṃ bhava sarveśa bhītānām abhayaprada ।। sarveṣām eva jantūnāṃ tvam eva śaraṇaṃ śiva ।। sā jighāṃsati lokāṃs trīṃs tvaṃ nas trātā na cetaraḥ ।।
ihaivāsadhvam amarās tasyā vo na bhayaṃ bhavet ।। tat tyaktvātra kathaṃ nātha vatsyāmas tridaśārcita ।। devānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā śivo vākyam athābravīt ।। yo raśmibhis tu dhamate nityaṃ yo janako mataḥ ।।
sthitiṃ karotu tanmūrtau bhaviṣyanty akhilāḥ sthitāḥ ।। devā divākaraṃ cakrus tvaṣṭā bhāskaram abravīt ।। svāṃśaiś ca vayam apy atra tiṣṭhāmaḥ śaṃbhusaṃnidhau ।। gaṅgāyā ubhayaṃ tīram āsādyāsan surottamāḥ ।।
tīrthānāṃ tatra vyuṣṭiṃ ca kaḥ śṛṇoti bravīti vā ।। tataḥ suragaṇāḥ sarve vinītāḥ śivam abruvan ।। pippalādaṃ sureśāna śamaṃ naya jaganmaya ।। om ity uktvā jagannāthaḥ pippalādam avocata ।।
dattāḥ pitrā tava prāṇā devānāṃ kāryasiddhaye ।। tathā yātā divaṃ tāta tava mātā pativratā ।। yad asthibhiḥ surāḥ sarve jayinaḥ sukhinaḥ sadā ।। tvayā putreṇa sarvatra nātaḥ parataraṃ kṛtam ।।
nārtatrāṇād abhyadhikaṃ sukṛtaṃ kvāpi vidyate ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā natvā nātham athābravīt ।। tannāmnā jāyatāṃ tīrthaṃ devadeva jagattraye ।। yāni kṣetrāṇi devānāṃ yāni tīrthāni bhūtale ।।
tataḥ kṣame ahaṃ devānām aparādhaṃ nirañjanaḥ ।। prāpsyase vada kalyāṇaṃ nānyathā tvaṃ manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।। abhinandya ca taṃ devaiḥ sārdhaṃ vākyam athābravīt ।। idam ūcuḥ sarva eva dādhīcaṃ śivasaṃnidhau ।।
pālitā devadevasya ājñā trailokyamaṇḍanī ।। tasmād anyatamaṃ brūhi kiṃcid dāsyāmahe vayam ।। uvāca pippalādaś ca umāṃ natvā ca pippalān ।। te dhanyāḥ prāṇino loke mātāpitror vaśe sthitāḥ ।।
indriyāṇi śarīraṃ ca kulaṃ śaktiṃ dhiyaṃ vapuḥ ।। paśūnāṃ pakṣiṇāṃ cāpi sulabhaṃ mātṛdarśanam ।। durlabhaṃ ca tathā cet syāt sarveṣāṃ yasya kasyacit ।। tayor darśanamātraṃ ca yadi prāpsye surottamāḥ ।।
teṣāṃ mahāpātakānāṃ kaḥ saṃkhyāṃ kartum īśvaraḥ ।। vimānavaram ārūḍhau pitarau daṃpatī śubhau ।। viṣādaṃ lobhamohau ca tyaktvā cittaṃ śamaṃ naya ।। vimānavaram ārūḍhau svargiṇau svarṇabhūṣaṇau ।।
vījyamānau surastrībhiḥ stūyamānau ca kiṃnaraiḥ ।। harṣabāṣpāśrunayanau sa kathaṃcid uvāca tau ।। evaṃbhūto api tau mohāt paśyeyam atidurmatiḥ ।। devāś ca mātāpitarau pippalādam athābruvan ।।
tvayā putreṇa sallokā na kṣīyante kadācana ।। jayaśabdaḥ surair uktaḥ prādurbhūto mahāmune ।। śaṃbhuṃ gaṅgāṃ surān natvā putraṃ vākyam athābravīt ।। kṛtakṛtyas tato vatsa ākramasva ciraṃ divam ।।
dadhīciḥ putram āśvāsya bhāryayā ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। devā apy ūcire sarve pippalādaṃ sasaṃbhramāḥ ।। kṛtyāṃ śamaya bhadraṃ te tad utpannaṃ mahānalam ।। asatyaṃ naiva vaktāhaṃ yūyaṃ kṛtyāṃ tu brūta tām ।।
tām eva gatvā vibudhāḥ procus te śāntikāraṇam ।। sarveṣāṃ bhakṣaṇāyaiva sṛṣṭā cāhaṃ dvijanmanā ।। mahābhūtāni pañcāpi sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ tathā ।। mayā saṃmantrya te devāḥ punar ūcur ubhāv api ।।
vaḍavāpi surān evam uvāca śṛṇu nārada ।। bhavatām icchayā sarvaṃ bhakṣyaṃ me surasattamāḥ ।। tam āhur amarā vahniṃ bhūtānām ādito viduḥ ।। yathaiva tu vayaṃ brūmo gaccha bhuṅkṣva yathāsukham ।।
vrajeyaṃ yadi māṃ tatra prāpayanty udakaṃ mahat ।। agnir apy āha tān devān kanyā māṃ guṇaśālinī ।। tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā kanyām ūcuḥ sarasvatīm ।। nayainam analaṃ śīghraṃ śirasā varuṇālayam ।।
yuktā catasṛbhiḥ śīghraṃ vaheyaṃ varuṇālayam ।। narmadāṃ tapatīṃ caiva surāḥ procuḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।। saṃsthāpya śirasādhārya tā jagmur varuṇālayam ।। adhyāste vibudhaiḥ sārdhaṃ prabhāse śaśibhūṣaṇaḥ ।।
adhyāste ca mahān agniḥ piban vāri śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।। tataḥ suragaṇāḥ sarve śivam ūcuḥ surottamam ।। asthnāṃ ca pāvanaṃ brūhi asmākaṃ ca gavāṃ tathā ।। devāś ca gāvas tatpāpān mucyante nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
tāni prakṣālanād eva tatra prāptāni pūtatām ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca brahmahatyāvināśanam ।। tatra snānān mahābuddhir gomedhaphalam āpnuyāt ।। pitṛtīrthaṃ tu vai jñeyaṃ pitṝṇāṃ prītivardhanam ।।
tatra tīrthe saṃkrameran yāvac candrārkatārakam ।। tataḥ pūtāḥ suragaṇā gāvaḥ śaṃbhum athābruvan ।। asmin sthite dinakare surāḥ sarve pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। sūryo hy ātmāsya jagatas tasthuṣaś ca sanātanaḥ ।।
suravāsaṃ pratiṣṭhānaṃ bhaved yatra ca tryambakam ।। pippalāḥ kālaparyāye svargaṃ jagmur athākṣayam ।। kṣetrādhipatye saṃsthāpya pūjayām āsa śaṃkaram ।। sarvakratuphalaṃ puṇyaṃ smaraṇād aghanāśanam ।।
cakreśvaraḥ pippaleśo devadevasya nāmanī ।। pratiṣṭhānaṃ tu tat kṣetraṃ surāṇām api vallabham ।। yatra nāgeśvaro devaḥ śṛṇu tasyāpi vistaram ।। somavaṃśabhavaḥ śrīmān matimān guṇasāgaraḥ ।।
tasya putraś cirād āsīt sarpo vai bhīṣaṇākṛtiḥ ।। rājñaḥ putraḥ sarpa iti na kaścid vindate janaḥ ।। dhātreyy api na jānāti nāmātyo na purohitaḥ ।। saṃtāpaṃ nityam āpnoti sarpād varam aputratā ।।
sa sarpaḥ pitaraṃ prāha kuru cūḍām api kriyām ।। yāvad vedaṃ na cādhīte tāvac chūdrasamo dvijaḥ ।। adhītavedaḥ sarpo api pitaraṃ cābravīd idam ।। anyathāpi ca kṛtyaṃ te na sidhyed iti me matiḥ ।।
na kuryād yaḥ pitā tasya narakān nāsti niṣkṛtiḥ ।। vismitaḥ sa pitā prāha sutaṃ tam uragākṛtim ।। tasmai kanyāṃ tu ko dadyād vada putra karomi kim ।। tat pitur vacanaṃ śrutvā sarpaḥ prāha vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।
prasahyāharaṇaṃ cāpi śastrair vaivāha eva ca ।। no ced atraiva gaṅgāyāṃ mariṣye nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। vivāhārtham amātyāṃs tān āhūyedaṃ vaco abravīt ।। guṇavān matimāñ śūro durjayaḥ śatrutāpanaḥ ।।
vivāhas tasya kartavyo hy ahaṃ vṛddhas tathaiva ca ।। na dārasaṃgraho yāvat tāvat putro mama priyaḥ ।। vivāhāyātha kurvantu yatnaṃ mama hite ratāḥ ।। sute nyastabharā yānti kṛtinas tapase vanam ।।
ūcuḥ prāñjalayo harṣād rājānaṃ bhūritejasam ।। vivāhe tava putrasya kiṃ mantryaṃ kiṃ tu cintyate ।। putraṃ sarpaṃ tv amātyānāṃ na cākhyāti na te viduḥ ।। mahāvaṃśabhavaḥ śrīmān ko rājā syād guṇāśrayaḥ ।।
tad rājavacanaṃ śrutvā amātyānāṃ mahāmatiḥ ।। rājño matiṃ viditvā tu iṅgitajño abravīd idam ।। vājivāraṇaratnānāṃ yasya saṃkhyā na vidyate ।। tava putrasya yogyā sā bhāryā rājan mayoditā ।।
vṛddhāmātyavacaḥ śrutvā rājā taṃ pratyabhāṣata ।। sutā tasya kathaṃ me asya sutasya syād vadasva tat ।। yac chūrasena kṛtyaṃ syād anujānīhi māṃ tataḥ ।। saṃpūjya preṣayām āsa mahatyā senayā saha ।।
saṃpūjya vividhair vākyair upāyair nītisaṃbhavaiḥ ।। śūrasenasya nṛpateḥ sūnor nāgasya dhīmataḥ ।। pūjayām āsa nṛpatiṃ bhūṣaṇācchādanādibhiḥ ।। tata āgatya rājñe asau vṛddhāmātyo mahāmatiḥ ।।
tato bahutithe kāle vṛddhāmātyo mahāmatiḥ ।। jagāma tarasā sarvair anyaiś ca sacivair vṛtaḥ ।। sarvaṃ provāca vṛddho asāv amātyaḥ sacivair vṛtaḥ ।। putro nāga iti khyāto buddhimān guṇasāgaraḥ ।।
tasmāc chastrair alaṃkārair vivāhaḥ syān mahāmate ।। tasmāc chastrair alaṃkārair vivāhas tv anumanyatām ।। mene vākyaṃ tathā satyam amātyaṃ bhūpatiṃ tadā ।। śastreṇa ca yathāśāstraṃ preṣayām āsa tāṃ punaḥ ।।
bahu dattvātha vijayo harṣeṇa mahatā yutaḥ ।। pratiṣṭhānam athābhyetya śūrasenāya tāṃ snuṣām ।। bhūṣaṇāni vicitrāṇi dāsyo vastrādikaṃ ca yat ।। vijayasya tu ye amātyā bhogavatyā sahāgatāḥ ।।
vijayāya yathā prītis tathā kṛtvā vyasarjayat ।। śvaśrūśvaśurayor nityaṃ śuśrūṣantī sumadhyamā ।। ekāntadeśe vijane gṛhe ratnasuśobhite ।। sa sarpo mātaraṃ prāha pitaraṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ ।।
tat putravacanaṃ śrutvā sarpamātedam abravīt ।। tava bhartā sarpa iti tataḥ sā kiṃ vadiṣyati ।। rahogatā uvācedaṃ vinītavad apūrvavat ।। na cākhyeyaṃ tvayā kvāpi sarpo na puruṣo dhruvam ।।
tasyās tad vacanaṃ śrutvā bhogavaty abravīd idam ।। kiṃ punar devajātis tu bhartā puṇyena labhyate ।। sarpāya sarpamātre ca rājñe caiva yathākramam ।। bhogavaty api tāṃ prāha uktapūrvāṃ punaḥ sakhīm ।।
kāntaṃ darśaya bhadraṃ te vṛthā yāti vayo mama ।। sugandhakusumākīrṇe śayane sā rahogatā ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭā vākyam avadat kāntam añjasā ।। dhanyāsmy anugṛhītāsmi yasyā me daivataṃ patiḥ ।।
khelayām āsa tanvaṅgī gītaiś caivāṅgasaṃgamaiḥ ।। smṛtvā sarvaṃ daivakṛtaṃ rātrau sarpo abravīt priyām ।। patir eva gatiḥ strīṇāṃ sarvadaiva viśeṣataḥ ।। śrutveti hṛṣṭas tām āha nāgaḥ prahasitānanaḥ ।।
tava prasādāc cārvaṅgi sarvasmṛtir abhūd iyam ।। maheśvarakare nāgaḥ śeṣaputro mahābalaḥ ।। umāvākyāj jahāsoccaiḥ śaṃbhuḥ prīto rahogataḥ ।। tatas tu kupitaḥ śaṃbhuḥ prādāc chāpaṃ mamedṛśam ।।
manuṣyayonau tvaṃ sarpo bhavitā jñānavān iti ।। tataś coktaṃ tena bhadre gautamyāṃ mama pūjanam ।। tadā viśāpo bhavitā bhogavatyāḥ prasādataḥ ।। tasmān nītvā gautamīṃ māṃ pūjāṃ kuru mayā saha ।।
sarveṣāṃ sarvadārtānāṃ śiva eva parā gatiḥ ।। tataḥ snātvā tu gautamyāṃ pūjāṃ cakre śivasya tu ।। śivalokaṃ tato jñātvā pitā prāha mahāmatiḥ ।। yāte mayi paraṃ dhāma tato yāhi śivaṃ puram ।।
kāmarūpam avāpyātha bhāryayā saha suvrataḥ ।। yāte pitari svarlokaṃ putrān sthāpya svake pade ।। tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ nāgatīrtham iti śrutam ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvakratuphalapradam ।।
ādhibhir mucyate jantus tattīrthasmaraṇād api ।। nāśaknuvaṃs tadā jetuṃ devā dānavasaṃgaram ।। astavaṃ vividhair vākyaiḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ śanaiḥ ।। tataś ca tuṣṭo bhagavān ādikartā trilocanaḥ ।।
dāsye ahaṃ yad abhīṣṭaṃ vo bruvantu surasattamāḥ ।। jahi śatrūn surān pāhi nāthavantas tvayā prabho ।। tadākariṣyan kim iva duḥkhārtāḥ sarvadehinaḥ ।। tatra tad yuddham abhavac chaṃkareṇa suradviṣām ।।
lalāṭād vyapataṃs tasya yudhyataḥ svedabindavaḥ ।। tāṃ mūrtim asurā dṛṣṭvā merupṛṣṭhād bhuvaṃ yayuḥ ।। itaś cetaś ca bhītās te adhāvan sarvāṃ mahīm imām ।। tathaiva yudhyataḥ śaṃbhoḥ patitāḥ svedabindavaḥ ।।
tatra tatra śivākārā mātaro jajñire tataḥ ।। tataḥ provāca bhagavān sarvaiḥ suragaṇair vṛtaḥ ।। anuprāptās tataḥ sarvāḥ śṛṇvantu mama bhāṣitam ।। bhavatyo apy anugacchantu rasātalam anu dviṣaḥ ।।
tān hatvā mātaraḥ sarvān devārīn atibhīṣaṇān ।। gatāś ca mātaro yāvad yāvac ca punar āgatāḥ ।। prasthānāt tatra mātṝṇāṃ surāṇāṃ ca pratiṣṭhiteḥ ।। mātṝṇāṃ yatra cotpattir mātṛtīrthaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।।
surās tābhyo varān procur loke pūjāṃ yathā śivaḥ ।। ity uktvāntardadhur devā āsaṃs tatraiva mātaraḥ ।। surāṇām api sevyāni kiṃ punar mānuṣādibhiḥ ।। sarvaṃ tad akṣayaṃ jñeyaṃ śivasya vacanaṃ yathā ।।
ākhyānaṃ mātṛtīrthānām āyuṣmān sa sukhī bhavet ।। brahmatīrtham iti khyātaṃ bhuktimuktipradaṃ nṛṇām ।। daityeṣu ca muniśreṣṭha tathā mātṛṣu tān anu ।। tad vaktraṃ devasainyeṣu mayi tiṣṭhaty uvāca ha ।।
āgacchantu surān sarvān bhakṣayiṣye kṣaṇād iti ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā vibudhāḥ sarve vitrastā viṣṇum abruvan ।। cakradhṛg vibudhān āha cchedmi cakreṇa vai śiraḥ ।। mantraṃ brūmo atra vibudhāḥ śrūyatāṃ sarvam eva hi ।।
mayā ca śaṃbhuḥ sarvaiś ca stutaḥ proktas tathaiva ca ।। lokānām upakārārthaṃ tathety āha surān prati ।। nikṛtya nakhaśastraiś ca kva sthāpyaṃ cety athābravīt ।। rasātalam atho yāsye udadhiś cāpy athābravīt ।।
tvayaivaitad brahmaśiro dhāryaṃ lokānukampayā ।। evaṃ vimṛśya someśo dadhāra kaśiras tadā ।। astuvañ jagatām īśaṃ praṇayād bhaktitaḥ surāḥ ।। tuṣṭuvur vibudheśānaṃ karma dṛṣṭvātidaivatam ।।
adyāpi brahmaṇo rūpaṃ caturmukham avasthitam ।। yatra sthitvā svayaṃ rudro lūnavān brahmaṇaḥ śiraḥ ।। devānāṃ ca svarūpeṇa sthito yasmāt tad uttamam ।। tatra snātvā raviṃ dṛṣṭvā punarjanma na vidyate ।।
kṣetre avimukte saṃsthāpya devatānāṃ hitaṃ kṛtam ।। kapālaṃ brahmaṇaḥ puṇyaṃ brahmahā pūtatāṃ vrajet ।। tatrāpi vṛttam ākhyāsye śṛṇu nārada bhaktitaḥ ।। samāptir naiva sattrasya saṃjātā vighnadoṣataḥ ।।
tato dhyānagato ahaṃ tān avocaṃ vīkṣya kāraṇam ।। tasmāt stuvantu te sarve ādidevaṃ vināyakam ।। astuvan bhaktito devā ādidevaṃ gaṇeśvaram ।। iti stutaḥ suragaṇair vighneśaḥ prāha tān punaḥ ।।
ito nirvighnatā sattre mattaḥ syād asurāriṇaḥ ।। devasattre nivṛtte tu gaṇeśaḥ prāha tān surān ।। teṣāṃ dāridryaduḥkhāni na bhaveyuḥ kadācana ।। teṣāṃ sarvāṇi kāryāṇi bhaveyur iti manyatām ।।
nivṛtte tu makhe tasmin surā jagmuḥ svam ālayam ।। sarvakāmapradaṃ puṃsāṃ sarvavighnavināśanam ।। tasya rūpaṃ pravakṣyāmi yan mayā paribhāṣitam ।। sarvanāgaiḥ parivṛto rasātalam athābhyagāt ।।
tair nirasto bhogipatir mām uvācātha vihvalaḥ ।। te me sthānaṃ na dāsyanti tasmāt tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। tatra stutvā mahādevaṃ lapsyase tvaṃ manoratham ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā tuṣṭāva tridaśeśvaram ।।
ādikartre namas tubhyaṃ namas trailokyarūpiṇe ।। somasūryāgnirūpāya jalarūpāya te namaḥ ।। jagannātha namas tubhyaṃ dehi me manasepsitam ।। vināśāya surārīṇāṃ daityadānavarakṣasām ।।
tataḥ proktaḥ śivenāsau śeṣaḥ śūlena bhogibhiḥ ।। nihatya nāgaḥ śūlena daityadānavarākṣasān ।। pathā yena samāyāto devaṃ draṣṭuṃ sa nāgarāṭ ।। tasmād bilatalād yātaṃ gāṅgaṃ vāry atipuṇyadam ।।
devasya purataś cāpi kuṇḍaṃ tatra suvistaram ।। soṣṇaṃ tad abhavad vāri gaṅgāyās tatra saṃgamaḥ ।। rasātalaṃ tato abhīṣṭaṃ śivāt prāpya talaṃ yayau ।। sarvakāmapradaṃ puṇyaṃ rogadāridryanāśanam ।।
śṛṇuyād vā paṭhed bhaktyā yo vāpi smarate tu tat ।। śatāni muniśārdūla sarvasaṃpatpradāyinām ।। mahānalo yatra devo vaḍavā yatra sā nadī ।। purāsan naimiṣāraṇye ṛṣayaḥ sattrakāriṇaḥ ।।
vartamāne sattrayāge mṛtyau śamitari sthite ।। vinā paśūn muniśreṣṭha martyaṃ cāmartyatāṃ gatam ।। mṛtyunopekṣite devā rākṣasān ūcire tadā ।। iti devavacaḥ śrutvā procus te rākṣasāḥ surān ।।
pravartate vinā hetuṃ na kopi kvāpi jātucit ।। bhaved eva tato yāntu ṛṣīṇāṃ sattram uttamam ।। jagmus tatra vināśāya devavākyād viśeṣataḥ ।। āgatā devavacanād rākṣasā yajñanāśinaḥ ।।
sarve tyaktvā svāśramaṃ taṃ śamitrā saha nārada ।। kratuniṣpattaye jagmur gautamīṃ prati satvarāḥ ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭās te tu tuṣṭuvus tridaśeśvaram ।। tam ahaṃ tridaśeśānaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāmi śaṃkaram ।।
mahāmūrtidharaṃ devaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāmi śaṃkaram ।। tataḥ provāca bhagavān mṛtyo kā prītir astu te ।। yajñam asmāṃś ca rakṣasva yāvat sattraṃ samāpyate ।। śamitrā mṛtyunā sattram ṛṣīṇāṃ pūrṇatāṃ yayau ।।
tān avocan munigaṇāḥ saṃkṣubdhā mṛtyunā saha ।। tasmād bhavadbhyaḥ pāpiṣṭhā rākṣasāḥ santu śatravaḥ ।। kṛtyāṃ ca vaḍavāṃ tatra devāś ca ṛṣayo amalāḥ ।। abhiṣekodakaṃ yat tu sā nadī vaḍavābhavat ।।
tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ vaḍavāsaṃgamaṃ viduḥ ।। ubhayos tīrayos tatra smaraṇād aghaghātinām ।। tasya prabhāvaṃ vakṣyāmi yatra jñāneśvaraḥ śivaḥ ।। sa gatvā pitaraṃ prāha vinayena praṇamya ca ।।
brahmajñānaṃ kathaṃ me syāt kaṃ pṛcchāmi kva yāmi ca ।। tac chrutvātriḥ putravākyaṃ dhyātvā vacanam abravīt ।। sa tu prīto yadaiva syāt tadā jñānam avāpsyasi ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā bhaktyā tuṣṭāva śaṃkaram ।।
varado asmīti taṃ prāha yoginaṃ viśvakṛd bhavaḥ ।। tīrthasyāpi ca māhātmyaṃ varo ayaṃ tridaśārcita ।। tatra snānena dānena muktiḥ syād iha nārada ।। uttare mandatīrthaṃ tu tatra vyuṣṭim itaḥ śṛṇu ।।
devais tu preritaḥ pūrvaṃ vindhyasya prārthanaṃ prati ।। tam āgatya nagaśreṣṭhaṃ bahuvṛkṣasamākulam ।। atyunnataṃ nagaṃ dhīro lopāmudrāpatir muniḥ ।। idam āha muniśreṣṭho devakāryārthasiddhaye ।।
tīrthayātrāṃ karomīti dakṣiṇāśāṃ vrajāmy aham ।। yāvad āgamanaṃ me syāt sthātavyaṃ tāvad eva hi ।। ākrāman dakṣiṇām āśāṃ tair vṛto munibhir muniḥ ।। yāvat saṃvatsaraṃ sattram akarod ṛṣibhir vṛtaḥ ।।
aśvatthaḥ pippalaś ceti vikhyātau tridaśālaye ।। tāv ubhāv antaraṃ prepsū yajñavidhvaṃsanāya tu ।। aśvattho vṛkṣarūpeṇa pippalo brāhmaṇākṛtiḥ ।। ālabhante ca ye aśvatthaṃ tāṃs tān aśnāty asau taruḥ ।।
tasmād adyāpi vipreṣu sāmago atīva niṣkṛpaḥ ।। iti buddhvā mahāprājñā dakṣiṇaṃ tīram āśritam ।। gatvā munigaṇāḥ sarve rakṣaḥkarma nyavedayan ।। rākṣasau hanmy apūrṇe tu tapasy akṣama eva hi ।।
ity ukto brāhmaṇaiḥ sauriḥ kṛtam ity āha tān api ।। rākṣasaṃ brāhmaṇo bhūtvā pradakṣiṇam athākarot ।। nityavad rākṣasaḥ pāpo bhakṣayām āsa māyayā ।। dṛṣṭaḥ sa rākṣasaḥ pāpo mandena ravisūnunā ।।
aśvatthaṃ bhasmasāt kṛtvā anyaṃ brāhmaṇarūpiṇam ।। adhīyāno vipra iva śiṣyarūpo vinītavat ।। sa bhakṣitaḥ pūrvavac ca kukṣāv antrāṇy avaikṣata ।। ubhau hatvā bhānusutaḥ kiṃ kṛtyaṃ me vadantv atha ।।
tataḥ prasannā hy abhavann ṛṣayo agastyapūrvakāḥ ।। sa prīto brāhmaṇān āha śaniḥ sūryasuto balī ।। teṣāṃ sarvāṇi kāryāṇi syuḥ pīḍā madbhavā na ca ।। teṣāṃ sarvāṇi kāryāṇi bhaveyur aparo varaḥ ।।
ālabhante ca teṣāṃ vai grahapīḍā vyapohatu ।। tīrthaṃ śanaiścaraṃ tatra tatrāgastyaṃ ca sāttrikam ।। teṣu snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sattrayāgaphalapradam ।। tatra snānena dānena somapānaphalaṃ labhet ।।
mamāpi mātaro devyaḥ pūrvāsāṃ pūrvavattarāḥ ।। ābhir eva dhṛtaṃ sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।। atrauṣadhyo jagadvandyā mām ūcur anahaṃkṛtāḥ ।। asmākaṃ tvaṃ patiṃ dehi rājānaṃ surasattama ।।
patiṃ prāpsyatha sarvāś ca rājānaṃ prītivardhanam ।। gantavyaṃ kva punaś coktā gautamīṃ yāntu mātaraḥ ।। tāś ca gatvā muniśreṣṭha tuṣṭuvur gautamīṃ nadīm ।। ity evaṃ stuvatām īśā kiṃ dadāmīty avocata ।।
patiṃ dehi jaganmātā rājānam atitejasam ।। tadovāca nadī gaṅgā oṣadhīs tā idaṃ vacaḥ ।। tādṛśaṃ cāmṛtātmānaṃ patiṃ somaṃ dadāmi vaḥ ।। oṣadhyaś cāpi tad vākyaṃ tato jagmuḥ svam ālayam ।।
somaṃ samastasaṃtāpa- pāpasaṃghanivārakam ।। tatra snānena dānena pitaraḥ svargam āpnuyuḥ ।। dīrgham āyur avāpnoti sa putrī dhanavān bhavet ।। subhikṣaṃ kṣemadaṃ puṃsāṃ sarvāpadvinivāraṇam ।।
ūcuḥ sarvasya lokasya gaṅgāyāś cepsitaṃ vacaḥ ।। bhūmiṃ sasyavatīṃ kaścin mātaraṃ mātṛsaṃmitām ।। bhūmiṃ sasyavatīṃ gāś ca oṣadhīś ca mudānvitaḥ ।। sarvaṃ tad akṣayaṃ vidyāt sarvakāmān avāpnuyāt ।।
iti jñātvā brahmavida oṣadhīr yaḥ pradāsyati ।। tā eva somarājanyāḥ prītāḥ procuḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। tvam uttamaś cauṣadhīśa tvadadhīnaṃ carācaram ।। yo asmān dadāti viprebhyas taṃ rājan pārayāmasi ।।
yo asmān dadāti viprebhyas taṃ rājan pārayāmasi ।। upāstir asti sāsmākaṃ taṃ rājan pārayāmasi ।। yo asmān dadāti viprebhyas taṃ rājan pārayāmasi ।। tadgarīyaś ca yo dadyāt taṃ rājan pārayāmasi ।।
