paṭhate bhaktim āpannas taṃ rājan pārayāmasi ।। gaṅgātīre cauṣadhībhir dhānyatīrthaṃ tad ucyate ।। amṛtaṃ vedagāthaṃ ca mātṛtīrthaṃ tathaiva ca ।। annadānaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt tad ānantyāya kalpate ।।
sarvapāpanihantṝṇāṃ sarvasaṃpadvivardhanam ।। tatra yad vṛttam ākhyāsye yat purāṇavido viduḥ ।। tasya svasā revatīti kurūpā vikṛtasvarā ।। cintayā parayā yukto gaṅgāyā dakṣiṇe taṭe ।।
na kaścit pratigṛhṇāti dātavyā ca svasā tathā ।। maraṇaṃ jīvato apy asya prāṇinas tu pade pade ।। draṣṭuṃ munivaraḥ prāyād bharadvājaṃ yatavratam ।। nāmnā kaṭha iti khyāto bharadvājaṃ nanāma saḥ ।।
tasyāgamanakāryaṃ ca papraccha purataḥ sthitaḥ ।। tathā ca darśanākāṅkṣī yad yuktaṃ tad vidhīyatām ।। purāṇaṃ smṛtayo vedā dharmasthānāny anekaśaḥ ।। abhimānī śrutadharaḥ śiṣyaḥ puṇyair avāpyate ।।
śuśrūṣaṇarataṃ bhaktaṃ kulīnaṃ satyavādinam ।। prāptavidyaḥ kaṭhaḥ prīto bharadvājam athābravīt ।। vadasva durlabhaṃ vāpi guro tubhyaṃ namo astu te ।। na prayacchanti nirayaṃ te yānty ācandratārakam ।।
asyāṃ prītyā vartitavyaṃ yāceyaṃ dakṣiṇām imām ।। guruś ca pitṛvac ca syāt saṃbandho atra kathaṃ bhavet ।। sarvaṃ smṛtvā kaṭhādya tvaṃ revatīṃ bhara tanmanāḥ ।। revatīṃ vidhivad dattāṃ tāṃ samīkṣya kaṭhas tv atha ।।
revatyā rūpasaṃpattyai śivaprītyai ca revatī ।। abhiṣekodakaṃ tatra revatyā yad viniḥsṛtam ।। revatīti samākhyātā rūpasaubhāgyadāyinī ।। puṇyarūpatvasaṃsiddhyai vidarbhā tad abhūn nadī ।।
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। snānaṃ karoty asau yāti bhuktiṃ muktiṃ ca tatkṣaṇāt ।। sarvapāpakṣayakaraṃ sarvasiddhipradāyakam ।। tatra snātvā naro ajñānāt tathāpi śubham āpnuyāt ।।
svayaṃ saṃsthīyate yatra cakriṇā ca pinākinā ।। iṣṭvā bahuvidhair yajñair aśvamedhapuraḥsaraiḥ ।। vijñāya bhogavaiṣamyaṃ paraṃ vairāgyam āśritaḥ ।। śivaviṣṇvor gṛhe vāpi viśeṣāt puṇyasaṃgame ।।
dhanvantarir iti jñātvā tatra tepe tapo mahat ।। tapaś cakāra vipulaṃ gaṅgāsāgarasaṃgame ।। sahasram ekaṃ varṣāṇāṃ samudraṃ prāviśad bhayāt ।। virāgaṃ ca gate rājñi tataḥ prāyād athārṇavāt ।।
gaṅgātīraṃ samāśritya rājā dhanvantarir yataḥ ।। taṃ ripuṃ nāśayāmīti tamaḥ prāyād athārṇavāt ।। taṃ ripuṃ nāśayāmīti tamaḥ prāyād athārṇavāt ।। nṛtyagītavatī subhrūr hasantī cārudarśanā ।।
śāntām anuvratāṃ bhaktāṃ kṛpayā cābravīn nṛpaḥ ।। kaṃ dṛṣṭvā harṣasīva tvaṃ vada kalyāṇi pṛcchate ।। pramadā cāpi tadvākyaṃ śrutvā rājānam abravīt ।। aham indrasya yā lakṣmīs tvāṃ dṛṣṭvā kāmasaṃbhṛtam ।।
agaṇyapuṇyavirahād ahaṃ sarvasya durlabhā ।। tām eva manasā dhyāyaṃs tanniṣṭhas tatparāyaṇaḥ ।। antardhānaṃ gato brahman nāśayitvā tapo bṛhat ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā vihvalībhūtaṃ tapobhraṣṭaṃ yathā mṛtam ।।
tava śatrus tamo nāma kṛtvā tāṃ tapasaś cyutim ।। ānandayanti pramadās tāpayanti ca mānavam ।। tataḥ kṛtāñjalī rājā mām āha vigatabhramaḥ ।। kiṃ karomi kathaṃ brahmaṃs tapasaḥ pāram āpnuyām ।।
stuhi sarvaprayatnena tataḥ siddhim avāpsyasi ।। sarvārthasiddhidaḥ puṃsāṃ nānyo asti bhuvanatraye ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā viṣṇuṃ tuṣṭāva bhaktitaḥ ।। jaya gopāla lakṣmīśa jaya kṛṣṇa jaganmaya ।।
jaya sarvaga govinda jaya viśvakṛte namaḥ ।। jayeśa sadasat tvaṃ vai jaya mādhava dharmiṇe ।। jaya puṣṭida puṣṭīśa jaya kalyāṇadāyine ।। jaya karmada karma tvaṃ jaya pītāmbaracchada ।।
jaya sattvādhināthāya jaya vedavide namaḥ ।। jaya muktida muktis tvaṃ jaya bhuktida keśava ।। jaya vatsala bhaktānāṃ jaya cakradhṛte namaḥ ।। jaya dharmada dharmas tvaṃ jaya saṃsārapāraga ।।
jaya śaktida śaktis tvaṃ jaya jaitravaraprada ।। jaya dānada dānaṃ tvaṃ jaya kaiṭabhasūdana ।। jaya saukhyada saukhyātmañ jaya pāvanapāvana ।। jaya pānada pānas tvaṃ jaya jyotiḥsvarūpiṇe ।।
jaya sarvasya jagato dātṛmūrte namo astu te ।। vareṇa cchandayām āsa sarvakāmasamṛddhidaḥ ।। varadānāya deveśaṃ govindaṃ saṃsthitaṃ puraḥ ।। tac ca dattaṃ tvayā viṣṇo prāpto asmi kṛtakṛtyatām ।।
tathaiva tridaśeśatvam avāpa nṛpatiḥ kramāt ।। triḥkṛtvo nāśam agamat sahasrākṣaḥ svakāt padāt ।। ahalyāyāṃ ca gamanād yena kena ca hetunā ।। tataḥ surapatiḥ prāha vācaspatim idaṃ vacaḥ ।।
madhye madhye padabhraṃśād varaṃ niḥśrīkatā nṛṇām ।। rahasyaṃ sarvabhāvānāṃ jñātuṃ nānyaḥ pragalbhate ।। sa tu jānāti yad bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyac cāpi vartanam ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā mām ūcatur idaṃ vacaḥ ।।
rājyāt prabhraśyate nātha saṃśayaṃ chettum arhasi ।। khaṇḍadharmākhyadoṣeṇa tena rājyapadāc cyutaḥ ।। yathāvaddakṣiṇādānād asaddravyapradānataḥ ।। yat khaṇḍatvaṃ svadharmasya dehinām upajāyate ।।
kṛto api dharmo aniṣṭāya jāyate kṣubdhacetasā ।। asaṃpūrṇe svadharme hi kim aniṣṭaṃ na jāyate ।। āyuṣas tu sutaḥ śrīmān dhanvantarir udāradhīḥ ।। pūrvajanmasu vṛttāntam ityādi parikīrtitam ।।
tac chrutvā vismitau cobhau mām eva punar ūcatuḥ ।। taddoṣapratibandhas tu kena syāt surasattama ।। kāraṇaṃ sarvasiddhīnāṃ duḥkhasaṃsāratāraṇam ।। gatvā tu gautamīṃ devīṃ stūyetāṃ hariśaṃkarau ।।
snātau kṛtakṣaṇau cobhau devau tuṣṭuvatur mudā ।। narasiṃhāya devāya vāmanāya namo namaḥ ।। namo astu buddharūpāya rāmarūpāya kalkine ।। varuṇendrasvarūpāya yamarūpāya te namaḥ ।।
bibhratsarasvatīṃ vaktre sarvajño asi namo astu te ।। tvām eva sukhinaṃ prāpya bahavaḥ sukhino abhavan ।। yāvan na yānti śaraṇaṃ hare tvāṃ karuṇārṇavam ।। tataḥ prītau hariharāv ūcatus tridaśeśvarau ।।
vriyatāṃ yan manobhīṣṭaṃ yad varaṃ cātidurlabham ।। jāyate bhraśyate caiva tat pāpam upaśāmyatām ।। suprītau yadi deveśau sarvaṃ syān niścalaṃ sadā ।। paraṃ prasādam āpannau tāv ālokya smitānanau ।।
śaraṇyau sarvalokānāṃ bhuktimuktipradāv ubhau ।। tasyām anena mantreṇa kurutāṃ snānam ādarāt ।। karotu saṃsmarann āvāṃ saṃpadāṃ sthairyasiddhaye ।। tat sarvaṃ pūrṇatām etu godāvari namo astu te ।।
pūrvajanmakṛtād doṣāt sa muktaḥ puṇyavān bhavet ।। mahābhiṣekam indrasya cakāra dyusadāṃ guruḥ ।। tayā ca saṃgamaḥ puṇyo gaṅgāyāḥ śubhadas tv asau ।। trilokasaṃmitāṃ śakro bhūmiṃ lebhe jagatpateḥ ।।
trilokasaṃmitā labdhā tena gaur vajradhāriṇā ।। trailokyarājyaṃ yat prāptaṃ hariṇā ca harer mune ।। bṛhaspatir devagurur yatrāstauṣīn maheśvaram ।। siddheśvaras tatra devo liṅgaṃ tu tridaśārcitam ।।
maṅgalāsaṃgamaṃ caiva pūrṇatīrthaṃ tataḥ param ।। yatra siddheśvaro devo viṣṇur govinda eva ca ।। sarvaṃ tad akṣayaṃ vidyāt pitṝṇām ativallabham ।। tasya tīrthasya māhātmyaṃ bhraṣṭarājyapradāyakam ।।
ubhayor muniśārdūla sarvasiddhipradāyinām ।। niṣphalaṃ tasya janmādi yo na seveta tan naraḥ ।। tasya śravaṇamātreṇa sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। balavān matimāñ śūro yathā śakraḥ puraṃdaraḥ ।।
tasya tisro mahiṣyaḥ syū rājño daśarathasya hi ।। etāḥ kulīnāḥ subhagā rūpalakṣaṇasaṃyutāḥ ।। vasiṣṭhe brahmavicchreṣṭhe purodhasi viśeṣataḥ ।। brahmakṣatraviśāṃ nityaṃ śūdrāṇāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।
tasmiñ śāsati rājendra ikṣvākūṇāṃ kulodvahe ।। kvāpi tatra jayaṃ prāpur devāḥ kvāpi tathetare ।। abhūn nārada tatrāham avadaṃ daityadānavān ।। punaś ca saṃgaras teṣāṃ babhūva sumahān mithaḥ ।।
tāv ūcatur ubhau devān asurān daityadānavān ।। tathety āhur yayuḥ sarve tapase niyatavratāḥ ।। devānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca saṃgaro abhūt sudāruṇaḥ ।। saṃyuge vartamāne tu vāg uvācāśarīriṇī ।।
yeṣāṃ daśaratho rājā te jetāro na cetare ।। tatra vāyus tvaran prāpto rājānam avadat tadā ।। yatra rājā daśaratho jayas tatreti viśrutam ।। tasmāt tvaṃ devapakṣe syā bhaveyur jayinaḥ surāḥ ।।
āgamyate mayā satyaṃ gaccha vāyo yathāsukham ।। te apy ūcur bhagavann asmat- sāhāyyaṃ kartum arhasi ।। tasmāt tvaṃ vai daityapateḥ sāhāyyaṃ kartum arhasi ।। pratijñātaṃ mayā tac ca yāntu daityāś ca dānavāḥ ।।
yuddhaṃ cakre tathā daityair dānavaiḥ saha rākṣasaiḥ ।। vividhur niśitair bāṇair athākṣaṃ nṛpates tathā ।। rājāntike sthitā subhrūḥ kaikeyyājñāyi nārada ।। bhagnam akṣaṃ samālakṣya cakre hastaṃ tadā svakam ।।
rathena rathināṃ śreṣṭhas tayā dattakareṇa ca ।। tato devair anujñātas tv ayodhyāṃ punar abhyagāt ।। kaikeyyāḥ karma tad dṛṣṭvā vismayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ ।। anumānya nṛpaproktaṃ kaikeyī vākyam abravīt ।।
tvayi tiṣṭhantu rājendra tvayā dattā varā amī ।। rathena vijayī rājā yayau svanagaraṃ sukhī ।। sa kadācid daśaratho mṛgayāśīlibhir vṛtaḥ ।। saptavyasanahīnena bhavitavyaṃ tu bhūbhujā ।।
gartaṃ praviśya pānārtham āgatān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ।। gartaṃ praviṣṭe nṛpatau tasminn eva nagottame ।। tasya bhāryā tathābhūtā tāv abrūtāṃ tadā sutam ।। vṛddhānāṃ jīvitaṃ kṛtsnaṃ bālas tvam asi putraka ।।
jarājarjaradehānāṃ dhig dhik putraka jīvitam ।। yāvad ājñāpratihatā tīrthādāv anyathā mṛtiḥ ।। putraḥ provāca tad duḥkhaṃ girā madhurayā haran ।। na haraty ātmajaḥ pitror yaś caritrair manorujam ।।
tena kiṃ tanujeneha kulodvegavidhāyinā ।। taruskandhe samāropya vṛddhau ca pitarau tadā ।। sa ṛṣir na tu rājānaṃ jānāti nṛpatir dvijam ।। satvaraṃ kalaśe nyubje vāri gṛhṇantam āśugaiḥ ।।
vanadvipo api bhūpānām avadhyas tad vidann api ।। sa viddho marmadeśe tu duḥkhito vākyam abravīt ।। maitro brāhmaṇa ity ukto nāparādho asti kaścana ।। niśceṣṭaś ca nirutsāho śanais taṃ deśam abhyagāt ।।
asāv apy abhavat tatra saśalya iva mūrcchitaḥ ।। ātmānam ātmanā kṛtvā sthiraṃ rājābravīd idam ।। vada pāpakṛte mahyaṃ vada me niṣkṛtiṃ parām ।। na spraṣṭavyo mahābuddhe draṣṭavyo na kadācana ।।
tad rājavacanaṃ śrutvā muniputro abravīd vacaḥ ।। svacchandavṛttitājñāne viddhi pākaṃ ca karmaṇām ।। tayoḥ śuśrūṣakaḥ kaḥ syād andhayor ekaputrayoḥ ।। mamābhāgyam aho kīdṛk pitṛśuśrūṣaṇe kṣatiḥ ।।
tathāpi gaccha tatra tvaṃ gṛhītakalaśas tvaran ।। tābhyāṃ dehy udapānaṃ tvaṃ yathā tau na mariṣyataḥ ।। visṛjya saśaraṃ cāpam ādāya kalaśaṃ nṛpaḥ ।। vṛddhau cāpi tadā rātrau tāv anyonyaṃ samūcatuḥ ।।
na prāptaś cāvayor yaṣṭiḥ kiṃ kurmaḥ kā gatir bhavet ।। yaḥ pitror anyathā vākyaṃ na karoty api ninditaḥ ।। śīghraṃ na yānti yat prāṇās tadekāyattajīvayoḥ ।। tadā daśaratho rājā śanais taṃ deśam abhyagāt ।।
pādasaṃcāraśabdena menāte sutam āgatam ।। na brūṣe kiṃtu ruṣṭo asi vṛddhayor andhayoḥ sutaḥ ।। sa bhīta iva rājendras tāv uvācātha nārada ।। nāyaṃ vaktā suto asmākaṃ ko bhavāṃs tat purā vada ।।
paścāt pibāvaḥ pānīyaṃ tato rājābravīc ca tau ।। tatra tiṣṭhati vāṃ putro yatra vārisamāśrayaḥ ।। ācacakṣe tato rājā sarvam eva yathātatham ।। brahmaghnasparśanaṃ pāpaṃ na kadācid vinaśyati ।।
yatrāsau patitaḥ putras taṃ spṛṣṭvā tau vilepatuḥ ।। tvaṃ cāpi pāpa putrasya viyogān mṛtyum āpsyasi ।। agninā yojayām āsa vṛddhau ca ṛṣiputrakam ।। vasiṣṭhāya ca tat sarvaṃ nyavedayad aśeṣataḥ ।।
vasiṣṭho api dvijaśreṣṭhaiḥ saṃmantryāha ca niṣkṛtim ।। etān anyān samāhūya hayamedhāya yatnataḥ ।। yajasva hayamedhaiś ca bahubhir bahudakṣiṇaiḥ ।। etasminn antare tatra vāg uvācāśarīriṇī ।।
jyeṣṭhaputraprasādena rājāpāpo bhaviṣyati ।। devānāṃ kāryasiddhyarthaṃ sutā āsan suropamāḥ ।। śatrughnaś cāpi kaikeyyāṃ bharato matimattaraḥ ।। taṃ rājānam ṛṣiḥ prāpya viśvāmitraḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।
yajñasaṃrakṣaṇārthāya jñātatanmahimā muniḥ ।। ciraprāptasuto vṛddho rājā naivety abhāṣata ।। jātāv ānandasaṃdoha- dāyakau mama bālakau ।। saśarīram idaṃ rājyaṃ dāsye naiva sutāv imau ।।
vasiṣṭhena tadā prokto rājā daśarathas tv iti ।। raghavaḥ prārthanābhaṅgaṃ na rājan kvāpi śikṣitāḥ ।। rāmaṃ ca lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva kathaṃcid avadan nṛpaḥ ।। viśvāmitrasya brahmarṣeḥ kurutāṃ yajñarakṣaṇam ।।
putrau samarpayām āsa viśvāmitrasya śāstrakṛt ।। jagmatū rakṣaṇārthāya viśvāmitreṇa tau mudā ।। māheśvarīṃ mahāvidyāṃ dhanurvidyāpuraḥsarām ।। aśvavidyāṃ gadāvidyāṃ mantrāhvānavisarjane ।।
vanaukasāṃ hitārthāya jaghnatus tāṭakāṃ vane ।। yajñavidhvaṃsanāyātāñ jaghnatus tatra rākṣasān ।। tato mahāmakhe vṛtte viśvāmitro munīśvaraḥ ।। citrām adarśayat tatra rājamadhye nṛpātmajaḥ ।।
tatprīto janakaḥ prādāt sītāṃ lakṣmīm ayonijām ।। śatrughnabharatādīnāṃ vasiṣṭhādimate sthitaḥ ।। tato bahutithe kāle rājyaṃ tasya prayacchati ।। mantharātmakadurdaiva- preritā matsarākulā ।।
bharatasya ca tad rājyaṃ rājā naiva ca dattavān ।। viveśa sītayā sārdhaṃ tathā saumitriṇā saha ।। tasmin vinirgate rāme vanavāsāya dīkṣite ।। taṃ rāmaṃ cāpi saumitriṃ sītāṃ ca guṇaśālinīm ।।
tadā daśaratho rājā prāṇāṃs tatyāja duḥkhitaḥ ।। tasmai rājñe mahāprājña yāvat sthāvarajaṅgame ।। narakāṇy atha ghorāṇi bhīṣaṇāni bahūni ca ।। pacyate chidyate rājā piṣyate cūrṇyate tathā ।।
evamādiṣu ghoreṣu narakeṣu sa pacyate ।। tatraiva trīṇi varṣāṇi vyatītāni mahāmate ।। vikhyātaṃ triṣu lokeṣu deśānāṃ tad dhi puṇyadam ।। tadbhayād ṛṣibhis tyaktaṃ hatvā daityāṃs tu rākṣasān ।।
tatredaṃ vṛttam ākhyāsye śṛṇu nārada yatnataḥ ।। gautamīṃ samanuprāpto rājāpi narake sthitaḥ ।। gautamīm abhito yāti pitaraṃ tasya dhīmataḥ ।। uttīrya gautamīṃ yāti yāvad yojanapañcakam ।।
yad etan madvacaḥ puṇyaṃ na kuryur yadi dūtakāḥ ।। yā kāpy uktā parā śaktiḥ śivasya samavāyinī ।। haribrahmamaheśānāṃ mānyā vandyā ca saiva yat ।। pāpino apy ātmajaḥ kaścid yaś ca gaṅgām anusmaret ।।
kiṃ punas tādṛśaḥ putro gautamīnikaṭe sthitaḥ ।। dakṣiṇāśāpater vākyaṃ niśamya yamakiṃkarāḥ ।। uttārya ghoranarakād vacanaṃ cedam abruvan ।। iha cāmutra viśrāntiḥ suputraḥ kena labhyate ।।
sa viśrāntaḥ śanai rājā kiṃkarān vākyam abravīt ।। kathaṃ tv ākarṣitaḥ śīghraṃ tan me vaktum ihārhatha ।। tatra kaścic chāntamanā rājānam idam abravīt ।। prakāśyate tad api te sāmarthyaṃ putratīrthayoḥ ।।
tasmāt tvaṃ narakād ghorād ākṛṣṭo asi narottama ।। tatas tvaṃ sarvapāpebhyo mukto yāsi triviṣṭapam ।। bhavanta eva śaraṇam anujñāṃ dātum arhatha ।। ājñāṃ ca pradadus tasmai rājā prāgāt sutau prati ।।
nirīkṣya svaṃ lajjamānaḥ kṛtaṃ karma ca saṃsmaran ।। gautamyās taṭam āśritya rāmo lakṣmaṇa eva ca ।। naiva tatrābhavad bhojyaṃ bhakṣyaṃ vā gautamītaṭe ।। tad dṛṣṭvā duḥkhito bhrātā lakṣmaṇo rāmam abravīt ।।
nāsti bhojyam athāsmākaṃ gaṅgātīranivāsinām ।। pṛthivyām annapūrṇāyāṃ vayam annābhilāṣiṇaḥ ।। avajñayā mahīdevāṃs tarpayanty arcayanti na ।। tataḥ svasamaye devo vidhāsyaty aśanaṃ tu nau ।।
śanair daśaratho rājā taṃ deśam upajagmivān ।। dhanur ākṛṣya kopena rakṣas tvaṃ dānavo athavā ।। rāmo dāśarathī rājā dharmabhāk paśya vartate ।। trailokyarakṣādakṣo asau vartate yatra rāghavaḥ ।।
yadi praviśase pāpa tato vadham avāpsyasi ।। muhur antar vinidhyāyan gatiṃ duṣkṛtakarmaṇaḥ ।। chinnaṃ paśyata me dehaṃ narakeṣu ca pātitam ।। bhūmau praṇemus te sarve vacanaṃ caitad abruvan ।।
kasyedaṃ karmaṇas tāta phalaṃ nṛpatisattama ।। sa ca prāha yathāvṛttaṃ brahmahatyātrayaṃ tathā ।। niṣkṛtir brahmahantṝṇāṃ putrau kvāpi na vidyate ।। rājānaṃ vanavāsaṃ ca mātaraṃ pitaraṃ tathā ।।
visaṃjñaṃ nṛpatiṃ dṛṣṭvā sītā vākyam athābravīt ।। cintayanti pratīkāraṃ daivyam apy atha mānuṣam ।। vyāmoham āpnuvantīha na kadācid vicakṣaṇāḥ ।। dehi hatyāṃ prathamato yā jātā hy atibhīṣaṇā ।।
anāgā yo hato vipras tatpāpasyātra niṣkṛtim ।। dvitīyāṃ lakṣmaṇo hatyāṃ gṛhṇātu tv aparāṃ bhavān ।। tatheti cāhatur ubhau tato daśaratho abravīt ।। bhāryā rāmasya kiṃ citraṃ yad yuktam anubhāṣase ।।
gautamyāṃ snānadānena piṇḍanirvapaṇena ca ।। tvayā janakasaṃbhūte svakulocitam īritam ।। godāvaryāḥ prasādena kiṃ nāmāsty atra durlabham ।। naivāpaśyad bhakṣyabhojyaṃ tato lakṣmaṇam abravīt ।।
santi teṣāṃ ca piṇyākam ānītaṃ tatkṣaṇād iva ।। manaḥ kurvaṃs tato rāmo mando abhūd duḥkhitas tadā ।। rājyabhraṣṭo vanaṃ prāptaḥ kiṃ vai niṣkiṃcano bhavān ।। vittaśāṭhyena yo dharmaṃ karoti sa tu pātakī ।।
yadannaḥ puruṣo rājaṃs tadannās tasya devatāḥ ।। śavaṃ ca patitaṃ yatra śavatīrtham anuttamam ।। tatrāgacchaṃl lokapālā rudrādityās tathāśvinau ।। vimānavaram ārūḍhaḥ stūyamānaś ca kiṃnaraiḥ ।।
tam adṛṣṭvā svapitaraṃ devān dṛṣṭvā vimāninaḥ ।। iti divyābhavad vāṇī rāmaṃ saṃbodhya sītayā ।। vṛtaṃ paśya surais tāta devā apy ūcire ca tam ।। nānānirayasaṃghātāt pūrvajān uddharet tu yaḥ ।।
enaṃ paśya mahābāho muktapāpaṃ raviprabham ।। niṣkiṃcano api sukṛtī dṛśyate candramaulivat ।। dṛṣṭvābravīt sutaṃ rājā āśīrbhir abhinandya ca ।। dhanyaḥ sa putro loke asmin pitṝṇāṃ yas tu tārakaḥ ।।
tatas tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rāmas tān abravīt surān ।। gurau pitari me devāḥ kiṃ kṛtyam avaśiṣyate ।। na śivena samo devo na tāreṇa samo manuḥ ।। gacchantu sarve svasthānaṃ tvaṃ ca gaccha yathāsukham ।।
tad dṛṣṭvā gaṅgāmāhātmyaṃ vismito vākyam abravīt ।। vayaṃ dhanyā yato gaṅgā dṛṣṭāsmābhis tripāvanī ।। taṃ ṣoḍaśabhir īśānam upacāraiḥ prayatnataḥ ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā rāmas tuṣṭāva śaṃkaram ।।
varān vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te rāmaḥ prāha vṛṣadhvajam ।। teṣāṃ sarvāṇi kāryāṇi siddhiṃ yāntu maheśvara ।। teṣāṃ piṇḍādidānena pūtā yāntu triviṣṭapam ।। atra tu snānamātreṇa tat sadyo nāśam āpnuyāt ।।
sarvaṃ tad akṣayaṃ śaṃbho dātṝṇāṃ phalakṛd bhavet ।। gate tasmin suraśreṣṭhe rāmo apy anucaraiḥ saha ।। tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ rāmatīrtham udāhṛtam ।। tad bāṇatīrtham abhavat sarvāpadvinivāraṇam ।।
tat tīrthaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ jātaṃ tathā sītāsamudbhavam ।। yad aṅghrisaṃgād abhavad gaṅgā trailokyapāvanī ।। tad rāmatīrthasadṛśaṃ tīrthaṃ kvāpi na vidyate ।। sarvān kāmān avāpnoti yanmahimnaḥ śruter api ।।
adites tu sutā jyeṣṭhāḥ sarvabhāvena nārada ।। sādhvy etat sarvabhāvena praśrayāvanatā satī ।। evaṃ bruvāṇāṃ ca ditiṃ danuḥ provāca nārada ।। tuṣṭo yadi bhaved bhartā tataḥ kāmān avāpsyasi ।।
ditiṃ provāca bhagavān kaśyapo atha prajāpatiḥ ।। kiṃ dadāmi vadābhīṣṭaṃ dite varaya suvrate ।। jetāraṃ sarvalokānāṃ sarvalokanamaskṛtam ।। taṃ vareyaṃ surapitar ity āha vinayānvitā ।।
niṣpāpatāyāṃ jātāyāṃ sidhyanti hi manorathāḥ ।। upadiṣṭaṃ vrataṃ cakre bhartrādiṣṭaṃ yathāvidhi ।। katham āsādayiṣyanti prāṇino atra manorathān ।। punaḥ kāntām athovāca kaśyapas tāṃ ditiṃ rahaḥ ।।
yathāvihitakarmāṅga- avajñayā tac chucismite ।। na svaptavyaṃ na gantavyaṃ muktakeśī ca no bhava ।। saṃdhyākāle na kartavyaṃ bhūtasaṃghasamākule ।। gṛhāntadeśe saṃdhyāsu na sthātavyaṃ kadācana ।।
naivātikramaṇīyāni divā rātrau sadā priye ।। vaktavyaṃ nānṛtaṃ kiṃcin nānyagehāṭanaṃ tathā ।। tatas te bhavitā putras trailokyaiśvaryabhājanam ।। gataś ca kaśyapo brahmann itaś cetaḥ surān prati ।।
etat sarvaṃ mayo daityo māyayā vetti tattvataḥ ।। mayo gatvā rahaḥ prāha indraṃ sa vinayānvitaḥ ।। tasya vīryaṃ ca vividhaṃ prītyendrāya nyavedayat ।। arjitaṃ sukṛtaṃ nānā- vidhaṃ cet tad avāpyate ।।
bhrātṛhantrā kathaṃ maitryaṃ mayasyāsīt sureśvara ।। indreṇa vairam abhavad bhīṣaṇaṃ lomaharṣaṇam ।। dṛṣṭvā daityapatiḥ śūro namuciḥ pṛṣṭhato anvagāt ।। airāvataṃ gajaṃ tyaktvā indraḥ phenam athāviśat ।।
namucir nāśam agamat tasya bhrātā mayo anujaḥ ।। māyāṃ ca vividhām āpa devānām atibhīṣaṇām ।। dānaśauṇḍaḥ priyālāpī tadābhavad asau mayaḥ ।। dātāraṃ ca tadārthibhyaḥ stūyamānaṃ ca bandibhiḥ ।।
śacībhartā mayaṃ daityaṃ provācedaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।। tvāṃ śrutvā dātṛtilakam āgato ahaṃ dvijottamaḥ ।। vicārayanti kṛtino bahv alpaṃ vā puro arthini ।। indraṃ mayaḥ punaḥ prāha kim anena dvijottama ।।
tattvaṃ vadeti sa harir daityenoktaḥ svakaṃ vapuḥ ।। tataḥ savismayo daityo mayo harim uvāca ha ।। kim idaṃ vajrapāṇis tvaṃ tavāyogyā kṛtiḥ sakhe ।। kenāpi sādhayanty atra paṇḍitāś ca samīhitam ।।
suprītir muniśārdūla mayo harihitaḥ sadā ।। kiṃ me kṛtyam iti prāha mayaṃ māyāvinaṃ hariḥ ।। prāptaḥ saṃprītimān āha kiṃ kṛtyaṃ maya tad vada ।। tasyāḥ śuśrūṣaṇaṃ kurvann āssva tatra kiyanti ca ।।
prāpnoti tāvad vajreṇa tato na bhavitā ripuḥ ।। amoghaṃ tan munes tejaḥ kaśyapasya durāsadam ।। antaḥpraveśakāmo asau bahukālaṃ samāvasan ।। idam antaram ity uktvā dityāḥ kukṣiṃ samāviśat ।।
hantukāmaṃ tadovāca punaḥ punar abhītavat ।। nāraṇe māraṇād anyat pātakaṃ vidyate mahat ।। mayi tasmān naitad evaṃ tava yuktaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। vajrapāṇiḥ surendras tvaṃ te na yuktaṃ bhavet prabho ।।
tathā kuru mahābāho mārgād asmād apāsara ।। avidyaś cāpy aśastraś ca naiva cāyudhasaṃgrahaḥ ।। kurvanti garhitaṃ karma na kulīnāḥ kadācana ।। vadhyante bhrātaraḥ kāmād garbhasthāḥ kiṃ nu pauruṣam ।।
tato muṣṭiṃ puraskṛtya vajriṇe asau vyavasthitaḥ ।। evaṃbhūtaṃ phalaṃ śakra kasmān māṃ hantum udyataḥ ।। sa hantā bālakaṃ māṃ vai kiṃ yaśaḥ kiṃ tu pauruṣam ।। krodhāndhānāṃ lobhināṃ ca na ghṛṇā kvāpi vidyate ।।
punaś ciccheda tān khaṇḍān mā vadhīr iti cābruvan ।। dveṣavidhvastabuddhīnāṃ na citte karuṇākaṇaḥ ।। nirvikāraṃ tato dṛṣṭvā saptasapta suvismitaḥ ।। rudanti bahurūpāṇi mā rutety abravīd dhariḥ ।।
garbhasthā eva te anyonyam ūcuḥ śakraṃ gatabhramāḥ ।। asmatpitā tava bhrātā sakhyaṃ te bahu manyate ।। na yat karoti śvapacaḥ pravṛttas tatra vajradhṛk ।। ditiṃ saṃbodhayām āsa vyathitāṃ garbhavedanāt ।।
tatrāgastyaḥ śacīkāntam aśapat kupito bhṛśam ।। pṛṣṭhaṃ palāyamānānāṃ yat paśyanty ahitā raṇe ।। sāpi taṃ garbhasaṃsthaṃ ca śaśāpendraṃ ruṣā ditiḥ ।। strībhiḥ paribhavaṃ prāpya rājyāt prabhraśyase hare ।।
garbhāntaragataḥ śakraḥ pitaraṃ prāha bhītavat ।। agastyāc ca diteś caiva bibhemi kramituṃ bahiḥ ।। ditiśāpam agastyasya śrutvāsau duḥkhito abhavat ।। na nirmalakulotpannā manaḥ kurvanti pātake ।।
tanmūrtir eva vadati sadasacceṣṭitaṃ nṛṇām ।। yad uktam atra śreyaḥ syāt tatkartāham asaṃśayam ।। sarvaṃ vṛttam athovāca punaḥ papraccha māṃ suraiḥ ।। garbhasthānāṃ ca sarveṣām indreṇa saha mitratām ।।
agastyadattaśāpasya viśāpatvam api kramāt ।। prajāpate kaśyapa tvaṃ vasubhir lokapālakaiḥ ।। tatra snātvā maheśānaṃ stuhi sarvaiḥ samanvitaḥ ।। tathety uktvā jagāmāsau kaśyapo gautamīṃ tadā ।।
gautamī vā puṇyanadī śivo vā karuṇākaraḥ ।। pāhi pāvana vāgīśa pāhi pannagabhūṣaṇa ।। pāhi godhara lakṣmīśa pāhi śarva gajāmbara ।। pāhi yajñeśa someśa pāhy abhīṣṭapradāyaka ।।
pāhi prabhava sarvasya pāhi pālaka vāsava ।। pāhi viśveśa siddheśa pāhi pūrṇa namo astu te ।। śarīriṇāṃ kṛpāsindho tvam eva śaraṇaṃ śiva ।। vareṇa cchandayām āsa kaśyapaṃ taṃ prajāpatim ।।
sa prāha vistareṇātha indrasya tu viceṣṭitam ।। tato vṛṣākapiḥ prāha ditiṃ cāgastyam eva ca ।। sarve bhaveyuḥ subhagā bhaveyur yajñabhāginaḥ ।। indreṇa sahitā nityaṃ vartayeyur mudānvitāḥ ।।
ādau tu marutas tatra bhaveyur nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। jetā bhavet sarvadaiva sukhaṃ tiṣṭha prajāpate ।। vaṃśacchedo vipattiś ca nityaṃ teṣāṃ bhaviṣyati ।। agastyam ṛṣiśārdūlaṃ śaṃbhur apy āha yatnataḥ ।।
śamaṃ vraja mahāprājña marutas tv amarā bhavan ।। ditiṃ cāpi śivaḥ prāha prasanno vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ ।। ity evaṃ cintayantī tvaṃ tapase niyatābhavaḥ ।। anyān api varān subhrūr yācasva gatasaṃbhramā ।।
kṛtāñjalipuṭā natvā śaṃbhuṃ vākyam athābravīt ।। viśeṣeṇa tu tan mātuḥ priyaṃ syāt surapūjita ।। eko api tanayaḥ kiṃtu bahavaś cet kim ucyate ।। indrasya bhrātaraḥ satyaṃ putrāś caiva prajāpateḥ ।।
yatra deva prasādas te tac chubhaṃ ko atra saṃśayaḥ ।। śṛṇuṣva deva vacanaṃ kuruṣva ca jagaddhitam ।। vadety uktā jagaddhātrā ditir namrābravīd idam ।। viśeṣeṇa priyaṃ mātuḥ putraś cet kiṃ nu varṇyate ।।
kiṃ tu svargeṇa deveśa pārameṣṭhyapadena vā ।। tasmād āplavanād atra kriyatāṃ samanugrahaḥ ।। striyā vā puruṣasyāpi vandhyatvaṃ yadi jāyate ।। snātvā tatra phalaṃ dadyāt stotram etac ca yaḥ paṭhet ।।
aputriṇī tv atra snānaṃ kṛtvā putram avāpnuyāt ।। trimāsābhyantaraṃ yā tu gurviṇī bhaktitas tv iha ।। tasyāḥ śakrasamaḥ putro jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। dhanāpahāradoṣaiś ca tatraiṣā niṣkṛtiḥ parā ।।
kiṃcit suvarṇadānena tataḥ putro bhaved dhruvam ।। śrāddhakarmavihīnāś ca teṣāṃ vaṃśo na vardhate ।। saṃtatir jāyatāṃ ślāghyā jīvatāṃ tīrthasevanāt ।। anādyapāram ajaraṃ citsadānandavigraham ।।
liṅgātmakaṃ mahādevaṃ jyotirmayam anāmayam ।। stotreṇānena yaḥ stauti caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca ।। yaḥ karoty atra gaṅgāyāṃ sa putraśatam āpnuyāt ।। ṣaṇmāsāt putram āpnoti api vandhyāpy aśaṅkitam ।।
tatra tu snānadānādyaiḥ sarvakāmān avāpnuyāt ।। niṣpāpatvena cendrasya śakratīrthaṃ tad ucyate ।। etāni sarvatīrthāni sarvābhīṣṭapradāni hi ।। tīrthānāṃ puṇyadaṃ tatra lakṣam ekaṃ prakīrtitam ।।
dṛṣṭādṛṣṭeṣṭadaṃ sarva- devarṣigaṇasevitam ।। anuhrāda iti khyātaḥ kapoto balavān abhūt ।। mṛtyoḥ pautro hy anuhrādo dauhitrī hetir eva ca ।। tasya śatruś ca balavān ulūko nāma pakṣirāṭ ।।
tayoś ca vairam abhavad bahukālaṃ dvijanmanoḥ ।। tasyāś ca dakṣiṇe kūla ulūko nāma pakṣirāṭ ।। tayoś ca yuddham abhavad bahukālaṃ viruddhayoḥ ।। ulūko vā kapoto vā naivāpnoti jayājayau ।।
yāmyam astram avāpyātha sarvebhyo apy adhiko abhavat ।। varair unmattayor yuddham abhavac cātibhīṣaṇam ।। kapoto apy atha pāśān vai yāmyān ākṣipya śatrave ।। punas tad abhavad yuddhaṃ purāḍibakayor yathā ।।
pativratā mahāyuddhe bhartuḥ sā duḥkhavihvalā ।। sā gatvā jvalanaṃ hetis tuṣṭāva vividhoktibhiḥ ।। hotāraṃ cāpi devānāṃ devānāṃ dūtam eva ca ।। yo yajñasādhanaṃ yāmi śaraṇaṃ taṃ dhanaṃjayam ।।
yatra viśramayed astraṃ tan me brūhi pativrate ।। satyavāg bhava havyeśa jātavedo namo astu te ।। tavāpi bhartṛputrāṇāṃ heti kṣemaṃ dadāmy aham ।। na tvāṃ dahet tato yāhi sukhena tvaṃ kapotaki ।।
ulūkī duḥkhitā bhūtvā yamaṃ prāyād bhayāturā ।। evaṃ bruvatyāṃ tasyāṃ tām āha dakṣiṇadikpatiḥ ।। varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te dāsye ahaṃ manasaḥ priyam ।। yamasyeti vacaḥ śrutvā sā tam āha pativratā ।।
tasmād rakṣa suraśreṣṭha putrān bhartāram eva ca ।। tadvākyāt kṛpayā yukto yamaḥ prāha punaḥ punaḥ ।। pāśānāṃ cāpi daṇḍasya sthānaṃ vada śubhānane ।। tataḥ provāca bhagavān yamas tāṃ kṛpayā punaḥ ।।
tava bhartā ca putrāś ca sarve jīvantu vijvarāḥ ।। āhatuś ca dvijanmānau vriyatāṃ vara īpsitaḥ ।। vayaṃ ca pakṣiṇaḥ pāpāḥ kiṃ vareṇa surottamau ।। nātmārtham anuyācāvo dīyamānaṃ varaṃ śubham ।।
jīvitaṃ saphalaṃ tasya yaḥ parārthodyataḥ sadā ।। parārthaṃ vartanaṃ teṣāṃ satāṃ cāpi viśeṣataḥ ।। evaṃ jñātvā tu deveśau vṛthā svārthapariśramaḥ ।। kadācin nānyathā tad vai vṛthā kliśyanti jantavaḥ ।।
guṇadāyi tu sarveṣāṃ tad yuvām anumanyatām ।। dharmasya yaśaso avāptye lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। bhavetāṃ jagatāṃ nāthāv eṣa eva paro varaḥ ।। sarvaṃ tad akṣayaṃ puṇyaṃ syād ity eṣa paro varaḥ ।।
evam astu tathā cānyat suprītau tu bravāvahai ।। teṣāṃ saptasu vaṃśeṣu nākāle mṛtyum āpnuyāt ।। yas tv idaṃ paṭhate nityaṃ mṛtyustotraṃ jitātmavān ।। asmiṃs tīrthe dvijaśreṣṭhau trimāsād gurviṇī satī ।।
vīrasūḥ sā bhaven nārī śatāyuḥ sa suto bhavet ।। manovākkāyajāt pāpāt snānān mukto bhaven naraḥ ।। yamavākyād anu tathā havyavāḍ āha pakṣiṇau ।। teṣām ārogyam aiśvaryaṃ lakṣmīṃ rūpaṃ dadāmy aham ।।
naivāgnito bhayaṃ tasya likhite api gṛhe sthite ।। agniṣṭomaphalaṃ tasya bhaved eva na saṃśayaḥ ।। kapotaṃ ca tatholūkaṃ hetyulūkaṃ vidur budhāḥ ।। punar navatitīrthāni pratyekaṃ muktibhājanam ।।
pūtās te putravittāḍhyā ākrameyur divaṃ śubhāḥ ।। sarvakāmapradaṃ puṇyaṃ pitṝṇāṃ prītivardhanam ।। apām agneś ca saṃvādam ṛṣīṇāṃ ca parasparam ।। evaṃ bruvanto munayaḥ saṃvādaṃ cāgnivāriṇoḥ ।।
ātmabhūto havyabhūtaś cāgninā jāyate akhilam ।। tasmād agneḥ paraṃ nāsti pāvanaṃ daivataṃ mahat ।। vināgninā kiṃcid asti yasya dhāma jagattrayam ।। yoṣitkṣetre arpitaṃ bījaṃ puruṣeṇa yathā tathā ।।
devānāṃ hi mukhaṃ vahnis tasmān nātaḥ paraṃ viduḥ ।। adbhiḥ saṃpatsyate hy annaṃ śucir adbhiḥ prajāyate ।। trailokyajīvanaṃ vāri vadantīti purāvidaḥ ।। agnir jyeṣṭha iti prāhur āpo jyeṣṭhatamāḥ pare ।।
viruddhavādino māṃ ca samabhyetyedam abruvan ।। agner apāṃ vada jyaiṣṭhyaṃ trailokyasya bhavān prabhuḥ ।। ubhau pūjyatamau loka ubhābhyāṃ jāyate jagat ।। ubhābhyāṃ jīvanaṃ loke śarīrasya ca dhāraṇam ।।
tato madvacanāj jyaiṣṭhyam ubhayor naiva kasyacit ।। na tṛptā mama vākyena jagmur vāyuṃ tapasvinaḥ ।। kasya jyaiṣṭhyaṃ bhavān prāṇo vāyo satyaṃ tvayi sthitam ।। nety uktvānyonyam ṛṣayo jagmus te api vasuṃdharām ।।
satyaṃ bhūme vada jyaiṣṭhyam ādhārāsi carācare ।। bhūmir apy āha vinayād āgatāṃs tān ṛṣīn idam ।। adbhyas tu jāyate sarvaṃ jyaiṣṭhyam apsu pratiṣṭhitam ।। tuṣṭuvur vividhaiḥ stotraiḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।।
tataḥ prāha jagaddhātrī daivī vāg aśarīriṇī ।। yasya syāt prathamaṃ siddhis tad bhūtaṃ jyeṣṭham ucyate ।। śrāntāḥ khinnāntarātmānaḥ paraṃ vairāgyam āśritāḥ ।। gautamīm agaman sarve tapas taptuṃ yatavratāḥ ।।
tatra vāg abravīd daivī vedamātā sarasvatī ।। agneś ca pūjakā ye ca vinādbhiḥ pūjanaṃ katham ।। tāvat karmaṇy anarho ayam aśucir malino naraḥ ।। tasmāj jyaiṣṭhyam apām eva jananyo agner viśeṣataḥ ।।
niścayaṃ ca tataś cakrur bhavej jyaiṣṭhyam apām iti ।। tapastīrthaṃ tu tat proktaṃ sattratīrthaṃ tad ucyate ।। teṣu snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvakāmapradaṃ śubham ।। teṣu snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca svargamokṣapradāyakam ।।
māhātmyaṃ tasya ko vaktuṃ saṃgamasya kṣamo naraḥ ।। tasya prabhāvaṃ vakṣyāmi sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।। tasya bhāryā jayā nāma sākṣāl lakṣmīr ivāparā ।। dhanurvede ca vede ca niṣṇāto dakṣa eva ca ।।
ārṣṭiṣeṇas tato rājā putre rājyaṃ niveśya saḥ ।। sarasvatyās tatas tīre hayamedhāya yatnavān ।। dīkṣitaṃ taṃ nṛpaśreṣṭhaṃ brāhmaṇāgnisamīpataḥ ।। makhaṃ vidhvasya nṛpatiṃ sabhāryaṃ sapurohitam ।।
nīte tasmin nṛpavare yajñe naṣṭe tato amarāḥ ।। purohitasuto rājño devāpir iti viśrutaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā savismayo bhūtvā duḥkhito atīva cābhavat ।। pitṛhīno na jīveyaṃ mātaḥ satyaṃ vadasva me ।।
na vakṣi yadi me mātar jalam agnim athāviśe ।। dānavena talaṃ nīto rājñā saha pitā tava ।। keṣu paśyatsu kiṃ sthānaṃ dānavasya vadasva me ।। paśyatsu devasaṃgheṣu vahnibrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau ।।
devān paśye athavāgniṃ vā ṛtvijo vāsurāṃs tathā ।। iti niścitya devāpir bharaṃ prāha nṛpātmajam ।। ānetavyā mayā sarve nītā ye ca rasātalam ।। narādhamena kiṃ tena jīvatā vā mṛtena vā ।।
bhavec ca kṛtakāryasya anujānīhi māṃ bhara ।। bhareṇoktaḥ sa devāpiḥ sarvaṃ niścitya yatnataḥ ।। siddhiṃ kuru sukhaṃ yāhi mā cintām alpikāṃ bhaja ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo bālo devāpir vākyam abravīt ।।
purodhāś ca tathā rakṣyaḥ patnī yā dīkṣitasya tu ।। rājādayas tena nītās tan na yuktatamaṃ bhavet ।। dātum arhanti tān sarvān anyathā śāpam arhatha ।। tasmād vayaṃ na jānīmo hy agnīnāṃ paricārakāḥ ।।
sa eva dātā bhoktā ca hartā kartā ca havyavāṭ ।। pūjayitvā yathānyāyam agnaye tan nyavedayat ।। havyaṃ vahāmi devānāṃ bhoktāro rakṣakāś ca te ।। dāsye aham eṣa doṣo me tasmād yāhi surān prati ।।
ṛtvigvākyaṃ cāgnivākyaṃ śāpaṃ cāpi nyavedayat ।। bhokṣyāmahe havirbhāgān na svatantrā dvijottama ।। paratantrās tato vipra vedebhyas tan nivedaya ।। dhyānena tapasā yukto vedāś cāpi puro abhavan ।।
ṛtvigvākyaṃ cāgnivākyaṃ devavākyaṃ nyavedayat ।। aśeṣajagadādhāro nirādhāro nirañjanaḥ ।। sa tu kartā mahādevaḥ saṃhartā sa maheśvaraḥ ।। asmākam etat kṛtyaṃ syād vadāmo yat tu pṛcchasi ।।
bhakṣitāḥ kiṃ tu no naṣṭā etaj jānīmahe vayam ।। syād ity etac ca jānīmo yathā prāpsyasi tān puraḥ ।। etac chrutvāvadad vedān vicārya suciraṃ hṛdi ।। sarvān prāpsye talaṃ nītān alaṃ tebhyo namo astu vaḥ ।।
suprasannas tavābhīṣṭaṃ dāsyaty eva kṛpākaraḥ ।। ārṣṭiṣeṇaś ca nṛpatis tasya jāyā jayā satī ।। yaśaḥ prāpsyasi dharmaṃ ca etac chakyaṃ na cetarat ।। snātvā kṛtakṣaṇo vipras tuṣṭāva ca maheśvaram ।।
na me śaktis tvatstavane tubhyaṃ śaṃbho namo astu te ।। na brahmā nāpi vaikuṇṭho yo asi so asi namo astu te ।। pāpātmāno ye ca loke tāṃs tvaṃ pāsi maheśvara ।। tvayā dattaṃ phalaṃ tebhyo dāsyanti jagatāṃ pate ।।
bhavatīti na citraṃ syāt tvaṃ viparyayakārakaḥ ।। śiveti vacanān nātha tān pāsi tvaṃ jagadguro ।। evaṃ tu stuvatas tasya puraḥ prāha trilocanaḥ ।। varaṃ brūhy atha devāpe alaṃ dainyena bālaka ।।
prāptum icche jagannātha nidhanaṃ ca ripor mama ।। devāpeḥ sarvam abhavad ājñayā śaṃkarasya tat ।। nandinaṃ preṣayām āsa śaṃbhuḥ śūlena nārada ।। tatpitrādīn samānīya tasmai tān sa nyavedayat ।।
agniś ca ṛtvijo devā vedāś ca ṛṣayo abruvan ।। devadevo jagannātho devatīrtham abhūc ca tat ।। puṇyadaṃ tīrtham etat syāt tava kīrtiś ca śāśvatī ।। snātvā kṛtārthā gaṅgāyāṃ tatas te divam ākraman ।।
teṣu snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca hy atīva phaladaṃ viduḥ ।। siddheśvaraṃ tatra tīrthaṃ gautamyā dakṣiṇe taṭe ।। yasyākarṇanamātreṇa sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। bhāryāṃ prāpto dakṣasutāṃ svāhānāmnīṃ surūpiṇīm ।।
sa bhartā hutabhuk prāha bhāryāṃ svāhām aninditām ।। apatyāni bhaviṣyanti mā tapaḥ kuru śobhane ।। strīṇām abhīṣṭadaṃ nānyad bhartṛvākyaṃ vinā kvacit ।। anutpanne kārttikeye cirakālarahogate ।।
devānāṃ kāryasiddhyartham agniṃ procur divaukasaḥ ।। tārakād bhayam utpannaṃ śaṃbhave tvaṃ nivedaya ।। sāmānyamātrato nyāyaḥ kiṃ punaḥ śūlapāṇini ।। daṃpatyoḥ śṛṇuyād vākyaṃ nirayāt tasya noddhṛtiḥ ।।
nirīkṣaṇīyaḥ kena syād bhavānyā rahasi sthitaḥ ।। tārakād bhaya utpanne gaccha tvaṃ tārako bhavān ।। rūpeṇānyena vā gaccha vācaṃ vada yathā tathā ।। tato dāsyāmahe pūjām ubhayor lokayoḥ kave ।।
yatrāsīj jagatāṃ nātho ramamāṇas tadomayā ।। nāśakad dvāradeśe tu praveṣṭuṃ havyavāhanaḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā prahasañ śaṃbhur umāṃ prāha rahogataḥ ।। paśya devi śukaṃ prāptaṃ devavākyād dhutāśanam ।।
puraścarantaṃ deveśo hy agniṃ taṃ dvijarūpiṇam ।। vidārayasva svamukhaṃ gṛhāṇedaṃ nayasva tat ।। retogarbhas tadā cāgnir gantuṃ naiva ca śaktavān ।। kṛttikāsu ca tad retaḥ prakṣepāt kārttiko abhavat ।।
tad eva reto vahnis tu svabhāryāyāṃ dvidhākṣipat ।। purā sāśvāsitā tena saṃtatis te bhaviṣyati ।। tad agne retasas tasyāṃ jajñe mithunam uttamam ।। agneḥ prītikaraṃ nityaṃ lokānāṃ prītivardhanam ।।
evaṃ putrasya putryāś ca vivāham akarot kaviḥ ।। mām abhyetya tadovāca niṣkṛtiṃ vada putrayoḥ ।। stutvā tatra mahābāho nivedaya jagatpateḥ ।। evaṃvidhaṃ tv apatyaṃ te jātaṃ vahne tato bhavān ।।
svāpatyarakṣaṇāyāsau śaṃbhuḥ śreyaḥ kariṣyati ।। tatas tv apatyaviṣaye priyān kāmān avāpsyasi ।। tuṣṭāva niyato vākyaiḥ stutibhir vedasaṃmitaiḥ ।। ādikartā svayaṃbhūś ca taṃ namāmi jagatpatim ।।
sūryarūpeṇa yaḥ pāti taṃ namāmi ca tryambakam ।। vareṇa cchandayām āsa pāvakaṃ surapūjitam ।। tena jātaḥ suto ramyaḥ suvarṇo lokaviśrutaḥ ।। anyonyavīryasaṅgāc ca taddoṣād ubhayaṃ tv idam ।।
śāpaṃ daduḥ surāḥ sarve tayoḥ śāntiṃ kuru prabho ।। tadagnivacanāc chaṃbhuḥ provācedaṃ śubhodayam ।। samagrā ṛddhayaḥ sarvāḥ suvarṇe asmin samāhitāḥ ।। trayāṇām api lokānāṃ pāvanaḥ sa bhaviṣyati ।।
sa eva bhuktimuktī ca sa eva makhadakṣiṇā ।। vīryaṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ vidyād vīryaṃ matto yad uttamam ।। hīnaṃ tena vinā sarvaṃ saṃpūrṇās tena saṃpadaḥ ।। nirguṇo api dhanī mānyaḥ saguṇo apy adhano nahi ।।
tathā caiṣā suvarṇāpi syād utkṛṣṭāpi cañcalā ।। tapasā japahomaiś ca yeyaṃ prāpyā jagattraye ।। sarvatra yā tu saṃtiṣṭhed āyātu vicariṣyati ।। adya prabhṛty ātmajayos tathā svairaṃ viceṣṭatoḥ ।।
tathāpi caitayoḥ puṇyaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati ।। liṅgarūpeṇa sarveṣāṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। svabhartrā ca suvarṇā sā dharmeṇāgnisutā mudā ।। etasminn antare svarṇām agner duhitaraṃ mune ।।
aharad bhāgyasaubhāgya- vilāsavasatiṃ chalāt ।। jāmātāgneḥ sa dharmaś ca agniś caiva sa havyavāṭ ।। kāryavijñāpanaṃ cobhau cakratuḥ prabhaviṣṇave ।। sānītā viṣṇunā devī suvarṇā lokasundarī ।।
maheśvarāya tāṃ viṣṇur darśayām āsa nārada ।। cakraṃ prakṣālitaṃ yatra śārdūlacchedi dīptimat ।। yatra nītā suvarṇā sā viṣṇunā śaṃkarāntikam ।। yatrānandam anuprāpto hy agnir dharmaś ca śāśvataḥ ।।
ānandeti nadī jātā tathā vai nandinīti ca ।। tatraiva saṃgame sākṣāt suvarṇādyāpi saṃsthitā ।। ambikā jagadādhārā śivā kātyāyanīśvarī ।। tapas tepe yatra cāgnis tat tīrthaṃ tu tapovanam ।।
teṣu snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvakāmapradaṃ śubham ।। dakṣiṇe ca tathā pāre sahasrāṇy atha ṣoḍaśa ।। nāmāni ca pṛthak santi saṃkṣepāt tan mayocyate ।। sarveṣu tatra kāmyeṣu paripūrṇo bhaven naraḥ ।।
lakṣmīvāñ jāyate nityaṃ dharmavāṃś ca viśeṣataḥ ।। vārāṇasyāditīrthebhyaḥ sarvebhyo hy adhikaṃ bhavet ।। sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। tasyaikaikasya māhātmyaṃ na kenāpy atra varṇyate ।।
phenāyāḥ saṃgamo yatra hanūmataṃ tathaiva ca ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca punarāvṛttidurlabham ।। indreśvaraṃ cottare ca śṛṇu bhaktyā yatavrataḥ ।। tasyendreṇābhavad yuddhaṃ phenenendro aharac chiraḥ ।।
śiraś chittvā tac ca phenaṃ gaṅgāyā dakṣiṇe taṭe ।। rasātalabhavaṃ gāṅgaṃ vāri yad viśvapāvanam ।। taj jalaṃ phenanāmnā tu nadī pheneti gadyate ।। sarvapāpakṣayakaro gaṅgāyamunayor iva ।।
mārjāratvād abhūn muktā viṣṇugaṅgāprasādataḥ ।। hanūmataṃ ca tat proktaṃ tatrākhyānaṃ puroditam ।। hiraṇya iti vikhyāto daityānāṃ pūrvajo balī ।। tasyāpi balavān putro devānāṃ durjayaḥ sadā ।।
tenendrasyābhavad yuddhaṃ bahukālaṃ nirantaram ।। jitvā nāgena sahitaṃ śakraṃ pitre nyavedayat ।। vihāya krūratāṃ daityo hiraṇyāya nyavedayat ।। śacīkāntaṃ tale sthāpya tasya rakṣām athākarot ।।
varuṇo api mahābuddhiḥ prādāt kanyāṃ mahāśaneḥ ।। tayoś ca sakhyam abhavad varuṇasya mahāśaneḥ ।। vīryeṇa yaśasā cāpi śauryeṇa ca balena ca ।। nirindratvaṃ gate loke devāḥ sarve nyamantrayan ।।
mantradṛg vā sa eva syād indraṃ cānyaṃ kariṣyati ।। mamāvadhyo mahādaityo mahāśanir iti bruvan ।। keśavo varuṇaṃ gatvā prāhendrasya parābhavam ।। tadviṣṇuvacanāc chīghraṃ yayau jalapatir mune ।।
atisaṃmānitas tena jāmātrā varuṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। varuṇaḥ prāha taṃ daityaṃ yad āgamanakāraṇam ।। baddhaṃ rasātalasthaṃ taṃ devānām adhipaṃ sakhe ।। baddhvā vimokṣaṇaṃ śatror mahate yaśase satām ।।
prādād indraṃ śacīkāntaṃ vāraṇena samanvitam ।। prādād indraṃ punaś cedaṃ vacanaṃ tad abhāṣata ।। śvaśuro mama yena tvaṃ muktim āpto asi vāsava ।। no ced baddhvā punas tvāṃ vai kṣepsye caiva rasātalam ।।
abravīd gaccha gaccheti varuṇaṃ cānumanya tu ।। paulomyāṃ prāha tat sarvaṃ yat tac chatruparābhavam ।। nirvāpayāmi yena svam ātmānaṃ subhage vada ।। varadānaṃ tathā mṛtyuṃ jāne ahaṃ balasūdana ।।
jāyeta śṛṇu tat sarvaṃ vakṣye ahaṃ prītaye tava ।। tasmān mama syāt sa bhrātā varadānāc ca darpitaḥ ।। īdṛśaṃ balam āpannaṃ tapasā kiṃ na sidhyati ।। na kāryaḥ śṛṇu tatredaṃ kāryaṃ yat tu kramāgatam ।।
evam uktvā tu paulomī prāhendraṃ vinayānvitā ।। nāsādhyaṃ lokanāthasya viṣṇor bhaktyā harasya ca ।। strīṇāṃ svabhāvaṃ jānanti striya eva surādhipa ।। tapo vā yajñakarmādi tābhyām eva yato bhavet ।।
tatra viṣṇuṃ śivaṃ pūjya sarvān kāmān avāpsyasi ।। tā eva sarvaṃ jānanti dhṛtaṃ tābhiś carācaram ।। tatra gaṅgā jagaddhātrī tatreśaṃ pūjaya prabho ।। anāthānām iha nṛṇāṃ majjatāṃ duḥkhasāgare ।।
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena toṣayaitān samāhitaḥ ।। tataḥ prāpsyasi kalyāṇam īśaviṣṇuprasādajam ।। jñātvā śataguṇaṃ tat syād bhāryayā ca tad akṣayam ।। svalpānām api kāryāṇāṃ nahi siddhis tayā vinā ।।
jāyayā tu kṛtaṃ nātha puṣkalaṃ puruṣo labhet ।। śrūyate daṇḍakāraṇye saricchreṣṭhāsti gautamī ।। tasmād gaccha mayā tatra kuru puṇyaṃ mahāphalam ।। tataḥ śatrūn nihatyājau mahat sukham avāpsyasi ।।
yayau gaṅgāṃ jagaddhātrīṃ gautamīṃ ceti viśrutām ।। tapaḥ kartuṃ manaś cakre devadevāya śaṃbhave ।। śivaikaśaraṇo bhūtvā stotraṃ cedaṃ tato abravīt ।। śivaśaktyos tadādvaitaṃ sundaraṃ naumi vigraham ।।
evaṃ tu stuvatas tasya purastād abhavac chivaḥ ।। kim abhīṣṭaṃ varayase hare vada parāyaṇam ।। tena baddhas talaṃ nītaḥ paribhūtas tv anekadhā ।। tadarthaṃ jagatām īśa yena jeṣye ripuṃ prabho ।।
punarjātam ahaṃ manye varaṃ kīrtir jayaśriyoḥ ।। vadham āpnoti tasmāt tvaṃ viṣṇum apy avyayaṃ harim ।। lokatrayaikaśaraṇaṃ nārāyaṇam ananyadhīḥ ।। punaś covāca bhagavān ādikartā maheśvaraḥ ।।
saṃgame yatra kutrāpi siddhidaṃ munayo viduḥ ।। girīṇāṃ gahvare yad vā saritām atha saṃgame ।। gaṅgāyā dakṣiṇe tīra āpastambo munīśvaraḥ ।। tena tvaṃ bhāryayā caiva toṣayasva gadādharam ।।
tuṣṭāva devaṃ prayataḥ snātvā puṇye atha saṃgame ।। vaidikair vividhair mantrais tapasātoṣayat tadā ।। dehi me śatruhantāram ity āha bhagavān hariḥ ।। tatrābhavac chivasyaiva gaṅgāviṣṇvoḥ prasādataḥ ।।
cakrapāṇiḥ śūladharaḥ sa gatvā tu rasātalam ।। sakhābhavat sa cendrasya abjakaḥ sa vṛṣākapiḥ ।। śacīṃ tāṃ sāntvayann āha śatamanyur hasann idam ।। vāri vāpi havir yasya agneḥ priyakaraṃ sadā ।।
tasmān nārhasi māṃ vaktuṃ śaṅkayānyatra bhāmini ।। sāpatyā ca kulīnā ca tvatto anyā kā priyā mama ।। prasādād devadevasya viṣṇor vai cakrapāṇinaḥ ।। jalodbhavāc ca me mitrād abjakāl lokaviśrutāt ।।
kiṃ na sādhyaṃ yatra bhāryā bhartṛcittānugāminī ।। jāyaiva paramaṃ mitraṃ lokadvayahitaiṣiṇī ।। itas tavoditaṃ caiva kartavyaṃ nānyad asti me ।। ārtasya puruṣasyeha bhāryāvad bheṣajaṃ nahi ।।
gaṅgayā sadṛśaṃ nāsti śṛṇu cānyad varānane ।। śivaviṣṇvor ananyatva- jñānān nāsty atra muktaye ।। avāptaṃ ca śivād viṣṇor gaṅgāyāś ca prasādataḥ ।। vṛṣākapir mama sakhā yo jātas tv apsu bhāmini ।।
tīrthānāṃ gautamī gaṅgā devānāṃ hariśaṃkarau ।। mama prītikaraṃ cedaṃ tīrthaṃ trailokyaviśrutam ।। anumanyantu ṛṣayo gaṅgā ca hariśaṃkarau ।। ekatra śaṃkaro devo hy aparatra janārdanaḥ ।।
antare yāni tīrthāni sarvapuṇyapradāni ca ।। pāpiṣṭhāḥ pāpato muktim āpnuyur ye ca dharmiṇaḥ ।। atra kiṃcic ca ye dadyur arthibhyas tilamātrakam ।। dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyam ārogyaṃ puṇyavardhanam ।।
asya tīrthasya māhātmyaṃ ye śṛṇvanti paṭhanti ca ।। yāṃ prārthayanti munayo vijitendriyamānasāḥ ।। gautamyā uttare pāre tīrthānāṃ mokṣadāyinām ।। tathaiva dakṣiṇe tīre tīrthāny ekādaśaiva tu ।।
viśrāmasthānam īśasya viṣṇor brahmaṇa eva ca ।। smaraṇād apy aśeṣāgha- saṃghavidhvaṃsanakṣamam ।। tasya bhāryākṣasūtreti patidharmaparāyaṇā ।। tasyāśramam anuprāpto hy agastyo munisattamaḥ ।।
śiṣyair anugato dhīmāṃs taṃ praṣṭum upacakrame ।। bhuktir muktiś ca kasmād vā syād anādiś ca ko bhavet ।। etaṃ me saṃśayaṃ chettuṃ vadāgastya mahāmune ।। tatrāpi vaidikaḥ śabdaḥ pramāṇaṃ paramaṃ mataḥ ।।
mṛto aparaḥ sa vijñeyo hy amṛtaḥ para ucyate ।। guṇābhivyāptibhedena mūrto asau trividho bhavet ।। trayāṇām api devānāṃ vedyam ekaṃ paraṃ hi tat ।। lokānām upakārārtham ākṛtitritayaṃ bhavet ।।
tatra yo bhedam ācaṣṭe liṅgabhedī sa ucyate ।। trayāṇām api devānāṃ mūrtibhedaḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।। nirākāraṃ ca yat tv ekaṃ tat tebhyaḥ paramaṃ matam ।। niḥsaṃśayaṃ nirvikalpaṃ bhājanaṃ sarvasaṃpadām ।।
etad ākarṇya bhagavān agastyo vākyam abravīt ।। tathāpi sarvasiddhiḥ syāc chivād eva sukhātmanaḥ ।। gautamyāṃ sakalāghaugha- saṃhartā daṇḍake vane ।। bhuktido muktidaḥ puṃsāṃ sākāro atha nirākṛtiḥ ।।
dātā ca hanti sarvaṃ yo yasmād etat samāpyate ।। rudrākṛtir nihantrī sā sarvavedeṣu paṭhyate ।। tuṣṭāva śaṃkaraṃ devaṃ stotreṇānena nārada ।। ātmārthaṃ ca parārthaṃ ca āpastambo abravīc chivam ।।
paśyeyur jagatām īśam astv ity āha śivo munim ।। anādy avidyātimira- vrātanirmūlanakṣamam ।। aśeṣapāpaśamanaṃ tatra vṛttam idaṃ śṛṇu ।। sarameti prasiddhāsti nāmnā devaśunī mune ।।
gāminau pavanāhārau caturakṣau yamapriyau ।। rakṣantīm anujagmus te rākṣasā daityadānavāḥ ।। pralobhayitvā vividhair vākyair dānaiś ca yatnataḥ ।। tata āgatya sā devān idam āha kramāc chunī ।।
nītā gā yajñasiddhyarthaṃ kalpitāḥ paśavaḥ surāḥ ।। tasyā vācaṃ niśamyāśu surān prāha bṛhaspatiḥ ।। pāpeyaṃ sukṛtīveti lakṣyate dehaceṣṭitaiḥ ।। padāghātāt tadā tasyā mukhāt kṣīraṃ prasusruve ।।
rākṣasaiś ca tadā dattaṃ tasmān nītās tu gā mama ।। tasmād ruṣṭo asi kiṃ nātha ripavo balinas tu te ।। satyaṃ śakra tv iyaṃ duṣṭā ripūṇāṃ pakṣakāriṇī ।। martyaloke pāpabhūtā ajñānāt pāpakāriṇī ।।
yathā śaptā maghavatā pāpāt sā hy atibhīṣaṇā ।। yatnaṃ kurvan surapatir viṣṇave tan nyavedayat ।। hantuṃ prayatnam akaroj jagṛhe ca mahad dhanuḥ ।। jitāriḥ pūjito devaiḥ svayaṃ sthitvā janārdanaḥ ।।
tatrasthān daityadanujān rākṣasāṃś ca balīyasaḥ ।। tatra vai daṇḍakāraṇye śārṅgapāṇir iti śrutaḥ ।। te jagmur dakṣiṇām āśāṃ viṣṇos trāsān mahāmune ।। garutmatā tān avāpya śārṅgamuktair manojavaiḥ ।।
devārayaḥ kṣayaṃ nītā viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā ।। kṣayaṃ prāptā viṣṇubāṇais tatas te devaśatravaḥ ।। vaiṣṇavaṃ lokaviditaṃ gotīrthaṃ ceti viśrutam ।। pradrutās te surāḥ sarve gaṅgāyāṃ saṃnyaveśayan ।।
tair gobhis tatra gaṅgāyāṃ surayajño vyajāyata ।। devānāṃ yajanaṃ tac ca sarvakāmapradaṃ śubham ।। asārāpārasaṃsāra- sāgarottaraṇe tariḥ ।। gorakṣaṃ tu tatas tīrthaṃ gaṅgāyā dakṣiṇe taṭe ।।
mātuḥ śāpaṃ cāparādhaṃ sarvaṃ cāpi savistaram ।। viśāpakaraṇaṃ cāpi papracchatur ubhau yamam ।। śrutvā sūryaḥ sutaṃ prāha gaṅgāyāṃ surasattama ।। śraddhayā parayā vatsa susnātaḥ susamāhitaḥ ।।
stuhi tvaṃ sarvabhāvena bhṛtyau prītim avāpsyataḥ ।। tayoś ca prītaye prāyād devatarpaṇayor yamaḥ ।। tathaiva toṣayām āsa gaṅgāyāṃ surasattamān ।। brahmāṇaṃ toṣayām āsa bhānuṃ vai dakṣiṇe taṭe ।।
varān ayācata bahūṃl lokānām upakārakān ।। ātmārthaṃ ca parārthaṃ ca te kāmān āpnuyuḥ śubhān ।। tebhyo dāridryaduḥkhāni na bhaveyur yuge yuge ।। brahmāṇaṃ taṃ namasyātha dvīpasyāpi pradakṣiṇam ।।
pradakṣiṇīkṛtā tatra kiṃcid dattvā vasu dvijam ।। aśvamedhādiyajñānāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti puṣkalam ।। adhītās tena vedā vai niṣkāmo muktibhājanam ।। pūjayitvā yathānyāyaṃ sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt ।।
sarvān kāmān avāpnoti putravān dhanavān bhavet ।। snātvā paśyeta teneṣṭā yajñā vividhadakṣiṇāḥ ।। snātvā paśyeta taṃ natvā tasya viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam ।। snātaḥ paśyati yuktātmā sa karoty acireṇa hi ।।
api duṣkṛtakarmāṇaḥ pitaro mokṣam āpnuyuḥ ।। teṣu snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvam akṣayapuṇyadam ।। śravaṇāt pitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ paṭhanāt svakulaiḥ saha ।। tatra snānādi yaḥ kṛtvā kiṃcid dattvā yatātmavān ।।
dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ yaśo vīryam āyur ārogyasaṃpadaḥ ।। aviyuktaḥ prītamanā bandhubhiś cātimānitaḥ ।। tato muktipadaṃ gacched devānāṃ vacanaṃ yathā ।। tatra snānena dānena sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt ।।
tatra ca snānamātreṇa sattrayāgaphalaṃ labhet ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ sattram agamad gautamītīravartinām ।। yā gatvāśrāvaya vauṣaḍ astu śrauṣaḍ iti sthiram ।। tato nady abhavat tatra yakṣiṇīti suviśrutā ।।
saṃgamya caiva gautamyā tāṃ viśāpām athākarot ।। tatra snānādidānena sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt ।। śaivaṃ tat paramaṃ tīrthaṃ durgātīrthaṃ ca viśrutam ।। tīrthaṃ munivaraiḥ khyātaṃ sarvasiddhipradaṃ nṛṇām ।।
yasya smaraṇamātreṇa sarvakāmān avāpnuyāt ।। tasya paiṭhīnasī nāma bhāryā sukalabhūṣaṇā ।। agnīṣomīyam aindrāgnaṃ puroḍāśam akalpayat ।। puroḍāśaṃ bhakṣayitvā lokatritayabhīṣaṇaḥ ।।
tad ṛṣer vacanaṃ śrutvā rākṣasaḥ pratyuvāca tam ।। saṃdhyāsuto ahaṃ jyeṣṭhaś ca sutaḥ prācīnabarhiṣaḥ ।। mamānujaḥ kaliś cāpi balavān atibhīṣaṇaḥ ।। ahaṃ makhaṃ haniṣyāmi yūpaṃ chedmi kṛtāntakaḥ ।।
jāne tvāṃ yajñahantāraṃ saddvijaṃ rakṣa me kratum ।। brahmaṇāhaṃ purā śapto devadānavasaṃnidhau ।। amṛtaiḥ prokṣayiṣyanti yadā tvāṃ munisattamāḥ ।। evaṃ kariṣyasi yadā tataḥ sarvaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
makhasaṃrakṣaṇaṃ yena syān me vada karomi tat ।। alabhantāmṛtaṃ kaṣṭāt tad asmatsulabhaṃ katham ।। tad ṛṣer vacanaṃ śrutvā rakṣaḥ prāha tadā mudā ।। amṛtaṃ gobhavaṃ cājyam amṛtaṃ soma eva ca ।।
sarvebhyo apy adhikaṃ divyam amṛtaṃ gautamījalam ।। pāṇāv ādāya gaṅgāyāḥ salilāmṛtam ādarāt ।। punaś ca yūpe ca paśāv ṛtvikṣu makhamaṇḍale ।। tad rakṣo api tadā śuklo bhūtvotpanno mahābalaḥ ।।
yajñaṃ sarvaṃ samāpyātha bharadvājaḥ pratāpavān ।। gaṅgāmadhye tad dhi yūpam adyāpy āste mahāmate ।। tatra tīrthe punā rakṣo bharadvājam uvāca ha ।। tasmāt tavātra tīrthe ye snānadānādipūjanam ।।
smaraṇād api pāpāni nāśaṃ yāntu sadā mune ।। gautamyāṃ daṇḍakāraṇye svargadvāram apāvṛtam ।। tīrthānāṃ muniśārdūla sarvasiddhipradāyinām ।। tasya prabhāvaṃ vakṣyāmi śṛṇu yatnena nārada ।।
gautamyās tīram āśritya sattrayajñam upāsate ।। mām abhyetyātha munayo rakṣaḥkṛtyaṃ nyavedayan ।। yasyāś ca darśanād eva nāśaṃ yānty atha rākṣasāḥ ।। madvākyād ṛṣayo māyām ādāya punar āgaman ।।
muktakeśīty abhidhayā sāste adyāpi svarūpiṇī ।। tadbalāt svasthamanasaḥ sarve ca munipuṃgavaḥ ।। punas tanmakhanāśāya rākṣasāḥ samupāgaman ।। tato nṛtyanti gāyanti hasanti ca rudanti ca ।।
teṣāṃ madhye daityapatiḥ śambaro nāma vīryavān ।। tad adbhutam atīvāsīt tanmāyābaladarśinām ।। prādād viṣṇuś cakram atho munīnāṃ rakṣaṇāya tu ।। ciccheda tadbhayād eva mṛtā rākṣasapuṃgavāḥ ।।
viṣṇoḥ prakṣālitaṃ cakraṃ gaṅgāmbhobhiḥ sudarśanam ।। tatra snānena dānena sattrayāgaphalaṃ labhet ।। teṣu snānaṃ tathā dānaṃ pratyekaṃ muktidāyakam ।। tat tīrthaṃ sarvapāpānāṃ mocanaṃ sarvakāmadam ।।
brahmaviṣṇvoś ca saṃvāde mahattve ca parasparam ।। tatraiva vāg uvācedaṃ daivī putra tayoḥ śubhā ।। daivī vāk tāv ubhau prāha yas tv asyāntaṃ tu paśyati ।। tadvākyād viṣṇur agamad adho ahaṃ cordhvam eva ca ।।
aprāpyāntam ahaṃ prāyāṃ dūrād dūrataraṃ mune ।। tadaivaṃ mama dhīr āsīd dṛṣṭaś cānto mayā bhṛśam ।। punaś cāpi mama tv evaṃ matir āsīn mahāmate ।। nānāvidheṣu pāpeṣu nānṛtāt pātakaṃ param ।।
tato ahaṃ pañcamaṃ vaktraṃ gardabhākṛtibhīṣaṇam ।। abravaṃ taṃ hariṃ tatra āsīnaṃ jagatāṃ prabhum ।। mameti vadataḥ pārśve ubhau tau hariśaṃkarau ।। tataḥ kruddhau jagannāthau vācaṃ tām idam ūcatuḥ ।।
duṣṭe tvaṃ nimnagā bhūyā nānṛtād asti pātakam ।। tad dṛṣṭvā vismito bhītas tām abravam ahaṃ tadā ।। tasmād adṛśyā tvaṃ bhūyāḥ pāparūpāsy asaṃśayam ।। viśāpatvaṃ prārthayantī tuṣṭāva ca punaḥ punaḥ ।।
prītyā hariharāv evaṃ vācaṃ vācam athocatuḥ ।। tadā punar vapus te syāt pavitraṃ hi suśobhane ।। bhāgīrathī gautamī ca tataś cāpi svakaṃ vapuḥ ।। gautamyāṃ saiva vikhyātā nāmnā vāṇīti puṇyadā ।।
ubhayatrāpi vikhyātaḥ saṃgamo lokapūjitaḥ ।। gautamyā saṃgatā devī vāṇī vācā sarasvatī ।। deveśvaraṃ pūjayitvā viśāpam agamad yataḥ ।। tasmāt tatra śucir bhūtvā snātvā tatra ca saṃgame ।।
dānahomādikaṃ kiṃcid upavāsādikāṃ kriyām ।। nānājanmārjitāśeṣa- pāpakṣayavidhāyinām ।। maudgalya iti vikhyāto mudgalasya suto ṛṣiḥ ।। pitā ṛṣis tathā vṛddho mudgalo lokaviśrutaḥ ।।
sa maudgalyaḥ prātar eva gaṅgāṃ snāti yatavrataḥ ।। gaṅgātīre kuśair mṛdbhiḥ śamīpuṣpair aharniśam ।। āvāhanaṃ nityam eva viṣṇoś cakre sa maudgaliḥ ।। vainateyam athāruhya śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।।
prabrūte ca kathāś citrā maudgalyāya jagatprabhuḥ ।। yāhi vatsa svabhavanaṃ śrānto asīti punaḥ punaḥ ।। jagatprabhus tato yāti devair yuktaḥ svamandiram ।। svam eva bhavanaṃ vidvān bhāryāyai svārjitaṃ dhanam ।।
maudgalyasya priyā sāpi pativrataparāyaṇā ।। susaṃskṛtyāpy atithīnāṃ bālānāṃ bhartur eva ca ।। bhuktavatsv atha sarveṣu rātrau nityaṃ sa maudgaliḥ ।। maudgalyasya raho bhāryā bhartāraṃ vākyam abravīt ।।
tathāpi kaṣṭam asmākaṃ kasmād iti jagatprabhum ।। nāśaṃ yānti kuto dṛṣṭe tasmāt pṛccha jagatpatim ।। pūjayitvā vinītaś ca papraccha sa kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। nāśaṃ yāti vipattir me tvayi dṛṣṭe kathaṃ sthitā ।।
na kopi kasyacit kiṃcit karoty atra hitāhite ।। rasālaḥ syān na nimbasya bījāj jātv api kutracit ।। na dattaṃ yaiś ca viprebhyas te kathaṃ bhājanaṃ śriyaḥ ।। yad dīyate tad eveha parasmiṃś copatiṣṭhati ।।
karoti tasmāt pūtātmā śarīrasya ca śoṣaṇāt ।। satkarmācaraṇāc chuddho viraktaḥ syāt tato naraḥ ।। sarveṣāṃ sulabhā muktir madbhaktyā ceha pūrtataḥ ।। athavā lapsyase muktiṃ bhaktyā bhuktiṃ na lapsyase ।।
jātā ced dehināṃ muktiḥ kim anyena prayojanam ।। bhaktyā muktiḥ sarvapūjyā tām iccheyaṃ jaganmaya ।। brāhmaṇāyāthavārthibhyas tad evākṣayatāṃ vrajet ।। tat punar dattam eveha na bhogāyātra kalpate ।।
athavā vipramukhyāya gautamītīram āśritaḥ ।। nānyat kiṃcana dehādi yat tat tvayi samarpitam ।। ihānayasva kaṇiśaṃ mamāyaṃ cārpayiṣyati ।। ākarṇya svāminādiṣṭaṃ tathā cakre sa pakṣirāṭ ।।
etasminn antare viṣṇur viśvakarmāṇam abravīt ।। gāvo hiraṇyaṃ dhānyāni vastrāṇy ābharaṇāni ca ।। tat sarvam āpa maudgalyo viṣṇugaṅgāprabhāvataḥ ।। āśrame svasya sarvarddhiṃ dṛṣṭvā ṛṣir abhāṣata ।।
aho gaṅgāprabhāvaś ca kair vicāryo mahān ayam ।। pitṛbhyāṃ bubhuje bhogān bhuktiṃ muktim avāpa ca ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca bhuktimuktiphalapradam ।। tasya viṣṇur bhavet prītaḥ pāpair muktaḥ sukhī bhavet ।।
sarvārthadāyināṃ tatra snānadānajapādibhiḥ ।। alakṣmīnāśanaṃ puṇyam ākhyānaṃ śṛṇu nārada ।। parasparavirodhinyāv ubhe viśvaṃ samīyatuḥ ।। ahaṃ pūrvaṃ samudbhūtā ity āha śriyam ojasā ।।
mayā vinā dehabhājo jīvanto api mṛtā iva ।। muktir madāśritā nityaṃ daridraivaṃ vaco abravīt ।। yatrāham asmi tatraite na tiṣṭhanti kadācana ।। yatrāham asmi tatraite na tiṣṭhanti kadācana ।।
daridrāyā vacaḥ śrutvā lakṣmīs tāṃ pratyabhāṣata ।। nirdhanaḥ śivatulyo api sarvair apy abhibhūyate ।। sadyo nirgatya gacchanti dhīśrīhrīśāntikīrtayaḥ ।। arthī cet puruṣo jātaḥ kva guṇāḥ kva ca gauravam ।।
namasyaḥ sarvalokānāṃ yāvan nārthayate param ।। na mānayati no vakti na spṛśaty adhanaṃ janaḥ ।। aham eva tataḥ śreṣṭhā daridre śṛṇu me vacaḥ ।। tal lakṣmīvacanaṃ śrutvā daridrā vākyam abravīt ।।
pāpeṣu ramase nityaṃ vihāya puruṣottamam ।। sukhaṃ na tādṛk tvatprāptau paścāttāpo yathā guruḥ ।। tvatsaṃnidhānamātreṇa yathā vai viduṣām api ।। ahaṃ vasāmi yogyeṣu dharmaśīleṣu sarvadā ।।
sadācāreṣu śānteṣu gurusevodyateṣu ca ।। nivasāmi sadā lakṣmīs tasmāj jyaiṣṭhyaṃ mayi sthitam ।। nirbhayeṣu vasiṣyāmi lakṣmīs tvaṃ śṛṇu te sthitim ।। piśuneṣu ca lubdheṣu vikṛteṣu śaṭheṣu ca ।।
mitradrohiṣv aniṣṭeṣu bhagnacitteṣu vartase ।। tayor vākyam upaśrutya mayokte te ubhe api ।। strīṇāṃ vivādaṃ tā eva striyo jānanti netare ।। tatrāpi gautamī devī niścayaṃ kathayiṣyati ।।
te madvākyād bhuvaṃ gatvā bhūmyā ca sahite api ।। bhūmir āpas tayor vākyaṃ gautamyai kramaśaḥ sphuṭam ।। daridrāyāś ca lakṣmyāś ca vākyaṃ madhyasthavat tadā ।। saṃpraśasya tathā lakṣmīṃ gautamī vākyam abravīt ।।
dhanaśrīś ca yaśaśrīś ca vidyā prajñā sarasvatī ।। siddhis tuṣṭis tathā puṣṭiḥ śāntir āpas tathā mahī ।। dyaur jyotsnā āśiṣaḥ svastir vyāptir māyā uṣā śivā ।। brāhmaṇeṣv atha dhīreṣu kṣamāvatsv atha sādhuṣu ।।
yad yad ramyaṃ sundaraṃ vā tat tal lakṣmīvijṛmbhitam ।। yasmin kasmiṃś ca yat kiṃcid utkṛṣṭaṃ paridṛśyate ।। atremāṃ sundarīṃ devīṃ spardhayantī na lajjase ।। tataḥ prabhṛti gaṅgāmbho daridrāvairakāry abhūt ।।
tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrtham alakṣmīnāśanaṃ śubham ।। devarṣimunijuṣṭānāṃ sarvasiddhipradāyinām ।। tatredaṃ vṛttam ākhyāsye mahāpātakanāśanam ।। tasya bhāryā sthaviṣṭheti rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvi ।।
purodhās tasya nṛpater brahmarṣiḥ śamināṃ prabhuḥ ।। sthite yāme vayaṃ yāmo yāminī cārdhagāminī ।। vikāre smarasaṃjāte jīvātur nalinānanā ।। vihasya cābravīd rājā purodhasam ariṃdamaḥ ।।
kṣaṇavidhvaṃsini sukhe kā nāmāsthā mahātmanām ।। etad ākarṇya matimān madhucchandā vaco abravīt ।। na cedaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ rājan bhūṣaṇaṃ cātimanyatām ।। parīkṣārthaṃ ca tatprema puryāṃ vārttām adīdiśat ।।
hatvā rasātalaṃ yāto rājānaṃ sapurodhasam ।। vārttāṃ śrutvā dūtamukhān madhucchandaḥpriyā punaḥ ।। tasyā vṛttaṃ tu te dṛṣṭvā dūtā rājñe nyavedayan ।। vismito duḥkhito rājā punar dūtān abhāṣata ।।
rakṣantu vārttāṃ kuruta rājāgantā purodhasā ।। iti cintāture rājñi vāg uvācāśarīriṇī ।। sarvābhiṣaṅgaśamanī pāvanī bhuvi gautamī ।। brāhmaṇebhyo dhanaṃ dattvā tarpayitvā pitṝn dvijān ।।
anyatra tīrthe sārtheṣu dānaṃ dehi prayatnataḥ ।। gate tasmin gurau rājā vaiśvāmitre mahātmani ।। ity uktvā sa tu rājendro gaṅgāṃ bhānuṃ surān api ।। tena satyena sā sādhvī mamāyuṣyeṇa jīvatu ।।
tadaiva jīvitā bhāryā rājñas tasya purodhasaḥ ।। pativratāṃ tathā bhāryāṃ mṛtāṃ jīvānvitāṃ punaḥ ।। ātmanaś ca punaḥ kṛtyam asmaran nṛpater guruḥ ।। athaveha tapas tapsye tato niścayavān dvijaḥ ।।
jīvayāmi ca rājānaṃ tato yāmi priyāṃ punaḥ ।। na hy anyaḥ kopi devo asti sarvābhīṣṭaprado raveḥ ।। chandomayāya devāya oṃkārārthāya te namaḥ ।। sthityutpattivināśānāṃ hetave prabhaviṣṇave ।।
tataḥ prasannaḥ sūryo abhūd varayasvety abhāṣata ।। ātmanaś ca śubhān putrān rājñaś caiva śubhān varān ।। tāṃ ca bhāryāṃ varān anyān sarvaṃ kṣemamayaṃ tathā ।। yayau sukhī svakaṃ deśaṃ tat tu tīrthaṃ śubhaṃ smṛtam ।।
tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ bhānutīrtham udāhṛtam ।। mādhucchandasamākhyātaṃ smaraṇāt pāpanun mune ।। mṛtasaṃjīvanaṃ tat syād āyurārogyavardhanam ।। tatra snānena dānena muktibhāgī bhaven naraḥ ।।
pailūṣa iti vikhyātaḥ kavaṣasya suto dvijaḥ ।। na kimapy āsasādāsau tato vairāgyam āsthitaḥ ।। na vairāgyād anyad asti paṇḍitasyāvalambanam ।। kramāgataṃ dhanaṃ nāsti poṣyāś ca bahavo mama ।।
sa kadācid vṛttiyuto vṛttibhiḥ parivartayan ।। sevā niṣiddhā yā kācid gahanā duṣkaraṃ tapaḥ ।। tvayāpakṛtam ajñānāt tasmāt tṛṣṇe namo astu te ।। ity ālocya sa pailūṣaḥ pitaraṃ vākyam abravīt ।।
chedmīmāṃ kena he tāta tam upāyaṃ vada prabho ।। tasmād ārādhayeśānaṃ tato jñānam avāpsyasi ।। prāptajñāno mahābuddhir gāthāḥ provāca muktidāḥ ।। jñānakhaḍgena taṃ chittvā paramaṃ sukham āpnuyāt ।।
chittvaitāṃ jñānakhaḍgena sukhaṃ tiṣṭhati mānavaḥ ।। asaṅgasyātmano hy asya saṅgo ayaṃ paramo ripuḥ ।। saṃśayaḥ paramo nāśo dharmārthānāṃ vināśakṛt ।। pūrṇāhantāsinā chittvā jīvan muktim avāpnuyāt ।।
jñānakhaḍgena nirmohas tato muktim avāpa saḥ ।। jñānatīrthaṃ ca kavaṣaṃ pailūṣaṃ sarvakāmadam ।। aśeṣapāpatāpaugha- harāṇīṣṭapradāni ca ।। tasya prabhāvaṃ vakṣyāmi bhraṣṭarājyapradāyakam ।।
anvārebhe atha sattrāṇi ṛtvigbhir munibhir vṛtaḥ ।। evaṃ sattre tu saṃpūrṇa iṣṭiṃ māheśvarīṃ punaḥ ।। indrasya bhavanaṃ ramyaṃ svargalokaṃ rasātalam ।। sa kadācid divaṃ gatvā indralokam agāt punaḥ ।।
śṛṇvānaṃ madhuraṃ gītam apsarobhiś ca vījitam ।। kṣemas te bhavitā satyaṃ nānyathā munisattama ।। karomy eva mahābhāgāḥ satyenāgniṃ samālabhe ।। evam uktvā sa daiteyāṃs tvaṣṭāraṃ punar abravīt ।।
saṃharasva punaḥ śīghraṃ rakṣa māṃ brāhmaṇaṃ munim ।। sarvam akramam āyātaṃ na sukhāya manīṣiṇām ।। daityāś ca jagmuḥ svasthānaṃ kṛtvā deśam akaṇṭakam ।। ātreyo api tadā śiṣyaiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ saha bhāryayā ।।
vartamāne mahāyajñe lajjito vākyam abravīt ।। kiṃ mahendrapadaṃ labdhaṃ kiṃ mayātra purā kṛtam ।। evaṃ vadantam ātreyaṃ lajjitaṃ prābruvan surāḥ ।। ātreyatīrthe ye snānaṃ prāṇinaḥ kuryur añjasā ।।
tatra pañca sahasrāṇi tīrthāny āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ।। teṣu snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvam akṣayapuṇyadam ।। ity uktvā vibudhā yātāḥ saṃtuṣṭaś cābhavan muniḥ ।। tatra nārada vakṣyāmi kathāṃ puṇyām anuttamām ।।
krūraś cāpi prasannaś ca tapovrataparāyaṇaḥ ।। tam āgatya mahātmānaṃ vāmadevādayo abruvan ।। kapilaṃ siddham ācāryam ūcur munigaṇās tadā ।। gate vede gate dharme kiṃ kartavyaṃ munīśvara ।।
tato abravīn munir dhyātvā kapilas tv āgatān munīn ।। venasyorur vimathyo abhūt tataḥ kaścid bhaviṣyati ।। tatrotpanno mahāpāpaḥ kṛṣṇo raudraparākramaḥ ।। niṣādaḥ so abhavat tasmān niṣādāś cābhavaṃs tataḥ ।।
tataḥ pṛthusvaraś caiva sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitaḥ ।। tam āgatya surāḥ sarve abhinandya varāñ śubhān ।। tato abruvan munigaṇās taṃ pṛthuṃ kapilena ca ।। āhāraṃ dehi jīvebhyo bhuvā grastauṣadhīr api ।।
tataḥ sa dhanur ādāya bhuvam āha nṛpottamaḥ ।। oṣadhīr dehi yā grastāḥ prajānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। tam uvāca mahī bhītā pṛthuṃ taṃ pṛthulocanam ।। mayi jīrṇā mahauṣadhyaḥ kathaṃ dātum ahaṃ kṣamā ।।
tataḥ sakopo nṛpatis tām āha pṛthivīṃ punaḥ ।। no ced dadāsy adya tvāṃ vai hatvā dāsye mahauṣadhīḥ ।। vinā mayā kathaṃ cemāḥ prajāḥ saṃdhārayiṣyasi ।। na doṣas tatra pṛthivi tapasā dhāraye prajāḥ ।।
munayas tadvadhaṃ prāhur aśvamedhaśatādhikam ।। mahīṃ ca mātaraṃ devīm ūcuḥ suragaṇās tadā ।। prajāsaṃrakṣaṇaṃ ca syāt tataḥ kṣemaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। dudoha ca mahauṣadhyo rājā venakarodbhavaḥ ।।
mahīṃ gorūpam āpannāṃ narmadāyāṃ mahāmune ।। mahānadīṣu sarvāsu duduhe asau payo mahat ।। gautamyā saṃgatā cābhūt tad adbhutam ivābhavat ।। tatrāṣṭāśītiḥ pūjyāni sahasrāṇi mahāmate ।।
pāvanāni jagaty asmiṃs tāni sarvāṇy anukramāt ।। tasya prabhāvaṃ vakṣyāmi śṛṇu yatnena nārada ।। pravṛtte vā siṃhiketi vikhyātā daityasundarī ।। amṛte tu samutpanne saiṃhikeye ca bhedite ।।
pitaraṃ ghātitaṃ śrutvā tapas tepe atiduḥkhitaḥ ।। devāś ca ṛṣayaḥ sarve tam ūcur atibhītavat ।। śivagaṅgāprasādena kiṃ nāmāsty atra durlabham ।। tasyāpi mama cātyantaṃ prītiś ca kriyate yadi ।।
prārthayante bhavantaś cet pūrṇās tan me manorathāḥ ।। taṃ cāpi meghahāsaṃ te cakrū rākṣasapuṃgavam ।। punaś cāha surān daityo mama khyātir yathā bhavet ।। tathety uktvā dadur devāḥ sarvam eva manogatam ।।
devā yato abhavan sarve tatra sthāne mahāmate ।। yatra deveśvaro devo devatīrthaṃ tataḥ smṛtam ।। teṣu snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca mahāpātakanāśanam ।। tasya prabhāvaṃ vakṣyāmi sarvasiddhikaraṃ nṛṇām ।।
diśo vijitya sarvāś ca somalokam ajīgamat ।। mantraṃ dāsye nivartasva somayuddhād daśānana ।। śivasya rākṣasendrāya prādāṃ nārada śāntaye ।। śaraṇaṃ śiva evātra saṃsāre anyo na kaścana ।।
tasya svarūpaṃ vakṣyāmi śṛṇu pāpavināśanam ।। teṣu tuṣṭeṣu sa prāha putrā yūyaṃ bhaviṣyatha ।। tathā putratvam āpus te brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ।। dattaḥ somo atha durvāsāḥ putrās tasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
tasmād aṅgirase prādād ātreyīm atirociṣam ।। ātreyy api ca śuśrūṣāṃ kurvatī sarvadābhavat ।। aṅgirāḥ paruṣaṃ vādīd ātreyīṃ nityam eva ca ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭā dīnā prābravīc chvaśuraṃ gurum ।।
śuśrūṣaṇaparā nityaṃ putrāṇāṃ bhartur eva ca ।। praśādhi māṃ surajyeṣṭha bhartāraṃ mama daivatam ।। yathā śānto bhaved bhadre tathā nītir vidhīyatām ।। tadā tvaṃ jalarūpeṇa plāvayethā madājñayā ।।
bhartari pratikūlānāṃ yoṣitāṃ jīvanena kim ।। iccheyaṃ śāntivākyāni bhartāraṃ labhate tathā ।। tava bhartur ahaṃ dhāma nityaṃ ca janako mataḥ ।। iti buddhyā viniścitya mā viṣaṇṇā bhava snuṣe ।।
āgneyaṃ rūpam āpannam ambhasāplāvayat patim ।। śāntarūpadharau cobhau daṃpatī saṃbabhūvatuḥ ।। rohiṇyā ca yathā candras tathābhūn mithunaṃ tadā ।। paruṣṇī ceti vikhyātā gaṅgayā saṃgatā nadī ।।
tatra cāṅgirasāś cakrur yajñāṃś ca bahudakṣiṇān ।। ubhayos tīrayos tāta pṛthag yāgaphalaṃ viduḥ ।। viśeṣatas tu gaṅgāyāḥ paruṣṇyā saha saṃgame ।। snānadānādibhiḥ puṇyaṃ yat tad vaktuṃ na śakyate ।।
sarvakratuphalaṃ puṇyam aghaughavinivāraṇam ।। mārkaṇḍeyo bharadvājo vasiṣṭho atriś ca gautamaḥ ।। ete śāstrapraṇetāro vedavedāṅgapāragāḥ ।। mithaḥ samūcur vidvāṃso muktiṃ prati yathāmati ।।
evaṃ vivadamānās te mām ūcur ubhayaṃ matam ।। tasya cāpi mataṃ jñātvā ṛṣayas te mahaujasaḥ ।। gaṅgāyāṃ ca bhavaṃ pūjya tam evārthaṃ śaśaṃsire ।। kriyārūpaṃ ca taj jñānaṃ kriyā saiva tad ucyate ।।
karmaiva viśvatovyāpi tadṛte nāsti kiṃcana ।। sarvaṃ karmaiva nākarmī prāṇī kvāpy atra vidyate ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ yatra saṃvādo yatra devo maheśvaraḥ ।। mārkaṇḍaṃ mukhyataḥ kṛtvā tato mārkaṇḍam ucyate ।।
pitṝṇāṃ pāvanaṃ puṇyaṃ smaraṇād api sarvadā ।। vedena cāpi tat proktam ṛṣayo menire ca tat ।। sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ tadvṛttam ucyate mayā ।। tasya bhāryādvayaṃ cāsīt kulalakṣaṇabhūṣitam ।।
śarmiṣṭheti dvitīyā sā sutā syād vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ ।। yayāter abhavad bhāryā sā tu śukraprasādataḥ ।। devayānī śukrasutā dvau putrau samajījanat ।। śarmiṣṭhā ca nṛpāl lebhe trīn putrān devasaṃnibhān ।।
devayānyāḥ sutau brahman sadṛśau śukrarūpataḥ ।। devayānī kadācit tu pitaraṃ prāha duḥkhitā ।। mama dāsyāḥ sabhāgyāyā apatyatritayaṃ pitaḥ ।। mānabhaṅgād varaṃ tāta maraṇaṃ hi manasvinām ।।
kupito abhyāyayau śīghraṃ yayātim idam abravīt ।। rūponmattena rājendra tasmād vṛddho bhaviṣyasi ।। spṛhayan manasaivāste niḥśvāsocchvāsanaṣṭadhīḥ ।। tasmāc chīghraṃ prayāhi tvaṃ jarāṃ bhūpātidurdharām ।।
kṛtāñjalipuṭo rājā yayātiḥ śukram abravīt ।। adharmakāriṇaḥ pāpāḥ śāsyā eva mahātmanām ।। devayānī dvijaśreṣṭha vṛthā māṃ vakti kiṃcana ।। tadā na doṣo mūrkhāṇāṃ dveṣāgnipluṣṭacetasām ।।
asakṛd vipriyaṃ tasya divā rātrau pracaṇḍayā ।। gatakopo aham ity uktvā kāvyo rājānam abravīt ।। śāpasyemaṃ kariṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvānugrahaṃ nṛpa ।। tasya sā yātv iyaṃ rājañ jarā putrāya madvarāt ।।
punar yayātiḥ śvaśuraṃ śukraṃ prāha vinītavat ।। sa rājā syād daityaguro tad etad anumanyatām ।। taṃ śapeyam anujñātra dātavyaiva tvayā guro ।। tato yayātiḥ svaṃ putram āhūyedaṃ vaco abravīt ।।
putrī tenaiva janako yas tadājñāvaśe sthitaḥ ।। yayātiś ca yaduṃ śaptvā turvasuṃ kāmam abravīt ।। taṃ śaptvā cābravīd druhyuṃ gṛhāṇemāṃ jarāṃ mama ।। anum apy abravīd rājā gṛhāṇemāṃ jarāṃ mama ।।
abhinandya tadā pūrur jarāṃ tāṃ jagṛhe pituḥ ।। yauvane yāni bhogyāni vastūni vividhāni ca ।। tato harṣāt samāhūya pūruṃ putram athābravīt ।। gṛhāṇa yauvanaṃ putra jarāṃ me dehi kaśmalām ।।
vikārās tāta bhāvānāṃ durnivārāḥ śarīriṇām ।। sā ced gurūpakārāya gṛhītā tyajyate katham ।। athavā tu jarāṃ rājaṃs tapasā nāśayāmy aham ।। gautamyā dakṣiṇe pāre tatas tepe tapo mahat ।।
kiṃ dadāmīti taṃ prāha pūruṃ sa surasattamaḥ ।। madbhrātṝñ śāpato muktān kuruṣva surapūjita ।। anāśayaj jagannātho bhrātṝṃś cakre viśāpinaḥ ।। akālajajarādīnāṃ smaraṇād api nāśanam ।।
yāyātaṃ nāhuṣaṃ pauraṃ śaukraṃ śārmiṣṭham eva ca ।। śataṃ vidyān mahābuddhe sarvasiddhikaraṃ tathā ।। sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ bhuktimuktipradaṃ bhavet ।। tīre ca dakṣiṇe puṇyaṃ smaraṇāt subhago bhavet ।।
strī satī saṃgame tasminn ṛtusnātā ca nārada ।। snānadānena vartantī nānyathā madvaco bhavet ।। tatredaṃ kāraṇaṃ vakṣye śṛṇu nārada yatnataḥ ।। tapasyantaṃ gādhisutaṃ brāhmaṇyārthe yatavratam ।।
taṃ gatvā tapaso bhraṣṭaṃ kuru bhadre mamājñayā ।। kṛtvā kanyāṃ tathā dattvā jagāmendrapuraṃ punaḥ ।। taṃ tu deśaṃ parityajya tīrthaṃ tu suravallabham ।। tapasyantaṃ tadovāca punar indraḥ sahasradṛk ।।
naivety ūcur bhayatrastāḥ punar āha śacīpatiḥ ।। te ūcatur ubhe devaṃ sahasrākṣaṃ puraṃdaram ।। cyāvayāvo nṛtyagītai rūpayauvanasaṃpadā ।। nityaṃ vasati pañceṣus tābhiḥ ko atra na jīyate ।।
dadṛśāte tapasyantaṃ viśvāmitraṃ mahāmunim ।। sahasram ekaṃ varṣāṇām īkṣituṃ na ca śaknutaḥ ।। vilokya muniśārdūlas tataḥ kopākulo abhavat ।। nispṛho api mahābāhus tam indraṃ prahasann iva ।।
śaśāpa te sa gādheyo dravarūpe bhaviṣyathaḥ ।। tataḥ prasāditas tābhyāṃ śāpamokṣaṃ cakāra saḥ ।। tacchāpāt te nadīrūpe tatkṣaṇāt saṃbabhūvatuḥ ।। tābhyāṃ parasparaṃ cāpi tābhyāṃ gaṅgāsusaṃgamaḥ ।।
tatrāste dṛṣṭa evāsau sarvasiddhipradāyakaḥ ।। tatra snātvā tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā mucyate sarvabandhanāt ।। yasyānusmaraṇād eva sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। koṭidvayaṃ tatra pūrṇaṃ tīrthānāṃ śubhadāyinām ।।
kaṇvasya tu suto jyeṣṭho bāhlīka iti viśrutaḥ ।। iṣṭīḥ pārvāyaṇānīr yāḥ sabhāryo vedapāragaḥ ।। prātaḥkāle sabhāryo asau juhvad agnau samāhitaḥ ।। ekāhutiṃ sa hutvā tu samiddhe havyavāhane ।।
etasminn antare vahnir upaśānto abhavat tadā ।। antar vicārayām āsa viṣādaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ ।। agnyantaram upādeyaṃ vaidikaṃ laukikaṃ tathā ।। evaṃ mīmāṃsamāne tu daivī vāg abravīt tadā ।।
yāni tatra bhaviṣyanti śakalāni samīpataḥ ।। nety uvāca tadā kāṇvaḥ saiva vāg abravīt punaḥ ।। putre dattaṃ priyāyaiva pituḥ prītyai bhaviṣyati ।। daivī vāg abravīd evaṃ tataḥ sarve maharṣayaḥ ।।
etaj jñātvā jagaty atra putre dattaṃ pitur bhavet ।। tathā nānyena kenāpi jagaty etad dhi viśrutam ।। tasmin datte bhavet puṇyaṃ sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ suta ।। punar apy āha sā vāṇī kāṇve asmiṃs tīrtha uttame ।।
lokatrayāśrayāśeṣa- tīrthebhyo api mahāphalam ।। phalaṃ prāpsyasy aśeṣeṇa sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ mune ।। sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ vidyāt koṭitīrthaṃ tato viduḥ ।। vāṇīsaṃjñaṃ koṭitīrthaṃ koṭitīrthaphalaṃ yataḥ ।।
vācaspatiprabhṛtibhir athavānyaiḥ surair api ।। godāvaryāḥ prasādena sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet ।। tasya tīrthasya māhātmyād gokoṭiphalam aśnute ।। śraddhāyuktena manasā syāt tatkoṭiguṇottaram ।।
atraikanyūnapañcāśat tīrthāni munayo viduḥ ।। tasyānubhāvaṃ vakṣyāmi sarvarakṣāvidhāyakam ।। tapasā vikrameṇāpi devānām aparājitaḥ ।। āvirbhūya sabhāstambhād viśvātmatvaṃ pradarśayan ।।
sarvān hatvā mahādaityān krameṇājau mahāmṛgaḥ ।। tatra jitvā bhuvaṃ gatvā daityān hatvā nagasthitān ।। nānārūpadharān daityān nijaghāna mṛgākṛtiḥ ।। vajrapātādhikanakhaḥ samuddhūtamahāsaṭaḥ ।।
mahānādair vīkṣitaiś ca pralayānalasaṃnibhaiḥ ।। evaṃ hatvā bahuvidhān gautamīm agamad dhariḥ ।। tatrāmbarya iti khyāto daṇḍakādhipate ripuḥ ।। tenābhavan mahāraudraṃ bhīṣaṇaṃ lomaharṣaṇam ।।
nijaghāna hariḥ śrīmāṃs taṃ ripuṃ hy uttare taṭe ।। snānadānādikaṃ tatra sarvapāpagrahārdanam ।। yathā surāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ na kopi hariṇā samaḥ ।। tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā kuryān nṛharipūjanam ।।
ityādy aṣṭau mune tatra mahātīrthāni nārada ।। aśraddhayāpi yannāmni smṛte sarvāghasaṃkṣayaḥ ।। tat tīrthasevāsaṃjātaṃ phalaṃ kair iha varṇyate ।। tathā nṛsiṃhatīrthena samaṃ tīrthaṃ na kutracit ।।
piśācatvāt purā vipro muktim āpa mahāmate ।। kuṭumbabhāraduḥkhārto durbhikṣeṇa tu pīḍitaḥ ।। vikrītavān kṣatriyāya vadhāya bahulair dhanaiḥ ।। śamitṛtve dhanaṃ cāpi jagṛhe bahulaṃ muniḥ ।।
tato apratisamādheya- mahāroganipīḍitaḥ ।। bhogād ṛte na kṣayo asti prāktanānām ihāṃhasām ।। tataḥ piśāco hy abhavad dāruṇo dāruṇākṛtiḥ ।। grīṣme grīṣmadavavyāpte kṣipyate yamakiṃkaraiḥ ।।
narakān na nivartante yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam ।। saṃghāte pacyamāno asau rurodoccaiḥ kṛtaṃ smaran ।। śuśrāva rudato vāṇīṃ piśācasya muhur muhuḥ ।। pāpinaḥ putravikretur brahmahantuḥ pituś ca tām ।।
jīgartir abravīd duḥkhāc chunaḥśepapitā hy aham ।। ye ye duṣkṛtakarmāṇas teṣāṃ teṣām iyaṃ gatiḥ ।। tīrthānāṃ munijuṣṭānāṃ smaraṇād apy abhīṣṭadam ।। gaṅgāyā uttare pāre tīrthaṃ trailokyaviśrutam ।।
vedadvīpaś ca tatraiva darśanād vedavid bhavet ।। ko na moham upāyāti vilokya madirekṣaṇām ।। ānagnadarśanāt kṛtvā tasyāḥ kālāvadhiṃ nṛpaḥ ।। suptāyāṃ śayane tasyāṃ samuttasthau purūravāḥ ।।
vidyuccañcalacittānāṃ kva sthairyaṃ nanu yoṣitām ।। etasminn antare rājā yuddhāyāgād ripūn prati ।। sa cāgatya mahārājo vasiṣṭhāc ca purodhasaḥ ।। na juhoti na cāśnāti na śṛṇoti na paśyati ।।
bodhayām āsa vākyaiś ca hetubhūtaiḥ purohitaḥ ।। evaṃ sthitaṃ tu mā tvāṃ vai aśivāḥ spṛśyur āśugāḥ ।। śālāvṛkāṇāṃ yādṝṃśi tasmāt tvaṃ bhūpa mā śucaḥ ।। vañcakatvaṃ nṛśaṃsatvaṃ cañcalatvaṃ kuśīlatā ।।
kālena ko na nihataḥ ko arthī gauravam āgataḥ ।। svapnamāyopamā rājan madaviplutacetasaḥ ।। duḥkhināṃ śaraṇaṃ nānyad vidyate bhuvanatraye ।। gautamyā madhyasaṃstho asāv ailaḥ paramadhārmikaḥ ।।
brahmāṇaṃ bhāskaraṃ gaṅgāṃ devān anyāṃś ca yatnataḥ ।। sa kālavaśago jantuḥ kāṃ daśām anuyāsyati ।। parāṃ śraddhām upagataḥ saṃsārāsthāparāṅmukhaḥ ।। vedadvīpo abhavat tena yajñadvīpaḥ sa ucyate ।।
tasya dīpasya yaḥ kuryāt pradakṣiṇam atho naraḥ ।। vedānāṃ smaraṇaṃ tatra yajñānāṃ smaraṇaṃ tathā ।। ailatīrthaṃ tu taj jñeyaṃ tad eva ca purūravam ।। aile rājñi na kiṃcit syān nimnaṃ sarveṣu karmasu ।।
tac cāpi bheditaṃ nimnaṃ vasiṣṭhena ca gaṅgayā ।। tatra sapta śatāny āhus tīrthāni guṇavanti ca ।। snānaṃ kṛtvā nimnabhede yaḥ paśyati surān imān ।। sarvonnatim avāpyāsau modate divi śakravat ।।
tasya prabhāvaṃ vakṣyāmi śṛṇu yatnena nārada ।। sarvān vedāṃś ca vidhivad dhanurvedaṃ yathāvidhi ।। bṛhaspatis tadā prāha candraṃ śiṣyaṃ mudānvitaḥ ।। mama priyā tu jānīte tārā ratisamaprabhā ।।
tārāṃ tārāmukhīṃ dṛṣṭvā jagṛhe tāṃ kareṇa saḥ ।। tāvad dhairyanidhir jñānī matimān vijitendriyaḥ ।। viśeṣato rahaḥsaṃsthāṃ kāminīm āyatekṣaṇām ।। ata evānyapuruṣa- darśanaṃ na kadācana ।।
vijñāya tat parijanāt sahasotthāya nirgataḥ ।। śaśāpa kopāc cākṣipya vāgbhir vipriyakāribhiḥ ।। yuyudhe tena jīvo api devaś candramasā ruṣā ।। bṛhaspatipraṇītaiś ca na mantrair hanyate śaśī ।।
bubhuje bahuvarṣāṇi rohiṇīṃ cākutobhayaḥ ।। na rājabhir na ṛṣibhir na sāmnā bhedadaṇḍanaiḥ ।। sarvopāyakṣaye jīvas tadā nītim athāsmarat ।। svārtham uddharate prājñaḥ svārthabhraṃśo hi mūrkhatā ।।
vṛthābhimāninaḥ śīghraṃ vipadyante vimohitāḥ ।। tam āgataṃ kavir jñātvā saṃmānenābhyanandayat ।। paryapṛcchad daityagurus tadāgamanakāraṇam ।। tasmai sa vistareṇāha bhāryāharaṇam āditaḥ ।।
atikramam imaṃ śrutvā kopāt kavir athābravīt ।। yadānaye priyāṃ bhrātas tava bhāryāṃ parārditām ।। paścād bhokṣye mahābāho śṛṇu vācaṃ graheśvara ।। śivam ārādhya yatnena paraṃ sāmarthyam āptavān ।।
śivaprasādāt kiṃ nāma dehinām iha durlabham ।। vartate taṃ śaśāpoccaiḥ śṛṇu tvaṃ candra me vacaḥ ।। kuṣṭhī bhūyās tataś candraṃ śaśāpaivaṃ ruṣā kaviḥ ।। prāpuḥ kṣayaṃ na ke nāma gurusvāmisakhidruhaḥ ।।
śukro api devān āhūya ṛṣīn pitṛgaṇāṃs tathā ।। tataḥ saṃpraṣṭum ārebhe tārāvṛttaviniṣkrayam ।। snānaṃ karotu jīvena tārā pūtā bhaviṣyati ।। sarvāsv api daśāsv eha śaraṇaṃ gautamī nṛṇām ।।
puṣpavṛṣṭir abhūt tatra jayaśabdo vyavartata ।। rājānaḥ satyaṃ kṛṇvānā brahmajāyāṃ punar daduḥ ।। sarvaṃ kṣemam abhūt tatra tasmāt tīrthaṃ mahāmune ।। paramānandam āpanno gurur gaṅgām abhāṣata ।।
viśeṣatas tu siṃhasthe mayi trailokyapāvanī ।। tvāṃ snātuṃ tāni yāsyanti mayi siṃhasthite ambike ।। saubhāgyaiśvaryajananaṃ tīrtham ānandanāmakam ।। smaraṇāt paṭhanād vāpi iṣṭaiḥ saṃyujyate sadā ।।
ānandam api tat tīrthaṃ sarvānandavivardhanāt ।। aśeṣajagadantastho bhūtātmā saccidākṛtiḥ ।। sūryavaṃśakaraḥ śrīmān kṣatriyāṇāṃ dhuraṃdharaḥ ।। tisraḥ koṭyo ardhakoṭiś ca varṣāṇāṃ rājya āsthitaḥ ।।
bhaveyaṃ priyayā vāpi putrair vā priyavastubhiḥ ।। vivekināṃ kulīnānām idam evocitaṃ nṛṇām ।। tasmin praśāsati mahīṃ na viyogaḥ priyaiḥ kvacit ।। tasmiñ śāsati rājyaṃ tu na ca kaścid viyujyate ।।
tataḥ prasanno bhagavān varaṃ prādād yathepsitam ।। putraṃ dehīti rājā vai bhavaṃ prāha sa bhāryayā ।। tataḥ paśyati rājendre bhavasyākṣi tu mānada ।। yenākāri stutiḥ puṇyā mahimna iti viśrutā ।।
yaṃ nityam anuvartante haribrahmādayaḥ surāḥ ।। mahāpāpamahāroga- mahāvyasanināṃ nṛṇām ।। prādāj jyaiṣṭhyaṃ bhavaś cāpi bhāvatīrthaṃ tad ucyate ।। bhavaprasādād abhavat sutaḥ prācīnabarhiṣaḥ ।।
tatra saptati tīrthāni puṇyāny akhiladāni ca ।। yasya smaraṇamātreṇa sukhī saṃpadyate naraḥ ।। laṅkāṃ dagdhvā ripūn hatvā rāvaṇādīn raṇe śaraiḥ ।। paśyatsu lokapāleṣu tasyācārye puraḥ sthite ।।
ehi vaidehi śuddhāsi aṅkam āroḍhum arhasi ।। ayodhyāyāṃ tu vaidehi sārdhaṃ yāmaḥ suhṛjjanaiḥ ।। laukikeṣv api paśyatsu tataḥ śuddhā nṛpātmajā ।। asyāś caritraviṣaye saṃdehaḥ kasya jāyate ।।
tayor vākyam anādṛtya lakṣmaṇaḥ savibhīṣaṇaḥ ।। svastīty uktā devatābhī rājño aṅkaṃ cāruroha sā ।। ayodhyāṃ nagarīṃ prāpya tathā rājyaṃ svakaṃ tu yat ।। tataḥ katipayāheṣu anāryebhyo virūpikām ।।
mithyāpavādam api hi na sahante kulonnatāḥ ।। tatyāja lakṣmaṇaḥ sītām aduṣṭāṃ rudatīṃ rudan ।। tataḥ katipayāheṣu vyatīteṣu nṛpātmajaḥ ।। tatraivājagmatur ubhau rāmaputrau yaśasvinau ।।
rāmāyaṇaṃ samagraṃ tad gandharvāv iva susvarau ।। yajñavāṭaṃ rājasutau hetubhir lakṣitau tadā ।। tāv ānīya tataḥ putrāv abhiṣicya yathākramam ।। saṃsāraduḥkhakhinnānām agatīnāṃ śarīriṇām ।।
muhur āliṅgya tau putrau muhuḥ svajati cumbati ।। etasminn antare prāptā rākṣasā laṅkavāsinaḥ ।। anye ca vānarāḥ sarve vibhīṣaṇapuraḥsarāḥ ।। sītām adṛṣṭvā hanumān aṅgadaḥ kanakāṅgadaḥ ।।
rāmeṇa sā parityaktā ity ūcur dvārapālakāḥ ।। agnau śuddhigatāṃ sītāṃ kiṃ tu rājā niraṅkuśaḥ ।। mariṣyāva iti hy uktvā gautamīṃ punar īyatuḥ ।। āgatya gautamīṃ tatra akurvaṃs te paramaṃ tapaḥ ।।
saṃsārāsthāvirahitā gautamīsevanotsukāḥ ।। prāptaḥ snātvā ca gautamyāṃ śivārādhanatatparaḥ ।। yatra cāsīt sa vṛttāntaḥ sahasrakuṇḍam ucyate ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sahasraphaladāyakam ।।
sarvāpattārakaṃ homam akārayad aghāntakam ।। sarvān apekṣitān kāmān avāpāsau mahātapāḥ ।। sahasrakuṇḍābhidhaṃ tad abhūt tīrthaṃ mahāphalam ।। tad evādityam ākhyātaṃ saiṃhikeyaṃ tad ucyate ।।
ayājayann aṅgiraso dakṣiṇāṃ te bhuvaṃ daduḥ ।। sā bhūmiḥ saiṃhikī bhūtvā janān sarvān abhakṣayat ।। vibhītā jñānato jñātvā bhuvaṃ tāṃ saiṃhikīm iti ।। bhuvaṃ gṛhṇantu yā dattā nety ādityās tadābruvan ।।
svadattāṃ paradattāṃ vā yo hareta vasuṃdharām ।। bhūmeḥ svaparadattāyā haraṇān nādhikaṃ kvacit ।। evaṃ yadā svadattāyā haraṇe kiṃ tadā bhavet ।। tathety ukte tu te devāḥ kapilāṃ śubhalakṣaṇām ।।
bhuktimuktipradaḥ sākṣād viṣṇus tiṣṭhati mūrtimān ।। tatrābhavad dānatoyād āpagā kapilābhidhā ।। lokarakṣāṃ cakārāsau kṛtvā vinimayaṃ muniḥ ।। puṇyadaṃ tatra tīrthānāṃ śatam uktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।।
saṃgatā gaṅgayā tac ca kapilāsaṃgamaṃ viduḥ ।। tatra snātvā ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā mucyate bhavabandhanāt ।। purā kṛtayugasyādau brahmaṇaḥ sāmagāyinaḥ ।। brahmāṇaṃ khādituṃ prāptā balonmattā dhṛtāyudhāḥ ।।
sa viṣṇus tāni rakṣāṃsi hantuṃ cakreṇa codyataḥ ।। niṣkaṇṭakaṃ talaṃ kṛtvā svargaṃ nirvairam eva ca ।। tato rakṣāṃsi sarvāṇi hy anīnaśur aśeṣataḥ ।। śaṅkhatīrthaṃ tu tat proktaṃ sarvakṣemakaraṃ nṛṇām ।।
āyurārogyajananaṃ lakṣmīputrapravardhanam ।। tīrthānām ayutaṃ tatra sarvapāpanudaṃ mune ।। yeṣāṃ prabhāvaṃ jānāti vaktuṃ devo maheśvaraḥ ।। pāpakṣayapratinidhir naitebhyo asty aparaḥ kvacit ।।
sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ yatra saṃnihito bhavaḥ ।। purā dāśarathī rāmo rāvaṇaṃ lokarāvaṇam ।। saputraṃ sabalaṃ hatvā sītām ādāya śatruhā ।। vibhīṣaṇena balinā devaiḥ pratyāgato nṛpaḥ ।।
yad āsīd dhanarājasya kāmagenāśugāminā ।। rāmo virāmaḥ śatrūṇāṃ śaraṇyaḥ śaraṇārthinām ।। manonayanasaṃtāpa- nivāraṇaparāyaṇām ।। harīn sarvān athāmantrya hanumatpramukhān mune ।।
sarvapāpavinirmuktas tato yātas triviṣṭapam ।। nātaḥ parataraṃ kiṃcit pāvanaṃ sarvasiddhidam ।। antaṃ jijñāsavas te vai pṛthivyā jagmur ojasā ।। naiva te api samāyātā ye gatās te gatā gatāḥ ।।
vedavedāṅgatattvajñāḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradāḥ ।। tapase niścitāḥ sarve naiva pṛṣṭvā tu mātaram ।। tadā nārada kopena sā śaśāpa tadātmajān ।। sarvair api prakārais tan na teṣāṃ siddhim eṣyati ।।
vighnam anveti tān sarvān itaś cetaś ca dhāvataḥ ।। pramadābhiḥ kvacic cāpi kvāpi taddehadoṣataḥ ।। agastyaṃ tapatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ kumbhayoniṃ jagadgurum ।। dakṣiṇāśāpatiṃ śāntaṃ vinītāḥ praṣṭum udyatāḥ ।।
nānāvidhair apy upāyaiḥ kurvatāṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। upāyaṃ brūhi viprendra jyeṣṭho asi tapasā dhruvam ।। śānto asi yamināṃ nityaṃ dayāvān priyakṛt tathā ।। asatyavādinaḥ krūrā na te tattvaṃ vijānate ।।
agastyaḥ prāha tān sarvān kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।। na paryāptaṃ tapaś cābhūt smaradhvaṃ smayakāraṇam ।। ye gatāḥ punar anveṣṭuṃ te ca tv āṅgiraso abhavan ।। prajāpater apy adhikā bhavitāro na saṃśayaḥ ।।
nopāyo anyo asti saṃsāre vinā gaṅgāṃ śivapriyām ।। na siddhiḥ kvāpi keṣāṃcid vinā sadguruṇā yataḥ ।। brahmā viṣṇur maheśo vā ādityo vāpi candramāḥ ।। agastyaḥ punar apy āha jñānadaḥ śrūyatām ayam ।।
yaś ca sūryaḥ sa vai viṣṇur yaś ca viṣṇuḥ sa bhāskaraḥ ।। yasya sarvaṃ tu taj jñānaṃ jñānadaḥ so atra kīrtyate ।। guravaḥ santi bahavas teṣāṃ jñānaprado mahān ।। vadanti bahudhā viprā bhrāntopakṛtihetave ।।
jagmuḥ pañcottarāṃ gaṅgāṃ pañca jagmuś ca dakṣiṇām ।। āsaneṣu viśeṣeṇa hy āsīnās tattvacintakāḥ ।। sraṣṭṛtvaṃ tu yugādau yat kalpitaṃ viśvayoninā ।। lokānām upakārārthaṃ dharmakāmārthasiddhaye ।।
sraṣṭṛtvaṃ jagatām iṣṭaṃ tādṛgrūpā bhaviṣyatha ।। yadā hy adharmo bhavitā vedānāṃ ca parābhavaḥ ।। yadā yadā tu dharmasya glānir vedasya dṛśyate ।। teṣāṃ yat tapasaḥ sthānaṃ gaṅgāyās tīram uttamam ।।
agnir āpaḥ sarvam iti tatra saṃnihitaṃ sadā ।। tattadākāratāṃ prāptaṃ paraṃ brahmaiva kevalam ।। viśeṣatas tatra tīrthe sarvaprāṇyanukampayā ।। dharmavyāsās tu te jñeyā vedavyāsās tathaiva ca ।।
sarvasiddhipradaṃ puṃsāṃ vyāsatīrtham anuttamam ।। ṛṣibhiḥ sevitaṃ nityaṃ siddhai rājarṣibhis tathā ।। kadācic cintayām āsa rahaḥ sthitvā viniśvasan ।। nānyasevā kṛtā yais tu na yeṣāṃ vyasanāgamaḥ ।।
svadehaprabhavo dhanyā dhig dhig anyavaśe sthitān ।। paryapṛcchad ameyātmā vainateyo atha mātaram ।। dāsītvam āptā vada tat- kāraṇaṃ mama pṛcchataḥ ।। sābravīt putram ātmīyam aruṇasyānujaṃ priyam ।।
yasyā vākyaṃ viparyeti sā dāsī syān mayoditam ।। kadrvā mamābhavad vādaś chadmanāhaṃ tayā jitā ।। yadā dāsī tu jātāhaṃ dāso abhūs tvaṃ dvijanmaja ।। na kiṃcid ūce jananīṃ cintayan bhavitavyatām ।।
ātmano bhūtim icchantī vinatāṃ khagamātaram ।। aho lokatraye apy asmin dhanyāsi bata dāsy api ।। svaduḥkhaṃ gūhamānā sā kadrūṃ prāha suvismitā ।। tava putrās tu kim iti raviṃ draṣṭuṃ na yānti ca ।।
samudrasya samīpe tu tad āste śītalaṃ saraḥ ।। tataḥ provāca muditā vainateyasya mātaram ।। punaḥ prāha sarpamātā garuḍaṃ vinayānvitam ।। haṇḍe tvaṃ naya putrān me sūryamaṇḍalam anvaham ।।
sā vepamānā vinatā dīnā kadrūm abhāṣata ।। dṛṣṭvā dinakaraṃ devaṃ punar eva prayāntu te ।। namaskartum athecchanti nāgāḥ svāmitvam āgatāḥ ।। tathety uktvā sa garuḍo mām ārohantu pannagāḥ ।।
te dahyamānās tīkṣṇena bhānutāpena vivyathuḥ ।। yāmas tvayā vā garuḍa vihāya tvām athāpi vā ।। ity uktvā gaganaṃ śīghraṃ jagāmādityasaṃmukhaḥ ।। bahavaḥ śatasāhasrāḥ pīḍitā dagdhavigrahāḥ ।।
āśvāsituṃ samāyātā tān sā kadrūḥ suvihvalā ।। kṛtavān atidurmedhā yeṣāṃ śāntir na vidyate ।। sa kāśyapo bṛhattejā yady atra syād anāmayam ।। kadrvās tad vacanaṃ śrutvā vinatā hy atibhītavat ।।
putram āha mahātmānaṃ garuḍaṃ vihagādhipam ।। vartituṃ yuktam ity uktaṃ vaiparītyaṃ na yujyate ।। śrotriye cāntyaje vāpi samaṃ candraḥ prakāśate ।। prasahya kartuṃ ye sākṣād aśaktāḥ puruṣādhamāḥ ।।
vinatā ca tataḥ prāha kadrūṃ tāṃ sarpamātaram ।। jarayā tu gṛhītās te vada śāntiṃ karomi tat ।। tenābhiṣecitānāṃ me putrāṇāṃ śāntir eṣyati ।। tataḥ provāca garuḍo maghavānaṃ śatakratum ।।
meghāś cāpy atra varṣantu trailokyasyopakāriṇaḥ ।। rasātalabhavaṃ gāṅgaṃ nāgasaṃjīvanaṃ payaḥ ।। yatrābhiṣecitā nāgās tan nāgālayam ucyate ।। tad gāṅgaṃ vāri sarveṣāṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।।
rasātalabhavaṃ gāṅgaṃ nāgasaṃjīvanaṃ yataḥ ।। sākṣād amṛtasaṃvāhā vañjarā sābhavan nadī ।। rasātalabhavā gaṅgā martyalokabhavā tu yā ।। yasyānusmaraṇād eva nāśaṃ yānty aghasaṃcayāḥ ।।
sapādaṃ tatra tīrthānāṃ lakṣam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ।। yadanusmaraṇenāpi vipadyante vipattayaḥ ।। bhuktimuktipradaṃ nṝṇāṃ pitṝṇāṃ tṛptikārakam ।। devānām asurāṇāṃ ca spardhābhūd dhanahetave ।।
karmabhūmim avaṣṭabhya asurāḥ sarvato abhavan ।। tataḥ suragaṇāḥ sarve yajñabhāgair vinā kṛtāḥ ।। mayā coktāḥ suragaṇā yuddhe jitvāsurān balāt ।। tathety uktvā gatā devā bhūmiṃ te samarārthinaḥ ।।
ekībhūtvā yayus te api jayino yuddhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। ete cānye ca bahavo yoddhāro baladarpitāḥ ।। maruto lokapālāś ca nānāyuddhaviśāradāḥ ।। akurvanta mahāyatnaṃ dakṣiṇārṇavasaṃsthitāḥ ।।
tadvanena yayuḥ sarve taiḥ sārdhaṃ dakṣiṇārṇavam ।। malayasyāpi deśo asau devārīṇām abhūt tadā ।। iti teṣāṃ samāyogo devānām abhavat kila ।। gautamyāḥ saridambāyāḥ puline vimalāśayāḥ ।।
abhayaṃ cintayām āsus te sarve atha parasparam ।। sapatnair abhibhūtānāṃ jīvitaṃ dhiṅ manasvinām ।। etasminn antare putra vāg uvācāśarīriṇī ।। bhaktyā hariharau tatra samārādhayateśvarau ।।
godāvaryās tayoś caiva prasādāt kiṃ tu duṣkaram ।। avāpya sarvato jagmuḥ pālayanto divaukasaḥ ।। devāgamaṃ praśaṃsanti munayas tattvadarśinaḥ ।। tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ devapriyam ato viduḥ ।।
tīrthaṃ sarveṣu lokeṣu bhuktimuktipradāyakam ।। vindhyasya dakṣiṇe pārśve sahyo nāma mahāgiriḥ ।। yatrābhavat tad virajam ekavīrā ca yatra sā ।। tasmin girau puṇyadeśe śṛṇu nārada yatnataḥ ।।
yan na jānanti munayo devāś ca pitaro asurāḥ ।। paraḥ sa puruṣo jñeyo hy avyakto akṣara eva tu ।। nirākārāt sāvayavaḥ puruṣaḥ samajāyata ।। tābhyām abjaṃ samudbhūtaṃ tatrāham abhavaṃ mune ।।
ete mattaḥ pūrvatarā ekadaivābhavan mune ।। naiva vedās tadā cāsan nāhaṃ draṣṭāsmi kiṃcana ।। tūṣṇīṃ sthite mayi tadā aśrauṣaṃ vācam uttamām ।। brahman kuru jagatsṛṣṭiṃ sthāvarasya carasya ca ।।
kathaṃ srakṣye kva vā srakṣye kena srakṣya idaṃ jagat ।। viṣṇunā preritā mātā jagadīśā jaganmayī ।। yajño vai viṣṇur ity eṣā śrutir brahman sanātanī ।। kiṃ yajvanām asādhyaṃ syād iha loke paratra ca ।।
yajñaḥ kāryo mahābhāge tataḥ sovāca māṃ prati ।। karmabhūmau yajasveha yajñeśaṃ yajñapūruṣam ।। yajñaḥ svāhā svadhā mantrā brāhmaṇā havirādikam ।। harir evākhilaṃ tena sarvaṃ viṣṇor avāpyate ।।
tadā nārada naivāsīd bhāgīrathy atha narmadā ।। sā śaktiḥ punar apy evaṃ mām uvāca punaḥ punaḥ ।। sarvasya sarvakāle tu karmabhūmiḥ śubhodayā ।। tato mām abravīt saiva viṣṇor vāṇy aśarīriṇī ।।
saṃkalpaṃ kuru yajñasya sa te yajñaḥ samāpyate ।। yad vadanty akhilā vedā vidhe tat tat samācara ।। svato mukhe mama prāyād abhūc ca smṛtigocaram ।। tataḥ puruṣasūktaṃ tad asmaraṃ lokaviśrutam ।।
taduktena prakāreṇa yajñapātrāṇy akalpayam ।। dīkṣito vipradeśo asau mannāmnā tu prakīrtitaḥ ।। caturaśītiparyantaṃ yojanāni mahāmune ।। tatra madhye vedikā syād gārhapatyo asya dakṣiṇe ।।
