vinā patnyā na sidhyeta yajñaḥ śrutinidarśanāt ।। pūrvārdhena tataḥ patnī mamābhūd yajñasiddhaye ।। kālaṃ vasantam utkṛṣṭam ājyarūpeṇa nārada ।। ṛtuṃ ca prāvṛṣaṃ putra tadā barhir akalpayam ।।
kalākāṣṭhānimeṣā hi samitpātrakuśāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। yūparūpeṇa devarṣe yoktraṃ ca paśubandhanam ।। tato aham abravaṃ vācaṃ vaiṣṇavīm aśarīriṇīm ।। tato mām avadad devī saiva nityāśarīriṇī ।।
pauruṣeṇātha sūktena stuhi taṃ puruṣaṃ param ।। mama cotpādake bhaktyā sūktena puruṣasya hi ।। tadā vijñāya puruṣaṃ janakaṃ mama cāvyayam ।। barhisthitam ahaṃ praukṣaṃ puruṣaṃ jātam agrataḥ ।।
brāhmaṇās tu mukhāt tasya abhavan bāhvoś ca kṣatriyāḥ ।। diśaḥ śrotrāt tathā śīrṣṇaḥ sarvaḥ svargo abhavat tadā ।। antarikṣaṃ tathā nābher ūrubhyāṃ viśa eva ca ।। ṛṣayo romakūpebhya oṣadhyaḥ keśato abhavan ।।
kṛmikīṭapataṃgādi pāyūpasthād ajāyata ।। etasminn antare saiva viṣṇor vāg abravīc ca mām ।। idānīṃ juhudhi hy agnau pātrāṇi ca samāni ca ।। ṛtvigrūpaṃ yajñarūpam uddeśyaṃ dhyeyam eva ca ।।
sruvaṃ ca puruṣaṃ pāśān sarvaṃ brahman visarjaya ।। gārhapatye dakṣiṇāgnau tathā caiva mahāmune ।। tatra tatra jagadyonim anusaṃdhāya pūruṣam ।। lokanātho viśvakartā kuṇḍānāṃ tatra saṃnidhau ।।
śyāmo viṣṇur dakṣiṇāgneḥ pīto gṛhapateḥ kaveḥ ।। na tena rahitaṃ kiṃcid viṣṇunā viśvayoninā ।। praṇītodakam apy etat praṇīteti nadī śubhā ।। mārjane kriyamāṇe tu praṇītodakabindavaḥ ।।
saṃjātā muniśārdūla snānāt kratuphalapradā ।। sopānapaṅktiḥ sarveṣāṃ vaikuṇṭhārohaṇāya sā ।। kuśatarpaṇam ākhyātaṃ bahupuṇyaphalapradam ।। paścāc ca saṃgatā tatra gautamī kāraṇāntarāt ।।
kuśatarpaṇadeśe tu tat tīrthaṃ kuśatarpaṇam ।। visṛṣṭo lokapūjyo asau viṣṇor āsīt samāśrayaḥ ।। nityaś ca kālarūpo asau smaraṇāt kratupuṇyadaḥ ।। saṃpūrṇe tu kratau viṣṇur mayā bhaktyā prasāditaḥ ।।
yasmāc ca mama cotpattir yasyedaṃ vikṛtaṃ jagat ।। yojanāni caturviṃśan maddevayajanaṃ śubham ।। yajñeśvarasvarūpāṇi viṣṇor vai cakrapāṇinaḥ ।। tatrasthaḥ kṛmikīṭādiḥ so apy ante muktibhājanam ।।
viśeṣād gautamīśliṣṭo deśaḥ puṇyatamo abhavat ।। snānadānādi yaḥ kuryāt sa gacchet paramaṃ padam ।। sarvakāmapradaṃ puṃsāṃ bhuktimuktipradaṃ viduḥ ।। ṣaḍaśītisahasrāṇi teṣu puṇyaṃ puroditam ।।
nānena sadṛśaṃ tīrthaṃ vidyate sacarācare ।। tīrtham etan mune proktaṃ svargadvāraṃ mahītale ।। sarvakāmapradaṃ nṝṇāṃ smaraṇād aghanāśanam ।। devānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca saṃgaro abhūn mithaḥ purā ।।
parāṅmukhāḥ suragaṇāḥ saṃgarād gatacetasaḥ ।। tān ahaṃ pratyavocaṃ vai gaṅgāṃ gacchata sarvaśaḥ ।। anapāyanirāyāsa- sahajānandasundaram ।। tathety uktvā suragaṇāḥ stuvanti sma maheśvaram ।।
asnāpayaṃś ca kecic ca apūjayaṃś ca tathāpare ।। devān athābravīt tuṣṭo vriyatāṃ yad abhīpsitam ।। puruṣaṃ paramaślāghyaṃ raṇeṣu purataḥ sthitam ।। tathety uvāca bhagavān devān prati maheśvaraḥ ।।
manyunāmānam atyugraṃ devasainyapurogamam ।। manyunā saha cābhyetya punar yuddhāya tasthire ।। vibudhā jātasaṃnaddhā manyum ūcuḥ puraḥ sthitāḥ ।। tasmād darśaya cātmānaṃ manyo asmākaṃ yuyutsatām ।।
tad devavacanaṃ śrutvā manyur āha smayann iva ।। yaḥ sarvaṃ vetti sarveṣāṃ dhāmanāma manaḥsthitam ।। amūrtaṃ mūrtam apy etad vetti kartā jaganmayaḥ ।। kas tasya rūpaṃ yo veda kasya kartā jaganmayaḥ ।।
athavā draṣṭukāmā vai bhavanto mānupaśyata ।। tārtīyacakṣuṣodbhūtaṃ bhavasya parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। pauruṣaṃ puruṣeṣv eva ahaṃkāraś ca jantuṣu ।। taṃ śaṃkarapratinidhiṃ jvalantaṃ nijatejasā ।।
vitresur daityadanujāḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ surāḥ ।। tvayā dattam idaṃ rājyaṃ manyo bhokṣyāmahe vayam ।। tvam indras tvaṃ ca varuṇo lokapālās tvam eva ca ।। manyuḥ provāca tān sarvān vinā matto na kiṃcana ।।
sa eva bhagavān manyus tato jātaḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।। sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ caiva sarvaṃ vyāptaṃ hi manyunā ।। jayo manyuś ca śauryaṃ ca īśatejaḥsamudbhavam ।। yathāgataṃ yayuḥ sarve manyunā parirakṣitāḥ ।।
manyum āpur jayaṃ caiva manyutīrthaṃ tad ucyate ।। vijayo jāyate tasya na kaiścit paribhūyate ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca smaraṇaṃ sarvakāmadam ।। bhuktimuktipradaṃ nṝṇāṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।।
tatremaṃ śṛṇu vṛttāntaṃ vistareṇātha nārada ।। śubhro nāma giriśreṣṭho gautamyā dakṣiṇe taṭe ।। tasmiñ śubhre puṇyagirau tapas tepe hy anuttamam ।। sarve bhūtagaṇā nityaṃ praṇamanti stuvanti tam ।।
ṛṣigandharvasumanaḥ- sevite tatra parvate ।। yajñadveṣī brahmahantā paraśur nāma rākṣasaḥ ।। kṣaṇaṃ ca brahmarūpeṇa kadācid vyāghrarūpadhṛk ।। kadācit pramadārūpaḥ kadācin mṛgarūpataḥ ।।
yatrāste brāhmaṇo vidvāñ śākalyo munisattamaḥ ।। śuciṣmantaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ paraśur nityam eva ca ।। sa kadācid dvijaśreṣṭho devān abhyarcya yatnataḥ ।। kanyām ādāya kāṃcic ca śākalyaṃ vākyam abravīt ।।
ātithyakāle saṃprāptaṃ kṛtakṛtyo asi mānada ।। pūrṇābhilāṣā niryānti jīvanto api mṛtāḥ pare ।। atithibhyas tu yo dadyād dattā tena vasuṃdharā ।। āsane copaveśyāthā- jñānāt taṃ paraśuṃ dvijam ।।
āpośanaṃ kare kṛtvā paraśur vākyam abravīt ।। tasmiṃs tṛpte tu tṛptāḥ syur atṛpte tu viparyayaḥ ।। apavādī haret pāpam atithiḥ svargasaṃkramaḥ ।। tatkṣaṇād eva naśyanti tasya dharmayaśaḥśriyaḥ ।।
dāsyase yadi me kāmaṃ tad bhokṣye ahaṃ na cānyathā ।। tataḥ provāca paraśur ahaṃ rākṣasasattamaḥ ।। bahūni me vyatītāni varṣāṇi tvāṃ prapaśyataḥ ।। tasmān neṣye sānugaṃ tvāṃ bhakṣayiṣye dvijottama ।।
śrutvā paraśuvākyaṃ tac chākalyo vākyam abravīt ।। tat pratiśrutam abhyeti na jātv atra viparyayam ।। nihantum apy udyateṣu vaktavyaṃ hitam uttamaiḥ ।। pādau rakṣatu me viṣṇuḥ śiro devo janārdanaḥ ।।
hṛdayaṃ rakṣatāt kṛṣṇo hy aṅgulī rakṣatān mṛgaḥ ।। nānāpatsv ekaśaraṇaṃ devo nārāyaṇaḥ svayam ।। māṃ rākṣasendra paraśo tvam idānīm atandritaḥ ।। nāsty eva hṛdaye nūnaṃ pāpināṃ karuṇākaṇaḥ ।।
brāhmaṇaṃ taṃ nirīkṣyaivaṃ paraśur vākyam abravīt ।। sahasrapādaśirasaṃ sahasrākṣakaraṃ vibhum ।। tvām adya vipra paśyāmi nāsti te pūrvakaṃ vapuḥ ।। jñānaṃ dehi mahābuddhe tīrthaṃ brūhy aghaniṣkṛtim ।।
dveṣād ajñānato vāpi prasaṅgād vā pramādataḥ ।। ayasaḥ sparśasaṃsparśo rukmatvāyaiva jāyate ।। śākalyaḥ kṛpayā prāha varadā sā sarasvatī ।। manorathaphalaprāptau nānyan nārāyaṇastuteḥ ।।
prasannā tava sā devī madvākyāc ca bhaviṣyati ।। snātvā śucir yatamanā gaṅgām abhimukhaḥ sthitaḥ ।। sarasvatīṃ jagaddhātrīṃ śākalyavacane sthitām ।। tām uvāca vinītātmā paraśur gatakalmaṣaḥ ।।
tava prasādāt sā śaktir yathā me syāt tathā kuru ।। sarasvatyāḥ prasādena paraśus taṃ janārdanam ।। varaṃ prādād rākṣasāya kṛpāsindhur janārdanaḥ ।। yad yan manogataṃ rakṣas tat tat sarvaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
sarasvatyāḥ prasādena narasiṃhaprasādataḥ ।। sarvatīrthāṅghripadmasya prasādāc chārṅgadhanvanaḥ ।। tatra snānena dānena viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। bahūny abhūvaṃs tīrthāni tasmin vai śvetaparvate ।।
sarvacintāpraharaṇaṃ sarvaśāntikaraṃ nṛṇām ।। gaṅgāyā uttare pāre yatra devo gadādharaḥ ।। sadā vasati tatraiva māṃsāśī śvetaparvate ।। sevite dvijamukhyaiś ca gautamyā copaśobhite ।।
tatsamīpe nagaḥ kaścid dvipadāṃ ca catuṣpadām ।। evaṃ guṇānvite śaile nānāmunigaṇāvṛte ।। kṣatradharmarataḥ śrīmān devabrāhmaṇapālakaḥ ।। reme strībhir manojñābhir nṛtyavāditrajaiḥ sukhaiḥ ।।
evaṃ bhraman kadācit sa śrānto drumam upāgataḥ ।। āśramāṇāṃ gṛhapatiṃ dharmajñam iva sevitam ।। sa viśrānto janavṛta īkṣāṃ cakre nagottamam ।। cintāviṣṭaṃ tathā śrāntaṃ tam apṛcchan nṛpottamaḥ ।।
naivātra kaścid duḥkhārtaḥ kasmāt tvaṃ duḥkham āgataḥ ।। samāśvastamanāḥ pakṣī cicciko niḥśvasan muhuḥ ।। nānāpuṣpaphalākīrṇaṃ munibhiḥ parisevitam ।। nidrāṃ prāpnomi na kvāpi na viśrāntiṃ na nirvṛtim ।।
dvimukhasya dvijasyoktaṃ śrutvā rājātivismitaḥ ।। ekenāsyena tṛpyanti prāṇino atra nagottame ।। kiṃ vā te duṣkṛtaṃ prāptam iha janmany atho purā ।। tat sarvaṃ śaṃsa me satyaṃ trāsye tvāṃ mahato bhayāt ।।
rājānaṃ taṃ dvijaḥ prāha niḥśvasann atha ciccikaḥ ।। ahaṃ dvijātipravaro vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।। vade puras tathā pṛṣṭhe anyad anyac ca jantuṣu ।। kṛtaghnaḥ satyarahitaḥ paranindāvicakṣaṇaḥ ।।
manasā karmaṇā vācā tāpayāmi janān bahūn ।। yugmabhedaṃ gaṇocchedaṃ maryādābhedanaṃ sadā ।। na mayā sadṛśaḥ kaścit pātakī bhavanatraye ।। tasmād duḥkhena saṃtaptaḥ śūnyo ayaṃ parvato mama ।।
brahmahatyāsamaṃ pāpaṃ tad vinā tad avāpyate ।। palāyantaṃ nyastaśastraṃ viśvastaṃ ca parāṅmukham ।। taṃ yadi kṣatriyo hanyāt sa tu syād brahmaghātakaḥ ।। anādaraṃ ca guruṣu tam āhur brahmaghātakam ।।
anyad dhṛdi vacasy anyat karoty anyat sadaiva yaḥ ।। mithyā vinītaḥ pāpātmā sa tu syād brahmaghātakaḥ ।। etān nindati yo dveṣāt sa tu syād brahmaghātakaḥ ।। sadvṛtta iva varte ahaṃ tasmād rājan dvijo abhavam ।।
tenāhaṃ karmaṇā rājan svataḥ smartā purā kṛtam ।। karmaṇā kena te muktir ity āha nṛpatir dvijam ।। iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā nṛpatiṃ prāha pakṣirāṭ ।। gadādharaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ tatra māṃ naya suvrata ।।
sarvakāmapradaṃ ceti mahadbhir munibhiḥ śrutam ।। sarvabhāvena tat tīrthaṃ paśyeyam iti me matiḥ ।। katham ākāṅkṣitaprāptir bhaved duṣkṛtakarmaṇām ।। tasmāt tava prasādāc ca paśyeyaṃ hi gadādharam ।।
yasmin dṛṣṭe bhavakleśā na dṛśyante punar naraiḥ ।। dṛṣṭvaiva taṃ divaṃ yāsye prasādāt tava suvrata ।। darśayām āsa taṃ devaṃ tāṃ ca gaṅgāṃ dvijanmane ।। tataḥ sa ciccikaḥ snātvā gaṅgāṃ trailokyapāvanīm ।।
na paśyaty ucyate tāvad ihāmutrāpi pātakī ।। tvāṃ vinā viṣṇucaraṇa- saroruhasamudbhave ।। snānaṃ cakre smarann antar gaṅge trāyasva mām iti ।। pavamānābhyanujñātas tadaiva divam ākramat ।।
tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ pāvamānaṃ saciccikam ।। koṭikoṭiguṇaṃ karma kṛtaṃ tatra bhaven nṛṇām ।। sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ mahāśāntipradāyakam ।। chāyāpi bhāryā savitus tasyāḥ putraḥ śanaiścaraḥ ।।
tāṃ kanyāṃ savitā kasmai dadāmīti matiṃ dadhe ।। evaṃ tu vartamāne sā pitaraṃ prāha duḥkhitā ।। sa kṛtārtho bhavel loke na ced duṣkṛtavān pitā ।। tāvad vivāhaḥ kanyāyāḥ pitrā kāryaḥ prayatnataḥ ।।
udārāya sanāthāya kanyā deyā varāya vai ।। dharmasya sādhanaṃ kanyā viduṣām api bhāskara ।। ekataḥ pṛthivī kṛtsnā saśailavanakānanā ।। vikrīṇīte yaś ca kanyām aśvaṃ vā gāṃ tilān api ।।
vivāhātikramaḥ kāryo na kanyāyāḥ kadācana ।। yāval lajjāṃ na jānāti yāvat krīḍati pāṃśubhiḥ ।। pituḥ svarūpaṃ putraḥ syād yaḥ pitā putra eva saḥ ।। yat kanyāyāṃ pitā kuryād dānaṃ pūjanam īkṣaṇam ।।
yad dattaṃ tāsu kanyāsu tad ānantyāya kalpate ।। karoti yaḥ kanyakānāṃ sa saṃpadbhājanaṃ bhavet ।। evaṃ tāṃ vādinīṃ kanyāṃ viṣṭiṃ provāca bhāskaraḥ ।। kulaṃ rūpaṃ vayo vittaṃ vidyāṃ vṛttaṃ suśīlatām ।।
kiṃ karomi kva dāsyāmi vṛthā māṃ dhik karoṣi kim ।। evam uktvā punas tāṃ ca viṣṭiṃ provāca bhāskaraḥ ।। dīyase adya mayā viṣṭe anujānīhi māṃ tataḥ ।। āyū rūpaṃ ca saṃprītir jāyate prāktanānugam ।।
phalaṃ tadanurodhena prāpyate api bhavāntare ।। tādṛg eva phalaṃ tu syād yādṛg ācaritaṃ purā ।। karoti śeṣaṃ daivena yad bhāvyaṃ tad bhaviṣyati ।। viśvarūpāya tāṃ prādād viṣṭiṃ lokabhayaṃkarīm ।।
evaṃ mithaḥ saṃcaratoḥ śīlarūpasamānayoḥ ।। gaṇḍo nāmābhavat putro hy atigaṇḍas tathaiva ca ।। tebhyaḥ kanīyān abhavad dharṣaṇo nāma puṇyabhāk ।। sa kadācid yamagṛhaṃ draṣṭuṃ mātulam abhyagāt ।।
sa mātulaṃ tu papraccha natvā dharmaṃ sanātanam ।। ka ime sukhinas tāta pacyante narake ca ke ।। tatkarmaṇāṃ gatiṃ sarvām aśeṣeṇa nyavedayat ।। na te paśyanti nirayaṃ kadācid api mānavāḥ ।।
vihitātikramaṃ kuryur ye te narakagāminaḥ ।। sa tu śrutvā dharmavākyaṃ harṣaṇaḥ punar abravīt ।। bhrātaraś ca mahātmāno yena te śāntabuddhayaḥ ।। tan me karma vadasvādya tatkartāsmi surottama ।।
harṣaṇaṃ śuddhabuddhiṃ taṃ harṣaṇo asi na saṃśayaḥ ।। eka eva sutaḥ kaścid yena tad dhriyate kulam ।। yaḥ pūrvajān uddharati sa putras tv itaro gadaḥ ।। tasmāt tvaṃ gautamīṃ gaccha snātvā niyatamānasaḥ ।।
sa tu prīto yadi bhavet sarvam iṣṭaṃ pradāsyati ।। śucis tuṣṭāva deveśaṃ hariṃ prīto abhavad dhariḥ ।। sarvābhadrapraśamana- pūrvakaṃ bhadram astu te ।। tataḥ prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ bhadratīrthaṃ tad ucyate ।।
maṅgalaikanidhiḥ sākṣād devadevo janārdanaḥ ।। tasya śravaṇamātreṇa kṛtakṛtyo bhaven naraḥ ।। saṃpātiś ca jaṭāyuś ca saṃbhavetāṃ tadanvaye ।। tadanvaye saṃbhūtaḥ ca saṃpātiḥ patagottamaḥ ।।
anyonyaspardhayā yuktāv unmattau svabalena tau ।। yāvat sūryasya sāmīpyaṃ prāptau tau vihagottamau ।। bāndhavau patitau dṛṣṭvā niśceṣṭau gatacetasau ।। āśvāsayaitau tigmāṃśo yāvan naitau mariṣyataḥ ।।
garuḍo api tayoḥ śrutvā avasthāṃ saha viṣṇunā ।। sarva eva tadā jagmur gaṅgāṃ tāpāpanuttaye ।। sūryo viṣṇus tat prayayau tat tīrthaṃ bahupuṇyadam ।। svayaṃ sūryas tathā viṣṇuḥ suparṇenāruṇena ca ।।
trayāṇām api devānāṃ sthites tat tīrtham uttamam ।। ādhivyādhivinirmuktaḥ sa paraṃ saukhyam āpnuyāt ।। tasyākhyānaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu vismayakārakam ।। tasya putrā mahāprājñā guṇarūpadayānvitāḥ ।।
āsandiva iti khyātaḥ sarvajñāno mahāmatiḥ ।। etasminn antare rātrau suptaṃ taṃ dvijaputrakam ।। āsandivaṃ krūrarūpā rākṣasī kāmarūpiṇī ।। śrīgirer uttare pāre bahubrāhmaṇasevitam ।।
tatra rājā bṛhatkīrtiḥ sarvakṣatraguṇānvitaḥ ।। vṛddhā tathāpi cārvaṅgī divyālaṃkārabhūṣaṇā ।। evaṃ vadantī sarvatra yāti vakti karoti ca ।। tāṃ ca vṛddhāṃ guṇopetām asya māteti menire ।।
rākṣasīṃ tāṃ puraskṛtya prādāt tasmai dvijātaye ।। sa dvijo api guṇair yuktāṃ patnīṃ dṛṣṭvā suduḥkhitaḥ ।। kiṃ karomi kva gacchāmi kasyaitat kathayāmi vā ।। enām apy aśubhākasmād bhakṣayiṣyati rākṣasī ।।
vṛddhāpy atidurādharṣā sā gatā kutracit tadā ।। bhartāraṃ duḥkhitaṃ jñātvā patiṃ prāha rahaḥ śanaiḥ ।। kasmāt te duḥkham āpannaṃ svāmiṃs tattvaṃ vadasva me ।। kim akathyaṃ priye mitre kulīnāyāṃ ca yoṣiti ।।
bhartṛvākyaṃ niśamyedaṃ provāca vadatāṃ varā ।। kuto bhayaṃ hy ātmavatāṃ kiṃ punar gautamītaṭe ।। atra snātvā śucir bhūtvā stuhi devam anāmayam ।। tuṣṭāva gautamītīre dvijo nārāyaṇaṃ tathā ।।
nārāyaṇo api tāṃ pāpāṃ nijaghāna sa rākṣasīm ।। tasmai prādād varān iṣṭān prāpayac ca guruṃ prabhuḥ ।। snānadānena pūjādyair yatra sidhyati vāñchitam ।। aindraṃ yāmyaṃ tathāgneyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।।
hayamedhena puṇyena yaṣṭum ārabdhavān surān ।। kṣatriye yajamāne tu yajñabhūmiḥ kathaṃ bhavet ।। bhūpatau dīkṣite dātā ko bhavet ko nu yācate ।। kenāpy ato na kāryaiva kṣatriyeṇa viśeṣataḥ ।।
tatra prāha mahāprājño vasiṣṭho dharmavittamaḥ ।। dehi me deva savitar yajanaṃ devatocitam ।। yācitaḥ savitā rājñā devānāṃ yajanaṃ śubham ।। dadāty eva tato rājan prārthayeśaṃ divākaram ।।
śraddhayā prārthayām āsa harīśājātmakaṃ ravim ।। devānāṃ yajanaṃ dehi savitas te namo astu te ।। savitā devadeveśo dadāmīty abhyabhāṣata ।। tathā vājimakhe sattre brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ ।।
devānāṃ yajanaṃ dātuṃ bhānutīrthaṃ tad ucyate ।। daityāś ca danujāś caiva tathānye yajñaghātakāḥ ।। te api tatra mahāprājñāḥ prāviśann anivāritāḥ ।। somapānaṃ havis tyāgam ṛtvijo bhūpatiṃ tathā ।।
teṣāṃ ceṣṭāṃ na jānanti viśvarūpaṃ vinā mune ।। tat putravacanaṃ śrutvā tvaṣṭā prāha surān idam ।। ye nindanti makhaṃ puṇyaṃ camasaṃ somam eva ca ।। mayā tv apahatāḥ sarva ity uktvā pariṣiñcata ।।
bhasmībhūtās tataḥ sarve kāṃdiśīkās tato abhavan ।। tataḥ kṣīṇāyuṣo daityāḥ prātiṣṭhan kupitās tataḥ ।। tvāṣṭraṃ tīrthaṃ tad ākhyātaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।। kāladaṇḍena cakreṇa kālapāśena manyunā ।।
yatrābhavat kratuḥ pūrṇo hutvāgnau cāmṛtaṃ bahu ।। yatrābhavad dhavyavāhas tṛptas tasya hy abhiṣṭutaḥ ।। indro marudbhir nṛpatiṃ prāhedaṃ vacanaṃ śubham ।। sakhā mama priyo nityaṃ bhavitā nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
kuryāt pitṝṇāṃ prītyarthaṃ yamatīrthe viśeṣataḥ ।। bhaktiyuktena vipraiś ca sarvakarmaviśāradaiḥ ।। nṛtyair gītais tathā vādyair amṛtaiḥ pañcasaṃbhavaiḥ ।। dhūpair dīpaiś ca naivedyaiḥ puṣpair gandhaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ ।।
tataḥ prasannau deveśau varān dadatur ojasā ।। māhātmyam asya tīrthasya tathā dadatur uttamam ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sarvakāmapradaṃ viduḥ ।। vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyaḥ śivaviṣṇupuraṃ vrajet ।।
tatra tīrthe mahāpuṇyaṃ tīrthānāṃ śatam atra hi ।। mahādevapadāmbhoja- yugabhaktipradāyakam ।। gaṅgāyā dakṣiṇe tīre śrīgirer uttare taṭe ।। mahādevo liṅgarūpī sadāste sarvakāmadaḥ ।।
tasya bhrātā veda iti sa cāpi paramo ṛṣiḥ ।। nityaṃ pūjayate bhaktyā prāpte madhyaṃdine ravau ।। yāte tasmin dvijavare vyādhaḥ paramadhārmikaḥ ।। aṭitvā vividhān deśān mṛgān hatvā yathāsukham ।।
nyasya māṃsaṃ dhanuṣkoṭyāṃ śrānto vyādhaḥ śivaṃ prabhum ।। gaṅgāṃ gatvā mukhe vāri gṛhītvāgatya taṃ śivam ।। apareṇa ca māṃsāni naivedyārthaṃ ca tanmanāḥ ।। pādenāhatya tāṃ pūjāṃ mukhānītena vāriṇā ।।
kalpayitvā tu tan māṃsaṃ śivo me prīyatām iti ।। tato yāti svakaṃ sthānaṃ māṃsena tu yathāgatam ।। tathāpīśas tutoṣāsya vicitrā hīśvarasthitiḥ ।। bhaktānukampitāṃ śaṃbhor mānātītāṃ tu vetti kaḥ ।।
evaṃ bahutithe kāle yāte vedaś cukopa ha ।। ko nu vidhvaṃsate pāpo mattaḥ sa vadham āpnuyāt ।। sarvasyāpi vadhārho asau śivasya drohakṛn naraḥ ।। kasyeyaṃ pāpaceṣṭā syāt pāpiṣṭhasya durātmanaḥ ।।
kṛtāṃ pūjāṃ sa vidhvasya hy anyāṃ pūjāṃ karoti yaḥ ।। evaṃ saṃcintya medhāvī gopayitvā tanuṃ tadā ।। etasminn antare prāyād vyādho devaṃ yathā purā ।। nityavat pūjayantaṃ tam ādikeśas tadābravīt ।।
na vindāmi sukhaṃ kiṃcit samāśvasihi putraka ।। cukopa vismayāviṣṭo na ca kiṃcid uvāca ha ।। vedaś ca kupito bhūtvā āgatyeśam uvāca ha ।। prāṇihiṃsārataḥ krūro nirdayaḥ sarvajantuṣu ।।
sadānucitakārī cā- nirjitākhilagogaṇaḥ ।। pūjāṃ mantravidhānena karomīśa yatavrataḥ ।। vyādho māṃsena duṣṭena pūjāṃ tava karoty asau ।। śāstim asya kariṣyāmi bhillasya hy apakāriṇaḥ ।।
tasmād ahaṃ mūrdhni śilāṃ pātayeyam asaṃśayam ।। ity uktavati vai vede vihasyeśo abravīd idam ।। śvaḥ pratīkṣasva paścān me śilāṃ pātaya mūrdhani ।। upasaṃhṛtya taṃ kopaṃ śvaḥ karomīty uvāca ha ।।
vedo api nityavat pūjāṃ kurvan paśyati mastake ।। vedaḥ sa vismito bhūtvā kim idaṃ liṅgamūrdhani ।। mṛdbhiś ca gomayenāpi kuśais taṃ gāṅgavāribhiḥ ।। etasminn antare prāyād vyādho vigatakalmaṣaḥ ।।
śaṃkarasyādikeśasya dadṛśe antargatas tadā ।। ātmānaṃ bhedayām āsa śatadhā ca sahasradhā ।। muhur nininda cātmānaṃ mayi jīvaty abhūd idam ।। tataḥ provāca bhagavān vedaṃ vedavidāṃ varam ।।
tvaṃ tu mṛdbhiḥ kuśair vārbhir mūrdhānaṃ spṛṣṭavān asi ।। tasmād asmai varān dāsye paścāt tubhyaṃ dvijottama ।। vyādhaḥ provāca deveśaṃ nirmālyaṃ tava yad bhavet ।। sarvakratuphalaṃ tīrthaṃ smaraṇād eva jāyatām ।।
bhillatīrthaṃ samastāgha- saṃghavicchedakāraṇam ।। vedasyāpi varān prādāc chivo nānāvidhān bahūn ।। yatra yogeśvaro devo gautamyā dakṣiṇe taṭe ।। yatrāsau bhauvano rājā kṣatradharmaparāyaṇaḥ ।।
tatputro gautama iti khyāto vedaviduttamaḥ ।। sakhā tasya vaṇik kaścin maṇikuṇḍala ucyate ।। śrīmaddaridrayor nityaṃ parasparahitaiṣiṇoḥ ।। prāhedaṃ vacanaṃ prītyā rahaḥ sthitvā punaḥ punaḥ ।।
dhanaṃ vinā tat kathaṃ syād aho dhiṅ nirdhanaṃ naram ।। dvijaḥ punar uvācedaṃ maṇikuṇḍalam ojasā ।। utkarṣaprāptir evaiṣāṃ sakhe ślāghyā śarīriṇām ।। paradattārthasaṃtuṣṭāḥ kaṣṭajīvina eva te ।।
yaḥ paitryam abhilipseta na vācāpi tu kuṇḍala ।। sa kṛtārtho bhavel loke paitryaṃ vittaṃ na tu spṛśet ।। taṃ tu putraṃ vijānīyād itaro yonikīṭakaḥ ।। tatheti matvā tadvākyaṃ ratnāny ādāya satvaraḥ ।।
dhanenaitena deśāṃś ca paribhramya yathāsukham ।। satyam eva vaṇig vakti sa tu vipraḥ pratārakaḥ ।। tau parasparam āmantrya mātāpitror ajānatoḥ ।। vaṇigghastasthitaṃ vittaṃ brāhmaṇo hartum icchati ।।
aho pṛthivyāṃ ramyāṇi nagarāṇi sahasraśaḥ ।। manoharās tatra tatra santi kiṃ kriyate mayā ।। bhujyante tās tato nityaṃ saphalaṃ jīvitaṃ hi tat ।। bhokṣye kathaṃ tu tad vittaṃ vaiśyān maddhastam āgatam ।।
maṇikuṇḍalam āhedam adharmād eva jantavaḥ ।। dharmiṣṭhāḥ prāṇino loke dṛśyante duḥkhabhāginaḥ ।। tasmād dharmeṇa kiṃ tena duḥkhaikaphalahetunā ।। yato dharmas tato muktiḥ svadharmaḥ kiṃ vinaśyati ।।
yasya pakṣo bhavej jyāyān sa parārtham avāpnuyāt ।। vedāt tu laukikaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ loke dharmāt sukhaṃ bhavet ।। dharmasya vāpy adharmasya prābalyam anayor bhuvi ।। evaṃ tatrocire kecid ye dharmeṇānuvartinaḥ ।।
saṃparāye dhanaṃ sarvaṃ jitaṃ vipre nyavedayat ।। tatheti cety āha vaiśyo brāhmaṇaḥ punar abravīt ।। mayaiva vijito dharmo yatheṣṭacaraṇātmanā ।। tad brāhmaṇavacaḥ śrutvā vaiśyaḥ sasmita ūcivān ।।
tathaiva tān sakhe manye yeṣāṃ dharmo na vidyate ।। kathaṃ brūṣe dvijaśreṣṭha mayā vijitam ity adaḥ ।। tatheti manyate vaiśyas tau gatvā punar ūcatuḥ ।। ākṣipto brāhmaṇenaivaṃ vaiśyo vacanam abravīt ।।
mātā pitā suhṛd bandhur dharma eva śarīriṇām ।। vimukto vaiśyakas tatra bāhubhyāṃ ca dhanena ca ।। yadṛcchayā muniśreṣṭha mithas tāv ūcatuḥ punaḥ ।। atikopād dvijo vaiśyam ākṣipan punar abravīt ।।
tvam anyathā yadi brūṣa āhariṣye asinā śiraḥ ।। vihasya punar āhedaṃ vaiśyo gautamam añjasā ।। brāhmaṇāṃś ca gurūn devān vedān dharmaṃ janārdanam ।। upekṣaṇīyo durvṛttaḥ pāpātmā dharmadūṣakaḥ ।।
āvayoḥ prāṇayor atra paṇaḥ syād iti vai mune ।। punar apy ūcatur ubhau lokāṃl lokās tathocire ।। taṃ nipātya viśaṃ vipraś cakṣur utpāṭya cābravīt ।। pṛṣṭo asi mitra gacchāmi maivaṃ brūyāḥ kathāntare ।।
hā kaṣṭaṃ me kim abhavad dharmaikamanaso hare ।। gatanetraḥ śucaṃ prāpto dharmam evānusaṃsmaran ।। niśceṣṭo atha nirutsāhaḥ patitaḥ śokasāgare ।। ekādaśyāṃ śuklapakṣe tatrāyāti vibhīṣaṇaḥ ।।
snātvā tu gautamīṃ gaṅgāṃ saputro rākṣasair vṛtaḥ ।। vaibhīṣaṇir iti khyātas tam apaśyad uvāca ha ।। sa tu laṅkeśvaraḥ prāha putraṃ prītyā guṇākaram ।। hanumān iti vikhyātas tenānīto girir mahān ।।
jāte kārye tam ādāya himavantam athāgamat ।। tadānīya mahābuddhī rāmāyākliṣṭakarmaṇe ।। punar giriṃ samādāya āgacchad devaparvatam ।। tataḥ prāpsyaty ayaṃ sarvam apekṣitam udāradhīḥ ।।
apatad gautamītīre yatra yogeśvaro hariḥ ।। parārtiśamanād anyac chreyo na bhuvanatraye ।। vaiśyasya cāpi vai prītyā santaḥ parahite ratāḥ ।। tatspṛṣṭamātra evāsau svakaṃ rūpam avāpnuyāt ।।
tathā cakāra vai samyak kāṣṭhakhaṇḍaṃ nyaveśayat ।। maṇimantrauṣadhīnāṃ hi vīryaṃ ko api na budhyate ।। snātvā tu gautamīṃ gaṅgāṃ tathā yogeśvaraṃ harim ।। paribhraman nṛpapuraṃ mahāpuram iti śrutam ।।
tasya nāsti sutaḥ kaścit putrikā naṣṭalocanā ।। devo vā dānavo vāpi brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo bhavet ।। tasmai deyā iyaṃ putrī yo netre āhariṣyati ।। aharniśam asau vaiśyaḥ śrutvā ghoṣam athābravīt ।।
ahaṃ netre āhariṣye rājaputryā asaṃśayam ।। tatkāṣṭhasparśamātreṇa sanetrābhūn nṛpātmajā ।। vaiśyo rājñe yathāvṛttaṃ nyavedayad aśeṣataḥ ।। divyauṣadhiprabhāvena mama sāmarthyam īdṛśam ।।
etad vaiśyavacaḥ śrutvā vismito abhūn mahīpatiḥ ।। tasmād asmai tu tāṃ kanyāṃ pradāsye rājyapūrvikām ।। vihārārthaṃ gataḥ svairaṃ paraṃ khedam upāgataḥ ।। tam eva satataṃ vipraṃ cintayan vaiśyanandanaḥ ।।
kṛpārdraṃ yan mano nityaṃ teṣām apy ahiteṣu hi ।। tasmiñ śāsati rājyaṃ tu kadācid gautamaṃ dvijam ।। tam ādāya dvijaṃ mitraṃ pūjayām āsa dharmavit ।। snāpayām āsa gaṅgāyāṃ taṃ sarvāghanivṛttaye ।।
vaiśyaiḥ svadeśasaṃbhūtair brāhmaṇasya tu bāndhavaiḥ ।। yajñān iṣṭvā surān pūjya tataḥ svargam upeyivān ।। manaḥprasādajananaṃ sarvadurbhāvanāśanam ।। snānadānamahādeva- vāsudevārcanādibhiḥ ।।
pramatir nāma rājāsīt sārvabhaumaḥ pratāpavān ।। tatrāpaśyat surapatiṃ marudbhiḥ saha nārada ।। taṃ hasantam athālakṣya hariḥ pramatim abravīt ।। diśo jitvā divaṃ prāptaḥ kuru krīḍāṃ mayā saha ।।
tac chrutvā pramater vākyaṃ surarāṇ nṛpam abravīt ।। urvaśy eva paṇo asmākaṃ prāpyā yā nikhilair makhaiḥ ।। urvaśīṃ niṣkṛtiṃ manye tvaṃ rājan kiṃ nu manyase ।। savarma saśaraṃ dharmyaṃ dehi dīvyāmahe vayam ।।
tāṃ jitvā pramatiḥ prāha saṃrambhāt taṃ śatakratum ।। niṣkṛtyai punar anyan me paścād dīvye tvayā vibho ।। dīvye ahaṃ tena nṛpate kareṇāpy avicārayan ।। jitam ity abravīc chakraṃ pramatiḥ prahasaṃs tadā ।।
viśvāvasur iti khyāto gandharvāṇāṃ maheśvaraḥ ।। tathety uktvā sa nṛpatir jitam ity abravīt tadā ।। tau jitvā nṛpatir maurkhyād devendraṃ prāha kaśmalam ।। vada kena prakāreṇa jātā devendratā tava ।।
varteya sarvabhāvena na māṃ dhikkartum arhasi ।। tvaṃ kiṃ vilajjase bhadre gaccha karmakarī bhava ।। citrasena iti khyātaḥ suto viśvāvasor balī ।। rājyena jīvitenāpi madīyena tavāpi ca ।।
dīvyetām abhisaṃrabdhau citraseno ajayat tadā ।। citraseno ajayat sarvam urvaśīmukhyataḥ paṇaiḥ ।। citrasenasya taj jātaṃ yad āsīt pramater dhanam ।। vaiśvāmitraṃ mahāprājñaṃ madhucchandasam ojasā ।।
katham eṣyati svaṃ sthānaṃ kathaṃ pāśair vimokṣyate ।। madhucchandā jagādedaṃ pramater vartanaṃ tadā ।। kaitavair bahudoṣaiś ca bhraṣṭarājyo babhūva ha ।। dyūtamadyāmiṣādīni vyasanāni nṛpātmaja ।।
ekaikam apy anarthāya pāpāya narakāya ca ।। kulīnāḥ kaluṣībhūtāḥ kiṃ punaḥ kitavo janaḥ ।। sa cāpi kitavaḥ pāpo yoṣitaṃ vīkṣya tapyate ।। aho saṃsāracakre asmin mayā tulyo na pātakī ।।
lokadvaye api na sukhī kitavaḥ kopi dṛśyate ।। gatadharmo nirānando grastagarvas tathāṭati ।। kṛṣigorakṣyavāṇijyam api kuryān na kaitavam ।। dharmārthakāmābhijanaiḥ sa vimucyeta pauruṣāt ।।
tasmāt kiṃ kurmahe vatsa yad uktaṃ te vidhīyate ।। vidhātṛvihitaṃ mārgaṃ ko nu vātyeti paṇḍitaḥ ।। etat purodhaso vākyaṃ śrutvā sumatir abravīt ।। kiṃ kṛtvā pramatis tātaḥ punā rājyam avāpnuyāt ।।
punar dhyātvā madhucchandāḥ sumatiṃ cedam abravīt ।। aditiṃ varuṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ tataḥ pāśād vimokṣyate ।। pūjayām āsa śaṃbhuṃ ca tapas tepe yatavrataḥ ।। mocayām āsa devebhyaḥ punā rājyam avāpa saḥ ।।
avāpya vidyāṃ gāndharvīṃ priyaś cāsīc chatakratoḥ ।। tataḥprabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ kaitavaṃ ceti viśrutam ।। pāpapāśavimokṣaṃ tu sarvadurgatināśanam ।। tasya svarūpaṃ vakṣyāmi śṛṇu nārada tanmanāḥ ।।
lokānām upakārārthaṃ prāyāt pūrvārṇavaṃ prati ।। śirasā ca dhṛtā devī śaṃbhunā paramātmanā ।। ānītāṃ martyabhavanaṃ smaraṇād aghanāśanīm ।। yā vandyā jagatām īśā brahmeśādyair namaskṛtā ।।
āgacchantaṃ mahātmānaṃ yo mohān nopatiṣṭhate ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo gaṅgām āhedaṃ saritāṃpatiḥ ।। tan mām evātra viśatu nāhaṃ vakṣyāmi kiṃcana ।। etān apy akhilān anyān bhīmān saṃdhārayāmy aham ।।
mamāśakyaṃ na kimapi vidyate sacarācare ।। sa dharmādiparibhraṣṭo nirayaṃ tu samāpnuyāt ।। kiṃ tu tvaṃ gauraveṇaiṣām atiriktā tatas tv aham ।। naikarūpām ahaṃ śaktaḥ saṃgantuṃ bahudhā yadi ।।
gaṅge sameṣyasi yadi bahudhā tad vicāraye ।। gaṅgā sā gautamī devī kuru caitad vaco mama ।। bhartṛbhiḥ sahitāḥ sarvā ānaya tvaṃ tadā tv aham ।। tathety uktvā saptarṣīṇāṃ bhāryābhir ṛṣibhir vṛtaḥ ।।
sā ceyaṃ gautamī gaṅgā saptadhā sāgaraṃ gatā ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca śravaṇaṃ paṭhanaṃ tathā ।। pāpahānau bhuktimukti- prāptau ca manaso mude ।। niṣedus tapase yatra yatra bhīmeśvaraḥ śivaḥ ।।
śṛṇu yatnena vakṣyāmi sarvakāmapradaṃ śubham ।। vāsiṣṭhī dākṣiṇeyī syād vaiśvāmitrī taduttarā ।। bhāradvājī smṛtā cānyā ātreyī cety athāparā ।। taiḥ sarvair ṛṣibhis tatra yaṣṭum iṣṭair mahātmabhiḥ ।।
etasminn antare tatra devānāṃ prabalo ripuḥ ।। vinayenātha papraccha ṛṣīn sarvān anukramāt ।। yajñair vā tapasā vāpi munayo vaktum arhatha ।। tatra prāha mahābuddhir viśvāmitro mahāmanāḥ ।।
trayāṇāṃ kāraṇānāṃ ca karma prathamakāraṇam ।। upādānaṃ tathā bījaṃ na ca karma vidur budhāḥ ।। bhāvābhāvau phale dṛṣṭau tasmāt karmāśritaṃ phalam ।। kartavyaṃ kriyamāṇasya sādhanaṃ yad yad ucyate ।।
yad yad bhāvayate jantuḥ karma kurvan vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। karoti karma vidhivad vinā bhāvanayā yadi ।। tasmāt tapo vrataṃ dānaṃ japayajñādikāḥ kriyāḥ ।। tasmād bhāvānurūpeṇa karma vai dāsyate phalam ।।
tāmasas tu tathā jñeyaḥ phalaṃ karmānusārataḥ ।। tasmād icchānusāreṇa bhāvaṃ kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। phalaṃ dadāti phalināṃ phale yadi pravartate ।। tad eva copadānādi sattvādiguṇabhedataḥ ।।
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ karma caiva hi kāraṇam ।। svabhāvānuguṇaṃ karma svasyaiveha paratra ca ।। eka eva padārtho asau bhāvair bhedaḥ pradṛśyate ।। yathābhāvaṃ karma kuru yathepsitam avāpsyasi ।।
tapas taptvā bahukālaṃ tāmasaṃ bhāvam āśritaḥ ।। paśyatsu ṛṣimukhyeṣu vāryamāṇo api nityaśaḥ ।। bhīṣaṇe kuṇḍakhāte tu bhīṣaṇe jātavedasi ।। evaṃ tapantam ālakṣya vāg uvācāśarīriṇī ।।
vṛthātmānaṃ viśvarūpo juhuyāj jātavedasi ।। tyaktvātmānaṃ jaṭāmātraṃ hutavān vṛjinodbhavaḥ ।। bhīmasya mahimānaṃ ko jānāti jagadīśituḥ ।। virarāmeti saṃkīrtya sā vāṇy enaṃ munīśvarāḥ ।।
viśvarūpo mahābhīmo bhīmakarmā tathākṛtiḥ ।। tatra snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca muktidaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ sarve stuvanti hariśaṃkarau ।। samudrasya ca gaṅgāyā nityaṃ devau pratiṣṭhitau ।।
nityaṃ saṃnihitas tatra mādhavo ramayā saha ।। lokānām upakārārtham ātmanaḥ kāraṇāntare ।। tatra saṃnihito viṣṇur devaiḥ saha marudgaṇaiḥ ।। somatīrtham iti khyātaṃ yatra someśvaraḥ śivaḥ ।।
prārthitaḥ soma evādāv indrāyendo parisrava ।। devā ādityā ye sapta tebhiḥ somābhirakṣa na ।। arātīvā mā nas tārīn mo ca naḥ kiṃcanāmamad ।। somaṃ namasya rājānaṃ yo jajñe vīrudhāṃ patir ।।
nānādhiyo vasūyavo anu gā iva tasthima ।। tebhyo dattvā tato yajñaḥ pūrṇo jātaḥ śatakratoḥ ।। agnir iṣṭvā mahāyajñair mām ārādhya manīṣitam ।। sthito lokopakārārthaṃ tatra viṣṇuḥ śivas tathā ।।
yatrādityo vedamayo nityam eti upāsitum ।। namaskāryas tatra sadā madhyāhne sakalo janaḥ ।। tasmād ādityam ākhyātaṃ bārhaspatyam anantaram ।। īje ca yajñān vividhān bārhaspatyaṃ tato viduḥ ।।
tasmād apy aparaṃ tīrtham indragope nagottame ।। himālayena tat tīrtham adritīrthaṃ tad ucyate ।। evaṃ sā gautamī gaṅgā brahmādreś ca viniḥsṛtā ।। saṃkṣepeṇa mayoktāni rahasyāni śubhāni ca ।।
api lakṣmīpatir viṣṇur alaṃ someśvaraḥ śivaḥ ।। guṇavanti mahāprājña gautamī tu sadā nṛṇām ।। vaktuṃ śaktas tatas tasyai nama ity eva yujyate ।। brāhmaṇenāhṛtāṃ puṇyāṃ jagataḥ pāvanīṃ śubhām ।।
punaḥ saṃkṣepato brūhi na me tṛptiḥ prajāyate ।। maheśvarajaṭājūṭe sthitā saiva namaskṛtā ।। tataḥ prāptā giriṃ puṇyaṃ tataḥ pūrvārṇavaṃ prati ।। īpsitānāṃ tathā dātrī prabhāvo asyā viśiṣyate ।।
asyāś caiva prabhāveṇa bhāvyaṃ yac ca manaḥsthitam ।। bhaktito vakṣyate nityaṃ yā brahma paramārthataḥ ।। anyatīrthena sādharmyaṃ na yujyeta kathaṃcana ।। iti bhāti vicitraṃ me mune khalu jagattraye ।।
chandāṃsi sarahasyāni purāṇasmṛtayo api ca ।। tīrthānām atha dānānāṃ yajñānāṃ tapasāṃ tathā ।। yad brūṣe bhagavan bhaktyā tathā bhāvyaṃ na cānyathā ।। iṣṭaṃ manogataṃ śrutvā tasmād vismayam āgataḥ ।।
caturvidhāni tīrthāni tāvanty eva yugāni ca ।। vedāś ca smṛtibhir yuktāś catvāras te prakīrtitāḥ ।। guṇā hy api tu catvāraḥ samatveneti nārada ।। sādhyasādhanabhāvena sa eva bahudhā mataḥ ।।
kālāśrayaś ca yo dharmo hīyate vardhate sadā ।। dharmasyeti mahāprājña deśāpekṣā tathobhayam ।। yugeṣu kṣīyamāṇeṣu na deśeṣu sa hīyate ।। tasmād deśāśrito dharmaś catuṣpāt supratiṣṭhitaḥ ।।
kṛte deśaṃ ca kālaṃ ca dharmo avaṣṭabhya tiṣṭhati ।। dvāpare cārdhataḥ kāle dharmo deśe samāsthitaḥ ।। evaṃvidhaṃ tu yo dharmaṃ vetti tasya na hīyate ।। guṇebhyo guṇakartṛbhyo vicitrā dharmasaṃsthitiḥ ।।
tīrthānām api varṇānāṃ vedānāṃ svargamokṣayoḥ ।। kālo abhivyañjakaḥ prokto deśo abhivyaṅgya ucyate ।। tad eva vyañjanaṃ brahmaṃs tasmān nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ ।। karmaṇām api tīrthānāṃ jātīnām āśramasya tu ।।
dvidaivatyaṃ yuge anyasmin dvāpare caikadaivikam ।। daivaṃ kṛtayuge tīrthaṃ tretāyām āsuraṃ viduḥ ।। athānyad api vakṣyāmi śṛṇu nārada kāraṇam ।। yadā ceyaṃ haraśiraḥ prāptā gaṅgā mahāmune ।।
tad devasya mataṃ jñātvā gajavaktram uvāca sā ।। śāntā śrutir iti khyātā bhuktimuktipradāyinī ।। tan mātur vacanaṃ śrutvā gajavaktro abhyabhāṣata ।। kiṃ kṛtyaṃ śādhi māṃ mātas tatkartāham asaṃśayam ।।
tvayāvatāryatāṃ gaṅgā satyam īśapriyā satī ।। śivo yatra surās tatra tatra vedāḥ sanātanāḥ ।। tasmān nivartayeśānaṃ devadevaṃ maheśvaram ।। nivartaya tatas tasyāḥ sarvabhāvena śaṃkaram ।।
mātus tad vacanaṃ śrutvā punar āha gaṇeśvaraḥ ।। anivṛtte śive tasyā devā api nivartitum ।। gaṅgāvatāritā pūrvaṃ gautamena mahātmanā ।। sāmopāyena tadvākyāt pūjyena brahmatejasā ।।
tuṣṭena śaṃkareṇedam ukto asau gautamas tadā ।। yad yad icchasi tat sarvaṃ dātā te adya mahāmate ।। gaṅgāṃ me yācate puṇyāṃ kim anyena vareṇa me ।। punaḥ provāca taṃ śaṃbhuḥ sarvalokopakārakaḥ ।।
uktaṃ na cātmanaḥ kiṃcit tasmād yācasva duṣkaram ।। gautamo adīnasattvas taṃ bhavam āha kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। mayā tad adya saṃprāptaṃ kṛpayā tava śaṃkara ।। bhavanti kiṃ punaḥ sākṣāt tvayi dṛṣṭe maheśvare ।।
trayāṇām upakārārthaṃ lokānāṃ yācitaṃ tvayā ।। evaṃ proktaḥ punar vipro dhyātvā prāha śivaṃ tathā ।। śṛṇvatsu lokapāleṣu jagādedaṃ sa gautamaḥ ।। sarvatra sarvadā tasyāṃ sthātavyaṃ vṛṣabhadhvaja ।।
tīrthāny anyāni deveśa kvāpi kvāpi śubhāni ca ।। sarvatra tava sāṃnidhyāt sarvatīrthāni śaṃkara ।। tad gautamavacaḥ śrutvā punar harṣāc chivo abravīt ।। yātrāṃ snānam atho dānaṃ pitṝṇāṃ vāpi tarpaṇam ।।
yaḥ karoti naro bhaktyā godāvaryā yatavrataḥ ।। saratnā sauṣadhī ramyā sārṇavā dharmabhūṣitā ।। evaṃvidhā ilā vipra godānād yābhidhīyate ।। bhūbhṛte viṣṇave bhaktyā sarvakālaṃ kṛtā sudhīḥ ।।
yo dadāti dvijaśreṣṭha tatra yat puṇyam āpnuyāt ।। gautamyāṃ viśvavandyāyāṃ mahānadyāṃ tu bhaktitaḥ ।। sarvapāpakṣayakarī sarvābhīṣṭapradāyinī ।। etasmāt kāraṇāc chaṃbhur gaṅgāyāṃ niyataḥ sthitaḥ ।।
athāpi mātar etat syān mānuṣā vighnapāśakaiḥ ।। na namanti śivaṃ devaṃ na smaranti stuvanti na ।। saṃniroddhum atho kleśas tava vākyaṃ kṣamasva me ।। vighnam ācarate yas tu tam upāsya pravartate ।।
sa kṛtārtho bhavel loke na kṛtyam avaśiṣyate ।। saṃkṣepeṇa mayā proktam itihāsapadānugam ।। tad atra vidyate sarvam itihāse savistare ।। gaṅgā gaṅgeti vā vākyaṃ sa tu puṇyam avāpnuyāt ।।
ya enāṃ gautamīṃ gaṅgāṃ daṇḍakāraṇyam āpnuyāt ।। mucyate sarvapāpebhyo viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। tāni snātuṃ samāyānti gaṅgāyāṃ siṃhage gurau ।। sakṛd godāvarīsnānaṃ siṃhayukte bṛhaspatau ।।
sarveṣāṃ sarvadā nṝṇāṃ snānān muktiṃ pradāsyati ।। kṛtvā yat phalam āpnoti tad asya śravaṇād bhavet ।। na bhayaṃ vidyate tasya kalikālasya nārada ।। śraddadhānāya śāntāya vaiṣṇavāya mahātmane ।।
etacchravaṇamātreṇa kṛtakṛtyo bhaven naraḥ ।। sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ punar garbhaṃ na saṃviśet ।। punar eva paraṃ guhyaṃ vaktum arhasy aśeṣataḥ ।। śrotum icchāmahe deva vistareṇa vadasva naḥ ।।
anantavāsudevasya māhātmyaṃ bhuvi durlabham ।। viśvakarmāṇam āhūya vacanaṃ proktavān idam ।। pratimāṃ vāsudevasya kuru śailamayīṃ bhuvi ।। yena dānavarakṣobhyo vijñāya sumahad bhayam ।।
vāsudevaṃ samārādhya nirātaṅkā vasanti te ।। cakāra pratimāṃ śuddhāṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharām ।। śrīvatsalakṣmasaṃyuktām atyugrāṃ pratimottamām ।। pītavastrāṃ supīnāṃsāṃ kuṇḍalābhyām alaṃkṛtām ।।
pratiṣṭhākālam āsādya mayāsau nirmitā purā ।। jagāma brahmasadanam āruhya gajam uttamam ।। pratimāṃ tāṃ samārādhya svapuraṃ punar āgamat ।। vṛtrādyān asurān krūrān namucipramukhān sa ca ।।
dvitīye ca yuge prāpte tretāyāṃ rākṣasādhipaḥ ।। daśa varṣasahasrāṇi nirāhāro jitendriyaḥ ।। tapasā tena tuṣṭo ahaṃ varaṃ tasmai pradattavān ।। śāpapraharaṇair ugrair avadhyo yamakiṃkaraiḥ ।।
dhanādhyakṣaṃ vinirjitya śakraṃ jetuṃ samudyataḥ ।। devarājaṃ vinirjitya tadā indrajiteti vai ।। amarāvatīṃ tataḥ prāpya devarājagṛhe śubhe ।। pratimāṃ vāsudevasya sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutām ।।
vanamālāvṛtoraskāṃ mukuṭāṅgadabhūṣitām ।। sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktāṃ sarvakāmaphalapradām ।। puṣpakeṇa vimānena laṅkāṃ prāsthāpayad drutam ।। rāvaṇasyānujo mantrī nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ ।।
romāñcitatanur bhūtvā vismayaṃ samapadyata ।। adya me saphalaṃ janma adya me saphalaṃ tapaḥ ।। jyeṣṭhaṃ bhrātaram āsādya kṛtāñjalir abhāṣata ।। yām ārādhya jagannātha nistareyaṃ bhavārṇavam ।।
gṛhāṇa pratimāṃ vīra tv anayā kiṃ karomy aham ।। nānāścaryamayaṃ devaṃ sarvabhūtabhavodbhavam ।। śatam aṣṭottaraṃ cābdaṃ samārādhya janārdanam ।। rājyaṃ laṅkādhipatyaṃ ca bhogān bhuṅkte yathepsitān ।।
anantavāsudevasya saṃbhavaṃ bhuvi durlabham ।। tasya devasya māhātmyaṃ vaktum arhasy aśeṣataḥ ।। lokapālān samanujān munisiddhāṃś ca pāpakṛt ।। saṃsthāpya nagarīṃ laṅkāṃ punaḥ sītārthamohitaḥ ।।
tataḥ kruddhena rāmeṇa raṇe saumitriṇā saha ।। abhiṣiktaś ca sugrīvo yuvarājo aṅgadas tathā ।। gavayaś ca gavākṣaś ca pāṭhīnaḥ paramaujasaḥ ।। samāvṛto mahāghorai rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ ।।
balena mahatā rāmaḥ samuttīrya mahodadhim ।। yamahastaṃ prahastaṃ ca nikumbhaṃ kumbham eva ca ।। mālāḍhyaṃ mālikāḍhyaṃ ca hatvā rāmas tu vīryavān ।। vaidehīṃ cāgnināśodhya dattvā rājyaṃ vibhīṣaṇe ।।
līlayā samanuprāpad ayodhyāṃ pūrvapālitām ।। abhiṣicya tadā rāmaḥ sarvarājye adhirājavat ।। daśa varṣasahasrāṇi daśa varṣaśatāni ca ।। rājyam āsādya sugatiṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ padam āviśat ।।
dhanyo rakṣayitāsi tvaṃ toyaratnasamanvitaḥ ।। dharaṇyāś cānurodhena bhāvaśaithilyakāraṇāt ।। kaṃsādīnāṃ vadhārthāya saṃkarṣaṇasahāyavān ।। sarvalokahitārthāya kasyacit kāraṇāntare ।।
ujjahāra svayaṃ toyāt samudraḥ saritāṃ patiḥ ।। āste sa devo devānāṃ sarvakāmaphalapradaḥ ।। vāṅmanaḥkarmabhir nityaṃ te yānti paramaṃ padam ।। rājasūyāśvamedhābhyāṃ phalaṃ daśaguṇaṃ labhet ।।
vimānenārkavarṇena kiṅkiṇījālamālinā ।। upagīyamāno gandharvair naro viṣṇupuraṃ vrajet ।। divyarūpadharaḥ śrīmān yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam ।। vaiṣṇavaṃ yogam āsthāya tato mokṣam avāpnuyāt ।।
kaḥ śaknoti guṇān vaktuṃ tasya varṣaśatair api ।। bhuktimuktipradaṃ nṝṇāṃ mayā proktaṃ sudurlabham ।। pītāmbaradharaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kaṃsakeśiniṣūdanaḥ ।। saṃkarṣaṇaṃ subhadrāṃ ca dhanyās te nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
ye dhyāyanti sadā kṛṣṇaṃ muktās te nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। tasmin kṣetre prayatnena draṣṭavyo mokṣakāṅkṣibhiḥ ।। halāyudhaṃ subhadrāṃ ca hareḥ sthānaṃ vrajanti te ।। rauhiṇeyaṃ subhadrāṃ ca viṣṇulokaṃ vrajanti te ।।
pṛthivyās tīrthayātrāyāḥ phalaṃ prāpnoti cādhikam ।। jitendriyā jitakrodhā labhante tapasaḥ phalam ।। yad āpnoti tad āpnoti māsena puruṣottame ।। tat phalaṃ satataṃ tatra prāpnuvanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
tat phalaṃ satataṃ tatra prāpnuvanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। tat phalaṃ labhate tatra pratyahaṃ prayataḥ śuciḥ ।। tat phalaṃ labhate tatra pratyahaṃ saṃyatendriyaḥ ।। kalpavṛkṣaṃ samāsādya muktās te nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
te durlabhaṃ paraṃ mokṣaṃ prāpnuvanti na saṃśayaḥ ।। so api duḥkhavinirmukto muktiṃ prāpnoti durlabhām ।। tatra dehaṃ parityajya te yānti paramāṃ gatim ।। puruṣākhyena yat prāptam anyatīrthaphalādikam ।।
puruṣāṇāṃ sahasreṣu sa bhaved uttamaḥ pumān ।। tasmād vede purāṇe ca loke asmin puruṣottamaḥ ।। āste viśvopakārāya tenāsau puruṣottamaḥ ।। dehatyāgo naraiḥ kāryaḥ samyaṅ mokṣābhikāṅkṣibhiḥ ।।
tyaktvā yatra naro dehaṃ muktiṃ prāpnoti durlabhām ।। kaḥ samastān guṇān vaktuṃ śakto varṣaśatair api ।। tasmin kṣetravare puṇye nivasadhvam atandritāḥ ।। nivāsaṃ cakrire tatra avāpuḥ paramaṃ padam ।।
puruṣākhye vare kṣetre yadi muktim abhīpsatha ।। dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ phalade puruṣottame ।। satyavādī śucir dāntaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।। avāpa paramāṃ siddhim ārādhya puruṣottamam ।।
sarvabhūtahitā dāntā jitakrodhā vimatsarāḥ ।। śrotum icchāmahe tasya caritaṃ brūhi sattama ।। pravakṣyāmi samāsena munes tasya viceṣṭitam ।। kandamūlaphalaiḥ pūrṇe samitpuṣpakuśānvitaiḥ ।।
nānāpakṣirute ramye nānāmṛgagaṇānvite ।। sarvartuphalapuṣpāḍhyaṃ kadalīkhaṇḍamaṇḍitam ।। vratopavāsair niyamaiḥ snānamaunasusaṃyamaiḥ ।। ārdravāsās tu hemante sa tepe sumahat tapaḥ ।।
babhūvur devagandharvāḥ siddhavidyādharās tathā ।। kaṇḍuḥ saṃtāpayām āsa trailokyaṃ tapaso balāt ।। ity abruvaṃs tadā dṛṣṭvā devās taṃ tapasi sthitam ।। bhayāt tasya samudvignās tapovighnam abhīpsavaḥ ।।
pramlocākhyāṃ varārohāṃ rūpayauvanagarvitām ।। sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannāṃ provāca phalasūdanaḥ ।। vighnārthaṃ tasya tapasaḥ kṣobhayasvāṃśu suprabhe ।। kiṃtu śaṅkā mamaivātra jīvitasya ca saṃśayaḥ ।।
atyugraṃ dīptatapasaṃ jvalanārkasamaprabham ।। kaṇḍuḥ paramatejasvī śāpaṃ dāsyati duḥsaham ।। viśvācī sahajanyā ca pūrvacittis tilottamā ।। anyāś cāpsarasaḥ santi rūpayauvanagarvitāḥ ।।
kāmapradhānakuśalās tās tatra saṃniyojaya ।। tiṣṭhantu nāma cānyās tās tvaṃ cātra kuśalā śubhe ।। taiḥ sārdhaṃ gaccha suśroṇi yatrāste sa mahāmuniḥ ।। jagāmākāśamārgeṇa taiḥ sārdhaṃ cāśramaṃ muneḥ ।।
muniṃ ca dīptatapasam āśramastham akalmaṣam ।। sarvartuvarapuṣpāḍhyaṃ śākhāmṛgagaṇākulam ।। śrotraramyān sumadhurāñ śabdān khagamukheritān ।। apaśyat pādapāṃś caiva vihaṃgair anunāditān ।।
atha bilvāṃs tathā jīvān dāḍimān bījapūrakān ।। pārāvatāṃs tathā kolān arimedāmlavetasān ।। iṅgudān karavīrāṃś ca harītakīvibhītakān ।। tathaivāśokapuṃnāga- ketakībakulān atha ।।
pāṭalāḥ puṣpitā ramyā devadārudrumāṃs tathā ।। anyāṃś ca pādapaśreṣṭhān apaśyat phalapuṣpitān ।। kokilaiḥ kalaviṅkaiś ca hārītair jīvajīvakaiḥ ।। śrotraramyaṃ sumadhuraṃ kūjadbhiś cāpy adhiṣṭhitam ।।
kumudaiḥ puṇḍarīkaiś ca tathā nīlotpalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। kādambaiś cakravākaiś ca tathaiva jalakukkuṭaiḥ ।। etaiś cānyaiś ca kīrṇāni samantāj jalacāribhiḥ ।। evaṃ dṛṣṭvā vanaṃ ramyaṃ taiḥ sārdhaṃ paramādbhutam ।।
provāca vāyuṃ kāmaṃ ca vasantaṃ ca dvijottamāḥ ।। kurudhvaṃ mama sāhāyyaṃ yūyaṃ sarve pṛthak pṛthak ।। pratyuvācādya yāsyāmi yatrāsau saṃsthito muniḥ ।। smaraśastragaladraśmiṃ kariṣyāmi kusārathim ।।
tathāpy adya kariṣyāmi kāmabāṇakṣatāntaram ।। munes tapaḥprabhāveṇa praśāntaśvāpadāśramam ।। stokamātraṃ sthitā tasmād agāyata varāpsarāḥ ।। kokilārāvamadhuram akālikamanoharam ।।
puṣpān uccāvacān medhyān pātayaṃś ca śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।। muneś ca kṣobhayām āsa kāmas tasyāpi mānasam ।। jagāma yatra sā subhrūḥ kāmabāṇaprapīḍitaḥ ।। bhraṣṭottarīyo vikalaḥ pulakāñcitavigrahaḥ ।।
mano harasi me subhru brūhi satyaṃ sumadhyame ।। ādeśaṃ dehi me kṣipraṃ kiṃ karomi tavājñayā ।। ādāya haste tāṃ bālāṃ praviveśa svam āśramam ।। jagmur yathāgataṃ sarve kṛtakṛtyās triviṣṭapam ।।
śrutvā śakras tadā devāḥ prītāḥ sumanaso abhavan ।। ātmanaḥ paramaṃ rūpaṃ cakāra madanākṛti ।। divyālaṃkārasaṃyuktaṃ ṣoḍaśavatsarākṛti ।। sarvopabhogasaṃpannaṃ sahasā tapaso balāt ।।
aho asya tapaso vīryam ity uktvā muditābhavat ।। vratopavāsaniyamaṃ dhyānaṃ ca munisattamāḥ ।। manmathāviṣṭahṛdayo na bubodha tapaḥkṣayam ।। na bubodha gataṃ kālaṃ viṣayāsaktamānasaḥ ।।
varayām āsa suśroṇiḥ pralāpakuśalā tadā ।। atiṣṭhan mandaradroṇyāṃ grāmyadharmarato muniḥ ।। prasādasumukho brahmann anujñātuṃ tvam arhasi ।। dināni katicid bhadre sthīyatām ity abhāṣata ।।
bubhuje viṣayāṃs tanvī tena sārdhaṃ mahātmanā ।। uktas tayeti sa punaḥ sthīyatām ity abhāṣata ।। yāmy ahaṃ tridivaṃ brahman praṇayasmitaśobhanam ।। ihāsyatāṃ mayā subhru ciraṃ kālaṃ gamiṣyasi ।।
śatadvayaṃ kiṃcid ūnaṃ varṣāṇāṃ samatiṣṭhata ।। proktaḥ proktas tayā tanvyā sthīyatām ity abhāṣata ।। proktā praṇayabhaṅgārti- vedinī na jahau munim ।। navaṃ navam abhūt prema manmathāsaktacetasaḥ ।।
niṣkrāmantaṃ ca kutreti gamyate prāha sā śubhā ।। saṃdhyopāstiṃ kariṣyāmi kriyālopo anyathā bhavet ।। gatam etan na kurute vismayaṃ kasya kathyate ।। mayā dṛṣṭāsi suśroṇi praviṣṭā ca mamāśramam ।।
avahāsaḥ kimartho ayaṃ sadbhāvaḥ kathyatāṃ mama ।। kiṃtv adya tasya kālasya gatāny abdaśatāni te ।। kathyatāṃ bhīru kaḥ kālas tvayā me ramataḥ sadā ।। māsāś ca ṣaṭ tathaivānyat samatītaṃ dinatrayam ।।
dinam ekam ahaṃ manye tvayā sārdham ihoṣitam ।। viśeṣād adya bhavatā pṛṣṭā mārgānugāminā ।। dhig dhiṅ mām ity anācāraṃ vinindyātmānam ātmanā ।। hṛto vivekaḥ kenāpi yoṣin mohāya nirmitā ।।
gatir eṣā kṛtā yena dhik taṃ kāmamahāgraham ।। narakagrāmamārgeṇa kāmenādya hatāni me ।। satāṃ sāptapadaṃ maitryam uṣito ahaṃ tvayā saha ।। mamaiva doṣo nitarāṃ yenāham ajitendriyaḥ ।।
tvayā dṛṣṭimahāmoha- manunāhaṃ jugupsitaḥ ।। tāvat skhalatsvedajalā sā babhūvātivepathuḥ ।। gaccha gaccheti sakrodham uvāca munisattamaḥ ।। ākāśagāminī svedaṃ mamārja tarupallavaiḥ ।।
nirmamārja ca gātrāṇi galatsvedajalāni vai ।। nirjagāma saromāñca- svedarūpī tadaṅgataḥ ।। somenāpyāyito gobhiḥ sa tadā vavṛddhe śanaiḥ ।। prācetasānāṃ sā bhāryā dakṣasya jananī dvijāḥ ।।
puruṣottamākhyaṃ bho viprā viṣṇor āyatanaṃ yayau ।। dakṣiṇasyodadhes tīre sarvakāmaphalapradam ।। nānādrumalatākīrṇaṃ nānāpakṣirutaṃ śivam ।। sarvasaukhyapradaṃ nṝṇāṃ dhanyaṃ sarvaguṇākaram ।।
gandharvaiḥ kiṃnarair yakṣais tathānyair mokṣakāṅkṣibhiḥ ।। brāhmaṇādyais tathā varṇair āśramasthair niṣevitam ।। kṛtakṛtyam ivātmānaṃ mene sa munisattamaḥ ।। ūrdhvabāhur mahāyogī sthitvāsau munisattamaḥ ।।
japatā kaṇḍunā devo yenārādhyata keśavaḥ ।। tathā rāgādayo doṣāḥ prayāntu praśamaṃ mama ।। bhaktiṃ ca paramāṃ jñātvā sudṛḍhāṃ puruṣottamaḥ ।। gatvā tasya samīpaṃ tu provāca madhusūdanaḥ ।।
āruhya garuḍaṃ viprā vinatākulanandanam ।। varado aham anuprāpto varaṃ varaya suvrata ।। cakṣur unmīlya sahasā dadarśa purato harim ।। śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ mukuṭāṅgadadhāriṇam ।।
śrīvatsalakṣmasaṃyuktaṃ vanamālāvibhūṣitam ।। divyacandanaliptāṅgaṃ divyamālyavibhūṣitam ।। daṇḍavat praṇipatyorvyāṃ praṇāmam akarot tadā ।। ity uktvā muniśārdūlās taṃ stotum upacakrame ।।
jagadbīja jagaddhāma jagatsākṣin namo astu te ।। puṇḍarīkākṣa govinda lokanātha namo astu te ।। bhūgarbha dhruva īśāna hṛṣīkeśa namo astu te ।। ajitākhaṇḍa śrīkṛṣṇa śrīnivāsa namo astu te ।।
duḥkhārtināśana hare jalaśāyin namo astu te ।। bhūtādhivāsa bhūtātman bhūtagarbha namo astu te ।। yajñagarbha hiraṇyāṅga pṛśnigarbha namo astu te ।। kṣetrātman kṣetrarahita kṣetrasraṣṭre namo astu te ।।
guṇabhoktṛ guṇārāma guṇatyāgin namo astu te ।। tvaṃ bhūtas tvaṃ vaṣaṭkāras tvaṃ bhavyas tvaṃ bhavatprabhuḥ ।। tvaṃ bhūtabhāvano devas tvām āhur ajam īśvaram ।। tvaṃ rudras tvaṃ durādharṣas tvam amoghas tvam īśvaraḥ ।।
tvaṃ śaṃkaras tvam uśanā tvaṃ satyaṃ tvaṃ tapo janaḥ ।। tvaṃ śaṃbhus tvaṃ svayaṃbhūś ca tvaṃ jyeṣṭhas tvaṃ parāyaṇaḥ ।। tvaṃ parjanyas tvaṃ prathitas tvaṃ vedhās tvaṃ sureśvaraḥ ।। tvam agnis tvaṃ ca pavanas tvam āpo vasudhā bhavān ।।
tvaṃ prabhus tvaṃ vibhuḥ śreṣṭhas tvaṃ lokapatir acyutaḥ ।। tvam ahas tvaṃ tathā rātris tvām āhur vatsaraṃ budhāḥ ।। tvaṃ bālas tvaṃ tathā vṛddhas tvaṃ pumān strī napuṃsakaḥ ।। tvaṃ śāśvatas tvam ajitas tvam upendras tvam uttamaḥ ।।
tvaṃ vedavedas tvaṃ dhātā vidhātā tvaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। tvaṃ vaidyas tvaṃ dhṛtātmā ca tvam atīndriyagocaraḥ ।। tvaṃ saṃgrahas tvaṃ sumahat tvaṃ dhṛtātmā tvam acyutaḥ ।। tvam evānnāntarātmā tvaṃ paramātmā tvam ucyate ।।
tvaṃ pippalas tvam agamas tvaṃ vyaktas tvaṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। anirdeśyavapus tvaṃ vai tvaṃ yamas tvaṃ surārihā ।। tvaṃ vāsudevo ameyātmā tvam eva guṇavarjitaḥ ।। sahasraśīrṣā tvaṃ devas tvam avyaktaḥ sahasradṛk ।।
tvam eva tiṣṭhase bhūyo devadeva daśāṅgulaḥ ।। yad bhāvyaṃ tat tvam īśānas tvam ṛtas tvaṃ tathāmṛtaḥ ।। tvaṃ jyāyān puruṣas tvaṃ ca tvaṃ deva daśadhā sthitaḥ ।। navabhāgo antarikṣasthaḥ pauruṣeyaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।
tvatto yajñāḥ saṃbhavanti jagato vṛṣṭikāraṇam ।। so atiricyata bhūtebhyas tejasā yaśasā śriyā ।। grāmyāraṇyāś cauṣadhayas tvattaḥ paśumṛgādayaḥ ।। tvaṃ devadeva saptāsya kālākhyo dīptavigrahaḥ ।।
tvattaḥ sarvam idaṃ jātaṃ tvayi sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। deva sarvasuraśreṣṭha sarvalokaparāyaṇa ।। namas te bhagavan viṣṇo namas te puruṣottama ।। guṇālaya namas te astu namas te astu guṇākara ।।
janārdana namas te astu namas te astu sanātana ।। gopate śrīpate viṣṇo namas te astu marutpate ।। divaspate namas te astu namas te astu mahīpate ।। kaiṭabhaghna namas te astu subrahmaṇya namo astu te ।।
samudrasalilakṣobha padmajāhlādakāriṇe ।। madhukaiṭabhahantre ca namas te turagānana ।। vidhṛtādrisvarūpāya mahākūrmāya te namaḥ ।। namaś cādivarāhāya viśvarūpāya vedhase ।।
paramāṇusvarūpāya yogigamyāya te namaḥ ।। kṣipraṃ brūhi muniśreṣṭha matto yad abhivāñchasi ।। anitye duḥkhabahule kadalīdalasaṃnibhe ।। sarvopadravasaṃyukte dustare cātibhairave ।।
na cāntam abhigacchāmi viṣayāsaktamānasaḥ ।। gato asmi śaraṇaṃ kṛṣṇa mām uddhara bhavārṇavāt ।। prasādāt tava deveśa punarāvṛttidurlabham ।। matprasādād dhruvaṃ mokṣaṃ prāpyasi tvaṃ samīhitam ।।
prāpnuvanti parāṃ siddhiṃ kiṃ punas tvaṃ dvijottama ।। prāpnoty abhimatāṃ siddhim anyeṣāṃ tatra kā kathā ।। durvijñeyagatir viṣṇus tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। sarvān kāmān parityajya svasthacitto bhavat punaḥ ।।
ekāgramānasaḥ samyag dhyātvā taṃ puruṣottamam ।। avāpa paramaṃ mokṣaṃ surāṇām api durlabham ।। vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyaḥ svargalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। mokṣakṣetraṃ ca paramaṃ devaṃ ca puruṣottamam ।।
bhaktyā śrīpuruṣottamākhyam ajaraṃ saṃsāraduḥkhāpaham ।। paścād yānti samastadoṣarahitāḥ sthānaṃ harer avyayam ।। prītā babhūvuḥ saṃhṛṣṭā vismitāś ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। tadvac chrīpuruṣākhyasya kṣetrasya puruṣottama ।।
puruṣākhyasya kṣetrasya prītiś ca vadatāṃ vara ।। tvadṛte saṃśayasyāsya cchettā nānyo asti bhūtale ।। bhadrāyāś caiva kārtsnyena pṛcchāmas tvāṃ mahāmune ।। vasudevasutau vīrau sthitau nandagṛhe mune ।।
jalabudbudasaṃkāśe bhairave lomaharṣaṇe ।। kathaṃ ghorataraṃ teṣāṃ garbhavāsam arocata ।। vistareṇa mune tāni brūhi no vadatāṃ vara ।। kathaṃ sa bhagavān devaḥ sureśaḥ surasattamaḥ ।।
amaraiś cāvṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ puṇyakṛdbhir alaṃkṛtam ।। devamānuṣayor netā dyor bhuvaḥ prabhavo avyayaḥ ।। yaś cakraṃ vartayaty eko mānuṣāṇām anāmayam ।। gopāyanaṃ yaḥ kurute jagataḥ sārvabhautikam ।।
mahābhūtāni bhūtātmā yo dadhāra cakāra ca ।। yena lokān kramair jitvā tribhir vai tridaśepsayā ।। yo antakāle jagat pītvā kṛtvā toyamayaṃ vapuḥ ।। yaḥ purāṇaḥ purāṇātmā vārāhaṃ rūpam āsthitaḥ ।।
yaḥ purā puruhūtārthe trailokyam idam avyayam ।। yena saiṃhavapuḥ kṛtvā dvidhā kṛtvā ca tat punaḥ ।। yaḥ purā hy analo bhūtvā aurvaḥ saṃvartako vibhuḥ ।। sahasracaraṇaṃ brahma sahasrāṃśusahasradam ।।
nābhyāṃ padmaṃ samudbhūtaṃ yasya paitāmahaṃ gṛham ।। yena te nihatā daityāḥ saṃgrāme tārakāmaye ।। guhāsaṃsthena cotsiktaḥ kālanemir nipātitaḥ ।। yaḥ śete śāśvataṃ yogam āsthāya timiraṃ mahat ।।
agnim āhavanīyaṃ ca vedaṃ dīkṣāṃ samid dhruvam ।। avākpāṇis tu yaś cakre havyabhāgabhujas tathā ।। bhogārthe yajñavidhinā ayojayad yajñakarmaṇi ।। yūpaṃ samit sruvaṃ somaṃ pavitrān paridhīn api ।।
sadasyān yajamānāṃś ca medhādīṃś ca kratūttamān ।। yugānurūpaṃ yaḥ kṛtvā lokān anuparākramāt ।। muhūrtās tithayo māsā dinaṃ saṃvatsaras tathā ।। āyuḥkṣetrāṇy upacayo lakṣaṇaṃ rūpasauṣṭhavam ।।
traikālyaṃ trīṇi karmāṇi trayo varṇās trayo guṇāḥ ।। sarvabhūtagataḥ sraṣṭā sarvabhūtaguṇātmakaḥ ।। gatāgatābhyāṃ yogena ya eva vidhir īśvaraḥ ।। cāturvarṇyasya prabhavaś cāturvarṇyasya rakṣitā ।।
digantaraṃ nabho bhūmir vāyur vāpi vibhāvasuḥ ।। yaḥ paraṃ śrūyate jyotir yaḥ paraṃ śrūyate tapaḥ ।। ādityānāṃ tu yo devo yaś ca daityāntako vibhuḥ ।। setur yo lokasetūnāṃ medhyo yo medhyakarmaṇām ।।
somabhūtaś ca saumyānām agnibhūto agnivarcasām ।। vinayo nayavṛttīnāṃ tejas tejasvinām api ।। ākāśaprabhavo vāyur vāyoḥ prāṇād dhutāśanaḥ ।। rasāc choṇitasaṃbhūtiḥ śoṇitān māṃsam ucyate ।।
asthno majjā samabhavan majjātaḥ śukrasaṃbhavaḥ ।। tatrāpāṃ prathamo bhāgaḥ sa saumyo rāśir ucyate ।। śukraṃ somātmakaṃ vidyād ārtavaṃ pāvakātmakam ।। kaphavarge bhavec chukraṃ pittavarge ca śoṇitam ।।
dehasya madhye hṛdayaṃ sthānaṃ tan manasaḥ smṛtam ।। manaḥ prajāpatir jñeyaḥ kaphaḥ somo vibhāvyate ।। evaṃ pravartite garbhe vardhite arbudasaṃnibhe ।। sa pañcadhā śarīrastho bhidyate vartate punaḥ ।।
prāṇo asya paramātmānaṃ vardhayan parivartate ।। vyānas tu vyāpyate yena samānaḥ saṃnivartate ।। pṛthivī vāyur ākāśam āpo jyotiś ca pañcamam ।। pārthivaṃ deham āhus tu prāṇātmānaṃ ca mārutam ।।
jyotiś cakṣūṃṣi tejaś ca ātmā teṣāṃ manaḥ smṛtam ।। ity etān puruṣaḥ sarvān sṛjaṃl lokān sanātanaḥ ।। eṣa naḥ saṃśayo brahmann eṣa no vismayo mahān ।। āścaryaṃ paramaṃ viṣṇur devair daityaiś ca kathyate ।।
prakhyātabalavīryasya viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ ।। kathaṃ sa devo devānām ārtihā puruṣottamaḥ ।। sargasthityantakṛd devaḥ sarvalokasukhāvahaḥ ।। nirlepo nirguṇaḥ sūkṣmo nirvikāro nirañjanaḥ ।।
avikārī vibhur nityaḥ paramātmā sanātanaḥ ।। viśuddhaṃ śrūyate yasya haritvaṃ ca kṛte yuge ।। īśvarasya hi tasyemāṃ gahanāṃ karmaṇo gatim ।। avyakto vyaktaliṅgastho ya eṣa bhagavān prabhuḥ ।।
eṣa nārāyaṇo bhūtvā harir āsīt sanātanaḥ ।। pradhānātmā purā hy eṣa brahmāṇam asṛjat prabhuḥ ।। kimarthaṃ martyaloke asmin yāto yadukule hariḥ ।। puruṣāya purāṇāya śāśvatāyāvyayāya ca ।।
variṣṭhāya gariṣṭhāya vareṇyāyāmitāya ca ।। yasmād aṇutaraṃ nāsti yasmān nāsti bṛhattaram ।। āvirbhāvatirobhāva- dṛṣṭādṛṣṭavilakṣaṇam ।। brahmaṇe cādidevāya namaskṛtya samādhinā ।।
sadaikarūparūpāya jiṣṇave viṣṇave namaḥ ।। vāsudevāya tārāya sargasthityantakāriṇe ।। avyaktavyaktabhūtāya viṣṇave muktihetave ।। mūlabhūto namas tasmai viṣṇave paramātmane ।।
praṇamya sarvabhūtastham acyutaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tam evārthasvarūpeṇa bhrāntidarśanataḥ sthitam ।। anādiṃ jagatām īśam ajam akṣayam avyayam ।। pṛṣṭaḥ provāca bhagavān abjayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ ।।
praṇipatya tatheśānam ekārṇavavinirgatam ।। pravakṣyāmi mataṃ kṛtsnaṃ brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।। āpo nārā iti proktā munibhis tattvadarśibhiḥ ।। sa devo bhagavān sarvaṃ vyāpya nārāyaṇo vibhuḥ ।।
ekā mūrtir anuddeśyā śuklāṃ paśyanti tāṃ budhāḥ ।। dūrasthā cāntikasthā ca vijñeyā sā guṇātigā ।। rūpavarṇādayas tasyā na bhāvāḥ kalpanāmayāḥ ।। dvitīyā pṛthivīṃ mūrdhnā śeṣākhyā dhārayaty adhaḥ ।।
tṛtīyā karma kurute prajāpālanatatparā ।। caturthī jalamadhyasthā śete pannagatalpagā ।। yā tṛtīyā harer mūrtiḥ prajāpālanatatparā ।। proddhatān asurān hanti dharmavyucchittikāriṇaḥ ।।
yadā yadā ca dharmasya glāniḥ samupajāyate ।। bhūtvā purā varāheṇa tuṇḍenāpo nirasya ca ।। kṛtvā nṛsiṃharūpaṃ ca hiraṇyakaśipur hataḥ ।। vāmanaṃ rūpam āsthāya baliṃ saṃyamya māyayā ।।
bhṛgor vaṃśe samutpanno jāmadagnyaḥ pratāpavān ।। tathātritanayo bhūtvā dattātreyaḥ pratāpavān ।। rāmo dāśarathir bhūtvā sa tu devaḥ pratāpavān ।। yadā caikārṇave supto devadevo jagatpatiḥ ।।
yoganidrāṃ samāsthāya sve mahimni vyavasthitaḥ ।। janalokagataiḥ siddhaiḥ stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ ।। marutkiñjalkasaṃyuktaṃ gṛhaṃ paitāmahaṃ varam ।। tadā karṇamalodbhūtau dānavau madhukaiṭabhau ।।
jaghāna tau durādharṣau utthāya śayanodadheḥ ।। avatāro hy ajasyeha māthuraḥ sāṃpratas tv ayam ।। pradyumneti samākhyātā rakṣākarmaṇy avasthitā ।। gṛhṇāti tatsvabhāvaś ca vāsudevecchayā sadā ।।
mānuṣatvaṃ gato viṣṇuḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ cottaraṃ punaḥ ।। avatāraṃ hareś cātra bhārāvataraṇecchayā ।। dharmaś ca hrāsam abhyeti tadā devo janārdanaḥ ।। sādhūnāṃ rakṣaṇārthāya dharmasaṃsthāpanāya ca ।।
prajānāṃ rakṣaṇārthāya jāyate asau yuge yuge ।। jagāma dharaṇī merau samāje tridivaukasām ।। kathayām āsa tat sarvaṃ khedāt karuṇabhāṣiṇī ।। mamāpy akhilalokānāṃ vandyo nārāyaṇo guruḥ ।।
martyalokaṃ samāgamya bādhante aharniśaṃ prajāḥ ।। ugrasenasutaḥ kaṃsaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ sumahāsuraḥ ।। sundo asuras tathātyugro bāṇaś cāpi baleḥ sutaḥ ।। samutpannā durātmānas tān na saṃkhyātum utsahe ।।
mahābalānāṃ dṛptānāṃ daityendrāṇāṃ mamopari ।। vibhartum ātmānam aham iti vijñāpayāmi vaḥ ।। yathā rasātalaṃ nāhaṃ gaccheyam ativihvalā ।। bhuvo bhārāvatārārthaṃ brahmā prāha ca coditaḥ ।।
ahaṃ bhavo bhavantaś ca sarvaṃ nārāyaṇātmakam ।। ādhikyaṃ nyūnatā bādhya- bādhakatvena vartate ।। tatrārādhya hariṃ tasmai sarvaṃ vijñāpayāma vai ।। svalpāṃśenāvatīryorvyāṃ dharmasya kurute sthitim ।।
samāhitamanā bhūtvā tuṣṭāva garuḍadhvajam ।। ujjahārātmanaḥ keśau sitakṛṣṇau dvijottamāḥ ।। avatīrya bhuvo bhāra- kleśahāniṃ kariṣyataḥ ।। kurvantu yuddham unmattaiḥ pūrvotpannair mahāsuraiḥ ।।
prayāsyanti na saṃdeho nānāyudhavicūrṇitāḥ ।। tasyā garbho aṣṭamo ayaṃ tu matkeśo bhavitā surāḥ ।। kālanemisamudbhūtam ity uktvāntardadhe hariḥ ।। merupṛṣṭhaṃ surā jagmur avateruś ca bhūtale ।।
bhaviṣyatīty ācacakṣe bhagavān nārado muniḥ ।। devakīṃ vasudevaṃ ca gṛhe guptāv adhārayat ।। tathaiva vasudevo api putram arpitavān dvijāḥ ।। viṣṇuprayuktā tān nidrā kramād garbhe nyayojayat ।।
avidyayā jagat sarvaṃ tām āha bhagavān hariḥ ।। ekaikaśyena ṣaḍgarbhān devakījaṭhare naya ।। aṃśāṃśenodare tasyāḥ saptamaḥ saṃbhaviṣyati ।। tasyāḥ prasūtisamaye garbho neyas tvayodaram ।।
devakyāḥ patito garbha iti loko vadiṣyati ।। saṃjñām avāpsyate vīraḥ śvetādriśikharopamaḥ ।। garbhe tvayā yaśodāyā gantavyam avilambitam ।। utpatsyāmi navamyāṃ ca prasūtiṃ tvam avāpsyasi ।।
macchaktipreritamatir vasudevo nayiṣyati ।। prakṣepsyaty antarikṣe ca tvaṃ sthānaṃ samavāpsyasi ।। praṇipātānataśirā bhaginītve grahīṣyati ।। sthānair anekaiḥ pṛthivīm aśeṣāṃ maṇḍayiṣyasi ।।
lajjā puṣṭir uṣā yā ca kācid anyā tvam eva sā ।। bhadreti bhadrakālīti kṣemyā kṣemaṃkarīti ca ।। teṣāṃ hi vāñchitaṃ sarvaṃ matprasādād bhaviṣyati ।। nṛṇām aśeṣakāmāṃs tvaṃ prasannāyāṃ pradāsyasi ।।
asaṃdigdhaṃ bhaviṣyanti gaccha devi yathoditam ।। ṣaḍgarbhagarbhavinyāsaṃ cakre cānyasya karṣaṇam ।। lokatrayopakārāya devakyāḥ praviveśa vai ।। saṃbhūtā jaṭhare tadvad yathoktaṃ parameṣṭhinā ।।
viṣṇor aṃśe mahīṃ yāta ṛtavo apy abhavañ śubhāḥ ।। jājvalyamānāṃ tāṃ dṛṣṭvā manāṃsi kṣobham āyayuḥ ।। bibhrāṇāṃ vapuṣā viṣṇuṃ tuṣṭuvus tām aharniśam ।। tvaṃ sarvalokarakṣārtham avatīrṇā mahītale ।।
prītyarthaṃ dhārayeśānaṃ dhṛtaṃ yenākhilaṃ jagat ।। garbheṇa puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ jagatāṃ trāṇakāraṇam ।। devakyāḥ pūrvasaṃdhyāyām āvirbhūtaṃ mahātmanā ।। mandaṃ jagarjur jaladāḥ puṣpavṛṣṭimucaḥ surāḥ ।।
śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ jātaṃ tuṣṭāvānakadundubhiḥ ।। vijñāpayām āsa tadā kaṃsād bhīto dvijottamāḥ ।। divyaṃ rūpam idaṃ deva prasādenopasaṃhara ।। avatīrṇam iti jñātvā tvām asmin mandire mama ।।
jānātu māvatāraṃ te kaṃso ayaṃ ditijāntaka ।। saphalaṃ devi saṃjātaṃ jāto ahaṃ yat tavodarāt ।। vasudevo api taṃ rātrāv ādāya prayayau bahiḥ ।। mathurādvārapālāś ca vrajaty ānakadundubhau ।।
saṃchādya taṃ yayau śeṣaḥ phaṇair ānakadundubhim ।। vasudevo vahan viṣṇuṃ jānumātravahāṃ yayau ।। nandādīn gopavṛddhāṃś ca yamunāyāṃ dadarśa saḥ ।। tām eva kanyāṃ munayaḥ prāsūta mohite jane ।।
yaśodāśayane tūrṇam ājagāmāmitadyutiḥ ।। nīlotpaladalaśyāmaṃ tato atyarthaṃ mudaṃ yayau ।। devakīśayane nyasya yathāpūrvam atiṣṭhata ।। kaṃsam āvedayām āsur devakīprasavaṃ dvijāḥ ।।
muñca muñceti devakyā- sannakaṇṭhaṃ nivāritaḥ ।। prajahāsa tathaivoccaiḥ kaṃsaṃ ca ruṣitābravīt ।। tad etat saṃpradhāryāśu kriyatāṃ hitam ātmanaḥ ।। paśyato bhojarājasya stutā siddhair vihāyasā ।।
pralambakeśipramukhān āhūyāsurapuṃgavān ।। ariṣṭādyais tathā cānyaiḥ śrūyatāṃ vacanaṃ mama ।। madvīryatāpitān vīrān na tv etān gaṇayāmy aham ।। hāsyaṃ me jāyate vīrās teṣu yatnapareṣv api ।।
apakārāya daityendrā yatanīyaṃ durātmanām ।। ity etad bālikā prāha devakīgarbhasaṃbhavā ।। yatrodriktaṃ balaṃ bāle sa hantavyaḥ prayatnataḥ ।। uvāca vasudevaṃ ca devakīm avirodhataḥ ।।
ko apy anya eva nāśāya bālo mama samudgataḥ ।। arbhakā yuvayoḥ ko vā āyuṣo ante na hanyate ।। antargṛhaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ praviveśa punaḥ svakam ।। prahṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭavān nandaṃ putro jāto mameti vai ।।
vārdhake api samutpannas tanayo ayaṃ tavādhunā ।। yadartham āgatas tasmān nātra stheyaṃ mahātmanā ।। bhavadbhir gamyatāṃ nanda tac chīghraṃ nijagokulam ।। sa rakṣaṇīyo bhavatā yathāyaṃ tanayo nijaḥ ।।
śakaṭāropitair bhāṇḍaiḥ karaṃ dattvā mahābalāḥ ।। suptaṃ kṛṣṇam upādāya rātrau ca pradadau stanam ।। tasya tasya kṣaṇenāṅgaṃ bālakasyopahanyate ।। gṛhītvā prāṇasahitaṃ papau krodhasamanvitaḥ ।।
papāta pūtanā bhūmau mriyamāṇātibhīṣaṇā ।। dadṛśuḥ pūtanotsaṅge kṛṣṇaṃ tāṃ ca nipātitām ।। gopucchabhrāmaṇādyaiś ca bāladoṣam apākarot ।। kṛṣṇasya pradadau rakṣāṃ kurvann idam udairayat ।।
yasya nābhisamudbhūtāt paṅkajād abhavaj jagat ।। varāharūpadhṛg devaḥ sa tvāṃ rakṣatu keśavaḥ ।। vāmano rakṣatu sadā bhavantaṃ yaḥ kṣaṇād abhūt ।। śiras te pātu govindaḥ kaṇṭhaṃ rakṣatu keśavaḥ ।।
rakṣatv avyāhataiśvaryas tava nārāyaṇo avyayaḥ ।। hṛṣīkeśo ambare bhūmau rakṣatu tvāṃ mahīdharaḥ ।। śāyitaḥ śakaṭasyādho bālaparyaṅkikātale ।। mṛtāyāḥ paramaṃ trāsaṃ vismayaṃ ca tadā yayuḥ ।।
cikṣepa caraṇāv ūrdhvaṃ stanārthī praruroda ca ।। vidhvastabhāṇḍakumbhaṃ tad viparītaṃ papāta vai ।। ājagāma tadā jñātvā bālam uttānaśāyinam ।। tatraiva bālakāḥ procur bālenānena pātitam ।।
śakaṭaṃ parivṛttaṃ vai naitad anyasya ceṣṭitam ।। nandagopo api jagrāha bālam atyantavismitaḥ ।। śakaṭaṃ cārcayām āsa dadhipuṣpaphalākṣataiḥ ।। pracchanna eva gopānāṃ saṃskāram akarot tayoḥ ।।
gargo matimatāṃ śreṣṭho nāma kurvan mahāmatiḥ ।। ghṛṣṭajānukarau viprā babhūvatur ubhāv api ।। na nivārayituṃ śaktā yaśodā tau na rohiṇī ।। tadaharjātagovatsa- pucchākarṣaṇatatparau ।।
śaśāka no vārayituṃ krīḍantāv aticañcalau ।। kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakarmāṇam āha cedam amarṣitā ।। yadi śakto asi gaccha tvam aticañcalaceṣṭita ।। vyagrāyām atha tasyāṃ sa karṣamāṇa ulūkhalam ।।
karṣatā vṛkṣayor madhye tiryag evam ulūkhalam ।। tataḥ kaṭakaṭāśabda- samākarṇanakātaraḥ ।। bhagnaskandhau nipātitau bhagnaśākhau mahītale ।। tayor madhyagataṃ baddhaṃ dāmnā gāḍhaṃ tathodare ।।
gopavṛddhās tataḥ sarve nandagopapurogamāḥ ।। sthāneneha na naḥ kāryaṃ vrajāmo anyan mahāvanam ।। pūtanāyā vināśaś ca śakaṭasya viparyayaḥ ।। vṛndāvanam itaḥ sthānāt tasmād gacchāma mā ciram ।।
iti kṛtvā matiṃ sarve gamane te vrajaukasaḥ ।। tataḥ kṣaṇena prayayuḥ śakaṭair godhanais tathā ।। sarvāvayavanirdhūtaṃ kṣaṇamātreṇa tat tadā ।। vṛndāvanaṃ bhagavatā kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā ।।
tatas tatrātirukṣe api dharmakāle dvijottamāḥ ।। sa samāvāsitaḥ sarvo vrajo vṛndāvane tataḥ ।। vatsabālau ca saṃvṛttau rāmadāmodarau tataḥ ।। barhipattrakṛtāpīḍau vanyapuṣpāvataṃsakau ।।
kākapakṣadharau bālau kumārāv iva pāvakau ।। kvacid dhasantāv anyonyaṃ krīḍamānau tathā paraiḥ ।। kālena gacchatā tau tu saptavarṣau babhūvatuḥ ।। prāvṛṭkālas tato atīva meghaughasthagitāmbaraḥ ।।
prarūḍhanavapuṣpāḍhyā śakragopavṛtā mahī ।। ūhur unmārgagāmīni nimnagāmbhāṃsi sarvataḥ ।। gopaiḥ samānaiḥ sahitau cikrīḍāte amarāv iva ।। vicacāra vṛto gopair vanyapuṣpasragujjvalaḥ ।।
tīrasaṃlagnaphenaughair hasantīm iva sarvataḥ ।। hradaṃ kālīyanāgasya dadarśātivibhīṣaṇam ।। vātāhatāmbuvikṣepa- sparśadagdhavihaṃgamam ।। vilokya cintayām āsa bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ ।।
yo mayā nirjitas tyaktvā duṣṭo naṣṭaḥ payonidhau ।। na narair godhanair vāpi tṛṣārtair upabhujyate ।। nityatrastāḥ sukhaṃ yena careyur vrajavāsinaḥ ।। yad eṣām utpathasthānāṃ kāryā śāstir durātmanām ।।
adhiruhyotpatiṣyāmi hrade asmiñ jīvanāśinaḥ ।। nipapāta hrade tatra sarparājasya vegataḥ ।। atyarthadūrajātāṃś ca tāṃś cāsiñcan mahīruhān ।। jajvaluḥ pādapāḥ sadyo jvālāvyāptadigantarāḥ ।।
tacchabdaśravaṇāc cātha nāgarājo abhyupāgamat ।। vṛto mahāviṣaiś cānyair aruṇair anilāśanaiḥ ।। prakampitatanūtkṣepa- calatkuṇḍalakāntayaḥ ।। dadaṃśuś cāpi te kṛṣṇaṃ viṣajvālāvilair mukhaiḥ ।।
gopā vrajam upāgatya cukruśuḥ śokalālasāḥ ।। bhakṣyate sarparājena tad āgacchata mā ciram ।। gopyaś ca tvaritā jagmur yaśodāpramukhā hradam ।। yaśodayā samaṃ bhrānto drutaḥ praskhalito yayau ।।
tvaritaṃ yamunāṃ jagmuḥ kṛṣṇadarśanalālasāḥ ।। niṣprayatnaṃ kṛtaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ sarpabhogena veṣṭitam ।। yaśodā ca mahābhāgā babhūva munisattamāḥ ।। procuś ca keśavaṃ prītyā bhayakātaragadgadam ।।
nāgarājasya no gantum asmākaṃ yujyate vraje ।। vinākṛtā na yāsyāmaḥ kṛṣṇenānena gokulam ।। uvāca gopān vidhurān vilokya stimitekṣaṇaḥ ।। mūrchākulāṃ yaśodāṃ ca kṛṣṇamāhātmyasaṃjñayā ।।
vyajyate svaṃ tam ātmānaṃ kim anyaṃ tvaṃ na vetsi yat ।। kartāpahartā pātā ca trailokyaṃ tvaṃ trayīmayaḥ ।। gopyaś ca sīdataḥ kasmāt tvaṃ bandhūn samupekṣase ।। tad ayaṃ damyatāṃ kṛṣṇa durātmā daśanāyudhaḥ ।।
āsphālya mocayām āsa svaṃ dehaṃ bhogabandhanāt ।। āruhya bhugnaśirasaḥ prananartoruvikramaḥ ।। yatronnatiṃ ca kurute nanāmāsya tataḥ śiraḥ ।। daṇḍapātanipātena vavāma rudhiraṃ bahu ।।
vilokya śaraṇaṃ jagmus tatpatnyo madhusūdanam ।। paraṃ jyotir acintyaṃ yat tadaṃśaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। svarūpavarṇanaṃ tasya kathaṃ yoṣit kariṣyati ।। brahmāṇḍam alpakāṃśāṃśaḥ stoṣyāmas taṃ kathaṃ vayam ।।
prāṇāṃs tyajati nāgo ayaṃ bhartṛbhikṣā pradīyatām ।। prasīda devadeveti prāha vākyaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।। nirastātiśayaṃ yasya tasya stoṣyāmi kiṃ nv aham ।। parasmāt paramo yas tvaṃ tasya stoṣyāmi kiṃ nv aham ।।
svabhāvena ca saṃyuktas tathedaṃ ceṣṭitaṃ mayā ।। nyāyyo daṇḍanipātas te tavaiva vacanaṃ yathā ।। sa soḍho ayaṃ varo daṇḍas tvatto nānyo astu me varaḥ ।। jīvitaṃ dīyatām ekam ājñāpaya karomi kim ।।
sabhṛtyaparivāras tvaṃ samudrasalilaṃ vraja ।। garuḍaḥ pannagaripus tvayi na prahariṣyati ।। praṇamya so api kṛṣṇāya jagāma payasāṃ nidhim ।। samastabhāryāsahitaḥ parityajya svakaṃ hradam ।।
gopā mūrdhani govindaṃ siṣicur netrajair jalaiḥ ।। tuṣṭuvur muditā gopā dṛṣṭvā śivajalāṃ nadīm ।। saṃstūyamāno gopālaiḥ kṛṣṇo vrajam upāgamat ।। bhramamāṇau vane tatra ramyaṃ tālavanaṃ gatau ।।
nṛgomāṃsakṛtāhāraḥ sadādhyāste kharākṛtiḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā spṛhānvitā gopāḥ phalādāne abruvan vacaḥ ।। bhūpradeśo yatas tasmāt tyaktānīmāni santi vai ।। vayam etāny abhīpsāmaḥ pātyantāṃ yadi rocate ।।
kṛṣṇaś ca pātayām āsa bhuvi tālaphalāni vai ।। ājagāma sa duṣṭātmā kopād daiteyagardabhaḥ ।। jaghānorasi tābhyāṃ ca sa ca tenāpy agṛhyata ।। tasminn eva pracikṣepa vegena tṛṇarājani ।।
pṛthivyāṃ pātayām āsa mahāvāto ambudān iva ।। kṛṣṇaś cikṣepa tālāgre balabhadraś ca līlayā ।। daityagardabhadehaiś ca munayaḥ śuśubhe adhikam ।। navaśaṣpaṃ sukhaṃ cerur yatra bhuktam abhūt purā ।।
sarvagopālagopīnāṃ ramyaṃ tālavanaṃ babhau ।। śuśubhāte mahātmānau bālaśṛṅgāv ivarṣabhau ।। niyogapāśaskandhau tau vanamālāvibhūṣitau ।। mahendrāyudhasaṃkāśau śvetakṛṣṇāv ivāmbudau ।।
samastalokanāthānāṃ nāthabhūtau bhuvaṃ gatau ।। tajjātiguṇayuktābhiḥ krīḍābhiś ceratur vanam ।। vyāyāmaṃ cakratus tatra kṣepaṇīyais tathāśmabhiḥ ।। ājagāma pralambākhyo gopaveṣatirohitaḥ ।।
mānuṣaṃ rūpam āsthāya pralambo dānavottamaḥ ।। kṛṣṇaṃ tato rauhiṇeyaṃ hantuṃ cakre manoratham ।। prakrīḍitās tu te sarve dvau dvau yugapad utpatan ।। gopālair aparaiś cānye gopālāḥ saha pupluvuḥ ।।
jitavān kṛṣṇapakṣīyair gopair anyaiḥ parājitāḥ ।। punar nivṛttās te sarve ye ye tatra parājitāḥ ।। na tasthau prajagāmaiva sacandra iva vāridaḥ ।। vavṛdhe sumahākāyaḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakaḥ ।।
sragdāmalambābharaṇaṃ mukuṭāṭopamastakam ।। hriyamāṇas tataḥ kṛṣṇam idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। kenāpi paśya daityena gopālacchadmarūpiṇā ।। tat kathyatāṃ prayāty eṣa durātmātitvarānvitaḥ ।।
mahātmā rauhiṇeyasya balavīryapramāṇavit ।। sarvātman sarvaguhyānāṃ guhyād guhyātmanā tvayā ।। ātmānam ekaṃ tadvac ca jagaty ekārṇave ca yaḥ ।। jagato asya jagaty arthe bhedenāvāṃ vyavasthitau ।।
mānuṣyam evam ālambya bandhūnāṃ kriyatāṃ hitam ।। vihasya pīḍayām āsa pralambaṃ balavān balaḥ ।। tena cāsya prahāreṇa bahir yāte vilocane ।। nipapāta mahīpṛṣṭhe daityavaryo mamāra ca ।।
prahṛṣṭās tuṣṭuvur gopāḥ sādhu sādhv iti cābruvan ।। pralambe saha kṛṣṇena punar gokulam āyayau ।। prāvṛḍvyatītā vikasat- sarojā cābhavac charat ।। dadarśendrotsavārambha- pravṛttān vrajavāsinaḥ ।।
kautūhalād idaṃ vākyaṃ prāha vṛddhān mahāmatiḥ ।। prāha taṃ nandagopaś ca pṛcchantam atisādaram ।। yena saṃcoditā meghā varṣanty ambumayaṃ rasam ।। vartayāmopabhuñjānās tarpayāmaś ca devatāḥ ।।
tena saṃvardhitaiḥ sasyaiḥ puṣṭās tuṣṭā bhavanti vai ।। dṛśyate yatra dṛśyante vṛṣṭimanto balāhakāḥ ।। parjanyaḥ sarvalokasya bhavāya bhuvi varṣati ।। mahe sureśam arghanti vayam anye ca dehinaḥ ।।
kopāya tridaśendrasya prāha dāmodaras tadā ।। gāvo asmaddaivataṃ tāta vayaṃ vanacarā yataḥ ।। vidyācatuṣṭayaṃ tv etad vārttām atra śṛṇuṣva me ।। vidyā hy etā mahābhāgā vārttā vṛttitrayāśrayā ।।
asmākaṃ gāḥ parā vṛttir vārttā bhedair iyaṃ tribhiḥ ।। saiva pūjyārcanīyā ca saiva tasyopakārikā ।। iha ca pretya caivāsau tāta nāpnoti śobhanam ।। vanāntā girayaḥ sarve sā cāsmākaṃ parā gatiḥ ।।
kim asmākaṃ mahendreṇa gāvaḥ śailāś ca devatāḥ ।। girigoyajñaśīlāś ca vayam adrivanāśrayāḥ ।। arcyatāṃ pūjyatāṃ medhyaṃ paśuṃ hatvā vidhānataḥ ।। bhojyantāṃ tena vai viprās tathānye cāpi vāñchakāḥ ।।
śaratpuṣpakṛtāpīḍāḥ parigacchantu gogaṇāḥ ।। tataḥ kṛtā bhavet prītir gavām adres tathā mama ।। prītyutphullamukhā viprāḥ sādhu sādhv ity athābruvan ।। tat kariṣyāmy ahaṃ sarvaṃ giriyajñaḥ pravartyatām ।।
dadhipāyasamāṃsādyair daduḥ śailabaliṃ tataḥ ।। gāvaḥ śailaṃ tataś cakrur arcitās taṃ pradakṣiṇam ।। girimūrdhani govindaḥ śailo aham iti mūrtimān ।। kṛṣṇas tenaiva rūpeṇa gopaiḥ saha gireḥ śiraḥ ।।
kṛtvā girimahaṃ goṣṭhaṃ nijam abhyāyayuḥ punaḥ ।। saṃvartakaṃ nāma gaṇaṃ toyadānām athābravīt ।। ājñānantaram evāśu kriyatām avicāritam ।। kṛṣṇāśrayabalādhmāto mahabhaṅgam acīkarat ।।
tā gāvo vṛṣṭipātena pīḍyantāṃ vacanān mama ।। sāhāyyaṃ vaḥ kariṣyāmi vāyūnāṃ saṃgamena ca ।। vātavarṣaṃ mahābhīmam abhāvāya gavāṃ dvijāḥ ।। ekaṃ dhārāmahāsāra- pūraṇenābhavad dvijāḥ ।।
dhutāḥ prāṇāñ jahuḥ sarvās tiryaṅmukhaśirodharāḥ ।। gāvo vivatsāś ca kṛtā vāripūreṇa cāparāḥ ।। trāhi trāhīty alpaśabdāḥ kṛṣṇam ūcur ivārtakāḥ ।। atīvārtaṃ harir dṛṣṭvā trāṇāyācintayat tadā ।।
tad etad akhilaṃ goṣṭhaṃ trātavyam adhunā mayā ।। dhārayiṣyāmi goṣṭhasya pṛthucchattram ivopari ।। utpāṭyaikakareṇaiva dhārayām āsa līlayā ।। viśadhvam atra sahitāḥ kṛtaṃ varṣanivāraṇam ।।
praviśya nātra bhetavyaṃ giripātasya nirbhayaiḥ ।। śakaṭāropitair bhāṇḍair gopyaś cāsārapīḍitāḥ ।। vrajaukovāsibhir harṣa- vismitākṣair nirīkṣitaḥ ।। saṃstūyamānacaritaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śailam adhārayat ।।
indreṇa coditā meghā gopānāṃ nāśakāriṇā ।। mithyāpratijño balabhid vārayām āsa tān ghanān ।। niṣkramya gokulaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ svasthānaṃ punar āgamat ।। svasthāne vismitamukhair dṛṣṭas tair vrajavāsibhiḥ ।।
rocayām āsa kṛṣṇasya darśanaṃ pākaśāsanaḥ ।। govardhanagirau kṛṣṇaṃ dadarśa tridaśādhipaḥ ।। kṛtsnasya jagato gopaṃ vṛtaṃ gopakumārakaiḥ ।। kṛtacchāyaṃ harer mūrdhni pakṣābhyāṃ pakṣipuṃgavam ।।
śakraḥ sasmitam āhedaṃ prītivisphāritekṣaṇaḥ ।। tvatsamīpaṃ mahābāho naitac cintyaṃ tvayānyathā ।। avatīrṇo akhilādhāras tvam eva parameśvara ।। samādiṣṭā mahāmeghās taiś caitat kadanaṃ kṛtam ।।
tenāhaṃ toṣito vīra karmaṇātyadbhutena te ।। tvayāyam adripravaraḥ kareṇaikena coddhṛtaḥ ।। tvayā trātābhir atyarthaṃ yuṣmatkāraṇakāraṇāt ।। upendratve gavām indro govindas tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।।
abhiṣekaṃ tayā cakre pavitrajalapūrṇayā ।। prasravodbhūtadugdhārdrāṃ sadyaś cakrur vasuṃdharām ।। prītyā sapraśrayaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ punar āha śacīpatiḥ ।। yad bravīmi mahābhāga bhārāvataraṇecchayā ।।
avatīrṇo arjuno nāma sa rakṣyo bhavatā sadā ।। sa rakṣaṇīyo bhavatā yathātmā madhusūdana ।। tam ahaṃ pālayiṣyāmi yāvad asmi mahītale ।। na tāvad arjunaṃ kaścid devendra yudhi jeṣyati ।।
keśī kuvalayāpīḍo narakādyās tathāpare ।। tatra viddhi sahasrākṣa bhārāvataraṇaṃ kṛtam ।। nārjunasya ripuḥ kaścin mamāgre prabhaviṣyati ।। nivṛtte bhārate yuddhe kuntyai dāsyāmi vikṣatān ।।
āruhyairāvataṃ nāgaṃ punar eva divaṃ yayau ।। ājagāmātha gopīnāṃ dṛṣṭapūtena vartmanā ।। ūcuḥ prītyā dhṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā tena govardhanācalam ।। gāvaś ca bhavatā trātā giridhāraṇakarmaṇā ।।
divyaṃ ca karma bhavataḥ kim etat tāta kathyatām ।। dhṛto govardhanaś cāyaṃ śaṅkitāni manāṃsi naḥ ।। yathā tvadvīryam ālokya na tvāṃ manyāmahe naram ।। kiṃ cāsmākaṃ vicāreṇa bāndhavo asti namo astu te ।।
karma cedam aśakyaṃ yat samastais tridaśair api ।। cintyamānam ameyātmañ śaṅkāṃ kṛṣṇa prayacchati ।। ity evam uktas tair gopair āha kṛṣṇo dvijottamāḥ ।। ślāghyo vāhaṃ tataḥ kiṃ vo vicāreṇa prayojanam ।।
tad arghā bandhusadṛśī bāndhavāḥ kriyatāṃ mayi ।। ahaṃ vo bāndhavo jāto nātaś cintyam ato anyathā ।। yayur gopā mahābhāgās tasmin praṇayakopini ।। tathā kumudinīṃ phullām āmoditadigantarām ।।
vilokya saha gopībhir manaś cakre ratiṃ prati ।। jagau kamalapādo asau nāma tatra kṛtavrataḥ ।। ājagmus tvaritā gopyo yatrāste madhusūdanaḥ ।। dattāvadhānā kācic ca tam eva manasāsmarat ।।
yayau ca kācit premāndhā tatpārśvam avilajjitā ।। tanmayatvena govindaṃ dadhyau mīlitalocanā ।। mānayām āsa govindo rāsārambharasotsukaḥ ।। anyadeśagate kṛṣṇe cerur vṛndāvanāntaram ।।
kṛṣṇasya caraṇaṃ rātrau dṛṣṭvā vṛndāvane dvijāḥ ।। gopyo vyagrāḥ samaṃ cerū ramyaṃ vṛndāvanaṃ vanam ।। yamunātīram āgamya jagus taccaritaṃ dvijāḥ ।। gopyas trailokyagoptāraṃ kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakāriṇam ।।
kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kṛṣṇeti prāhotphullavilocanā ।। vilokya netrabhṛṅgābhyāṃ papau tanmukhapaṅkajam ।। tasyaiva rūpaṃ dhyāyantī yogārūḍheva sā babhau ।। ninye anunayam anyāś ca karasparśena mādhavaḥ ।।
rarāma rāsagoṣṭhībhir udāracarito hariḥ ।। gopījano na caivābhūd ekasthānasthirātmanā ।। cakāra ca karasparśa- nimīlitadṛśaṃ hariḥ ।। anuyātaśaratkāvya- geyagītir anukramām ।।
jagau gopījanas tv ekaṃ kṛṣṇanāma punaḥ punaḥ ।। dadau bāhulatāṃ skandhe gopī madhuvighātinaḥ ।। gopī gītastutivyāja- nipuṇā madhusūdanam ।। pulakodgamaśasyāya svedāmbughanatāṃ gatau ।।
sādhu kṛṣṇeti kṛṣṇeti tāvat tā dviguṇaṃ jaguḥ ।। pratilomānulomena bhejur gopāṅganā harim ।। sa varṣakoṭipratimaḥ kṣaṇas tena vinābhavat ।। kṛṣṇaṃ gopāṅganā rātrau ramayanti ratipriyāḥ ।।
reme tābhir ameyātmā kṣapāsu kṣapitāhitaḥ ।। ātmasvarūparūpo asau vyāpya sarvam avasthitaḥ ।। vāyuś cātmā tathaivāsau vyāpya sarvam avasthitaḥ ।। trāsayan samado goṣṭhān ariṣṭaḥ samupāgataḥ ।।
khurāgrapātair atyarthaṃ dārayan dharaṇītalam ।। saṃrambhākṣiptalāṅgūlaḥ kaṭhinaskandhabandhanaḥ ।। viṇmūtrāliptapṛṣṭhāṅgo gavām udvegakārakaḥ ।। pātayan sa gavāṃ garbhān daityo vṛṣabharūpadhṛk ।।
tatas tam atighorākṣam avekṣyātibhayāturāḥ ।। siṃhanādaṃ tataś cakre talaśabdaṃ ca keśavaḥ ।। agranyastaviṣāṇāgraḥ kṛṣṇakukṣikṛtekṣaṇaḥ ।। āyāntaṃ daityavṛṣabhaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇo mahābalam ।।
āsannaṃ caiva jagrāha grāhavan madhusūdanaḥ ।। tasya darpabalaṃ hatvā gṛhītasya viṣāṇayoḥ ।। utpāṭya śṛṅgam ekaṃ ca tenaivātāḍayat tataḥ ।। jambhe hate sahasrākṣaṃ purā devagaṇā yathā ।।
pralambe nidhanaṃ nīte dhṛte govardhanācale ।। hatāyāṃ pūtanāyāṃ ca śakaṭe parivartite ।। yaśodādevakīgarbha- parivartādy aśeṣataḥ ।। vasudevaṃ prati tadā kopaṃ cakre sa durmatiḥ ।।
jagarhe yādavāṃś cāpi kāryaṃ caitad acintayat ।। tāvad eva mayā vadhyāv asādhyau rūḍhayauvanau ।। etābhyāṃ mallayuddhe tau ghātayiṣyāmi durmadau ।। tathā tathā kariṣyāmi yāsyataḥ saṃkṣayaṃ yathā ।।
hantuṃ kṛtamatir vīram akrūraṃ vākyam abravīt ।। itaḥ syandanam āruhya gamyatāṃ nandagokulam ।। nāśāya kila saṃbhūtau mama duṣṭau pravardhataḥ ।। āneyau bhavatā tau tu mallayuddhāya tatra vai ।।
tābhyāṃ sahānayor yuddhaṃ sarvaloko atra paśyatu ।। sa tau nihaṃsyate pāpau vasudevātmajau śiśū ।। haniṣye pitaraṃ caiva ugrasenaṃ ca durmatim ।। vittaṃ cāpahariṣyāmi duṣṭānāṃ madvadhaiṣiṇām ।।
eteṣāṃ ca vadhāyāhaṃ prayatiṣyāmy anukramāt ।। prasādhiṣye tvayā tasmān matprītyā vīra gamyatām ।। gopāḥ samānayanty āśu tvayā vācyās tathā tathā ।। prītimān abhavat kṛṣṇaṃ śvo drakṣyāmīti satvaraḥ ।।
niścakrāma tadā puryā mathurāyā madhupriyaḥ ।। kṛṣṇasya nidhanākāṅkṣī vṛndāvanam upāgamat ।। punar vikrāntacandrārka- mārgo gopāntam āgamat ।। gopyaś ca bhayasaṃvignā govindaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।।
satoyajaladadhvāna- gambhīram idam uktavān ।। bhavadbhir gopajātīyair vīravīryaṃ vilopyate ।। daiteyabalavāhyena valgatā duṣṭavājinā ।। pātayiṣyāmi daśanān vadanād akhilāṃs tava ।।
vivṛtāsyaś ca so apy enaṃ daiteyaś ca upādravat ।। praveśayām āsa tadā keśino duṣṭavājinaḥ ।। śātitā daśanās tasya sitābhrāvayavā iva ।। vināśāya yathā vyādhir āptabhūtair upekṣitaḥ ।।
sṛkkaṇī vivṛte cakre viśliṣṭe muktabandhane ।। svedārdragātraḥ śrāntaś ca niryatnaḥ so abhavat tataḥ ।। nipapāta dvidhābhūto vaidyutena yathā drumaḥ ।। keśinas te dvidhā bhūte śakale ca virejatuḥ ।।
anāyastatanuḥ svastho hasaṃs tatraiva saṃsthitaḥ ।। tuṣṭuvuḥ puṇḍarīkākṣam anurāgamanoramam ।। keśinaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā harṣanirbharamānasaḥ ।। nihato ayaṃ tvayā keśī kleśadas tridivaukasām ।।
yāni vai vismitaṃ cetas toṣam etena me gatam ।। dhutakesarajālasya hreṣato abhrāvalokinaḥ ।। tasmāt keśavanāmnā tvaṃ loke geyo bhaviṣyasi ।। paraśvo ahaṃ sameṣyāmi tvayā keśiniṣūdana ।।
bhārāvatārakartā tvaṃ pṛthivyā dharaṇīdhara ।। draṣṭavyāni mayā yuṣmat- praṇītāni janārdana ।। tvayā sabhājitaś cāhaṃ svasti te astu vrajāmy aham ।। viveśa gokulaṃ gopī- netrapānaikabhājanam ।।
kṛṣṇasaṃdarśanāsaktaḥ prayayau nandagokule ।। yo aham aṃśāvatīrṇasya mukhaṃ drakṣyāmi cakriṇaḥ ।। yad unnidrābjapattrākṣaṃ viṣṇor drakṣyāmy aham mukham ।। tat puṇḍarīkanayanaṃ viṣṇor drakṣyāmy ahaṃ mukham ।।
drakṣyāmi yat paraṃ dhāma devānāṃ bhagavanmukham ।। ijyate yo akhilādhāras taṃ drakṣyāmi jagatpatim ।। avāpa tam anantādim ahaṃ drakṣyāmi keśavam ।। yasya svarūpaṃ jānanti spṛśaty adya sa me hariḥ ।।
yo bhavaty avyayo vyāpī sa vīkṣyate mayādya ha ।। cakāra yogato yogaṃ sa mām ālāpayiṣyati ।। kartuṃ manuṣyatāṃ prāptaḥ svecchādehadhṛg avyayaḥ ।। so avatīrṇo jagatyarthe mām akrūreti vakṣyati ।।
yanmāyāṃ nālam uddhartuṃ jagat tasmai namo namaḥ ।। yogamāyām imāṃ martyās tasmai vidyātmane namaḥ ।। vedāntavedibhir viṣṇuḥ procyate yo nato asmi tam ।। sadasattvaṃ sa sattvena mayy asau yātu saumyatām ।।
puruṣapravaraṃ nityaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ harim ।। akrūro gokulaṃ prāptaḥ kiṃcit sūrye virājati ।। vatsamadhyagataṃ phulla- nīlotpaladalacchavim ।। pralambabāhum āyāma- tuṅgorasthalam unnasam ।।
tuṅgaraktanakhaṃ padbhyāṃ dharaṇyāṃ supratiṣṭhitam ।। sāndranīlalatāhastaṃ sitāmbhojāvataṃsakam ।। tasyānu balabhadraṃ ca dadarśa yadunandanam ।। meghamālāparivṛtaṃ kailāsādrim ivāparam ।।
pulakāñcitasarvāṅgas tadākrūro abhavad dvijāḥ ।। abhavad vāsudevo asau dvidhā yo ayaṃ vyavasthitaḥ ।। akrūro asmīti caraṇau nanāma śirasā hareḥ ।। saṃspṛśyākṛṣya ca prītyā sugāḍhaṃ pariṣasvaje ।।
tataḥ praviṣṭau sahasā tam ādāyātmamandiram ।। bhuktabhojyo yathānyāyam ācacakṣe tatas tayoḥ ।। yathā ca devakī devī dānavena durātmanā ।। yaṃ caivārthaṃ samuddiśya kaṃsena sa visarjitaḥ ।।
uvācākhilam etat tu jñātaṃ dānapate mayā ।। vicintyaṃ nānyathaitat te viddhi kaṃsaṃ hataṃ mayā ।। gopavṛddhāś ca yāsyanti ādāyopāyanaṃ bahu ।। trirātrābhyantare kaṃsaṃ haniṣyāmi sahānugam ।।
suṣvāpa balabhadraś ca nandagopagṛhe gataḥ ।। akrūreṇa samaṃ gantum udyatau mathurāṃ purīm ।। niśvasaṃś cātiduḥkhārtaḥ prāha cedaṃ parasparam ।। nāgarastrīkalālāpa- madhu śrotreṇa pāsyati ।।
cittam asya kathaṃ grāmya- gopagopīṣu yāsyati ।। prahṛtaṃ gopayoṣitsu nighṛṇena durātmanā ।। nāgarīṇām atīvaitat kaṭākṣekṣitam eva tu ।। bhavatīnāṃ punaḥ pārśvaṃ kayā yuktyā sameṣyati ।।
akrūrakrūrakeṇāpi hatāśena pratāritaḥ ।। yenemam akṣarāhlādaṃ nayaty anyatra no harim ।। ratham āruhya govindas tvaryatām asya vāraṇe ।। guravaḥ kiṃ kariṣyanti dagdhānāṃ virahāgninā ।।
nodyamaṃ kurute kaścid govindavinivartane ।। yāsām acyutavaktrābje yāti netrālibhogyatām ।। udvahiṣyanti paśyantaḥ svadehaṃ pulakāñcitam ।। govindavadanālokād atīvādya bhaviṣyati ।।
vistārikāntanayanā yā drakṣyanty anivāritam ।। uddhṛtāny adya netrāṇi vidhātrākaruṇātmanā ।। śaithilyam upayānty āśu kareṣu valayāny api ।। evam ārtāsu yoṣitsu ghṛṇā kasya na jāyate ।।
dūrīkṛto harir yena so api reṇur na lakṣyate ।। tatyāja vrajabhūbhāgaṃ saha rāmeṇa keśavaḥ ।। prāptā madhyāhnasamaye rāmākrūrajanārdanāḥ ।। yāvat karomi kālindyām āhnikārhaṇam ambhasi ।।
dadhyau brahma paraṃ viprāḥ praviśya yamunājale ।। kundāmalāṅgam unnidra- padmapattrāyatekṣaṇam ।। saṃstūyamānam udgandhi- vanamālāvibhūṣitam ।। cārukuṇḍalinaṃ mattam antarjalatale sthitam ।।
caturbāhum udārāṅgaṃ cakrādyāyudhabhūṣaṇam ।। śakracāpataḍinmālā- vicitram iva toyadam ।। dadarśa kṛṣṇam akliṣṭaṃ puṇḍarīkāvataṃsakam ।। saṃcintyamānaṃ manasā nāsāgranyastalocanaiḥ ।।
acintayad atho śīghraṃ katham atrāgatāv iti ।। tato niṣkramya salilād ratham abhyāgataḥ punaḥ ।। rāmakṛṣṇau yathā pūrvaṃ manuṣyavapuṣānvitau ।। saṃstūyamānau gandharvair munisiddhamahoragaiḥ ।।
tuṣṭāva sarvavijñāna- mayam acyutam īśvaram ।। vyāpine naikarūpaika- svarūpāya namo namaḥ ।। namo vijñānarūpāya parāya prakṛteḥ prabho ।। ātmā ca paramātmā ca tvam ekaḥ pañcadhā sthitaḥ ।।
brahmaviṣṇuśivādyābhiḥ kalpanābhir udīritaḥ ।। anākhyeyābhidhāna tvāṃ nato asmi parameśvaram ।। tad brahma paramaṃ nityam avikāri bhavān ajaḥ ।। tataḥ kṛṣṇācyutānanta viṣṇusaṃjñābhir īḍyase ।।
pradyumnāya namas tubhyam aniruddhāya te namaḥ ।। arghayām āsa sarveśaṃ dhūpapuṣpair manomayaiḥ ।। brahmabhūte ciraṃ sthitvā virarāma samādhitaḥ ।। ājagāma rathaṃ bhūyo nirgamya yamunāmbhasaḥ ।।
vismitākṣaṃ tadākrūraṃ taṃ ca kṛṣṇo abhyabhāṣata ।। vismayotphullanayano bhavān saṃlakṣyate yataḥ ।। tad atraiva hi paśyāmi mūrtimat purataḥ sthitam ।। tenāścaryapareṇāhaṃ bhavatā kṛṣṇa saṃgataḥ ।।
bibhemi kaṃsād dhig janma parapiṇḍopajīvinaḥ ।। vilokya mathurāṃ kṛṣṇaṃ rāmaṃ cāha sa yādavaḥ ।। yuvayor hi kṛte vṛddhaḥ kaṃsena sa nirasyate ।। praviṣṭau rāmakṛṣṇau ca rājamārgam upāgatau ।।
jagmatur līlayā vīrau prāptau bālagajāv iva ।। ayācetāṃ svarūpāṇi vāsāṃsi rucirāṇi tau ।। bahūny ākṣepavākyāni prāhoccai rāmakeśavau ।। pātayām āsa kopena rajakasya śiro bhuvi ।।
kṛṣṇarāmau mudāyuktau mālākāragṛhaṃ gatau ।। etau kasya kuto yātau manasācintayat tataḥ ।। sa tarkayām āsa tadā bhuvaṃ devāv upāgatau ।। bhuvaṃ viṣṭabhya hastābhyāṃ pasparśa śirasā mahīm ।।
dhanyo aham arcayiṣyāmīty āha tau mālyajīvikaḥ ।। cārūṇy etāni caitāni pradadau sa vilobhayan ।। puṣpāṇi tābhyāṃ cārūṇi gandhavanty amalāni ca ।। śrīs tvāṃ matsaṃśrayā bhadra na kadācit tyajiṣyati ।।
yāvad dharaṇisūryau ca saṃtatiḥ putrapautrikī ।। mamānusmaraṇaṃ prāpya divyalokam avāpsyasi ।। yuṣmatsaṃtatijātānāṃ dīrgham āyur bhaviṣyati ।। avāpsyati mahābhāga yāvat sūryo bhaviṣyati ।।
nirjagāma muniśreṣṭhā mālākāreṇa pūjitaḥ ।। dadarśa kubjām āyāntīṃ navayauvanagocarām ।। bhavatyā nīyate satyaṃ vadendīvaralocane ।। prāha sā lalitaṃ kubjā dadarśa ca balāt tataḥ ।।
naikavakreti vikhyātām anulepanakarmaṇi ।। bhavaty aham atīvāsya prasādadhanabhājanam ।। āvayor gātrasadṛśaṃ dīyatām anulepanam ।। anulepaṃ ca pradadau gātrayogyam athobhayoḥ ।।
sendracāpau virājantau sitakṛṣṇāv ivāmbudau ।। ullāpya tolayām āsa dvyaṅgulenāgrapāṇinā ।। tataḥ sā ṛjutāṃ prāptā yoṣitām abhavad varā ।। vastre pragṛhya govindaṃ vraja gehaṃ mameti vai ।।
visasarja jahāsoccai rāmasyālokya cānanam ।। dhanuḥśālāṃ tato yātau citramālyopaśobhitau ।। ākhyātaṃ sahasā kṛṣṇo gṛhītvāpūrayad dhanuḥ ।। cakārātimahāśabdaṃ mathurā tena pūritā ।।
rakṣisainyaṃ nikṛtyobhau niṣkrāntau kārmukālayāt ।। bhagnaṃ śrutvātha kaṃso api prāha cāṇūramuṣṭikau ।। mallayuddhena hantavyau mama prāṇaharau hi tau ।। dāsyāmy abhimatān kāmān nānyathaitan mahābalau ।।
hantavyau tadvadhād rājyaṃ sāmānyaṃ vo bhaviṣyati ।। provācoccais tvayā mattaḥ samājadvāri kuñjaraḥ ।। ghātanīyau niyuddhāya raṅgadvāram upāgatau ।। āsannamaraṇaḥ kaṃsaḥ sūryodayam udaikṣata ।।
rājamañceṣu cārūḍhāḥ saha bhṛtyair mahībhṛtaḥ ।। kṛtaḥ kaṃsena kaṃso api tuṅgamañce vyavasthitaḥ ।। anye ca vāramukhyānām anye nagarayoṣitām ।। akrūravasudevau ca mañcaprānte vyavasthitau ।।
antakāle api putrasya drakṣyāmīti mukhaṃ sthitā ।। hāhākārapare loka āsphoṭayati muṣṭike ।। madāsṛganuliptāṅgau gajadantavarāyudhau ।। praviṣṭau sumahāraṅgaṃ baladevajanārdanau ।।
kṛṣṇo ayaṃ balabhadro ayam iti lokasya vismayāt ।। prakṣiptaṃ śakaṭaṃ yena bhagnau ca yamalārjunau ।। dhṛto govardhano yena saptarātraṃ mahāgiriḥ ।। hato yena ca durvṛtto dṛśyate so ayam acyutaḥ ।।
prayāti līlayā yoṣin- manonayananandanaḥ ।। gopālo yādavaṃ vaṃśaṃ magnam abhyuddhariṣyati ।। avatīrṇo mahīm aṃśo nūnaṃ bhāraharo bhuvaḥ ।। uras tatāpa devakyāḥ snehasnutapayodharam ।।
yuveva vasudevo abhūd vihāyābhyāgatāṃ jarām ।। nāgarastrīsamūhaś ca draṣṭuṃ na virarāma tau ।। gajayuddhakṛtāyāsa- svedāmbukaṇikāñcitam ।। paribhūtākṣaraṃ janma saphalaṃ kriyatāṃ dṛśaḥ ।।
vipakṣakṣapaṇaṃ vakṣo bhujayugmaṃ ca bhāmini ।। kriyate balabhadrasya hāsyam īṣad vilokyatām ।। samupaiti na santy atra kiṃ vṛddhā yuktakāriṇaḥ ।। kva vajrakaṭhinābhoga- śarīro ayaṃ mahāsuraḥ ।।
