daiteyamallāś cāṇūra- pramukhās tv atidāruṇāḥ ।। yad bālabalinor yuddhaṃ madhyasthaiḥ samupekṣyate ।। vavarṣa harṣotkarṣaṃ ca janasya bhagavān hariḥ ।। pade pade tadā bhūmir na śīrṇā yat tad adbhutam ।।
niyuddhakuśalo daityo baladevena muṣṭikaḥ ।। kṣepaṇair muṣṭibhiś caiva kīlāvajranipātanaiḥ ।। aśastram atighoraṃ tat tayor yuddhaṃ sudāruṇam ।। yāvad yāvac ca cāṇūro yuyudhe hariṇā saha ।।
kṛṣṇo api yuyudhe tena līlayaiva jaganmayaḥ ।। balakṣayaṃ vivṛddhiṃ ca dṛṣṭvā cāṇūrakṛṣṇayoḥ ।। mṛdaṅgādiṣu vādyeṣu pratiṣiddheṣu tatkṣaṇāt ।। jaya govinda cāṇūraṃ jahi keśava dānavam ।।
cāṇūreṇa ciraṃ kālaṃ krīḍitvā madhusūdanaḥ ।। bhrāmayitvā śataguṇaṃ daityamallam amitrajit ।। bhūmāv āsphoṭitas tena cāṇūraḥ śatadhā bhavan ।। baladevas tu tatkālaṃ muṣṭikena mahābalaḥ ।।
so apy enaṃ muṣṭinā mūrdhni vakṣasy āhatya jānunā ।। kṛṣṇas tośalakaṃ bhūyo mallarājaṃ mahābalam ।। cāṇūre nihate malle muṣṭike ca nipātite ।। vavalgatus tadā raṅge kṛṣṇasaṃkarṣaṇāv ubhau ।।
kaṃso api koparaktākṣaḥ prāhoccair vyāyatān narān ।। nando api gṛhyatāṃ pāpo nigaḍair āśu badhyatām ।। valganti gopāḥ kṛṣṇena ye ceme sahitāḥ punaḥ ।। evam ājñāpayantaṃ taṃ prahasya madhusūdanaḥ ।।
keśeṣv ākṛṣya vigalat- kirīṭam avanītale ।। niḥśeṣajagadādhāra- guruṇā patatopari ।। mṛtasya keśeṣu tadā gṛhītvā madhusūdanaḥ ।। gauraveṇātimahatā paripātena kṛṣyatā ।।
kaṃse gṛhīte kṛṣṇena tadbhrātābhyāgato ruṣā ।। tato hāhākṛtaṃ sarvam āsīt tad raṅgamaṇḍalam ।। kṛṣṇo api vasudevasya pādau jagrāha satvaram ।। smṛtajanmoktavacanau tāv eva praṇatau sthitau ।।
tathāvayoḥ prasādena kṛtābhyuddhāra keśava ।। durvṛttanidhanārthāya tena naḥ pāvitaṃ kulam ।। vartate ca samastātmaṃs tvatto bhūtabhaviṣyatī ।। tvam eva yajño yajvā ca yajñānāṃ parameśvara ।।
devakyāś cātmaja prītyā tad atyantaviḍambanā ।। kva ca me mānuṣasyaiṣā jihvā putreti vakṣyati ।। kayā yuktyā vinā māyāṃ so asmattaḥ saṃbhaviṣyati ।। sa koṣṭhotsaṅgaśayano manuṣyāj jāyate katham ।।
devakīvasudevau tu dṛṣṭvā māyāṃ punar hariḥ ।। uvāca cāmba bhos tāta cirād utkaṇṭhitena tu ।। kurvatāṃ yāti yaḥ kālo mātāpitror apūjanam ।। gurudevadvijātīnāṃ mātāpitroś ca pūjanam ।।
kaṃsavīryapratāpābhyām āvayoḥ paravaśyayoḥ ।। pādānatibhiḥ sasnehaṃ cakratuḥ pauramānasam ।। vilepur mātaraś cāsya śokaduḥkhapariplutāḥ ।। tāḥ samāśvāsayām āsa svayam asrāvilekṣaṇaḥ ।।
abhyaṣiñcat tathaivainaṃ nijarājye hatātmajam ।। cakāra pretakāryāṇi ye cānye tatra ghātitāḥ ।। uvācājñāpaya vibho yat kāryam aviśaṅkayā ।। mayi bhṛtye sthite devān ājñāpayatu kiṃ nṛpaiḥ ।।
nṛvācā caiva bhagavān keśavaḥ kāryamānuṣaḥ ।। dīyatām ugrasenāya sudharmā bhavatā sabhā ।। sudharmākhyā sabhā yuktam asyāṃ yadubhir āsitum ।। dadau so api sudharmākhyāṃ sabhāṃ vāyoḥ puraṃdaraḥ ।।
bubhujuḥ sarvaratnāḍhyāṃ govindabhujasaṃśrayāḥ ।। śiṣyācāryakramaṃ vīrau khyāpayantau yadūttamau ।। astrārthaṃ jagmatur vīrau baladevajanārdanau ।। darśayāṃ cakratur vīrāv ācāram akhile jane ।।
ahorātraiś catuḥṣaṣṭyā tad adbhutam abhūd dvijāḥ ।। vicintya tau tadā mene prāptau candradivākarau ।। ūcatur vriyatāṃ yā te dātavyā gurudakṣiṇā ।। ayācata mṛtaṃ putraṃ prabhāse lavaṇārṇave ।।
ūcutuś ca guroḥ putro dīyatām iti sāgaram ।। uvāca na mayā putro hṛtaḥ sāṃdīpaner iti ।। jagrāha so asti salile mamaivāsurasūdana ।। kṛṣṇo jagrāha tasyāsthi- prabhavaṃ śaṅkham uttamam ।।
devānāṃ vardhate tejo yāty adharmaś ca saṃkṣayam ।। baladevaś ca balavāñ jitvā vaivasvataṃ yamam ।। pitre pradattavān kṛṣṇo balaś ca balināṃ varaḥ ।। prahṛṣṭapuruṣastrīkāv ubhau rāmajanārdanau ।।
astiḥ prāptiś ca bho viprās tayor bhartṛhaṇaṃ harim ।। hantum abhyāyayau kopāj jarāsaṃdhaḥ sayādavam ।। akṣauhiṇībhiḥ sainyasya trayoviṃśatibhir vṛtaḥ ।। yuyudhāte samaṃ tasya balinau balisainikaiḥ ।।
āyudhānāṃ purāṇānām ādāne munisattamāḥ ।। ākāśād āgatau vīrau tadā kaumodakī gadā ।। balasyābhimataṃ viprāḥ sunandaṃ muśalaṃ tathā ।। purīṃ viviśatur vīrāv ubhau rāmajanārdanau ।।
jīvamāne gate tatra kṛṣṇo mene na taṃ jitam ।। jitaś ca rāmakṛṣṇābhyām apakṛtya dvijottamāḥ ।। yadubhir māgadho rājā cakre kṛṣṇapurogamaiḥ ।। apakrānto jarāsaṃdhaḥ svalpasainyair balādhikaḥ ।।
tat tu saṃnidhimāhātmyaṃ viṣṇor aṃśasya cakriṇaḥ ।। astrāṇy anekarūpāṇi yad arātiṣu muñcati ।। tasyāripakṣakṣapaṇe kiyān udyamavistaraḥ ।। kurvan balavatā saṃdhiṃ hīnair yuddhaṃ karoty asau ।।
karoti daṇḍapātaṃ ca kvacid eva palāyanam ।। līlā jagatpates tasya cchandataḥ saṃpravartate ।। yadūnāṃ saṃnidhau sarve jahasur yādavās tadā ।। sutam icchaṃs tapas tepe yaducakrabhayāvaham ।।
dadau varaṃ ca tuṣṭo asau varṣe dvādaśake haraḥ ।। tadyoṣitsaṃgamāc cāsya putro abhūd alisaprabhaḥ ।। abhiṣicya vanaṃ yāto vajrāgrakaṭhinorasam ।। papraccha nāradaś cāsmai kathayām āsa yādavān ।।
gajāśvarathasaṃpannaiś cakāra paramodyamam ।। yādavān prati sāmarṣo munayo mathurāṃ purīm ।। yavanena samālokya māgadhaḥ saṃprayāsyati ।। hantā tad idam āyātaṃ yadūnāṃ vyasanaṃ dvidhā ।।
striyo api yatra yudhyeyuḥ kiṃ punar vṛṣṇiyādavāḥ ।। yādavābhibhavaṃ duṣṭā mā kurvan vairiṇo adhikam ।। yayāce dvādaśa purīṃ dvārakāṃ tatra nirmame ।। prākāraśatasaṃbādhām indrasyevāmarāvatīm ।।
āsanne kālayavane mathurāṃ ca svayaṃ yayau ।। nirjagāma sa govindo dadarśa yavanaś ca tam ।। anuyāto mahāyogi- cetobhiḥ prāpyate na yaḥ ।। yatra śete mahāvīryo mucukundo nareśvaraḥ ।।
pādena tāḍayām āsa kṛṣṇaṃ matvā sa durmatiḥ ।। tatkrodhajena munayo bhasmībhūtaś ca tatkṣaṇāt ।। nidrārtaḥ sumahākālaṃ nidrāṃ vavre varaṃ surān ।। dehajenāgninā sadyaḥ sa tu bhasmībhaviṣyati ।।
kas tvam ity āha so apy āha jāto ahaṃ śaśinaḥ kule ।। mucukundo api tac chrutvā vṛddhagārgyavacaḥ smaran ।। prāha jñāto bhavān viṣṇor aṃśas tvaṃ parameśvaraḥ ।। dvāparānte harer janma yaduvaṃśe bhaviṣyati ।।
tathā hi sumahat tejo nālaṃ soḍhum ahaṃ tava ।। vākyaṃ tam iti hovāca yuṣmatpādasulālitam ।। na śekus te mahat tejas tat tejo na sahāmy aham ।। saṃprasīda prapannārti- hartā hara mamāśubham ।।
medinī gaganaṃ vāyur āpo agnis tvaṃ tathā pumān ।। śabdādihīnam ajaraṃ vṛddhikṣayavivarjitam ।। siddhāś cāpsarasas tvatto manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ khagāḥ ।। yac ca bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyad vā kiṃcid atra carācare ।।
tat sarvaṃ tvaṃ jagatkartar nāsti kiṃcit tvayā vinā ।। tāpatrayābhibhūtena na prāptā nirvṛtiḥ kvacit ।। mayā nātha gṛhītāni tāni tāpāya me abhavan ।। bhāryā bhṛtyajanā ye ca śabdādyā viṣayāḥ prabho ।।
pariṇāme ca deveśa tāpātmakam abhūn mama ।। mattaḥ sāhāyyakāmo abhūc chāśvatī kutra nirvṛtiḥ ।। śāśvatī prāpyate kena parameśvara nirvṛtiḥ ।। avāpya pāpān paśyanti pretarājānam antarā ।।
prāpnuvanti mahad duḥkhaṃ viśvarūpam idaṃ tava ।। mamatvāgādhagartānte bhramāmi parameśvara ।। prāheśaḥ sarvabhūtānām anādinidhano hariḥ ।। avyāhataparaiśvaryo matprasādopabṛṃhitaḥ ।।
jātismaro matprasādāt tato mokṣam avāpsyasi ।। guhāmukhād viniṣkrānto dadṛśe so alpakān narān ।। naranārāyaṇasthānaṃ prayayau gandhamādanam ।। jagrāha mathurām etya hastyaśvasyandanojjvalam ।।
parābhibhavaniḥśaṅkaṃ babhūva ca yadoḥ kulam ।। jñātidarśanasotkaṇṭhaḥ prayayau nandagokulam ।। tathaivābhyavadat premṇā bahumānapuraḥsaram ।। hāsaṃ cakre samaṃ kaiścid gopagopījanais tathā ।।
gopyaś ca premamuditāḥ procuḥ serṣyam athāparāḥ ।। kaccid āste sukhaṃ kṛṣṇaś calatpremarasākulaḥ ।। saubhāgyamānam adhikaṃ karoti kṣaṇasauhṛdaḥ ।। apy asau mātaraṃ draṣṭuṃ sakṛd apy āgamiṣyati ।।
yad asmābhir vinā tena vināsmākaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। na tyaktas tatkṛte śmābhir akṛtajñas tato hi saḥ ।। karoti kṛṣṇo vaktavyaṃ bhavatā vacanāmṛtam ।। apetaprītir asmāsu durdarśaḥ pratibhāti naḥ ।।
jahasuḥ susvaraṃ gopyo hariṇā kṛṣṭacetasaḥ ।। rāmeṇāśvāsitā gopyaḥ kṛṣṇasyātimadhusvaraiḥ ।। kathāś cakāra premṇā ca saha tair vrajabhūmiṣu ।। mānuṣacchadmarūpasya śeṣasya dharaṇībhṛtaḥ ।।
upabhogārtham atyarthaṃ varuṇaḥ prāha vāruṇīm ।। anantasyopabhogāya tasya gaccha mude śubhe ।। vṛndāvanataṭotpanna- kadambatarukoṭare ।। āghrāya madirāharṣam avāpātha purātanam ।।
patantīṃ vīkṣya munayaḥ prayayau paramāṃ mudam ।। upagīyamāno lalitaṃ gītavādyaviśāradaiḥ ।। āgaccha yamune snātum icchāmīty āha vihvalaḥ ।। nājagāma tataḥ kruddho halaṃ jagrāha lāṅgalī ।।
pāpe nāyāsi nāyāsi gamyatām icchayānyataḥ ।। yatrāste baladevo asau plāvayām āsa tad vanam ।। prasīdety abravīd rāmaṃ muñca māṃ muśalāyudha ।। so ahaṃ tvāṃ halapātena nayiṣyāmi sahasradhā ।।
bhūbhāge plāvite tatra mumoca yamunāṃ balaḥ ।। avataṃsotpalaṃ cāru gṛhītvaikaṃ ca kuṇḍalam ।। samudrārhe tathā vastre nīle lakṣmīr ayacchata ।। nīlāmbaradharaḥ sragvī śuśubhe kāntisaṃyutaḥ ।।
māsadvayena yātaś ca punaḥ sa mathurāṃ purīm ।। upayeme balas tasyāṃ jajñāte niśaṭholmukau ।। rukmiṇī tasya duhitā rukmī caiva suto dvijāḥ ।। na dadau yācate caināṃ rukmī dveṣeṇa cakriṇe ।।
bhīṣmako rukmiṇā sārdhaṃ rukmiṇīm uruvikramaḥ ।। bhīṣmakasya puraṃ jagmuḥ śiśupālaś ca kuṇḍinam ।। prayayau kuṇḍinaṃ draṣṭuṃ vivāhaṃ caidyabhūpateḥ ।। vipakṣabhāvam āsādya rāmādyeṣv eva bandhuṣu ।।
śiśupālo jarāsaṃdhaḥ śālvādyāś ca mahībhṛtaḥ ।। nirjitāś ca samāgamya rāmādyair yadupuṃgavaiḥ ।। kṛtvā pratijñāṃ rukmī ca hantuṃ kṛṣṇam abhidrutaḥ ।। nirjitaḥ pātitaś corvyāṃ līlayaiva sa cakriṇā ।।
rākṣasena vidhānena saṃprāpto madhusūdanaḥ ।। jahāra śambaro yaṃ vai yo jaghāna ca śambaram ।। śambaraś ca mahāvīryaḥ pradyumnena kathaṃ hataḥ ।। mamaiṣa hanteti dvijā hṛtavān kālaśambaraḥ ।।
kallolajanitāvarte sughore makarālaye ।। na mamāra ca tasyāpi jaṭharānaladīpitaḥ ।। ghātito asuravaryāya śambarāya niveditaḥ ।। kārayām āsa sūdānām ādhipatyam aninditā ।।
kumāraṃ manmathataror dagdhasya prathamāṅkuram ।। ity evaṃ kautukāviṣṭāṃ tāṃ tanvīṃ prāha nāradaḥ ।। śambareṇa hṛtaḥ kṛṣṇa- tanayaḥ sūtikāgṛhāt ।। nararatnam idaṃ subhru viśrabdhā paripālaya ।।
bālyād evātirāgeṇa rūpātiśayamohitā ।। sābhilāṣā tadā sā tu babhūva gajagāminī ।। prasajjantīṃ tu tām āha sa kārṣṇiḥ kamalalocanaḥ ।। mātṛbhāvaṃ vihāyaiva kimarthaṃ vartase anyathā ।।
tanayaṃ tvām ayaṃ viṣṇor hṛtavān kālaśambaraḥ ।। sā tu roditi te mātā kāntādyāpy ativatsalā ।। krodhākulīkṛtamanā yuyudhe ca mahābalaḥ ।। sapta māyā vyatikramya māyāṃ saṃyuyuje aṣṭamīm ।।
utpatya ca tayā sārdham ājagāma pituḥ puram ।। rukmiṇī cābravīt premṇā āsaktadṛṣṭir aninditā ।। asmin vayasi putro me pradyumno yadi jīvati ।। harer apatyaṃ suvyaktaṃ bhavān vatsa bhaviṣyati ।।
antaḥpuravarāṃ devīṃ rukmiṇīṃ prāha harṣitaḥ ।। hṛto yenābhavat pūrvaṃ putras te sūtikāgṛhāt ।। śambarasya na bhāryeyaṃ śrūyatām atra kāraṇam ।। śambaraṃ mohayām āsa māyārūpeṇa rukmiṇi ।।
darśayām āsa daityasya tasyeyaṃ madirekṣaṇā ।। viśaṅkā nātra kartavyā snuṣeyaṃ tava śobhanā ।। nagarī ca samastā sā sādhu sādhv ity abhāṣata ।। avāpa vismayaṃ sarvo dvāravatyāṃ janas tadā ।।
suṣeṇaṃ cāruguptaṃ ca bhadracāruṃ tathāparam ।। rukmiṇy ajanayat putrān kanyāṃ cārumatīṃ tathā ।। kālindī mitravindā ca satyā nāgnajitī tathā ।। madrarājasutā cānyā suśīlā śīlamaṇḍalā ।।
ṣoḍaśātra sahasrāṇi strīṇām anyāni cakriṇaḥ ।। svayaṃvarasthāṃ jagrāha sāpi taṃ tanayaṃ hareḥ ।। aniruddho raṇe ruddho vīryodadhir ariṃdamaḥ ।। dauhitrāya dadau rukmī spardhayann api śauriṇā ।।
rukmiṇo nagaraṃ jagmur nāmnā bhojakaṭaṃ dvijāḥ ।। kaliṅgarājapramukhā rukmiṇaṃ vākyam abruvan ।। tan nayāmo balaṃ tasmād dyūtenaiva mahādyute ।। sabhāyāṃ saha rāmeṇa cakre dyūtaṃ ca vai tadā ।।
dvitīye divase cānyat sahasraṃ rukmiṇā jitaḥ ।। balabhadraprapannāni rukmī dyūtavidāṃ varaḥ ।। dantān vidarśayan mūḍho rukmī cāha madoddhataḥ ।। mṛṣaivākṣāvalepatvād yo ayaṃ mene akṣakovidam ।।
rukmiṇaṃ cāpi durvākyaṃ kopaṃ cakre halāyudhaḥ ।। glahaṃ jagrāha rukmī ca tatas tv akṣān apātayat ।। mameti rukmī prāhoccair alīkoktair alaṃ balam ।। evaṃ tvayā ced vijitaṃ na mayā vijitaṃ katham ।।
baladevasya taṃ kopaṃ vardhayantī mahātmanaḥ ।। anuktvā vacanaṃ kiṃcit kṛtaṃ bhavati karmaṇā ।। jaghānāṣṭāpadenaiva rukmiṇaṃ sa mahābalaḥ ।। babhañja dantān kupito yaiḥ prakāśaṃ jahāsa saḥ ।।
jaghāna ye tatpakṣās tān bhūbhṛtaḥ kupito balaḥ ।। tad rājamaṇḍalaṃ sarvaṃ babhūva kupite bale ।। novāca vacanaṃ kiṃcid rukmiṇībalayor bhayāt ।। dvārakām ājagāmātha yaducakraṃ sakeśavam ।।
ājagāmātha munayo mattairāvatapṛṣṭhagaḥ ।। kathayām āsa daityasya narakasya viceṣṭitam ।। praśamaṃ sarvaduḥkhāni nītāni madhusūdana ।। pralambādyās tathā keśī te sarve nihatās tvayā ।।
nāśaṃ nītās tvayā sarve ye anye jagadupadravāḥ ।। yajñe yajñahaviḥ prāśya tṛptiṃ yānti divaukasaḥ ।। tac chrutvā tatpratīkāra- prayatnaṃ kartum arhasi ।। karoti sarvabhūtānām apaghātam ariṃdama ।।
hatvā tu so asuraḥ kanyā rurodha nijamandire ।। mandarasya tathā śṛṅgaṃ hṛtavān maṇiparvatam ।। jahāra so asuro adityā vāñchaty airāvataṃ dvipam ।। yad atra pratikartavyaṃ tat svayaṃ parimṛśyatām ।।
gṛhītvā vāsavaṃ haste samuttasthau varāsanāt ।। satyabhāmāṃ samāropya yayau prāgjyotiṣaṃ puram ।। tato jagāma sumanāḥ paśyatāṃ dvārakaukasām ।। ācitaṃ bhairavaiḥ pāśaiḥ parasainyanivāraṇe ।।
tato muraḥ samuttasthau taṃ jaghāna ca keśavaḥ ।। cakradhārāgninirdagdhāṃś cakāra śalabhān iva ।। prāgjyotiṣapuraṃ dhīmāṃs tvarāvān samupādravat ।। kṛṣṇasya yatra govindo jaghne daityān sahasraśaḥ ।।
kṣiptvā cakraṃ dvidhā cakre cakrī daiteyacakrahā ।। upatasthe jagannāthaṃ vākyaṃ cedam athābravīt ।। tvatsaṃsparśabhavaḥ putras tadāyaṃ mayy ajāyata ।। gṛhāṇa kuṇḍale ceme pālayāsya ca saṃtatim ।।
aṃśena lokam āyātaḥ prasādasumukha prabho ।। jagatsvarūpo yaś ca tvaṃ stūyase acyuta kiṃ mayā ।। sarvabhūtātmabhūtātmā stūyase acyuta kiṃ mayā ।। yadā tadā stutir nāsti kimarthaṃ te pravartatām ।।
tat kṣamyatām adoṣāya matsutaḥ sa nipātitaḥ ।। ratnāni narakāvāsāj jagrāha munisattamāḥ ।। śatādhikāni dadṛśe sahasrāṇi dvijottamāḥ ।। kāmbojānāṃ tathāśvānāṃ niyutāny ekaviṃśatim ।।
prāpayām āsa govindaḥ sadyo narakakiṃkaraiḥ ।। āropayām āsa harir garuḍe patageśvare ।। adityāḥ kuṇḍale dātuṃ jagāma tridaśālayam ।। sabhāryaṃ ca hṛṣīkeśaṃ līlayaiva vahan yayau ।।
upatasthus tato devāḥ sārghapātrā janārdanam ।। sitābhraśikharākāraṃ praviśya dadṛśe aditim ।। dadau narakanāśaṃ ca śaśaṃsāsyai janārdanaḥ ।। tuṣṭāvāditir avyagraṃ kṛtvā tatpravaṇaṃ manaḥ ।।
sanātanātman bhūtātman sarvātman bhūtabhāvana ।। sitadīrghādiniḥśeṣa- kalpanāparivarjita ।। saṃdhyā rātrir ahar bhūmir gaganaṃ vāyur ambu ca ।। sṛṣṭisthitivināśānāṃ kartā kartṛpatir bhavān ।।
māyābhir etad vyāptaṃ te jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। ahaṃ mameti bhāvo atra yayā samupajāyate ।। yaiḥ svadharmaparair nātha narair ārādhito bhavān ।। brahmādyāḥ sakalā devā manuṣyāḥ paśavas tathā ।।
ārādhya tvām abhīpsante kāmān ātmabhavakṣaye ।। mayā tvaṃ putrakāminyā vairipakṣakṣayāya ca ।। kaupīnācchādanaprāyā vāñchā kalpadrumād api ।। tat prasīdākhilajagan- māyāmohakarāvyaya ।।
namas te cakrahastāya śārṅgahastāya te namaḥ ।। na jānāmi paraṃ yat te prasīda parameśvara ।। adityaivaṃ stuto viṣṇuḥ prahasyāha surāraṇim ।। mātā devi tvam asmākaṃ prasīda varadā bhava ।।
ajeyaḥ puruṣavyāghra martyaloke bhaviṣyasi ।। satyabhāmā praṇamyāha prasīdeti punaḥ punaḥ ।। bhaviṣyaty anavadyāṅgi sarvakāmā bhaviṣyasi ।। yathāvat pūjayām āsa bahumānapuraḥsaram ।।
devodyānāni sarvāṇi nandanādīni sattamāḥ ।। śaityāhlādakaraṃ divyaṃ tāmrapallavaśobhitam ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā prāha govindaṃ satyabhāmā dvijottamāḥ ।। yadi te tad vacaḥ satyaṃ satyātyarthaṃ priyeti me ।।
na me jāmbavatī tādṛg abhīṣṭā na ca rukmiṇī ।। satyaṃ tad yadi govinda nopacārakṛtaṃ vacaḥ ।। sapatnīnām ahaṃ madhye śobheyam iti kāmaye ।। āropayām āsa haris tam ūcur vanarakṣiṇaḥ ।।
pārijātaṃ na govinda hartum arhasi pādapam ।। utpādito ayaṃ na kṣemī gṛhītvainaṃ gamiṣyasi ।। avaśyam asya devendro vikṛtiṃ kṛṣṇa yāsyati ।। vipākakaṭu yat karma na tac chaṃsanti paṇḍitāḥ ।।
ity ukte tair uvācaitān satyabhāmātikopinī ।। sāmānyaḥ sarvalokānāṃ yady eṣo amṛtamanthane ।। yathā surā yathā cendur yathā śrīr vanarakṣiṇaḥ ।। bhartṛbāhumahāgarvād ruṇaddhy enam atho śacī ।।
satyabhāmā vadaty evaṃ bhartṛgarvoddhatākṣaram ।। madbhartur harato vṛkṣaṃ tat kāraya nivāraṇam ।। pārijātaṃ tathāpy enaṃ mānuṣī hārayāmi te ।। śacī cotsāhayām āsa tridaśādhipatiṃ patim ।।
pravṛktaḥ pārijātārtham indro yodhayituṃ dvijāḥ ।। babhūvus tridaśāḥ sajjāḥ śakre vajrakare sthite ।। śakraṃ devaparīvāraṃ yuddhāya samupasthitam ।। mumoca ca śaravrātaṃ sahasrāyutasaṃmitam ।।
mumucus tridaśāḥ sarve śastrāṇy astrāṇy anekaśaḥ ।। ciccheda līlayaiveśo jagatāṃ madhusūdanaḥ ।। cacāla khaṇḍaśaḥ kṛttvā bālapannagadehavat ।। pṛthivyāṃ pātayām āsa bhagavān devakīsutaḥ ।।
cakāra śaurir arkendū dṛṣṭipātahataujasau ।। cakravicchinnaśūlāgrā rudrā bhuvi nipātitāḥ ।। śārṅgiṇā preritāḥ sarve vyomni śālmalitūlavat ।। bhakṣayann ahanad devān dānavāṃś ca sadā khagaḥ ।।
parasparaṃ vavarṣāte dhārābhir iva toyadau ।। devaiḥ sametair yuyudhe śakreṇa ca janārdanaḥ ।। jagrāha vāsavo vajraṃ kṛṣṇaś cakraṃ sudarśanam ।। vajracakradharau dṛṣṭvā devarājajanārdanau ।।
na mumoca tadā cakraṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt ।। satyabhāmābravīd vākyaṃ palāyanaparāyaṇam ।। pārijātasragābhogāt tvām upasthāsyate śacī ।। apaśyato yathāpūrvaṃ praṇayābhyāgatāṃ śacīm ।।
nīyatāṃ pārijāto ayaṃ devāḥ santu gatavyathāḥ ।। na dadarśa gṛhāyātām upacāreṇa māṃ śacī ।। tataḥ kṛtavatī śakra bhavatā saha vigraham ।। rūpeṇa yaśasā caiva bhavet strī kā na garvitā ।।
prāha cainām alaṃ caṇḍi sakhi khedātivistaraiḥ ।। jitasya tena me vrīḍā jāyate viśvarūpiṇā ।। prahasya bhāvagambhīram uvācedaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। kṣantavyaṃ bhavataivaitad aparādhakṛtaṃ mama ।।
gṛhīto ayaṃ mayā śakra satyāvacanakāraṇāt ।। tavaivaitat praharaṇaṃ śakra vairividāraṇam ।। jānīmas tvāṃ bhagavato anantasaukhyavido vayam ।। jagataḥ śalyaniṣkarṣaṃ karoṣy asurasūdana ।।
martyaloke tvayā mukte nāyaṃ saṃsthāsyate bhuvi ।। prayuktaiḥ siddhagandharvaiḥ stūyamānas tv atharṣibhiḥ ।। tataḥ śaṅkham upādhmāya dvārakopari saṃsthitaḥ ।। avatīryātha garuḍāt satyabhāmāsahāyavān ।।
yam abhyetya janaḥ sarvo jātiṃ smarati paurvikīm ।। tatas te yādavāḥ sarve devagandhān amānuṣān ।। kiṃkaraiḥ samupānītaṃ hastyaśvādi tato dhanam ।। tataḥ kāle śubhe prāpta upayeme janārdanaḥ ।।
ekasminn eva govindaḥ kālenāsāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। ṣoḍaśa strīsahasrāṇi śatam ekaṃ tathādhikam ।। ekaikaśaś ca tāḥ kanyā menire madhusūdanam ।। uvāsa viprāḥ sarvāsāṃ viśvarūpadharo hariḥ ।।
bhānvādikāṃś ca vai putrān satyabhāmā vyajāyata ।। babhūvur jāmbavatyāś ca sāmbādyā bāhuśālinaḥ ।। saṃgrāmajitpradhānās tu śaibyāyāṃ cābhavan sutāḥ ।। avāpa lakṣmaṇā putrān kālindyāś ca śrutādayaḥ ।।
aṣṭāyutāni putrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi śataṃ tathā ।। pradyumnād aniruddho abhūd vajras tasmād ajāyata ।। bāṇasya tanayām ūṣām upayeme dvijottamāḥ ।। chinnaṃ sahasraṃ bāhūnāṃ yatra bāṇasya cakriṇā ।।
kathaṃ kṣayaṃ ca bāṇasya bāhūnāṃ kṛtavān hariḥ ।। mahat kautūhalaṃ jātaṃ śrotum etāṃ kathāṃ śubhām ।। tataḥ sakalacittajñā gaurī tām āha bhāminīm ।। alam ity anutāpena bhartrā tvam api raṃsyase ।।
ko vā bhartā mamety enāṃ punar apy āha pārvatī ।। kariṣyati sa te bhartā rājaputri bhaviṣyati ।। tataḥ prabuddhā puruṣam apaśyantī tam utsukā ।। bāṇasya mantrī kumbhāṇḍaś citralekhā tu tatsutā ।।
yadā lajjākulā nāsya kathayām āsa sā sakhī ।। devyā tathaiva tatprāptau yo abhyupāyaḥ kuruṣva tam ।। manuṣyāṃś cābhilikhyāsau citralekhāpy adarśayat ।। manuṣyeṣu dadau dṛṣṭiṃ teṣv apy andhakavṛṣṇiṣu ।।
pradyumnadarśane vrīḍā- dṛṣṭiṃ ninye tato dvijāḥ ।। yayau dvāravatīm ūṣāṃ samāśvāsya tataḥ sakhī ।। bāṇo api praṇipatyāgre tataś cāha trilocanam ।। bhaviṣyati vinā yuddhaṃ bhārāya mama kiṃ bhujaiḥ ।।
piśitāśijanānandaṃ prāpsyasi tvaṃ tadā raṇam ।। bhagnaṃ dhvajam athālokya hṛṣṭo harṣaṃ paraṃ yayau ।। aniruddham athāninye citralekhā varā sakhī ।। vijñāya rakṣiṇo gatvā śaśaṃsur daityabhūpateḥ ।।
jaghāna parighaṃ lauham ādāya paravīrahā ।। yudhyamāno yathāśakti yadā vīreṇa nirjitaḥ ।। tataś ca pannagāstreṇa babandha yadunandanam ।। yadūnām ācacakṣe taṃ baddhaṃ bāṇena nāradaḥ ।।
yoṣitā pratyayaṃ jagmur yādavā nāma vairiti ।। balapradyumnasahito bāṇasya prayayau puram ।। yayau bāṇapurābhyāśaṃ nītvā tān saṃkṣayaṃ hariḥ ।। bāṇarakṣārtham atyarthaṃ yuyudhe śārṅgadhanvanā ।।
avāpa baladevo api samaṃ saṃmīlitekṣaṇaḥ ।। vaiṣṇavena jvareṇāśu kṛṣṇadehān nirākṛtaḥ ।। taṃ vīkṣya kṣamyatām asyety āha devaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। ātmany eva layaṃ ninye bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ ।।
vijvarās te bhaviṣyantīty uktvā cainaṃ yayau hariḥ ।। dānavānāṃ balaṃ viṣṇuś cūrṇayām āsa līlayā ।। yuyudhe śaṃkaraś caiva kārttikeyaś ca śauriṇā ।। cukṣubhuḥ sakalā lokāḥ śastrāstrair bahudhārditāḥ ।।
menire tridaśā yatra vartamāne mahāhave ।। tataḥ praṇeśur daiteyāḥ pramathāś ca samantataḥ ।। na śaśāka tadā yoddhuṃ kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā ।। kṛṣṇahuṃkāranirdhūta- śaktiś cāpayayau guhaḥ ।।
nīte pramathasainye ca saṃkṣayaṃ śārṅgadhanvanā ।। bāṇas tatrāyayau yoddhuṃ kṛṣṇakārṣṇibalaiḥ saha ।। vivyādha bāṇaiḥ pradyumno dharmataś cāpalāyataḥ ।। balaṃ balena dadṛśe bāṇo bāṇaiś ca cakriṇaḥ ।।
parasparaṃ tu saṃdīptān kāyatrāṇavibhedinaḥ ।। bibheda keśavaṃ bāṇo bāṇaṃ vivyādha cakradhṛk ।। parasparakṣatiparau parighāṃś ca tato dvijāḥ ।। prācuryeṇa harir bāṇaṃ hantuṃ cakre tato manaḥ ।।
jagrāha daityacakrārir hariś cakraṃ sudarśanam ।। nagnā daiteyavidyābhūt koṭarī purato hareḥ ।। mumoca bāṇam uddiśya chettuṃ bāhuvanaṃ ripoḥ ।। chedaṃ cakre asurasyāśu śastrāstrakṣepaṇād drutam ।।
mumukṣur bāṇanāśāya vijñātas tripuradviṣā ।। vilokya bāṇaṃ dordaṇḍa- cchedāsṛksrāvavarṣiṇam ।। pareśaṃ paramātmānam anādinidhanaṃ param ।। līleyaṃ tava ceṣṭā hi daityānāṃ vadhalakṣaṇā ।।
tat tvayā nānṛtaṃ kāryaṃ yan mayā vyāhṛtaṃ vacaḥ ।। mayā dattavaro daityas tatas tvāṃ kṣamayāmy aham ।। prasannavadano bhūtvā gatāmarṣo asuraṃ prati ।। tvadvākyagauravād etan mayā cakraṃ nivartitam ।।
matto avibhinnam ātmānaṃ draṣṭum arhasi śaṃkara ।। avidyāmohitātmānaḥ puruṣā bhinnadarśinaḥ ।। tadbandhaphaṇino neśur garuḍānilaśoṣitāḥ ।। ājagmur dvārakāṃ rāma- kārṣṇidāmodarāḥ purīm ।।
jigāya śakraṃ śarvaṃ ca sarvadevāṃś ca līlayā ।। kathyatāṃ tan muniśreṣṭha paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। narāvatāre kṛṣṇena dagdhā vārāṇasī yathā ।। avatīrṇas tvam ity ukto janair ajñānamohitaiḥ ।।
dūtaṃ ca preṣayām āsa sa kṛṣṇāya dvijottamāḥ ।। vāsudevātmakaṃ mūḍha muktvā sarvam aśeṣataḥ ।। ātmano jīvitārthaṃ ca tathā me praṇatiṃ vraja ।। ity uktaḥ sa prahasyaiva dūtaṃ prāha janārdanaḥ ।।
vācyaś ca pauṇḍrako gatvā tvayā dūta vaco mama ।। gṛhītacihna evāham āgamiṣyāmi te puram ।। ājñāpūrvaṃ ca yad idam āgaccheti tvayoditam ।। yathā tvatto bhayaṃ bhūyo naiva kiṃcid bhaviṣyati ।।
garutmantaṃ samāruhya tvaritaṃ tatpuraṃ yayau ।। sarvasainyaparīvāra- pārṣṇigrāham upāyayau ।। pauṇḍrako vāsudevo asau keśavābhimukhaṃ yayau ।। cakraśaṅkhagadāpāṇiṃ pāṇinā vidhṛtāmbujam ।।
vakṣasthalakṛtaṃ cāsya śrīvatsaṃ dadṛśe hariḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā taṃ bhāvagambhīraṃ jahāsa madhusūdanaḥ ।। nistriṃśarṣṭigadāśūla- śaktikārmukaśālinā ।। gadācakrātipātaiś ca sūdayām āsa tadbalam ।।
uvāca pauṇḍrakaṃ mūḍham ātmacihnopalakṣaṇam ।। samutsṛjeti cihnāni tat te saṃpādayāmy aham ।। garutmān eṣa nirdiṣṭaḥ samārohatu te dhvajam ।। pothito gadayā bhagno garutmāṃś ca garutmatā ।।
yuyudhe vāsudevena mitrasyāpacitau sthitaḥ ।। kāśipuryāṃ sa cikṣepa kurvaṃl lokasya vismayam ।। reme dvāravatīṃ prāpto amaraḥ svargagato yathā ।। janaḥ kim etad ity āha kenety atyantavismitaḥ ।।
purohitena sahitas toṣayām āsa śaṃkaram ।। varaṃ vṛṇīṣveti tadā taṃ provāca nṛpātmajam ।। samuttiṣṭhatu kṛṣṇasya tvatprasādān maheśvara ।। mahākṛtyā samuttasthau tasyaivāgniniveśanāt ।।
kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kupitā kṛtvā dvāravatīṃ yayau ।। yayau śaraṇyaṃ jagatāṃ śaraṇaṃ madhusūdanam ।। jahi kṛtyām imām ugrāṃ vahnijvālājaṭākulām ।। tad agnimālājaṭilaṃ jvālodgārātibhīṣaṇam ।।
tataḥ sā cakravidhvastā kṛtyā māheśvarī tadā ।। kṛtyā vārāṇasīm eva praviveśa tvarānvitā ।। tataḥ kāśibalaṃ bhūri pramathānāṃ tathā balam ।। śastrāstramokṣabahulaṃ dagdhvā tad balam ojasā ।।
prabhūtabhṛtyapaurāṃ tāṃ sāśvamātaṅgamānavām ।। jvālāparivṛtāśeṣa- gṛhaprākāratoraṇām ।। tac cakraṃ prasphuraddīpti viṣṇor abhyāyayau karam ।। mune parākramaṃ śauryaṃ tan no vyākhyātum arhasi ।।
tat kathyatāṃ mahābhāga yad anyat kṛtavān balaḥ ।। anantenāprameyena śeṣeṇa dharaṇībhṛtā ।। balād ādattavān vīraḥ sāmbo jāmbavatīsutaḥ ।। bhīṣmadroṇādayaś caiva babandhur yudhi nirjitam ।।
munayaḥ praticakruś ca tān vihantuṃ mahodyamam ।। mokṣyanti te madvacanād yāsyāmy eko hi kauravān ।। bāhyopavanamadhye abhūn na viveśa ca tat puram ।। gṛhītvā vidhivat sarvaṃ tatas tān āha kauravān ।।
ājñāpayaty ugrasenaḥ sāmbam āśu vimuñcata ।। karṇaduryodhanādyāś ca cukrudhur dvijasattamāḥ ।। arājārhaṃ yador vaṃśam avekṣya muśalāyudham ।। ājñāṃ kurukulotthānāṃ yādavaḥ kaḥ pradāsyati ।।
tad alaṃ pāṇḍuraiś chattrair nṛpayogyair alaṃkṛtaiḥ ।। vimokṣyāmo na bhavato nograsenasya śāsanāt ।। na nāma sā kṛtā keyam ājñā svāmini bhṛtyataḥ ।। ko doṣo bhavatāṃ nītir yat prīṇāty anapekṣitā ।।
premṇaiva na tad asmākaṃ kulād yuṣmatkulocitam ।। kṛtaikaniścayāḥ sarve viviśur gajasāhvayam ।। utthāya pārṣṇyā vasudhāṃ jaghāna sa halāyudhaḥ ।। uvāca cātitāmrākṣo bhrukuṭīkuṭilānanaḥ ।।
kauravāṇām ādhipatyam asmākaṃ kila kālajam ।। ājñāṃ pratīcched dharmeṇa saha devaiḥ śacīpatiḥ ।। dhiṅ manuṣyaśatocchiṣṭe tuṣṭir eṣāṃ nṛpāsane ।। bibharti yasya bhṛtyānāṃ so apy eṣāṃ na mahīpatiḥ ।।
adya niṣkauravām urvīṃ kṛtvā yāsyāmi tāṃ purīm ।। duḥśāsanādīn bhūriṃ ca bhūriśravasam eva ca ।। yamajau kauravāṃś cānyān hanyāṃ sāśvarathadvipān ।। dvārakām ugrasenādīn gatvā drakṣyāmi bāndhavān ।।
bhārāvataraṇe śīghraṃ devarājena coditaḥ ।। bhāgīrathyāṃ kṣipāmy āśu nagaraṃ nāgasāhvayam ।। prākāravapre vinyasya cakarṣa muśalāyudhaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā saṃkṣubdhahṛdayāś cukruśuḥ sarvakauravāḥ ।।
upasaṃhriyatāṃ kopaḥ prasīda muśalāyudha ।। avijñātaprabhāvāṇāṃ kṣamyatām aparādhinām ।। niṣkramya svapurīṃ tūrṇaṃ kauravā munisattamāḥ ।। kṣāntam eva mayety āha balo balavatāṃ varaḥ ।।
eṣa prabhāvo rāmasya balaśauryavato dvijāḥ ।। preṣayām āsur udvāha- dhanabhāryāsamanvitam ।। kṛtaṃ yad anyad evābhūt tad api śrūyatāṃ dvijāḥ ।। sakhābhavan mahāvīryo dvivido nāma vānaraḥ ।।
vairānubandhaṃ balavān sa cakāra surān prati ।। kariṣye sarvadevānāṃ tasmād eṣa pratikriyām ।। tato vidhvaṃsayām āsa yajñān ajñānamohitaḥ ।। dadāha capalo deśaṃ puragrāmāntarāṇi ca ।।
śailān utpāṭya toyeṣu mumocāmbunidhau tathā ।। tenātikṣobhitaś cābdhir udvelo jāyate dvijāḥ ।। kāmarūpaṃ mahārūpaṃ kṛtvā sasyāny anekaśaḥ ।। tena viprakṛtaṃ sarvaṃ jagad etad durātmanā ।।
kadācid raivatodyāne papau pānaṃ halāyudhaḥ ।। udgīyamāno vilasal- lalanāmaulimadhyagaḥ ।। tataḥ sa vānaro abhyetya gṛhītvā sīriṇo halam ।। tathaiva yoṣitāṃ tāsāṃ jahāsābhimukhaṃ kapiḥ ।।
tataḥ kopaparītātmā bhartsayām āsa taṃ balam ।। tataḥ samutthāya balo jagṛhe muśalaṃ ruṣā ।। cikṣepa ca sa tāṃ kṣiptāṃ muśalena sahasradhā ।। apatan muśalaṃ cāsau samullaṅghya plavaṃgamaḥ ।।
tato balena kopena muṣṭinā mūrdhni tāḍitaḥ ।। patatā taccharīreṇa gireḥ śṛṅgam aśīryata ।। puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ tato devā rāmasyopari cikṣipuḥ ।। jagan nirākṛtaṃ vīra diṣṭyā sa kṣayam āgataḥ ।।
karmāṇy aparimeyāni śeṣasya dharaṇībhṛtaḥ ।। cakre duṣṭakṣitīśānāṃ tathaiva jagataḥ kṛte ।। avatārayām āsa hariḥ samastākṣauhiṇīvadhāt ।। śāpavyājena viprāṇām upasaṃhṛtavān kulam ।।
svāṃśo viṣṇumayaṃ sthānaṃ praviveśa punar nijam ।। kathaṃ ca mānuṣaṃ deham utsasarja janārdanaḥ ।। piṇḍārake mahātīrthe dṛṣṭā yadukumārakaiḥ ।। prasṛtās tān munīn ūcuḥ praṇipātapuraḥsaram ।।
iyaṃ strī putrakāmā tu prabho kiṃ janayiṣyati ।। śāpaṃ dadus tadā viprās teṣāṃ nāśāya suvratāḥ ।। yenākhilakulotsādo yādavānāṃ bhaviṣyati ।। ugrasenāya muśalaṃ jajñe sāmbasya codarāt ।।
jajñe tac cairakā cūrṇaṃ prakṣiptaṃ vai mahodadhau ।। khaṇḍaṃ cūrṇayituṃ śekur naiva te tomarākṛti ।। ghātitasyodarāt tasya lubdho jagrāha taj jarā ।। naicchat tad anyathā kartuṃ vidhinā yat samāhṛtam ।।
rahasy evam ahaṃ dūtaḥ prahito bhagavan suraiḥ ।। vijñāpayati vaḥ śakras tad idaṃ śrūyatāṃ prabho ।। bhagavān avatīrṇo atra tridaśaiḥ saṃprasāditaḥ ।। tvayā sanāthās tridaśā vrajantu tridiveśatām ।।
idānīṃ gamyatāṃ svargo bhavatā yadi rocate ।। tat sthīyatāṃ yathākālam ākhyeyam anujīvibhiḥ ।। prārabdha eva hi mayā yādavānām api kṣayaḥ ।। avatāraṃ karomy asya saptarātreṇa satvaraḥ ।।
yādavān upasaṃhṛtya yāsyāmi tridaśālayam ।। prāpta evāsmi mantavyo devendreṇa tathā suraiḥ ।। kṣites tebhyaḥ sa bhāro hi yadūnāṃ samadhīyata ।। yāsyāmy amaralokasya pālanāya bravīhi tān ।।
dvijāḥ sa divyayā gatyā devarājāntikaṃ yayau ।। dadarśa dvārakāpuryāṃ vināśāya divāniśam ।। mahotpātāñ śamāyaiṣāṃ prabhāsaṃ yāma mā ciram ।। mahābhāgavataḥ prāha praṇipatyoddhavo harim ।।
nāśāyāsya nimittāni kulasyācyuta lakṣaye ।। badarīm āśramaṃ puṇyaṃ gandhamādanaparvate ।। manmanā matprasādena tatra siddhim avāpsyasi ।। dvārakāṃ ca mayā tyaktāṃ samudraḥ plāvayiṣyati ।।
naranārāyaṇasthānaṃ keśavenānumoditaḥ ।। prabhāsaṃ prayayuḥ sārdhaṃ kṛṣṇarāmādibhir dvijāḥ ।। cakrus tatra surāpānaṃ vāsudevānumoditāḥ ।। yādavānāṃ tato jajñe kalahāgniḥ kṣayāvahaḥ ।।
kṣīṇaśastrās tu jagṛhuḥ pratyāsannām athairakām ।। tayā parasparaṃ jaghnuḥ saṃprahāraiḥ sudāruṇaiḥ ।। aniruddhādayaś cānye pṛthur vipṛthur eva ca ।। erakārūpibhir vajrais te nijaghnuḥ parasparam ।।
sahāyaṃ menire prāptaṃ te nijaghnuḥ parasparam ।। vadhāya teṣāṃ muśalaṃ muṣṭiloham abhūt tadā ।। jaghnuś ca sahasābhyetya tathānye tu parasparam ।। paśyato dārukasyāśu hṛto aśvair dvijasattamāḥ ।।
pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā jagmur ādityavartmanā ।। ṛte kṛṣṇaṃ mahābāhuṃ dārukaṃ ca dvijottamāḥ ।। dadṛśāte mukhāc cāsya niṣkrāmantaṃ mahoragam ।। prayātaś cārṇavaṃ siddhaiḥ pūjyamānas tathoragaiḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā balasya niryāṇaṃ dārukaṃ prāha keśavaḥ ।। niryāṇaṃ baladevasya yādavānāṃ tathā kṣayam ।। vācyaś ca dvārakāvāsī janaḥ sarvas tathāhukaḥ ।। tasmād rathaiḥ susajjais tu pratīkṣyo hy arjunāgamaḥ ।।
tenaiva saha gantavyaṃ yatra yāti sa kauravaḥ ।। pālanīyas tvayā śaktyā jano ayaṃ matparigrahaḥ ।। gṛhītvā yātu vajraś ca yadurājo bhaviṣyati ।। pradakṣiṇaṃ ca bahuśaḥ kṛtvā prāyād yathoditam ।।
ānināya mahābuddhiṃ vajraṃ cakre tathā nṛpam ।। brahmātmani samāropya sarvabhūteṣv adhārayat ।। yogayukto abhavat pādaṃ kṛtvā jānuni sattamāḥ ।। muśalaśeṣalohasya sāyakaṃ dhārayan param ।।
tato vivyādha tenaiva tomareṇa dvijottamāḥ ।। praṇipatyāha caivainaṃ prasīdeti punaḥ punaḥ ।। kṣamyatām ātmapāpena dagdhaṃ mā dagdhum arhasi ।। gaccha tvaṃ matprasādena lubdha svargeśvarāspadam ।।
āruhya prayayau svargaṃ lubdhakas tatprasādataḥ ।। brahmabhūte avyaye acintye vāsudevamaye amale ।। tyaktvā sa mānuṣaṃ deham avāpa trividhāṃ gatim ।। saṃskāraṃ lambhayām āsa tathānyeṣām anukramāt ।।
upagṛhya harer dehaṃ viviśus tā hutāśanam ।। viveśa jvalitaṃ vahniṃ tatsaṅgāhlādaśītalam ।। devakī rohiṇī caiva viviśur jātavedasam ।। niścakrāma janaṃ sarvaṃ gṛhītvā vajram eva ca ।।
vajraṃ janaṃ ca kaunteyaḥ pālayañ śanakair yayau ।। svargaṃ jagāma bho viprāḥ pārijātaś ca pādapaḥ ।। tasmin dine avatīrṇo ayaṃ kālakāyaḥ kaliḥ kila ।। yaduśreṣṭhagṛhaṃ tv ekaṃ nāplāvayata sāgaraḥ ।।
nityaṃ saṃnihitas tatra bhagavān keśavo yataḥ ।। viṣṇukrīḍānvitaṃ sthānaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāpāt pramucyate ।। cakāra vāsaṃ sarvasya janasya munisattamāḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā striyo nīyamānā dasyūnāṃ nihateśvarāḥ ।।
ābhīrā mantrayām āsuḥ sametyātyantadurmadāḥ ।। nayaty asmān atikramya dhig etat kriyatāṃ balam ।। karṇādīṃś ca na jānāti balaṃ grāmanivāsinām ।। sarvān evāvajānāti kiṃ vo bahubhir uttaraiḥ ।।
tato nivṛttaḥ kaunteyaḥ prāhābhīrān hasann iva ।। nivartadhvam adharmajñā yadīto na mumūrṣavaḥ ।। strījanaṃ cāpi kaunteyād viṣvaksenaparigraham ।। āropayitum ārebhe na śaśāka sa vīryavān ।।
na sasmāra tathāstrāṇi cintayann api pāṇḍavaḥ ।। na bhedaṃ te paraṃ cakrur astā gāṇḍīvadhanvanā ।। yudhyataḥ saha gopālair arjunasyābhavat kṣayaḥ ।। yan mayā śarasaṃghātaiḥ sabalā bhūbhṛto jitāḥ ।।
apākṛṣyanta cābhīraiḥ kāmāc cānyāḥ pravavrajuḥ ।। jaghāna dasyūṃs te cāsya prahārāñ jahasur dvijāḥ ।। jagmur ādāya te mlecchāḥ samantān munisattamāḥ ।। aho bhagavatā tena mukto asmīti ruroda vai ।।
sarvam ekapade naṣṭaṃ dānam aśrotriye yathā ।। yad asāmarthyayukto ahaṃ nīcair nītaḥ parābhavam ।। puṇyeneva vinā tena gataṃ sarvam asāratām ।। vinā tena yad ābhīrair jito ahaṃ katham anyathā ।।
cakāra tatra rājānaṃ vajraṃ yādavanandanam ।। tam upetya mahābhāgaṃ vinayenābhyavādayat ।। uvāca pārthaṃ vicchāyaḥ katham atyantam īdṛśaḥ ।। jayāśābhaṅgaduḥkhī vā bhraṣṭacchāyo asi sāṃpratam ।।
agamyastrīratir vāpi tenāsi vigataprabhaḥ ।। kiṃ vā kṛpaṇavittāni hṛtāni bhavatārjuna ।। duṣṭacakṣur hato vāpi niḥśrīkaḥ katham anyathā ।। tenātīvāsi vicchāyo nyūnair vā yudhi nirjitaḥ ।।
prokto yathāvad ācaṣṭa viprā ātmaparābhavam ।। yā śrīś chāyā ca naḥ so asmān parityajya harir gataḥ ।। hīnā vayaṃ mune tena jātās tṛṇamayā iva ।। sāratā yābhavan mūrtā sa gataḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।।
na tatyāja sa govindas tyaktvāsmān bhagavān gataḥ ।। yatprabhāvena nirdagdhāḥ sa kṛṣṇas tyaktavān bhuvam ।। vibhāti tāta naiko ahaṃ virahe tasya cakriṇaḥ ।। vinā tenādya kṛṣṇena gopālair asmi nirjitaḥ ।।
mama tena vinābhīrair laguḍais tu tiraskṛtam ।। yatato mama nītāni dasyubhir laguḍāyudhaiḥ ।। hṛtaṃ yaṣṭipraharaṇaiḥ paribhūya balaṃ mama ।। nīcāvamānapaṅkāṅkī nirlajjo asmi pitāmaha ।।
duḥkhitasya ca dīnasya pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ ।। avehi sarvabhūteṣu kālasya gatir īdṛśī ।। kālamūlam idaṃ jñātvā kuru sthairyam ato arjuna ।। devā manuṣyāḥ paśavas taravaś ca sarīsṛpāḥ ।।
kālātmakam idaṃ sarvaṃ jñātvā śamam avāpnuhi ।। bhārāvatārakāryārtham avatīrṇaḥ sa medinīm ।। tadartham avatīrṇo asau kāmarūpī janārdanaḥ ।। vṛṣṇyandhakakulaṃ sarvaṃ tathā pārthopasaṃhṛtam ।।
tato gataḥ sa bhagavān kṛtakṛtyo yathecchayā ।। ante tāpasamartho ayaṃ sāṃprataṃ vai yathā kṛtam ।। bhavanti bhavakāleṣu puruṣāṇāṃ parākramāḥ ।। teṣām arjuna kālotthaḥ kiṃ nyūnābhibhavo na saḥ ।।
tvattas tathaiva bhavato dasyubhyo ante tadudbhavaḥ ।। karoti sarvabhūtānāṃ nāśaṃ cānte jagatpatiḥ ।। bhavānte tvadvipakṣās te keśavenāvalokitāḥ ।। ābhīrebhyaś ca bhavataḥ kaḥ śraddadhyāt parābhavam ।।
tvayā yat kauravā dhvastā yad ābhīrair bhavāñ jitaḥ ।। tad apy ahaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ kathayāmi tavārjuna ।। bahūn varṣagaṇān pārtha gṛṇan brahma sanātanam ।। babhūva tatra gacchantyo dadṛśus taṃ surastriyaḥ ।।
tuṣṭuvus taṃ mahātmānaṃ praśaśaṃsuś ca pāṇḍava ।। vinayāvanatāś caiva praṇemuḥ stotratatparāḥ ।। sarvās tāḥ kauravaśreṣṭha variṣṭhaṃ taṃ dvijanmanām ।। mattas tad vriyatāṃ sarvaṃ pradāsyāmy api durlabham ।।
rambhātilottamādyāś ca divyāś cāpsaraso abruvan ।। prasanne tvayy asaṃprāptaṃ kim asmākam iti dvijāḥ ।। tad icchāmaḥ patiṃ prāptuṃ viprendra puruṣottamam ।। tam uttīrṇaṃ ca dadṛśur virūpaṃ vakram aṣṭadhā ।।
tāḥ śaśāpa muniḥ kopam avāpya kurunandana ।। bhavatībhiḥ kṛtā tasmād eṣa śāpaṃ dadāmi vaḥ ।। macchāpopahatāḥ sarvā dasyuhastaṃ gamiṣyatha ।। punaḥ surendralokaṃ vai prāha bhūyo gamiṣyatha ।।
bhartāraṃ prāpya tāḥ prāptā dasyuhastaṃ varāṅganāḥ ।। tenaivākhilanāthena sarvaṃ tad upasaṃhṛtam ।। balaṃ tejas tathā vīryaṃ māhātmyaṃ copasaṃhṛtam ।। viprayogāvasānaṃ tu saṃyogaḥ saṃcayaḥ kṣayaḥ ।।
teṣām evetare ceṣṭāṃ śikṣantaḥ santi tādṛśāḥ ।। parityajyākhilaṃ rājyaṃ gantavyaṃ tapase vanam ।। paraśvo bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ gatiṃ vīra yathā kuru ।। dṛṣṭaṃ caivānubhūtaṃ vā kathitaṃ tad aśeṣataḥ ।।
rājye parīkṣitaṃ kṛtvā yayuḥ pāṇḍusutā vanam ।। jātasya ca yador vaṃśe vāsudevasya ceṣṭitam ।। rāmasya ca muniśreṣṭha tvayoktaṃ bhuvi durlabham ।। tasmād brūhi mahābhāga bhūyo devasya ceṣṭitam ।।
satāṃ kathayatām eva varāha iti naḥ śrutam ।। na karmaguṇasadbhāvaṃ na hetutvamanīṣitam ।। kimācāraprabhāvo vā kiṃ vā tena tadā kṛtam ।। mahāvarāhacaritaṃ sarvalokasukhāvaham ।।
daṃṣṭrayā gāṃ samudrasthām ujjahārārimardanaḥ ।। śrotuṃ no vartate buddhir hareḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ ।। yā vāsya prakṛtir brahmaṃs tāś cākhyātuṃ tvam arhasi ।। yathāśaktyā tu vakṣyāmi śrūyatāṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ yaśaḥ ।।
tasmād viṣṇoḥ samastā vai śṛṇudhvaṃ yāḥ pravṛttayaḥ ।। sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ sahasrakaram avyayam ।। sahasradaṃ sahasrādiṃ sahasrabhujam avyayam ।। pātrāṇi ca pavitrāṇi vediṃ dīkṣāṃ samit sruvam ।।
adhvaryuṃ sāmagaṃ vipraṃ sadasyaṃ sadanaṃ sadaḥ ।। prāgvaṃśaṃ yajñabhūmiṃ ca hotāraṃ ca paraṃ ca yat ।। prāyaścittāni vārghyaṃ ca sthaṇḍilāni kuśās tathā ।। agrāsinaṃ somabhujaṃ hutārciṣam udāyudham ।।
tasya viṣṇoḥ sureśasya śrīvatsāṅkasya dhīmataḥ ।। bhūyaś caiva bhaviṣyanti hy evam āha pitāmahaḥ ।। prādurbhāvāśritāṃ viṣṇoḥ sarvapāpaharāṃ śivām ।। pravakṣyāmy ānupūrvyeṇa yat pṛcchadhvaṃ mamānaghāḥ ।।
hitārthaṃ suramartyānāṃ lokānāṃ prabhavāya ca ।। prādurbhāvāṃś ca vakṣyāmi puṇyān divyān guṇānvitān ।। pūrṇe yugasahasre atha devadevo jagatpatiḥ ।। devāḥ saptarṣayaś caiva nāgāś cāpsarasas tathā ।।
naṣṭe devāsuranare pranaṣṭoragarākṣase ।। hatau bhagavatā tena tayor dattvāmitaṃ varam ।। puṣkare tatra saṃbhūtā devāḥ sarṣigaṇās tathā ।। purāṇaṃ kathyate yatra devaśrutisamāhitam ।।
yatra viṣṇuḥ suraśreṣṭho vārāhaṃ rūpam āsthitaḥ ।। agnijihvo darbharomā brahmaśīrṣo mahātapāḥ ।। ājyanāsaḥ sruvatuṇḍaḥ sāmaghoṣasvaro mahān ।। prāyaścittanakho ghoraḥ paśujānur mukhākṛtiḥ ।।
vādyantarātmā mantrasphig vikṛtaḥ somaśoṇitaḥ ।। prāgvaṃśakāyo dyutimān nānādīkṣābhir anvitaḥ ।। upākarmāṣṭarucakaḥ pravargāvartabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। chāyāpatnīsahāyo asau maṇiśṛṅga ivotthitaḥ ।।
ekārṇavajalabhraṣṭām ekārṇavagataḥ prabhuḥ ।। sahasraśīrṣo lokādiś cakāra jagatīṃ punaḥ ।। uddhṛtā pṛthivī devī sāgarāmbudharā purā ।। yatra bhūtvā mṛgendreṇa hiraṇyakaśipur hataḥ ।।
daityānām ādipuruṣaś cakāra sumahat tapaḥ ।। japopavāsaniratas tasthau maunavratasthitaḥ ।। prīto abhavat tatas tasya tapasā niyamena ca ।। vimānenārkavarṇena haṃsayuktena bhāsvatā ।।
rudrair viśvasahāyaiś ca yakṣarākṣasakiṃnaraiḥ ।। nakṣatraiś ca muhūrtaiś ca khecaraiś ca mahāgrahaiḥ ।। rājarṣibhiḥ puṇyatamair gandharvair apsarogaṇaiḥ ।। brahmā brahmavidāṃ śreṣṭho daityaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।
varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te yatheṣṭaṃ kāmam āpnuhi ।। ṛṣayo vātha māṃ śāpaiḥ kruddhā lokapitāmaha ।। na śastreṇa na vāstreṇa giriṇā pādapena vā ।। pāṇiprahāreṇaikena sabhṛtyabalavāhanam ।।
bhaveyam aham evārkaḥ somo vāyur hutāśanaḥ ।। dhanadaś ca dhanādhyakṣo yakṣaḥ kiṃpuruṣādhipaḥ ।। sarvān kāmān imāṃs tāta prāpsyasi tvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। vairājaṃ brahmasadanaṃ brahmarṣigaṇasevitam ।।
varapradānaṃ śrutvaiva pitāmaham upasthitāḥ ।। tat prasīdāśu bhagavan vadho apy asya vicintyatām ।। sraṣṭā ca havyakavyānām avyaktaṃ prakṛtir dhruvam ।। provāca bhagavān vākyaṃ sarvadevagaṇāṃs tathā ।।
tapaso ante ca bhagavān vadhaṃ viṣṇuḥ kariṣyati ।। svāni sthānāni divyāni jagmus te vai mudānvitāḥ ।। hiraṇyakaśipur daityo varadānena darpitaḥ ।। satyadharmaratān dāntāṃs tadā dharṣitavāṃs tathā ।।
trailokyaṃ vaśam ānīya svarge vasati so asuraḥ ।। yajñīyān akarod daityān ayajñīyāś ca devatāḥ ।। śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ viṣṇum upatasthur mahābalam ।। nārāyaṇaṃ vibhuṃ devaṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।।
tvaṃ hi naḥ paramo devas tvaṃ hi naḥ paramo guruḥ ।। kṣayāya ditivaṃśasya śaraṇaṃ tvaṃ bhavasva naḥ ।। tathaiva tridivaṃ devāḥ pratilapsyatha mā ciram ।। avadhyam amarendrāṇāṃ dānavendraṃ nihanmi tam ।।
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sthānam ājagāma mahābalaḥ ।। nārasiṃhena vapuṣā pāṇiṃ saṃspṛśya pāṇinā ।। ghanajīmūtadīptaujā jīmūta iva vegavān ।। dṛptair daityagaṇair guptaṃ hatavān ekapāṇinā ।।
yatra vāmanam āsthāya rūpaṃ daityavināśanam ।। vikramais tribhir akṣobhyāḥ kṣobhitās te mahāsurāḥ ।। ayaḥśirā aśvaśirā hayagrīvaś ca vīryavān ।। puṣkaraḥ puṣkalaś caiva śāśvo aśvapatir eva ca ।।
anuhrādo harihayo vārāhaḥ saṃharo anujaḥ ।। bṛhatkīrtir mahājihvaḥ śaṅkukarṇo mahāsvanaḥ ।। vāyur gariṣṭho namuciḥ sambaro viskaro mahān ।। kālakaḥ kālakopaś ca vṛtraḥ krodho virocanaḥ ।।
indratāpanavātāpī ketumān baladarpitaḥ ।। svamiśraḥ kālavadanaḥ karālaḥ keśir eva ca ।। śataghnīcakrahastāś ca tathā muśalapāṇayaḥ ।। śūlolūkhalahastāś ca paraśvadhadharās tathā ।।
mahāśilāpraharaṇāḥ śūlahastāś ca dānavāḥ ।। kūrmakukkuṭavaktrāś ca śaśolūkamukhās tathā ।। mārjāraśikhivaktrāś ca mahāvaktrās tathā pare ।। godhāśallakivaktrāś ca kroṣṭuvaktrāś ca dānavāḥ ।।
bhīmā makaravaktrāś ca krauñcavaktrāś ca dānavāḥ ।। gajendracarmavasanās tathā kṛṣṇājināmbarāḥ ।। uṣṇīṣiṇo mukuṭinas tathā kuṇḍalino asurāḥ ।। nānāveśadharā daityā nānāmālyānulepanāḥ ।।
kramamāṇaṃ hṛṣīkeśam upāvartanta sarvaśaḥ ।। rūpaṃ kṛtvā mahābhīmaṃ jahārāśu sa medinīm ।। nabhaḥ prakramamāṇasya nābhyāṃ kila tathā sthitau ।। viṣṇor amitavīryasya vadanty evaṃ dvijātayaḥ ।।
dadau śakrāya vasudhāṃ viṣṇur balavatāṃ varaḥ ।। vedavidbhir dvijair etat kathyate vaiṣṇavaṃ yaśaḥ ।। dattātreya iti khyātaḥ kṣamayā parayā yutaḥ ।। cāturvarṇye ca saṃkīrṇe dharme śithilatāṃ gate ।।
prajāsu śīryamāṇāsu dharme cākulatāṃ gate ।। cāturvarṇyam asaṃkīrṇaṃ kṛtaṃ tena mahātmanā ।। varadena varo datto dattātreyeṇa dhīmatā ।। śatāni daśa bāhūnāṃ bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ ।।
durnirīkṣyo arivṛndānāṃ yuddhasthaś ca bhaviṣyasi ।। bhūyaś ca jāmadagnyo ayaṃ prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ ।। rāmo arjunam anīkasthaṃ jaghāna nṛpatiṃ prabhuḥ ।। dharṣayitvārjunaṃ rāmaḥ krośamānaṃ ca meghavat ।।
paraśvadhena dīptena jñātibhiḥ sahitasya vai ।। triḥ saptakṛtvaḥ pṛthivī tena niḥkṣatriyā kṛtā ।। sarvapāpavināśāya vājimedhena ceṣṭavān ।। mārīcāya dadau prītaḥ kaśyapāya vasuṃdharām ।।
hiraṇyam akṣayaṃ dhenur gajendrāṃś ca mahīpatiḥ ।। adyāpi ca hitārthāya lokānāṃ bhṛgunandanaḥ ।। āste vai devavac chrīmān mahendre parvatottame ।। jāmadagnya iti khyātaḥ prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ ।।
jajñe daśarathasyātha putraḥ padmāyatekṣaṇaḥ ।। loke rāma iti khyātas tejasā bhāskaropamaḥ ।। dharmasya ca vivṛddhyarthaṃ jajñe tatra mahāyaśāḥ ।। yaḥ samāḥ sarvadharmajñaś caturdaśa vane avasat ।।
caturdaśa vane taptvā tapo varṣāṇi rāghavaḥ ।। pūrvoditā tu yā lakṣmīr bhartāram anugacchati ।। tasyāpakāriṇaṃ krūraṃ paulastyaṃ manujarṣabhaḥ ।। devāsuragaṇānāṃ ca yakṣarākṣasabhoginām ।।
yuktaṃ rākṣasakoṭībhir nīlāñjanacayopamam ।। durjayaṃ durdharaṃ dṛptaṃ śārdūlasamavikramam ।। jaghāna sacivaiḥ sārdhaṃ sasainyaṃ rāvaṇaṃ yudhi ।। rāvaṇaṃ nijaghānāśu rāmo bhūtapatiḥ purā ।।
vālī vinihataḥ saṃkhye sugrīvaś cābhiṣecitaḥ ।। hato madhuvane vīro varamatto mahāsuraḥ ।। mārīcaś ca subāhuś ca balena balināṃ varau ।। samare yuddhaśauṇḍena tathānye cāpi rākṣasāḥ ।।
jaghāna puruṣavyāghro gandharvau śāpamohitau ।। vadhārthaṃ devaśatrūṇāṃ durdharṣāṇāṃ surair api ।। bhagnaṃ māheśvaraṃ cāpaṃ krīḍatā līlayā purā ।। daśāśvamedhāñ jārūthyān ājahāra nirargalān ।।
na vittaharaṇaṃ cāsīd rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati ।। sarvam āsīc chubhaṃ tatra rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati ।। na cāpi vṛddhā bālānāṃ pretakāryāṇi cakrire ।। śūdrāś caiva hi varṇāṃs trīñ śuśrūṣanty anahaṃkṛtāḥ ।।
sarvam āsīj jagad dāntaṃ nirdasyur abhavan mahī ।। āsan varṣasahasrāṇi tathā putrasahasriṇaḥ ।। devatānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।। gāthām apy atra gāyanti ye purāṇavido janāḥ ।।
śyāmo yuvā lohitākṣo dīptāsyo mitabhāṣitaḥ ।। daśa varṣasahasrāṇi rāmo rājyam akārayat ।। avyucchinno abhavad rāṣṭre dīyatāṃ bhujyatām iti ।। ati candraṃ ca sūryaṃ ca rāmo dāśarathir babhau ।।
hitvāyodhyāṃ divaṃ yāto rāghavo hi mahābalaḥ ।। rāvaṇaṃ sagaṇaṃ hatvā divam ācakrame vibhuḥ ।। vikhyāto māthure kalpe sarvalokahitāya vai ।। ariṣṭaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ keśiṃ pūtanāṃ daityadārikām ।।
daityān mānuṣadehena sūdayām āsa vīryavān ।। narakaś ca hataḥ saṃkhye yavanaś ca mahābalaḥ ।। durācārāś ca nihitāḥ pārthivā ye mahītale ।। kalkī viṣṇuyaśā nāma śambhalagrāmasaṃbhavaḥ ।।
ete cānye ca bahavo divyā devagaṇair vṛtāḥ ।। yatra devā vimuhyanti prādurbhāvānukīrtane ।। etad uddeśamātreṇa prādurbhāvānukīrtanam ।। prīyante pitaras tasya prādurbhāvānukīrtanāt ।।
viṣṇor amitavīryasya yaḥ śṛṇoti kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। sarvapāpaharāḥ puṇyāḥ prādurbhāvāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। mune tvanmukhagītasya tathā kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। vetsi sarvaṃ mune tena pṛcchāmas tvāṃ mahāmatim ।।
duḥkhakleśakaraḥ śaśvat sarvabhūtabhayāvahaḥ ।। pramāṇaṃ caiva mārgasya brūhi no vadatāṃ vara ।। kathaṃ narakaduḥkhāni nāpnuvanti narān mune ।। mānuṣasya ca yāmyasya lokasya kiyad antaram ।।
svargasthānāni kiyanti kiyanti narakāṇi ca ।। jīvasya nīyamānasya yamalokaṃ bravīhi naḥ ।। saṃsāracakram ajaraṃ sthitir yasya na vidyate ।। utkrāntikālād ārabhya yathā nānyo vadiṣyati ।।
yamalokasya cādhvānam antaraṃ mānuṣasya ca ।। taptatāmram ivātaptaṃ tad adhvānam udāhṛtam ।। puṇyān puṇyakṛto yānti pāpān pāpakṛto adhamāḥ ।। yeṣu duṣkṛtakarmāṇo vipacyante pṛthak pṛthak ।।
kumbhīpāko mahāghoraḥ śālmalo atha vimohanaḥ ।। nadyaḥ pūyavahāś cānyā rudhirāmbhas tathaiva ca ।। ghorā vaitaraṇī caiva asipattravanaṃ tathā ।। na vāpyo dīrghikā vāpi na kūpo na prapā sabhā ।।
na kiṃcid āśramasthānaṃ vidyate tatra vartmani ।। avaśyam eva gantavyaḥ sa sarvais tu mahāpathaḥ ।। jarāyujāṇḍajāś caiva svedajāś codbhijās tathā ।। devāsuramanuṣyaiś ca vaivasvatavaśānugaiḥ ।।
pūrvāhṇe cāparāhṇe vā madhyāhne vā tathā punaḥ ।। vṛddhair vā madhyamair vāpi yauvanasthais tathaiva ca ।। pravāsasthair gṛhasthair vā parvatasthaiḥ sthale api vā ।। āsīnaiś cāsthitair vāpi śayanīyagatais tathā ।।
ihānubhūya nirdiṣṭam āyur jantuḥ svayaṃ tadā ।। jalam agnir viṣaṃ śastraṃ kṣud vyādhiḥ patanaṃ gireḥ ।। vihāya sumahat kṛtsnaṃ śarīraṃ pāñcabhautikam ।। dṛḍhaṃ śarīram āpnoti sukhaduḥkhopabhuktaye ।।
sukhāni dhārmiko hṛṣṭa iha nīto yamakṣaye ।। bhinatti marmasthānāni dīpyamāno nirandhanaḥ ।। bhujyatām ambubhakṣyāṇām adhogatinirodhakṛt ।। dattāḥ sa tasyām āhlādam āpadi pratipadyate ।।
so api tṛptim avāpnoti vināpy annena vai tadā ।। āstikaḥ śraddadhānaś ca sukhamṛtyuṃ sa gacchati ।। śuklā vadānyā hrīmantas te narāḥ sukhamṛtyavaḥ ।। yathoktakārī saumyaś ca sa sukhaṃ mṛtyum ṛcchati ।।
prāpnuvanti narāḥ kāle mṛtyuṃ sukhasamanvitam ।। prāṇaghnīṃ vedanāṃ kaṣṭāṃ ye cānyodvegadhāriṇaḥ ।। kūṭasākṣī mṛṣāvādī yo gurur nānuśāsti vai ।। vibhīṣaṇāḥ pūtigandhāḥ kūṭamudgarapāṇayaḥ ।।
prāpteṣu dṛkpathaṃ teṣu jāyate tasya vepathuḥ ।। sā tu vāg asphuṭā viprā ekavarṇā vibhāvyate ।। tataḥ sa vedanāviṣṭaṃ tac charīraṃ vimuñcati ।। tatkarmayātanārthe ca na mātṛpitṛsaṃbhavam ।।
tato dūto yamasyātha pāśair badhnāti dāruṇaiḥ ।। bhūtaiḥ saṃtyaktadehasya kaṇṭhaprāptānilasya ca ।। nirgato vāyubhūtas tu ṣāṭkauśikakalevare ।। dāraiḥ putrair vayasyaiś ca gurubhis tyajyate bhuvi ।।
svaśarīraṃ samutsṛjya vāyubhūtas tu gacchati ।। sukhaduḥkhapradātāraṃ durgamaṃ pāpakarmaṇām ।। durāpam atidurgaṃ ca pāpiṣṭhānāṃ sadāhitam ।। mudgarais tāḍyamānāś ca nīyante taṃ mahāpatham ।।
ninīṣavaḥ samāyānti yamadūtā bhayaṃkarāḥ ।। uṣṭreṣu vānareṣv anye vṛścikeṣu vṛkeṣu ca ।। śyenaśṛgālam ārūḍhāḥ saraghākaṅkavāhanāḥ ।। nānārūpadharā ghorāḥ sarvaprāṇibhayaṃkarāḥ ।।
mahāhanukapolāsyāḥ pralambadaśanacchadāḥ ।। māṃsaśoṇitadigdhāṅgā daṃṣṭrābhir bhṛśam ulbaṇaiḥ ।। netraiḥ suvikṛtākārair jvalatpiṅgalacañcalaiḥ ।। kekaraiḥ saṃkulais stabdhair locanaiḥ pāvakopamaiḥ ।।
śoṇāsaralagātraiś ca muṇḍamālāvibhūṣitaiḥ ।। vahnijvālopamaiḥ keśaiḥ stabdharukṣair bhayaṃkaraiḥ ।। bhujadaṇḍair mahāghoraiḥ pralambaiḥ parighopamaiḥ ।। dviraṣṭabāhavaś cānye daśaviṃśabhujās tathā ।।
āyudhair vikṛtākāraiḥ prajvaladbhir bhayānakaiḥ ।। pāśaśṛṅkhaladaṇḍaiś ca bhīṣayanto mahābalāḥ ।। grahītuṃ prāṇinaḥ sarve yamasyājñākarās tathā ।। tad asya nīyate jantor yamasya sadanaṃ prati ।।
tāḍayitvā bhṛśaṃ kruddhair nīyate yamakiṃkaraiḥ ।। hā tāta mātaḥ putreti vadantaṃ karmadūṣitam ।। khaḍgaśaktiprahāraiś ca vajradaṇḍaiḥ sudāruṇaiḥ ।। ekaikaśo bhṛśaṃ kruddhais tāḍayadbhiḥ samantataḥ ।।
ākṛṣya nīyate jantur adhvānaṃ subhayaṃkaraiḥ ।। tathā pradīptajvalane kṣāravajraśatotkaṭe ।। kṛṣyate yamadūtaiś ca śivāsaṃnādabhīṣaṇaiḥ ।। prayāti dāruṇe mārge pāpakarmā yamālayam ।।
duḥkhenākrandamānaiś ca gantavyaḥ sa mahāpathaḥ ।। kampamānaśarīrais tu gantavyaṃ jīvasaṃjñakaiḥ ।। dahyamānais tu gantavyaṃ narair dānavivarjitaiḥ ।। dagdhasphuṭatvacākīrṇair gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥ ।।
vedanārtaiś ca sadbhiś ca gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥ ।। bhidyadbhis tīkṣṇaśūlāgrair gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥ ।। śvānair vyāghrair vṛkaiḥ kaṅkair bhakṣyamāṇaiś ca pāpibhiḥ ।। mahiṣarṣabhaśṛṅgāgrair bhidyamānaiḥ samantataḥ ।।
sūcībhramarakākola- makṣikābhiś ca saṃghaśaḥ ।। viśvastaṃ svāminaṃ mitraṃ striyaṃ vā yas tu ghātayet ।। ghātayanti ca ye jantūṃs tāḍayanti nirāgasaḥ ।। ye haranti parastrīṇāṃ varaprāvaraṇāni ca ।।
vāso dhānyaṃ hiraṇyaṃ vā gṛhakṣetram athāpi vā ।। pāṣāṇair laguḍair daṇḍais tāḍyamānais tu jarjaraiḥ ।। brahmasvaṃ ye harantīha narā narakanirbhayāḥ ।। śuṣkakāṣṭhanibaddhās te chinnakarṇākṣināsikāḥ ।।
kiṃkarair bhīṣaṇaiś caṇḍais tāḍyamānāś ca dāruṇaiḥ ।। evaṃ paramadurdharṣam adhvānaṃ jvalanaprabham ।। prataptatāmravarṇābhaṃ vahnijvālāsphuliṅgavat ।। śaktivajraiś ca saṃkīrṇam ujjvalaṃ tīvrakaṇṭakam ।।
jvālāmālākulaṃ raudraṃ sūryaraśmipratāpitam ।। yadaiva krandate jantur duḥkhārtaḥ patitaḥ kvacit ।। evaṃ saṃtāḍyamānaś ca lubdhaḥ pāpeṣu yo anayaḥ ।। sarvair eva hi gantavyam adhvānaṃ tat sudurgamam ।।
nītvā sudāruṇaṃ mārgaṃ prāṇinaṃ yamakiṃkaraiḥ ।। sā purī vipulākārā lakṣayojanam āyatā ।। prākārāḥ kāñcanās tasyā yojanāyutam ucchritāḥ ।। sā purī vividhaiḥ saṃghair ghorā ghoraiḥ samākulā ।।
pūrvadvāraṃ śubhaṃ tasyāḥ patākāśataśobhitam ।। gītanṛtyaiḥ samākīrṇaṃ gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ ।। gandharvasiddhayakṣāṇāṃ vidyādharavisarpiṇām ।। chattracāmaravinyāsaṃ nānāratnair alaṃkṛtam ।।
ṛgyajuḥsāmanirghoṣair munivṛndasamākulam ।। grīṣme vāripradā ye ca śīte cāgnipradā narāḥ ।। ye ca dānaratāḥ śūrā mātāpitṛparāś ca ye ।। paścimaṃ tu mahādvāraṃ puryā ratnair vibhūṣitam ।।
bherīmṛdaṅgasaṃnādaiḥ śaṅkhakāhalanāditam ।। praveśas tena hṛṣṭānāṃ śivabhaktimatāṃ nṛṇām ।। prasthāne ye mṛtā vīrā mṛtāḥ kālañjare girau ।। ye svāmimitralokārthe gograhe saṃkule hatāḥ ।।
puryāṃ tasyā mahāghoraṃ sarvasattvabhayaṃkaram ।। andhakārasamāyuktaṃ tīkṣṇaśṛṅgaiḥ samanvitam ।। vilumpadbhir vṛkair vyāghrair ṛkṣaiḥ siṃhaiḥ sajambukaiḥ ।। praveśas tena vai nityaṃ sarveṣām apakāriṇām ।।
śaraṇāgataṃ viśvastaṃ striyaṃ mitraṃ nirāyudham ।। nikṣepasyāpahartāro viṣavahnipradāś ca ye ।। pararandhreṣu ye krūrā ye sadānṛtavādinaḥ ।। kūṭasākṣipradātāraḥ kanyāvikrayakārakāḥ ।।
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ caiva ye vadanti ca pauruṣam ।। dakṣiṇena tu te sarve dvāreṇa praviśanti vai ।। mune tvanmukhagītasya tathā kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। vetsi sarvaṃ mune tena pṛcchāmas tvāṃ mahāmatim ।।
duḥkhakleśakaraḥ śaśvat sarvabhūtabhayāvahaḥ ।। pramāṇaṃ caiva mārgasya brūhi no vadatāṃ vara ।। kathaṃ narakaduḥkhāni nāpnuvanti narān mune ।। mānuṣasya ca yāmyasya lokasya kiyad antaram ।।
svargasthānāni kiyanti kiyanti narakāṇi ca ।। jīvasya nīyamānasya yamalokaṃ bravīhi naḥ ।। saṃsāracakram ajaraṃ sthitir yasya na vidyate ।। utkrāntikālād ārabhya yathā nānyo vadiṣyati ।।
yamalokasya cādhvānam antaraṃ mānuṣasya ca ।। taptatāmram ivātaptaṃ tad adhvānam udāhṛtam ।। puṇyān puṇyakṛto yānti pāpān pāpakṛto adhamāḥ ।। yeṣu duṣkṛtakarmāṇo vipacyante pṛthak pṛthak ।।
kumbhīpāko mahāghoraḥ śālmalo atha vimohanaḥ ।। nadyaḥ pūyavahāś cānyā rudhirāmbhas tathaiva ca ।। ghorā vaitaraṇī caiva asipattravanaṃ tathā ।। na vāpyo dīrghikā vāpi na kūpo na prapā sabhā ।।
na kiṃcid āśramasthānaṃ vidyate tatra vartmani ।। avaśyam eva gantavyaḥ sa sarvais tu mahāpathaḥ ।। jarāyujāṇḍajāś caiva svedajāś codbhijās tathā ।। devāsuramanuṣyaiś ca vaivasvatavaśānugaiḥ ।।
pūrvāhṇe cāparāhṇe vā madhyāhne vā tathā punaḥ ।। vṛddhair vā madhyamair vāpi yauvanasthais tathaiva ca ।। pravāsasthair gṛhasthair vā parvatasthaiḥ sthale api vā ।। āsīnaiś cāsthitair vāpi śayanīyagatais tathā ।।
ihānubhūya nirdiṣṭam āyur jantuḥ svayaṃ tadā ।। jalam agnir viṣaṃ śastraṃ kṣud vyādhiḥ patanaṃ gireḥ ।। vihāya sumahat kṛtsnaṃ śarīraṃ pāñcabhautikam ।। dṛḍhaṃ śarīram āpnoti sukhaduḥkhopabhuktaye ।।
sukhāni dhārmiko hṛṣṭa iha nīto yamakṣaye ।। bhinatti marmasthānāni dīpyamāno nirandhanaḥ ।। bhujyatām ambubhakṣyāṇām adhogatinirodhakṛt ।। dattāḥ sa tasyām āhlādam āpadi pratipadyate ।।
so api tṛptim avāpnoti vināpy annena vai tadā ।। āstikaḥ śraddadhānaś ca sukhamṛtyuṃ sa gacchati ।। śuklā vadānyā hrīmantas te narāḥ sukhamṛtyavaḥ ।। yathoktakārī saumyaś ca sa sukhaṃ mṛtyum ṛcchati ।।
prāpnuvanti narāḥ kāle mṛtyuṃ sukhasamanvitam ।। prāṇaghnīṃ vedanāṃ kaṣṭāṃ ye cānyodvegadhāriṇaḥ ।। kūṭasākṣī mṛṣāvādī yo gurur nānuśāsti vai ।। vibhīṣaṇāḥ pūtigandhāḥ kūṭamudgarapāṇayaḥ ।।
prāpteṣu dṛkpathaṃ teṣu jāyate tasya vepathuḥ ।। sā tu vāg asphuṭā viprā ekavarṇā vibhāvyate ।। tataḥ sa vedanāviṣṭaṃ tac charīraṃ vimuñcati ।। tatkarmayātanārthe ca na mātṛpitṛsaṃbhavam ।।
tato dūto yamasyātha pāśair badhnāti dāruṇaiḥ ।। bhūtaiḥ saṃtyaktadehasya kaṇṭhaprāptānilasya ca ।। nirgato vāyubhūtas tu ṣāṭkauśikakalevare ।। dāraiḥ putrair vayasyaiś ca gurubhis tyajyate bhuvi ।।
svaśarīraṃ samutsṛjya vāyubhūtas tu gacchati ।। sukhaduḥkhapradātāraṃ durgamaṃ pāpakarmaṇām ।। durāpam atidurgaṃ ca pāpiṣṭhānāṃ sadāhitam ।। mudgarais tāḍyamānāś ca nīyante taṃ mahāpatham ।।

mahāhanukapolāsyāḥ pralambadaśanacchadāḥ ।। māṃsaśoṇitadigdhāṅgā daṃṣṭrābhir bhṛśam ulbaṇaiḥ ।। netraiḥ suvikṛtākārair jvalatpiṅgalacañcalaiḥ ।। kekaraiḥ saṃkulais stabdhair locanaiḥ pāvakopamaiḥ ।।
śoṇāsaralagātraiś ca muṇḍamālāvibhūṣitaiḥ ।। vahnijvālopamaiḥ keśaiḥ stabdharukṣair bhayaṃkaraiḥ ।। bhujadaṇḍair mahāghoraiḥ pralambaiḥ parighopamaiḥ ।। dviraṣṭabāhavaś cānye daśaviṃśabhujās tathā ।।
āyudhair vikṛtākāraiḥ prajvaladbhir bhayānakaiḥ ।। pāśaśṛṅkhaladaṇḍaiś ca bhīṣayanto mahābalāḥ ।। grahītuṃ prāṇinaḥ sarve yamasyājñākarās tathā ।। tad asya nīyate jantor yamasya sadanaṃ prati ।।
tāḍayitvā bhṛśaṃ kruddhair nīyate yamakiṃkaraiḥ ।। hā tāta mātaḥ putreti vadantaṃ karmadūṣitam ।। khaḍgaśaktiprahāraiś ca vajradaṇḍaiḥ sudāruṇaiḥ ।। ekaikaśo bhṛśaṃ kruddhais tāḍayadbhiḥ samantataḥ ।।
ākṛṣya nīyate jantur adhvānaṃ subhayaṃkaraiḥ ।। tathā pradīptajvalane kṣāravajraśatotkaṭe ।। kṛṣyate yamadūtaiś ca śivāsaṃnādabhīṣaṇaiḥ ।। prayāti dāruṇe mārge pāpakarmā yamālayam ।।

vedanārtaiś ca sadbhiś ca gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥ ।। bhidyadbhis tīkṣṇaśūlāgrair gantavyaṃ jīvaghātakaiḥ ।। śvānair vyāghrair vṛkaiḥ kaṅkair bhakṣyamāṇaiś ca pāpibhiḥ ।। mahiṣarṣabhaśṛṅgāgrair bhidyamānaiḥ samantataḥ ।।
sūcībhramarakākola- makṣikābhiś ca saṃghaśaḥ ।। viśvastaṃ svāminaṃ mitraṃ striyaṃ vā yas tu ghātayet ।। ghātayanti ca ye jantūṃs tāḍayanti nirāgasaḥ ।। ye haranti parastrīṇāṃ varaprāvaraṇāni ca ।।
vāso dhānyaṃ hiraṇyaṃ vā gṛhakṣetram athāpi vā ।। pāṣāṇair laguḍair daṇḍais tāḍyamānais tu jarjaraiḥ ।। brahmasvaṃ ye harantīha narā narakanirbhayāḥ ।। śuṣkakāṣṭhanibaddhās te chinnakarṇākṣināsikāḥ ।।
kiṃkarair bhīṣaṇaiś caṇḍais tāḍyamānāś ca dāruṇaiḥ ।। evaṃ paramadurdharṣam adhvānaṃ jvalanaprabham ।। prataptatāmravarṇābhaṃ vahnijvālāsphuliṅgavat ।। śaktivajraiś ca saṃkīrṇam ujjvalaṃ tīvrakaṇṭakam ।।
jvālāmālākulaṃ raudraṃ sūryaraśmipratāpitam ।। yadaiva krandate jantur duḥkhārtaḥ patitaḥ kvacit ।। evaṃ saṃtāḍyamānaś ca lubdhaḥ pāpeṣu yo anayaḥ ।। sarvair eva hi gantavyam adhvānaṃ tat sudurgamam ।।
nītvā sudāruṇaṃ mārgaṃ prāṇinaṃ yamakiṃkaraiḥ ।। sā purī vipulākārā lakṣayojanam āyatā ।। prākārāḥ kāñcanās tasyā yojanāyutam ucchritāḥ ।। sā purī vividhaiḥ saṃghair ghorā ghoraiḥ samākulā ।।
pūrvadvāraṃ śubhaṃ tasyāḥ patākāśataśobhitam ।। gītanṛtyaiḥ samākīrṇaṃ gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ ।। gandharvasiddhayakṣāṇāṃ vidyādharavisarpiṇām ।। chattracāmaravinyāsaṃ nānāratnair alaṃkṛtam ।।
ṛgyajuḥsāmanirghoṣair munivṛndasamākulam ।। grīṣme vāripradā ye ca śīte cāgnipradā narāḥ ।। ye ca dānaratāḥ śūrā mātāpitṛparāś ca ye ।। paścimaṃ tu mahādvāraṃ puryā ratnair vibhūṣitam ।।
bherīmṛdaṅgasaṃnādaiḥ śaṅkhakāhalanāditam ।। praveśas tena hṛṣṭānāṃ śivabhaktimatāṃ nṛṇām ।। prasthāne ye mṛtā vīrā mṛtāḥ kālañjare girau ।। ye svāmimitralokārthe gograhe saṃkule hatāḥ ।।
puryāṃ tasyā mahāghoraṃ sarvasattvabhayaṃkaram ।। andhakārasamāyuktaṃ tīkṣṇaśṛṅgaiḥ samanvitam ।। vilumpadbhir vṛkair vyāghrair ṛkṣaiḥ siṃhaiḥ sajambukaiḥ ।। praveśas tena vai nityaṃ sarveṣām apakāriṇām ।।
śaraṇāgataṃ viśvastaṃ striyaṃ mitraṃ nirāyudham ।। nikṣepasyāpahartāro viṣavahnipradāś ca ye ।। pararandhreṣu ye krūrā ye sadānṛtavādinaḥ ।। kūṭasākṣipradātāraḥ kanyāvikrayakārakāḥ ।।
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ caiva ye vadanti ca pauruṣam ।। dakṣiṇena tu te sarve dvāreṇa praviśanti vai ।। śrotum icchāma tad brūhi vistareṇa tapodhana ।। nānāśvāpadasaṃkīrṇaṃ śivāśatanināditam ।।
bhūtapretapiśācaiś ca vṛtaṃ cānyaiś ca rākṣasaiḥ ।। mohaṃ gacchanti sahasā trāsād vipralapanti ca ।। tāḍayanti ca daṇḍaiś ca bhartsayanti punaḥ punaḥ ।। vrajanti dakṣiṇaṃ dvāraṃ praskhalantaḥ pade pade ।।
kṣuradhārānibhais tīkṣṇaiḥ pāṣāṇair nicitena ca ।। lohasūcīnibhair dantaiḥ saṃchannena kvacit kvacit ।। prataptāṅgārayuktena yānti mārgeṇa duḥkhitāḥ ।। sutaptavālukābhiś ca tathā tīkṣṇaiś ca śaṅkubhiḥ ।।
kvacit taptaśilābhiś ca kvacid vyāptaṃ himena ca ।। kvacid duṣṭāmbunā vyāptaṃ kvacit karṣāgninā punaḥ ।। kvacin mahājalaukābhiḥ kvacid ajagaraiḥ punaḥ ।। kvacid duṣṭagajaiś caiva balonmattaiḥ pramāthibhiḥ ।।
mahāśṛṅgaiś ca mahiṣair uṣṭrair mattaiś ca khādanaiḥ ।। vyādhibhiś ca mahāraudraiḥ pīḍyamānā vrajanti te ।। mahāpāṣāṇavarṣeṇa hanyamānā nirāśrayāḥ ।। mahatā bāṇavarṣeṇa bhidyamānāś ca sarvaśaḥ ।।
pradīptāṅgāravarṣeṇa dahyamānā viśanti ca ।। meghāravaiḥ sughoraiś ca vitrāsyante muhur muhuḥ ।। mahākṣārāmbudhārābhiḥ sicyamānā vrajanti ca ।। samantād dīryamāṇāś ca śuṣyante saṃkucanti ca ।।
nirālambena durgeṇa nirjalena samantataḥ ।। nīyante dehinaḥ sarve ye mūḍhāḥ pāpakarmiṇaḥ ।। ekākinaḥ parādhīnā mitrabandhuvivarjitāḥ ।। pretībhūtā niṣiddhās te śuṣkakaṇṭhauṣṭhatālukāḥ ।।
baddhāḥ śṛṅkhalayā kecit kecid uttānapādayoḥ ।। narā adhomukhāś cānye kṛṣyamāṇāḥ suduḥkhitāḥ ।। dehi dehīti bhāṣantaḥ sāśrugadgadayā girā ।। bhakṣyān uccāvacān dṛṣṭvā bhojyān peyāṃś ca puṣkalān ।।
dadhikṣīraghṛtonmiśraṃ dṛṣṭvā śālyodanaṃ tathā ।। vacobhiḥ paruṣair bhīmāḥ krodharaktāntalocanāḥ ।। prasabhaṃ dīyamānaṃ ca vāritaṃ ca dvijātiṣu ।। nāgnau dagdhaṃ jale naṣṭaṃ na hṛtaṃ nṛpataskaraiḥ ।।
yair dattāni tu dānāni sādhubhiḥ sāttvikāni tu ।। bhakṣyabhojyāś ca peyāś ca lehyāś coṣyāś ca saṃvṛtāḥ ।। yais tu dattaṃ hutaṃ ceṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇāś caiva pūjitāḥ ।। parasvaṃ katham asmābhir dātuṃ śakyeta nārakāḥ ।।
tatas te dāruṇaiś cāstraiḥ pīḍyante yamakiṃkaraiḥ ।। parighair bhindipālaiś ca gadāparaśubhiḥ śaraiḥ ।। agrataḥ siṃhavyāghrādyair bhakṣyante pāpakāriṇaḥ ।। svakarmopahatāḥ pāpāḥ krandamānāḥ sudāruṇāḥ ।।
nīyante pāpinas tatra yatra tiṣṭhet svayaṃ yamaḥ ।। evaṃ pathātikaṣṭena prāptāḥ pretapuraṃ narāḥ ।। tatas te pāpakarmāṇas taṃ paśyanti bhayānakam ।। daṃṣṭrākarālavadanaṃ bhrukūṭīkuṭilekṣaṇam ।।
aṣṭādaśabhujaṃ kruddhaṃ nīlāñjanacayopamam ।। mahāmahiṣam ārūḍhaṃ dīptāgnisamalocanam ।। pralayāmbudanirghoṣaṃ pibann iva mahodadhim ।। mṛtyuṃ ca tatsamīpasthaṃ kālānalasamaprabham ।।
mārīcogrā mahāmārī kālarātrī ca dāruṇā ।। śaktiśūlāṅkuśadharāḥ pāśacakrāsidhāriṇaḥ ।। asaṃkhyātā mahāvīryāḥ krūrāś cāñjanasaprabhāḥ ।। anena parivāreṇa mahāghoreṇa saṃvṛtam ।।
nirbhartsayati cātyarthaṃ yamas tān pāpakāriṇaḥ ।। citraguptas tu bhagavān dharmavākyaiḥ prabodhayan ।। garvitā rūpavīryeṇa paradāravimardakāḥ ।। tat kim ātmopaghātārthaṃ bhavadbhir duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ।।
bhuñjadhvaṃ svāni duḥkhāni nahi doṣo asti kasyacit ।। svakīyaiḥ karmabhir ghorair duṣprajñā balagarvitāḥ ।। alpakālasya rājyasya kṛte kiṃ duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ।। yad daṇḍitāḥ phalaṃ tasya bhuñjadhvam adhunā nṛpāḥ ।।
tat sarvaṃ saṃparityajya yūyam ekākinaḥ sthitāḥ ।। yamadūtaiḥ pāṭyamānā adhunā kīdṛśaṃ phalam ।। śocantaḥ svāni karmāṇi tūṣṇīṃ tiṣṭhanti pārthivāḥ ।। tatpātakaviśuddhyartham idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।
viśodhayadhvaṃ pāpebhyaḥ krameṇa narakāgniṣu ।। bhrāmayitvā tu vegena kṣiptvā cordhvaṃ pragṛhya ca ।। āsphoṭayanti tarasā vajreṇeva mahādrumam ।। niḥsaṃjñaḥ sa tadā dehī niśceṣṭaś ca prajāyate ।।
tataḥ pāpaviśuddhyarthaṃ kṣipanti narakārṇave ।। nivedayanti viprendrā yamāya bhṛśaduḥkhitān ।। ānīto dharmavimukhaḥ sadā pāparataḥ paraḥ ।। upapātakakartā ca sadā hiṃsārato śuciḥ ।।
kanyākrayī kūṭasākṣī kṛtaghno mitravañcakaḥ ।। pāpam ācaritaṃ karma martyaloke durātmanā ।। prabhur asya kriyāyoge vayaṃ vā paripanthinaḥ ।। narakāṇāṃ sahasreṣu lakṣakoṭiśateṣu ca ।।
pratipanne kṛte doṣe yamo vai pāpakāriṇām ।। yathā yasya vinirdiṣṭo vasiṣṭhādyair vinigrahaḥ ।। aṅkuśair mudgarair daṇḍaiḥ krakacaiḥ śaktitomaraiḥ ।। narakāṇāṃ sahasreṣu lakṣakoṭiśateṣu ca ।।
śṛṇudhvaṃ narakāṇāṃ ca svarūpaṃ ca bhayaṃkaram ।। mahāvācīti vikhyātaṃ narakaṃ śoṇitaplutam ।। tatra saṃpīḍyate magno bhidyate vajrakaṇṭake ।। yojanānāṃ śataṃ lakṣaṃ kumbhīpākaṃ sudāruṇam ।।
brahmahā bhūmihartā ca nikṣepasyāpahārakaḥ ।। rauravo vajranārācaiḥ prajvaladbhiḥ samāvṛtaḥ ।। bhidyante tatra nārācaiḥ sajvālair narake narāḥ ।। ayomayaṃ prajvalitaṃ mañjūṣaṃ narakaṃ smṛtam ।।
apratiṣṭheti narakaṃ pūyamūtrapurīṣakam ।। lākṣāprajvalitaṃ ghoraṃ narakaṃ tu vilepakam ।। mahāprabheti narakaṃ dīptaśūlamahocchrayam ।। narakaṃ ca mahāghoraṃ jayantī cāyasī śilā ।।
narakaṃ śālmalākhyaṃ tu pradīptadṛḍhakaṇṭakam ।। ye vadanti sadāsatyaṃ paramarmāvakartanam ।। ye tu rāgaiḥ kaṭākṣaiś ca vīkṣante parayoṣitam ।। teṣāṃ cakṣūṃṣi nārācair vidhyante yamakiṃkaraiḥ ।।
jvālāmālākulaṃ raudraṃ mahārauravasaṃjñitam ।। puraṃ kṣetraṃ gṛhaṃ grāmaṃ yo dīpayati vahninā ।। tāmisram iti vikhyātaṃ lakṣayojanavistṛtam ।। tatra caurā narāḥ kṣiptās tāḍyante yamakiṃkaraiḥ ।।
tāmisrād dviguṇaṃ proktaṃ mahātāmisrasaṃjñitam ।। mātṛhā pitṛhā caiva mitravisrambhaghātakaḥ ।। asipattravanaṃ nāma narakaṃ bhūriduḥkhadam ।। pātitas tatra taiḥ khaḍgaiḥ śatadhā tu samāhataḥ ।।
karambhavālukā nāma narakaṃ yojanāyutam ।। dahyate bhidyate varṣa- lakṣāyutaśatatrayam ।। kākolaṃ nāma narakaṃ kṛmipūyapariplutam ।। kuḍmalaṃ nāma narakaṃ pūrṇaṃ viṇmūtraśoṇitaiḥ ।।
sudurgandhaṃ mahābhīmaṃ māṃsaśoṇitasaṃkulam ।। krimikīṭasamākīrṇaṃ śavapūrṇaṃ mahāvaṭam ।। nāmnā vai tilapāketi narakaṃ dāruṇaṃ smṛtam ।। narakaṃ tailapāketi jvalattailamahīplavam ।।
nāmnā vajrakapāṭeti vajraśṛṅkhalayānvitam ।। nirucchvāsa iti proktaṃ tamondhaṃ vātavarjitam ।। aṅgāropacayaṃ nāma dīptāṅgārasamujjvalam ।। mahāpāyīti narakaṃ lakṣayojanam āyatam ।।
mahājvāleti narakaṃ jvālābhāsvarabhīṣaṇam ।। narakaṃ krakacākhyātaṃ pīḍyante tatra vai narāḥ ।। narakaṃ guḍapāketi jvaladguḍahradair vṛtam ।। kṣuradhāreti narakaṃ tīkṣṇakṣurasamāvṛtam ।।
narakaṃ cāmbarīṣākhyaṃ pralayānaladīpitam ।। nāmnā vajrakuṭhāreti narakaṃ vajrasaṃkulam ।। narakaṃ paritāpākhyaṃ pralayānaladīpitam ।। narakaṃ kālasūtraṃ ca vajrasūtravinirmitam ।।
narakaṃ kaśmalaṃ nāma śleṣmaśiṅghāṇakāvṛtam ।। narakaṃ cogragandheti lālāmūtrapurīṣavat ।। narakaṃ durdharaṃ nāma jalaukāvṛścikākulam ।। yac ca vajramahāpīḍā narakaṃ vajranirmitam ।।
dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ hiraṇyaṃ vā parakīyaṃ haranti ye ।। ye hatvā prāṇinaṃ mūḍhāḥ khādante kākagṛdhravat ।। āsanaṃ śayanaṃ vastraṃ parakīyaṃ haranti ye ।। phalaṃ pattraṃ nṛṇāṃ vāpi hṛtaṃ yais tu kubuddhibhiḥ ।।
paradravye kalatre ca yaḥ sadā duṣṭadhīr naraḥ ।। karmaṇā manasā vācā ye dharmavimukhā narāḥ ।। evaṃ śatasahasrāṇi lakṣakoṭiśatāni ca ।। iha kṛtvā svalpam api naraḥ karmāśubhātmakam ।।
na śṛṇvanti narā mūḍhā dharmoktaṃ sādhu bhāṣitam ।। divā rātrau prayatnena pāpaṃ kurvanti ye narāḥ ।। ihaiva phalabhoktāraḥ paratra vimukhāś ca ye ।। naraiḥ saṃprāpyate tatra karma kṛtvā śubhāśubham ।।
narakāṇi ca ghorāṇi dvāraṃ yāmyaṃ ca sattama ।। brūhi yena narā yānti sukhena yamasādanam ।। guruśuśrūṣaṇe yuktā devabrāhmaṇapūjakāḥ ।। tam adhvānaṃ ca gacchanti yathā tat kathayāmi vaḥ ।।
dharmarājapuraṃ yānti sevamānāpsarogaṇaiḥ ।। ye prayacchanti te yānti sukhenaiva mahāpathe ।। śrotriyebhyo viśeṣeṇa bhaktyā paramayā yutāḥ ।। dharmarājapuraṃ yānti vimānair abhyalaṃkṛtaiḥ ।।
te api yānty amaraprakhyā vimānair yamamandiram ।। ye prayacchanti dharmajñāḥ kṛśeṣu kṛśavṛttiṣu ।। dharmarājapuraṃ śrīmān sevyamānāpsarogaṇaiḥ ।। ye prayacchanti vastrāṇi tathaivābharaṇāni ca ।।
dharmarājapuraṃ divyaṃ chattraiḥ sauvarṇarājataiḥ ।। odanaṃ ca dvijāgryebhyo viśuddhenāntarātmanā ।। varastrībhir yathākāmaṃ sevyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayatnena śuddhyopetaṃ susaṃskṛtam ।।
yānti gandharvavāditraiḥ sevyamānā yamālayam ।। haṃsayuktair vimānais tu yānti dharmapuraṃ narāḥ ।। śrotriyebhyaḥ prayacchanti viprebhyaḥ śraddhayānvitāḥ ।। gandharvair upagīyante pure vaivasvatasya te ।।
dīrghikāḥ puṣkariṇyaś ca śītalāś ca jalāśayāḥ ।। vyajanais tālavṛntaiś ca vījyamānā mahāprabhāḥ ।। ratnaiḥ prasphuramāṇāni manojñāni śubhāni ca ।। dharmarājapuraṃ divyaṃ nānājanasamākulam ।।
te vitṛṣṇāḥ sukhaṃ yānti vimānais taṃ mahāpatham ।। yair dattāni dvijātibhyas te adhvānaṃ yānti vai sukham ।। te prayānti vimānais tu apsarogaṇamaṇḍitaiḥ ।। ropayanti phalāḍhyāni narāṇām upakāriṇaḥ ।।
varastrīgītavādyaiś ca sevyamānā vrajanti te ।। ye prayacchanti te yānti vimānaiḥ kanakojjvalaiḥ ।। uditādityasaṃkāśair vimānair bhṛśanāditaiḥ ।। divyakanyāvṛtā yānti vimānais te yamālayam ।।
prayacchanti dvijātibhyo bhaktyā paramayānvitāḥ ।। yānti dharmapuraṃ yānair vicitrair abhyalaṃkṛtāḥ ।। ādityasadṛśair yānair dīpyamānā yathāgnayaḥ ।। vrajanti bālārkanibhair dharmarājagṛhaṃ narāḥ ।।
pūjamānāpsarobhiś ca yānti dṛptā mahāgajaiḥ ।। ye prayacchanti viprebhyas te yānty aśvair yamālayam ।। cakravākaprayuktena yānti yānena te sukham ।। sa gacchati tam adhvānaṃ sukhaṃ paramanirvṛtaḥ ।।
gāṃ ca pāpaharety uktvā sukhaṃ yānti ca tat patham ।। te api sārasayuktais tu yānti yānaiś ca tat patham ।। haṃsayuktair vimānais tu sukhaṃ yānti yamālayam ।। te yānti dharmanagaraṃ yānair barhiṇayojitaiḥ ।।
te api hastirathair divyair yānti yānaiś ca tat padam ।। sa yāti kuñjarasthas tu śacīpatir iva svayam ।। nānāsvarasamāyuktaṃ jayaśabdaravair yutam ।। puraṃ tad dharmarājasya sevyamānāḥ surāsuraiḥ ।।
te api sūryapradīptais tu yānti yānair yamālayam ।। sevyamānas tu gandharvair yāti yānair yamālayam ।। sa rathenāgnivarṇena yātīha tridaśālayam ।। sa yāty agniprakāśena vimānena yamālayam ।।
yānenārkaprakāśena yāti dharmapuraṃ naraḥ ।। somamaṇḍalakalpena yāti yānena vai sukham ।। sa yāti rathamukhyena kāñcanena yamālayam ।। sa yāty amarakanyābhiḥ sevyamāno raviprabhaḥ ।।
tat pathaṃ yānti te ghoraṃ sukhayānair alaṃkṛtāḥ ।। taptahāṭakasaṃkāśair vimānair yānti te sukham ।। kurvanti te sukhaṃ yānti vimānaiḥ kanakojjvalaiḥ ।। krodhamohavinirmuktā nirmadāḥ saṃyatendriyāḥ ।।
yānti vaivasvatapuraṃ devagandharvasevitāḥ ।। pūjayanti hi te yānti vimānair bhāskaraprabhaiḥ ।। te api yānti sukhenaiva dharmarājapuraṃ narāḥ ।। tasmān māṃsaṃ na bhuñjīta nāsti miṣṭaiḥ sukhodayaḥ ।।
samāv etau purā prāha brahmā vedavidāṃ varaḥ ।। amāṃsabhakṣaṇe viprās tac ca tac ca ca tatsamam ।। dānavrataparā yānair yatra devo raveḥ sutaḥ ।। svāgatāsanadānena pādyārghyeṇa priyeṇa tu ।।
yena divyasukhārthāya bhavadbhiḥ sukṛtaṃ kṛtam ।। svargaṃ gacchadhvam atulaṃ sarvakāmasamanvitam ।। yat kiṃcid alpam aśubhaṃ phalaṃ tad iha bhokṣyatha ।। paśyanti saumyamanasaṃ pitṛbhūtam ivātmanaḥ ।।
dharmād arthas tathā kāmo mokṣaś ca parikīrtyate ।। dharmaḥ svāmī sakhā goptā tathā dhātā ca poṣakaḥ ।। dharmād aiśvaryam ekāgryaṃ dharmāt svargagatiḥ parā ।। devatvaṃ ca dvijatvaṃ ca dharmāt prāpnoty asaṃśayam ।।
tadaiṣāṃ bhajate buddhir dharmaṃ cātra dvijottamāḥ ।। yo hi nācarate dharmaṃ bhavet sa khalu vañcitaḥ ।। parapreṣyāś ca mūrkhāś ca jñeyā dharmavivarjitāḥ ।। arogā rūpavantaś ca tais tu dharmaḥ purā kṛtaḥ ।।
adharmaṃ sevamānās tu tiryagyoniṃ vrajanti te ।। te svapne api na paśyanti yamaṃ vā narakāṇi vā ।। ye namanti narā nityaṃ nahi paśyanti te yamam ।। na samartho yamas teṣāṃ te muktiphalabhāginaḥ ।।
namanti nahi te viṣṇoḥ sthānād anyatra gāminaḥ ।। praṇamya viṣṇuṃ paśyanti narakāṇi kathaṃcana ।। na yānti narakaṃ natvā sarvapāpaharaṃ harim ।। te api yānti tanuṃ tyaktvā viṣṇulokam anāmayam ।।
so api doṣakṣayān muktiṃ labhec cedipatir yathā ।। papracchuś ca punar vyāsaṃ saṃśayaṃ munisattamāḥ ।। martyasya kaḥ sahāyo vai pitā mātā suto guruḥ ।। gacchanty amutra loke vai kaś ca tān anugacchati ।।
ekas tarati durgāṇi gacchaty ekas tu durgatim ।। jñātisaṃbandhivargaś ca mitravargas tathaiva ca ।। muhūrtam iva roditvā tato yānti parāṅmukhāḥ ।। tasmād dharmaḥ sahāyaś ca sevitavyaḥ sadā nṛbhiḥ ।।
tathaivādharmasaṃyukto narakaṃ copapadyate ।। dharma eko manuṣyāṇāṃ sahāyaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। naraḥ karoty akāryāṇi parārthe lobhamohitaḥ ।। etat trayam avāptavyam adharmaparivarjitam ।।
śarīranicayaṃ jñātuṃ buddhir no atra prajāyate ।। acakṣurviṣayaṃ prāptaṃ kathaṃ dharmo anugacchati ।। buddhir ātmā ca sahitā dharmaṃ paśyanti nityadā ।। etaiś ca saha dharmo hi taṃ jīvam anugacchati ।।
śarīraṃ varjayanty ete jīvitena vivarjitam ।। ihaloke pare caiva kiṃ bhūyaḥ kathayāmi vaḥ ।। etat tu jñātum icchāmaḥ kathaṃ retaḥ pravartate ।। pṛthivī vāyur ākāśam āpo jyotir manas tathā ।।
manaḥṣaṣṭheṣu śuddhātmā retaḥ saṃpadyate mahat ।। etad vaḥ sarvam ākhyātaṃ kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotum icchatha ।। yathā jātas tu puruṣaḥ prapadyate tad ucyatām ।। viprayuktas tu tair bhūtaiḥ punar yāty aparāṃ gatim ।।
devatāḥ pañcabhūtasthāḥ kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotum icchatha ।। jīvaḥ sa bhagavan kvasthaḥ sukhaduḥkhe samaśnute ।। strīṇāṃ puṣpaṃ samāsādya tataḥ kālena bho dvijāḥ ।। duḥkhaṃ saṃsāracakraṃ ca naraḥ kleśaṃ ca vindati ।।
sukṛtaṃ karma vai bhuṅkte dharmasya phalam āśritaḥ ।। tataḥ sa puruṣo bhūtvā sevate nityadā sukham ।। sukhasyānantaraṃ duḥkhaṃ sa jīvo apy adhigacchati ।। mahāduḥkhaṃ samāsādya tiryagyonau prajāyate ।।
jīvo mohasamāyuktas tan me śṛṇuta sāṃpratam ।। yamasya viṣayaṃ ghoraṃ martyalokaṃ pravartate ।। tiryagyonyatiriktāni gatimanti ca sarvaśaḥ ।। karmabhir niyatair baddho jantur duḥkhāny upāśnute ।।
prayāti puruṣo ghorāṃ tathā vakṣyāmy ataḥ param ।। patitāt pratigṛhyātha kharayonau prajāyate ।। kharo mṛto balīvardaḥ sapta varṣāṇi jīvati ।। brahmarakṣas tu māsāṃs trīṃs tato jāyeta brāhmaṇaḥ ।।
tatra jīvati varṣāṇi daśa pañca ca bho dvijāḥ ।। gardabhaḥ pañca varṣāṇi pañca varṣāṇi śūkaraḥ ।। śvā varṣam ekaṃ bhavati tato jāyeta mānavaḥ ।। sa janmānīha saṃsāre trīn āpnoti na saṃśayaḥ ।।
pretya ca parikliṣṭeṣu paścāj jāyeta brāhmaṇaḥ ।। udagrān praiti saṃsārān adharmeṇeha cetasā ।। tatrāpi nidhanaṃ prāptaḥ krimiyonau prajāyate ।। tatas tu nidhanaṃ prāpya brahmayonau prajāyate ।।
ātmanaḥ kāmakāreṇa so api hiṃsraḥ prajāyate ।। so api viprā mṛto jantuḥ pūrvaṃ jāyeta gardabhaḥ ।। saṃvatsaraṃ tu kumbhīras tato jāyeta mānavaḥ ।। gurvapadhyānataḥ so api mṛto jāyeta gardabhaḥ ।।
biḍālaḥ sapta māsāṃs tu tato jāyeta mānavaḥ ।। tāḍayitvā tu tāv eva jāyate kacchapo dvijāḥ ।। vyālo bhūtvā tu ṣaṇ māsāṃs tato jāyeta mānuṣaḥ ।। so api mohasamāpanno mṛto jāyeta vānaraḥ ।।
śvā ca bhūtvā tu ṣaṇ māsāṃs tato jāyeta mānavaḥ ।। saṃsārāṇāṃ śataṃ gatvā kṛmiyonau prajāyate ।। duṣkṛtasya kṣayaṃ kṛtvā tato jāyeta mānuṣaḥ ।। viśvāsahartā ca naro mīno jāyeta durmatiḥ ।।
mṛgas tu caturo māsāṃs tataś chāgaḥ prajāyate ।। kīṭaḥ saṃjāyate jantus tato jāyeta mānuṣaḥ ।। kalāyān atha mudgāṃś ca godhūmān atasīs tathā ।। saṃjāyate muniśreṣṭhā mūṣiko nirapatrapaḥ ।।
śūkaro jātamātras tu rogeṇa mriyate punaḥ ।। bhūtvā śvā pañca varṣāṇi tato jāyeta mānavaḥ ।। śvā śṛgālas tato gṛdhro vyālaḥ kaṅko bakas tathā ।। puṃskokilatvam āpnoti so api saṃvatsaraṃ dvijāḥ ।।
pradharṣayitvā kāmātmā mṛto jāyeta śūkaraḥ ।। pipīlikas tu māsāṃs trīn kīṭaḥ syān māsam eva ca ।। tatra jīvati māsāṃs tu kṛmiyonau caturdaśa ।। pūrvaṃ dattvā tu yaḥ kanyāṃ dvitīye dātum icchati ।।
tatra jīvati varṣāṇi trayodaśa dvijottamāḥ ।। devakāryam akṛtvā tu pitṛkāryam athāpi vā ।। vāyasaḥ śatavarṣāṇi tato jāyeta kukkuṭaḥ ।। jyeṣṭhaṃ pitṛsamaṃ cāpi bhrātaraṃ yo avamanyate ।।
krauñco jīvati varṣāṇi daśa jāyeta jīvakaḥ ।। vṛṣalo brāhmaṇīṃ gatvā kṛmiyonau prajāyate ।। śūkaro jātamātras tu rogeṇa mriyate dvijāḥ ।। śvā bhūtvā kṛtakarmāsau jāyate mānuṣas tataḥ ।।
kṛtaghnas tu mṛto viprā yamasya viṣayaṃ gataḥ ।। daṇḍakaṃ mudgaraṃ śūlam agnidaṇḍaṃ ca dāruṇam ।। etāś cānyāś ca bahavo yamasya viṣayaṃ gatāḥ ।। saṃsāracakram āsādya krimiyonau prajāyate ।।
tato garbhaṃ samāsādya tatraiva mriyate naraḥ ।। saṃsārān subahūn gatvā tatas tiryak prajāyate ।। sa punarbhavasaṃyuktas tataḥ kūrmaḥ prajāyate ।। corayitvā tu durbuddhir madhudaṃśaḥ prajāyate ।।
corayitvā tu niṣpāvaṃ jāyate phalamūṣakaḥ ।। hṛtvā piṣṭamayaṃ pūpaṃ kumbholūkaḥ prajāyate ।। kāṃsyaṃ hṛtvā tu durbuddhir hārīto jāyate naraḥ ।। hṛtvā tu kāñcanaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ kṛmiyonau prajāyate ।।
kośakāraṃ tato hṛtvā naro jāyeta nartakaḥ ।। corayitvā dukūlaṃ tu mṛto haṃsaḥ prajāyate ।। corayitvā naraḥ paṭṭaṃ tv āvikaṃ caiva bho dvijāḥ ।। cūrṇaṃ tu hṛtvā puruṣo mṛto jāyeta barhiṇaḥ ।।
varṇakādīṃs tathā gandhāṃś corayitveha mānavaḥ ।। tatra jīvati varṣāṇi tato daśa ca pañca ca ।। corayitvā payaś cāpi balākā saṃprajāyate ।। so api viprā mṛto jantus tailapāyī prajāyate ।।
arthārthaṃ yadi vā vairī mṛto jāyeta vai kharaḥ ।। sa mṛto mṛgayonau tu nityodvigno abhijāyate ।। hato mṛgas tato mīnaḥ so api jālena badhyate ।। śvāpado daśa varṣāṇi dvīpī varṣāṇi pañca ca ।।
adharmasya kṣayaṃ kṛtvā mānuṣatvam avāpnuyāt ।। tathā piṇyākasaṃmiśram annaṃ yaś corayen naraḥ ।। daśan vai mānuṣān nityaṃ pāpātmā sa dvijottamāḥ ।। matsyamāṃsam atho hṛtvā kāko jāyeta mānavaḥ ।।
viśvāsena tu nikṣiptaṃ yo apanihnoti mānavaḥ ।। matsyayonim anuprāpya mṛto jāyeta mānuṣaḥ ।। pāpāni tu naraḥ kṛtvā tiryag jāyeta bho dvijāḥ ।। ye pāpāni narāḥ kṛtvā nirasyanti vrataiḥ sadā ।।
asaṃvītāḥ prajāyante mlecchāś cāpi na saṃśayaḥ ।। varjayanti hi pāpāni janmaprabhṛti ye narāḥ ।। striyo apy etena kalpena kṛtvā pāpam avāpnuyuḥ ।। prāyeṇa haraṇe doṣāḥ sarva eva prakīrtitāḥ ।।
aparasmin kathāyoge bhūyaḥ śroṣyatha bho dvijāḥ ।। surarṣīṇāṃ śrutaṃ madhye pṛṣṭaṃ cāpi yathā tathā ।। etac chrutvā muniśreṣṭhā dharme kuruta mānasam ।। dharmasya ca gatiṃ śrotum icchāmo vadatāṃ vara ।।
karmaṇā ca kṛteneha kena yānti śubhāṃ gatim ।। manasā viparītena nirayaṃ pratipadyate ।। manaḥsamādhisaṃyukto na sa seveta duṣkṛtam ।। tato adharmakṛtāt kṣipram aparādhāt pramucyate ।।
samāhitena manasā vimuñcati tathā tathā ।। tathā tathā śarīraṃ tu tenādharmeṇa mucyate ।। dattvā viprasya dānāni vividhāni samāhitaḥ ।। dānāni tu pravakṣyāmi yāni dattvā dvijottamāḥ ।।
sarveṣām eva dānānām annaṃ śreṣṭham udāhṛtam ।। prāṇā hy annaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tasmāj jantuḥ prajāyate ।। annam eva praśaṃsanti devarṣipitṛmānavāḥ ।। nyāyalabdhaṃ pradātavyaṃ dvijātibhyo annam uttamam ।।
yasya tv annam upāśnanti brāhmaṇāś ca sakṛd daśa ।। brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasrāṇi daśābhojya dvijottamāḥ ।। bhaikṣeṇānnaṃ samāhṛtya vipro vedapuraskṛtaḥ ।। ahiṃsan brāhmaṇasvāni nyāyena paripālya ca ।।
dvijebhyo vedamukhyebhyaḥ prayataḥ susamāhitaḥ ।। ṣaḍbhāgapariśuddhaṃ ca kṛṣer bhāgam upārjitam ।। avāpya prāṇasaṃdehaṃ kārkaśyena samārjitam ।। aurasena balenānnam arjayitvā vihiṃsakaḥ ।।
nyāyenāvāptam annaṃ tu naro harṣasamanvitaḥ ।। annam ūrjaskaraṃ loke dattvorjasvī bhaven naraḥ ।। dānavidbhiḥ kṛtaḥ panthā yena yānti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। sarvāvasthaṃ manuṣyeṇa nyāyenānnam upārjitam ।।
annasya hi pradānena naro yāti parāṃ gatim ।। evaṃ puṇyasamāyukto naraḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। yas tu prāṇāhutīpūrvam annaṃ bhuṅkte gṛhī sadā ।। bhojayitvā śataṃ nityaṃ naro vedavidāṃ varam ।।
na yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ saṃsāraṃ na ca sevate ।। evaṃ karmasamāyukto ramate vigatajvaraḥ ।। mūlam etat tu dharmāṇāṃ pradānānāṃ ca bho dvijāḥ ।। teṣāṃ śrāddhaṃ kathaṃ jñeyaṃ putraiś cānyaiś ca bandhubhiḥ ।।
śṛṇudhvaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi śrāddhakalpaṃ yathoditam ।। śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā tadā devo yathā tatra dvijottamāḥ ।। kathaṃ tenoddhṛtās te vai vārāheṇa dvijottama ।। śrotum icchāmahe brūhi paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।।
purā merugireḥ pṛṣṭhe viśvair devaiḥ saha sthitāḥ ।। tām ūcuḥ pitaro divyā ye tatrāsan samāgatāḥ ।। kāsi bhadre prabhuḥ ko vā bhavatyā vaktum arhasi ।। prabhutve bhavatām eva varayāmi yadīcchatha ।।
bhavadbhiś cādyaiva kṛtaṃ nāma koketi bhāvitam ।। tasyā mukhaṃ nirīkṣanto na tṛptim adhijagmire ।। yogacyutān nirīkṣyaiva vihāya tridivaṃ gatāḥ ।। samākulamanā dadhyau kva gateti mahāyaśāḥ ।।
taiś cāvalokitāṃ hārdāt svīkṛtāṃ ca tapobalāt ।। śaśāpa nipatiṣyadhvaṃ yogabhraṣṭā vicetasaḥ ।। yasmād dhṛtavatī ceyaṃ patīn pitṛmatī satī ।। koketi prathitā loke śiśirādrisamāśritā ।।
yogabhraṣṭā nipatitā himavatpādabhūtale ।। prasthe tīrthaṃ samāsādya saptasāmudram uttamam ।। plāvayantī gireḥ śṛṅgaṃ sarpaṇāt tu sarit smṛtā ।। dadṛśuḥ śītasalilāṃ na vidus tāṃ sulocanām ।।
badarīm ādideśātha dhenuṃ caikāṃ madhusravām ।। idaṃ girivareṇaiṣāṃ poṣaṇāya nirūpitam ।। daśa varṣasahasrāṇi yayur ekam aho yathā ।। daityā babhūvur balino yātudhānāś ca rākṣasāḥ ।।
viśvair devair virahitān sarvataḥ samupādravan ।। kokātaṭasthām uttuṅgāṃ śilāṃ te jagṛhū ruṣā ।। chādayām āsa toyena plāvayantī himācalam ।। vibhītakaṃ samāruhya nirāhārās tirohitāḥ ।।
jagur janārdanaṃ devaṃ pitaraḥ śaraṇaṃ harim ।। niśācaragaṇaṃ bhīmam atas tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। bhītaṃ pitṛgaṇaṃ viṣṇur uddhartuṃ matir ādadhe ।। pitṝn ādāya ca vibhur ujjahāra śilātalāt ।।
kokāmukhe gatabhayāḥ kṛtā devena viṣṇunā ।। dadau samāhitas tebhyo viṣṇur lohārgale jalam ।। svedodbhavāṃs tilāṃś caiva cakre colmukam uttamam ।। sthitaḥ koṭivaṭasyādho vāri gaṅgādharaṃ śuci ।।
madhukṣīrarasān gandhān puṣpadhūpānulepanān ।। daṃṣṭrayollikhya dharaṇīm abhyukṣya salilena ca ।। pariṇīyolmukenainām abhyukṣya ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। ṛṣīn āhūya papraccha kariṣye pitṛtarpaṇam ।।
āhūya mantratas teṣāṃ viṣṭarāṇi dadau prabhuḥ ।। akṣatair daivatārakṣāṃ cakre cakragadādharaḥ ।। rakṣanti sarvatra diśo rakṣārthaṃ nirmitā hi te ।। nahi kaścit kṣayaṃ teṣāṃ kartuṃ śaktaś carācare ।।
devānāṃ te hi rakṣārthaṃ niyuktā viṣṇunā purā ।। viśvebhyo devebhya iti tatas tān paryapṛcchata ।। āvāhayasveti ca tair uktas tv āvāhayec chuciḥ ।। jānāv āropya hastaṃ tu dadau savyena cāsanam ।।
vārāhaḥ pitṛviprāṇām āyāntu na itīrayan ।। kṛtvā cāvāhanaṃ cakre pitṝṇāṃ nāmagotrataḥ ।। saṃvatsarair ity udīrya tato arghyaṃ teṣu vinyaset ।। yan me pitāmahāity evaṃ dadāv arghyaṃ pitāmaha ।।
kuśagandhatilonmiśraṃ sapuṣpam apasavyataḥ ।। tān arcya bhūyo gandhādyair dhūpaṃ dattvā tu bhaktitaḥ ।। tataś cānnaṃ samādāya sarpistilakuśākulam ।। agnau kariṣya iti taiḥ kuruṣveti ca coditaḥ ।।
ye māmakāiti ca japed yajuḥsaptakam acyutam ।। trir āhutikam ekaikaṃ pitaraṃ tu prati dvijāḥ ।। tato annaṃ sarasaṃ svādu dadau pāyasapūrvakam ।। alpaśākaṃ bahuphalaṃ ṣaḍrasam amṛtopamam ।।
vedapūrvaṃ pitṛsvannam ājyaplutaṃ madhūkṣitam ।। bhuñjāneṣu tu vipreṣu japan vai mantrapañcakam ।। trimadhu trisuparṇaṃ ca bṛhadāraṇyakaṃ tathā ।। bhuktavatsu ca vipreṣu pṛṣṭvā tṛptā stha ity uta ।।
piṇḍapātraṃ samādāya cchāyāyai pradadau tataḥ ।। vārāho bhūm athollikhya samācchādya kuśair api ।। satileṣu samūleṣu kuśeṣv eva tu saṃśrayaḥ ।। pṛthivī dadhīr ity uktvā tataḥ piṇḍaṃ pradattavān ।।
mātāmahānām apy evaṃ dadau piṇḍān sa śūkaraḥ ।। etad vaḥ pitar ity uktvā dadau vāsāṃsi bhaktitaḥ ।। gandhapuṣpādikaṃ dattvā kṛtvā caiṣāṃ pradakṣiṇām ।। tatas tv abhyukṣya tāṃ bhūmiṃ dattvāpaḥ sumanokṣatān ।।
akṣayyaṃ nas tv iti pitṝn prīyatām iti devatāḥ ।। tato nivṛtya tu japed yan me nāma itīrayan ।। arghyapātrāṇi piṇḍānām antare sa pavitrakān ।। himakṣīraṃ madhutilān pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ dadau ।।
rajataṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā viprān devo gadādharaḥ ।। kaścit saṃpannam ity uktvā pratyuktas tair dvijottamāḥ ।। śiṣṭam annaṃ ca papraccha tair iṣṭaiḥ saha coditaḥ ।। vāje vāje iti paṭhan bahir vedi vinirgataḥ ।।
alagnān vipulān vālān prārthayām āsa cāśiṣam ।। pradakṣiṇam upāvṛtya kṛtvā pādābhivādanam ।। viśrāmyatāṃ praviśyātha piṇḍaṃ jagrāha madhyamam ।। ādhatta pitaro garbham ity uktvā sāpi rūpiṇī ।।
visarjanaṃ pitṝṇāṃ sa kartukāmaś ca śūkaraḥ ।। śaptāś ca bhagavan pūrvaṃ divasthā himabhānunā ।। tad evaṃ bhavatā trātāḥ praviśanto rasātalam ।। tat te bhūyo abhirakṣantu viśve devā hi naḥ sadā ।।
somo adhidevo asmākaṃ ca bhavatv acyuta yogadhṛk ।। divi bhūmau sadā vāso bhavatv asmāsu yogataḥ ।। ūrjā ceyaṃ hi naḥ patnī svadhānāmnā tu viśrutā ।। ity evam uktaḥ pitṛbhir vārāho bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।।
yad uktaṃ tu bhavadbhir me sarvam etad bhaviṣyati ।। adhiyajñas tathaivāgnir bhavatāṃ kalpanā tv iyam ।। brahmā viṣṇuś ca rudraś ca bhavatām adhipūruṣāḥ ।। yogino yogadehāś ca yogadhārāś ca suvratāḥ ।।
svargasthān narakasthāṃś ca bhūmisthāṃś ca carācarān ।। iyam ūrjā śaśisutā kīlālamadhuvigrahā ।। tatreyaṃ bhavatāṃ patnī bhaviṣyati varānanā ।। tīrthakoṭimahāpuṇyā madrūpaparipālitā ।।
varāhadarśanaṃ puṇyaṃ pūjanaṃ bhuktimuktidam ।। tīrtheṣv āplavanaṃ puṇyam upavāsaś ca svargadaḥ ।। māghe māsy asite pakṣe bhavadbhir uḍupakṣaye ।। tasmin kāle tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nirvapiṣyati ।।
ekādaśīṃ dvādaśīṃ ca stheyam atra mayā sadā ।। tad vrajadhvaṃ mahābhāgāḥ sthānam iṣṭaṃ yatheṣṭataḥ ।। gate varāhe pitaraḥ kokām āmantrya te yayuḥ ।। chāyā mahīmayī kroḍī piṇḍaprāśanabṛṃhitā ।।
prāgjyotiṣaṃ ca nagaram asya dattaṃ ca viṣṇunā ।। kathaṃ kva ca kadā keṣu kais tad brūhi tapodhana ।। yathā yatra yadā yeṣu yair dravyais tad vadāmy aham ।। kuladharmam anutiṣṭhadbhir dātavyaṃ mantrapūrvakam ।।
amantrakaṃ vidhipūrvaṃ vahniyāgavivarjitam ।। śikhareṣu girīndrāṇāṃ puṇyadeśeṣu bho dvijāḥ ।। saṃgameṣu nadīnāṃ ca samudreṣu ca saptasu ।। divyapādapamūleṣu yajñiyeṣu hradeṣu ca ।।
kirāteṣu kaliṅgeṣu koṅkaṇeṣu kṛmiṣv api ।। sindhor uttarakūleṣu narmadāyāś ca dakṣiṇe ।। śrāddhaṃ deyam uśantīha māsi māsy uḍupakṣaye ।। nityaśrāddham adaivaṃ ca manuṣyaiḥ saha gīyate ।।
kāmyāny anyāni śrāddhāni pratisaṃvatsaraṃ dvijaiḥ ।। tatra yugmān dvijān āhur mantrapūrvaṃ tu vai dvijāḥ ।। pūrveṇaiveha vidhinā śrāddhaṃ tatra vidhīyate ।। putrārthinī tṛtīyā tu caturthī śatrunāśinī ।।
gaṇādhipatyaṃ saptamyām aṣṭamyāṃ buddhim uttamām ।। vedāṃs tathāpnuyāt sarvān ekādaśyāṃ kriyāparaḥ ।। prajāvṛddhiṃ paśuṃ medhāṃ svātantryaṃ puṣṭim uttamām ।। avāpnoti na saṃdehaḥ śrāddhaṃ śraddhāsamanvitaḥ ।।
yuvānaḥ pitaro yasya mṛtāḥ śastreṇa vā hatāḥ ।। śrāddhaṃ kurvann amāvāsyāṃ yatnena puruṣaḥ śuciḥ ।। ataḥparaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ vadato mama ।। māsaṃ tṛptiḥ pitṝṇāṃ tu haviṣyānnena jāyate ।।
trīn māsān hāriṇaṃ māṃsaṃ vijñeyaṃ pitṛtṛptaye ।। śākunaṃ pañca vai māsān ṣaṇ māsāñ śūkarāmiṣam ।। karoti tṛptiṃ nava vai rurumāṃsaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। tathaikādaśa māsāṃs tu aurabhraṃ pitṛtṛptidam ।।
vādhrīnam āmiṣaṃ lohaṃ kālaśākaṃ tathā madhu ।। anantaṃ vai prayacchanti tṛptiyogaṃ sutāṃs tathā ।। yo dadāti guḍonmiśrāṃs tilān vā śrāddhakarmaṇi ।। api naḥ sa kule bhūyād yo no dadyāj jalāñjalim ।।
eṣṭavyā bahavaḥ putrā yady eko api gayāṃ vrajet ।। kṛttikāsu pitṝn arcya svargam āpnoti mānavaḥ ।। śauryam ārdrāsu cāpnoti kṣetrāṇi ca punarvasau ।। maghāsu ca prajāṃ puṣṭiṃ saubhāgyaṃ phālgunīṣu ca ।।
