prayāti śreṣṭhatāṃ śāstre haste śrāddhaprado naraḥ ।। vāṇijyalābhadā svātī viśākhā putrakāmadā ।। ādhipatyaṃ ca jyeṣṭhāsu mūle cārogyam uttamam ।। śravaṇena śubhāṃl lokān dhaniṣṭhāsu dhanaṃ mahat ।।
ajāvikaṃ prauṣṭhapadyāṃ vinded gāvas tathottare ।। śrāddhaṃ kurvaṃs tathāpnoti bharaṇīṣv āyur uttamam ।। tasmāt kāmyāni śrāddhāni deyāni vidhivad dvijāḥ ।। yān yān kāmān abhidhyāyan kanyārāśigate ravau ।।
nāndīmukhānāṃ kartavyaṃ kanyārāśigate ravau ।। divyabhaumāntarikṣāṇi sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।। kanyāṃ gate savitari yāny ahāni tu ṣoḍaśa ।। rājasūyāśvamedhābhyāṃ ya icched durlabhaṃ phalam ।।
uttarāhastanakṣatra- gate tīkṣṇāṃśumālini ।। hastarkṣage dinakare pitṛrājānuśāsanāt ।। vṛścike samatikrānte pitaro daivataiḥ saha ।। aṣṭakāsu ca kartavyaṃ śrāddhaṃ manvantarāsu vai ।।
grahaṇe ca vyatīpāte ravicandrasamāgame ।। ayanadvitaye śrāddhaṃ viṣuvadvitaye tathā ।। eṣu kāryaṃ dvijāḥ śrāddhaṃ piṇḍanirvāpaṇād ṛte ।। śrāddhaṃ kāryaṃ tu śuklāyāṃ saṃkrāntividhinā naraiḥ ।।
śrāddhaṃ kāryaṃ pāyasena dakṣiṇāyanavac ca tat ।। tenaikena ca kartavyaṃ śrāddhaṃ vidhivad uttamam ।। pārvaṇena vidhānena śrāddhaṃ kāryaṃ tathā dvijaiḥ ।। pitṛvyasyāpy aputrasya bhrātur jyeṣṭhasya caiva hi ।।
dvau daive pitṛkārye trīn ekaikam ubhayatra vā ।। pretībhūtasya satataṃ bhuvi piṇḍaṃ jalaṃ tathā ।। tṛtīye ahni ca kartavyaṃ pretāsthicayanaṃ dvijaiḥ ।। vaiśyaḥ pañcadaśāhena śūdro māsena śudhyati ।।
dvādaśe ahani māse ca tripakṣe ca tataḥ param ।। tata parataraṃ kāryaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kramāt ।। tataḥ prabhṛti nirmuktāḥ pretatvāt pitṛtāṃ gatāḥ ।। ekoddiṣṭāśinaḥ pretāḥ pitṝṇāṃ nirṇayas tridhā ।।
pretībhūtasya vidhivad brūhi no vadatāṃ vara ।। tac cāpi devarahitam ekārghaikapavitrakam ।। apasavyaṃ ca tatrāpi bhojayed ayujo dvijān ।। taṃ kathyamānam ekāgrāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ me dvijottamāḥ ।।
kuryāt pitṝṇāṃ tritayam ekaṃ pretasya ca dvijāḥ ।। ye samānā iti japan pūrvavac cheṣam ācaret ।। sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tāsāṃ putrābhāve na vidyate ।। mṛtāhani ca tat kāryaṃ pitṝṇāṃ vidhicoditam ।।
kuryur etaṃ vidhiṃ samyak putrasya ca sutāḥ sutāḥ ।। dvyāmuṣyāyaṇasaṃjñās tu mātāmahapitāmahān ।। sarvābhāve striyaḥ kuryuḥ svabhartṝṇām amantrakam ।। tajjātīyair naraiḥ samyag vāhādyāḥ sakalāḥ kriyāḥ ।।
etā vaḥ kathitā viprā nityā naimittikās tathā ।। darśas tatra nimittaṃ tu vidyād indukṣayānvitaḥ ।। sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvaṃ pitur yaḥ prapitāmahaḥ ।। teṣāṃ hi yaś caturtho anyaḥ sa tu lepabhujo bhavet ।।
pitā pitāmahaś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ ।। lepasaṃbandhinaś cānye pitāmahapitāmahāt ।। ity eṣa munibhiḥ proktaḥ saṃbandhaḥ sāptapauruṣaḥ ।। tato anye pūrvajāḥ sarve ye cānye narakaukasaḥ ।।
tān sarvān yajamāno vai śrāddhaṃ kurvan yathāvidhi ।। annaprakiraṇaṃ yat tu manuṣyaiḥ kriyate bhuvi ।। yad ambu snānavastrotthaṃ bhūmau patati bho dvijāḥ ।। yās tu gandhāmbukaṇikāḥ patanti dharaṇītale ।।
uddhṛteṣv atha piṇḍeṣu yāś cāmbukaṇikā bhuvi ।। ye cādantāḥ kule bālāḥ kriyāyogād bahiṣkṛtāḥ ।। bhuktvā cācāmatāṃ yac ca yaj jalaṃ cāṅghriśaucajam ।। evaṃ yo yajamānasya yaś ca teṣāṃ dvijanmanām ।।
tenānnena kule tatra ye ca yonyantaraṃ gatāḥ ।। anyāyopārjitair arthair yac chrāddhaṃ kriyate naraiḥ ।। evam āpyāyanaṃ viprā bahūnām eva bāndhavaiḥ ।। tasmāc chrāddhaṃ naro bhaktyā śākenāpi yathāvidhi ।।
śrāddhaṃ deyaṃ tu vipreṣu saṃyateṣv agnihotriṣu ।। triṇāciketas trimadhus trisuparṇaḥ ṣaḍaṅgavit ।। ṛtvikpurohitācāryam upādhyāyaṃ ca bhojayet ।। maṇḍalabrāhmaṇo yas tu purāṇārthaviśāradaḥ ।।
ete śrāddhe niyoktavyā brāhmaṇāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ ।। daive niyoge pitrye ca tāṃs tathaivopakalpayet ।। śrāddhaṃ dattvā ca bhuktvā ca maithunaṃ yo adhigacchati ।। gatvā ca yoṣitaṃ śrāddhe yo bhuṅkte yas tu gacchati ।।
tasmāt tv aprathamaṃ kāryaṃ prājñenopanimantraṇam ।। bhikṣārtham āgatāṃś cāpi kālena saṃyatān yatīn ।। yoginaś ca tadā śrāddhe bhojanīyā vipaścitā ।। brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasrāṇi eko yogī bhaved yadi ।।
pitṛgāthā tathaivātra gīyate brahmavādibhiḥ ।। kadā naḥ saṃtatāv agryaḥ kasyacid bhavitā sutaḥ ।। gayāyām athavā piṇḍaṃ khaḍgamāṃsaṃ tathā haviḥ ।। vaiśvadevaṃ ca saumyaṃ ca khaḍgamāṃsaṃ paraṃ haviḥ ।।
dadyāc chrāddhaṃ trayodaśyāṃ maghāsu ca yathāvidhi ।। tasmāt saṃpūjayed bhaktyā svapitṝn vidhivan naraḥ ।। vasūn rudrāṃs tathādityān nakṣatragrahatārakāḥ ।। āyuḥ prajāṃ dhanaṃ vidyāṃ svargaṃ mokṣaṃ sukhāni ca ।।
tathāparāhṇaḥ pūrvāhṇāt pitṝṇām atiricyate ।। pavitrapāṇir ācāntān āsaneṣūpaveśayet ।। visarjayet priyāṇy uktvā praṇipatya ca bhaktitaḥ ।। tato nityakriyāṃ kuryād bhojayec ca tathātithīn ।।
na pitṝṇāṃ tathaivānye śeṣaṃ pūrvavad ācaret ।। tatas tad annaṃ bhuñjīta saha bhṛtyādibhir naraḥ ।। yathā ca vipramukhyānāṃ paritoṣo abhijāyate ।। mitradhruk kunakhī klībaḥ kṣayī śuklī vaṇikpathaḥ ।।
mūkaḥ paṅguḥ kuṇiḥ ṣaṇḍho duścarmā vyaṅgakekarau ।। mitraśatrur duṣkulīnaḥ paśupālo nirākṛtiḥ ।। vṛṣalīpatis tatsutaś ca na bhavec chrāddhabhug dvijaḥ ।। bhṛtakādhyāpako yas tu bhṛtakādhyāpitaś ca yaḥ ।।
abhiśastas tathā stenaḥ patito vārddhuṣiḥ śaṭhaḥ ।। rājñaḥ purohito bhṛtyo vidyāhīno atha matsarī ।। nakṣatrasūcakaś caiva parvakāraś ca garhitaḥ ।। na te śrāddhe niyoktavyā dṛṣṭvāmī paṅktidūṣakāḥ ।।
daṇḍo devakṛtas tatra sadyaḥ patati dāruṇaḥ ।। ādidharmaṃ samutsṛjya dātā tatra vinaśyati ।। tanniḥśvāsāgninirdagdhas tatra dātā vinaśyati ।। tasmād vāsāṃsi deyāni śrāddhakāle viśeṣataḥ ।।
śrāddhe tv etāni yo dadyāt kāmān āpnoti cottamān ।। tathānnaṃ tatra viprāṇāṃ jantur yatrāvatiṣṭhate ।। api ye nidhanaṃ prāptās tṛptis tān upatiṣṭhate ।। namaḥ svāhāyai svadhāyai nityam eva bhavantv iti ।।
piṇḍanirvapaṇe vāpi japed evaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। prīyante triṣu lokeṣu mantro ayaṃ tārayaty uta ।। pattrorṇaṃ paṭṭasūtraṃ ca kauśeyaṃ ca vivarjayet ।। na prīṇayanty athaitāni dātuś cāpy anayo bhavet ।।
iṣṭenānnena bhakṣyeṇa bhojayet taṃ yathāvidhi ।। patnyai dadyāt prajārthī ca madhyamaṃ mantrapūrvakam ।। prajñāṃ caiva yaśaḥ kīrtim apsu caiva nivedayet ।। kumāraśālām anvicchan kukkuṭebhyaḥ prayacchati ।।
anujñātas tu viprais taiḥ kāmam uddhriyatām iti ।। anyathā tu bhaved doṣaḥ pitṝṇāṃ nopatiṣṭhati ।। saṃtarpayet pitṝn mudgaiḥ śyāmākaiḥ sarṣapadravaiḥ ।। prasātikāṃ satūlikāṃ dadyāc chrāddhe vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।
prācīnāmalakaṃ kṣīraṃ nārikelaṃ parūṣakam ।। paṭolaṃ ca priyālaṃ ca karkandhūbadarāṇi ca ।। etāni phalajātāni śrāddhe deyāni yatnataḥ ।। gavyaṃ payo dadhi ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ ca tilasaṃbhavam ।।
nivedayec chucīn gandhāṃś candanāgurukuṅkumān ।। śākam āraṇyakaṃ cāpi dadyāt puṣpāṇy amūni ca ।। vṛntāśokāṭarūṣaṃ ca tulasī tilakaṃ tathā ।। kubjakaṃ tagaraṃ caiva mṛgam āraṇyaketakīm ।।
kamalaṃ kumudaṃ padmaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ ca yatnataḥ ।। kuṣṭhaṃ māṃsī vālakaṃ ca kukkuṭī jātipattrakam ।। punar apy evamādīni gandhayogyāni cakṣate ।। dhūpāni pitṛyogyāni ṛṣiguggulam eva ca ।।
vipruṣān markaṭāṃś caiva kodravāṃś caiva varjayet ।। straiṇam auṣṭram āvikaṃ ca dadhi kṣīraṃ ghṛtaṃ tyajet ।। jambīraṃ raktabilvaṃ ca śālasyāpi phalaṃ tyajet ।। pūtikaṃ mṛganābhiṃ ca rocanāṃ padmacandanam ।।
pālaṅkaṃ ca kumārīṃ ca kirātaṃ piṇḍamūlakam ।। jīvaṃ ca śatapuṣpāṃ ca nālikāṃ gandhaśūkaram ।। mānakandaṃ viṣakandaṃ vajrakandaṃ gadāsthikam ।। alābuṃ tiktaparṇāṃ ca kūṣmāṇḍaṃ kaṭukatrayam ।।
kālīyaṃ raktavāṇāṃ ca balākā lakucaṃ tathā ।। āranālaṃ ca śuktaṃ ca śīrṇaṃ paryuṣitaṃ tathā ।। atyamlaṃ picchilaṃ sūkṣmaṃ yātayāmaṃ ca sattamāḥ ।। hiṅgūgragandhaṃ phaṇiśaṃ bhūnimbaṃ nimbarājike ।।
dāḍimaṃ māgadhīṃ caiva nāgarārdrakatittiḍīḥ ।। pāyasaṃ śālmalīmudgān modakādīṃś ca bhaktitaḥ ।। yāni cābhyavahāryāṇi svādusnigdhāni bho dvijāḥ ।। atyamlaṃ cātilavaṇam atiriktakaṭūni ca ।।
mṛṣṭasnigdhāni yāni syur īṣatkaṭvamlakāni ca ।। chāgamāṃsaṃ vārtikaṃ ca taittiraṃ śaśakāmiṣam ।। vāghrīṇasaṃ raktaśivaṃ lohaṃ śalkasamanvitam ।। yad apy uktaṃ hi manunā rohitaṃ pratiyojayet ।।
evam uktaṃ mayā viprā vārāheṇāvalokitam ।। etāni ca niṣiddhāni vārāheṇa tapodhanāḥ ।। rohitaṃ śūkaraṃ kūrmaṃ godhāhaṃsaṃ ca varjayet ।। kuraraṃ ca nirasthiṃ ca vāsahātaṃ ca kukkuṭān ।।
nakulolūkamārjārāṃl lopān anyān sudurgrahān ।। etān anyāṃś ca saṃduṣṭān yo bhakṣayati durmatiḥ ।। pitṛṣv etāṃs tu yo dadyāt pāpātmā garhitāmiṣān ।। kusumbhaśākaṃ jambīraṃ sigrukaṃ kovidārakam ।।
kodravaṃ kokilākṣaṃ ca cukraṃ kambukapadmakam ।। phalaṃ tālatarūṇāṃ ca bhuktyā narakam ṛcchati ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena nāharet tu vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। varam evātmamāṃsasya bhakṣaṇaṃ munayaḥ kṛtam ।।
ajñānād vā pramādād vā sakṛd etāni ca dvijāḥ ।। phalamūladadhikṣīra- takragomūtrayāvakaiḥ ।। evaṃ niṣiddhācaraṇe kṛte sakṛd api dvijaiḥ ।। niṣiddhaṃ varjayed dravyaṃ yathoktaṃ ca dvijottamāḥ ।।
ābrahmastambaparyantaṃ jagat prīṇāti mānavaḥ ।। kathaṃ śrāddhaṃ hi kartavyam etad vistaraśo vada ।। evaṃ na hīyate dharmo laukiko vaidikas tathā ।। sa hi śrāddhaṃ kathaṃ kuryād etat tvaṃ vaktum arhasi ।।
prapitāmahasya piṇḍaṃ vai hy ayaṃ śāstreṣu nirṇayaḥ ।। sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ nāsti na ca pārvaṇam iṣyate ।। āyuṣā dhanaputraiś ca vardhaty āśu na saṃśayaḥ ।। tad annam asya pitaro aśnanti ca triyugaṃ dvijāḥ ।।
saṃpūjyā havyakavyābhyām annenātithibāndhavāḥ ।। bhikṣavo yācamānāś ca ye cānye pānthakā gṛhe ।। pāpaṃ bhuṅkte samullaṅghya nityanaimittikīḥ kriyāḥ ।। nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ trividhaṃ karma pauruṣam ।।
yaṃ kurvan sukham āpnoti paratreha ca mānavaḥ ।। na hy ācāravihīnasya bhadram atra paratra vā ।। bhavanti yaḥ sadācāraṃ samullaṅghya pravartate ।। kāryo dharmaḥ sadācāra ācārasyaiva lakṣaṇam ।।
ātmanaikamanā bhūtvā tathaiva paripālayet ।। tatsaṃsiddhau gṛhasthasya siddhir atra paratra ca ।। ardhena cātmabharaṇaṃ nityanaimittikāni ca ।। evam ācarato viprā arthaḥ sāphalyam ṛcchati ।।
paratrārthas tathaivānyaḥ kāryo atraiva phalapradaḥ ।। dvidhā kāmo api racitas trivargāyāvirodhakṛt ।। viparītānubandhāṃś ca budhyadhvaṃ tān dvijottamāḥ ।। ubhābhyāṃ ca dvidhā kāmaṃ tena tau ca dvidhā punaḥ ।।
samutthāya tathācamya prasnāto niyataḥ śuciḥ ।। upāsīta yathānyāyaṃ naināṃ jahyād anāpadi ।। asacchāstram asadvādam asatsevāṃ ca vai dvijāḥ ।। nodayāstamane caivam udīkṣeta vivasvataḥ ।।
pūrvāhṇa eva kāryāṇi devatānāṃ ca tarpaṇam ।। na viṇmūtram anuṣṭheyaṃ na ca kṛṣṭe na govraje ।। udakyādarśanasparśam evaṃ saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ tathā ।। nādhitiṣṭhec chakṛnmūtre keśabhasmasapālikāḥ ।।
nādhitiṣṭhet tathā prājñaḥ pathi vastrāṇi vā bhuvi ।। kṛtvā vibhavataḥ paścād gṛhastho bhoktum arhati ।। bhuñjīta cānnaṃ taccitto hy antarjānuḥ sadā naraḥ ।। pratyakṣalavaṇaṃ varjyam annam ucchiṣṭam eva ca ।।
kurvīta caivam ucchiṣṭaṃ na kiṃcid api bhakṣayet ।। na paśyec ca raviṃ cenduṃ nakṣatrāṇi ca kāmataḥ ।। gurūṇām āsanaṃ deyam abhyutthānādisatkṛtam ।। tatrānugamanaṃ kuryāt pratikūlaṃ na saṃcaret ।।
nāvāhayed dvijān agnau homaṃ kurvīta buddhimān ।। na pāṇibhyām ubhābhyāṃ tu kaṇḍūyeta śiras tathā ।। śiraḥsnātaś ca tailena nāṅgaṃ kiṃcid upaspṛśet ।। brāhmaṇānalagosūryān nāvamanyet kadācana ।।
ābādhāsu yathākāmaṃ kuryān mūtrapurīṣayoḥ ।। parivādaṃ na śṛṇuyād anyeṣām api kurvatām ।। vidyādhikasya garbhiṇyā rogārtasya mahīyataḥ ।। devālayaṃ caidyataruṃ tathaiva ca catuṣpatham ।।
upānadvastramālyādi dhṛtam anyair na dhārayet ।। tailābhyaṅgaṃ tathā bhogaṃ yoṣitaś ca vivarjayet ।। na cāpi vikṣipet pādau pādaṃ pādena nākramet ।। marmābhighātam ākrośaṃ paiśunyaṃ ca vivarjayet ।।
mūrkhonmattavyasanino virūpān api vā tathā ।। parasya daṇḍaṃ nodyacchec chikṣārthaṃ śiṣyaputrayoḥ ।। saṃyāvaṃ kṛśaraṃ māṃsaṃ nātmārtham upasādhayet ।। prāṅmukhodaṅmukho vāpi vāgyato dantadhāvanam ।।
nodakśirāḥ svapej jātu na ca pratyakśirā naraḥ ।। na tu gandhavatīṣv apsu śayīta na tathoṣasi ।। apamṛjyān na vastrāntair gātrāṇy ambarapāṇibhiḥ ।। anulepanam ādadyān nāsnātaḥ karhicid budhaḥ ।।
na ca kuryād viparyāsaṃ vāsasor nāpi bhūṣayoḥ ।। kīṭakeśāvapannaṃ ca tathā śvabhir avekṣitam ।। pṛṣṭhamāṃsaṃ vṛthāmāṃsaṃ varjyamāṃsaṃ ca varjayet ।। varjyaṃ ciroṣitaṃ viprāḥ śuṣkaṃ paryuṣitaṃ ca yat ।।
tathā māṃsavikārāś ca naiva varjyāś ciroṣitāḥ ।। nāsnāto naiva saṃviṣṭo na caivānyamanā naraḥ ।। preṣyāṇām apradāyātha na bhuñjīta kadācana ।। paradārā na gantavyāḥ puruṣeṇa vipaścitā ।।
nahīdṛśam anāyuṣyaṃ loke kiṃcana vidyate ।। devāgnipitṛkāryāṇi tathā gurvabhivādanam ।। aphenaśabdagandhābhir adbhir acchābhir ādarāt ।। antarjalād āvasathād valmīkān mūṣikāsthalāt ।।
prakṣālya hastau pādau ca samabhyukṣya samāhitaḥ ।। parimṛjya dvir āvartya khāni mūrdhānam eva ca ।। kṣute avalīḍhe vāte ca tathā niṣṭhīvanādiṣu ।। kurvītālambhanaṃ cāpi dakṣiṇaśravaṇasya ca ।।
na vidyamāne pūrvokta uttaraprāptir iṣyate ।। svāpe adhvani tathā bhuñjan svādhyāyaṃ ca vivarjayet ।। tathāparāhṇe kurvīta śraddhayā pitṛtarpaṇam ।। prāṅmukhodaṅmukho vāpi śmaśrukarma ca kārayet ।।
udvahet pitṛmātroś ca saptamīṃ pañcamīṃ tathā ।। paropatāpakaṃ karma jantupīḍāṃ ca sarvadā ।। strījanmaparihārārthaṃ pañcamīṃ cāpi varjayet ।। yugmāsu putrā jāyante striyo ayugmāsu rātriṣu ।।
kṣurakarmaṇi riktāṃ vai varjayīta vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। na cotkṛṣṭāsanaṃ deyam anutkṛṣṭasya cādarāt ।। snāyīta cailavān prājñaḥ kaṭabhūmim upetya ca ।। guroḥ pativratānāṃ ca brahmayajñatapasvinām ।।
dhavalāmbarasaṃvītaḥ sitapuṣpavibhūṣitaḥ ।। noddhatonmattamūḍhaiś ca nāvinītaiś ca paṇḍitaḥ ।। na cātivyayaśīlaiś ca puruṣair naiva vairibhiḥ ।। nisvair na vādaikaparair naraiś cānyais tathādhamaiḥ ।।
uttiṣṭhed vibhavāc cainān arcayed gṛham āgatān ।। samyag gṛhe arcanaṃ kṛtvā yathāsthānam anukramāt ।। prathamāṃ brahmaṇe dadyāt prajānāṃ pataye tataḥ ।। tato anumataye dadyād dadyād bahubaliṃ tataḥ ।।
vaiśvadevaṃ tataḥ kuryād vadata śṛṇuta dvijāḥ ।। parjanyāpodharitrīṇāṃ dadyāt tu maṇike trayam ।। brahmaṇe cāntarikṣāya sūryāya ca yathākramāt ।। uṣase bhūtapataye dadyād vottarataḥ śuciḥ ।।
kṛtvāpasavyaṃ vāyavyāṃ yakṣmaitat taiti saṃvadan ।। devānāṃ ca tataḥ kuryād brāhmaṇānāṃ namaskriyām ।। etad brāhmam iti khyātaṃ tīrtham ācamanāya vai ।। pitṝṇāṃ tena toyāni dadyān nāndīmukhād ṛte ।।
tīrthaṃ kaniṣṭhikāmūle kāyaṃ tatra prajāpateḥ ।। sadā kāryāṇi kurvīta nānyatīrthaḥ kadācana ।। devatīrthena devānāṃ prājāpatyaṃ jitena ca ।। prājāpatyena tīrthena yac ca kiṃcit prajāpateḥ ।।
gurudevapitṝn viprān na ca pādau prasārayet ।। na vilambeta medhāvī na mukhenānalaṃ dhamet ।। ṛṇapradātā vaidyaś ca śrotriyaḥ sajalā nadī ।। tatra nityaṃ vaset prājñaḥ kutaḥ kunṛpatau sukham ।।
śāntāmatsariṇo lokās tatra vāsaḥ sukhodayaḥ ।। yatrauṣadhāny aśeṣāṇi vaset tatra vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। jigīṣuḥ pūrvavairaś ca janaś ca satatotsavaḥ ।। yatrāpradhṛṣyo nṛpatir yatra sasyapradā mahī ।।
ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhakṣyabhojyavidhikriyām ।। asnehā api godhūma- yavagorasavikriyāḥ ।। bhakṣyāś caite tathā varjyau grāmaśūkarakukkuṭau ।। prokṣitaṃ cauṣadhārthaṃ ca khādan māṃsaṃ na duṣyati ।।
śākamūlaphalānāṃ ca tathā vidalacarmaṇām ।। pātrāṇāṃ camasānāṃ ca ambunā śaucam iṣyate ।। sasnehānāṃ ca pātrāṇāṃ śuddhir uṣṇena vāriṇā ।। saṃhatānāṃ ca vastrāṇāṃ prokṣaṇāt saṃcayasya ca ।।
āvikānāṃ samastānāṃ keśānāṃ caivam iṣyate ।। śodhanaṃ caiva bhavati upaghātavatāṃ sadā ।। dārudantāsthiśṛṅgāṇāṃ takṣaṇāc chuddhir iṣyate ।। śuddhaṃ bhaikṣyaṃ kāruhastaḥ paṇyaṃ yoṣinmukhaṃ tathā ।।
prākpraśastaṃ cirātītam anekāntaritaṃ laghu ।। karmāntāgāraśālāś ca stanadvayaṃ śuci striyāḥ ।। bhūmir viśudhyate kālād dāhamārjanagokulaiḥ ।। keśakīṭāvapanne ca goghrāte makṣikānvite ।।
audumbarāṇām amlena vāriṇā trapusīsayoḥ ।। amedhyāktasya mṛttoyair gandhāpaharaṇena ca ।। śuci māṃsaṃ tu cāṇḍāla- kravyādair vinipātitam ।। rajo agnir aśvagochāyā raśmayaḥ pavano mahī ।।
ajāśvaṃ mukhato medhyaṃ na gor vatsasya cānanam ।। āsanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ taṭau nadyās tṛṇāni ca ।। rathyāpasarpaṇe snāne kṣutpānānāṃ ca karmasu ।। spṛṣṭānām atha saṃsparśair dvirathyākardamāmbhasi ।।
prabhūtopahatād annād agram uddhṛtya saṃtyajet ।। upavāsas trirātraṃ tu duṣṭabhaktāśino bhavet ।। udakyāṃ vāvalagnāṃ ca sūtikāntyāvasāyinaḥ ।। nāraṃ spṛṣṭvāsthi sasnehaṃ snātvā vipro viśudhyati ।।
na laṅghayet tathaivātha ṣṭhīvanodvartanāni ca ।। pañcapiṇḍān anuddhṛtya na snāyāt paravāriṇi ।। nodyānādau vikāleṣu prājñas tiṣṭhet kadācana ।। devatāpitṛsacchāstra- yajvisaṃnyāsinindakaiḥ ।।
avalokya tathodakyāṃ saṃnyastaṃ patitaṃ śavam ।। mṛtaniryātakāṃś caiva paradāraratāś ca ye ।। abhojyabhikṣupākhaṇḍa- mārjārakharakukkuṭān ।। saṃspṛśya śudhyate snānād udakyāgrāmaśūkarau ।।
yasya cānudinaṃ hānir gṛhe nityasya karmaṇaḥ ।। nityasya karmaṇo hāniṃ na kurvīta kadācana ।। daśāhaṃ brāhmaṇas tiṣṭhed dānahomavivarjitaḥ ।। śūdraś ca māsam āsīta nijakarmavivarjitaḥ ।।
pretāya salilaṃ deyaṃ bahir gatvā tu gotrakaiḥ ।। tasyāsthisaṃcayaḥ kāryaś caturthe ahani gotrakaiḥ ।। gotrakais tu kriyāḥ sarvāḥ kāryāḥ saṃcayanāt param ।। anvartham icchayā śastra- rajjubandhanavahniṣu ।।
bāle deśāntarasthe ca tathā pravrajite mṛte ।। sapiṇḍānāṃ sapiṇḍas tu mṛte anyasmin mṛto yadi ।। eṣa eva vidhir dṛṣṭo janmany api hi sūtake ।। putre jāte pituḥ snānaṃ sacailasya vidhīyate ।।
tatrāpi śuddhir uditā pūrvajanmavato dinaiḥ ।। svāḥ svāḥ karmakriyāḥ kuryuḥ sarve varṇā yathāvidhi ।। dānāni caiva deyāni brāhmaṇebhyo manīṣibhiḥ ।। tat tad guṇavate deyaṃ tad evākṣayam icchatā ।।
dattapretodapiṇḍāś ca sarve varṇāḥ kṛtakriyāḥ ।। adhyetavyā trayī nityaṃ bhavitavyaṃ vipaścitā ।। yena prakupito nātmā jugupsām eti bho dvijāḥ ।। evam ācarato viprāḥ puruṣasya gṛhe sataḥ ।।
idaṃ rahasyam āyuṣyaṃ dhanyaṃ buddhivivardhanam ।। yaśaḥkīrtipradaṃ nṝṇāṃ tejobalavivardhanam ।। brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiś ca munisattamāḥ ।। jñātvaiva yaḥ sadā kālam anuṣṭhānaṃ karoti vai ।।
sārāt sārataraṃ cedam ākhyātaṃ dvijasattamāḥ ।। na dāmbhikāya mūrkhāya na kutarkapralāpine ।। caturāśramadharmāṃś ca dvijavarya bravīhi tān ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ saṃyatā bhūtvā varṇadharmān mayoditān ।।
nityodakī bhaved vipraḥ kuryāc cāgniparigraham ।। kuryāt pratigrahādānaṃ yajñārthaṃ jñānato dvijāḥ ।। maitrī samastasattveṣu brāhmaṇasyottamaṃ dhanam ।। ṛtāv abhigamaḥ patnyāṃ śasyate vāsya bho dvijāḥ ।।
yajec ca vividhair yajñair adhīyīta ca bho dvijāḥ ।। tasyāpi prathame kalpe pṛthivīparipālanam ।। bhavanti nṛpate rakṣā yato yajñādikarmaṇām ।। prāpnoty abhimatāṃl lokān varṇasaṃsthāpako nṛpaḥ ।।
vaiśyāya jīvikāṃ brahmā dadau lokapitāmahaḥ ।। nityanaimittikādīnām anuṣṭhānaṃ ca karmaṇām ।। krayavikrayajair vāpi dhanaiḥ kārubhavais tu vā ।। pitryādikaṃ ca vai sarvaṃ śūdraḥ kurvīta tena vai ।।
ṛtukālābhigamanaṃ svadāreṣu dvijottamāḥ ।। satyaṃ śaucam anāyāso maṅgalaṃ priyavāditā ।। anasūyā ca sāmānyā varṇānāṃ kathitā guṇāḥ ।। guṇās tathopadharmāś ca viprādīnām ime dvijāḥ ।।
rājanyasya ca vaiśyoktaṃ śūdrakarmāṇi caitayoḥ ।। tad evāpadi kartavyaṃ na kuryāt karmasaṃkaram ।। dharmam āśramiṇāṃ samyag bruvato api nibodhata ।। guror gehe vasan viprā brahmacārī samāhitaḥ ।।
vratāni caratā grāhyo vedaś ca kṛtabuddhinā ।। upatiṣṭhet tathā kuryād guror apy abhivādanam ।। śiṣyo gurau dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ pratikūlaṃ ca saṃtyajet ।। anujñātaṃ ca bhikṣānnam aśnīyād guruṇā tataḥ ।।
samijjalādikaṃ cāsya kalyakalyam upānayet ।। gārhasthyam āvaset prājño niṣpannaguruniṣkṛtiḥ ।। gṛhasthakāryam akhilaṃ kuryād viprāḥ svaśaktitaḥ ।। annair munīṃś ca svādhyāyair apatyena prajāpatim ।।
prāpnoti lokān puruṣo nijakarmasamārjitān ।। te apy atra pratitiṣṭhanti gārhasthyaṃ tena vai param ।। aṭanti vasudhāṃ viprāḥ pṛthivīdarśanāya ca ।। teṣāṃ gṛhasthaḥ satataṃ pratiṣṭhā yonir ucyate ।।
gṛhāgatānāṃ dadyāc ca śayanāsanabhojanam ।। sa dattvā duṣkṛtaṃ tasmai puṇyam ādāya gacchati ।। parivādopaghātau ca pāruṣyaṃ ca na śasyate ।। sarvabandhavinirmukto lokān āpnoti cottamān ।।
putreṣu bhāryāṃ nikṣipya vanaṃ gacchet sahaiva vā ।। bhūmiśāyī bhavet tatra muniḥ sarvātithir dvijāḥ ।। tadvat triṣavaṇaṃ snānaṃ śastam asya dvijottamāḥ ।। bhikṣā balipradānaṃ tu śastam asya praśasyate ।।
tapasyā tasya viprendrāḥ śītoṣṇādisahiṣṇutā ।। sa dahaty agnivad doṣāñ jayel lokāṃś ca śāśvatān ।। tasya svarūpaṃ gadato budhyadhvaṃ mama sattamāḥ ।। caturtham āśramasthānaṃ gacchen nirdhūtamatsaraḥ ।।
mitrādiṣu samo maitraḥ samasteṣv eva jantuṣu ।। yuktaḥ kurvīta na drohaṃ sarvasaṅgāṃś ca varjayet ।। tathā prītir na tiryakṣu dveṣo vā nāsya jāyate ।। kāle praśastavarṇānāṃ bhikṣārthī paryaṭed gṛhān ।।
prāṇayātrikamātraḥ syān mātrāsaṅgād vinirgataḥ ।। atipūjitalābhais tu yatir mukto api badhyate ।। tāṃs tu doṣān parityajya parivrāṇ nirmamo bhavet ।। tasya dehād vimuktasya bhayaṃ notpadyate kvacit ।।
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca na te asty aviditaṃ mune ।। uttamā ca bhavet kena brūhi teṣāṃ mahāmate ।। śrotum icchāmahe kena brāhmaṇaḥ śūdratām iyāt ।। nānādrumalatākīrṇe nānāścaryasamanvite ।।
śailarājasutā devī praṇipatya sureśvaram ।। tad ahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ mama sattamāḥ ।। dakṣakratuhara tryakṣa saṃśayo me mahān ayam ।। kena karmavipākena vaiśyo gacchati śūdratām ।।
pratilome kathaṃ deva śakyo dharmo nivartitum ।। kṣatriyaḥ śūdratām eti kena vā karmaṇā vibho ।। trayo varṇāḥ prakṛtyeha kathaṃ brāhmaṇyam āpnuyuḥ ।। kṣatriyo vaiśyaśūdrau vā nisargād iti me matiḥ ।।
śreṣṭhaṃ varṇam anuprāpya tasmād ākṣipyate punaḥ ।। kṣatriyo vātha vaiśyo vā brahmabhūyaṃ sa gacchati ।। brāhmaṇyāt sa paribhraṣṭaḥ kṣatrayonau prajāyate ।। brāhmaṇyaṃ durlabhaṃ prāpya karoty alpamatiḥ sadā ।।
svadharmāt pracyuto vipras tataḥ śūdratvam āpnuyāt ।। brahmalokāt paribhraṣṭaḥ śūdrayonau prajāyate ।। svāni karmāṇy apākṛtya śūdrakarma niṣevate ।। brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ śūdratvaṃ yāti tādṛśaḥ ।।
dharmajño dharmanirataḥ sa dharmaphalam aśnute ।। adhyātmaṃ naiṣṭhikī siddhir dharmakāmair niṣevyate ।। ghuṣṭānnaṃ naiva bhoktavyaṃ śūdrānnaṃ naiva vā kvacit ।। pitāmahamukhotsṛṣṭaṃ pramāṇam iti me matiḥ ।।
āhitāgnis tathā yajvā sa śūdragatibhāg bhavet ।। brāhmaṇaḥ śūdratām eti nāsti tatra vicāraṇā ।। tāṃ tāṃ yoniṃ vrajed vipro yasyānnam upajīvati ।। abhojyānnāni vāśnāti sa dvijatvāt pateta vai ।।
svādhyāyavarjitaḥ pāpo lubdho naikṛtikaḥ śaṭhaḥ ।। vihīnasevī vipro hi patate brahmayonitaḥ ।। brahmadviḍ vāpi patati brāhmaṇo brahmayonitaḥ ।। śūdro brāhmaṇatāṃ gacched vaiśyaḥ kṣatriyatāṃ vrajet ।।
sarvātithyam upātiṣṭhañ śeṣānnakṛtabhojanaḥ ।। kuryād avimanāḥ śreṣṭhaḥ satataṃ satpathe sthitaḥ ।। ṛtukālābhigāmī ca niyato niyatāśanaḥ ।। vṛthā māṃsaṃ na bhuñjīta śūdro vaiśyatvam ṛcchati ।।
yajate nityayajñaiś ca svādhyāyaparamaḥ śuciḥ ।। gṛhasthavratam ātiṣṭhan dvikālakṛtabhojanaḥ ।। agnihotram upāsīno juhvānaś ca yathāvidhi ।। tretāgnimātravihitaṃ vaiśyo bhavati ca dvijaḥ ।।
sa vaiśyaḥ kṣatriyo jāto janmaprabhṛti saṃskṛtaḥ ।। dadāti yajate yajñaiḥ samṛddhair āptadakṣiṇaiḥ ।। ārdrahastaprado nityaṃ prajā dharmeṇa pālayan ।। dharmadaṇḍena nirdagdho dharmakāmārthasādhakaḥ ।।
grāmyadharmān na seveta svacchandenārthakovidaḥ ।। sadopavāsī niyataḥ svādhyāyanirataḥ śuciḥ ।। sarvātithyaṃ trivargasya kurvāṇaḥ sumanāḥ sadā ।। svārthād vā yadi vā kāmān na kiṃcid upalakṣayet ।।
svaveśmani yathānyāyam upāste bhaikṣyam eva ca ।। gobrāhmaṇahitārthāya raṇe cābhimukho hataḥ ।। jñānavijñānasaṃpannaḥ saṃskṛto vedapāragaḥ ।। etaiḥ karmaphalair devi nyūnajātikulodbhavaḥ ।।
brāhmaṇo vāpy asadvṛttaḥ sarvasaṃkarabhojanaḥ ।। karmabhiḥ śucibhir devī śuddhātmā vijitendriyaḥ ।। svabhāvakarmaṇā caiva yatra śūdro adhitiṣṭhati ।। na yonir nāpi saṃskāro na śrutir na ca saṃtatiḥ ।।
sarvo ayaṃ brāhmaṇo loke vṛttena tu vidhīyate ।। brahmasvabhāvaḥ suśroṇi samaḥ sarvatra me mataḥ ।। ete ye vimalā devi sthānabhāvanidarśakāḥ ।। brahmaṇo hi mahat kṣetraṃ loke carati pādavat ।।
saṃtuṣṭena sadā bhāvyaṃ satpathālambinā sadā ।। saṃhitādhyāyinā bhāvyaṃ gṛhe vai gṛhamedhinā ।। evaṃbhūto hi yo vipraḥ satataṃ satpathe sthitaḥ ।। brāhmaṇyaṃ devi saṃprāpya rakṣitavyaṃ yatātmanā ।।
brāhmaṇo vā cyuto dharmād yathā śūdratvam āpnuyāt ।। dharmādharme nṛṇāṃ deva brūhi me saṃśayaṃ vibho ।। badhyante bandhanaiḥ kair vā mucyante vā kathaṃ vada ।। samācārair guṇaiḥ kair vā svargaṃ yāntīha mānavāḥ ।।
sarvaprāṇihitaḥ praśnaḥ śrūyatāṃ buddhivardhanaḥ ।। nādharmeṇa na dharmeṇa badhyante chinnasaṃśayāḥ ।। vītarāgā vimucyante puruṣāḥ karmabandhanaiḥ ।। ye na majjanti kasmiṃścit te na badhnanti karmabhiḥ ।।
tulyadveṣyapriyā dāntā mucyante karmabandhanaiḥ ।। tyaktahiṃsrasamācārās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। dharmalabdhārthabhoktāras te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। paradāreṣu vartante te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।
agrāmyasukhabhogāś ca te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। svabhāgyāny upajīvanti te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। jitendriyāḥ śīlaparās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। akaṣāyakṛtaś caiva mārgaḥ sevyaḥ sadā budhaiḥ ।।
svargamārgam abhīpsadbhir na sevyas tv ata uttaraḥ ।। tāni karmāṇi me deva vada bhūtapate anagha ।। ye mṛṣā na vadantīha te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। anṛtaṃ ye na bhāṣante te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।
svagatenābhibhāṣante te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। na paiśunyaratāḥ santas te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। parapīḍākaraṃ caiva te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। sarvabhūtasamā dāntās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।
saumyapralāpino nityaṃ te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। śāntiṃ vindanti ye kruddhās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। śubhasatyaguṇair nityaṃ varjanīyā mṛṣā budhaiḥ ।। tan me brūhi mahābhāga devadeva pinākadhṛk ।।
svargaṃ gacchanti kalyāṇi tan me kīrtayataḥ śṛṇu ।। naro badhyeta yeneha śṛṇu vā taṃ śubhānane ।। manasāpi na gṛhṇanti te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। manasāpi na hiṃsanti te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।
bhajanti maitryaṃ saṃgamya te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। svair arthaiḥ parisaṃtuṣṭās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। sarvabhūtadayāvantas te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। dharmādharmavido nityaṃ te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।।
nirākāṅkṣāś ca ye devi te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। samutthānam anuprāptās te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ ।। svargamārgaparā bhūyaḥ kiṃ tvaṃ śrotum ihecchasi ।। tasmāt tvaṃ nipuṇenādya mama vyākhyātum arhasi ।।
tapasā vāpi deveśa kenāyur labhate mahat ।। vipākaṃ karmaṇāṃ deva vaktum arhasy anindita ।। akulīnāḥ kulīnāś ca saṃbhavanti tathā pare ।। priyadarśās tathā cānye darśanād eva mānavāḥ ।।
mahāprajñās tathā cānye jñānavijñānabhāvinaḥ ।। dṛśyante puruṣā deva tato vyākhyātum arhasi ।। martyaloke naraḥ sarvo yena svaṃ phalam aśnute ।। nityam udyataśastraś ca hanti bhūtagaṇān naraḥ ।।
api kīṭapataṃgānām aśaraṇyaḥ sunirghṛṇaḥ ।। viparītas tu dharmātmā svarūpeṇābhijāyate ।। yātanāṃ niraye raudrāṃ sakṛcchrāṃ labhate naraḥ ।। mānuṣyaṃ labhate vāpi hīnāyus tatra jāyate ।।
ahitaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ hīnāyur upajāyate ।। nikṣiptaśastro nirdaṇḍo na hiṃsati kadācana ।। sarvabhūteṣu sasneho yathātmani tathā pare ।। upapannān sukhān bhogān sadāśnāti mudā yutaḥ ।।
prāṇihiṃsāvimokṣeṇa brahmaṇā samudīritaḥ ।। svargaṃ samabhipadyeta saṃpradānena kena vā ।। bhakṣabhojyānnapānānāṃ vāsasāṃ ca mahāmatiḥ ।। nityakādīni karmāṇi karoti prayataḥ śuciḥ ।।
sasyajātāni sarvāṇi sakṣetrāṇy atha yoṣitaḥ ।। evaṃbhūto naro devi devaloke abhijāyate ।। sahāpsarobhir mudito ramitvā nandanādiṣu ।। mahābhāgakule devi dhanadhānyasamācite ।।
mahākāryo mahābhogo dhanī bhavati mānavaḥ ।। brahmaṇā vai purā proktāḥ sarvasya priyadarśanāḥ ।। ye annāni na prayacchanti vidyamāne apy abuddhayaḥ ।। yācyamānā nivartante jihvālobhasamanvitāḥ ।।
na gāś ca nānnavikṛtiṃ prayacchanti kadācana ।। evaṃbhūtā narā devi nirayaṃ yānty abuddhayaḥ ।। dhanarikte kule janma labhante svalpabuddhayaḥ ।। nirāśāḥ sarvabhogebhyo jīvanty adharmajīvikāḥ ।।
anena karmaṇā devi bhavanty adhanino narāḥ ।। āsanārhasya ye pīṭhaṃ na yacchanty alpacetasaḥ ।। arghārhān na ca saṃskārair arcayanti yathāvidhi ।। śubhaṃ cābhimataṃ premṇā guruṃ nābhivadanti ye ।।
saṃmānyāṃś cāvamanyante vṛddhān paribhavanti ca ।। te ced yadi narās tasmān nirayād uttaranti ca ।। śvapākapulkasādīnāṃ kutsitānām acetasām ।। na dambhī na ca mānī yo devatātithipūjakaḥ ।।
sarvakarmapriyakaraḥ sarvabhūtapriyaḥ sadā ।। svāgatenaiva sarveṣāṃ bhūtānām avihiṃsakaḥ ।। mārgārhāya dadan mārgaṃ gurum abhyarcayan sadā ।। evaṃbhūto naro devi svargatiṃ pratipadyate ।।
tatrāsau vipulair bhogaiḥ sarvaratnasamāyutaḥ ।। saṃmataḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ ।। eṣa dharmo mayā prokto vidhātrā svayam īritaḥ ।। hastābhyāṃ yadi vā padbhyāṃ rajjvā daṇḍena vā punaḥ ।।
hiṃsārthaṃ niṣkṛtiprajñaḥ prodvejayati caiva hi ।। evaṃ śīlasamācāro nirayaṃ pratipadyate ।। bahvābādhāparikliṣṭe kule jayati so adhame ।। eṣa devi manuṣyeṣu boddhavyo jñātibandhuṣu ।।
maitrī dṛṣṭiḥ pitṛsamo nirvairo niyatendriyaḥ ।। hastapādaiś ca niyatair viśvāsyaḥ sarvajantuṣu ।। udvejayati bhūtāni śubhakarmā dayāparaḥ ।। tatrāsau bhavane divye mudā vasati devavat ।।
alpāyāso nirātaṅkaḥ sa jātaḥ sukham edhate ।। eṣa devi satāṃ mārgo bādhā yatra na vidyate ।। jñānavijñānasaṃpannāḥ prajñāvanto arthakovidāḥ ।। kena karmavipākena prajñāvān puruṣo bhavet ।।
evaṃ tvaṃ saṃśayaṃ chindhi sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ vara ।। narāḥ klībāś ca dṛśyante kāraṇaṃ brūhi tatra vai ।। paripṛcchanty aharahaḥ kuśalākuśalaṃ sadā ।। labhante svargatiṃ nityam iha loke yathāsukham ।।
śrutaṃ yajñānugaṃ yasya kalyāṇam upajāyate ।। tena duṣṭasvabhāvena jātyandhās te bhavanti hi ।। rogārtās te bhavantīha narā duṣkṛtakāriṇaḥ ।। puruṣeṣu suduṣprajñāḥ klībatvam upayānti te ।।
prakīrṇamaithunā ye ca klībā jāyanti vai narāḥ ।। śreyaḥ kurvann avāpnoti mānavo devasattama ।। dharmānveṣī guṇākāṅkṣī sa svargaṃ samupāśnute ।। medhāvī dhāraṇāyuktaḥ prājñas tatrāpi jāyate ।।
nṛṇāṃ hitārthāya sadā mayā caivam udāhṛtaḥ ।। brāhmaṇān vedaviduṣo necchanti parisarpitum ।। avratā bhraṣṭaniyamās tathānye rākṣasopamāḥ ।। kena karmavipākena bhavantīha vadasva me ।।
pramāṇenānuvartante dṛśyante ha dṛḍhavratāḥ ।। avratā naṣṭamaryādās te narā brahmarākṣasāḥ ।। nirhomā nirvaṣaṭkārās te bhavanti narādhamāḥ ।। kuśalākuśalo nṝṇāṃ vyākhyāto dharmasāgaraḥ ।।
hṛṣṭā babhūva suprītā vismitā ca tadā dvijāḥ ।। tīrthayātrāprasaṅgena gatās tasmin girau dvijāḥ ।। papracchuḥ saṃśayaṃ caiva lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। pṛcchāmas tvāṃ jagannātha saṃśayaṃ hṛdi saṃsthitam ।।
bhramanti suciraṃ kālaṃ puruṣāś cālpamedhasaḥ ।। brūhi tac chrotum icchāmaḥ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। nānyopāyaṃ prapaśyāmi vāsudevāt paraṃ dvijāḥ ।। vāṅmanaḥkarmabhiḥ samyak te yānti paramāṃ gatim ।।
yeṣāṃ na pravaṇaṃ cittaṃ vāsudeve jaganmaye ।। māhātmyaṃ vāsudevasya śrotum icchāma śaṃkara ।। kṛṣṇo jāmbūnadābhāso vyabhre sūrya ivoditaḥ ।। śrīvatsāṅko hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarvadaivatayūthapaḥ ।।
śiroruhebhyo jyotīṃṣi romabhyaś ca surāsurāḥ ।। pitāmahagṛhaṃ sākṣāt sarvadevagṛhaṃ ca saḥ ।। saṃhartā caiva bhūtānāṃ sthāvarasya carasya ca ।। sarvajñaḥ sarvasaṃsraṣṭā sarvagaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ ।।
sanātano mahābhāgo govinda iti viśrutaḥ ।। surakāryārtham utpanno mānuṣyaṃ vapur āsthitaḥ ।। bhuvane devakāryāṇi kartuṃ nāyakavarjitaḥ ।। etasya devanāthasya kāryasya ca parasya ca ।।
brahmā vasati nābhisthaḥ śarīre ahaṃ ca saṃsthitaḥ ।। sa devaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ śrīgarbhaḥ śrīsahoṣitaḥ ।। uttamena suśīlena śaucena ca damena ca ।। ārohaṇapramāṇena vīryeṇārjavasaṃpadā ।।
astraiḥ samuditaḥ sarvair divyair adbhutadarśanaiḥ ।। vācā mitrajanaślāghī jñātibandhujanapriyaḥ ।। bhayahartā bhayārtānāṃ mitrānandavivardhanaḥ ।। śrutavān atha saṃpannaḥ sarvabhūtanamaskṛtaḥ ।।
nītijño nītisaṃpanno brahmavādī jitendriyaḥ ।। prājāpatye śubhe mārge mānave dharmasaṃskṛte ।। aṃśo nāma manoḥ putro hy antardhāmā tataḥ param ।। prācīnabarhir bhavitā havirdhāmnaḥ suto dvijāḥ ।।
prācetasas tathā dakṣo bhaviteha prajāpatiḥ ।। manoś ca vaṃśaja ilā sudyumnaś ca bhaviṣyati ।। nahuṣo bhavitā tasmād yayātis tasya cātmajaḥ ।। kroṣṭuś caiva mahān putro vṛjinīvān bhaviṣyati ।।
uṣaṅgor bhavitā putraḥ śūraś citrarathas tathā ।। teṣāṃ vikhyātavīryāṇāṃ cāritraguṇaśālinām ।। sa śūraḥ kṣatriyaśreṣṭho mahāvīryo mahāyaśāḥ ।। vasudevam iti khyātaṃ putram ānakadundubhim ।।
dātā brāhmaṇasatkartā brahmabhūto dvijapriyaḥ ।। jarāsaṃdhaṃ tu rājānaṃ nirjitya girigahvare ।। pṛthivyām apratihato vīryeṇāpi bhaviṣyati ।। śūraḥ saṃhanano bhūto dvārakāyāṃ vasan prabhuḥ ।।
taṃ bhavantaḥ samāsādya brāhmaṇair arhaṇair varaiḥ ।। yo hi māṃ draṣṭum iccheta brahmāṇaṃ ca pitāmaham ।। dṛṣṭe tasminn ahaṃ dṛṣṭo na me atrāsti vicāraṇā ।। sa yasya puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ prītiyukto bhaviṣyati ।।
yas tu taṃ mānavo loke saṃśrayiṣyati keśavam ।। dharmāṇāṃ deśikaḥ sākṣād bhaviṣyati sa dharmavān ।। dharma eva sadā hi syād asminn abhyarcite vibhau ।। dharmārthaṃ puruṣavyāghra ṛṣikoṭīḥ sasarja ca ।।
sanatkumārapramukhās tiṣṭhanti tapasānvitāḥ ।। vandito hi sa vandeta mānito mānayīta ca ।। arcitaś cārcayen nityaṃ sa devo dvijasattamāḥ ।। ādidevasya mahataḥ sajjanācaritaṃ sadā ।।
abhayenānurūpeṇa prapadya tam anuvratāḥ ।। yatnavadbhir upasthāya draṣṭavyo devakīsutaḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvadeveśaṃ dṛṣṭāḥ syuḥ surasattamāḥ ।। ahaṃ caiva namasyāmi nityam eva jagatpatim ।।
samastā hi vayaṃ devās tasya dehe vasāmahe ।। halī bala iti khyāto bhaviṣyati dharādharaḥ ।। suparṇo yasya vīryeṇa kaśyapasyātmajo balī ।। sa ca śeṣo vicarate parayā vai mudā yutaḥ ।।
ya eṣa viṣṇuḥ so ananto bhagavān vasudhādharaḥ ।। tāv ubhau puruṣavyāghrau divyau divyaparākramau ।। tad bhavanto yaduśreṣṭhaṃ pūjayeyuḥ prayatnataḥ ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ dhanyaṃ saṃsāranāśanam ।।
kāṃ gatiṃ yānti manujā vāsudevārcane ratāḥ ।। athavā kiṃ muniśreṣṭha prāpnuvanty ubhayaṃ phalam ।। chettā nānyo asti loke asmiṃs tvadṛte munisattama ।। śṛṇudhvam ānupūrvyeṇa vaiṣṇavānāṃ sukhāvaham ।।
kiṃ punar ye sadā bhaktyā pūjayanty acyutaṃ dvijāḥ ।। labhante vaiṣṇavāḥ kāmān yān yān vāñchanti durlabhān ।। svecchayā muniśārdūlās tathā kṛṣṇān manorathān ।। gṛhṇāti puruṣo viprās tathā kṛṣṇān manorathān ।।
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ prāpnuvanti narāḥ phalam ।। prāpnuvanti narāḥ kāmān surāṇām api durlabhān ।। na teṣāṃ durlabhaṃ kiṃcid vidyate bhuvanatraye ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ devaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam ।।
saṃpūjya taṃ suravaraṃ prāpnuvanti parāṃ gatim ।। pravakṣyāmi samāsena gatiṃ teṣāṃ mahātmanām ।। jarāmaraṇasaṃyuktaṃ jalabudbudasaṃnibham ।। asthisthūṇam amedhyaṃ ca snāyucarmaśirānvitam ।।
taruṇādityavarṇena kiṅkiṇījālamālinā ।। vrajanti lokapālānāṃ bhavanaṃ tu pṛthak pṛthak ।। bhuvanāni pṛthak teṣāṃ sarvabhogair alaṃkṛtāḥ ।। tatra bhuktvā varān bhogān daśamanvantaraṃ dvijāḥ ।।
viṃśanmanvantaraṃ kālaṃ tatra bhuktvā manoramān ।। triṃśanmanvantaraṃ tatra bhogān bhuktvātidaivatān ।। manvantarāṇāṃ te tatra catvāriṃśad guṇānvitam ।। tasmān nakṣatralokaṃ tu vimānaiḥ samalaṃkṛtam ।।
manvantarāṇāṃ pañcāśad bhuktvā bhogān yathepsitān ।। ṣaṣṭimanvantaraṃ yāvat tatra bhuktvā sudurlabhān ।। śakralokaṃ punas tasmād gacchanti surapūjitāḥ ।। bhogān uccāvacān divyān manasaḥ prītivardhanān ।।
bhuktvā tatrepsitān bhogān sarvakāmaguṇānvitān ।। tasmāt paitāmahaṃ lokaṃ yānti te vaiṣṇavā dvijāḥ ।। ihāgatya punas tasmād viprāṇāṃ pravare kule ।। evaṃ sarveṣu lokeṣu bhuktvā bhogān yathepsitān ।।
saṃbhave saṃbhave te tu śatavarṣaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। daśajanma yadā teṣāṃ krameṇaivaṃ prapūryate ।। gatvā tatrākṣayān bhogān bhuktvā sarvaguṇānvitān ।। gacchanti bhuvanaṃ paścād vārāhasya dvijottamāḥ ।।
krīḍanti tatra viprendrāḥ kṛtvā rūpaṃ caturbhujam ।। tiṣṭhanti śāśvate bhāve sarvair devair namaskṛtāḥ ।। krīḍante tatra muditā varṣakoṭyayutāni ca ।। krīḍante tatra saukhyena varṣāṇām ayutāni ca ।।
tatra sthitvā ciraṃ kālaṃ varṣakoṭiśatān bahūn ।। bhuktvā bhogāṃś ca vividhān varṣakoṭyarbudāni ca ।। gacchanti sādhakavarāḥ stūyamānāḥ surāsuraiḥ ।। tiṣṭhanti vaiṣṇavās tatra jarāmaraṇavarjitāḥ ।।
tatra tiṣṭhanti te viprā lakṣakoṭiśatatrayam ।। gacchanti yoginaḥ paścād yatra saṃkarṣaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। viśanti vāsudevaiti virūpākhye nirañjane ।। tatra gatvā vimuktās te bhaveyur nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
muktiṃ ca muniśārdūlā vāsudevārcane ratāḥ ।। snātvā samyag vidhānena dhautavāsā jitendriyaḥ ।। puṣpair gandhais tathā dīpair dhūpair naivedyakais tathā ।। stotrair nānāvidhair divyair gītavādyair manoharaiḥ ।।
evaṃ saṃpūjya vidhivad rātrau kṛtvā prajāgaram ।। yāti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ sthānaṃ naro nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ ।। brūhi tac chrotum icchāmaḥ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। gītikāyāḥ phalaṃ viṣṇor jāgare yad udāhṛtam ।।
tatrāste bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।। sadvṛttyotpāditadhano bhṛtyānāṃ bharaṇe rataḥ ।। ekādaśyāṃ samāgamya sopavāso atha gāyati ।। gāndhāraṣaḍjanaiṣāda- svarapañcamadhaivataiḥ ।।
prabhāte ca praṇamyeśaṃ dvādaśyāṃ gṛham etya ca ।। tataḥ saparivāras tu paścād bhuṅkte dvijottamāḥ ।। gītikābhir vicitrābhir vayaḥ pratigataṃ bahu ।। viṣṇuśuśrūṣaṇārthāya yayau vanam anuttamam ।।
kṣiprātaṭe mahāraṇye vibhītakataror adhaḥ ।। cāṇḍālas tam athovāca nādya bhakṣyas tvayā hy aham ।। adya kāryaṃ mama mahat tasmān muñcasva rākṣasa ।। kāryaṃ na vratavighnaṃ me kartum arhasi rākṣasa ।।
mamābhūd adya ca bhavān mayā labdho mataṅgaja ।। sāntvayañ ślakṣṇayā vācā sa satyavacanair dṛḍhaiḥ ।। satyenāhaṃ śapiṣyāmi punarāgamanāya ca ।। ahorātraṃ yamaḥ saṃdhye dve vidur naraceṣṭitam ।।
yac ca brahmahanaḥ pāpaṃ surāpe gurutalpage ।। yac ca devalake pāpaṃ matsyamāṃsāśinaś ca yat ।। vṛthā māṃsāśino yac ca pṛṣṭhamāṃsāśinaś ca yat ।। sūtakasya ca yat pāpaṃ yat pāpaṃ krūrakarmaṇaḥ ।।
amāvāsyāṣṭamī ṣaṣṭhī kṛṣṇaśuklacaturdaśī ।। rajasvalāṃ tathā paścāc chrāddhaṃ kṛtvā striyaṃ vrajet ।। mitrabhāryāṃ gacchatāṃ ca yat pāpaṃ piśunasya ca ।। brāhmaṇasya pratiśrutya yat pāpaṃ tadayacchataḥ ।।
strībālahantur yat pāpaṃ yac ca mithyābhibhāṣiṇaḥ ।। yac ca nindayatāṃ pāpaṃ gurumithyāpacārataḥ ।। gṛheṣṭyā pātake yac ca yad goghne yad dvijādhame ।। tayor dātṛgrahītroś ca yat pāpaṃ bhrūṇaghātinaḥ ।।
śrūyatāṃ śapathaṃ bhīmaṃ durvācyam api kathyate ।। ayājyayājake ṣaṇḍhe yat pāpaṃ śravaṇe adhame ।। etais tu pāpair lipye ahaṃ yadi naiṣyāmi te antikam ।। prāha gacchasva satyena samayaṃ caiva pālaya ।।
samādāyāgamac caiva viṣṇoḥ sa nilayaṃ gataḥ ।। viṣṇum abhyarcya nilayaṃ jagāma sa tapodhanāḥ ।। gāyan hi bāhyabhūmiṣṭhaḥ prajāgaram upākarot ।। satyaṃ sa samayaṃ kartuṃ pratasthe yatra rākṣasaḥ ।।
sa tathākathayat sarvaṃ so apy enaṃ punar abravīt ।। mahatā tu prayatnena śarīraṃ pālayed budhaḥ ।। mātaṅgas tad vacaḥ śrutvā pratyuvācātha hetumat ।। bhadra satyaṃ puraskṛtya gacchāmi śapathāḥ kṛtāḥ ।।
kiṃ na śrutaṃ tvayā sādho manunā yad udīritam ।। evaṃ tad vākyam ākarṇya mātaṅgaḥ pratyuvāca ha ।। satyenāvāpyate saukhyaṃ yat kiṃcij jagatīgatam ।। jvalaty agniś ca satyena vāti satyena mārutaḥ ।।
satyena jāyate puṃsāṃ tasmāt satyaṃ na saṃtyajet ।। satyaṃ svargasamāyātaṃ tasmāt satyaṃ na saṃtyajet ।। jagāma tatra yatrāste prāṇihā brahmarākṣasaḥ ।। vismayotphullanayanaḥ śiraḥkampaṃ tam abravīt ।।
na mātaṅgam ahaṃ manye bhavantaṃ satyalakṣaṇam ।। kiṃ tatra bhavatā rātrau kṛtaṃ viṣṇugṛhe vada ।। yat kṛtaṃ rajanībhāge yathātathyaṃ vadāmi te ।। prajāgaraḥ kṛto rātrau gāyatā viṣṇugītikām ।।
prajāgaro viṣṇugṛhe kṛtaṃ bhaktimatā vada ।। mātaṅgavacanaṃ śrutvā provāca brahmarākṣasaḥ ।। ekarātrikṛtaṃ sādho mama dehi prajāgaram ।। triḥ satyena mahābhāga ity uktvā virarāma ha ।।
niveditaḥ kim uktena khādasva svecchayāpi mām ।। sagītaṃ me prayacchasva kṛpāṃ kartuṃ tvam arhasi ।। mātaṅgavacanaṃ śrutvā prāha taṃ brahmarākṣasaḥ ।। dharṣayituṃ pīḍayituṃ rakṣitaṃ dharmakarmaṇā ।।
narakārtasya mūḍhasya sādhavaḥ syur dayānvitāḥ ।। yāmasyaikasya me dehi gaccha vā nilayaṃ svakam ।। taṃ prahasyātha cāṇḍālaṃ provāca brahmarākṣasaḥ ।। tasyāḥ phalaṃ prayacchasva trāhi pāpāt samuddhara ।।
evam uccārite tena mātaṅgas tam uvāca ha ।। yena tvaṃ doṣajātena saṃbhūto brahmarākṣasaḥ ।। provāca duḥkhasaṃtaptaḥ saṃsmṛtya svakṛtaṃ kṛtam ।। yasmin kṛte pāpayoniṃ gatavān asmi rākṣasīm ।।
putro adhyayanaśīlasya devaśarmasya yajvanaḥ ।। nṛpasya karmasaktena yūpakarmasuniṣṭhitaḥ ।। tasmin parisamāpte tu maurkhyād dambham anuṣṭhitaḥ ।। pravartamāne tasmiṃs tu kukṣiśūlo abhavan mama ।।
virūpākṣasya dīyantyām āhutyāṃ rākṣase kṣaṇe ।। mūrkheṇa mantrahīnena sūtrasvaravivarjitam ।। tena karmavipākena saṃbhūto brahmarākṣasaḥ ।। prajāgare gītikaikāṃ paścimāṃ dātum arhasi ।।
nivṛttiṃ kurute dadyāṃ tataḥ paścimagītikām ।। gītikāphalam āmantrya muhūrtārdhaprajāgaram ।। praṇamya prayayau hṛṣṭas tīrthavaryaṃ pṛthūdakam ।। rākṣasatvād vinirmukto gītikāphalabṛṃhitaḥ ।।
daśa varṣasahasrāṇi nirātaṅko avasat tataḥ ।। tasyāhaṃ caritaṃ bhūyaḥ kathayiṣyāmi bho dvijāḥ ।। rākṣase tu gate dhīmān gṛham etya yatātmavān ।। putreṣu bhāryāṃ nikṣipya dadau bhūmyāḥ pradakṣiṇām ।।
dṛṣṭvā skandaṃ yayau dhārā- cakre cāpi pradakṣiṇam ।। pāpapramocanaṃ tīrtham āsasāda sa tu dvijāḥ ।। vimuktapāpaḥ sasmāra pūrvajātīr anekaśaḥ ।। yatakāyaś ca matimān vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।।
bhikṣāvadhūtā rajasā muktā tenātha bhikṣuṇā ।। pāpapramocane snātaḥ sa mṛto narmadātaṭe ।। tatrāsya vasato abdais tu triṃśadbhiḥ siddhapūruṣaḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā sopahāsārtham abhivādyābhyuvāca ha ।।
kuśalaṃ siddhapuruṣaṃ kutas tv āgamyate tvayā ।। pratyuvācātha vandyas taṃ svargalokād upāgataḥ ।। nārāyaṇoruprabhavām urvaśīm apsarovarām ।। svargasyābharaṇaṃ mukhyam urvaśīṃ sādhusaṃbhavām ।।
tan mitra matkṛte vārttām urvaśyā bhavatādarāt ।। bāḍham ity abravīt siddhaḥ so api vipro mudānvitaḥ ।। sametya corvaśīṃ prāha yad ukto asau dvijena tu ।। jānāmi satyam uktaṃ te na cetasi mama sthitam ।।
vārāṇasīṃ yayau siddho dṛṣṭo mūrkheṇa vai punaḥ ।। siddho abravīn na jānāmi mām uvācorvaśī svayam ।। punaḥ prāha kathaṃ vetsīty evaṃ vācyā tvayorvaśī ।। dadarśa śakrabhavanān niṣkrāmantīm athorvaśīm ।।
niyamaṃ kaṃcid api hi karotu dvijasattamaḥ ।। tad urvaśīvaco abhyetya tasmai mūrkhadvijāya tu ।। tavāgre siddhapuruṣa niyamo ayaṃ kṛto mayā ।। ity uktaḥ prayayau siddhaḥ svarge dṛṣṭvorvaśīm atha ।।
taṃ siddham urvaśī prāha jñāto asau sāṃprataṃ mayā ।। ity uktvā prayayau śīghraṃ vāsaṃ nārāyaṇātmajā ।। urvaśy api varārohā gatvā vārāṇasīṃ purīm ।। athāsāv api mūrkhas tu nadīṃ matsyodarīṃ mune ।।
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā vavṛdhe athāsya manmathaḥ kṣobhakṛd dṛḍham ।। taṃ mūrkhaṃ siddhagaditaṃ jñātvā sasmitam āha tam ।। kariṣyāmi vacas tubhyaṃ tvaṃ viśrabdhaṃ kariṣyasi ।। ātmapradānena mama prāṇān rakṣa śucismite ।।
tvaṃ tiṣṭhasva kṣaṇam atha pratīkṣasvāgataṃ mama ।। māsamātreṇa sāyātā dadarśa taṃ kṛśaṃ dvijam ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā niścayayutaṃ bhūtvā vṛddhavapus tataḥ ।। ghṛtena madhunā caiva nadīṃ matsyodarīṃ gatā ।।
taṃ brāhmaṇaṃ samāhūya vākyam āha sulocanā ।। vratānte niṣkṛtiṃ dadyāṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva bho dvija ।। kṣutkṣāmakaṇṭhaḥ pṛcchāmi sādhu bhadre samīraya ।। imaṃ tvaṃ samupādāya prāṇaṃ tarpaya mā ciram ।।
prāha bhadre na gṛhṇāmi niyamo hi kṛto mayā ।। parijñānārtham urvaśyā dadasvānyasya kasyacit ।। nāsau kāṣṭhamayo bhuṅkṣva kṣudhayā cātipīḍitaḥ ।। kṛtaṃ bhadre atha niyamaḥ sāmānyenaiva me kṛtaḥ ।।
gṛhaṃ gṛhītvā gacchasva kuṭumbaṃ tava bhokṣyati ।। ihāyātā varārohā trailokye apy adhikā guṇaiḥ ।। sthīyatāṃ kṣaṇam ity evaṃ sthāsyāmīti mayoditam ।। mama satyānuraktasya saṃgamāya dhṛtavrate ।।
vihasya bhāvagambhīram urvaśī prāha taṃ dvijam ।। niṣpāditaṃ haṭhād eva mama darśanam icchatā ।। parīkṣito niścitavān bhavān satyatapā ṛṣiḥ ।। siddhiṃ yāsyasi viprendra tatas tvaṃ mām avāpsyasi ।।
sa ca satyatapā vipro rūpatīrthaṃ jagāma ha ।। dehotsarge jagāmāsau gāndharvaṃ lokam uttamam ।। babhūva sukule rājā prajārañjanatatparaḥ ।। putreṣu rājyaṃ nikṣipya yayau śaukaravaṃ punaḥ ।।
tatra manvantaraśataṃ bhogān bhuktvā tataś cyutaḥ ।। babhūva tatra corvaśyāḥ saṃgamāya tapodhanāḥ ।। kṛṣṇasya yena cāṇḍālo gato asau paramāṃ gatim ।। tapasā karmaṇā yena śrotum icchāma sāṃpratam ।।
yathā kṛṣṇe bhaved bhaktiḥ puruṣasya mahāphalā ।। mahāmohakare nṝṇāṃ nānāduḥkhaśatākule ।। kathaṃcil labhate janma dehī mānuṣyakaṃ dvijāḥ ।। vivekād dharmabuddhis tu buddhyā tu śreyasāṃ grahaḥ ।।
tāvan na jāyate bhaktir vāsudeve jaganmaye ।। anyadeveṣu yā bhaktiḥ puruṣasyeha jāyate ।। tena tasya bhaved bhaktir yajane munisattamāḥ ।। tuṣṭe hutāśane tasya bhaktir bhavati bhāskare ।।
prasanne bhāskare tasya bhaktir bhavati śaṃkare ।। tuṣṭe trilocane tasya bhaktir bhavati keśave ।। tato bhuktiṃ ca muktiṃ ca sa prāpnoti dvijottamāḥ ।। kiṃ te viṣṇuṃ nārcayanti brūhi tatkāraṇaṃ dvija ।।
āsuraś ca tathā daivaḥ purā sṛṣṭaḥ svayaṃbhuvā ।। āsurīṃ yonim āpannā dūṣayanti narā harim ।। aprāpya taṃ hariṃ viprās tato yānty adhamāṃ gatim ।। mahāmohakarī nṝṇāṃ dustarā cākṛtātmabhiḥ ।।
vaktum arhasi dharmajña paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। kaḥ śaknoti harer māyāṃ jñātuṃ tāṃ keśavād ṛte ।। viḍambanāṃ tu tāṃ viprāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ gadato mama ।। nagare kāmadamanas tasyātha tanayaḥ śuciḥ ।।
prajānurañjako dakṣaḥ śrutiśāstrakṛtaśramaḥ ।। taṃ pitā prāha kim iti necchase dārasaṃgraham ।। sukhamūlā hi dārāś ca tasmāt taṃ tvaṃ samācara ।। muhur muhus taṃ ca pitā codayām āsa bho dvijāḥ ।।
mayā samāśritā vyaktā vaiṣṇavī paripālinī ।। na vidhārayitavyā syāt puruṣeṇa vipaścitā ।। mā nimajja kulaṃ mahyaṃ narake saṃtatikṣayāt ।। prītaḥ saṃsmṛtya paurāṇīṃ saṃsārasya vicitratām ।।
nāmānurūpaṃ kartavyaṃ satyaṃ bhavati pārthiva ।। prāptāni dārasaṃyoga- viyogāni ca sarvaśaḥ ।। paśustrīpuruṣādyāni prāptāni śataśo mayā ।। yakṣaguhyakarakṣāṃsi dānavāpsarasaḥ surāḥ ।।
sṛṣṭas tu bahuśaḥ sṛṣṭau saṃhāre cāpi saṃhṛtaḥ ।। kathayāmi samāsena tīrthamāhātmyasaṃbhavam ।। prādurbhāvāśritaṃ puṇyaṃ māyā viṣṇoś ca durvidā ।। mahāpralayasaṃjñāṃ ca kalpānte ca mahāmune ।।
kalpānte prākṛte caiva pralaye jāyate yathā ।। caturyugasahasre tu brahmaṇo ahar dvijottamāḥ ।। daivair varṣasahasrais tu tad dvādaśābhir ucyate ।। ādyaṃ kṛtayugaṃ proktaṃ munayo antyaṃ tathā kalim ।।
kriyate copasaṃhāras tathānte api kalau yuge ।। dharmaś catuṣpād bhagavān yasmin vaikalyam ṛcchati ।। nibodhadhvaṃ samāsena vartate yan mahattaram ।। na sāma-ṛgyajurveda- viniṣpādanahaitukī ।।
na putrā dhārmikāś caiva na ca vahnikriyākramaḥ ।। sarvebhya eva varṇebhyo naraḥ kanyopajīvanaḥ ।। yaiva saiva ca viprendrāḥ prāyaścittakriyā kalau ।। devatāś ca kalau sarvāḥ sarvaḥ sarvasya cāśramaḥ ।।
dharmo yathābhirucitair anuṣṭhānair anuṣṭhitaḥ ।। strīṇāṃ rūpamadaś caiva keśair eva bhaviṣyati ।। kalau striyo bhaviṣyanti tadā keśair alaṃkṛtāḥ ।। bhartā bhaviṣyati kalau vittavān eva yoṣitām ।।
svāmitvahetusaṃbandho bhavitābhijanas tadā ।। arthāś cāthopabhogāntā bhaviṣyanti tadā kalau ।। anyāyāvāptavitteṣu puruṣeṣu spṛhālavaḥ ।। paṇasyārdhārdhamātre api kariṣyati tadā dvijāḥ ।।
kṣīrapradānasaṃbandhi bhāti goṣu ca gauravam ।। bhaviṣyanti tadā sarvā gaganāsaktadṛṣṭayaḥ ।। ātmānaṃ ghātayiṣyanti tadāvṛṣṭyābhiduḥkhitāḥ ।। prāpsyanti vyāhatasukhaṃ pramādān mānavāḥ kalau ।।
kariṣyanti kalau prāpte na ca piṇḍodakakriyām ।। bahuprajālpabhāgyāś ca bhaviṣyanti kalau striyaḥ ।। kurvatyo gurubhartṝṇām ājñāṃ bhetsyanty anāvṛtāḥ ।। paruṣānṛtabhāṣiṇyo bhaviṣyanti kalau striyaḥ ।।
asadvṛttā bhaviṣyanti puruṣeṣu kulāṅganāḥ ।। gṛhasthāś ca na hoṣyanti na dāsyanty ucitāny api ।। bhikṣavaś cāpi putrā hi snehasaṃbandhayantrakāḥ ।। hāriṇo janavittānāṃ saṃprāpte ca kalau yuge ।।
yaś ca yaś cābalaḥ sarvaḥ sa sa bhṛtyaḥ kalau yuge ।। śūdravṛttyā bhaviṣyanti kārukarmopajīvinaḥ ।। pākhaṇḍasaṃśrayāṃ vṛttim āśrayiṣyanty asaṃskṛtāḥ ।। godhūmānnayavānnādyān deśān yāsyanti duḥkhitāḥ ।।
adharmavṛddhyā lokānām alpam āyur bhaviṣyati ।। nareṣu nṛpadoṣeṇa bālamṛtyur bhaviṣyati ।। navāṣṭadaśavarṣāṇāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tathā kalau ।। na jīviṣyati vai kaścit kalau varṣāṇi viṃśatim ।।
yatas tato vinaśyanti kālenālpena mānavāḥ ।। tadā tadā kaler vṛddhir anumeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। tadā tadā kaler vṛddhir anumeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। tadānumeyaṃ prādhānyaṃ kaler viprā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।।
ijyate puruṣair yajñais tadā jñeyaṃ kaler balam ।। kaler vṛddhis tadā prājñair anumeyā dvijottamāḥ ।। nārcayiṣyanti bho viprāḥ pākhaṇḍopahatā narāḥ ।। ity evaṃ pralapiṣyanti pākhaṇḍopahatā narāḥ ।।
phalaṃ tathālpasāraṃ ca viprāḥ prāpte kalau yuge ।। śūdraprāyās tathā varṇā bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।। bhaviṣyati kalau prāpta auśīraṃ cānulepanam ।। śālādyāhāribhāryāś ca suhṛdo munisattamāḥ ।।
iti codāhariṣyanti śvaśurānugatā narāḥ ।। narāḥ pāpāny anudinaṃ kariṣyanty alpamedhasaḥ ।। yad yad duḥkhāya tat sarvaṃ kalikāle bhaviṣyati ।। tadā praviralo vipraḥ kaścil loke bhaviṣyati ।।
karoti yaḥ kṛtayuge kriyate tapasā hi yaḥ ।। vaktum arhasy aśeṣeṇa śrotuṃ vāñchā pravartate ।। tathā bhavetāṃ strīśūdrau dhanyau cānyan nibodhata ।। dvāpare tac ca māsena ahorātreṇa tat kalau ।।
prāpnoti puruṣas tena kalau sādhv iti bhāṣitum ।। yad āpnoti tad āpnoti kalau saṃkīrtya keśavam ।। svalpāyāsena dharmajñās tena tuṣṭo asmy ahaṃ kalau ।। tatas tu dharmasaṃprāptair yaṣṭavyaṃ vidhivad dhanaiḥ ।।
patanāya tathā bhāvyaṃ tais tu saṃyatibhiḥ saha ।। bhojyapeyādikaṃ caiṣāṃ necchāprāptikaraṃ dvijāḥ ।। lokān kleśena mahatā yajanti vinayānvitāḥ ।। nijaṃ jayati vai lokaṃ śūdro dhanyataras tataḥ ।।
niyamo muniśārdūlās tenāsau sādhv itīritam ।। pratipādanīyaṃ pātreṣu yaṣṭavyaṃ ca yathāvidhi ।। tathā sadviniyogāya vijñeyaṃ gahanaṃ nṛṇām ।। nijāñ jayanti vai lokān prājāpatyādikān kramāt ।।
etad viṣayam āpnoti tatsālokyaṃ yato dvijāḥ ।। tṛtīyaṃ vyāhṛtaṃ tena mayā sādhv iti yoṣitaḥ ।। tat pṛcchadhvaṃ yathākāmam ahaṃ vakṣyāmi vaḥ sphuṭam ।। narair ātmaguṇāmbhobhiḥ kṣālitākhilakilbiṣaiḥ ।।
tathā strībhir anāyāsāt patiśuśrūṣayaiva hi ।। dharmasaṃrādhane kleśo dvijātīnāṃ kṛtādiṣu ।। dhanyā dharmaṃ cariṣyanti yugānte munisattamāḥ ।। apṛṣṭenāpi dharmajñāḥ kim anyat kriyatāṃ dvijāḥ ।।
tato dvāparavidhvaṃsaṃ yugāntaṃ spṛhayāmahe ।। ādadyāma paraṃ dharmaṃ sukham alpena karmaṇā ।। pranaṣṭadharmaṃ dharmajña nimittair vaktum arhasi ।। yugānte prabhaviṣyanti svarakṣaṇaparāyaṇāḥ ।।
śūdrāś ca brāhmaṇācārā bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।। ekapaṅktyām aśiṣyanti yugānte munisattamāḥ ।। mitrabhāryāṃ bhajiṣyanti yugānte puruṣādhamāḥ ।। bhṛtyā hy anirdiṣṭabhujo bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।।
akutsanā ca patite bhaviṣyati yugakṣaye ।। ūnaṣoḍaśavarṣāś ca prasoṣyanti tathā striyaḥ ।। pramadāḥ keśaśūlāś ca bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।। śūdrābhā vādinaś caiva brāhmaṇāś cāntyavāsinaḥ ।।
śūdrā dharmaṃ vadiṣyanti śāṭhyabuddhyopajīvinaḥ ।। sādhūnāṃ parivṛttiś ca vidyād antagate yuge ।। nirhrīkāś ca prajāḥ sarvā naṣṭās tatra yugakṣaye ।। ṛtavo viparītāś ca bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।।
citravarṣī ca parjanyo yuge kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati ।। yathā nimnāḥ prajāḥ sarvā bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।। na ca dharmaṃ cariṣyanti mānavā nirgate yuge ।। sarve vāṇikāś caiva bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।।
haraṇe yatnavanto api lobhādibhir virodhinaḥ ।। bhaviṣyanti yugasyānte nāryaḥ keśair alaṃkṛtāḥ ।। yugānte samanuprāpte nānyā bhāryāsamā ratiḥ ।। puruṣālpaṃ bahustrīkaṃ tad yugāntasya lakṣaṇam ।।
rājacaurāgnidaṇḍādi- kṣīṇaḥ kṣayam upaiṣyati ।। aśīlāḥ sukhino loke bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।। saṃdigdhaḥ paralokaś ca bhaviṣyati yugakṣaye ।। yugāpakramaṇe pūrvaṃ bhaviṣyanti na bāndhavāḥ ।।
ṛṇaṃ savinayabhraṃśaṃ yuge kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati ।। ajāś cāpi nirotsyanti payaso arthe yugakṣaye ।। apramāṇaṃ kariṣyanti narāḥ paṇḍitamāninaḥ ।। sarvaḥ sarvaṃ vijānāti vṛddhān anupasevya vai ।।
nakṣatrāṇi viyogāni na karmasthā dvijātayaḥ ।। kuṇḍīvṛṣā naikṛtikāḥ surāpā brahmavādinaḥ ।। yājayiṣyanty ayājyāṃs tu tathābhakṣyasya bhakṣiṇaḥ ।। bhoḥśabdam abhidhāsyanti na ca kaścit paṭhiṣyati ।।
nakṣatrāṇi vivarṇāni viparitā diśo daśa ।। preṣayanti pitṝn putrā vadhūḥ śvaśrūḥ svakarmasu ।। akṛtvāgrāṇi bhokṣyanti dvijāś caivāhutāgnayaḥ ।। vañcayitvā patīn suptān gamiṣyanti striyo anyataḥ ।।
kṛte na pratikartā ca yuge kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati ।। kutra deśe nivatsyanti kimāhāravihāriṇaḥ ।। kāṃ ca kāṣṭhāṃ samāsādya prapatsyanti kṛtaṃ yugam ।। śīlavyasanam āsādya prāpsyanti hrāsam āyuṣaḥ ।।
vaivarṇyād vyādhisaṃpīḍā nirvedo vyādhipīḍanāt ।। evaṃ gatvā parāṃ kāṣṭhāṃ prapatsyanti kṛtaṃ yugam ।। kiṃdharmaśīlāḥ kecit tu kecid atra kutūhalāḥ ।। apramāṇaṃ kariṣyanti sarvam ity apare janāḥ ।।
bhaviṣyanti narā mūḍhā dvijāḥ paṇḍitamāninaḥ ।। dāmbhikās te bhaviṣyanti narā jñānavilopitāḥ ।। śubhān samācariṣyanti dānaśīlaparāyaṇāḥ ।। bhaviṣyanti tadā loke tat kaṣāyasya lakṣaṇam ।।
siddhim alpena kālena prāpsyanti nirupaskṛtāḥ ।। saṃśrayiṣyanti bho viprās tat kaṣāyasya lakṣaṇam ।। bhaviṣyati yuge kṣīṇe tat kaṣāyasya lakṣaṇam ।। pṛthivīm upabhokṣyanti yugānte samupasthite ।।
kravyādā brahmarūpeṇa sarvabhakṣyā vṛthāvratāḥ ।। vyavahāropavṛttāś ca cyutā dharmāś ca śāśvatāt ।। kāmātmāno durātmānaḥ sopadhāḥ priyasāhasāḥ ।। abhāvino bhaviṣyanti munayo bahurūpiṇaḥ ।।
kathāyogena tān sarvān pūjayiṣyanti mānavāḥ ।। bhokṣyabhojyaharāś caiva karaṇḍānāṃ ca hāriṇaḥ ।। cauraiś caurakṣaye cāpi kṛte kṣemaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। narā vanaṃ śrayiṣyanti karabhāraprapīḍitāḥ ।।
kīṭamūṣikasarpāś ca dharṣayiṣyanti mānavān ।। uddeśeṣu narāḥ śreṣṭhā bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।। maṇḍalaiḥ saṃbhaviṣyanti deśe deśe pṛthak pṛthak ।। narāḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti tadā kālaparikṣayāt ।।
kauśikīṃ saṃtariṣyanti narāḥ kṣudbhayapīḍitāḥ ।। ṛṣikāntagiridroṇīḥ saṃśrayiṣyanti mānavāḥ ।। vividhaṃ jīrṇapattraṃ ca valkalāny ajināni ca ।। araṇyeṣu ca vatsyanti narā mlecchagaṇaiḥ saha ।।
agoptāraś ca goptāro bhaviṣyanti narādhipāḥ ।। madhuśākaphalair mūlair vartayiṣyanti mānavāḥ ।। svayaṃ kṛtvā nivatsyanti yathā munijanas tathā ।। ajaiḍakaṃ kharoṣṭraṃ ca pālayiṣyanti nityaśaḥ ।।
pakvānnavyavahāreṇa vipaṇantaḥ parasparam ।। bahvapatyāḥ prajāhīnāḥ kulaśīlavivarjitāḥ ।। hīnā hīnaṃ tathā dharmaṃ prajā samanuvatsyati ।। durbalā viṣayaglānā jarāśokair abhiplutāḥ ।।
āyuḥpratyayasaṃrodhād viṣayād uparaṃsyate ।। satyaṃ ca pratipatsyanti vyavahāropasaṃkṣayāt ।। kariṣyanti ca saṃskāraṃ svayaṃ ca kṣayapīḍitāḥ ।। tataḥ pādapravṛtte tu dharme śreyo nipatsyate ।।
svādu kiṃ tv iti vijñāya dharma eva ca dṛśyate ।। pragṛhīte tato dharme prapaśyanti kṛtaṃ yugam ।। eka eva tu kālo ayaṃ hīnavarṇo yathā śaśī ।। muktaś ca tamasā soma evaṃ kṛtayugaṃ ca tat ।।
aviviktam avijñātaṃ dāyādyam iha dhāryate ।। guṇaiḥ karmābhinirvṛttir guṇāḥ śudhyanti karmaṇā ।। yuge yuge yathākālam ṛṣibhiḥ samudāhṛtā ।। āśiṣaś ca śivāḥ puṇyās tathaivāyur yuge yuge ।।
naimittikaḥ prākṛtikas tathaivātyantiko mataḥ ।। ātyantiko vai mokṣaś ca prākṛto dviparārdhikaḥ ।। dviguṇīkṛtayajjñeyaḥ prākṛtaḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ ।। tato aṣṭādaśame bhāge parārdham abhidhīyate ।।
tadāvyakte akhilaṃ vyaktaṃ sahetau layam eti vai ।। taiḥ pañcadaśabhiḥ kāṣṭhā triṃśat kāṣṭhās tathā kalā ।। unmānenāmbhasaḥ sā tu palāny ardhatrayodaśa ।। māgadhena pramāṇena jalaprasthas tu sa smṛtaḥ ।।
ahorātraṃ muhūrtās tu triṃśan māso dinais tathā ।। tribhir varṣaśatair varṣaṃ ṣaṣṭyā caivāsuradviṣām ।। caturyugasahasraṃ tu kathyate brahmaṇo dinam ।। tadante caiva bho viprā brahmanaimittiko layaḥ ।।
śṛṇudhvaṃ prākṛtaṃ bhūyas tato vakṣyāmy ahaṃ layam ।। anāvṛṣṭir atīvogrā jāyate śatavārṣikī ।। kṣayaṃ yānti muniśreṣṭhāḥ pārthivāny atipīḍanāt ।। kṣayāya yatate kartum ātmasthāḥ sakalāḥ prajāḥ ।।
sthitaḥ pibaty aśeṣāṇi jalāni munisattamāḥ ।। śoṣaṃ nayati bho viprāḥ samastaṃ pṛthivītalam ।। pātāleṣu ca yat toyaṃ tat sarvaṃ nayati kṣayam ।। sahasraraśmayaḥ sapta jāyante tatra bhāskarāḥ ।।
dahanty aśeṣaṃ trailokyaṃ sapātālatalaṃ dvijāḥ ।। sādrinagārṇavābhogaṃ niḥsneham abhijāyate ।। bhavaty eṣā ca vasudhā kūrmapṛṣṭhopamākṛtiḥ ।। śeṣāhiśvāsasaṃtāpāt pātālāni dahaty adhaḥ ।।
bhūmim abhyetya sakalaṃ dagdhvā tu vasudhātalam ।। jvālāmālāmahāvartas tatraiva parivartate ।। jvālāvartaparīvāram upakṣīṇabalās tataḥ ।। hṛtāvakāśā gacchanti maharlokaṃ dvijās tadā ।।
gacchanti janalokaṃ te daśāvṛtyā paraiṣiṇaḥ ।। mukhaniḥśvāsajān meghān karoti munisattamāḥ ।। uttiṣṭhanti tadā vyomni ghorāḥ saṃvartakā ghanāḥ ।। dhūmavarṇā ghanāḥ kecit kecit pītāḥ payodharāḥ ।।
kecid vaidūryasaṃkāśā indranīlanibhās tathā ।। indragopanibhāḥ kecin manaḥśilānibhās tathā ।। kecit puravarākārāḥ kecit parvatasaṃnibhāḥ ।। mahākāyā mahārāvā pūrayanti nabhastalam ।।
śamayanty akhilaṃ viprās trailokyāntaravistṛtam ।। plāvayanto jagat sarvaṃ varṣanti munisattamāḥ ।। bhuvo lokaṃ tathaivordhvaṃ plāvayanti divaṃ dvijāḥ ।। varṣanti te mahāmeghā varṣāṇām adhikaṃ śatam ।।
ekārṇavaṃ bhavaty etat trailokyam akhilaṃ tataḥ ।। nāśaṃ nayati bho viprā varṣāṇām adhikaṃ śatam ।। anādir ādir viśvasya pītvā vāyum aśeṣataḥ ।। brahmarūpadharaḥ śete bhagavān ādikṛd dhariḥ ।।
brahmalokagataiś caiva cintyamāno mumukṣubhiḥ ।। ātmānaṃ vāsudevākhyaṃ cintayan parameśvaraḥ ।। nimittaṃ tatra yac chete brahmarūpadharo hariḥ ।। nimīlaty etad akhilaṃ māyāśayyāśaye acyute ।।
ekārṇavakṛte loke tāvatī rātrir ucyate ।। brahmasvarūpadhṛg viṣṇur yathā vaḥ kathitaṃ purā ।। naimittiko vaḥ kathitaḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ prākṛtaṃ param ।। samasteṣv eva lokeṣu pātāleṣv akhileṣu ca ।।
kṛṣṇecchākārite tasmin pravṛtte pratisaṃcare ।। āttagandhā tato bhūmiḥ pralayāya prakalpate ।। āpas tadā pravṛttās tu vegavatyo mahāsvanāḥ ।। salilenaivormimatā lokālokaḥ samantataḥ ।।
naśyanty āpaḥ sutaptāś ca rasatanmātrasaṃkṣayāt ।। agnyavasthe tu salile tejasā sarvato vṛte ।। sarvam āpūryato cābhis tadā jagad idaṃ śanaiḥ ।। jyotiṣo api paraṃ rūpaṃ vāyur atti prabhākaram ।।
pranaṣṭe rūpatanmātre kṛtarūpo vibhāvasuḥ ।। nirāloke tadā loke vāyusaṃsthe ca tejasi ।। ūrdhvaṃ ca vāyus tiryak ca dodhavīti diśo daśa ।। praśāmyati tadā vāyuḥ khaṃ tu tiṣṭhaty anāvṛtam ।।
sarvam āpūrayac caiva sumahat tat prakāśate ।। śabdamātraṃ tathākāśaṃ sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati ।। bhūtendriyeṣu yugapad bhūtādau saṃsthiteṣu vai ।। bhūtādiṃ grasate cāpi mahābuddhir vicakṣaṇā ।।
evaṃ sapta mahābuddhiḥ kramāt prakṛtayas tathā ।। yenedam āvṛtaṃ sarvam aṇḍam apsu pralīyate ।। udakāvaraṇaṃ hy atra jyotiṣā pīyate tu tat ।। ākāśaṃ caiva bhūtādir grasate taṃ tathā mahān ।।
guṇasāmyam anudriktam anyūnaṃ ca dvijottamāḥ ।। ity eṣā prakṛtiḥ sarvā vyaktāvyaktasvarūpiṇī ।। ekaḥ śuddho akṣaro nityaḥ sarvavyāpī tathā punaḥ ।। naśyanti sarvā yatrāpi nāmajātyādikalpanāḥ ।।
sa brahma tat paraṃ dhāma paramātmā pareśvaraḥ ।। prakṛtir yā mayākhyātā vyaktāvyaktasvarūpiṇī ।। paramātmā ca sarveṣām ādhāraḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttaṃ ca dvividhaṃ karma vaidikam ।।
ṛgyajuḥsāmabhir mārgaiḥ pravṛttair ijyate hy asau ।। jñānātmā jñānayogena jñānamūrtiḥ sa ijyate ।। hrasvadīrghaplutair yat tu kiṃcid vastv abhidhīyate ।। vyaktaḥ sa evam avyaktaḥ sa eva puruṣo avyayaḥ ।।
vyaktāvyaktātmikā tasmin prakṛtiḥ sā vilīyate ।। dviparārdhātmakaḥ kālaḥ kathito yo mayā dvijāḥ ।। vyakte tu prakṛtau līne prakṛtyāṃ puruṣe tathā ।। naivāhas tasya ca niśā nityasya paramātmanaḥ ।।
ity eṣa muniśārdūlāḥ kathitaḥ prākṛto layaḥ ।। utpannajñānavairāgyaḥ prāpnoty ātyantikaṃ layam ।। śārīro bahubhir bhedair bhidyate śrūyatāṃ ca saḥ ।। gulmārśaḥśvayathuśvāsa- cchardyādibhir anekadhā ।।
bhidyate dehajas tāpo mānasaṃ śrotum arhatha ।। śokāsūyāvamānerṣyā- mātsaryābhibhavas tathā ।। ity evamādibhir bhedais tāpo hy ādhyātmikaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। sarīsṛpādyaiś ca nṛṇāṃ janyate cādhibhautikaḥ ।।
tāpo dvijavaraśreṣṭhāḥ kathyate cādhidaivikaḥ ।। duḥkhaṃ sahasraśo bhedair bhidyate munisattamāḥ ।। ulbasaṃveṣṭito bhagna- pṛṣṭhagrīvāsthisaṃhatiḥ ।। atitāpibhir atyarthaṃ bādhyamāno ativedanaḥ ।।
śakṛnmūtramahāpaṅka- śāyī sarvatra pīḍitaḥ ।। āste garbhe atiduḥkhena nijakarmanibandhanaḥ ।। prājāpatyena vātena pīḍyamānāsthibandhanaḥ ।। kleśair niṣkrāntim āpnoti jaṭharān mātur āturaḥ ।।
vijñānabhraṃśam āpnoti jātas tu munisattamāḥ ।। pūtivraṇān nipatito dharaṇyāṃ krimiko yathā ।। stanapānādikāhāram avāpnoti parecchayā ।। bhakṣyamāṇo api naivaiṣāṃ samartho vinivāraṇe ।।
bālabhāve yadāpnoti ādhibhūtādikāni ca ।। na jānāti kutaḥ ko ahaṃ kutra gantā kimātmakaḥ ।। kiṃ kāryaṃ kim akāryaṃ vā kiṃ vācyaṃ kiṃ na cocyate ।। kiṃ kartavyam akartavyaṃ kiṃ vā kiṃ guṇadoṣavat ।।
avāpyate narair duḥkhaṃ śiśnodaraparāyaṇaiḥ ।। ajñānināṃ pravartante karmalopas tato dvijāḥ ।। tasmād ajñānināṃ duḥkham iha cāmutra cottamam ।। vicalacchīrṇadaśano valisnāyuśirāvṛtaḥ ।।
nāsāvivaraniryāta- romapuñjaś caladvapuḥ ।। utsannajaṭharāgnitvād alpāhāro alpaceṣṭitaḥ ।। mandībhavacchrotranetra- galallālāvilānanaḥ ।। tatkṣaṇe apy anubhūtānām asmartākhilavastunām ।।
śvāsakāsāmayāyāsa- samudbhūtaprajāgaraḥ ।। bhṛtyātmaputradārāṇām apamānaparākṛtaḥ ।। hāsyaḥ parijanasyāpi nirviṇṇāśeṣabāndhavaḥ ।। saṃsmaran yauvane dīrghaṃ niśvasity atitāpitaḥ ।।
maraṇe yāni duḥkhāni prāpnoti śṛṇu tāny api ।। muhur glāniparaś cāsau muhur jñānabalānvitaḥ ।। ete kathaṃ bhaviṣyantīty atīva mamatākulaḥ ।। śarair ivāntakasyograiś chidyamānāsthibandhanaḥ ।।
saṃśuṣyamāṇatālvoṣṭha- kaṇṭho ghuraghurāyate ।। tāpena mahatā vyāptas tṛṣā vyāptas tathā kṣudhā ।। tataś ca yātanādehaṃ kleśena pratipadyate ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ narake yāni prāpyante puruṣair mṛtaiḥ ।।
yamasya darśanaṃ cogram ugramārgavilokanam ।। pratyekaṃ yātanāyāś ca yātanādi dvijottamāḥ ।। kuṭhāraiḥ pāṭyamānānāṃ bhūmau cāpi nikhanyatām ।। gṛdhraiḥ saṃbhakṣyamāṇānāṃ dvīpibhiś copabhujyatām ।।
uccān nipātyamānānāṃ kṣipyatāṃ kṣepayantrakaiḥ ।। prāpyante nārakair viprās teṣāṃ saṃkhyā na vidyate ।। svarge api pātabhītasya kṣayiṣṇor nāsti nirvṛtiḥ ।। garbhe vilīyate bhūyo jāyamāno astam eti ca ।।
yad yat prītikaraṃ puṃsāṃ vastu viprāḥ prajāyate ।। kalatraputramitrādi- gṛhakṣetradhanādikaiḥ ।। iti saṃsāraduḥkhārka- tāpatāpitacetasām ।। tad asya trividhasyāpi duḥkhajātasya paṇḍitaiḥ ।।
nirastātiśayāhlādaṃ sukhabhāvaikalakṣaṇam ।। tasmāt tatprāptaye yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ paṇḍitair naraiḥ ।। āgamotthaṃ vivekāc ca dvidhā jñānaṃ tathocyate ।। andhaṃ tama ivājñānaṃ dīpavac cendriyodbhavam ।।
manur apy āha vedārthaṃ smṛtvā yan munisattamāḥ ।। dve brahmaṇī veditavye śabdabrahma paraṃ ca yat ।। dve vidye vai veditavye iti cātharvaṇī śrutiḥ ।। yat tad avyaktam ajaram acintyam ajam avyayam ।।
vittaṃ sarvagataṃ nityaṃ bhūtayonim akāraṇam ।। tad brahma paramaṃ dhāma tad dheyaṃ mokṣakāṅkṣibhiḥ ।। utpattiṃ pralayaṃ caiva bhūtānām āgatiṃ gatim ।। jñānaśaktibalaiśvarya- vīryatejāṃsy aśeṣataḥ ।।
sarvāṇi tatra bhūtāni nivasanti parātmani ।। uvācedaṃ maharṣibhyaḥ purā pṛṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। dhātā vidhātā jagatāṃ vāsudevas tataḥ prabhuḥ ।। yaṃ viditvāvyayaṃ tatra yuñjāmaḥ puruṣottamam ।।
abravīt paramaprīto yogī yogavidāṃ varaḥ ।। yam abhyasyāpnuyād yogī mokṣaṃ paramadurlabham ।। itihāsaṃ purāṇaṃ ca vedāṃś caiva vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। jñātvā samabhyased yogaṃ nirdvaṃdvo niṣparigrahaḥ ।।
yāvakaṃ kaṇapiṇyākam āhāraṃ yogasādhanam ।। na dvaṃdve na ca śīte ca na coṣṇe nānilātmake ।। sarīsṛpe śmaśāne ca na nadyante agnisaṃnidhau ।। na śuṣkaparṇanicaye yogaṃ yuñjīta karhicit ।।
pravakṣye tasya ye doṣā jāyante vighnakārakāḥ ।। jvaraś ca jāyate sadyas tadvad ajñānasaṃbhavaḥ ।। dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ śarīraṃ sādhanaṃ yataḥ ।। śūnyāgāre śucau ramye caikānte devatālaye ।।
pūrvāhṇe madhyame cāhni yuktāhāro jitendriyaḥ ।। nātinīce na cocchrite niḥspṛhaḥ satyavāk śuciḥ ।। sarvadvaṃdvasaho dhīraḥ samakāyāṅghrimastakaḥ ।। saṃsthāpya dṛṣṭiṃ nāsāgre prāṇān āyamya vāgyataḥ ।।
praṇavaṃ dīrgham udyamya saṃvṛtāsyaḥ suniścalaḥ ।। saṃchādya nirmale śānte sthitaḥ saṃvṛtalocanaḥ ।। yuñjīta satataṃ yogī muktidaṃ puruṣottamam ।। kṣetrajñaś ca pare yojyas tato yuñjati yogavit ।।
saṃtyajya viṣayāṃs tasya yogasiddhiḥ prakāśitā ।। samādhau yogayuktasya tadābhyeti paraṃ padam ।। bhavaty ānandam āsādya tadā nirvāṇam ṛcchati ।। prāpya yogabalād yogī mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
sarvatrānityabuddhis tu yogī mucyeta nānyathā ।। sadā cābhyāsayogena mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। manasaś cendriyāṇāṃ ca saṃyogo yoga ucyate ।। saṃsāramokṣahetuś ca kim anyac chrotum icchatha ।।
vyāsaṃ praśasya saṃpūjya punaḥ praṣṭuṃ samudyatāḥ ।। pibatāṃ no dvijaśreṣṭha na tṛptir iha dṛśyate ।। sāṃkhyaṃ ca dvipadāṃ śreṣṭha śrotum icchāmahe vayam ।। satyadharmamatir brahman kathaṃ brahmādhigacchati ।।
sāṃkhye vā yadi vā yoga etat pṛṣṭo vadasva naḥ ।। yenopāyena puruṣas tat tvaṃ vyākhyātum arhasi ।। nānyatra sarvasaṃtyāgāt siddhiṃ vindati kaścana ।। bhūyiṣṭhaṃ prāṇabhṛdgrāme niviṣṭāni śarīriṣu ।।
prāṇāpānāśrayo vāyuḥ koṣṭhāākāśaṃ śarīriṇām ।। karṇayoḥ pradiśaḥ śrotre jihvāyāṃ vāk sarasvatī ।। daśa tānīndriyoktāni dvārāṇy āhārasiddhaye ।। indriyārthān pṛthag vidyād indriyebhyas tu nityadā ।।
manaś cāpi sadā yuṅkte bhūtātmā hṛdayāśritaḥ ।। niyame ca visarge ca bhūtātmā manasas tathā ।। prāṇāpānau ca jīvaś ca nityaṃ deheṣu dehinām ।। sattvaṃ hi tejaḥ sṛjati na guṇān vai kathaṃcana ।।
manīṣī manasā viprāḥ paśyaty ātmānam ātmani ।। manasā tu pradīptena mahān ātmā prakāśate ।। aśarīraṃ śarīre sve nirīkṣeta nirindriyam ।। yo anupaśyati sa pretya kalpate brahmabhūyataḥ ।।
śuni caiva śvapāke ca paṇḍitāḥ samadarśinaḥ ।। vasaty eko mahān ātmā yena sarvam idaṃ tatam ।। yadā paśyati bhūtātmā brahma saṃpadyate tadā ।। ya evaṃ satataṃ veda so amṛtatvāya kalpate ।।
devāpi mārge muhyanti apadasya padaiṣiṇaḥ ।। yathā gatir na dṛśyeta tathā jñānavidāṃ gatiḥ ।। yasmiṃs tu pacyate kālas tan na vedeha kaścana ।। na madhye pratigṛhṇīte naiva kiṃcin na kaścana ।।
yady apy agre samāgacched yathā bāṇo guṇacyutaḥ ।। tasmāt sūkṣmataraṃ nāsti nāsti sthūlataraṃ tathā ।। sarvataḥśrutimal loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati ।। tad antaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ dhruvaṃ tiṣṭhan na dṛśyate ।।
kṣaraḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu divyaṃ tv amṛtam akṣaram ।। īdṛśaḥ sarvabhūtasya sthāvarasya carasya ca ।। śarīrāṇām ajasyāhur haṃsatvaṃ pāradarśinaḥ ।। tad vidvān akṣaraṃ prāpya jahāti prāṇajanmanī ।।
sāṃkhyaṃ jñānena saṃyuktaṃ yad etat kīrtitaṃ mayā ।। ekatvaṃ buddhimanasor indriyāṇāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।। tad etad upaśāntena dāntenādhyātmaśīlinā ।। yogadoṣān samucchidya pañca yān kavayo viduḥ ।।
krodhaṃ śamena jayati kāmaṃ saṃkalpavarjanāt ।। dhṛtyā śiśnodaraṃ rakṣet pāṇipādaṃ ca cakṣuṣā ।। apramādād bhayaṃ jahyād dambhaṃ prājñopasevanāt ।। agnīṃś ca brāhmaṇāṃś cātha devatāḥ praṇamet sadā ।।
brahmatejomayaṃ śukraṃ yasya sarvam idaṃ jagat ।। dhyānam adhyayanaṃ dānaṃ satyaṃ hrīr ārjavaṃ kṣamā ।। etair vivardhate tejaḥ pāpmānaṃ cāpakarṣati ।। dhūtapāpmā tu tejasvī laghvāhāro jitendriyaḥ ।।
manasaś cendriyāṇāṃ ca kṛtvaikāgryaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। jantoḥ pañcendriyasyāsya yady ekaṃ klinnam indriyam ।। manasaḥ pūrvam ādadyāt kūrmāṇām iva matsyahā ।। tata etāni saṃyamya manasi sthāpayed yadi ।।
pañcendriyāṇi manasi hṛdi saṃsthāpayed yadi ।। prasīdanti ca saṃsthāyāṃ tadā brahma prakāśate ।। vaidyuto agnir ivākāśe paśyanty ātmānam ātmani ।। taṃ paśyanti mahātmāno brāhmaṇā ye manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
evaṃ parimitaṃ kālam ācaran saṃśitavrataḥ ।। pramoho bhrama āvarto ghrāṇaṃ śravaṇadarśane ।। pratibhān upasargāś ca pratisaṃgṛhya yogataḥ ।। kuryāt paricayaṃ yoge trailokye niyato muniḥ ।।
saṃniyamyendriyagrāmaṃ koṣṭhe bhāṇḍamanā iva ।। yenopāyena śakyeta niyantuṃ cañcalaṃ manaḥ ।। śūnyāgārāṇi caikāgro nivāsārtham upakramet ।। upekṣako yatāhāro labdhālabdhasamo bhavet ।।
samas tayoś cāpy ubhayor nābhidhyāyec chubhāśubham ।। samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu sadharmā mātariśvanaḥ ।। ṣaṇ māsān nityayuktasya śabdabrahmābhivartate ।। evaṃ tu nirato mārgaṃ viramen na vimohitaḥ ।।
tāv apy etena mārgeṇa gacchetāṃ paramāṃ gatim ।। kāṃ diśaṃ vidyayā yānti kāṃ ca gacchanti karmaṇā ।। etad anyonyavairūpyaṃ vartate pratikūlataḥ ।। karmavidyāmayau cobhau vyākhyāsyāmi kṣarākṣarau ।।
śṛṇudhvaṃ sāṃprataṃ viprā gahanaṃ hy etad uttaram ।। yakṣasya sādṛśyam idaṃ yakṣasyedaṃ bhaved atha ।। pravṛttilakṣaṇo dharmo nivṛtto vā vibhāṣitaḥ ।। tasmāt karma na kurvanti yatayaḥ pāradarśinaḥ ।।
vidyayā jāyate nityam avyaktaṃ hy akṣarātmakam ।। tena te dehajālena ramayanta upāsate ।। na te karma praśaṃsanti kūpaṃ nadyāṃ pibann iva ।। vidyayā tad avāpnoti yatra gatvā na śocati ।।
na jīryate yatra gatvā yatra gatvā na vardhate ।। avyākṛtam anāyāmam amṛtaṃ cādhiyogavit ।। samāḥ sarvatra maitrāś ca sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ ।। viprāś candrasamasparśaḥ sūkṣmayā kalayā sthitaḥ ।।
na vaktuṃ śakyate draṣṭuṃ cakratantum ivāmbare ।। mūrtimān iti taṃ vidyād viprāḥ karmaguṇātmakam ।। kṣetrajñaṃ taṃ vijānīyān nityaṃ yogajitātmakam ।। jīvam ātmaguṇaṃ vidyād ātmānaṃ paramātmanaḥ ।।
te cainaṃ na prajānanti na jānāti sa tān api ।। sudāntair iva saṃyantā dṛḍhaḥ paramavājibhiḥ ।। manasas tu parā buddhir buddher ātmā mahān paraḥ ।। amṛtān na paraṃ kiṃcit sā kāṣṭhā paramā gatiḥ ।।
dṛśyate tv agryayā buddhyā sūkṣmayā sūkṣmadarśibhiḥ ।। indriyair indriyārthāṃś ca bahucittam acintayan ।। anīśvaraḥ praśāntātmā tato gacchet paraṃ padam ।। ātmanaḥ saṃpradānena martyo mṛtyum upāśnute ।।
sattve cittaṃ samāveśya tataḥ kālañjaro bhavet ।। prasannātmātmani sthitvā sukham atyantam aśnute ।। nirvāte vā yathā dīpo dīpyamāno na kampate ।। laghvāhāro viśuddhātmā paśyaty ātmānam ātmani ।।
ātmapratyāyakaṃ śāstram idaṃ putrānuśāsanam ।। daśavarṣasahasrāṇi nirmathyāmṛtam uddhṛtam ।। tathaiva viduṣāṃ jñānaṃ muktihetoḥ samuddhṛtam ।। tad idaṃ nāpraśāntāya nādāntāya tapasvine ।।
nāsūyakāyānṛjave na cānirdiṣṭakāriṇe ।। ślāghine ślāghanīyāya praśāntāya tapasvine ।। rahasyadharmaṃ vaktavyaṃ nānyasmai tu kathaṃcana ।। idam eva tataḥ śreya iti manyeta tattvavit ।।
yat tan maharṣibhir dṛṣṭaṃ vedānteṣu ca gīyate ।। śrutaṃ bhavadbhis tat sarvaṃ kim anyat kathayāmi vaḥ ।। yad adhyātmaṃ yathā vidmo bhagavann ṛṣisattama ।। yuṣmabhyaṃ kathayiṣyāmi tasya vyākhyāvadhāryatām ।।
mahābhūtāni yaś caiva sarvabhūteṣu bhūtakṛt ।। indriyāṇāṃ guṇāḥ kecit kathaṃ tān upalakṣayet ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ tad ihaikāgryā yathātattvaṃ yathā ca tat ।। prāṇaś ceṣṭā tathā sparśa ete vāyuguṇās trayaḥ ।।
raso atha rasanaṃ svedo guṇās tv ete trayo ambhasām ।। etāvān indriyagrāmo vyākhyātaḥ pāñcabhautikaḥ ।। ākāśaprabhavaḥ śabdo gandho bhūmiguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। te guṇān ativartante guṇebhyaḥ paramā matāḥ ।।
evam evendriyagrāmaṃ buddhiśreṣṭho niyacchati ।। etasminn eva kṛtye sā vartate buddhir uttamā ।। manaḥṣaṣṭhāni sarvāṇi buddhyā bhāvāt kuto guṇāḥ ।। saptamīṃ buddhim evāhuḥ kṣetrajñaṃ viddhi cāṣṭamam ।।
buddhir adhyavasānāya sākṣī kṣetrajña ucyate ।। samāḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu tān guṇān upalakṣayet ।। praśāntam iva saṃyuktaṃ sattvaṃ tad upadhārayet ।। pravṛttaṃ raja ity evaṃ tatra cāpy upalakṣayet ।।
apratarkyam avijñeyaṃ tamas tad upadhārayet ।। akasmād yadi vā kasmād vadanti sāttvikān guṇān ।। liṅgāni rajasas tāni vartante hetutattvataḥ ।। kathaṃcid abhivartante vijñeyās tāmasā guṇāḥ ।।
hṛdayaṃ priyam eveha trividhā karmacodanā ।। manasas tu parā buddhir buddher ātmā paraḥ smṛtaḥ ।। yadā vikurute bhāvaṃ tadā bhavati sā manaḥ ।। śṛṇvatī bhavati śrotraṃ spṛśatī sparśa ucyate ।।
jighrantī bhavati ghrāṇaṃ buddhir vikurute pṛthak ।। tiṣṭhati puruṣe buddhir buddhibhāvavyavasthitā ।। na sukhena ca duḥkhena kadācid iha muhyate ।। saritāṃ sāgaro bhartā mahāvelām ivormimān ।।
adhiṣṭhāne ca vai buddhyā pṛthag etāni saṃsmaret ।। sarvāṇy evānupūrveṇa yad yadā ca vidhīyate ।। pravartamānas tu rajaḥ sattvam apy ativartate ।। anv arthān saṃpravartante rathanemim arā iva ।।
niścaradbhir yathāyogam udāsīnair yadṛcchayā ।। aśocan saṃprahṛṣyaṃś ca nityaṃ vigatamatsaraḥ ।। pravartamānair anekair durdharair akṛtātmabhiḥ ।। tadā prakāśate śyātmā dīpadīptā yathākṛtiḥ ।।
prakāśaṃ bhavate sarvaṃ tathaivam upadhāryatām ।। vimuktātmā tathā yogī guṇadoṣair na lipyate ।। asajjamānaḥ sarveṣu na kathaṃcit pralipyate ।। sarvabhūtātmabhūtasya guṇasaṅgena sajjataḥ ।।
na guṇā vidur ātmānaṃ guṇān veda sa sarvadā ।। sattvakṣetrajñayor evam antaraṃ lakṣayen naraḥ ।। pṛthagbhūtau prakṛtyaitau saṃprayuktau ca sarvadā ।। maśakodumbarau vāpi saṃprayuktau yathā saha ।।
tathaiva sahitāv etau anyonyasmin pratiṣṭhitau ।। guṇān vikriyataḥ sarvān udāsīnavad īśvaraḥ ।। ūrṇanābhir yathā sūtraṃ sṛjate tad guṇāṃs tathā ।। evam eke vyavasyanti nivṛttim iti cāpare ।।
anenaiva vidhānena bhaved vai saṃśayo mahān ।। akrudhyann aprahṛṣyaṃś ca nityaṃ vigatamatsaraḥ ।। anityaṃ sukham āsīnam aśocyaṃ chinnasaṃśayaḥ ।। avagāhya ca vidvāṃso viprā lolam imaṃ tathā ।।
evaṃ vicintya cātmānaṃ kevalaṃ jñānam ātmanaḥ ।। samaceṣṭaś ca vai samyag labhate śamam uttamam ।। ātmajñānasamasneha- paryāptaṃ tatparāyaṇam ।। vijñāyaitad vimucyante kṛtakṛtyā manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
yo viśiṣṭaś ca bhūtebhyas tad bhavān prabravītu naḥ ।। viśiṣṭaṃ sarvadharmebhyaḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ munisattamāḥ ।। sarvataḥ prasṛtānīha pitā bālān ivātmajān ।। vijñeyaḥ sarvadharmebhyaḥ sa dharmaḥ para ucyate ।।
ātmatṛptaḥ sa evāsīd bahucintyam acintayan ।। tadā caivātmanātmānaṃ paraṃ drakṣyatha śāśvatam ।। prapaśyanti mahātmānaṃ brāhmaṇā ye manīṣiṇaḥ ।। ātmano nābhijānīte kva me puṣpaṃ kva me phalam ।।
anyo hy asyāntarātmāsti yaḥ sarvam anupaśyati ।। dṛṣṭvātmānaṃ tathā yūyaṃ virāgā bhavata dvijāḥ ।। parāṃ buddhim avāpyehāpy acintā vigatajvarāḥ ।। pañcendriyagrāhavatīṃ manaḥsaṃkalparodhasam ।।
satyatīrthānṛtakṣobhāṃ krodhapaṅkāṃ saridvarām ।। prataradhvaṃ nadīṃ buddhyā dustarām akṛtātmabhiḥ ।। ātmajanmodbhavāṃ tāṃ tu jihvāvartadurāsadām ।। tāṃ tīrṇaḥ sarvato mukto vidhūtātmātmavāñ śuciḥ ।।
uttīrṇaḥ sarvasaṃkleśān prasannātmā vikalmaṣaḥ ।। akrudhyann aprasīdaṃś ca nanṛśaṃsamatis tathā ।। etad dhi sarvadharmebhyo viśiṣṭaṃ menire budhāḥ ।। ātmāno vyāpino viprā iti putrānuśāsanam ।।
ātmajñānam idaṃ guhyaṃ sarvaguhyatamaṃ mahat ।। naiva strī na pumān evaṃ na caivedaṃ napuṃsakam ।। naitaj jñātvā pumān strī vā punarbhavam avāpnuyāt ।। kathitāni mayā viprā bhavanti na bhavanti ca ।।
tam upāyaṃ yathānyāyaṃ śrotum icchāmahe mune ।। yadupāyena sarvārthān mṛgayadhvaṃ sadānaghāḥ ।। evaṃ dharmādyupāyārthe nānyadharmeṣu kāraṇam ।। ekaḥ panthā hi mokṣasya tac chṛṇudhvaṃ mamānaghāḥ ।।
sattvasaṃsevanād dhīro nidrām ucchettum arhati ।। icchāṃ dveṣaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca dhairyeṇa vinivartayet ।। upadravāṃs tathā yogī hitajīrṇamitāśanāt ।। anukrośād adharmaṃ ca jayed dharmam upekṣayā ।।
anityatvena ca snehaṃ kṣudhāṃ yogena paṇḍitaḥ ।। utthānena jayet tandrāṃ vitarkaṃ niścayāj jayet ।। yacched vāṅmanasī buddhyā tāṃ yacchej jñānacakṣuṣā ।। tad etad upaśāntena boddhavyaṃ śucikarmaṇā ।।
kāmaṃ krodhaṃ ca lobhaṃ ca bhayaṃ svapnaṃ ca pañcamam ।। dhyānam adhyayanaṃ dānaṃ satyaṃ hrīr ārjavaṃ kṣamā ।। etair vivardhate tejaḥ pāpmānam upahanti ca ।। dhūtapāpaḥ sa tejasvī laghvāhāro jitendriyaḥ ।।
amūḍhatvam asaṅgitvaṃ kāmakrodhavivarjanam ।। tathā vākkāyamanasāṃ niyamāḥ kāmato avyayāḥ ।। tava dharmajña sarvaṃ hi viditaṃ munisattama ।। vadanti kāraṇaiḥ śreṣṭhaiḥ svapakṣodbhavanāya vai ।।
vadanti kāraṇaiḥ śreṣṭhaṃ yogaṃ samyaṅ manīṣiṇaḥ ।। vijñāyeha gatīḥ sarvā virakto viṣayeṣu yaḥ ।। etad āhur mahāprājñāḥ sāṃkhyaṃ vai mokṣadarśanam ।। śiṣṭānāṃ hi mataṃ grāhyaṃ bhavadbhiḥ śiṣṭasaṃmataiḥ ।।
ubhe caite mate tattve samavete dvijottamāḥ ।। anuṣṭhite yathāśāstraṃ nayetāṃ paramāṃ gatim ।। vratānāṃ dhāraṇaṃ tulyaṃ darśanaṃ tv asamaṃ tayoḥ ।। tulyaṃ taddarśanaṃ kasmāt tan no brūhi dvijottama ।।
yogāsthiroditān doṣān pañcaitān prāpnuvanti tān ।। prāpnuvanti tathā yogāt tat padaṃ vītakalmaṣāḥ ।। prāpnuyur vimalaṃ mārgaṃ vimuktāḥ sarvabandhanaiḥ ।। chittvā yogāt paraṃ mārgaṃ gacchanti vimalaṃ śubham ।।
vinaśyanti na saṃdehas tadvad yogabalād ṛte ।। bandhaṃ na gacchanty anaghā yogās te tu sudurlabhāḥ ।। tatrāśaktā vipadyante mucyante tu balānvitāḥ ।। abalā na vimucyante mucyante ca balānvitāḥ ।।
ākrānta indhanaiḥ sthūlais tadvad yogabalaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। samīraṇagataḥ kṛtsnāṃ dahet kṣipraṃ mahīm imām ।। antakāla ivādityaḥ kṛtsnaṃ saṃśoṣayej jagat ।। balahīnas tathā yogī viṣayair hriyate ca saḥ ।।
tadvad yogabalaṃ labdhvā na bhaved viṣayair hṛtaḥ ।। prajāpatīn manūn sarvān mahābhūtāni ceśvarāḥ ।। viśante tad dvijāḥ sarve yogasyāmitatejasaḥ ।। yogaṃ kuryād balaṃ prāpya taiś ca sarvair mahīṃ caret ।।
saṃkṣipyec ca punar viprāḥ sūryas tejoguṇān iva ।। vimokṣaprabhavaṃ viṣṇum upapannam asaṃśayam ।। nidarśanārthaṃ sūkṣmāṇi vakṣyāmi ca punar dvijāḥ ।। nidarśanāni sūkṣmāṇi śṛṇudhvaṃ munisattamāḥ ।।
yuktaḥ samyak tathā yogī mokṣaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam ।। puruṣo yukta ārohet sopānaṃ yuktamānasaḥ ।। karoty amalam ātmānaṃ bhāskaropamadarśane ।। mahārṇavagatāṃ śīghraṃ nayed viprāṃs tu pattanam ।।
durgamaṃ sthānam āpnoti hitvā deham imaṃ dvijāḥ ।। deśam iṣṭaṃ nayaty āśu dhanvinaṃ puruṣarṣabham ।। prāpnoty āśu paraṃ sthānaṃ lakṣyamukta ivāśugaḥ ।। pāśaṃ hatveva mīnānāṃ padam āpnoti so ajaram ।।
darśane śravaṇe vāpi ghrāṇe cāmitavikramaḥ ।। ātmanā sūkṣmam ātmānaṃ yuṅkte samyag dvijottamāḥ ।। uttamaṃ yogam āsthāya yadīcchati vimucyate ।। yogī balam avāpnoti tad bhavān vaktum arhati ।।
snehānāṃ varjane yukto yogī balam avāpnuyāt ।। ekāhārī viśuddhātmā yogī balam avāpnuyāt ।। apaḥ pītvā payomiśrā yogī balam avāpnuyāt ।। upoṣya samyak śuddhātmā yogī balam avāpnuyāt ।।
bhayaṃ śokaṃ tathā svāpaṃ pauruṣān viṣayāṃs tathā ।। sparśaṃ nidrāṃ tathā tandrāṃ durjayāṃ munisattamāḥ ।। vītarāgā mahāprājñā dhyānādhyayanasaṃpadā ।। yaḥ kaścid vrajati kṣipraṃ kṣemeṇa munipuṃgavāḥ ।।
śvabhravat toyahīnaṃ ca durgamaṃ bahukaṇṭakam ।। panthānaṃ taskarākīrṇaṃ kṣemeṇābhipatet tathā ।। kṣemeṇoparamen mārgād bahudoṣo api saṃmataḥ ।। dhāraṇā sā tu yogasya durgeyam akṛtātmabhiḥ ।।
netṛhīnā yathā nāvaḥ puruṣāṇāṃ tu vai dvijāḥ ।। maraṇaṃ janmaduḥkhitvaṃ sukhitvaṃ sa viśiṣyate ।। paraṃ yogasya panthānaṃ niścitaṃ taṃ dvijātiṣu ।। yogamārgo yathānyāyaṃ śiṣyāyeha hitaiṣiṇā ।।
triṣu lokeṣu yaj jñānaṃ sarvaṃ tad viditaṃ hi te ।। vihitaṃ yatibhir vṛddhaiḥ kapilādibhir īśvaraiḥ ।। guṇāś ca yasmin bahavo doṣahāniś ca kevalā ।। mānuṣān durjayān kṛtsnān paiśācān viṣayāṃs tathā ।।
pitṝṇāṃ viṣayāñ jñātvā tiryaktvaṃ caratāṃ dvijāḥ ।। maharṣiviṣayāṃś caiva rājarṣiviṣayāṃs tathā ।। devarṣiviṣayāñ jñātvā yogānām api vai parān ।। āyuṣaś ca paraṃ kālaṃ lokair vijñāya tattvataḥ ।।
prāptakāle ca yad duḥkhaṃ patatāṃ viṣayaiṣiṇām ।। svargasya ca guṇāñ jñātvā doṣān sarvāṃś ca bho dvijāḥ ।। jñānayoge ca ye doṣā jñānayoge ca ye guṇāḥ ।। sattvaṃ daśaguṇaṃ jñātvā rajo navaguṇaṃ tathā ।।
ṣaḍguṇaṃ ca nabho jñātvā tamaś ca triguṇaṃ mahat ।। mārgaṃ vijñāya tattvena pralayaprekṣaṇena tu ।। prāpnuvanti śubhaṃ mokṣaṃ sūkṣmā iva nabhaḥ param ।। śabdagrāhyaṃ tathā śrotraṃ jihvāṃ rasaguṇena ca ।।
mohaṃ tamasi saṃyuktaṃ lobhaṃ moheṣu saṃśritam ।। apsu devīṃ samāyuktām āpas tejasi saṃśritāḥ ।। nabho mahati saṃyuktaṃ tamo mahasi saṃsthitam ।। saktam ātmānam īśe ca deve nārāyaṇe tathā ।।
jñātvā sattvaguṇaṃ dehaṃ vṛtaṃ ṣoḍaśabhir guṇaiḥ ।। madhyastham iva cātmānaṃ pāpaṃ yasmin na vidyate ।। indriyāṇīndriyārthāṃś ca sarvān ātmani saṃśritān ।। prāṇāpānau samānaṃ ca vyānodānau ca tattvataḥ ।।
saptadhā tāṃs tathā śeṣān saptadhā vidhivat punaḥ ।। saptarṣīṃś ca bahūñ jñātvā rājarṣīṃś ca paraṃtapān ।। aiśvaryāc cyāvitān dṛṣṭvā kālena mahatā dvijāḥ ।। gatiṃ vācāṃ śubhāṃ jñātvā arcārhāḥ pāpakarmaṇām ।।
yoniṣu ca vicitrāsu saṃcārān aśubhāṃs tathā ।। śleṣmamūtrapurīṣe ca tīvragandhasamanvite ।। śirāśatasamākīrṇe navadvāre pure atha vai ।। tāmasānāṃ ca jantūnāṃ ramaṇīyānṛtātmanām ।।
garhitaṃ mahatām arthe sāṃkhyānāṃ viditātmanām ।। tārāṇāṃ patanaṃ dṛṣṭvā nakṣatrāṇāṃ ca paryayam ।। anyonyabhakṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhūtānām api cāśubham ।। rāgaṃ mohaṃ ca saṃprāptaṃ kvacit sattvaṃ samāśritam ।।
durlabhatvaṃ ca mokṣasya vijñānaṃ śrutipūrvakam ।। viṣayāṇāṃ ca daurātmyaṃ vijñāya ca punar dvijāḥ ।। vāsaṃ kuleṣu jantūnāṃ maraṇāya dhṛtātmanām ।। brahmaghnānāṃ gatiṃ jñātvā patitānāṃ sudāruṇām ।।
gurudāraprasaktānāṃ gatiṃ vijñāya cāśubhām ।। sadevakeṣu lokeṣu yena vartanti mānavāḥ ।। tiryagyonigatānāṃ ca vijñāya ca gatīḥ pṛthak ।। kṣayaṃ saṃvatsarāṇāṃ ca māsānāṃ ca kṣayaṃ tathā ।।
kṣayaṃ vṛddhiṃ ca candrasya dṛṣṭvā pratyakṣatas tathā ।। kṣayaṃ dhanānāṃ dṛṣṭvā ca punar vṛddhiṃ tathaiva ca ।। dehavaiklavyatāṃ caiva samyag vijñāya tattvataḥ ।। svadehād utthitān gandhāṃs tathā vijñāya cāśubhān ।।
etaṃ naḥ saṃśayaṃ kṛtsnaṃ vaktum arhasy aśeṣataḥ ।। mārgajñāḥ kāpilāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ munisattamāḥ ।। ete doṣāḥ śarīreṣu dṛśyante sarvadehinām ।। sattvasaṃsevanān nidrām apramādād bhayaṃ tathā ।।
guṇān guṇaśatair jñātvā doṣān doṣaśatair api ।। apāṃ phenopamaṃ lokaṃ viṣṇor māyāśataiḥ kṛtam ।। tamaḥsaṃbhramitaṃ dṛṣṭvā varṣabudbudasaṃnibham ।। rajas tamasi saṃmagnaṃ paṅke dvipam ivāvaśam ।।
jñānajñeyena sāṃkhyena vyāpinā mahatā dvijāḥ ।। puṇyāṃś ca sāttvikān gandhān sparśajān dehasaṃśritān ।। tato duḥkhādikaṃ ghoraṃ cintāśokamahāhradam ।। tamaḥkūrmaṃ rajomīnaṃ prajñayā saṃtaranty uta ।।
karmāgādhaṃ satyatīraṃ sthitaṃ vratamanīṣiṇaḥ ।। nānāprītimahāratnaṃ duḥkhajvarasamīritam ।। asthisaṃghātasaṃghaṭṭaṃ śleṣmayogaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। hasitotkruṣṭanirghoṣaṃ nānājñānasuduṣkaram ।।
pralabdhvā janmaloko yaṃ putrabāndhavapattanam ।। vṛndānugāminaṃ kṣīraṃ sarvabhūtapayodadhim ।। taranti yatayaḥ siddhā jñānayogena cānaghāḥ ।। tatas tān sukṛtīñ jñātvā sūryo vahati raśmibhiḥ ।।
tatra tān pravaho vāyuḥ pratigṛhṇāti cānaghāḥ ।। sūkṣmaḥ śītaḥ sugandhaś ca sukhasparśaś ca bho dvijāḥ ।। sa tān vahati viprendrā nabhasaḥ paramāṃ gatim ।। rajo vahati viprendrāḥ sattvasya paramāṃ gatim ।।
prabhur vahati śuddhātmā paramātmānam ātmanā ।। amṛtatvāya kalpante na nivartanti ca dvijāḥ ।। satyārjavaratānāṃ vai sarvabhūtadayāvatām ।। ājanmamaraṇaṃ vā te ramante tatra vā na vā ।।
tvadṛte mānavaṃ nānyaṃ praṣṭum arhāma sattama ।। yadi tatraiva vijñāne vartante yatayaḥ pare ।। magnasya hi pare jñāne kiṃtu duḥkhāntaraṃ bhavet ।। budhānām api saṃmohaḥ praśne asmin munisattamāḥ ।।
buddhiś ca paramā yatra kapilānāṃ mahātmanām ।। karaṇāny ātmanas tāni sūkṣmaṃ paśyanti tais tu saḥ ।। vinaśyanti na saṃdeho velā iva mahārṇave ।। sūkṣmaś carati sarvatra nabhasīva samīraṇaḥ ।।
budhyamāno yathāpūrvam akhileneha bho dvijāḥ ।। anīśatvāt pralīyante sarpā viṣahatā iva ।। ākramya gatayaḥ sūkṣmā varaty ātmā na saṃśayaḥ ।। guṇāṃś ca tamasaḥ sarvān guṇān buddheś ca sattamāḥ ।।
guṇān vāyoś ca sarvajñāḥ snehajāṃś ca guṇān punaḥ ।। sarvān eva guṇair vyāpya kṣetrajñeṣu dvijottamāḥ ।। śiṣyā iva mahātmānam indriyāṇi ca taṃ dvijāḥ ।। nārāyaṇaṃ mahātmānaṃ nirvikāraṃ parāt param ।।
paramātmānam aguṇaṃ nirvṛtaṃ taṃ ca sattamāḥ ।। āgacchanti yathākālaṃ guroḥ saṃdeśakāriṇaḥ ।। evam uktena viprendrāḥ sāṃkhyayogena mokṣiṇīm ।। jñānenānena viprendrās tulyaṃ jñānaṃ na vidyate ।।
akṣaraṃ dhruvam evoktaṃ pūrvaṃ brahma sanātanam ।। kūṭasthaṃ caiva nityaṃ ca yad vadanti śamātmakāḥ ।। evaṃ śaṃsanti śāstreṣu pravaktāro maharṣayaḥ ।। brahmaṇyaṃ paramaṃ devam anantaṃ paramācyutam ।।
samyag uktās tathā yogāḥ sāṃkhyāś cāmitadarśanāḥ ।। abhijñānāni tasyāhur mahānti munisattamāḥ ।। agamyagamyasaṃjñāni gamyaṃ tatra viśiṣyate ।। kiṃsvit tat kṣaram ity uktaṃ yasmād āvartate punaḥ ।।
upalabdhuṃ muniśreṣṭha tattvena munipuṃgava ।। ṛṣibhiś ca mahābhāgair yatibhiś ca mahātmabhiḥ ।। na tṛptim adhigacchāmaḥ śṛṇvanto amṛtam uttamam ।। vasiṣṭhasya ca saṃvādaṃ karālajanakasya ca ।।
papraccha janako rājā jñānaṃ naiḥśreyasaṃ param ।। maitrāvaruṇim āsīnam abhivādya kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। papraccharṣivaraṃ rājā karālajanakaḥ purā ।। yasmin na punarāvṛttiṃ prāpnuvanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
yac cākṣaram iti proktaṃ śivaṃ kṣemam anāmayam ।। yatra kṣarati pūrveṇa yāvatkālena cāpy atha ।। daśakalpaśatāvartam ahas tad brāhmam ucyate ।। sṛjaty anantakarmāṇi mahāntaṃ bhūtam agrajam ।।
