yatrotpattiṃ pravakṣyāmi mūlato nṛpasattama ।। sarvataḥpāṇipādāntaṃ sarvatokṣiśiromukham ।। hiraṇyagarbho bhagavān eṣa buddhir iti smṛtiḥ ।। sāṃkhye ca paṭhyate śāstre nāmabhir bahudhātmakaḥ ।।
dhṛtam ekātmakaṃ yena kṛtsnaṃ trailokyam ātmanā ।। eṣa vai vikriyāpannaḥ sṛjaty ātmānam ātmanā ।। ahaṃkāraṃ mahātejāḥ prajāpatinamaskṛtam ।। mahāntaṃ cāpy ahaṃkāram avidyāsarga eva ca ।।
vidyāvidyeti vikhyāte śrutiśāstrānucintakaiḥ ।। ahaṃkāreṣu nṛpate caturthaṃ viddhi vaikṛtam ।। śabdasparśau ca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhas tathaiva ca ।। pañcamaṃ viddhi rājendra bhautikaṃ sargam arthakṛt ।।
vāg hastau caiva pādau ca pāyur meḍhraṃ tathaiva ca ।। saṃbhūtānīha yugapan manasā saha pārthiva ।। yāṃ jñātvā nābhiśocanti brāhmaṇās tattvadarśinaḥ ।। veditavyaṃ naraśreṣṭha sadaiva narakārṇave ।।
sacāraṇapiśāce vai sadevarṣiniśācare ।। śuni śvapāke caiṇeye sacāṇḍāle sapulkase ।। yā ca mūrtiś ca yat kiṃcit sarvatraitan nidarśanam ।। sthānaṃ dehavatām āsīd ity evam anuśuśruma ।।
ahany ahani bhūtātmā yac cākṣara iti smṛtam ।। jagan mohātmakaṃ cāhur avyaktād vyaktasaṃjñakam ।। kathitaṃ te mahārāja yasmān nāvartate punaḥ ।। sattvasaṃśrayaṇāt tattvaṃ sattvam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
caturviṃśatimo vyakto hy amūrtiḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ ।। cetayaṃś cetano nityaṃ sarvamūrtir amūrtimān ।। gocare vartate nityaṃ nirguṇo guṇasaṃjñitaḥ ।। vikurvāṇaḥ prakṛtimān nābhimanyeta buddhimān ।।
līyate pratibuddhatvād abuddhajanasevanāt ।। yo ahaṃ na so aham ity ukto guṇān evānuvartate ।। rajasā rājasāṃś caiva sāttvikān sattvasaṃśrayāt ।। sarvāṇy etāni rūpāṇi jānīhi prākṛtāni tu ।।
sāttvikā devalokāya gacchanti sukhabhāginaḥ ।। puṇyapāpeṣu mānuṣyaṃ puṇyamātreṇa devatāḥ ।। pañcaviṃśatimo yo ayaṃ jñānād eva pravartate ।। dehād dehasahasrāṇi tathā ca na sa bhidyate ।।
utpadyati tapoyogād guṇaiḥ saha guṇakṣayāt ।। mānuṣyān nirayasthānam ālayaṃ pratipadyate ।। sūtratantuguṇair nityaṃ tathāyam aguṇo guṇaiḥ ।। śīrṣaroge akṣiroge ca dantaśūle galagrahe ।।
śvitrakuṣṭhe agnidagdhe ca sidhmāpasmārayor api ।। utpadyante vicitrāṇi tāny evātmābhimanyate ।। ekavāsāś caturvāsāḥ śāyī nityam adhas tathā ।। vīram āsanam ākāśe tathā śayanam eva ca ।।
bhasmaprastaraśāyī ca bhūmiśayyānulepanaḥ ।। vividhāsu ca śayyāsu phalagṛhyānvitāsu ca ।। maṇivālaparīdhāno vyāghracarmaparicchadaḥ ।। phalakaṃ paridhānaś ca tathā kaṭakavastradhṛk ।।
vastrāṇi cānyāni bahūny abhimatya ca buddhimān ।। ekarātrāntarāśitvam ekakālikabhojanam ।। ṣaḍrātrabhojanaś caiva tathā cāṣṭāhabhojanaḥ ।। vāyubhakṣaś ca piṇyāka- dadhigomayabhojanaḥ ।।
śaivālabhojanaś caiva tathā cānyena vartayan ।। vividhāni ca kṛcchrāṇi sevate siddhikāṅkṣayā ।। cāturāśramyayuktāni dharmādharmāśrayāṇy api ।। viviktāś ca śilāchāyās tathā prasravaṇāni ca ।।
kānaneṣu viviktāś ca śailānāṃ mahatīr guhāḥ ।। yajñāṃś ca vividhākārān vidyāś ca vividhās tathā ।। dānaṃ ca vividhākāraṃ dīnāndhakṛpaṇādiṣu ।। sattvaṃ rajas tamaś caiva dharmārthau kāma eva ca ।।
svāhākāravaṣaṭkārau svadhākāranamaskriye ।। yājanādhyāpane caiva tathānyad api kiṃcana ।। śubhāśubhabhayaṃ sarvam etad āhuḥ sanātanam ।। divasānte guṇān etān atītyaiko avatiṣṭhate ।।
evam evaiṣa tat sarvaṃ krīḍārtham abhimanyate ।। evam etāṃ prakurvāṇaḥ sargapralayadharmiṇīm ।। kriyākriyāpathopetas tathā tad iti manyate ।। rajasā tamasā caiva vyāptaṃ sarvam anekadhā ।।
matta etāni jāyante pralaye yānti mām api ।। manyate pakṣabuddhitvāt tathaiva sukṛtāny api ।। ihaiva cainaṃ bhokṣyāmi śubhāśubhaphalodayam ।। yāvad eva tu me saukhyaṃ jātyāṃ jātyāṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
sukhaduḥkhaṃ hi mānuṣyaṃ niraye cāpi majjanam ।। manuṣyatvāc ca devatvaṃ devatvāt pauruṣaṃ punaḥ ।। eṣa evaṃ dvijātīnām ātmā vai sa guṇair vṛtaḥ ।। mamatvenāvṛto nityaṃ tatraiva parivartate ।।
ya evaṃ kurute karma śubhāśubhaphalātmakam ।। prakṛtiḥ kurute karma śubhāśubhaphalātmakam ।। tiryagyonimanuṣyatve devaloke tathaiva ca ।। aliṅgaprakṛtitvāc ca liṅgair apy anumīyate ।।
sa liṅgāntaram āsādya prākṛtaṃ liṅgam avraṇam ।। śrotrādīni tu sarvāṇi pañca karmendriyāṇy atha ।। aham etāni vai kurvan mamaitānīndriyāṇi ha ।। aliṅgo liṅgam ātmānam akālaṃ kālam ātmanaḥ ।।
amṛtyuṃ mṛtyum ātmānam acaraṃ caram ātmanaḥ ।। atattvaṃ tattvam ātmānam abhavaṃ bhavam ātmanaḥ ।। evam apratibuddhatvād abuddhajanasevanāt ।। janmāntarasahasrāṇi maraṇāntāni gacchati ।।
candramā iva kośānāṃ punas tatra sahasraśaḥ ।। kalā pañcadaśī yonis tad dhāma iti paṭhyate ।। kalayā jāyate ajasraṃ punaḥ punar abuddhimān ।। ṣoḍaśī tu kalā sūkṣmā sa soma upadhāryatām ।।
prakṛtes triguṇāyās tu sa eva triguṇo bhavet ।। strīpuṃsayor vā saṃbandhaḥ sa vai puruṣa ucyate ।। ṛte striyaṃ na puruṣo rūpaṃ nirvartate tathā ।। rūpaṃ nirvartayed etad evaṃ sarvāsu yoniṣu ।।
ṛtau nirvartate rūpaṃ tad vakṣyāmi nidarśanam ।। asthi snāyu ca majjā ca jānīmaḥ pitṛto dvija ।। evam etad dvijaśreṣṭha vedaśāstreṣu paṭhyate ।। vedaśāstrapramāṇaṃ ca pramāṇaṃ tat sanātanam ।।
yac cāpi bhagavaṃs tasmān mokṣadharmo na vidyate ।। tan mamācakṣva tattvena pratyakṣo hy asi sarvadā ।। ajeyam ajaraṃ nityam atīndriyam anīśvaram ।। evam etad yathā vakṣye tattvagrāhī yathā bhavān ।।
na ca granthasya tattvajño yathātattvaṃ nareśvara ।। na ca granthārthatattvajñas tasya taddhāraṇaṃ vṛthā ।। yas tu granthārthatattvajño nāsya granthāgamo vṛthā ।। yathātattvābhigamanād arthaṃ tasya sa vindati ।।
sa kathaṃ mandavijñāno granthaṃ vakṣyati nirṇayāt ।। lobhād vāpy athavā dambhāt sa pāpī narakaṃ vrajet ।। so apīhāsyārthatattvajño yasmān naivātmavān api ।। yathā tattvena sāṃkhyeṣu yogeṣu ca mahātmasu ।।
ekaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ ca yogaṃ ca yaḥ paśyati sa buddhimān ।। etad aindriyakaṃ tāta yad bhavān ittham āttha mām ।। dehād deham avāpnoti bījād bījaṃ tathaiva ca ।। kathaṃ guṇā bhaviṣyanti nirguṇatvān mahātmanaḥ ।।
evaṃ guṇāḥ prakṛtijā jāyante na ca yānti ca ।। aṣṭau tāny atha śukreṇa jānīhi prākṛtena vai ।। vāyur eṣa pumāṃś caiva rasa ity abhidhīyate ।। yathā puṣpaphalair nityaṃ mūrtaṃ cāmūrtayas tathā ।।
pañcaviṃśatikas tāta liṅgeṣu niyatātmakaḥ ।। kevalaṃ tv abhimānitvād guṇeṣu guṇa ucyate ।। tasmād evaṃ vijānanti ye janā guṇadarśinaḥ ।। tadā sa guṇavān eva guṇabhedān prapaśyati ।।
budhyamānaṃ mahāprājñāḥ prabuddhaparivarjanāt ।। nirguṇaṃ ceśvaraṃ nityam adhiṣṭhātāram eva ca ।। sāṃkhyayoge ca kuśalā budhyante paramaiṣiṇaḥ ।। budhyamānaṃ na budhyante avagacchanti samaṃ tadā ।।
budhyamānaṃ prabudhyante dvābhyāṃ pṛthag ariṃdama ।। ekatvam akṣaraṃ prāhur nānātvaṃ kṣaram ucyate ।। ekatvadarśanaṃ cāsya nānātvaṃ cāsya darśanam ।। pañcaviṃśatibhis tattvaṃ tattvam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
varjyasya varjyam ācāraṃ tattvaṃ tattvāt sanātanam ।। paśyatas tad dhi saṃdigdham etayor vai nidarśanam ।। sthūlabuddhyā na paśyāmi tattvam etan na saṃśayaḥ ।। tad apy asthirabuddhitvāt pranaṣṭam iva me anagha ।।
dvaṃdvaṃ caivāniruddhaṃ ca budhyamānaṃ ca tattvataḥ ।। sāṃkhyayogaṃ ca kṛtsnena buddhābuddhiṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।। yogakṛtyaṃ mahārāja pṛthag eva śṛṇuṣva me ।। tac cāpi dvividhaṃ dhyānam āhur vidyāvido janāḥ ।।
prāṇāyāmas tu saguṇo nirguṇo mānasas tathā ।। dvikālaṃ nopabhuñjīta śeṣaṃ bhuñjīta tatparaḥ ।। daśadvādaśabhir vāpi caturviṃśāt paraṃ yataḥ ।। tiṣṭhantam ajaraṃ taṃ tu yat tad uktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।।
dravyaṃ hy ahīnamanaso nānyatheti viniścayaḥ ।। pūrvarātre parārdhe ca dhārayīta mano hṛdi ।। mano buddhyā sthiraṃ kṛtvā pāṣāṇa iva niścalaḥ ।। buddhyā vidhividhānajñas tato yuktaṃ pracakṣate ।।
na ca sparśaṃ vijānāti na ca saṃkalpate manaḥ ।। tadā prakṛtim āpannaṃ yuktam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ।। niliṅgaś cādhaś cordhvaṃ ca tiryaggatim avāpnuyāt ।। hṛdayastho antarātmeti jñeyo jñas tāta madvidhaiḥ ।।
vaidyuto agnir ivākāśe paśyaty ātmānam ātmani ।। brāhmaṇā brahmayonisthā hy ayonim amṛtātmakam ।। sarvatra sarvabhūteṣu dhruvaṃ tiṣṭhan na dṛśyate ।। mahatas tamasas tāta pāre tiṣṭhan na tāmasaḥ ।।
vimalo vimataś caiva nirliṅgo aliṅgasaṃjñakaḥ ।। evaṃ paśyan prapaśyeta ātmānam ajaraṃ param ।। sāṃkhyajñānaṃ pravakṣyāmi parisaṃkhyānidarśanam ।। tasmān mahat samutpannaṃ dvitīyaṃ rājasattama ।।
pañcabhūtāny ahaṃkārād āhuḥ sāṃkhyātmadarśinaḥ ।। pañca caiva viśeṣāś ca tathā pañcendriyāṇi ca ।। sāṃkhye sāṃkhyavidhānajñā nityaṃ sāṃkhyapathe sthitāḥ ।। līyante pratilomāni gṛhyante cāntarātmanā ।।
guṇā guṇeṣu satataṃ sāgarasyormayo yathā ।। ekatvaṃ pralaye cāsya bahutvaṃ ca tathā sṛji ।। adhiṣṭhātāram avyaktam asyāpy etan nidarśanam ।। ekatvaṃ pralaye cāsya bahutvaṃ ca pravartanāt ।।
tac ca kṣetraṃ mahān ātmā pañcaviṃśo adhitiṣṭhati ।। adhiṣṭhānād adhiṣṭhātā kṣetrāṇām iti naḥ śrutam ।। avyaktike pure śete puruṣaś ceti kathyate ।। kṣetram avyakta ity uktaṃ jñātāraṃ pañcaviṃśakam ।।
jñānam avyaktam ity uktaṃ jñeyo vai pañcaviṃśakaḥ ।। anīśvaram atattvaṃ ca tattvaṃ tat pañcaviṃśakam ।। saṃkhyā prakurute caiva prakṛtiṃ ca pravakṣyate ।। saṃkhyā sahasrakṛtyā tu nistattvaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ ।।
yadā budhyati ātmānaṃ tadā bhavati kevalaḥ ।। evam etad vijānantaḥ sāmyatāṃ pratiyānty uta ।। guṇavattvād yathaitāni nirguṇebhyas tathā bhavet ।। vidyate kṣarabhāvaś ca na parasparam avyayam ।।
te vyaktiṃ pratipadyante punaḥ punar ariṃdama ।। vyaktibhūtā bhaviṣyanti vyaktasyaivānuvartanāt ।। ya evam abhijānanti na bhayaṃ teṣu vidyate ।। vidyāvidye tv idānīṃ me tvaṃ nibodhānupūrvaśaḥ ।।
sargapralaya ity uktaṃ vidyāvidye ca viṃśakaḥ ।। yathoktam ṛṣibhis tāta sāṃkhyasyātinidarśanam ।। buddhīndriyāṇāṃ ca tathā viśeṣā iti naḥ śrutam ।। manasaḥ pañca bhūtāni vidyā ity abhicakṣate ।।
ahaṃkāras tathā vidyā buddhir vidyā nareśvara ।। vidyā jñeyā naraśreṣṭha vidhiś ca paramaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। sarvasya sarvam ity uktaṃ jñeyajñānasya pāragaḥ ।। tathaiva jñānam avyaktaṃ vijñātā pañcaviṃśakaḥ ।।
akṣaraṃ ca kṣaraṃ caiva yad uktaṃ tan nibodha me ।। kāraṇaṃ tu pravakṣyāmi yathājñānaṃ tu jñānataḥ ।। tattvasaṃjñāv ubhāv eva procyete jñānacintakaiḥ ।। tad etad guṇasargāya vikurvāṇaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।।
adhiṣṭhānaṃ kṣetram āhur etad vai pañcaviṃśakam ।। tad ahaṃ tad guṇais tais tu pañcaviṃśe vilīyate ।। kṣetrajño api tadā tāvat kṣetrajñaḥ saṃpraṇīyate ।। nirguṇatvaṃ ca vai dehe guṇeṣu parivartanāt ।।
prakṛtyā nirguṇas tv eṣa ity evam anuśuśruma ।। prakṛtiṃ tv atha jānāti nirguṇatvaṃ tathātmanaḥ ।। anyo aham anyeyam iti yadā budhyati buddhimān ।। prakṛtyā caiṣa rājendra miśro anyo anyasya dṛśyate ।।
paśyate ca paraṃ paśyaṃs tadā paśyan nu saṃsṛjet ।। yathā matsyo hy abhijñānād anuvartitavāñ jalam ।। matsyo yathodakajñānād anuvartitavān iha ।। ātmānaṃ tad avajñānād anyaṃ caiva na vedmy aham ।।
anuvartitavān mohād anyam anyaṃ janāj janam ।। sāmyam ekatvatāṃ yāto yādṛśas tādṛśas tv aham ।। ayaṃ hi vimalo vyaktam aham īdṛśakas tadā ।। saṃsargād atisaṃsargāt sthitaḥ kālam imaṃ tv aham ।।
uttamādhamamadhyānāṃ tām ahaṃ katham āvase ।। gacchāmy abuddhabhāvatvād ihedānīṃ sthiro bhava ।। vañcito hy anayā yad dhi nirvikāro vikārayā ।। yo aham atrābhavaṃ saktaḥ parāṅmukham upasthitaḥ ।।
amūrtiś cāpy amūrtātmā mamatvena pradharṣitaḥ ।। nirmamasya mamatvena vikṛtaṃ tāsu tāsu ca ।। samatā na mayā kācid ahaṃkāre kṛtā mayā ।। idānīm avabuddho asmi nirmamo nirahaṃkṛtaḥ ।।
apalagnām imāṃ hitvā saṃśrayiṣye nirāmayam ।। kṣemaṃ mama sahānena naivaikam anayā saha ।। akṣaratvaṃ nigacchati tyaktvā kṣaram anāmayam ।। nirguṇaṃ prathamaṃ dṛṣṭvā tādṛg bhavati maithila ।।
mayeha jñānasaṃpannaṃ yathā śrutinidarśanāt ।। pravakṣyāmi tu te bhūyas tan nibodha yathāśrutam ।। yad eva sāṃkhyaśāstroktaṃ yogadarśanam eva tat ।। vispaṣṭaṃ procyate tatra śiṣyāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā ।।
asmiṃś ca śāstre yogānāṃ punarbhavapuraḥsaram ।। sāṃkhyānāṃ tu paraṃ tattvaṃ yathāvad anuvarṇitam ।। budhyamānaṃ ca buddhatvaṃ prāhur yoganidarśanam ।। guṇānāṃ dhāryatāṃ tattvaṃ sṛjaty ākṣipate tathā ।।
ātmānaṃ bahudhā kṛtvā nāneva praticakṣate ।। guṇān ācarate hy eṣa sṛjaty ākṣipate tathā ।। na tv evaṃ budhyate avyaktaṃ saguṇaṃ tāta nirguṇam ।। budhyate yadi cāvyaktam etad vai pañcaviṃśakam ।।
anyonyapratibuddhena vadanty avyaktam acyutam ।। pañcaviṃśaṃ mahātmānaṃ na cāsāv api budhyate ।। satataṃ pañcaviṃśaṃ tu caturviṃśaṃ vibudhyate ।। avyaktaṃ caiva tad brahma budhyate tāta kevalam ।।
budhyamāno yadātmānam anyo aham iti manyate ।। budhyate ca parāṃ buddhiṃ viśuddhām amalāṃ yathā ।। tatas tyajati so avyaktaṃ sargapralayadharmiṇam ।। tataḥ kevaladharmāsau bhavaty avyaktadarśanāt ।।
etat tu tattvam ity āhur nistattvam ajarāmaram ।। pañcaviṃśatitattvāni pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। eṣām upaiti tattvaṃ hi kṣipraṃ budhyasva lakṣaṇam ।। kevalena balenaiva samatāṃ yāty asaṃśayam ।।
etan nānātvam ity uktaṃ sāṃkhyaśrutinidarśanāt ।। ekatvaṃ vai bhavet tasya yadā buddhyānubudhyate ।। saṅgadharmā bhavaty eṣa niḥsaṅgātmā narādhipa ।। vibhus tyajati cāvyaktaṃ yadā tv etad vibudhyate ।।
eṣa hy apratibuddhaś ca budhyamānas tu te anagha ।। maśakodumbare yadvad anyatvaṃ tadvad etayoḥ ।। evam eva ca gantavyaṃ nānātvaikatvam etayoḥ ।। pañcaviṃśatikasyāśu yo ayaṃ dehe pravartate ।।
so ayam evaṃ vimucyeta nānyatheti viniścayaḥ ।। viśuddhadharmā śuddhena nāśuddhena ca buddhimān ।। viyogadharmiṇā caiva vimuktātmā bhavaty atha ।। śucikarmā śuciś caiva bhavaty amitabuddhimān ।।
svatantraś ca svatantreṇa svatantratvam avāpyate ।। pañcaviṃśaṃ muniśreṣṭhā vasiṣṭhena yathā purā ।। nāti budhyati tattvena budhyamāno ajarāmaram ।। kathitaṃ tattvato viprāḥ śrutvā devarṣito dvijāḥ ।।
vasiṣṭhād ṛṣiśārdūlo nārado avāptavān idam ।। mā śucadhvaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ śrutvaitat paramaṃ padam ।। vidyate tu bhayaṃ yasya yo nainaṃ vetti tattvataḥ ।। pretya jātisahasrāṇi maraṇāntāny upāśnute ।।
yadi vā mucyate vāpi tasmād ajñānasāgarāt ।। ahany ahani majjanti yatra bhūtāni bho dvijāḥ ।। tasmād yūyaṃ virajaskā vitamaskāś ca bho dvijāḥ ।। kathitaṃ paramaṃ mokṣaṃ yaṃ jñātvā na nivartate ।।
na duṣṭamataye viprā na śraddhāvimukhāya ca ।। daśāṣṭadoṣarahitair vākyaiḥ sāratarair dvijāḥ ।। jātiśuddhasamāyuktaṃ sādhuśabdopaśobhitam ।। śrāvayitvā yathānyāyaṃ virarāma mahāmatiḥ ।।
ādyaṃ brāhmābhidhānaṃ ca sarvavāñchāphalapradam ।। praśaśaṃsus tadā vyāsaṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ munim ।। sarvābhipretaphaladaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ param ।। na te asty aviditaṃ kiṃcit triṣu lokeṣu vai prabho ।।
namasyāmo mahāprājñaṃ brahmiṣṭhaṃ tvāṃ mahāmunim ।। kaḥ śaknoti guṇān vaktuṃ tava sarvān mahāmune ।। kṛtavān bhārataṃ śāstraṃ tasmai jñānātmane namaḥ ।। jñānāñjanaśalākena tvayā conmīlitā dṛśaḥ ।।
jagmur yathāgataṃ sarve kṛtakṛtyāḥ svam āśramam ।। purāṇaṃ sumahāpuṇyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।। vyāsaprasādāt tat sarvaṃ mayā saṃparikīrtitam ।। dhanasaukhyapradaṃ nṝṇāṃ pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam ।।
śrotavyaṃ suprayatnena samyak śreyobhikāṅkṣibhiḥ ।। vaiśyas tu dhanam akṣayyaṃ śūdraḥ sukham avāpnuyāt ।। taṃ taṃ kāmam avāpnoti naro nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ ।। viśiṣṭaṃ sarvaśāstrebhyaḥ puruṣārthopapādakam ।।
śrute asmin sarvadoṣotthaḥ pāparāśiḥ praṇaśyati ।। upoṣya yad avāpnoti tad asya śravaṇān naraḥ ।। mahāpuṇyamayaṃ viprās tad asya śravaṇāt sakṛt ।। mathurāyāṃ hariṃ dṛṣṭvā prāpnoti puruṣaḥ phalam ।।
purāṇe asya hito viprāḥ keśavārpitamānasaḥ ।। tat phalaṃ samavāpnoti yaḥ paṭhec chṛṇuyād api ।। yaḥ paṭhec chṛṇuyān martyaḥ sa yāti bhuvanaṃ hareḥ ।। ekādaśyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ ca viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
balapuṣṭipradaṃ nṝṇāṃ dhanyaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam ।। idaṃ variṣṭham ākhyānaṃ sa sarvam īpsitaṃ labhet ।। bhayād vimucyate bhīta āpadāpanna āpadaḥ ।। dharmaṃ cārthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca mokṣaṃ tu labhate naraḥ ।।
tāṃs tān sarvān avāpnoti puruṣo nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। na deyaṃ duṣṭamataye nāstikāya viśeṣataḥ ।।
